B_5_C_1_0
BEGIN_
ततो रावणनीतायाः सीतायाः शत्रुकर्शनः |
इयेष पदमन्वेष्टुं चारणाचरिते पथि ||५-१-१
_END
BEGIN_
After that, Hanuma, the destroyer of foes, desired to travel in the sky where
celestials like chaaranas tread, to search for Seetha, who was taken away by Ravana._END

B_5_C_1_1
BEGIN_
दुष्करं निष्प्रतिद्वन्द्वं चिकीर्षन् कर्म वानरः |
समुदग्रशिरोग्रीवो गवांपतिरिवाबभौ || ५-१-२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma who desired to perform a deed done by no one else, shone like a bull without
any obstacles, with his stretched neck and raised head._END

B_5_C_1_2
BEGIN_
अथ वैडूर्यवर्णेषु शाद्वलेषु महाबलः |
धीरः सलिलकल्पेषु विच्चार यथासुखम् ||५-१-३_END
BEGIN_
After that, the mighty and courageous Hanuma roamed at ease on the lawns with the
hue of an emerald, which looked like still water from a distance._END

B_5_C_1_3
BEGIN_
द्विजान् वित्रासयन् धीमानुरसा पादपान् हरन् |
मृगांश्च सुबाहुन्निघ्नन् प्रवृद्ध इव केसरी|| ५-१-४_END
BEGIN_
The thoughtful Hanuma tread like a rampant lion, making birds fear, uprooting trees
by his breast and also killing many animals._END

B_5_C_1_4
BEGIN_
नीललोहितमाञ्जिष्ठपत्रवर्णैः सितासितैः |
स्वभावविहितैश्चित्रैर्धातुभिः समलंकृतम् ||५-१-५
कामरूपिभिराविष्टमभीक्ष्णं सपरिच्छिदैः |
यक्षकिन्नरगन्धर्वैर्देवक्ल्पैश्च पन्नगैः ||५-१-६
स तस्य गिरिवर्यस्य तले नागवरायुते |
तिष्ठन् कपिवरस्तत्र ह्रदे नाग इवाबभौ ||५-१-७_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey Hanuma shone like an elephant in a lake, standing on the foot of
that great mountain by the name of Mahendra, where many elephants of good breed resided, which was
beautifully decorated with many naturally formed mineral rocks of varied hue like black, white,
red, blue, yellow and green and which was surrounded by godly serpents and Yakshas, Kinnaras,
Gandharvas who were capable of assuming desired form, together with their families._END

B_5_C_1_5
BEGIN_
स सूर्याय महेन्द्राय पवनाय स्वयंभुवे |
भूतेभ्यश्चाञ्जलिं कृत्वा चकार गमने मतिम् || ५-१-८_END
BEGIN_
He saluted with joined palms to the Sun-God, Lord Indra, God of Wind, Lord Brahma
and Bhutas and decided to leave._END

B_5_C_1_6
BEGIN_
अञ्जलिं प्राङ्मुखः कृत्वा पवनायात्मयोओनयो |
ततो हि ववृधे गन्तुं दक्षिणो दक्षिणां दिश्म् || ५-१-९_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma turned towards east, saluted his father, the Lord of Wind and increased his
body to go towards southern direction._END

B_5_C_1_7
BEGIN_
प्लवङ्गप्रवरैर्दृष्टः प्लवने कृतनिश्चयः |
ववृधे रामवृद्ध्यर्थम् समुद्र इव पर्वसु || ५-१-१०_END
BEGIN_
With all the Vaanaras seeing, Hanuma decided to fly and like an ocean swelling on
full moon days, grew for Rama's success._END

B_5_C_1_8
BEGIN_
निष्प्रमाणशरीरः सन् लिलङ्घयिषुरर्णवम् |
बाहुभ्यां पीडयामास चरणाभ्यां च पर्वतम् || ५-१-११_END
BEGIN_
With a desire to cross the ocean, Hanuma grew his body immeasurably and pressed the
mountain with his feet and hands._END

B_5_C_1_9
BEGIN_
स चचालाचलश्चापि मुहूर्तं कपिपीडितः |
तरूणां पुष्पिताग्राणां सर्वं पुष्पमशातयत् || ५-१-१२_END
BEGIN_
Thus tormented by Hanuma, that mountain shook for an instant and showered all
flowers of trees on it._END

B_5_C_1_10
BEGIN_
तेन पादपमुक्तेन पुष्पौघेन सुगन्धिना |
सर्वतः संवृतः शैलो बभौ पुष्पमयो यथा ||५-१-१३_END
BEGIN_
Covered all through by those fragrant flowers which fell down from the trees, that
mountain shone like a mountain made of flowers._END

B_5_C_2_0
BEGIN_
स सागरमनाधृष्यमतिक्रम्य महाबलः |त्रिकूटशिखरे लङ्कां स्थितां स्वस्थो ददर्श ह || ५-२-१_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma with great strength crossed the insurmountable ocean without becoming tired and viewed the city of 
Lanka located on the peak of Mount Trikuta._END

B_5_C_1_11
BEGIN_
तेन चोत्तमवीर्येण पीड्यमानः स पर्वतः |
सलिलं संप्रसुस्राव मदं मत्त इव द्विपः ||५-१-१४_END
BEGIN_
That mountain shed water like an elephant in rut emitting rut juice, after being
pressed by the mighty Hanuma._END

B_5_C_2_1
BEGIN_
ततः पादपमुक्तेन पुष्पवर्षेण वीर्यवान् |अभिवृष्टः स्थितस्तत्र बभौ पुष्पमयो यथा || ५-२-२_END
BEGIN_
After that, the powerful Hanuma standing there shone like one made of flowers being showered by a rain of flowers 
released by trees._END

B_5_C_1_12
BEGIN_
पीड्यमानस्तु बलिना महेन्द्रस्तेन पर्वतः |
रीतीर्निर्वर्तयामास काञ्चनाञ्जनराजतीः ||५-१-१५_END
BEGIN_
Pressed by that mighty Hanuma, streaks of gold silver and antimony color appeared on
the Mahendra mountain._END

B_5_C_2_2
BEGIN_
योजनानां शतं श्रीमांस्तीर्त्वाप्युत्तमविक्रमः |अनिःस्वसन् कपिस्तत्र न ग्लानिमधिगच्छति || ५-२-३_END
BEGIN_
The glorious Hanuma with the best courage, even though crossing a hundred yojanas, was without a sigh and did 
not obtain any tiredness._END

B_5_C_1_13
BEGIN_
मुमोच च शिलाः शैलो विशालाः समनःशिलाः |
मध्यमेनार्चिषा जुष्टो धूमराजीरिवानलः ||५-१-१६_END
BEGIN_
Huge Rocks of Sulfur were also shot forth from that mountain, just as a fire burning
with a medium flame would emit columns of smoke._END

B_5_C_2_3
BEGIN_
शतान्यहं योजनानां क्रमेयं सुबहुन्यपि |किं पुनः सागरस्यान्तं संख्यातं शतयोजनम् || ५-२-४_END
BEGIN_
"I can cross many hundreds of yojanas. What to say about the end of the ocean which had been counted to be hundred 
yojanas long?"_END

B_5_C_2_4
BEGIN_
स तु वीर्यवतां श्रेष्ठः प्लवतामपि चोत्तमः |जगाम वेगवान् लङ्कां लङ्घयित्वा महोदधिम् || ५-२-५_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma, the best among powerful ones and the foremost also among those who can fly, reached the city of Lanka 
by crossing the great ocean with good speed._END

B_5_C_1_14
BEGIN_
गिरिणा पीड्यमानेन पीड्यमानानि सर्वशः |
गुहाविष्टानि भूतानि विनेदुर्विकृतैः स्वरैः ||५-१-१७_END
BEGIN_
Being pressed on all sides by the mountain which itself was being pressed by Hanuma,
creatures living in the caves of that mountain shrieked in horrifying tones._END

B_5_C_2_5
BEGIN_
शाद्वलानि च नीलानि गन्धवन्ति वनानि च |गण्डवन्ति च मध्येन जगाम नगवन्ति च || ५-२-६_END
BEGIN_
He passed through forests with dark green hued fragrant lawns and also consisting of great rocks and hills._END

B_5_C_1_15
BEGIN_
स महासत्त्वसंनादः शैलपीडानिमित्तजः |
पृथिवीं पूरयामास दिशश्चोपवनानि च ||५-१-१८_END
BEGIN_
That loud noise from creatures which emanated because of stress caused to the
mountain, filled the earth and all four directions and forests near that mountain._END

B_5_C_2_6
BEGIN_
शैलांश्च तरुसंचन्नान् वनराजीश्च पुष्पिताः |अभिचक्राम तेजस्वी हनुमान् प्लवगर्षभः || ५-२-७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the best among Vanaras and the radiant one, tread on mountains covered with trees and on series of trees 
full of flowers._END

B_5_C_1_16
BEGIN_
शिरोभिः पृथुभिः सर्पा व्यक्तस्वस्तिकलक्षणैः |
वमन्तः पावकं घोरं ददंशुर्दशनैः शिलाः ||५-१-१९_END
BEGIN_
Great snakes with clear swastika signs on their hoods, spewed out frightening flames
with their great heads and bit the rocks with their teeth._END

B_5_C_2_7
BEGIN_
स तस्मिन्नचले तिष्ठन्वनान्युपवनानि च |स नगाग्रे च तां लङ्कां ददर्श पवनात्मजः || ५-२-८_END
BEGIN_
That son of God Vayu stood on a mountain and saw forests and gardens and also the city of Lanka situated on the 
top of a mountain._END

B_5_C_1_17
BEGIN_
तास्तदा सविषैर्दष्टाः कुपितैस्तैर्महाशिलाः|
जज्ज्वलुः पावकोद्दीप्ता बिभिदुश्च सहस्रधा ||५-१-२०_END
BEGIN_
Then those great rocks bit by those snakes with anger and venom, burned due to the
flame and split into thousand pieces._END

B_5_C_2_8
BEGIN_
सरळान् कर्णिकारांश्च खर्जूरांश्च सुपुष्पितान् |प्रियाळान्मुचुळिन्दांश्च कुटजान् केतकानपि || ५-२-९प्रियङ्गून् 
गन्धपूर्णांश्च नीपान् सप्तच्छदांस्तथा |असनान् कोविदारांश्च करवीरांश्च पुष्पितान् || ५-२-१०पुष्पभारनिबद्धांश्च 
तथा मुकुळितानपि |पादपान् विहगाकीर्णान् पवनाधूतमस्तकान् || ५-२-११हंसकारण्डवाकीर्णान्वापीः पद्मोत्मलायुताः 
|आक्रीडान् विविधान् रम्यान्विविधांश्च जलाशयान् || ५-२-१२संततान् विविधैर्वऋकैः सर्वर्तुफलपुष्पितैः |
उद्यानानि च रम्याणि ददर्श कपिकुञ्जरः || ५-२-१३_END
BEGIN_
Standing on that mountain, the elephant among monkeys, Hanuma, saw pine trees, Karnikaras, date-palms in full 
blossom, Priyalas, lemon trees, wild jasmine trees, mogra trees, long pepper trees filled with sweet fragrance, 
Kadamba trees and seven leaved banana trees, Asana trees, Kovidaras, Karaviras in full blossom, trees that were 
tied by the weight of their flowers and flower buds, that were distressed by birds, with their crests moved by 
wind, wells and various glorious pleasure-groves filled by various trees that give fruits and flowers in all seasons 
and beautiful gardens also, surrounded by various ponds consisting of swans and ducks._END

B_5_C_1_18
BEGIN_
यानि चौषधजालानि तस्मिन् जातानि पर्वते |
विषघ्नान्यपि नागानां न शेकुः शमितुं विषम्|| ५-१-२१_END
BEGIN_
Medicinal herbs from that mountain, although capable of destroying ordinary poisons,
could not neutralize the poison from those snakes._END

B_5_C_3_0
BEGIN_
स लम्ब शिखरे लम्बे लम्ब तोयद सम्निभे |सत्त्वम् आस्थाय मेधावी हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-३-१
निशि लन्काम् महा सत्त्वः विवेश कपि कुन्जरः |रम्य कानन तोय आढ्याम् पुरीम् रावण पालिताम् || ५-३-२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, best among monkeys, the intellectual son of Vayu, one with great might, stood on the 
moutain called Lamba with its high peaks equalling a high cloud, gathered courage and entered at night the city 
of Lanka ruled by Ravana and filled with beautiful forests and places of water such as lakes._END

B_5_C_2_9
BEGIN_
समासाद्य च लक्ष्मीवन् लङ्कां रावणपालिताम् |परिखाभिः सपद्माभिः सोत्पलाभिरलंकृताम् || ५-२-१४सीतापहरणार्थेन 
रावणेन सुरक्षिताम् |समन्ताद्विचरद्भिश्च राक्षसैरुग्रधन्विभिः || ५-२-१५काञ्चनेनावृतां रम्यां प्राकारेण 
महापुरीम् |गृहैश्च ग्रहसंकाशैः शारदाम्बुदसन्निभैः || ५-२-१६पाण्डुराभिः प्रतोळीभिरुच्चाभिरभिसंवृताम् |
अट्टालकशताकीर्णां पताकाध्वजमालिनीम् || ५-२-१७तोरणैः काञ्चनैर्दिव्यैर्लतापङ्किविचित्रितैः |ददर्श हनुमान् 
लङ्कां दिवि देवपुरीं यथा || ५-२-१८_END
BEGIN_
The glorious Hanuma neared the city of Lanka ruled by Ravana, and saw the city which looked like the city of Gods 
in heaven, decorated by moats filled with lotuses and water-lilies, which was well protected, since the time of 
Seetha's abduction, by Ravana and by Rakshasas with horrifying voices roaming around, which was surrounded by 
a golden boundary wall, that beautiful great city consisted of houses equal in height to mountains and which looked 
like autumnal clouds, with white and elevated main streets, decorated with flags and pennons, with excellent golden 
hued archways adorned with sculpted rows of vines._END

B_5_C_1_19
BEGIN_
भिद्यतेऽयं गिरिर्भूतैरिति मत्त्वा तपस्विनः |
त्रस्ता विद्याधरास्तस्मादुत्पेतुः स्त्रीगणैः सह|| ५-१-२२
पानभूमिगतं हित्वा हैममासवभाजनम् |
पात्रणि च महार्हाणि करकांश्च हिरण्मयान् ||५-१-२३
लेह्यानुच्चावचान् भक्ष्यान् मांसानि विविधानि च |
आर्षभाणि च चर्माणि खड्गांश्च कनकत्सरून् || ५-१-२४_END
BEGIN_
Ascetics residing on that mountain flew away from there thinking that some demons
were destroying it. Vidhyadharas who lived there, became afraid and flew away with their women
folk, leaving behind them golden jugs of wine in the liquor house, gold vases, a varieties of
sauces that can be licked, eatables, various meats, skins of oxen and swords with golden hilts._END

B_5_C_3_1
BEGIN_
शारद अम्बु धर प्रख्यैः भवनैः उपशोभिताम् |सागर उपम निर्घोषाम् सागर अनिल सेविताम् || ५-३-३
सुपुष्ट बल सम्गुप्ताम् यथैव विटपावतीम् |चारु तोरण निर्यूहाम् पाण्डुर द्वार तोरणाम्|| ५-३-४_END
BEGIN_The city of Lanka was shone by buildings equalling autumnal clouds. With a sound resembling that 
of an ocean, it was served by ocean breeze. It was filled with well fed and mighty armies like Vitapati, the capital 
of Kubera. It had elephants positioned at archways and had white gates and archways._END

B_5_C_2_10
BEGIN_
गिरिमूर्ध्नि स्थितां लङ्कां पाण्डुरैर्भवनैः शुभैः |ददर्श स कपिश्रेष्ठः पुरमाकाशगं यथा || ५-२-१९_END
BEGIN_
That best among monkeys Hanuma saw the city of Lanka with beautiful white buildings situated on the top of a mountain 
like a city located in the sky._END

B_5_C_1_20
BEGIN_
कृतक्ण्ठगुणाः क्षीबा र्क्तमाल्यानुलेपनाः |
र्क्तक्षाः पुष्कराक्षाश्च गगनं प्रतिपेदिरे ||५-१-२५_END
BEGIN_
The intoxicated Vidyadharas with garlands around their neck decked with red flower
garlands and smeared with sandal paste, with reddened eyes, and with lotus shaped eyes, obtained
the sky._END

B_5_C_3_2
BEGIN_भुजग आचरिताम् गुप्ताम् शुभाम् भोगवतीम् इव |ताम् सविद्युत् घन आकीर्णाम् ज्योतिः मार्ग निषेविताम् 
|| ५-३-५चण्ड मारुत निर्ह्रादाम् यथा इन्द्रस्य अमरावतीम् |शातकुम्भेन महता प्राकारेण अभिसम्वृताम् || ५-३-६
किन्किणी जाल घोषाभिः पताकाभिः अलम्कृताम् |आसाद्य सहसा हृष्टः प्राकारम् अभिपेदिवान् || ५-३-७_END
BEGIN_Quickly approaching that city of Lanka which was protected by Rakshasas, like the the auspicious 
city of Bhogavati being protected by serpents moving about, spread with cloud illumined by flashes of lightening, 
served by pathways of stars, witha light breeze like the Indra's city of Amaravati, surrounded by a wall with 
a golden hue, decorated by flags with sounds from groups of small bells. He became happy and leapt up the wall._END

B_5_C_2_11
BEGIN_
पालितां राक्षसेन्द्रेण निर्मितां विश्वकर्मणा |प्लवमानामिवाकाशे ददर्श हनुमान् पुरीम् || ५-२-२०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw that city of Lanka ruled by Ravana the king of Rakshasas, constructed by Visvakarma (architect of Gods), 
and which looked as though it were floating in the sky._END

B_5_C_1_21
BEGIN_
हारनूपुरकेयूरपारिहार्यधराः स्त्रियः |
विस्मिताः सस्मितास्तस्थुराकाशे रमणैः सह ||५-१-२६_END
BEGIN_
Vidyadhara women wearing necklaces, anklets, armlets and bangles stood in the sky
with surprise and with smiles along with their loved ones._END

B_5_C_3_3
BEGIN_विस्मय आविष्ट हृदयः पुरीम् आलोक्य सर्वतः |जाम्बूनदमयैः द्वारैः वैदूर्य कृत वेदिकैः || 
५-३-८मणि स्फटिक मुक्ताभिः मणि कुट्टिम भूषितैः |तप्त हाटक निर्यूहैः राजत अमल पाण्डुरैः || ५-३-९वैदूर्य 
तल सोपानैः स्फाटिक अन्तर पांसुभिः |चारु सम्जवन उपेतैः खम् इव उत्पतितैः शुभैः || ५-३-१०क्रौन्च बर्हिण सम्घुष्टे 
राज हंस निषेवितैः |तूर्य आभरण निर्घोषैः सर्वतः प्रतिनादिताम् || ५-३-११वस्वोकसारा प्रतिमाम् समीक्ष्य नगरीम् 
ततः |खम् इव उत्पतिताम् लन्काम् जहर्ष हनुमान् कपिः || ५-३-१२_END
BEGIN_Seeing the city everywhere Hanuma became surprised at heart. Thereafter Hanuma the monkey, became 
happy seeing the doors which were of golden color, with platforms of cat's eye gems, inlaid with diamonds, crystals 
and pearls, embellished with floors of gems, graced with elephants made of refined gold, crowned with spotless 
white silver, stairs studded with cat's eye gems, with inside walls made of crystal free from dust, provided with 
lovely assembly halls, with sounds of Krauncha birds and peacocks, served by royal swans, looking as though flying 
toward the sky, with auspicious houses resounding everywhere with the sounds of clarionets and ornaments, equalling 
the city of Vasvaukasaara, as though flying towards the sky._END

B_5_C_2_12
BEGIN_
पप्रप्राकारजघनां विपुलाम्बुनवाम्बराम् |शतघ्नीशूलकेशान्तामट्टालकवतंसकाम् || ५-२-२१मन्सेव कृतां लङ्कां निर्मितां 
विश्वकर्मणा |द्वारमुत्तरमासाद्य चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-२-२२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw the city of Lanka with buttress and enclosure wall as her hip and loins, the vast body pf water in 
the moat as her raiment, Satagnis and Sulas as her locks, the mansions as her earrings, constructed by thought. 
He reached the northern gate and thought thus._END

B_5_C_1_22
BEGIN_
दर्शयन्तो महाविद्यां विद्याधरमहर्षयः |
सहितास्तस्थुराकाशे वीक्षाञ्चक्रुश्च पर्वतम्|| ५-१-२७_END
BEGIN_
Vidyadharas and great sages stood in the sky in a group, showing their great prowess
and viewed the mountain._END

B_5_C_3_4
BEGIN_ताम् समीक्ष्य पुरीम् लन्काम् राक्षस अधिपतेः शुभाम् |अनुत्तमाम् ऋद्धि युताम् चिन्तयाम् 
आस वीर्यवान् || ५-३-१३_END
BEGIN_Seeing that city of Ravana, which was best among cities, a wealthy city, a beautiful and auspicious 
city, that powerful Hanuma thought thus._END

B_5_C_2_13
BEGIN_
कैलासशिखरप्रख्यामालिख्स्न्तीमिवाम्बरम् |डीयमानामिवाकाशमुच्छ्रितैर्भवनोत्तमैः || ५-२-२३संपूर्णां राक्षसैर्घोरैर्नागैर्भोगवतीमिव 
|अचिन्त्यां सुकृतां स्पष्टां कुबेराध्युषितां पुरा || ५-२-२४दंष्ट्रिभिर्बहुभिः शूरैः शूलपट्टिसपाणिभिः |
रक्षितां राक्षसैर्घोरैर्गुहामाशीविषैरिव || ५-२-२५तस्याश्च महतीं गुप्तिं सागरं च निरीक्ष्य सः |रावणं च 
रिपुं घोरं चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-२-२६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw the city of Lanka equal to peak of Kailasa as though touching the sky, as though flying to reach the 
sky, with its best mansions, filled with horrible rakshasas and serpants like the city of Bhogavati (capital of 
Patala), one which was unfathomable, a well arranged and a clear city governed by Kubera in earlier times, protected 
by courageous, horrible serpents and Rakshasas with mouths with sharp teeth like a cave, with spikes and Pattisas 
(spears) in their hands. Hanuma saw that Lanka's great protection and the ocean and Ravana the horrible enemy 
and thought thus._END

B_5_C_1_23
BEGIN_
शुश्रुवुश्चतदा शब्दमृषीणां भावितात्मनाम्|
चारणानां च सिद्धानां स्थितानांविमलेऽम्बरे|| ५-१-२८_END
BEGIN_
Then they heard words of Charanas, Siddhas and pure hearted Rishis who were located
in that clear sky._END

B_5_C_3_5
BEGIN_न इयम् अन्येन नगरी शक्या धर्षयितुम् बलात् |रक्षिता रावण बलैः उद्यत आयुध धारिभिः || ५-३-१४_END
BEGIN_"It is not possible for anyone else to oppose this city, by strength alone, which is being guarded 
by armies of Ravana with raised weapons."_END

B_5_C_1_24
BEGIN_
एष पर्वतसंकाशो हनूमान् मारुतात्मजः |
तितीर्षति महावेगः समुद्रं मकरालयम् ||५-१-२९_END
BEGIN_
"This Hanuma, who is equal to a mountain, who is the son of Vayu, and who has great
speed, wants to cross the ocean which is abode to crocodiles."_END

B_5_C_2_14
BEGIN_
आगत्यापीह हरयो भविष्यन्ति निररथकाः |न हि युद्धेन व लङ्का शक्या जेतुं सुरैरपि || ५-२-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Even if Vanaras were to come here they would not meet with success. It is not possible even for Devas to be victorious 
against Lanka in war"._END

B_5_C_3_6
BEGIN_कुमुद अन्गदयोः वा अपि सुषेणस्य महा कपेः |प्रसिद्धा इयम् भवेत् भूमिः मैन्द द्विविदयोः अपि 
|| ५-३-१५_END
BEGIN_This land may be conquerable by Kumuda or Angada, to the great monkey Sushena or to Mainda or Dvivida._END

B_5_C_1_25
BEGIN_
रामार्थं वानरार्थं च चिकीर्षन् कर्मदुष्करम् |
समुद्रस्य परं पारं दुष्प्रापं प्राप्तुमिच्छति|| ५-१-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Hanuma has decided to perform an impossible task for the sake of Rama and Vanaras
and wants to obtain the other side of ocean which is hard to obtain."_END

B_5_C_2_15
BEGIN_
इमां तु विषमां दुर्गां लङ्कां रावणपालिताम् |प्राप्यापि स महाबाहुः किम् करिष्यति राघवः || ५-२-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Even if He reaches this very difficult and impenetrable Lanka ruled by Ravana, what can that Sri Rama with mighty 
arms do"?_END

B_5_C_3_7
BEGIN_विवस्वतः तनूजस्य हरेः च कुश पर्वणः |ऋक्षस्य केतु मालस्य मम चैव गतिः भवेत् || ५-३-१६_END
BEGIN_There may be access to this land to the son of Sun God Sugreeva, to the monkey Kusaparvana, to 
the chief among monkeys Riksha and to me._END

B_5_C_1_26
BEGIN_
इति विद्याधराः श्रुत्वा वचस्तेषां महात्मनाम् |
तमप्रमेयं ददृशुः पर्वते वानरर्षभम् ||५-१-३१_END
BEGIN_
Vidyadharas thus listened to the words of those great people and looked at the
incomparable Hanuma, best among Vanaras, standing on the mountain._END

B_5_C_2_16
BEGIN_
अवकाशो न सान्त्वस्य रक्षसेष्वभिगम्यते |न दानस्य न भेदस्य नैव युद्धस्य दृश्यते || ५-२-२९_END
BEGIN_
"In the matter of overcoming rakshasas, there seems to be no opportunity for persuasion, gifts, dissension or 
even war"._END

B_5_C_3_8
BEGIN_समीक्ष्य तु महा बाहः राघवस्य पराक्रमम् |लक्ष्मणस्य च विक्रान्तम् अभवत् प्रीतिमान् कपिः 
|| ५-३-१७_END
BEGIN_Considering the long armed Sri Rama's strength and Lakshmana's valour, Hanuma became happy._END

B_5_C_2_17
BEGIN_
चतुर्णामेव हि गतिर्वानराणां महात्मनाम् |वालिपुत्रस्य नीलस्य मम राज्ञश्च धीमतः || ५-२-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Only four great Vanaras can come here - the son of Vali (Angada), Nila, myself and the wise king Sugriva"._END

B_5_C_1_27
BEGIN_
दुधुवे च स रोमाणि चकम्पे चाचलोपमः |
ननाद सुमहानादं सुमहानिव तोयदः || ५-१-३२_END
BEGIN_
He, who is equal to a mountain, shook his hair, quivered his body and let out a
great roar like from a vast cloud._END

B_5_C_3_9
BEGIN_ताम् रत्न वसन उपेताम् कोष्ठ आगार अवतंसकाम् |यन्त्र अगार स्तनीम् ऋद्धाम् प्रमदाम् इव भूषिताम् 
|| ५-३-१८ताम् नष्ट तिमिराम् दीपैः भास्वरैः च महा गृहैः |नगरीम् राक्षस इन्द्रस्य ददर्श स महा कपिः || ५-३-१९_END
BEGIN_That great monkey saw that city of king of rakshasas like a wealthy woman decorated with diamonds 
for her clothes, with various storage houses as earrings, with amouries for her breasts. Due to the lamps that 
illuminated the radiant great houses, all darkness was lost._END

B_5_C_4_0
BEGIN_
स निर्जत्य पुरीम् लण्का श्रेष्ठाम् ताम् कामरूपिणीम् |
विक्रमेण महातेजा हनुमान् कपिसत्तमः || ५-४-१
अद्वारेण मःआतेजा हौमान् कपिसत्तमः |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the best among Vanaras, the great radiant one, the long armed one,
conquered with His might the best Lanka who is capable of assuming desired form. He then leapt over
the city wall at a place that was not a gate._END

B_5_C_1_28
BEGIN_
आनुपूर्व्येण वृत्तं च लाङ्गूलं लोमभिश्चितम् |
उत्पतिष्यन् विचिक्षेप पक्षिराज इवोरगम् ||५-१-३३_END
BEGIN_
About to fly, Hanuma jolted his tail, which was rolled into a circle from top to
bottom, and which was covered with hair, just as Garuda, the king of birds would jolt a snake._END

B_5_C_2_18
BEGIN_
यावज्जानामि वैदेहीं यदि जीवति वा न वा |तत्रैव चिन्तयिष्यामि दृष्ट्वा तां जनकात्मजाम् || ५-२-३१_END
BEGIN_
"I will first find out if Seetha is alive or not. I will think all this later, after seeing that daughter of Janaka"._END

B_5_C_3_10
BEGIN_अथ सा हरिशार्दूलम् प्रविशन्तिम् महाबलम् |नगरी स्वेन रूपेण ददर्श पवनात्मजम् || ५-३-२०_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, the guardian of that city, in her own form, saw Hanuma, the best among monkeys and 
the mighty one, entering._END

B_5_C_4_1
BEGIN_
प्रविश्य नगरीम् लङ्काम् कपिराजहितम्करः || ५-४-२
चक्रेणाऽथ पदम् सव्यम् शत्रूणाम् स तु मूर्धनि |_END
BEGIN_
Desiring the benefit of the king of Vanaras Sugreeva, that Hanuma entered the city
of Lanka and thus actually placed His left foot on the enemies' heads._END

B_5_C_1_29
BEGIN_
तस्य लाङ्गूलमाविद्धमात्तवेगस्य पृष्ठतः |
ददृशे गरुडेनेव ह्रियमाणो महोरगः || ५-१-३४_END
BEGIN_
Receiving his vigor, the tail curled at his back was seen like a great serpent being
stolen by Garuda._END

B_5_C_2_19
BEGIN_
ततः स चिन्तयामास मुहूर्तं कपिकुञ्जरः |गिरिशृङ्गे स्थितस्तस्मिन् रामस्याभ्युदये रतः || ५-२-३२_END
BEGIN_
After that, that elephant among monkeys Hanuma who was interested in the welfare of Sri Rama, stood on that mountain 
peak and thought for an instant._END

B_5_C_3_11
BEGIN_सा तम् हरिवरम् दृष्ट्वा लङ्का रावणपालिता |स्वयमेवोत्थिता तत्र विकृताननदर्शना || ५-३-२१_END
BEGIN_Seeing that best among monkeys Hanuma there, that Lanka ruled by Ravana, rose up herself with a 
horrific appearance of face an eyes._END

B_5_C_4_2
BEGIN_
प्रविष्टः सत्त्वसंपन्नो विशायाम् मारुतात्मजः || ५-४-३
स महापथमास्थाय मुक्तापुष्पविराजितम् |
ततस्तु ताम् पुरीम् लङ्काम् रम्यामभिययौ कपिः || ५-४-४_END
BEGIN_
That son of Vayu endowed with great strength, entered the city at night and took the
grand road shone by flowers and pearls. After that Hanuma went towards that beautiful city of
Lanka._END

B_5_C_1_30
BEGIN_
बाहू संस्तंभयामास महापरिघसंनिभौ |
ससाद च कपिः क्ट्यां चरणौ संचुकोच च ||५-१-३५_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma firmly supported his arms (on the mountain surface) which resembled huge iron
clubs, crouched the waist and contracted his feet._END

B_5_C_2_20
BEGIN_
अनेन रूपेण मया न शक्या रक्षसां पुरी |प्रवेष्टुं राक्षसैर्गुप्ता क्रूरैर्बलसमन्वितैः || ५-२-३३_END
BEGIN_
"It is not possible for me to enter the city of ogres protected by cruel and strong rakshasas, with this appearance"._END

B_5_C_3_12
BEGIN_पुरस्तत्क पिवर्यस्य वायुसूनोरतिष्ठत |मुञ्चमाना महानादमब्रवीत्पवनात्मजम् || ५-३-२२_END
BEGIN_She stood in front of the best among Vanaras Hanuma. She made a great sound and spoke to Hanuma 
thus._END

B_5_C_4_3
BEGIN_
हसित उद्घुष्ट निनदैः तूर्य घोष पुरः सरैः |
वज्र अन्कुश निकाशैः च वज्र जाल विभूषितैः || ५-४-५
गृह मेधैः पुरी रम्या बभासे द्यौः इव अम्बुदैः |_END
BEGIN_
The beautiful city shone like the sky together with clouds, with its cloud like
houses filled with sounds of laughter and with sounds of musical instruments at the interior, equal
in strength to diamonds and clubs and with windows decorated with diamonds._END

B_5_C_1_31
BEGIN_
संहृत्य च भुजौ श्रीमांस्तथैव च शिरोधराम् |
तेजः स्त्त्वं तथा वीर्यमाविवेश स वीर्यवान् ||५-१-३६_END
BEGIN_
Bending shoulders and neck, that mighty and glorious Hanuma, increased his energy,
strength and courage._END

B_5_C_2_21
BEGIN_
उग्रौजसो महावीर्या बलवन्तश्च राक्षसाः |वञ्चनीया मया सर्वे जानकीं परिमार्गता || ५-२-३४_END
BEGIN_
"All these mighty ogres with extraordinary energy and great prowess are to be cheated by me while engaged in the 
search of Seetha"._END

B_5_C_3_13
BEGIN_कस्त्वम् केन च कार्येण इह प्राप्तो वनालय |कथय स्वेह यत्तत्त्वम् यावत्प्राणा धरन्ति ते 
|| ५-३-२३_END
BEGIN_"O one who lives in gardens! Who are you? For what reason did you come here? As long as your lives 
are sustained, tell me the truth here before that."_END

B_5_C_4_4
BEGIN_
प्रजज्वाल तदा लन्का रक्षः गण गृहैः शुभैः || ५-४-६
सित अभ्र सदृशैः चित्रैः पद्म स्वस्तिक संस्थितैः |
वर्धमान गृहैः च अपि सर्वतः सुविभाषितैः || ५-४-७_END
BEGIN_
Then that city of Lanka shone brilliantly being well decorated by the houses of
Rakshasas. These were modern houses which equalled white clouds, which were surprising with the
shape of lotus and swastika and which were auspicious._END

B_5_C_1_32
BEGIN_
मार्गमालोकयन्दूरादूर्ध्वं प्रणिहितेक्षणः |
रुरोध हृदये प्राणानाकाशमवलोकयन् || ५-१-३७_END
BEGIN_
With his eyes raised up, seeing the way from a distance, viewing the sky, he held
his breath in his heart._END

B_5_C_2_22
BEGIN_
लक्ष्यालक्ष्येण रूपेण रात्रौ लङ्का पुरी मया |प्रवेष्टुं प्राप्तकालं मे कृत्यं साधयितुं महत् || ५-२-३५_END
BEGIN_
"To achieve this great deed successfully, entering the city of Lanka in a small form at night is a timely thing 
to do" ._END

B_5_C_3_14
BEGIN_न शक्यम् खल्वियम् लङ्का प्रवेष्टुम् वानर त्वया |रक्षिता रावणबलैरभिगुप्ता समन्ततः || ५-३-२४_END
BEGIN_"O Vanara! It is indeed not possible for you to enter this city of Lanka which is protected by 
Ravana's forces and strongly guarded all around."_END

B_5_C_5_0
BEGIN_
ततः स मध्यंगतमंशुमन्तं |
ज्योत्स्नावितानम् महदुद्वमन्तम् |
ददर्श धीमान् दिवि भानुमन्तम् |
गोष्ठे वृषं मत्तमिव भ्रामन्तम् ||५-५-१_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter that intellectual Hanuma saw the moon in the sky shining with rays,
obtaining the middle portion of sky. Spreading a great quantity of moon shine, moon looked like a
bull in heat among cows._END

B_5_C_4_5
BEGIN_
ताम् चित्र माल्य आभरणाम् कपि राज हितम् करः |
राघव अर्थम् चरन् श्रीमान् ददर्श च ननन्द च || ५-४-८_END
BEGIN_
That glorious Hanuma, performer of beneficial deeds for Sugreeva the king of
monkeys, moved around the city of Lanka which had wonderful garlands and jewellery, for the sake of
Sri Rama. He saw the city and became happy too._END

B_5_C_2_23
BEGIN_
तां पुरीं तादृशीं दृष्ट्वा दुराधर्शां सुरासुरैः |हनुमान् चिन्तयामास विनिश्चित्य मुहुर्मुहुः || ५-२-३६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw such that city of Lanka, which was difficult to overcome even for Devas or asuras, and thought thus 
repeatedly._END

B_5_C_1_33
BEGIN_
पद्भ्यां दृढमवस्थानं कृत्वा स कपिकुञ्जरः |
निकुञ्च्य कर्णौ हनुमानुत्पतिष्यन् महाबलः |
वानरान् वानरश्रेष्ठ इदं वचनमब्रवीत् || ५-१-३८_END
BEGIN_
That mighty Hanuma, equal to an elephant among monkeys and the best among Vaanaraas,
stood firmly with his legs, bent his ears and before flying spoke these words to the Vaanaraas._END

B_5_C_3_15
BEGIN_अथ तामब्रवीद्वीरो हनुमानग्रतः स्थिताम् |कथयिष्यामि ते तत्त्वम् यन्मम् त्वम् परिपृच्छसि 
|| ५-३-२५_END
BEGIN_Therafter the mighty Hanuma spoke to Lanka standing in front of Him as follows : "Whatever matter 
you are asking me, I will tell you that truthfully."_END

B_5_C_5_1
BEGIN_
लोकस्य पापानि विनाशयन्तम् |
महोदधिं चापि समेधयन्तम् |
भूतानि सर्वाणि विराजयन्तम् |
ददर्श शीतांशुमथाभियान्तम् || ५-५-२_END
BEGIN_
After that Hanuma saw the moon coming up destroying the sins of the world, causing
the great ocean to grow and causing all living beings to shine._END

B_5_C_4_6
BEGIN_
भवनाद्भवनं गच्छ्न् ददर्श पवनात्मजः |
विविधाकृतिरूपाणि भवनानि ततस्ततः || ५-४-९_END
BEGIN_
Going from one building to another, Hanuma saw buildings in various shapes and forms
on every side._END

B_5_C_2_24
BEGIN_
केनोपायेन पशेयं मैथिलीं जनकात्मजाम् |अदृष्टो राक्षसेन्द्रेण रावणेन दुरात्मना || ५-२-३७_END
BEGIN_
"By what idea can I see Seetha the daughter of Janaka, unseen by the wicked Ravana, the king of the ogres._END

B_5_C_1_34
BEGIN_
यथा राघवनिर्मुक्तः शरः श्वसनविक्रमः |
गच्चेत्तद्वद्गमिष्यामि लङ्कां रावणपालिताम् || ५-१-३९
न हि द्रक्ष्यामि यदि तां लङ्कायां जनकात्मजाम् |
अनेनैव हि वेगेन गमिष्यामि सुरालयम् || ५-१-४०
यदि वा त्रिदिवे सीतां न द्रक्ष्याम्यकृतश्रमः |
बद्ध्वा राक्षसराजानमानयिष्यामि रावणम् || ५-१-४१
सर्वथा कृतकार्योऽहमेष्यामि सह सीतया |
आनयिष्यामि वा लङ्कां समुत्पाट्य सरावणाम् || ५-१-४२_END
BEGIN_
"I will go to the city of Lanka, ruled by Ravana just like an arrow released by Rama
will go, with wind-like speed. If I do not see the daughter of Janaka there, I will go with the
same speed to the abode of gods. If I do not see Seetha there in heaven, I will get Ravana the king
of raakshasaas tied up in chains without any effort. I will, in all events, return successfully
along with Seetha or I will get Lanka along with Ravana after uprooting it."_END

B_5_C_3_16
BEGIN_का त्वम् विरूपनयना पुरद्वारेऽवतिष्ठसि |किमर्थम् चापि माम् रुद्ध्वा निर्भर्त्सयसि दारुणा 
|| ५-३-२६_END
BEGIN_"You are standing at the entrance to the city. O one with ugly eyes! Who are you? O horrible one! 
Stopping me, for what reason are you threatening me?"_END

B_5_C_5_2
BEGIN_
या भाति लक्ष्मीर्भुवि मन्दरस्था |
तथा प्रदोषेषु च सागरस्था |
तथैव तोयेषु च पुष्करस्था |
रराज सा चारुनिशाकरस्था || ५-५-३_END
BEGIN_
What ever splendour shines over Mount Mandara on earth, on the ocean during
evenings, over the lotuses in the waters, the same splendour shone on the beautiful moon._END

B_5_C_4_7
BEGIN_
शुश्राव मधुरम् गीतम् त्रि स्थान स्वर भूषितम् |
स्त्रीणाम् मद समृद्धानाम् दिवि च अप्सरसाम् इव || ५-४-१०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma heard a sweet song which was decorated by sound from the three svaras -
Mandra, Madhya and Tara of love lorne women like Apsara women in heaven._END

B_5_C_2_25
BEGIN_
न विनश्येत्कथं कार्यं रामस्य विदितात्मनः |एकामेकश्च पश्येयं रहिते जनकात्मजाम् || ५-२-३८_END
BEGIN_
"How can the task of Sri Rama, one who knows self, not be destroyed? How can I alone see Seetha alone in a place 
devoid of people?."_END

B_5_C_1_35
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा तु हनुमान्वानरान्वानरोत्तमः || ५-१-४३
उत्पपाताथ वेगेन वेगवानविचारयन् |
सुपर्णमिव चात्मानं मेने स कपिकुञ्जरः || ५-१-४४_END
BEGIN_
The best among Vaanaraas, Hanuma, spoke in this way to Vaanaraas and then without
thinking about anything else, flew up with lot of vigor. That great monkey also thought himself
equal to Garuda, the king of birds._END

B_5_C_3_17
BEGIN_हनुमद्वचनम् श्रुत्वा लङ्का सा कामरूपिणी |उवाच वचनम् क्रुद्धा परुषं पवनात्मजम् || ५-३-२७_END
BEGIN_Listening to Hanuma's words, that Lanka, with ability to achieve desired form, became angry and 
spoke these strong words to Hanuma._END

B_5_C_5_3
BEGIN_
हंसो यथा राजतपञ्जरसथः |
सिम्हो यथा मन्दरकन्दरस्थः |
वीरो यथा गर्वितकुञ्जरस्थ |
श्चन्द्रो विबभ्राज तथामभरस्थः || ५-५-४_END
BEGIN_
Like a swan in a silver cage, like a lion in the cave of Mount Mandara, like a
warrior on a proud elephant, in the same way the moon shone in the sky._END

B_5_C_4_8
BEGIN_
शुश्राव कान्ची निनदम् नूपुराणाम् च निह्स्वनम् |
सोपान निनदामः चैव भवनेषु महात्मनम् || ५-४-११_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma also heard there and there sound from the tinkling of ornaments worn around
the waist in the houses of wealthy people, sounds of footfall over stair, sound from clapping of
arms by warriors and roar of ogres._END

B_5_C_2_26
BEGIN_
भूताश्चार्था विपद्यन्ते देशकालविरोधिताः |विक्लबं दूतमासाद्य तमः सूर्योदये यथा || ५-२-३९_END
BEGIN_
"With a mediator who has an unsteady and gloomy mind working against time and place, tasks that are otherwise 
ready to succeed get harmed, like the darkness that gets destroyed at dawn"._END

B_5_C_1_36
BEGIN_
समुत्पतति तस्मिंस्तु वेगात्ते नगरोहिणः |
संहृत्य विटपान् सर्वान् समुत्पेतुः समन्ततः || ५-१-४५_END
BEGIN_
While he was flying up, due to that force, all trees on that mountain flew away in
all directions, drawing together all their branches._END

B_5_C_3_18
BEGIN_अहम् राक्षसराजस्य रावणस्य महात्मनः |आज्ञाप्रतीक्षा दुर्धर्षा रक्षामि नगरीमिमाम् || ५-३-२८_END
BEGIN_"I protect this city, being invincible. I wait for the orders of the king of demons Ravana, the 
great one."_END

B_5_C_5_4
BEGIN_
स्थितह् ककुद्मानिव तीक्ष्णशृङ्गो |
महाचलः श्वेत इवोच्चशृङ्गः |
हस्तीव जाम्बूनदबद्धश्^इङ्गो |
रराज चन्द्रह् परिपूर्णशृङ्गः || ५-५-५_END
BEGIN_
The full moon with its horn like spot shone like a sharp horned standing ox with a
high hump, like a great white mountain with tall summits, like an elephant with golden tusks._END

B_5_C_4_9
BEGIN_
आस्फोटित निनादामः च क्ष्वेडितामः च ततः ततः |
शुश्राव जपताम् तत्र मन्त्रन् रक्षोगृहेषु वै || ५-४-१२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma also heard there and there sound from the tinkling of ornaments worn around
the waist in the houses of wealthy people, sounds of footfall over stair, sound from clapping of
arms by warriors and roar of ogres._END

B_5_C_2_27
BEGIN_
अर्थानर्थान्तरे बुद्धिर्निश्चितापि न शोभते |घातयन्ति हि कार्याणि दूताः पण्डितमानिनः || ५-२-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Even a decided mind will not shine when thinking about gain and loss. Mediators who are respected by scholarly 
people will also harm tasks due to their arrogance."_END

B_5_C_1_37
BEGIN_
स मत्तकोयष्टिभकान् पादपान् पुष्पशालिनः |
उद्वहन्नूरुवेगेन जगाम विमलेऽम्बरे || ५-१-४६_END
BEGIN_
While flying in the sky, he took along with him, because of the force of his thighs,
trees shining with flowers and with fattened lapwing birds._END

B_5_C_3_19
BEGIN_न शक्या मामवज्ञाय प्रवेष्टुम् नगरी त्वया |अद्य प्राणैः परित्यक्तः स्वप्स्यसे निहतो मया 
|| ५-३-२९_END
BEGIN_"After humilliating me it is not possible for you to enter the city. Being beaten by me, you will 
leave life and have a permanent sleep."_END

B_5_C_5_5
BEGIN_
विनष्टशीताम्बुतुषारपङ्को |
महाग्रहग्राहविनष्टपङ्कः |
प्रकाशलक्ष्म्याश्रयनिर्मलाङ्को |
रराज चन्द्रो भगवान् शशाङ्कः || ५-५-६_END
BEGIN_
The Divine moon who lost the stain of cold water and frost, with lost stain due to
eclipse by the great planet sun, one who has a calm spot which is an abode of brilliant splendour,
with a symbol of hare, shone brilliantly._END

B_5_C_4_10
BEGIN_
स्वाध्याय निरतामः चैव यातु धानान् ददर्श सः |
रावण स्तव सम्युक्तान् गर्जतः राक्षसान् अपि || ५-४-१३_END
BEGIN_
There Hanuma heard ritual chantings muttered by rakshasas in their houses. He saw
ogres engaged in study of Vedas. He also saw roaring rakshasas who came together to praise
Ravana._END

B_5_C_2_28
BEGIN_
न विनश्येत्कथं कार्यं वैक्लब्यम् न कथं भवेत् |लङ्घनं च समुद्रस्य कथं नु न वृथा भवेत् || ५-२-४१_END
BEGIN_
"How will the task at hand be not harmed? How will my mind not get gloominess? How will not the crossing of ocean 
go waste?."_END

B_5_C_1_38
BEGIN_
ऊरुवेगोत्थिता वृक्षा मुहूर्तं कपिमन्वयुः |
प्रस्थितं दीर्घमध्वानं स्वबन्धमिव बान्धवाः || ५-१-४७_END
BEGIN_
The trees thus being held aloft by the speed of Hanuma's thighs, followed him for a
while just as relatives would follow their loved ones embarking on a long journey._END

B_5_C_3_20
BEGIN_अहम् हि नगरी लङ्का स्वयमेव प्लवङ्गम |सर्वतः परिरक्षामि ह्येतत्ते कथितम् मया || ५-३-३०_END
BEGIN_"O Vanara! I am protecting this city of Lanka in all directions. This matter has been already told 
to you by me."_END

B_5_C_5_6
BEGIN_
शीलातलम् प्राप्य यथा मृगेन्द्रो |
महारणम् प्राप्य यथा गजेन्द्रह् |
राज्यम् समासाद्य यथा नरेन्द्र |
स्तथाप्रकाशो विरराज चन्द्रः || ५-५-७_END
BEGIN_
In whatever way a lion obtaining a level surfaced rock (shines), in whatever way
best elephant obtaining a great battle(shines), in whatever way a king obtaining kingdom(shines),
in the same way the clear moon shone._END

B_5_C_4_11
BEGIN_
राज मार्गम् समावृत्य स्थितम् रक्षः बलम् महत् |
ददर्श मध्यमे गुल्मे राक्षसस्य चरान् बहून् || ५-४-१४_END
BEGIN_
He saw many spies of Ravana and a big army of ogres which stood surrounding the
royal highway in the central zone of city._END

B_5_C_2_29
BEGIN_
मयि दृष्टे तु रक्षोभी रामस्य विदितात्मनः |भवेद्व्यर्थमिदं कार्यं रावणानर्थमिच्छतः || ५-२-४२_END
BEGIN_
"If I were to be seen by rakshasas, this task of Sri Rama, with a famed mind, who desires the slaying of Ravana 
will become wasteful."_END

B_5_C_1_39
BEGIN_
तमूरुवेगोन्मथिताःसालाश्चन्ये नगोत्तमाः|
अनुजग्मुर्हनूमन्तं सैन्या इव महीपतिम् || ५-१-४८_END
BEGIN_
Uprooted by the force of Hanuma's thighs, Sal and other excellent trees followed
Hanuma like soldiers following their king._END

B_5_C_3_21
BEGIN_लङ्काया वचनम् श्रुत्वा हनुमान् मारुतात्मजः |यत्नवान्स हरिश्रेष्ठः स्थितश्शैल इवापरः || 
५-३-३१_END
BEGIN_The son of Vayu and best among Vanaras heard Lanka's words and stood up like a second mountain, 
with a purpose._END

B_5_C_5_7
BEGIN_
प्रकाशचन्द्रोदयनष्टदोषः |
प्रवृत्तरक्षः पिशिताशदोषः |
रामाभिरामेरितचित्तदोषः |
स्वर्गप्रकाशो भगवान् प्रदोषः || ५-५-८_END
BEGIN_
The Divine evening with lost stain due to rise of shining moon, with the stain due
to meal of flesh eating rakshasas, and in which the bitterness of mind of young women and their
lovers is wiped away, became with a heavenly glow._END

B_5_C_4_12
BEGIN_
दीक्षितान् जटिलान् मुण्डान् गः अजिन अम्बर वाससः |
दर्भ मुष्टि प्रहरणान् अग्नि कुण्ड आयुधामः तथा || ५-४-१५
कूट मुद्गर पाणीमः च दण्ड आयुध धरान् अपि |
एक अक्ष अनेक कर्णामः च चलल् लम्ब पयः धरान् || ५-४-१६
करालान् भुग्न वक्त्रामः च विकटान् वामनामः तथा |
धन्विनः खड्गिनः चैव शतघ्नी मुसल आयुधान् || ५-४-१७
परिघ उत्तम हस्तामः च विचित्र कवच उज्ज्वलान् |
नातिस्थूलान् नातिकृशान् नातिदीर्घ अतिह्रस्वकान् || ५-४-१८
नातिगौरान्नातिकृष्णान्नातिकुब्जान्न वामनान् |
विरूपान् बहु रूपामः च सुरूपामः च सुवर्चसः || ५-४-१९_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw those who were initiated into various Vedic practices, those who wore
matted locks on their head, those who had shaven heads, those who wore cow hides and other
clothing, those who were carrying Kusa grass as weapons and also those who had fire vessels as
weapons, those who carried hammers and clubs in their hands and also those who had worn staffs as
weapons, hose who were one-eyed, those who had one ear, hose who were pot-bellied and with hanging
breast, those who had horrible appearances, those with twisted mouths, those who were horrific and
also short people, those who carried bows and arrows those who carried swords, those who carried
pestles and clubs as weapons, those who carried excellent Parighas in their hands, those who shone
with strange armour, those who were not very fat, those who were not too thin, those who were
neither tall nor short, those who were not very fair, those who were not very dark, those who were
not very hunchbacked, those who were not very short, those who had great brilliance, those who
carried banners, those who carried flags and those who carried different weapons._END

B_5_C_2_30
BEGIN_
न हि शक्यं क्वचित् स्थातुमविज्ञातेन राक्षसैः |अपि राक्षसरूपेण किमुतान्येन केनचित् || ५-२-४३_END
BEGIN_
"It is not possible to be in Lanka even in the form of a rakshasa. What to say about being there in any other 
form?"_END

B_5_C_1_40
BEGIN_
सुपुष्पिताग्रैर्बहुभिः पादपैरन्वितः कपिः |
हनुमान् पर्वताकारो बभूवाद्भुतदर्शनः || ५-१-४९_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma the great monkey presented a wonderful sight, with his mountain-like
appearance together with the well flowered trees._END

B_5_C_6_0
BEGIN_
स निकामम् विमानेषु विषण्णः काम रूपधृत् |
विचचार पुनर्लङ्काम् लाघवेन समन्वितः || ५-६-१_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma who could assume any desire form, searching among houses had a lot of
grief. Endowed with great speed, He roamed again the city of Lanka._END

B_5_C_3_22
BEGIN_स ताम् स्त्रीरूपविकृताम् दृष्ट्वा वानरपुङ्गवः |आबभाषेऽथ मेधावि सत्त्वान् प्लवगर्षभः || 
५-३-३२_END
BEGIN_Thereafter that Hanuma the wise one, with great strength, best among those who can fly and best 
among Vanaras, saw that city of Lanka in the form of an ugly woman and spoke thus._END

B_5_C_5_8
BEGIN_
तन्त्रीस्वनाह् कर्णसुखाः प्रवृत्ताः |
स्वपन्ति नार्यः पतिभिः सुवृत्ताः |
नक्तंचराश्चापि तथा प्रवृत्ता |
विहर्तुमत्यद्भुतरौद्रवृत्ताः || ५-५-९_END
BEGIN_
Musical notes from stringed instruments which were comforting to ears started. Women
with good character were sleeping with husbands and also rakshasas with extremely strange character
started to roam._END

B_5_C_4_13
BEGIN_
ध्वजीन् पताकिनश्चैव ददर्श विविधायुधान् |
शक्ति वृक्ष आयुधामः चैव पट्टिश अशनि धारिणः || ५-४-२०
क्षेपणी पाश हस्तामः च ददर्श स महा कपिः |
स्रग्विणः त्व् अनुलिप्तामः च वर आभरण भूषितान् || ५-४-२१
नानावेषसमायुक्तान्यथास्वैरगतान् बहून् |
तीक्ष्ण शूल धरामः चैव वज्रिणः च महा बलान् | | ५-४-२२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw many people, who had great might, who carried javelins and trees as
weapons, those who carried Pattisas and thunderbolts, those who carried in their hands sling and
nooses, those who carried flowered garlands, wearing sandal paste and decorated with best
jewellery, those who had various kinds of appearances roaming freely at will, those who carried
sharp spikes and thunderbolts._END

B_5_C_2_31
BEGIN_
वायुरप्यत्र नाज्ञातश्चरेदिति मतिर्मम |न ह्यस्त्यविदितं किंचिद्राक्षसानां बलीयसाम् || ५-२-४४_END
BEGIN_
"My thought goes thus: Even wind cannot pass here without being known. There is nothing not known to the might 
rakshasas."_END

B_5_C_1_41
BEGIN_
सारवन्तोऽथ ये वृक्षा न्यमज्जन् लवणाम्भसि |
भयादिव महेन्द्रस्य पर्वता वरुणालये || ५-१-५०_END
BEGIN_
After that, powerful trees sank into the salt ocean like mountains sinking into
ocean due to fear of Mahendra._END

B_5_C_6_1
BEGIN_
आससाद अथ लक्ष्मीवान् राक्षस इन्द्र निवेशनम् |
प्राकारेण अर्क वर्णेन भास्वरेण अभिसम्व्ऱ्तम् || ५-६-२_END
BEGIN_
After that, the glorious Hanuma neared the house of Ravana shining with the golden
hue of Sun, surrounded by a compound wall._END

B_5_C_3_23
BEGIN_द्रक्ष्यामि नगरीम् लङ्काम् साट्टप्राकारतोरणाम् |इत्यर्थमिह सम्प्राप्तः परम् कौतूहलम् हि 
मे || ५-३-३३_END
BEGIN_"I should like to see the city of Lanka with its palaces, defensive walls and archways. I came 
here for that reason. I am very curious to see them."_END

B_5_C_5_9
BEGIN_
मत्तप्रमत्तानि समाकुलानि |
तथाश्वभद्रासनसम्कुलानि |
वीरः श्रिया चापि समाकुलानि |
ददर्श धीमान् स कपिः कुलानि || ५-५-१०_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the courageous one, the intellectual one, saw houses with people in
heat, houses filled with people, full chariots, horses, elephants and best furniture and also full
of wealth._END

B_5_C_4_14
BEGIN_
शत साहस्रम् अव्यग्रम् आरक्षम् मध्यमम् कपिः |
रक्षोधिपतिनिर्दिष्टम् ददर्शान्तःपुराग्रतः || | ५-४-२३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw at the front of inner city, a hundred thousand central protective force
which was attentive and was positioned there at the command of Ravana._END

B_5_C_2_32
BEGIN_
इहाहं यदि तिष्ठामि स्वेन रूपेण संवृतः |विनाशमुपयास्यामि भर्तुरर्थश्च हीयते || ५-२-४५_END
BEGIN_
"If I stay here with my usual form, I can be destroyed. The task of the Lord will also be harmed."_END

B_5_C_1_42
BEGIN_
स नानाकुसुमैः कीर्णः कपिः साङ्कुरकोरकैः |
शुशुभे मेघसंकाशः खद्योतैरिव पर्वतः || ५-१-५१_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma who was equal to a cloud, covered with flowers of various kinds, shoots
and buds, shone like a mountain with fireflies._END

B_5_C_6_2
BEGIN_
रक्षितम् राक्षसैर् भीमैः सिम्हैर् इव महद् वनम् |
समीक्षमाणो भवनम् चकाशे कपि कुन्जरः || ५-६-३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma shined purveying the building protected by horrible rakshasas, like a forest
by lions._END

B_5_C_3_24
BEGIN_वनान्युपवनानीह लङ्कायाः काननानि च |सर्वतो गृहमुख्यानि द्रष्टुमागमनम् हि मे || ५-३-३४_END
BEGIN_"My arrival here is indeed to see Lanka's gardens, parks, forests and important houses all over."_END

B_5_C_5_10
BEGIN_
परस्परं चाधिकमाक्षिपन्ति |
भुआंश्च पीनानधिनिक्षिपन्ति |
मत्तप्रलापानधिकम् क्षिपन्ति |
मत्तानि चान्योन्यमधिक्षिपन्ति || ५-५-११_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw rakshasas railing a lot at one another moving their heavy shoulders,
throwing wild and incoherent words a lot, insulting one another being intoxicated._END

B_5_C_4_15
BEGIN_
स तदा तद्गृहम् दृष्ट्वा महाहाटकतोरणम् |
राक्षसेन्द्रस्य विख्यातमद्रिमूर्ध्नि प्रतिष्ठितम् || ५-४-२४
पुण्डरीकावतंसाभिः परिखाभिरलम्कृतम् |
प्राकार आवृतम् अत्यन्तम् ददर्श स महा कपिः || ५-४-२५_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma saw Ravana's house with a golden doorway. That famed house was on the
top of a mountain. Motes filled with white lotuses surrounded it. It was also surrounded by a
compound wall. He watched the house again and again._END

B_5_C_2_33
BEGIN_
तदहं स्वेन रूपेण रजन्यां ह्रस्वतां गतः |लङ्कामभिपतिष्यामि राघवस्यार्थसिद्धये || ५-२-४६_END
BEGIN_
"For that reason, I will become small in my appearance and will enter Lanka at night for the success of the task 
of Sri Rama."_END

B_5_C_1_43
BEGIN_
विमुक्तास्तस्य वेगेन मुक्त्वा पुष्पाणि ते द्रुमाः |
अवशीर्यन्त सलिले निवृत्ताः सुहृदो यथा ||५-१-५२_END
BEGIN_
Those trees which were released by Hanuma's speed, dropped flowers and fell down in
the water like friends going back after bidding farewell to their dear one._END

B_5_C_6_3
BEGIN_
रूप्य कोप हितैः चित्रैः तोरणैर् हेम भूषितैः |
विचित्राभिः च कक्ष्याभिर् द्वारैः च रुचिरैर् व्ऱ्तम् || ५-६-४_END
BEGIN_
Ravana's house consisted of surprising archways decorated with sliver and gold,
strange entrances and beautiful doors._END

B_5_C_3_25
BEGIN_तस्य तद्वचनम् श्रुत्वा लङ्का सा कामरूपिणी |भूय एव पुनर्वाक्यम् बभाषे परुषाक्षरम् || ५-३-३५_END
BEGIN_Listening to Hanuma's words, Lanka with the ability to assume desired form, spoke harsh words stronger 
than before._END

B_5_C_5_11
BEGIN_
रक्षांसि वक्षांसि च विक्षिपन्ति |
गात्राणि कान्तासु च विक्षिपन्ति |
रूपाअणि चित्राणि च विक्षिपन्ति |
दृढानि चापानि च विक्षिपन्ति || ५-५-१२_END
BEGIN_
(Hanuma saw) rakshasas who smote breast, those who threw limbs on women, those who
were spreading their strange forms sporting their strong bows._END

B_5_C_4_16
BEGIN_
त्रिविष्टप निभम् दिव्यम् दिव्य नाद विनादितम् |
वाजि हेषित सम्घुष्टम् नादितम् भूषणैः तथा || ५-४-२६
रथैः यानैः विमानैः च तथा गज हयैः शुभैः |
वारणैः च चतुः दन्तैः श्वेत अभ्र निचय उपमैः || ५-४-२७
भूषितम् रुचिर द्वारम् मत्तैः च मृग पक्षिभिः |
राक्षस अधिपतेः गुप्तम् आविवेश गृहम् कपिः || ५-४-२८_END
BEGIN_
The great Hanuma entered secretly Ravana's inner city which was equal to paradise,
rendered noisy by neighing of horses and tinkling of ornaments, by chariots, vehicles and
aerial-cars and decorated by auspicious elephants and horses and great elephants with four tusks
and by birds and animals in heat. It had beautiful entrances and was protected by thousands of
rakshasas with great strength._END

B_5_C_2_34
BEGIN_
रावणस्य पुरीं रात्रौ प्रविश्य सुदुरासदाम् |विचिन्वन् भवनं स्र्वं द्रक्ष्यामि जनकात्मजाम् || ५-२-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Entering the unapproachable city of Lanka at night and searching all the mansion of Ravana, I can see Seetha."_END

B_5_C_6_4
BEGIN_
गज आस्थितैर् महा मात्रैः शूरैः च विगत श्रमैः |
उपस्थितम् असम्हार्यैर् हयैः स्यन्दन यायिभिः || ५-६-५_END
BEGIN_
Ravana's house waited upon by men on elephants, warriors, people with removed
tiredness, drivers of elephants, by undefeatable horses, and by charioteers._END

B_5_C_1_44
BEGIN_
लघुत्वेनोपपन्नं तद्विचित्रं सागरेऽपतत् |
द्रुमाणां विविधं पुष्पं कपिवायुसमीरितम् || ५-१-५३
ताराचितमिवाकाशं प्रबभौ च महार्णवः |_END
BEGIN_
Set in motion by the wind from the movement of Hanuma, that variety of blossom, with
various hues, from the trees fell down into the sea. That great ocean shone like the sky filled
with stars._END

B_5_C_3_26
BEGIN_मामनिर्जत्य दुर्बद्धे राक्षसेश्वरपालिता |न शक्यमद्य ते द्रष्टुम् पुरीयम् वनराधम || ५-३-३६_END
BEGIN_"O lowly Vanara with an evil mind! It is not possile for you to see this city ruled by king of 
rakshasas, without first defeating me."_END

B_5_C_5_12
BEGIN_
ददर्श कान्ताश्च समालभन्त्य |
स्तथा परास्तत्र पुनः स्वपन्त्यः |
सुरूपवक्त्राश्च तथा हसन्त्यः |
क्रुद्धाः पराश्चपि विनिःश्वसन्त्यः || ५-५-१३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw some women applying sandal paste on their bodies and also some other
women sleeping there, in the same way some women with good appearance were smiling, and some other
women were sighing in anger._END

B_5_C_4_17
BEGIN_
सहेमजाम्बूनदचक्रवाळम् |
महार्ह मुक्तामणिभूषितान्तम् |
परार्थ्यकालागुरुचन्दनाक्तं |
स रावणान्तःपुरमाविवेश || ५-४-२९_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma entered the inner city of Ravana which was filled with gold, which had a
golden court-yard , with a central area decorated by pearls and diamonds of great value and
sprinkled daily with water containing superb algallocum and sandal-wood._END

B_5_C_2_35
BEGIN_
इति संचिन्त्य हनुमान् सूर्यस्यास्तमयं कपिः |आचकांक्षे ततो वीरो वैदेह्या द्रशनोतुसकः || ५-२-४८_END
BEGIN_
The courageous Hanuma thus thinking and being interested in discovering Seetha, then desired the sun to set._END

B_5_C_6_5
BEGIN_
सिम्ह व्याघ्र तनु त्राणैर् दान्त कान्चन राजतैः |
घोषवद्भिर् विचित्रैः च सदा विचरितम् रथैः || ५-६-६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw Ravana's house with protective shields made of lion and tiger skins,
decorated with ivory, gold and silver, being roamed always by strange chariots with great
sound._END

B_5_C_1_45
BEGIN_
पुष्पौघेनानुबद्धेन नानावर्णेन वानरः |
बभौ मेघ इवाकाशे विद्युद्गणविभूषितः || ५-१-५४_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma shone like a cloud in the sky decorated by lightening, with flowers of
various hues sticking to his body._END

B_5_C_3_27
BEGIN_ततः स कपिशार्दूलस्तामुवाच निशाचरीम् |दृष्वा पुरीमिमाम् भद्रे पुनर्यास्ये यथागतम् || ५-३-३७_END
BEGIN_Then that tiger among Vanaras Hanuma spoke to that demon : "O auspicious one! After seeing this 
city I will return back again to where I came from."_END

B_5_C_5_13
BEGIN_
महागजैश्चापि तथा नदद्भिः |
सुपूजितैश्चापि तथा सुसद्भिः |
रराज वीरैश्च विनिःश्वसद्भि |
र्ह्रदो भुजङ्गैरिव निःश्वसद्भिः || ५-५-१४_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw (the city of Lanka that) shone with great elephants making sound and also
with gentlemen well respected, shone with warriors in a wresting bout, with long sighs, like
serpents in a lake hissing._END

B_5_C_2_36
BEGIN_
सूर्ये चास्तं गते रात्रौ देहं संक्षिप्य मारुतिः |वृषदंशकमात्रः सन् बभूवाद्भुतदर्शनः || ५-२-४९_END
BEGIN_
After the sun had set, Hanuma reduced His body at night with a size equal to that of a cat and became a wonderful 
sight to behold._END

B_5_C_6_6
BEGIN_
बहु रत्न समाकीर्णम् पर अर्ध्य आसन भाजनम् |
महा रथ समावासम् महा रथ महा आसनम् || ५-६-७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw Ravana's house filled with a lot of diamonds, having valuable seats and
utensils, abode of great warriors, with great chariots and great utensils._END

B_5_C_1_46
BEGIN_
तस्य वेगसमाधूतैः पुष्पैस्तोयमदृश्यत ||५-१-५५
ताराभिरभिरामाभिरुदिताभिरिवाम्बरम् |_END
BEGIN_
That sea water looked like the sky with delightful stars rising up, with flowers
flown up by Hanuma's speed._END

B_5_C_7_0
BEGIN_
स वेश्म जालम् बलवान् ददर्श |
व्यासक्त वैदूर्य सुवर्ण जालम् |
यथा महत् प्राव्ऱ्षि मेघ जालम् |
विद्युत् पिनद्धम् सविहम्ग जालम् || ५-७-१_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma, the strong one, saw a group of houses with windows in golden hue,
embedded with cat's-eye gems, like a great group of clouds in rainy season with lighting, together
with a group of birds._END

B_5_C_3_28
BEGIN_ततः कृत्वा महानादम् सा वै लङ्का भयावहम् |तलेन वानरश्रेष्ठम् ताडयामास वेगिता || ५-३-३८_END
BEGIN_Thereafter that Lanka made a great sound causing terror and hit Hanuma, the best among Vanaras, 
with her palm quickly._END

B_5_C_5_14
BEGIN_
बुद्धिप्रधानान् रुचिराभिधानान् |
संश्रद्दधानान् जगतः प्रधानान् |
नानाविधानान् रुचिराभिधानान् |
ददर्श तस्याम् पुरि यातुधानान् || ५-५-१५_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw Yatudhanaas who were intellectuals, who were good talkers, who had good
devotion, important people to the world, who had various ways, and people who had beautiful names
in that city._END

B_5_C_2_37
BEGIN_
प्रदोषकाले हनुमांस्तूर्णमुत्प्लुत्य वीर्यवान् |प्रविवेश पुरीं रम्यां सुविभक्तमहापथाम् || ५-२-५०_END
BEGIN_
The courageous Hanuma quickly flew during evening time and entered the beautiful city with well divided main pathways._END

B_5_C_6_7
BEGIN_
दृश्यैः च परम उदारैः तैः तैः च मृग पक्षिभिः |
विविधैर् बहु साहस्रैः परिपूर्णम् समन्ततः || ५-६-८_END
BEGIN_
Filled all around with those and those various kinds of animals and birds in
thousands, lovely to watch - very beautiful ones._END

B_5_C_1_47
BEGIN_
तस्याम्बरगतौ बाहू ददृशाते प्रसारितौ || ५-१-५६
पर्वताग्राद्विनिष्क्रान्तौ पञ्चास्याविव पन्नगौ |_END
BEGIN_
That sky-borne Hanuma's arms which were spread out, were seen like five-headed
serpents coming out of a mountain's peak._END

B_5_C_7_1
BEGIN_
निवेशनानाम् विविधाः च शालाः |
प्रधान शन्ख आयुध चाप शालाः |
मनो हराः च अपि पुनर् विशाला |
ददर्श वेश्म अद्रिषु चन्द्र शालाः || ५-७-२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw various halls of the houses, important buildings storing conches, bows,
and other weapons, and also heartening spacious attics at the top of mountain- like houses._END

B_5_C_3_29
BEGIN_ततः स कपिशार्दुलो लङ्काया ताडितो भृशम् |ननाद सुमहानादम् वीर्यवान् पवनात्मजः || ५-३-३९_END
BEGIN_Then that tiger among Vanaras, the powerful son of Vayu, being hit powerfully by Lanka made a great 
sound._END

B_5_C_5_15
BEGIN_
ननन्द दृष्ट्वा स च तान् सुरूपा |
न्नानागुणानात्मगुणानुरूपान् |
विद्योतमानान्स तदानुरूपान् |
ददर्श कांश्चिच्च पुनर्विरूपान् || ५-५-१६_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma seeing people with good appearance, who had various good virtues, those
who were according to their character, those who were radiant, all those - became happy. Then that
Hanuma saw those who had horrific appearance, those who were according to their appearance - some
of those too._END

B_5_C_2_38
BEGIN_
प्रासादमालाविततां स्तम्भैः काञ्चनराजतैः |शातकुम्भमयैर्जालैर्गन्धर्वनगरोपमाम् || ५-२-५१सप्तभौमाष्टभौमैश्च 
स ददर्श महापुरीम् |तलैः स्फतिकसंकीर्णैः कार्तस्वरविभूषितैः || ५-२-५२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw that great city filled with series of mansions, golden hued pillars and window lattices, which was 
equal to the city of Gandharvas, consisting of seven and eight storied buildings with their top portions studded 
with crystals and pearls and decorated with gold._END

B_5_C_6_8
BEGIN_
विनीतैर् अन्त पालैः च रक्षोभिः च सुरक्षितम् |
मुख्याभिः च वर स्त्रीभिः परिपूर्णम् समन्ततः || ५-६-९_END
BEGIN_
Well protected by well trained rakshasas, protecting the inner area, filled all over
by best women who were important._END

B_5_C_1_48
BEGIN_
पिबन्निव बभौ चापि सोओर्मिमालं महार्णवम् || ५-१-५७
पिपासुरिव चाकाशं ददृशे स महाकपिः |_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey shone like one who is drinking the great sea together with its
waves. He also seemed like one who desires to drink the whole of sky._END

B_5_C_7_2
BEGIN_
गृहाणि नाना वसु राजितानि |
देव असुरैः च अपि सुपूजितानि |
सर्वैः च दोषैः परिवर्जितानि |
कपिर् ददर्श स्व बल अर्जितानि || ५-७-३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw houses glittered by various riches, well worshipped by Devas and Asuras,
devoid of all flaws and obtained by the self-might of rakshasas._END

B_5_C_3_30
BEGIN_ततः सम्वर्तयामास वामहस्तस्य सोऽङ्गुळीः |मुष्टिनाभिजघूनैनाम् हनुमान् क्रोधमूर्चितः || ५-३-४०
स्त्री चेति मन्यमानेन नातिक्रोधः स्वयम् कृतः |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter that Hanuma became dizzy with anger and folded his fingers of left hand. He then hit 
her with His fist. "She is a woman" - thinking thus He did not show much anger by Himself._END

B_5_C_5_16
BEGIN_
ततो वरार्हः सुविशुद्धभावा |
स्तेषाम् स्त्रियस्तत्र महानुभावाह् |
प्रियेषु पानेषु च सक्तभावा |
ददर्श ताराइव सुप्रभावाः || ५-५-१७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw thereafter there, their women - those who were eligible for distinction,
those who were of great skill with an interested heart in lovers and in drinks and those who were
like stars with good effect._END

B_5_C_2_39
BEGIN_
वैडूर्यमणिचित्रैश्च मुक्ताजालविभूषितैः |तलैः शुशुभिरे तानि भवनान्यत्र रक्षसाम् || ५-२-५३_END
BEGIN_
There in that city of Lanka, the houses of rakshasas shone with top portions painted by cats-eyes and emeralds 
and decorated by groups of pearls._END

B_5_C_6_9
BEGIN_
मुदित प्रमदा रत्नम् राक्षस इन्द्र निवेशनम् |
वर आभरण निर्ह्रादैः समुद्र स्वन निह्स्वनम् || ५-६-१०_END
BEGIN_
Having happy women, the abode of Ravana with the tinkling of best jewellery had a
sound like that of an ocean._END

B_5_C_1_49
BEGIN_
तस्य विद्युत्प्रभाकारे वायुमार्गानुसारिणः ||५-१-५८
नयने विप्रकाशेते पर्वतस्थाविवानलौ |_END
BEGIN_
The eyes of that Hanuma, who was following the path of sky, which had a brilliance
equal to that of lightening, were shining like two fires on a mountain._END

B_5_C_7_3
BEGIN_
तानि प्रयत्न अभिसमाहितानि |
मयेन साक्षाद् इव निर्मितानि |
मही तले सर्व गुण उत्तराणि |
ददर्श लन्का अधिपतेर् ग्ऱ्हाणि || ५-७-४_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw those houses of the ruler of Lanka, constructed by great effort as though
constructed by Mayaa himself on earth with all best qualities._END

B_5_C_3_31
BEGIN_सा तु तेन प्रहारेण विह्वलाङ्गी नीशाचरी || ५-३-४१पपात सहसा भूमौ विकृताननदर्शना |_END
BEGIN_That demon fell on land immediately by that hit with a distressed body and appeared with a horrific 
face._END

B_5_C_5_17
BEGIN_
श्रिया ज्वलन्तीस्त्रपयोगूढा |
निशीथकाले रमणोपगूढाः |
ददर्श काश्चित्प्रमदोपगूढा |
यथा विहङ्गाः कुसुमोपगूढाः || ५-५-१८_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw some women who were brilliant with radiance, adorned a lot with
bashfulness, those who were hugged by lovers in the middle of night, those who were hugged with
great pleasure, those who were hugged by flowers like birds._END

B_5_C_2_40
BEGIN_
काञ्चनानि च चित्राणि तोरणानि च रक्षसाम् |लङ्कामुद्द्योतयामासुः सर्वतः समलंकृताम् || ५-२-५४_END
BEGIN_
Golden archways with strange hues illuminated the well decorated city of Lanka in all directions._END

B_5_C_6_10
BEGIN_
तद् राज गुण सम्पन्नम् मुख्यैः च वर चन्दनैः |
भेरी म्ऱ्दन्ग अभिरुतम् शन्ख घोष विनादितम् || ५-६-११_END
BEGIN_
Together with royal insignia, with best scents and sandal wood, spread with great
number of people like a great forest with lions._END

B_5_C_1_50
BEGIN_
पिङ्गे पिङ्गाक्षमुख्यस्य बृहती परिमण्डले || ५-१-५९
चक्षुषी संप्रकाशेते चन्द्रसूर्याविवोदितौ |_END
BEGIN_
The round, wide, reddish brown eyes of Hanuma, the best among the monkeys shone like
fully risen sun and moon._END

B_5_C_7_4
BEGIN_
ततो ददर्श उच्च्रित मेघ रूपम् |
मनो हरम् कान्चन चारु रूपम् |
रक्षो अधिपस्य आत्म बल अनुरूपम् |
गृह उत्तमम् हि अप्रतिरूप रूपम् || ५-७-५_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter Hanuma saw the best house of the lord of rakshasas, having the appearance
of a cloud, soul-captivating one having a beautiful form made of gold which has no comparison,
suitable of Ravana's might_END

B_5_C_3_32
BEGIN_ततस्तु हनुमान् प्राज्ञस्ताम् दृष्ट्वा विनिपातिताम् || ५-३-४२कृपाम् चकार तेजस्वी मन्यमानः 
स्त्रियम् तु ताम् |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the intellectual and glorious Hanuma saw her fallen down and thinking her to be woman, 
showed kindness._END

B_5_C_8_0
BEGIN_
स तस्य मध्ये भवनस्य संस्थितम् |
महद्विमानम् मणिवज्रचित्रितम् |
प्रतप्तजाम्बूनदजालकृत्रिमम् |
ददर्श वीरः पवनात्मजः कपिः || ५-८-१_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the courageous one, the son of Lord Vayu, saw the great aerial plane
standing in the middle of that building with a surprising hue, due to diamonds, and gems decorated
by series of refined gold._END

B_5_C_5_18
BEGIN_
अन्याः पुनर्हर्म्यतलोपविष्टा |
स्तत्र प्रियाङ्केषु सुखोपविष्टाः |
भर्तुः प्रिया धर्मपरा निविष्टा |
ददर्श धीमान् मदनाभिविष्टाः || ५-५-१९_END
BEGIN_
The intellectual Hanuma saw some other women there comfortably sitting on the laps
of their lovers, at the top of their buildings, dear to their husbands and (some other women)
interested in virtuous deeds, and some possessed by the lord of love._END

B_5_C_2_41
BEGIN_
अचिन्त्यामद्भुताकारां दृष्ट्वा लङ्कां महाकपिः |आसीद्विष्ण्डो हृष्टश्च वैदेह्या दर्शनोत्सुकः || ५-२-५५_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma on seeing the unimaginable city of Lanka with a wonderful appearance became sad thinking about the prospect 
of capturing Lanka and also happy being eager to see Seetha._END

B_5_C_6_11
BEGIN_
भेरीमृदङ्गाभिरुतम् शङ्खघोषनिनादितम् |
नित्य अर्चितम् पर्व हुतम् पूजितम् राक्षसैः सदा || ५-६-१२_END
BEGIN_
Resounded by bheris and mridagas, resounded by the sound of conch-shells, prayed
upon daily by Rakshsas, with rituals on festivals, always worshipped by rakshasas._END

B_5_C_1_51
BEGIN_
मुखं नासिकया तस्य ताम्रया ताम्रमाबभौ || ५-१-६०
सन्ध्यया समभिस्पृष्टं यथा तत्सूर्यमण्डलम् |_END
BEGIN_
The ruddy face of Hanuma, with His reddish face shone like the Sun touched by
twilight._END

B_5_C_7_5
BEGIN_
मही तले स्वर्गम् इव प्रकीर्णम् |
श्रिया ज्वलन्तम् बहु रत्न कीर्णम् |
नाना तरूणाम् कुसुम अवकीर्णम् |
गिरेर् इव अग्रम् रजसा अवकीर्णम् || ५-७-६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw Ravana's house like heaven thrown upon earth, effulgent with glory,
embedded with variety of diamonds covered by flowers of various trees, like the summit of a
mountain covered by pollen._END

B_5_C_3_33
BEGIN_ततो वै भृशसम्विग्ना लङ्का गद्गदाक्षरम् || ५-३-४३उवाचागर्वितम् वाक्यम् हनूमन्तम् प्लवङ्गमम् 
|_END
BEGIN_Thereafter that Lanka being very gloomy spoke with a falterting tone without pride these words 
to Hanuma the Vanara._END

B_5_C_8_1
BEGIN_
तदप्रमेयाप्रतिकारकृत्रिमम् |
कृतम् स्वयम् साध्विति विश्वकर्मणाः |
दिवम् गतम् वायुपथप्रतिष्ठितम् |
व्यराजतादित्यपथस्य लक्ष्मिवत् || ५-८-२_END
BEGIN_
That plane shone like symbol for solar path standing in the aerial path obtaining
the sky. Manufactured by Vishvakarma himself and praised by him as one without comparison in
beauty._END

B_5_C_5_19
BEGIN_
अप्रावृताः काञ्चनराजिवर्णाः |
काश्चित्परार्थ्यास्तपनीयवर्णाः |
पुनश्च काश्चिच्छशलक्ष्मवर्णाः |
कान्तप्रहीणारुचिराङ्गवर्णाः || ५-५-२०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw women with golden complexion lacking clothes, women with a complexion of
refined gold suitable for mating and some other women also with the colour of moon and some other
women with beautiful bodies lacking a lover._END

B_5_C_2_42
BEGIN_
स पाण्डुराविद्धविमानमालिनीं |महार्हजाम्बूनदजालतोरणाम् |यशस्विनीं रावणबाहुपालितां |क्षपाचरैर्भिमबलैः 
समावृताम् || ५-२-५६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw that city of Lanka of great fame, with white, closely built buildings having golden windows and doorways 
of great value, consisting of ogres of great strength and ruled by the hands of Ravana._END

B_5_C_6_12
BEGIN_
समुद्रम् इव गम्भीरम् समुद्रम् इव निह्स्वनम् |
महात्मानो महद् वेश्म महा रत्न परिच्चदम् || ५-६-१३
महा जन समाकीर्णम् ददर्श स महा कपिः |_END
BEGIN_
The great Hanuma saw the wealthy Ravana's huge house, inscrutable like an ocean,
like a noiseless ocean, with a roof embedded with great diamondsand filled with great diamonds._END

B_5_C_1_52
BEGIN_
लाङ्गूलं च समाविद्धं प्लवमानस्य शोभते ||५-१-६१
अम्बरे वायुपुत्रस्य शक्रध्वज इवोच्छ्रितः |_END
BEGIN_
The tail of Hanuma, the son of Vayu floating in the sky, being risen up looked like
the pillar erected in honour of Indra._END

B_5_C_7_6
BEGIN_
नारी प्रवेकैर् इव दीप्यमानम् |
तडिद्भिर् अम्भोदवद् अर्च्यमानम् |
हंस प्रवेकैर् इव वाह्यमानम् |
श्रिया युतम् खे सुक्ऱ्ताम् विमानम् || ५-७-७_END
BEGIN_
Being shone by the best among women like a cloud by lightening, being worshipped,
like being carried by the best swans, like an aerial car full of splendor, of good people in
sky._END

B_5_C_3_34
BEGIN_प्रसीद सुमहाबाहो त्रायस्व हरिसत्तम || ५-३-४४समये सौम्य तिष्ठन्ति स्त्त्ववन्तो महाबलाः 
|_END
BEGIN_"O long armed one! O best among Vanaras! Get propitiated and protect me. O gentle one! Those with 
great strength and courage always stand firm on tradition."_END

B_5_C_8_2
BEGIN_
न तत्र किंचिन्न कृतम् प्रयत्नतो |
न तत्र किंचिन्न महर्हरत्नवत् |
न ते विशेषा नियताः सुरेष्वपि |
न तत्र किंचिन्न महाविशेषवत् || ५-८-३_END
BEGIN_
In that plane there is not even a small thing that is not made with great effort, in
that there is nothing without the best diamonds, those characteristics definitely are not in Devas
also, in that there is nothing that is not of great significance._END

B_5_C_5_20
BEGIN_
ततह् प्रियान् प्राप्य मनोभिरामान् |
सुप्रीतियुक्ताः सुमनोभिरामाः |
गृहेषु हृष्टाः परमाभिरामाः |
हरिप्रवीरः स ददर्श रामाः || ५-५-२१_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter that Vanara warrior saw those with great happiness, those who obtained
lovers who entertained, those who attracted like flowers, those with great beauty and women in
their houses filled with happiness._END

B_5_C_2_43
BEGIN_
चन्द्रोऽपि साचिव्यमिवास्य कुर्वं |स्तारागणैर्मध्यगतो विराजन् |ज्योत्स्नावितानेन वितत्य लोक |मुत्तिष्ठते 
नैकसहस्ररश्मिः || ५-२-५७_END
BEGIN_
The shining moon too rose up with its many thousands of rays, as though performing help to Hanuma, being at the 
middle of its retinue of stars and covering the earth with a canopy of light. That Hanuma saw the moon rising 
up with a glow of a conch shell, shining with a milky white hue of a lotus-fiber, like a swan swimming in a lake._END

B_5_C_6_13
BEGIN_
विराजमानम् वपुषा गज अश्व रथ सम्कुलम् || ५-६-१४
लन्का आभरणम् इति एव सो अमन्यत महा कपिः |
चचार हनुमांस्तत्र रावणस्य समीपतः || ५-६-१५_END
BEGIN_
That great Hanuma thought the house, which was shining with its form filled with
elephants, horses, chariots, to be the jewel of Lanka. Hanuma walked about there in the near-hood
of Ravana._END

B_5_C_1_53
BEGIN_
लाङ्गूलचक्रेण महान् शुक्लदंष्ट्रोऽनिलात्मजः || ५-१-६२
व्यरोचत महाप्राज्ञः परिवेषीव भास्करः |_END
BEGIN_
The great intellectual Hanuma, with his great body, and with white teeth, shone like
the Sun, being surrounded by his circular tail._END

B_5_C_7_7
BEGIN_
यथा नग अग्रम् बहु धातु चित्रम् |
यथा नभः च ग्रह चन्द्र चित्रम् |
ददर्श युक्ती कृत मेघ चित्रम् |
विमान रत्नम् बहु रत्न चित्रम् || ५-७-८_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw the best house like a beautiful cloud endowed with many hues, like the
sky illumined by planets including the moon, decked with numerous precious stones like a mountain
peak, looking picturesque with numerous minerals._END

B_5_C_3_35
BEGIN_अहं तु नगरी लङ्का स्वयमेव प्लवङ्गम || ५-३-४५निर्जिताहम् त्वया वीर विक्रमेण महाबल |_END
BEGIN_"O Vanara! I am myself the city of Lanka. O strong one! O courageous one! I am defeated by your 
strength."_END

B_5_C_8_3
BEGIN_
तपह्समाधानपराक्रमार्जितम् |
मनःसमाधानविचारचारिणम् |
अनेकसंस्थानविषेषनिर्मितम् |
ततस्ततस्तुल्यविशेषदर्शनम् || ५-८-४_END
BEGIN_
One that has been obtained by austerities and by prowess, one that moves about by
thoughts of concentrated mind, made from various significant parts with an appearance of parts of
equal significance, collected from here and there from all over the world._END

B_5_C_5_21
BEGIN_
चन्द्रप्रकाशाश्च हि वक्त्रमाला |
वक्राक्षिपक्ष्माश्च सुनेत्रमालाः |
विभूषाणानाम् च ददर्श मालाः |
शतह्रदानामिव चारुमालाः || ५-५-२२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw rows of faces shining like the moon, beautiful rows of eyes with curved
eyebrows and rows of ornaments like beautiful rows of lighting._END

B_5_C_2_44
BEGIN_
शङ्खप्रभं क्षीरमृणालवर्ण |मुद्गच्छमानं व्यवभासमानम् |ददर्श चन्द्रं स हरिप्रवीरः |प्लोप्लूयमानं सरसीव 
हंसम् || ५-२-५८_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma saw the moon, who was rising up in the sky with the splendour of a couch-shell, shining in white colour 
as milk or lotus-fibre, and looking like a swan swimming in a lake._END

B_5_C_6_14
BEGIN_
गृहाद् गृहम् राक्षसानाम् उद्यानानि च वानरः |
वीक्षमाणो हि असम्त्रस्तः प्रासादामः च चचार सः || ५-६-१६_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma moved about from one house to another of Rakshasas and also parks and
observing in all directions without fear and also courtyards._END

B_5_C_1_54
BEGIN_
स्फिग्देशेनाभिताम्रेण रराज स महाकपिः || ५-१-६३
महता दारितेनेव गिरिर्गैरिकधातुना |_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey Hanuma, with his red colored buttocks, shone like a mountain with
a large deposit of red Gairika herb broken into pieces._END

B_5_C_7_8
BEGIN_
मही कृता पर्वत राजि पूर्णा |
शैलाः कृता वृक्ष वितान पूर्णाः |
वृक्षाः क्ऱ्ताः पुष्प वितान पूर्णाः |
पुष्पम् क्ऱ्तम् केसर पत्र पूर्णम् || ५-७-९_END
BEGIN_
The earth was made to be full of mountain ranges. The mountains were made to be
abounded of trees. The trees were made to be full of flowers. The flower was made to be full of
filaments and petals._END

B_5_C_3_36
BEGIN_इदम् तु तथ्यम् शृणु वै ब्रुवन्त्य मे हरीश्वर || ५-३-४६स्वयम्भुवा पुरा दत्तम् वरदानम् यथा 
मम |_END
BEGIN_"O lord of Vanaras! In earlier times I had been given a boon by Lord Brahma. Hear from me about 
this matter."_END

B_5_C_8_4
BEGIN_
विशेषमालम्ब्य विशेषसंस्थितम् |
विचित्रकूटम् बहुकूटमण्डितम् |
मनोऽभिरामम् शरद्न्दुनिर्मलम् |
विचित्रकूटम् शिखरम् गिरेर्यथा || ५-८-५_END
BEGIN_
Obtaining a special construction as a special object, like a mountain with wonderful
peaks adorned by many peaks, attractive to soul, calm like an autumnal moon, like the peak of a
mountain with other wonderful small peaks._END

B_5_C_5_22
BEGIN_
न त्वेव सीताम् परमाभिजाताम् |
पथि स्थिते राजकुले प्रजाताम् |
लताम् प्रपुल्लामिव साधु जाताम् |
ददर्श तन्वीम् मनसाभिजाताम् || ५-५-२३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma did not see Seetha, one with great beauty born in a royal family following a
virtuous path, well brought up, like a creeper in full blossom, one who was thin, and one who was
born from the mind (of creator)._END

B_5_C_6_15
BEGIN_
अवप्लुत्य महा वेगः प्रहस्तस्य निवेशनम् |
ततो अन्यत् पुप्लुवे वेश्म महा पार्श्वस्य वीर्यवान् || ५-६-१७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma with great prowess, and one with great speed, jumped for the house of
Prahasta and from there leapt for another house that of Mahaparshva._END

B_5_C_1_55
BEGIN_
तस्य वानरसिंहस्य प्लवमानस्य सागरम् || ५-१-६४
कक्षान्तरगतो वायुर्जीमूत इव गर्जति |_END
BEGIN_
Air passing through the lion among monkeys Hanuma's arm pits sounded like a
thundering cloud._END

B_5_C_7_9
BEGIN_
कृतानि वेश्मानि च पाण्डुराणि |
तथा सुपुष्पा अपि पुष्करिण्यः |
पुनः च पद्मानि सकेसराणि |
धन्यानि चित्राणि तथा वनानि || ५-७-१०_END
BEGIN_
White mansions were also built in the same way. Lakes also with beautiful flowers
and also lotuses together with filaments and forest that were the best and wonderful._END

B_5_C_3_37
BEGIN_यदा त्वाम् वानरः कश्चिद्विक्रमाद्वशमानयेत् || ५-३-४७तदा त्वया हि विज्ञेयम् रक्षसाम् भयामागतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Let this be known by you - whenever a Vanara conquers you with his might, then a fear will come 
for Rakshasas."_END

B_5_C_5_23
BEGIN_
सनातने वर्त्मानि सम्निविष्टाम् |
रामेक्षणां तां मदनाभिविष्टाम् |
भर्तुर्मनः श्रीमदनुप्रविष्टाम् |
स्त्रीभ्यो वराभ्यश्च सदा विशिष्टाम् || ५-५-२४_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma did not see that Seetha who stood in the path of ancient righteousness with
Her sight on Sri Rama, who was possessed by the love for Sri Rama, who entered the glorious mind of
husband and always the best among women who were the best._END

B_5_C_8_5
BEGIN_
वहन्ति यम् कुण्डशोभितानना |
महाशना व्योमचरा निशाचराः |
विवृत्तविध्वस्तविशाललोचना |
महाजवा भूतगणाः सहस्रशः || ५-८-६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw that aerial plane which rakshasas who were great eaters, with a face
beautified by earnings, who roamed around in the sky and thousands of genii with round eyes,
crooked eyes and wide eyes capable of great speed carrying it._END

B_5_C_6_16
BEGIN_
अथ मेघ प्रतीकाशम् कुम्भ कर्ण निवेशनम् |
विभीषणस्य च तथा पुप्लुवे स महा कपिः || ५-६-१८_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter the great Hanuma leapt for the house of Kumbhakarna which resembled a
cloud and in the same way for the house of Vibhishana._END

B_5_C_1_56
BEGIN_
खे यथा निपतन्त्युल्का ह्युत्तरान्ताद्विनिःसृता ||५-१-६५
दृश्यते सानुबन्धा च तथा स कपिकुञ्जरः |_END
BEGIN_
The best among monkeys Hanuma flying thus in the sky, looked like a meteor darting
away with great speed in the sky from northern direction._END

B_5_C_7_10
BEGIN_
पुष्प आह्वयम् नाम विराजमानम् |
रत्न प्रभाभिः च विवर्धमानम् |
वेश्म उत्तमानाम् अपि च उच्च मानम् |
महा कपिः तत्र महा विमानम् || ५-७-११_END
BEGIN_
There the great Hanuma saw a great aerial car, the best among best of aerial cars,
shining with the name of Pushpaka with the rays of precious stones, and capable of traveling long
distances._END

B_5_C_3_38
BEGIN_स हि म् समयः सौम्य प्राप्तोऽय तव द्र्शनात् || ५-३-४८स्वयम्भूविहितः सत्यो न तस्यास्ति व्यतिक्रमः 
|_END
BEGIN_"O gentle one! With your appearance now, that time has come for me. Ordinance of Brahma is the 
truth and is immutable."_END

B_5_C_5_24
BEGIN_
उष्णार्दिताम् सानुसृतास्रकण्ठीम् |
पुरा वरार्होत्तमनिष्ककण्ठीम् |
सुजातपक्ष्मामभिरक्तकण्ठीम् |
वनेऽप्रनृत्तामिव नीलकण्ठीम् || ५-५-२५_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma did not see Seetha, tortured by separation from Sri Rama, with unabounding
tears in her throat, in earlier times who had invaluable and best jewellery on her neck, born with
beautiful eyebrows, with a sweet voice, like a she- hen who did not dance in a forest because of
Her current sorrow._END

B_5_C_8_6
BEGIN_
वसन्तपुष्पोत्करचारुदर्शनम् |
वसन्तमासदपि कान्तदर्शनम् |
स पुष्पकम् तत्र विमानमुत्तमम् |
ददर्श तद्वानरवीरसत्तमः || ५-८-७_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the best among Vanara warriors saw there a best plane with the name of
Pushpaka with a more beautiful appearance than a group of flowers during spring, a more attractive
appearance than even the spring season._END

B_5_C_6_17
BEGIN_
महा उदरस्य च तथा विरूप अक्षस्य चैव हि |
विद्युज् जिह्वस्य भवनम् विद्युन् मालेः तथैव च || ५-६-१९
वज्र दम्ष्ट्रस्य च तथा पुप्लुवे स महा कपिः |_END
BEGIN_
That great Hanuma in the same way leapt for the house of Mahodara and also that of
Virupaaksha, that of Viddutjihva._END

B_5_C_1_57
BEGIN_
पतत्पतङ्गसंकाशो व्यायतः शुशुभे कपिः || ५-१-६६
प्रवृद्ध इव मातङ्गः कक्ष्यया बध्यमानया |_END
BEGIN_
With a fast pace equaling that of Sun god, the tall Hanuma shone like an elephant
which increases its size when being festered by a rope._END

B_5_C_3_39
BEGIN_सीतानिमित्तंम् राज्ञस्तु रावणस्य दुरात्मनः || ५-३-४९विधत्स्व सर्वकार्याणि यानि यानिह वाञ्चसि 
|_END
BEGIN_"The destruction has come for Ravana the evil minded king and to all Rakshasas due to Seetha."_END

B_5_C_7_11
BEGIN_
कृताः च वैदूर्यमया विहम्गा |
रूप्य प्रवालैः च तथा विहम्गाः |
चित्राः च नाना वसुभिर् भुजम्गा |
जात्या अनुरूपाः तुरगाः शुभ अन्गाः || ५-७-१२_END
BEGIN_
Artificial birds made of cat's-eye gems, as well as birds made of silver and coral,
wonderful serpants made of various jewels, horses of beautiful limbs suitable by their noble breed
were arranged._END

B_5_C_5_25
BEGIN_
अव्यक्तरेखामिव चन्द्ररेखां |
पांसुप्रदिग्धामिव हेमरेखाम् |
क्षतप्ररूढामिव बाणरेखां |
वायुप्रभिन्नामिव मेघरेक्षाम् || ५-५-२६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma did not see Seetha who was like a crescent with a blurred outline, like a
streek of gold coated by dust, like an arrow in an injury, like a series of clouds scattered by
wind._END

B_5_C_6_18
BEGIN_
शुकस्य च महा वेगः सारणस्य च धीमतः |
तथा च इन्द्रजितो वेश्म जगाम हरि यूथपः || ५-६-२०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma the commander of Vanara army with great radiance went for the intellectual
Suka's house, for Sarana's house, and in the same way for the house of Indrajit._END

B_5_C_1_58
BEGIN_
उपरिष्टाच्छरीरेण छायया चावगाढया |
सागरे मारुताविष्टा नौरिवासीत्तदा कपिः || ५-१-६७_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma who was flying above the ocean with his body above the ocean and his
shadow being immersed in the sea below, looked like a boat being driven by wind._END

B_5_C_7_12
BEGIN_
प्रवाल जाम्बूनद पुष्प पक्षाः |
सलीलम् आवर्जित जिह्म पक्षाः |
कामस्य साक्षाद् इव भान्ति पक्षाः |
कृता विहम्गाः सुमुखाः सुपक्षाः || ५-७-१३_END
BEGIN_
Birds were made with corals on their wings and ogether with golden flowers, with
good wings, with curved and bent wings in a playful way, shining like helpers of the god of love
himself_END

B_5_C_3_40
BEGIN_तत्प्रविश्य हरिश्रेष्ठम् पुरीम् रावणपालिताम् || ५-३-५०विधत्स्व सर्वकार्याण् यानि यानीह 
वाञ्चसि |_END
BEGIN_"O best aming Vanaras! For that reason, enter the city of Lanka ruled by Ravana and do here whatever 
tasks you want to."_END

B_5_C_5_26
BEGIN_
सीतामपश्यन् मनुजेश्वरस्य |
रामस्य पत्नीम् वदताम् वरस्य |
बभूव दुःखाभिहतश्चिरस्य |
प्लवङ्गमो मन्द इवाचिरस्य || ५-५-२७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma became a numb minded one for sometime, stricken with grief not seeing for a
moment Seetha, wife of Sri Rama the best among those who talk, and the lord of all humans._END

B_5_C_6_19
BEGIN_
जम्बु मालेः सुमालेः च जगाम हरि यूथपः || ५-६-२१
रश्मि केतोः च भवनम् सूर्य शत्रोः तथैव च |
वज्रकायस्य च तथा पुप्लुवे स महाकपिः || ५-६-२२_END
BEGIN_
The best among Vanaras Hanuma went for the house of Jambumali and for the house of
Sumali. The great Hanuma jumped for the house Rasmiketu and in the same way for the house of
Suryaketu and in that way for the building of Vajrakaaya._END

B_5_C_1_59
BEGIN_
यं यं देशं समुद्रस्य जगाम स महाकपिः |
स स तस्योरुवेगेन सोन्माद इव लक्ष्यते | ५-१-६८_END
BEGIN_
Whatever place Hanuma went towards on the ocean, that place became agitated due to
the force of thighs._END

B_5_C_7_13
BEGIN_
नियुज्यमानाः च गजाः सुहस्ताः |
सकेसराः च उत्पल पत्र हस्ताः |
बभूव देवी च कृता सुहस्ता |
लक्ष्मीः तथा पद्मिनि पद्म हस्ता || ५-७-१४_END
BEGIN_
Images of elephants in a lotus-pool with filaments of lotus on body, with lotus
petals held in their trunks, were devoted to the worship of an image of Goddess Lakshmi. And also
an image of Goddess Lakshmi with four graceful hands and holding lotus in Her hand was made to
exist in Pushpaka._END

B_5_C_3_41
BEGIN_प्रविश्य शापोपहताम् हरीश्वर |शुभाम् पुरीम् राक्षसराजपालिताम् |यदृच्छया त्वम् जनकात्मजाम् 
सतीम् |विमार्ग सर्वत्र गतो यथासुखम् || ५-३-५१_END
BEGIN_"O lord of Vanaras! Enter the auspicious city of Lanka stuck by the curse, ruled by the king of 
Rakshasas, roam everywhere and search for the chaste wife Seetha according to your comfort."_END

B_5_C_6_20
BEGIN_
धूम्र अक्षस्य च सम्पातेर् भवनम् मारुत आत्मजः |
विद्युद् रूपस्य भीमस्य घनस्य विघनस्य च || ५-६-२३
शुक नाभस्य वक्रस्य शठस्य विकटस्य च |
ह्रस्व कर्णस्य दम्ष्ट्रस्य रोमशस्य च रक्षसः || ५-६-२४
युद्ध उन्मत्तस्य मत्तस्य ध्वज ग्रीवस्य नादिनः |
विद्युज् जिह्व इन्द्र जिह्वानाम् तथा हस्ति मुखस्य च || ५-६-२५
करालस्य पिशाचस्य शोणित अक्षस्य चैव हि |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma jumped for Dhumrah's house, for Sampati's house, for Vidhudrupa's, Bhiima's
house, for Ghana's house and Vighana's house, for Sukhana's house, for Vakra's, for Satha's house
and also for Vikata's house, for Brahmakarna's house, for Damshra's house, for Roma's house, for
Raksha's house, for Ydhonmata's and Indrajihva's house, in the same way for Hastimukas house, for
Karala's house, for Pisacha's house, and also for the building of Shonita._END

B_5_C_1_60
BEGIN_
सागरस्योओर्मिजालानामुरसा शैलवर्ष्मणाम् |
अभिघ्नंस्तु महावेगः पुप्लुवे स महाकपिः |५-१-६९_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey with great speed flew in the sky striking with his chest series of
waves which had a great body like that of mountains._END

B_5_C_7_14
BEGIN_
इति इव तद् ग्ऱ्हम् अभिगम्य शोभनम् |
सविस्मयो नगम् इव चारु शोभनम् |
पुनः च तत् परम सुगन्धि सुन्दरम् |
हिम अत्यये नगम् इव चारु कन्दरम् || ५-७-१५_END
BEGIN_
In this fashion, nearing that house which was shining like a mountain with a
beautiful glow that house with great sweet fragrance like a beautiful mountain during spring, with
beautiful cave became surprised and saw (again)._END

B_5_C_6_21
BEGIN_
क्रममाणः क्रमेण एव हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-६-२६
तेषु तेषु महा अर्हेषु भवनेषु महा यशाः |
तेषाम् ऱ्^द्धिमताम् ऋद्धिम् ददर्श स महा कपिः || ५-६-२७_END
BEGIN_
The son of Vayu, one with great fame, great one among Vanaras , moving about in a
sequence in those and those best buildings, saw the wealth of those rakshasas, who were rich._END

B_5_C_1_61
BEGIN_
कपिवातश्च बलवान् मेघवातश्च निःसृतः |
सागरं भीमनिर्घोषं कम्पयामासतुर्भृशम् || ५-१-७०_END
BEGIN_
Wind from the mighty Hanuma and the wind released from the clouds caused the ocean
with a fearful sound to shake a lot._END

B_5_C_7_15
BEGIN_
ततः स ताम् कपिर् अभिपत्य पूजिताम् |
चरन् पुरीम् दश मुख बाहु पालिताम् |
अदृश्य ताम् जनक सुताम् सुपूजिताम् |
सुदुह्खिताम् पति गुण वेग निर्जिताम् || ५-७-१६_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter that Hanuma nearing that city of Lanka worshipped by Rakshasas, ruled by
arms of ten-headed Ravana, moving thereabout became very gloomy on not seeing that Seetha well
worshipped by all and greatly conquered by the virtues of Her husband Sri Rama_END

B_5_C_6_22
BEGIN_
सर्वेषाम् समतिक्रम्य भवनानि समन्ततः |
आससाद अथ लक्ष्मीवान् राक्षस इन्द्र निवेशनम् || ५-६-२८_END
BEGIN_
The glorious Hanuma passing everyone's houses all round, there-after neared the
house of Ravana._END

B_5_C_9_0
BEGIN_
तस्य आलय वरिष्ठस्य मध्ये विपुलम् आयतम् |
ददर्श भवन श्रेष्ठम् हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-९-१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the son of Vayu, saw a best tall building and a wide one in the middle of
that best group of houses._END

B_5_C_1_62
BEGIN_
विकर्षन्नूर्मिजालानि बृहन्ति लवणाम्भसि |
पुप्लुवे कपिशार्दूलो विकिरन्निव रोदसी || ५-१-७१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma flew in the sky dragging along with him big waves from the ocean as though he
were sprinkling them in the sky._END

B_5_C_7_16
BEGIN_
ततः तदा बहु विध भावित आत्मनः |
कृत आत्मनो जनक सुताम् सुवर्त्मनः |
अपश्यतो अभवद् अतिदुह्खितम् मनः |
सुचक्षुषः प्रविचरतो महात्मनः || ५-७-१७_END
BEGIN_
