Thereafter then the heart of the great souled Hanuma who contemplated supreme spirit
in many ways with a disciplined mind following righteous path, with good observant eyes, moving
about in the city of Lanka became greatly sorrowful on not seeing Seetha._END

B_5_C_6_23
BEGIN_
रावणस्य उपशायिन्यो ददर्श हरि सत्तमः |
विचरन् हरि शार्दूलो राक्षसीर् विकृत ईक्षणाः || ५-६-२९
शूल मुद्गल हस्ताः च शक्तो तोमर धारिणीः |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma best among Vanaras, tiger among Vanaras, moving about saw Rakshas women,
those who were sleeping near to Ravana, those who had horrific eyes, those who had Sulaas, Mudgaras
in their hands, those who had Shaktis and Tomaras._END

B_5_C_9_1
BEGIN_
अर्ध योजन विस्तीर्णम् आयतम् योजनम् हि तत् |
भवनम् राक्षस इन्द्रस्य बहु प्रासाद सम्कुलम् || ५-९-२_END
BEGIN_
That building of Ravana filled with many edifices was half a Yojana long and one
Yojana tall._END

B_5_C_1_63
BEGIN_
मेरुमन्दरसंकाशानुद्धतान् स महार्णवे |
अत्यक्रामन्महावेगस्तरङ्गान् गणयन्निव || ५-१-७२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma with great speed crossed waves which were equal to Mount Meru and Mount
Mandara, that had risen up in the sea, as if counting them._END

B_5_C_6_24
BEGIN_
ददर्श विविधान् गुल्मामः तस्य रक्षः पतेर् गृहे |
राक्षसांश्च महाकायान्नानाप्रहरणोद्यतान् || ५-६-३०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw in that house of Ravana a variety of army divisions and also Rakshasas
those who had huge bodies having different weapons raise up._END

B_5_C_1_64
BEGIN_
तस्य वेगसमुद्धूतं जलं सजलदं तदा |
अम्बर्स्थं विबभ्राज शारदाभ्रमिवाततम् || ५-१-७३_END
BEGIN_
Then the water together with clouds which was driven up by the force of Hanuma,
shone like a stretched autumnal cloud in the sky._END

B_5_C_9_2
BEGIN_
मार्गमाणः तु वैदेहीम् सीताम् आयत लोचनाम् |
सर्वतः परिचक्राम हनूमान् अरि सूदनः || ५-९-३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the destructor of enemies, moved around in all directions searching for
Seetha the wide eyed daughter of King of Videha_END

B_5_C_6_25
BEGIN_
रक्तान् श्वेतान् सितामः चैव हरीमः चैव महा जवान् ||५-६-३१
कुलीनान् रूप सम्पन्नान् गजान् पर गज आरुजान् |
निष्ठितान् गज शिखायाम् ऐरावत समान् युधि || ५-६-३२
निहन्त्ऱ्ऱ्न् पर सैन्यानाम् गृहे तस्मिन् ददर्श सः |
क्षरतः च यथा मेघान् स्रवतः च यथा गिरीन् || ५-६-३३
मेघ स्तनित निर्घोषान् दुर्धर्षान् समरे परैः |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma in that house saw horses in red colour and in white colour, slightly
whitish, capable of great speed, elephants born in a good breed having good appearance capable of
harassing enemy's elephants, skilled in good elephant training, equalling Iraavata, capable of
killing enemies armies in war, rutting like raining clouds, like mountains with water falls that
are pouring down, with trumpeting resembling thundering of clouds, unassailable by enemies in a
battle._END

B_5_C_1_65
BEGIN_
तिमिनक्रझषाः कूर्मा दृश्यन्ते विवृतास्तदा |
वस्त्रापकर्षणेनेव शरीराणि शरीरिणाम् || ५-१-७४_END
BEGIN_
Then various whales, fishes, turtles and crocodiles were being seen clearly in the
sea just as bodies of humans would be seen when clothes are removed._END

B_5_C_9_3
BEGIN_
उत्तमम् राक्षसावासम् हनुमानवलोकयन् |
आससादाथ लक्ष्मीवान् राक्षसेन्द्रनिवेशनम् || ५-९-४
चतुर् विषाणैर् द्विरदैः त्रिविषाणैः तथैव च |
परिक्षिप्तम् असम्बाधम् रक्ष्यमाणम् उदायुधैः || ५-९-५_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, Hanuma the glorious one neared and observed the best residence of
Rakshasas and the house of Ravana, containing elephants with four tusks and also those with three
tusks, those with two tusks and still not crowded. It was protected by soldiers bearing raised
weapons._END

B_5_C_6_26
BEGIN_
सहस्रम् वाहिनीः तत्र जाम्बूनद परिष्कृताः || ५-६-३४
हेम जालैर् अविच्चिन्नाः तरुण आदित्य सम्निभाः |
ददर्श राक्षस इन्द्रस्य रावणस्य निवेशने || ५-६-३५_END
BEGIN_
There Hanuma saw in the house of Ravana, the king of rakshasas, army divisions in
thousands decorated with gold, covered with heaps of gold, equalling the Sun who has fully come
up._END

B_5_C_1_66
BEGIN_
प्लवमानं समीक्ष्यथ भुजङ्गाः सागरालयाः |
व्योम्नि तं कपिशार्दूलं सुपर्ण इति मेनिरे || ५-१-७५_END
BEGIN_
Serpents living in the sea saw Hanuma flying in the sky and thought that it was
Garuda, the king of birds._END

B_5_C_9_4
BEGIN_
राक्षसीभिः च पत्नीभी रावणस्य निवेशनम् |
आह्ऱ्ताभिः च विक्रम्य राज कन्याभिर् आव्ऱ्तम् || ५-९-६
तन् नक्र मकर आकीर्णम् तिमिम्गिल झष आकुलम् |
वायु वेग समाधूतम् पन्नगैर् इव सागरम् || ५-९-७_END
BEGIN_
That building surrounded by the wives of Ravana, by demonesses, and princesses
brought by strength, was like an ocean filled with crocodiles, big fishes, sharks and other fishes,
moved by the speed of wind, and together with serpants._END

B_5_C_1_67
BEGIN_
दशयोजनविस्तीर्णा त्रिंशद्योजनमायता |
छाया वानरसिंहस्य जले चारुतराभवत् || ५-१-७६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma's shadow which was ten yojanas wide and thirty yojanas long appeared very
beautiful on water._END

B_5_C_6_27
BEGIN_
शिबिका विविध आकाराः स कपिर् मारुत आत्मजः |
लता गृहाणि चित्राणि चित्र शाला गृहाणि च || ५-६-३६
क्रीडा गृहाणि च अन्यानि दारु पर्वतकान् अपि |
कामस्य गृहकम् रम्यम् दिवा गृहकम् एव च || ५-६-३७
ददर्श राक्षस इन्द्रस्य रावणस्य निवेशने |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the son of Vayu saw in the house of Ravana the king of rakshasas,
palanquins of various shapes, wonderful bowers, art galleries and other pleasure houses which were
constructed with wooden mountains, house for sexual delight and a beautiful diurnal house._END

B_5_C_9_5
BEGIN_
या हि वैश्वरणे लक्ष्मीर् या च इन्द्रे हरि वाहने |
सा रावण ग्ऱ्हे सर्वा नित्यम् एव अनपायिनी || ५-९-८_END
BEGIN_
Whatever wealth is at Kubera, whatever riches at Indra with green horses, all that
affluence was at Ravana's house. That wealth was always without reduction._END

B_5_C_1_68
BEGIN_
श्वेताभ्रघनराजीव वायुपुत्रानुगामिनी |
तस्य सा शुशुभे छाया वितता लवणाम्भसि || ५-१-७७_END
BEGIN_
That shadow which was following Hanuma and spread on the ocean, shone like a series
of dense white clouds._END

B_5_C_6_28
BEGIN_
स मन्दर तल प्रख्यम् मयूर स्थान सम्कुलम् || ५-६-३८
ध्वज यष्टिभिर् आकीर्णम् ददर्श भवन उत्तमम् |
अनन्त रत्न निचयम् निधि जालम् समन्ततः || ५-६-३९
धीर निष्ठित कर्म अन्तम् गृहम् भूत पतेर् इव |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma saw the best among buildings equalling mount Mandara filled with pens
for peacocks, spread by flag staffs managed by courageous ones like the house of Kubera filled with
many diamonds and also heaps of riches._END

B_5_C_9_6
BEGIN_
या च राज्ञः कुबेरस्य यमस्य वरुणस्य च |
ताद्ऱ्शी तद् विशिष्टा वा ऱ्द्धी रक्षो ग्ऱ्हेष्व् इह || ५-९-९_END
BEGIN_
Whatever was the fortune of Kubera the King of Yakshas, of Yama and of Varuna, the
same fortune or even greater treasure was at this house of Ravana._END

B_5_C_1_69
BEGIN_
शुशुभे स महातेजा महाकायो महाकपिः |
वायुमार्गे निरालम्बे पक्षवानिव पर्वतः || ५-१-७८_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey Hanuma, the great resplendent one with a huge body, shone like a
mountain with wings flying in the sky without any support underneath._END

B_5_C_6_29
BEGIN_
अर्चिर्भिः च अपि रत्नानाम् तेजसा रावणस्य च || ५-६-४०
विरराज अथ तद् वेश्म रश्मिमान् इव रश्मिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
That building shone by the rays of diamonds, by the splendour of Ravana like the Sun
by rays._END

B_5_C_9_7
BEGIN_
तस्य हर्म्यस्य मध्यस्थम् वेश्म च अन्यत् सुनिर्मितम् |
बहुनिर्यूह सम्कीर्णम् ददर्श पवन आत्मजः || ५-९-१०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw another house in the middle of that house, a well built one consisting of
many elephants in rut._END

B_5_C_1_70
BEGIN_
येनासौ याति बलवान् वेगेन कपिकुञ्जरः |
तेन मार्गेण सहसा द्रोणीकृत इवार्णवः || ५-१-७९_END
BEGIN_
In whatever path Hanuma the mighty one went, in that path, there immediately
appeared a trough in the ocean below._END

B_5_C_6_30
BEGIN_
जाम्बू नदमयानि एव शयनानि आसनानि च || ५-६-४१
भाजनानि च शुभ्राणि ददर्श हरि यूथपः |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma leader of Vanaras saw couches and seats and chief vessels all made with
gold._END

B_5_C_10_0
BEGIN_तत्र दिव्य उपमम् मुख्यम् स्फाटिकम् रत्न भूषितम् |अवेक्षमाणो हनुमान् ददर्श शयन आसनम् || 
५-१०-१दान्तकाञ्चनिचित्राङ्गेर्वैश्च वरासनैः |महार्हस्तरणोपेतैरुपपन्नम् महाधनैः || ५-१०-२_END
BEGIN_In that house, while observing, Hanuma saw a portion of house with beds and couches, consisting 
of best couches equaling those in heaven, made of crystal decorated with diamonds, with wonderful parts made of 
ivory and gold, covered with best beds made of cat's eye gems of great value._END

B_5_C_9_8
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मणो अर्थे क्ऱ्तम् दिव्यम् दिवि यद् विश्व कर्मणा |
विमानम् पुष्पकम् नाम सर्व रत्न विभूषितम् ||५-९-११
परेण तपसा लेभे यत् कुबेरः पितामहात् |
कुबेरम् ओजसा जित्वा लेभे तद् राक्षस ईश्वरः || ५-९-१२_END
BEGIN_
Whatever wonderful aeroplane by the name of Pushpaka, decorated with all kinds of
precious stones, made by Visvakarma in heaven for lord Brahma, whatever plane Kubera obtained by
great austerity from Lord Brahma, Ravana obtained that plane by prowess defeating Kubera._END

B_5_C_1_71
BEGIN_
आपाते पक्षिसंघानां पक्षिराज इव व्रजन् |
हनुमान् मेघजालानि प्रकर्षन् मारुतो यथा || ५-१-८०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma while coursing through the path of birds like the king of birds Garuda,
dragged with him series of clouds like the god of wind._END

B_5_C_6_31
BEGIN_
मध्व् आसव कृत क्लेदम् मणि भाजन सम्कुलम् || ५-६-४२
मनो रमम् असम्बाधम् कुबेर भवनम् यथा |
नूपुराणाम् च घोषेण कान्चीनाम् निनदेन च || ५-६-४३
मृदन्ग तल घोषैः च घोषवद्भिर् विनादितम् |
प्रासाद सम्घात युतम् स्त्री रत्न शत सम्कुलम् || ५-६-४२
सुव्यूढ कक्ष्यम् हनुमान् प्रविवेश महा गृहम् |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma entered the big house moistened by liquor made of honey, filled with vessels
made of gems delightful one, un-congested one like the building of Kubera resounded by the sound of
tinkles by the sound of waist ornaments, by the sound of percussion on Mrudangas with deep sound,
which consisted of many mansions filled with hundreds of best women, encircled by many spacious
enclosures._END

B_5_C_10_1
BEGIN_तस्य च एकतमे देशे सो अग्र्य माल्य विभूषितम् |ददर्श पाण्डुरम् चत्रम् तारा अधिपति सम्निभम् 
|| ५-१०-३_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw in a part of that room, an umbrella white in colour decorated with best flower garlands 
and resembling moon - the lord of stars._END

B_5_C_9_9
BEGIN_
ईहा म्ऱ्ग समायुक्तैः कार्य स्वर हिरण्मयैः |
सुक्ऱ्तैर् आचितम् स्तम्भैः प्रदीप्तम् इव च श्रिया || ५-९-१३
मेरु मन्दर सम्काशैर् उल्लिखद्भिर् इव अम्बरम् |
कूट अगारैः शुभ आकारैः सर्वतः समलम्क्ऱ्तम् || ५-९-१४_END
BEGIN_
Supported by pillars decorated with images of wolves, with silver and golden hue and
which were well made, radiant with splendour, decorated all around with rooms equalling Mount Meru
and Mount Mandara, as though touching the sky with an auspicious shape._END

B_5_C_1_72
BEGIN_
पाण्डुरारुणवर्णानि नीलमाञ्जिष्ठकानि च |
कपिनाकृष्यमाणानि महाभ्राणि चकाशिरे || ५-१-८१_END
BEGIN_
Great clouds with white, red, blue and madder colors shone on being dragged by
Hanuma._END

B_5_C_10_2
BEGIN_जातरूपपरिक्षिप्तम् चित्रभानुसमप्रभम् |अशोकमालाविततम् ददर्श परमासनम् || ५-१०-४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw an excellent couch made of gold with radiance equaling that of fire, spread by garlands 
of Ashoka flowers._END

B_5_C_9_10
BEGIN_
ज्वलन अर्क प्रतीकाशम् सुक्ऱ्तम् विश्व कर्मणा |
हेम सोपान सम्युक्तम् चारु प्रवर वेदिकम् || ५-९-१५_END
BEGIN_
Well made by Visvakarma and resembling Fire and Sun in splendour, with stairways
made of gold and with beautiful and best platforms;_END

B_5_C_1_73
BEGIN_
प्रविशन्नभ्रजालानिनिष्पतंश्च पुनः पुनः |
प्रच्चन्नश्च प्रकाशश्च चन्द्रमा इव लक्ष्यते || ५-१-८२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma who is repeatedly entering and leaving series of clouds as He flies in the
sky, is being seen like the moon who shines and is hidden alternately._END

B_5_C_10_3
BEGIN_वाल व्यजन हस्ताभिर् वीज्यमानम् समन्ततः |गन्धैः च विविधैर् जुष्टम् वर धूपेन धूपितम् || 
५-१०-५_END
BEGIN_Fanned by women with fans in their hands in all the four directions and obtained by various fragrances 
fumigated by the best incense._END

B_5_C_9_11
BEGIN_
जाल वात अयनैर् युक्तम् कान्चनैः स्थाटिकैर् अपि |
इन्द्र नील महा नील मणि प्रवरवेदिकम् || ५-९-१६_END
BEGIN_
With windows and ventilation holes made of gold and also made of crystal, with
platforms made of sapphires and emeralds;_END

B_5_C_1_74
BEGIN_
प्लवमानं तु तं दृष्ट्वा प्लवङ्गं त्वरितं तदा |
ववर्षुः पुष्पवर्षणि देवगन्धर्वदानवाः || ५-१-८३_END
BEGIN_
Then, on seeing Hanuma flying quickly in the sky, Devas, Gandharvas and Danavas
showered flowers on him._END

B_5_C_10_4
BEGIN_परम आस्तरण आस्तीर्णम् आविक अजिन सम्व्र्तम् |दामभिर् वर माल्यानाम् समन्ताद् उपशोभितम् || 
५-१०-६_END
BEGIN_Covered by an excellent bed, spread by sheep skin everywhere and shone by rows of excellent garlands._END

B_5_C_9_12
BEGIN_
विद्रुमेण विचित्रेण मणिभिश्च महाधनैः |
विस्तुलाभिश्च मुक्ताभिस्तलेनाभिविराजितम् || ५-९-१७_END
BEGIN_
Shone by floors embellished with corals of strange hue and with precious stones of
great value, with pearls without comparison;_END

B_5_C_1_75
BEGIN_
तताप न हि तं सूर्यः प्लवन्तं वानरोत्तमम् |
सिषेवे च तदा वायू रामकार्याद्थसिद्धये || ५-१-८४_END
BEGIN_
Then, the Sun did not scorch Hanuma, the best among Vanaras, who was flying for
Rama's welfare. The wind god Vayu also served him with a delightful breeze._END

B_5_C_10_5
BEGIN_तस्मिन् जीमूत सम्काशम् प्रदीप्त उत्तम कुण्डलम् |लोहित अक्षम् महा बाहुम् महा रजत वाससम् 
|| ५-१०-७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Ravana in that house, equaling a cloud, wearing earrings with a brilliant shine with 
red eyes and with long arms wearing gold clothes._END

B_5_C_9_13
BEGIN_
चन्दनेन च रक्तेन तपनीयनिभेन च |
सुपुण्यगन्धिना युक्तमादित्यतरुणोपमम् || ५-९-१८_END
BEGIN_
Reddish and resembling gold, together with sandal wood having a good smell and
brilliant like the Sun at noon;_END

B_5_C_1_76
BEGIN_
ऋषयस्तुष्टुवुश्चैव प्लवमानं विहायसा |
जगुश्च देवगन्धर्वाः प्रशंसन्तो महौजसम् || ५-१-८५_END
BEGIN_
Sages praised the great resplendent Hanuma flying in the sky. Devas and Gandharvas
also sang in His praise._END

B_5_C_10_6
BEGIN_लोहितेन अनुलिप्त अन्गम् चन्दनेन सुगन्धिना |संध्या रक्तम् इव आकाशे तोयदम् सतडिद् गुणम् 
|| ५-१०-८_END
BEGIN_With his body smeared with red sandal-wood with good fragrance like a cloud in the red sky at sunset, 
together with groups of lightening._END

B_5_C_9_14
BEGIN_
कूटागारैर्वराकारैर्विविधैः समलम्कृतम् |
विमानम् पुष्पकम् दिव्यम् आरुरोह महा कपिः || ५-९-१९_END
BEGIN_
The great Hanuma alighted the best aeroplane called Pushpaka with an excellent form
decorated by rows of upper floors._END

B_5_C_1_77
BEGIN_
नागाश्च तुष्टुवुर्यक्षा रक्षांसि विबुधाः खगाः || ५-१-८६
प्रेक्ष्य सर्वे कपिवरं सहसा विगतक्लमम् |_END
BEGIN_
Immediately on seeing the best among monkeys, Hanuma, flying without any effort,
Nagas, Yakshas, Rakshasas, Devas and birds all praised Him._END

B_5_C_10_7
BEGIN_वृतम् आभरणैर् दिव्यैः सुरूपम् काम रूपिणम् |सव्र्क्ष वन गुल्म आढ्यम् प्रसुप्तम् इव मन्दरम् 
|| ५-१०-९_END
BEGIN_Ravana was filled with excellent jewellery, with a good appearance, with an ability to assume desired 
form, resembling mount Mandara in sleep, together with groups of trees and bushes._END

B_5_C_11_0
BEGIN_अवधूय च ताम् बुद्धिम् बभूव अवस्थितः तदा |जगाम च अपराम् चिन्ताम् सीताम् प्रति महा कपिः 
|| ५-११-१_END
BEGIN_The great Hanuma then removing that thought became with the right mind and had another thought 
about Seetha._END

B_5_C_9_15
BEGIN_
तत्रस्थः स तदा गन्धम् पान भक्ष्य अन्न सम्भवम् |
दिव्यम् सम्मूर्चितम् जिघ्रन् रूपवन्तम् इव अनिलम् || ५-९-२०_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma then being there, smelled a wonderful sweet fragrance like wind with an
appearance, created from drinks and foods, including cooked rice diffused on all sides._END

B_5_C_1_78
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् प्लवगशार्दूले प्लवमाने हनूमति || ५-१-८७
इक्ष्वाकुकुलमानार्थी चिन्तयामास सागरः |_END
BEGIN_
While that best among vanaras, Hanuma, was flying, the god of ocean thought thus for
the respect of Ikshvaaku dynasty:_END

B_5_C_10_8
BEGIN_क्रीडित्वा उपरतम् रात्रौ वर आभरण भूषितम् |प्रियम् राक्षस कन्यानाम् राक्षसानाम् सुख आवहम् 
|| ५-१०-१०_END
BEGIN_Resting after having pleasure at night, bedecked with the best ornaments, he was a lover to the 
rakshasa girls and causing comfort to rakshasas._END

B_5_C_11_1
BEGIN_न रामेण वियुक्ता सा स्वप्तुम् अर्हति भामिनी |न भोक्तुम् न अपि अलम्कर्तुम् न पानम् उपसेवितुम् 
|| ५-११-२न अन्यम् नरम् उपस्थातुम् सुराणाम् अपि च ईश्वरम् |न हि राम समः कश्चिद् विद्यते त्रिदशेष्व् अपि 
|| ५-११-३अन्या इयम् इति निश्चित्य पान भूमौ चचार सः |_END
BEGIN_That Seetha is not suitable to sleep separated from Rama, will not eat, will not decorate also, 
not suited to drink a beverage, to reach another man even though if he were Indra because there is indeed no one 
equaling Rama even among gods. This is another woman - thus deciding that Hanuma paced in that banqueting hall._END

B_5_C_9_16
BEGIN_
स गन्धः तम् महा सत्त्वम् बन्धुर् बन्धुम् इव उत्तमम् |
इत एहि इति उवाच इव तत्र यत्र स रावणः || ५-९-२१_END
BEGIN_
That sweet smell was as though saying thus to that Hanuma : "Come here!", like a
relative to a best relative pointing to there wherever that Ravana was._END

B_5_C_1_79
BEGIN_
साहाय्यं वानरेन्द्रस्य यदि नाहं हनूमतः || ५-१-८८
करिष्यामि भविष्यामि सर्ववाच्यो विवक्षताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"If I do not help this best among vanaras Hanuma, I shall become prone to all kinds
of ill-talk by those who want to speak against me."_END

B_5_C_11_2
BEGIN_क्रीडितेन अपराः क्लान्ता गीतेन च तथा पराः || ५-११-४नृत्तेन च अपराः क्लान्ताः पान विप्रहताः 
तथा |_END
BEGIN_Some women were tired from erotic dalliance and then some other women were tired from singing; 
some others were weary from dance and were unconscious from consumption of liquor._END

B_5_C_10_9
BEGIN_पीत्वा अपि उपरतम् च अपि ददर्श स महा कपिः |भास्करे शयने वीरम् प्रसुप्तम् राक्षस अधिपम् 
|| ५-१०-११_END
BEGIN_That great Hanuma saw the gallant king of rakshasas in sleep on a shining couch resting after drinking._END

B_5_C_9_17
BEGIN_
ततः ताम् प्रस्थितः शालाम् ददर्श महतीम् शुभाम् |
रावणस्य मनः कान्ताम् कान्ताम् इव वर स्त्रियम् || ५-९-२२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma started thereafter there (in that direction) and saw an auspicious great
hall, close to heart of Ravana, like a delightful best woman._END

B_5_C_1_80
BEGIN_
अहमिक्ष्वाकुनाथेन सगरेण विवर्धतः || ५-१-८९
इक्ष्वाकुसचिचश्चायं नावसीदितुमर्हति |_END
BEGIN_
"I was developed by Sagara of Ikshvaaku dynasty. This Hanuma who is helping a
descendant of that dynasty should not become tired."_END

B_5_C_10_10
BEGIN_निह्श्वसन्तम् यथा नागम् रावणम् वानर उत्तमः |आसाद्य परम उद्विग्नः सो अपासर्पत् सुभीतवत् 
|| ५-१०-१२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, best among Vanaras neared Ravana, became very gloomy and moved away with great dread, 
as though from a hissing serpent._END

B_5_C_11_3
BEGIN_मुरजेषु म्ऱ्दन्गेषु पीठिकासु च संस्थिताः || ५-११-५तथा आस्तरण मुख्य्येषु सम्विष्टाः च अपराः 
स्त्रियः |_END
BEGIN_Some women were stationed on tabors, on Mrudangas, on seats, some other women rested on chief carpets._END

B_5_C_9_18
BEGIN_
मणि सोपान विक्ऱ्ताम् हेम जाल विराजिताम् |
स्फाटिकैर् आव्ऱ्त तलाम् दन्त अन्तरित रूपिकाम् || ५-९-२३_END
BEGIN_
That hall was made of stairways embedded with diamonds, decorated with golden
windows, with a floor embellished with crystal, with shapes made from ivory in the middle._END

B_5_C_1_81
BEGIN_
तथा मया विधातव्यं विश्रमेत यथा कपिः || ५-१-९०
शेषं च मयि विश्रान्तः सुखेनातिपतिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"I have to behave in such a way that Hanuma would take rest. After resting in me for
a while, He can cross the remaining distance with comfort."_END

B_5_C_10_11
BEGIN_अथ आरोहणम् आसाद्य वेदिका अन्तरम् आश्रितः |सुप्तम् राक्षस शार्दूलम् प्रेक्षते स्म महा कपिः 
|| ५-१०-१३_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the great Hanuma neared staircase, sought another dais and observed closely Ravana._END

B_5_C_11_4
BEGIN_अङ्गनानाम् सहस्रेण भूषितेन विभूषणैः || ५-११-६रूप सम्ल्लाप शीलेन युक्त गीत अर्थ भाषिणा 
|देश काल अभियुक्तेन युक्त वाक्य अभिधायिना || ५-११-७रत अभिरत संसुप्तम् ददर्श हरि यूथपः |_END
BEGIN_The warrior among Vanaras saw a thousand of women decorated by jewellery with a nature of talking 
about beauty, conversing about the correct meaning of songs being sung, behaving according to time and place, 
wont to speak appropriate words, indulged in sleep after sexual dalliance._END

B_5_C_9_19
BEGIN_
मुक्ताभिः च प्रवालैः च रूप्य चामी करैर् अपि |
विभूषिताम् मणि स्तम्भैः सुबहु स्तम्भ भूषिताम् || ५-९-२४_END
BEGIN_
Well decorated with pearls, corals and also with silver and gold and with diamond
studded pillars and also decorated with many pillars._END

B_5_C_1_82
BEGIN_
इति कृत्वा मतिं साध्वीं समुद्रश्चन्नमम्भसि || ५-१-९१
हिरण्यनाभं मैनाकमुवाच गिरिसत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
Samudra thus making a good thought, spoke to Mainaka, the best among mountains with
gold in the middle hidden in water._END

B_5_C_11_5
BEGIN_तासाम् मध्ये महा बाहुः शुशुभे राक्षस ईश्वरः || ५-११-८गोष्ठे महति मुख्यानाम् गवाम् मध्ये 
यथा वृषः |_END
BEGIN_In the middle of that group of women, Ravana with great arms shone like a bull in the middle of 
cows in a big cow-pen._END

B_5_C_10_12
BEGIN_शुशुभे राक्षस इन्द्रस्य स्वपतः शयन उत्तमम् |गन्ध हस्तिनि सम्विष्टे यथा प्रस्रवणम् महत् 
|| ५-१०-१४_END
BEGIN_The excellent couch of the sleeping Ravana shone like a great lake when a scented elephant resides 
in it._END

B_5_C_9_20
BEGIN_
नम्रैरृजुभिरत्युच्चैः समन्तात्सुविभूषितैः |
स्तम्भैः पक्षैर् इव अत्युच्चैर् दिवम् सम्प्रस्थिताम् इव || ५-९-२५_END
BEGIN_
By pillars slightly bent with no distortion, which were very tall and well decorated
all over, that hall was as though starting for sky with very high wings._END

B_5_C_1_83
BEGIN_
त्वमिहासुरसंघानां पाताळतलवासिनां || ५-१-९२
देवराज्ञा गिरिश्रेष्ठ परिघः संनिवेशितः |_END
BEGIN_
"O best among mountains Mainaka! You have been positioned here by Devendra as an
obstacle to the groups of asuras living in paataala."_END

B_5_C_11_6
BEGIN_स राक्षस इन्द्रः शुशुभे ताभिः परिवृतः स्वयम् || ५-११-९करेणुभिर् यथा अरण्यम् परिकीर्णो 
महा द्विपः |_END
BEGIN_That Ravana himself surrounded by those women, shone like a great elephant surrounded by she elephants 
in a great forest._END

B_5_C_10_13
BEGIN_कान्चन अन्गद नद्धौ च ददर्श स महात्मनः |विक्षिप्तौ राक्षस इन्द्रस्य भुजाव् इन्द्र ध्वज 
उपमौ || ५-१०-१५_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma also saw the wealthy Ravana's arms tied with golden armlets thrown apart, resembling 
flag staffs raised in honor of Indra._END

B_5_C_9_21
BEGIN_
महत्या कुथय आस्त्रीणम् प्ऱ्थिवी लक्षण अन्कया |
पृथिवीम् इव विस्तीर्णाम् सराष्ट्र ग्ऱ्ह मालिनीम् || ५-९-२६_END
BEGIN_
Covered by a wonderful large carpet with all earth's characteristics like rivers,
mountains, oceans, forests, painted over, that hall was like the vast earth together with states
and rows of houses._END

B_5_C_1_84
BEGIN_
त्वमेषां जातवीर्याणां पुनरेवोत्पतिष्यताम् || ५-१-९३
पाताळस्याप्रमेयस्य द्वारमावृत्य तिष्ठसि |_END
BEGIN_
"You are standing at the entrance of paataala which is difficult to measure, fully
covering it, when asuras courageous by birth are trying to rise up again."_END

B_5_C_11_7
BEGIN_सर्व कामैर् उपेताम् च पान भूमिम् महात्मनः || ५-११-१०ददर्श कपि शार्दूलः तस्य रक्षः पतेर् 
गृहे |_END
BEGIN_The best among Vanaras saw in that wealthy Ravana's house a bar also, consisting of all desirables._END

B_5_C_10_14
BEGIN_ऐरावत विषाण अग्रैर् आपीडित क्र्त व्रणौ |वज्र उल्लिखित पीन अंसौ विष्णु चक्र परिक्षितौ || 
५-१०-१६_END
BEGIN_Those arms had wounds made by stabbing from the pointed edges of tusks of Iraavata and fleshy shoulders 
smeared with diamond and hit by Vishnu chakra._END

B_5_C_9_22
BEGIN_
नादिताम् मत्त विहगैर् दिव्य गन्ध अधिवासिताम् |
पर अर्ध्य आस्तरण उपेताम् रक्षो अधिप निषेविताम् || ५-९-२७_END
BEGIN_
It was resounded by birds in heat, made fragrant by excellent perfumes, hung with
best tapestries and inhabited by the king of rakshasas_END

B_5_C_1_85
BEGIN_
तिर्यगूर्ध्वमधश्चैव शक्तिस्ते शैल वर्धितुम् || ५-१-९४
तस्मात्संचोदयामि त्वामुत्तिष्ठ गिरिसत्तम |_END
BEGIN_
"O mountain, you have capability to grow wide, up or down. O best among mountains,
for that reason I am encouraging you. Raise up."_END

B_5_C_11_8
BEGIN_मृगाणाम् महिषाणाम् च वराहाणाम् च भागशः || ५-११-११तत्र न्यस्तानि मांसानि पान भूमौ ददर्श 
सः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw there in that bar, meat of dear and of buffalo, of wild boar kept separately._END

B_5_C_10_15
BEGIN_पीनौ समसुजात अंसौ सम्गतौ बल सम्युतौ |सुलक्षण नख अन्गुष्ठौ स्वन्गुली तल लक्षितौ || ५-१०-१७_END
BEGIN_These arms of Ravana were corpulent with well grown and equal strong shoulders proportionate to 
body, with knees and thumbs of good characteristics, with good fingers and palms._END

B_5_C_9_23
BEGIN_
धूम्राम् अगरु धूपेन विमलाम् हंस पाण्डुराम् |
चित्राम् पुष्प उपहारेण कल्माषीम् इव सुप्रभाम् || ५-९-२८_END
BEGIN_
It was made smokey by the fumes of agallocum. It was a pure one white like a swan,
wonderful by the decoration of flowers, like divine cow with a great radiance._END

B_5_C_1_86
BEGIN_
न एष कपिशार्दूलस्त्वमुपर्येति वीर्यवान् || ५-१-९५
हनूमान्रामकार्यार्थं भीमकर्मा खमाप्लुतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Hanuma, the best among monkeys, the courageous one, who has taken up a fearful task
for the benefit of Rama, that such Hanuma while flying in the sky is coming over you."_END

B_5_C_11_9
BEGIN_रौक्मेषु च विशलेषु भाजनेष्व् अर्ध भक्षितान् || ५-११-१२ददर्श कपि शार्दूल मयूरान् कुक्कुटामः 
तथा |_END
BEGIN_The best among Vanaras saw half eaten peacocks and chicken in wide vessels of golden colour._END

B_5_C_10_16
BEGIN_सम्हतौ परिघ आकारौ व्र्त्तौ करि कर उपमौ |विक्षिप्तौ शयने शुभ्रे पन्च शीर्षाव् इव उरगौ || 
५-१०-१८_END
BEGIN_With strong joints in the shape of club, round in shape resembling the trunks of an elephant, like 
five headed snakes thrown on clean couch._END

B_5_C_9_24
BEGIN_
मनः सम्ह्लाद जननीम् वर्णस्य अपि प्रसादिनीम् |
ताम् शोक नाशिनीम् दिव्याम् श्रियः सम्जननीम् इव || ५-९-२९_END
BEGIN_
That excellent hall was causing happiness to heart, causing a fair complexion,
destroying sorrow and was as though producing prosperity._END

B_5_C_1_87
BEGIN_
अस्य साह्यं मया कार्यमिक्ष्वाकुकुलवर्तिनः || ५-१-९६
मम हीक्ष्वाकवः पूज्याः परं पूज्यतमास्तव |_END
BEGIN_
"To this Hanuma, who is a follower of the Ikshvaaku dynasty, help should be done by
me now. Descendants of Ikshvaaku are repectable to me. They are even more respectable to you."_END

B_5_C_10_17
BEGIN_शश क्षतज कल्पेन सुशीतेन सुगन्धिना |चन्दनेन पर अर्ध्येन स्वनुलिप्तौ स्वलम्क्र्तौ || ५-१०-१९
उत्तम स्त्री विम्र्दितौ गन्ध उत्तम निषेवितौ |यक्ष पन्नग गन्धर्व देव दानव राविणौ || ५-१०-२०_END
BEGIN_Shoulders well smeared by best sandal with good smell and very cool resembling in color to a hare's 
blood, well decorated, massaged by the best women, served by the best sandal and which made yakshas, nagas, gandharvas, 
devas and daanavaas scream._END

B_5_C_11_10
BEGIN_वराह वार्ध्राणसकान् दधि सौवर्चल आयुतान् || ५-११-१३शल्यान् म्ऱ्ग मयूरामः च हनूमान् अन्ववैक्षत 
|_END
BEGIN_Hanuma observed meat of pigs and goats, porcupines, deer and peacocks preserved in curds and sochal 
salt._END

B_5_C_9_25
BEGIN_
इन्द्रियाणि इन्द्रिय अर्थैः तु पन्च पन्चभिर् उत्तमैः |
तर्पयाम् आस माता इव तदा रावण पालिता || ५-९-३०_END
BEGIN_
Like a mother, then that hall governed by Ravana caused satisfaction to all five
sensory organs with all the excellent five objects of the senses._END

B_5_C_1_88
BEGIN_
कुरु साचिव्यमस्माकं न नः कार्यमतिक्रमेत् || ५-१-९७
कर्तव्यमकृतं कार्यं सतां मन्युमुदीरयेत् |_END
BEGIN_
"Do help to us. Our task may not be miscarried. A task which needs to be performed
and not done, will increase the anger of good people."_END

B_5_C_10_18
BEGIN_ददर्श स कपिः तस्य बाहू शयन संस्थितौ |मन्दरस्य अन्तरे सुप्तौ महा अर्ही रुषिताव् इव || ५-१०-२१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saw there arms on the couch like great serpents in anger sleeping in the middle of 
mount Mandara._END

B_5_C_11_11
BEGIN_कृकरान् विविधान् सिद्धामः चकोरान् अर्ध भक्षितान् || ५-११-१४महिषान् एक शल्यामः च चागामः 
च कृत निष्ठितान् |लेख्यम् उच्च अवचम् पेयम् भोज्यानि विविधानि च || ५-११-१५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw birds called Krakara cooked ready to be eaten in variety of ways, birds called Chakoras 
half eaten, wild buffalos, fishes called ekashleya, goats, food to be licked of various kinds, beverages and various 
foods._END

B_5_C_9_26
BEGIN_
स्वर्गो अयम् देव लोको अयम् इन्द्रस्य इयम् पुरी भवेत् |
सिद्धिर् वा इयम् परा हि स्याद् इति अमन्यत मारुतिः || ५-९-३१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma thought thus : "This is heaven! This is indeed the abode of Devas! This is a
city of Indra. This might be the result of a great austerity."_END

B_5_C_1_89
BEGIN_
सलिलादूर्ध्वमुत्तिष्ठ तिष्ठत्वेष कपिस्त्वयि || ५-१-९८
अस्माकमतिथिश्चैव पूज्यश्च प्लवतां वरः |_END
BEGIN_
"Raise up above from the water. This Hanuma is the best among fliers and is a guest
to be worshipped for us. Let him stand on you."_END

B_5_C_11_12
BEGIN_तथा अम्ल लवण उत्तंसैर् विविधै राग षाडवैः |हार नूपुर केयूरैर् अपविद्धैर् महा धनैः || ५-११-१६
पान भाजन विक्षिप्तैः फलैः च विविधैर् अपि |कृत पुष्प उपहारा भूर् अधिकम् पुष्यति श्रियम् || ५-११-१७_END
BEGIN_In the same way that floor was obtaining glory greatly with Ragas and Shadabas seasoned with sour 
and salty sauces, with necklaces, anklets and armlets of great value thrown around, with various fruits left in 
drinking vessels, with flowers sprinkled._END

B_5_C_10_19
BEGIN_ताभ्याम् स परिपूर्णाभ्याम् भुजाभ्याम् राक्षस अधिपः |शुशुभे अचल सम्काशः श्र्न्गाभ्याम् 
इव मन्दरः || ५-१०-२२_END
BEGIN_That king of Rakshasas equaling a mountain with those shoulders, which were well built and shone 
like Mount Mandara with twin peaks._END

B_5_C_9_27
BEGIN_
प्रध्यायत इव अपश्यत् प्रदीपामः तत्र कान्चनान् (ःइअतुस्!)|
धूर्तान् इव महा धूर्तैर् देवनेन पराजितान् || ५-९-३२_END
BEGIN_
Like gamblers defeated by greater gamblers in gambling, Hanuma saw golden hued lamps
being still, as though in thought._END

B_5_C_1_90
BEGIN_
चामीकरमहानाभ देवगन्धर्व सेवित ||५-१-९९
हनुमांस्त्वयि विश्रान्तस्ततः शेषं गमिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"O mountain with golden hued middle area and one who is served by Devas and
Gandharvas! Hanuma can take rest on you and then traverse rest of the distance."_END

B_5_C_11_13
BEGIN_तत्र तत्र च विन्यस्तैः सुश्लिष्टैः शयन आसनैः |पान भूमिर् विना वह्निम् प्रदीप्ता इव उपलक्ष्यते 
|| ५-११-१८_END
BEGIN_That bar was seen as though radiant without fire, with couches and chairs well arranged and placed 
there and there._END

B_5_C_10_20
BEGIN_चूत पुम्नाग सुरभिर् बकुल उत्तम सम्युतः |मृष्ट अन्न रस सम्युक्तः पान गन्ध पुरः सरः || ५-१०-२३
तस्य राक्षस सिम्हस्य निश्चक्राम मुखान् महान् |शयानस्य विनिह्श्वासः पूरयन्न् इव तद् ग्र्हम् || ५-१०-२४_END
BEGIN_From the great face of that king of Rakshasas who was sleeping, came out breath with fragrance 
like that of flowers of chuuta and punnaaga, consisting of the best fragrance of Vakula flowers, together with 
the flavor of best cooked rice, with the smell of liquor as though filling that house._END

B_5_C_9_28
BEGIN_
दीपानाम् च प्रकाशेन तेजसा रावणस्य च |
अर्चिर्भिर् भूषणानाम् च प्रदीप्ता इति अभ्यमन्यत || ५-९-३३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma thought thus : "This building shines by the light of lamps and the brilliance
of Ravana and also due to the radiance of jewellery."_END

B_5_C_1_91
BEGIN_
काकुत्थ्सस्यानृशंस्यं च मैथिल्याश्च विवासनम् || ५-१-१००
श्रमं च प्लवगेन्द्रस्य समीक्ष्योत्थातुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"You are fit to raise up after seeing the gentleness of Sri Rama, and the exile of
Seetha, and the effort of Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_11_14
BEGIN_बहु प्रकारैर् विविधैर् वर संस्कार संस्कृतैः |मांसैः कुशल सम्युक्तैः पान भूमि गतैः पृथक् 
|| ५-११-१९_END
BEGIN_Many meats of different kinds cultured with various best seasonings, well arranged separately obtained 
that bar._END

B_5_C_9_29
BEGIN_
ततो अपश्यत् कुथा आसीनम् नाना वर्ण अम्बर स्रजम् |
सहस्रम् वर नारीणाम् नाना वेष विभूषितम् || ५-९-३४_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter Hanuma saw a thousand of best women sitting on the rug with clothing of
various colours and decorated in a variety of ways._END

B_5_C_10_21
BEGIN_मुक्ता मणि विचित्रेण कान्चनेन विराजता |मुकुटेन अपव्र्त्तेन कुण्डल उज्ज्वलित आननम् || ५-१०-२५
रक्त चन्दन दिग्धेन तथा हारेण शोभिता |पीन आयत विशालेन वक्षसा अभिविराजितम् || ५-१०-२६पाण्डुरेण अपविद्धेन 
क्षौमेण क्षतज ईक्षणम् |महा अर्हेण सुसम्वीतम् पीतेन उत्तम वाससा || ५-१०-२७माष राशि प्रतीकाशम् निह्श्वसन्तम् 
भुजन्गवत् |गान्गे महति तोय अन्ते प्रसुतमिव कुन्जरम् || ५-१०-२८चतुर्भिः कान्चनैर् दीपैर् दीप्यमानैः चतुर् 
दिशम् |प्रकाशी क्र्त सर्व अन्गम् मेघम् विद्युद् गणैर् इव || ५-१०-२९पाद मूल गताः च अपि ददर्श सुमहात्मनः 
|पत्नीः स प्रिय भार्यस्य तस्य रक्षः पतेर् ग्र्हे || ५-१०-३०_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saw in the house of that king of Rakshasa's, wives at the feet, Ravana being a gigantic 
one with loving wives, shone with crown tilted to the side, having strange hue with pearls and diamonds and of 
golden colour, with a face made brilliant by earrings, shone with the chest region smeared with red sandal, shining 
with a necklace wide, high and corpulent with a silk cloth of white colour falling on him, with eyes reddish like 
blood, well tied by a best cloth of yellow colour and of very best quality, resembling a heap of black beans, 
snoring like a hiss of a snake, like an elephant sleeping in the middle of water belonging to the great river 
Ganga with all the four directions shone by the four lamps of golden colour, resembling a cloud with all the parts 
being shone by groups of lighting._END

B_5_C_1_92
BEGIN_
हिरण्य नाभो मैनाको निशम्य लवणाम्भसः || ५-१-१०१
उत्पपात जलात्तूर्णं महाद्रुमलतायुतः |_END
BEGIN_
The mountain with gold in the middle, Mainaka, listening to the words of the salty
ocean, got up quickly from the water, together with great trees and creepers._END

B_5_C_11_15
BEGIN_दिव्याः प्रसन्ना विविधाः सुराः कृत सुरा अपि |शर्कर आसव माध्वीकाः पुष्प आसव फल आसवाः || 
५-११-२०वास चूर्णैः च विविधैर् मृष्टाः तैः तैः पृथक् पृथक् |_END
BEGIN_Excellent and clear various liquors, a liquor called Sura, liquor made of sugar, liquor made of 
honey, liquor made of flowers and liquors made of fruits also, artificially made liquors - those and those were 
cultured separately with various fragrant powders._END

B_5_C_9_30
BEGIN_
परिव्ऱ्त्ते अर्ध रात्रे तु पान निद्रा वशम् गतम् |
क्रीडित्वा उपरतम् रात्रौ सुष्वाप बलवत् तदा || ५-९-३५_END
BEGIN_
Then at the turn of midnight, those women slept deeply resting after playing during
night, with a deep sleep caused by liquor._END

B_5_C_10_22
BEGIN_शशि प्रकाश वदना वर कुण्डल भूषिताः |अम्बाल माल्य आभरणा ददर्श हरि यूथपः || ५-१०-३१_END
BEGIN_The leader of Vanaras saw those wives of Ravana with faces with radiance of moon, adorned with 
beautiful earrings, wearing jewellery and flower garlands which were not worn out._END

B_5_C_1_93
BEGIN_
स सागरजलं भित्त्वा बभूवाभ्युत्थितस्तदा || ५-१-१०२
यथा जलधरं भित्त्वा दीप्तरश्मिर्दिवाकरः |_END
BEGIN_
Then that Mainaka became in the risen state, passing through the ocean water, just
like the Sun piercing through a cloud with His shining rays._END

B_5_C_11_16
BEGIN_सम्तता शुशुभे भूमिर् माल्यैः च बहु संस्थितैः || ५-११-२१हिरण्मयैः च करकैर् भाजनैः स्फाटिकैर् 
अपि |जाम्बूनदमयैश्चान्याः करकैरभिवम्वृता || ५-११-२२_END
BEGIN_The floor shone filled by flower garlands in a variety of forms, with various vessels of golden 
hue and also made of crystal, filled with other small vessels of golden colour._END

B_5_C_10_23
BEGIN_नृत्त वादित्र कुशला राक्षस इन्द्र भुज अन्कगाः |वर आभरण धारिण्यो निषन्ना दद्र्शे कपिः || 
५-१०-३२_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw wives of Ravana with skill in dance and musical instruments, who obtained the shoulders 
of Ravana wearing the best jewellery and being in sleep._END

B_5_C_9_31
BEGIN_
तत् प्रसुप्तम् विरुरुचे निह्शब्द अन्तर भूषणम् |
निह्शब्द हंस भ्रमरम् यथा पद्म वनम् महत् || ५-९-३६_END
BEGIN_
That sleeping group of women, adorned with jewels which were not making sound, shone
like a great park of lotuses with calm swans and bees._END

B_5_C_1_94
BEGIN_
स महात्मा मुहूर्तेन सर्वतः सलिलावृतः || ५-१-१०३
द्र्शयामास शृङ्गाणि सागरेण नियोजितः |
शातकुम्भमयैः शृङ्गैः सकिन्नरमहोरगैः || ५-१-१०४
आदित्योदयसंकाशैरालिखद्भिरिवाम्बरम् |_END
BEGIN_
That great Mainaka who was covered by water in all directions, who had peaks with
Kinnaras and great serpents, which were equal to a sun rise, which were touching the sky, and which
had a golden hue, being ordered by the ocean, showed his peaks in an instant._END

B_5_C_10_24
BEGIN_वज्र वैदूर्य गर्भाणि श्रवण अन्तेषु योषिताम् |ददर्श तापनीयानि कुण्डलानि अन्गदानि च || ५-१०-३३_END
BEGIN_He saw earrings of those women at the end of ears with embedded diamonds and cats eye gems and 
having golden colour._END

B_5_C_11_17
BEGIN_राजतेषु च कुम्भेषु जाम्बूनदमयेषु च |पान श्रेष्ठम् तदा भूरि कपिः तत्र ददर्श ह || ५-११-२३_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw indeed then lot of best quality liquor in pots of silver and of golden colour._END

B_5_C_9_32
BEGIN_
तासाम् सम्व्ऱ्त दन्तानि मीलित अक्षाणि मारुतिः |
अपश्यत् पद्म गन्धीनि वदनानि सुयोषिताम् || ५-९-३७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw faces of those best women, with teeth covered by lips with closed eyes
and with lotus fragrance._END

B_5_C_1_95
BEGIN_
तप्तजाम्बूनदैः शृङिगाः पर्वतस्य समुत्थितैः || ५-१-१०५
आकाशं शस्त्रसंकाशमभवत्काञ्चनप्रभम् |_END
BEGIN_
The sky which had a bluish tinge like that of a sword, shone with a golden hue
because of the peaks of the mountain which rose up and which was like molten gold._END

B_5_C_11_18
BEGIN_सो अपश्यत् शात कुम्भानि शीधोर् मणिमयानि च |राजतानि च पूर्णानि भाजनानि महा कपिः || ५-११-२४_END
BEGIN_That great Hanuma saw vessels full of liquor of golden colour, embedded with gem stones and also 
of silver hue._END

B_5_C_10_25
BEGIN_तासाम् चन्द्र उपमैर् वक्त्रैः शुभैर् ललित कुण्डलैः |विरराज विमानम् तन् नभः तारा गणैर् 
इव || ५-१०-३४_END
BEGIN_With the faces of those women with delicate earrings which were equal to moon and auspicious that 
house shone like the sky with clusters of stars._END

B_5_C_9_33
BEGIN_
प्रबुद्धानि इव पद्मानि तासाम् भूत्वा क्षपा क्षये |
पुनः सम्व्ऱ्त पत्राणि रात्राव् इव बभुः तदा || ५-९-३८_END
BEGIN_
At that time, those faces shone which became like lotuses in blossom during day time
and again were like lotuses with closed petals at night._END

B_5_C_1_96
BEGIN_
जातरूपमयैः शृङ्गैर्भ्राजमानैः स्वयंप्रभैः || ५-१-१०६
आदित्यशतसंकाशः सोऽभवद्गिरिसत्तमः |_END
BEGIN_
That best among mountains became equal to a hundred suns with its peaks which had a
golden hue and which were shining with a self generated shine._END

B_5_C_11_19
BEGIN_क्वचिद् अर्ध अवशेषाणि क्वचित् पीतानि सर्वशः |क्वचिन् न एव प्रपीतानि पानानि स ददर्श ह || 
५-११-२५_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saw indeed at some places drinks half filled and at some places completely drunk and 
some places not at all drunk._END

B_5_C_10_26
BEGIN_मद व्यायाम खिन्नाः ताः राक्षस इन्द्रस्य योषितः |तेषु तेष्व् अवकाशेषु प्रसुप्ताः तनु मध्यमाः 
|| ५-१०-३५_END
BEGIN_Women of that Ravana being tired from lustful passion and exertion and having lean waists slept 
at first opportunity._END

B_5_C_9_34
BEGIN_
इमानि मुख पद्मानि नियतम् मत्त षट्पदाः |
अम्बुजानि इव फुल्लानि प्रार्थयन्ति पुनः पुनः || ५-९-३९_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma thought that drunk bees definitely are desiring again and again these lotus
faces like lotuses in blossom._END

B_5_C_1_97
BEGIN_
तमुत्थितमसंगेन हनुमानग्रतः स्थितम् || ५-१-१०७
मध्ये लवणतोयस्य विघ्नोऽयमिति निश्चितः |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma on seeing the mountain which stood before Him, rising up from the middle of
the salty ocean suddenly, decided that it as an obstacle._END

B_5_C_11_20
BEGIN_क्वचिद् भक्ष्यामः च विविधान् क्वचित् पानानि भागशः |क्वचिद् अन्न अवशेषाणि पश्यन् वै विचचार 
ह || ५-११-२६_END
BEGIN_Hanuma paced about seeing at some places various eatables and at some places drinks separately, 
and at some places remnants of cooked rice._END

B_5_C_10_27
BEGIN_अङ्गहारैस्तथैवान्या कोवलैर्नृत्तशालिनी |विन्यस्तशुभसर्वाङ्गी प्रसुप्ता वरवर्णिनी || ५-१०-३६_END
BEGIN_Another woman with skill in dancing consisting of delicate body postures slept in the same way 
with all her body parts making the same dance postures._END

B_5_C_9_35
BEGIN_
इति वा अमन्यत श्रीमान् उपपत्त्या महा कपिः |
मेने हि गुणतः तानि समानि सलिल उद्भवैः || ५-९-४०_END
BEGIN_
The glorious great Hanuma thought as above by recourse to reason. He also thought
thus "Those faces equal lotuses by their qualities such as beauty, fragrance, and others"._END

B_5_C_1_98
BEGIN_
स तमुच्छ्रित मत्यर्थं महावेगो महाकपिः || ५-१-१०८
उरसा पातयामास जीमूतमिव मारुतः |_END
BEGIN_
That great monkey Hanuma with a great speed, brought that great tall mountain with
His chest just as the God of wind would a cloud._END

B_5_C_11_21
BEGIN_क्वचित् प्रभिन्नैः करकैः क्वचिद् आलोडितैर् घटैः |क्वचित् सम्पृक्त माल्यानि जलानि च फलानि 
च || ५-११-२७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw some places with vessels broken, some places with pots in shambles, some places with 
water together with flower garlands and fruits._END

B_5_C_10_28
BEGIN_काचिद् वीणाम् परिष्वज्य प्रसुप्ता सम्प्रकाशते |महा नदी प्रकीर्णा इव नलिनी पोतम् आश्रिता 
|| ५-१०-३७_END
BEGIN_One woman hugging veena and sleeping was shining like a lotus plant thrown away by the flow of 
a great river and resorting a boat._END

B_5_C_9_36
BEGIN_
सा तस्य शुशुभे शाला ताभिः स्त्रीभिर् विराजिता |
शारदी इव प्रसन्ना द्यौः ताराभिर् अभिशोभिता || ५-९-४१_END
BEGIN_
That hall of Ravana's being shone by those women, glittered like a calm cloudless
sky in autumn shone by stars._END

B_5_C_1_99
BEGIN_
स तथा पातितस्तेन कपिना पर्वतोत्तमः || ५-१-१०९
बुद्ध्वा तस्य कपेर्वेगं जहर्ष च ननन्द च |_END
BEGIN_
That best among mountains Mainaka, thus being fell down by that Hanuma, recognized
Hanuma's speed and lauded him with pleasure._END

B_5_C_11_22
BEGIN_शयनानि अत्र नारीणाम् शून्यानि बहुधा पुनः |परस्परम् समाश्लिष्य काश्चित् सुप्ता वर अन्गनाः 
|| ५-११-२८_END
BEGIN_Here couches again of women were varied and clean, some best women slept there hugging one another._END

B_5_C_10_29
BEGIN_अन्या कक्ष गतेन एव मड्डुकेन असित ईक्षणा |प्रसुप्ता भामिनी भाति बाल पुत्रा इव वत्सला || 
५-१०-३८_END
BEGIN_Another woman with black eyes sleeping with an instrument called madduka under arm pit shone like 
a woman carrying an infant boy with love._END

B_5_C_9_37
BEGIN_
स च ताभिः परिव्ऱ्तः शुशुभे राक्षस अधिपः |
यथा हि उडु पतिः श्रीमामः ताराभिर् अभिसम्व्ऱ्तः || ५-९-४२_END
BEGIN_
That lord of Rakshasas surrounded by those women shone like the radiant moon
surrounded by stars._END

B_5_C_1_100
BEGIN_
तमाकाशगतं वीरमाकाशे समुपस्थितः || ५-१-११०
प्रीतो हृष्टमना वाक्यमब्रवीत्पर्वतः कपिम् |
मानुषं धारयन् रूपमात्मनः शिखरे स्थितः || ५-१-१११_END
BEGIN_
Mount Mainaka with love and with gladdened heart obtained a human form and standing
on its own peak, spoke these words approaching that courageous Hanuma in the sky._END

B_5_C_11_23
BEGIN_काचिच् च वस्त्रम् अन्यस्या अपह्ऱ्त्य उपगुह्य च |उपगम्य अबला सुप्ता निद्रा बल पराजिता || 
५-११-२९_END
BEGIN_Some women conquered by the power of sleep pulled other sleeping women's clothing and slept covering 
themselves._END

B_5_C_9_38
BEGIN_
याः च्यवन्ते अम्बरात् ताराः पुण्य शेष समाव्ऱ्ताः |
इमाः ताः सम्गताः क्ऱ्त्स्ना इति मेने हरिः तदा || ५-९-४३_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma thought thus : "Whatever meteors together with residue of piety fall
down from the sky, all those meteors had been together as these women"._END

B_5_C_1_101
BEGIN_
दुष्करं कृतावन्कर्म त्वमिदं वानरोत्तम |
निपत्य मम शृङ्गेषु विश्रमस्व यथासुखम् || ५-१-११२_END
BEGIN_
"O the great Vanara! You have performed this impossible task of flying over the
ocean. Do come down on to my peaks and rest for a while to your comfort."_END

B_5_C_10_30
BEGIN_पटहम् चारु सर्व अन्गी पीड्य शेते शुभ स्तनी |चिरस्य रमणम् लब्ध्वा परिष्वज्य इव कामिनी || 
५-१०-३९_END
BEGIN_A woman with beautiful body features and with beautiful breasts slept tightly and hugged instrument 
called pataha as though hugging a lover, getting him after a long time._END

B_5_C_11_24
BEGIN_तासाम् उच्च्वास वातेन वस्त्रम् माल्यम् च गात्रजम् |न अत्यर्थम् स्पन्दते चित्रम् प्राप्य 
मन्दम् इव अनिलम् || ५-११-३०_END
BEGIN_Clothing and garland on the throats of those women was moving slightly and wonderfully as though 
obtaining air from the air of breath._END

B_5_C_1_102
BEGIN_
राघवस्य कुले जातैरुदधिः परिवर्धितः |
स त्वां रामहिते युक्तं प्रत्यर्चयति सागरः || ५-१-११३_END
BEGIN_
"The ocean was developed by people born in Sri Rama's dynasty. That such ocean is
worshipping in lieu of Sri Rama, you who is desirous of Sri Rama's welfare."_END

B_5_C_10_31
BEGIN_काचिद् अंशम् परिष्वज्य सुप्ता कमल लोचना |रहः प्रियतमम् गृह्य सकामेव च कामिनी || ५-१०-४०_END
BEGIN_Another woman with lotus like eyes hugging a flute slept like a woman with lust holding her lover 
in secret._END

B_5_C_9_39
BEGIN_
ताराणाम् इव सुव्यक्तम् महतीनाम् शुभ अर्चिषाम् |
प्रभा वर्ण प्रसादाः च विरेजुः तत्र योषिताम् || ५-९-४४_END
BEGIN_
There the luster, complexion and grace of those women clearly resembled great stars
which emitted an auspicious radience._END

B_5_C_11_25
BEGIN_चन्दनस्य च शीतस्य शीधोर् मधु रसस्य च |विविधस्य च माल्यस्य पुष्पस्य विविधस्य च || ५-११-३१
बहुधा मारुतः तत्र गन्धम् विविधम् उद्वहन् |_END
BEGIN_There wind blew carrying in a lot of directions, a variety of fragrances of cool sandal-paste and 
of sweet liquor, of various flower garlands and of various kinds of agallocum fumes._END

B_5_C_1_103
BEGIN_
कृते च प्रतिकर्तव्यमेष धर्मः सनातनः |
सोऽयं तत्प्रतिकारार्थी त्वत्तः संमानमर्हति || ५-१-११४_END
BEGIN_
"When a service is done, a return service needs to be rendered. This is an ancient
tradition. Such this ocean who wants to do a return service to the Raghu dynasty, is suitable for
respect by you."_END

B_5_C_10_32
BEGIN_विपञ्चैइम् परिगृह्यान्या नियता नृत्तशालिनी |निद्रा वशम् अनुप्राप्ता सह कान्ता इव भामिनी 
|| ५-१०-४१_END
BEGIN_Another woman skilled in dance obtained sleep getting an instrument like veena and being in tune 
with it like a woman together with her lover._END

B_5_C_9_40
BEGIN_
व्याव्ऱ्त्त गुरु पीन स्रक् प्रकीर्ण वर भूषणाः |
पान व्यायाम कालेषु निद्रा अपह्ऱ्त चेतसः || ५-९-४५_END
BEGIN_
Those women with dishevelled large thick garlands and scattered excellent jewels
during the time of drinking, dancing etc., were with consciousness stolen by sleep._END

B_5_C_11_26
BEGIN_स्नानानाम् चन्दनानाम् च धूपानाम् चैव मूर्चितः |प्रववौ सुरभिर् गन्धो विमाने पुष्पके तदा 
|| ५-११-३२_END
BEGIN_Then the blossoming fragrance from the baths and sandal paste and from agallocum fumes blew spreading 
all around in that Pushpaka plane._END

B_5_C_10_33
BEGIN_अन्या कनक सम्काशैर् म्र्दु पीनैर् मनो रमैः |मृदन्गम् परिपीड्य अन्गैः प्रसुप्ता मत्त लोचना 
|| ५-१०-४२_END
BEGIN_Another woman with lusty eyes slept hugging a percussion instrument called mridanga with her body 
parts which were pleasant which resembled gold and which were smooth and fleshy._END

B_5_C_1_104
BEGIN_
त्वन्निमित्तमनेनाहं बहुमानात्प्रचोदितः |
योजनानां शतं चापि कपिरेष समाप्लुतः ||५-१-११५
तव सानुषु विश्रान्तः शेषं प्रक्रमतामिति |
तिष्ठ त्वं हरिशार्दूल मयि विश्रम्य गम्यताम् || ५-१-११६_END
BEGIN_
""After flying a hundred yojanas, let this Hanuma rest on your peak and then travel
the rest of distance." - Thus I have been encouraged by this ocean for your sake due to His great
respect for you. O best among vanaras! Stop for a while and then go after resting on me."_END

B_5_C_9_41
BEGIN_
व्याव्ऱ्त्त तिलकाः काश्चित् काश्चिद् उद्भ्रान्त नूपुराः |
पार्श्वे गलित हाराः च काश्चित् परम योषितः || ५-९-४६_END
BEGIN_
Best women with disturbed sacred marks (tilaka) on forehead became with displaced
anklets, became with necklaces fallen off to side._END

B_5_C_11_27
BEGIN_श्याम अवदाताः तत्र अन्याः काश्चित् कृष्णा वर अन्गनाः || ५-११-३३काश्चित् कान्चन वर्ण अन्ग्यः 
प्रमदा राक्षस आलये |_END
BEGIN_There in that Ravana's house, some women had fair and white complexion some best women were black, 
some women had a body of golden complexion._END

B_5_C_10_34
BEGIN_भुज पार्श्व अन्तरस्थेन कक्षगेन क्र्श उदरी |पणवेन सह अनिन्द्या सुप्ता मद क्र्त श्रमा || 
५-१०-४३_END
BEGIN_Another woman with thin stomach, who was not to be blamed, slept due to tiresomeness from lust 
together with an instrument called Padama between her shoulders and reaching arm pits._END

B_5_C_1_105
BEGIN_
तदिदं गन्धवत्स्वादु कन्दमूलफलं बहु |
तदास्वाद्य हरिश्रेष्ठ विश्रान्तोऽनु गमिष्यसि || ५-१-११७_END
BEGIN_
"O best among vanaras! For that reason, here is lots of roots, fruits and other
eatables which are fragrant and sweet. May you leave after eating that and resting here for a
while."_END

B_5_C_9_42
BEGIN_
मुखा हार व्ऱ्ताः च अन्याः काश्चित् प्रस्रस्त वाससः |
व्याविद्ध रशना दामाः किशोर्य इव वाहिताः || ५-९-४७_END
BEGIN_
Some other women became tied with pearl necklaces, some others became with tied-up
waist ornaments (and) resembled young female horses who had walked long._END

B_5_C_11_28
BEGIN_तासाम् निद्रा वशत्वाच् च मदनेन विमूर्चितम् || ५-११-३४पद्मिनीनाम् प्रसुप्तानाम् रूपम् आसीद् 
यथैव हि |_END
BEGIN_Appearance of those sleeping women, tired from being possessed by sleep and from lust, was like 
lotuses sleeping._END

B_5_C_10_35
BEGIN_डिण्डिमम् परिग्र्ह्य अन्या तथैव आसक्त डिण्डिमा |प्रसुप्ता तरुणम् वत्सम् उपगूह्य इव भामिनी 
|| ५-१०-४४_END
BEGIN_Another woman with an instrument called Dindima near her slept in the same way as a woman hugging 
her husband and also her child._END

B_5_C_1_106
BEGIN_
अस्माकमपि सम्बन्धः कपिमुख्य त्वयास्ति वै |
प्रख्यातस्त्रिषु लोकेषु महागुणपरिग्रहः || ५-१-११८_END
BEGIN_
"O chief among vanaras! Besides this, there also exists a relationship which is
famous in all the three worlds, which is based on great virtues, for us with you."_END

B_5_C_12_0
BEGIN_स तस्य मध्ये भवनस्य वानरो |लता ग्ऱ्हामः चित्र गृहान् निशा गृहान् |जगाम सीताम् प्रति 
दर्शन उत्सुको |न च एव ताम् पश्यति चारु दर्शनाम् || ५-१२-१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma interested in sight of Seetha, in the middle of that building, went towards houses 
made of plant creepers, art houses, and nocturnal houses but did not see Her with a beautiful appearance._END

B_5_C_9_43
BEGIN_
सुकुण्डल धराः च अन्या विच्चिन्न म्ऱ्दित स्रजः |
गज इन्द्र म्ऱ्दिताः फुल्ला लता इव महा वने || ५-९-४८_END
BEGIN_
Some others wearing nice earrings with flower garlands that were torn and disturbed,
resembled creepers, tread upon by an elephant in a big forest._END

B_5_C_11_29
BEGIN_एवम् सर्वम् अशेषेण रावण अन्तः पुरम् कपिः || ५-११-३५ददर्श सुमहा तेजा न ददर्श च जानकीम् 
|_END
BEGIN_Hanuma with great radiance thus saw entire Ravana's house completely but did not see Seetha._END

B_5_C_1_107
BEGIN_
वेगवन्तः प्लवन्तो ये प्लवगा मारुतात्मज |
तेषां मुख्यतमं मन्ये त्वामहं कपिकुञ्जर || ५-१-११९_END
BEGIN_
"O son of Vayu, the god of wind! O best among vanaras! I am thinking you as being
very important among those vanaras who are fast and who are capable of flying."_END

B_5_C_10_36
BEGIN_काचिद् आडम्बरम् नारी भुज सम्भोग पीडितम् |कृत्वा कमल पत्र अक्षी प्रसुप्ता मद मोहिता || 
५-१०-४५_END
BEGIN_Another woman with eyes like lotus petals slept making the instrument called adambara pressing 
it by her shoulders being desired by lust._END

B_5_C_12_1
BEGIN_स चिन्तयाम् आस ततो महा कपिः |प्रियाम् अपश्यन् रघु नन्दनस्य ताम् |ध्रुवम् नु सीता म्रियते 
यथा न मे |विचिन्वतो दर्शनम् एति मैथिली || ५-१२-२_END
BEGIN_That great Hanuma then later not seeing that Seetha dear to Rama thought thus: "to me searching 
Seetha in whatever way appearance not being obtained, from that Seetha definitely has died."_END

B_5_C_9_44
BEGIN_
चन्द्र अंशु किरण आभाः च हाराः कासांचिद् उत्कटाः |
हंसा इव बभुः सुप्ताः स्तन मध्येषु योषिताम् || ५-९-४९_END
BEGIN_
Big pearl necklaces with the radiance of moon-rays in the middle of breasts of some
other women shone like sleeping swans._END

B_5_C_1_108
BEGIN_
अतिथिः किलपूजार्हः प्राकृतोऽपि विजानता |
धर्मं जिज्ञासमानेन किं पुनस्त्वादृशो महान् || ५-१-१२०_END
BEGIN_
"By a person who wants to know dharma or by one who knows dharma, a guest even
though ordinary is to be respected. What else can I say in the case of a great guest like you."_END

B_5_C_10_37
BEGIN_कलशीम् अपविद्ध्य अन्या प्रसुप्ता भाति भामिनी |वसन्ते पुष्प शबला माला इव परिमार्जिता || 
५-१०-४६_END
BEGIN_Another woman sleeping, felling down a small pot, shone like a flower garland with the flowers 
of strange hue made auspicious in spring._END

B_5_C_11_30
BEGIN_निरीक्षमाणः च ततः ताः स्त्रियः स महा कपिः || ५-११-३६जगाम महतीम् चिन्ताम् धर्म साध्वस शन्कितः 
|_END
BEGIN_Then that Hanuma seeing those women obtained great anguish being in doubt because of fear in the 
matter of dharma._END

B_5_C_12_2
BEGIN_सा राक्षसानाम् प्रवरेण बाला |स्व शील सम्रक्षण तत् परा सती |अनेन नूनम् प्रतिदुष्ट कर्मणा 
|हता भवेद् आर्य पथे परे स्थिता || ५-१२-३_END
BEGIN_"That Seetha standing in the best traditional path being chaste interested, in preserving her character 
must have been killed by the king of these Rakshasas who performed evil deeds - this is certain."_END

B_5_C_9_45
BEGIN_
अपरासाम् च वैदूर्याः कादम्बा इव पक्षिणः |
हेम सूत्राणि च अन्यासाम् चक्र वाका इव अभवन् || ५-९-५०_END
BEGIN_
And of some other women, necklaces made with cat's eye gems resembled birds called
Kadambas and for some others golden chains were like Chakravaka birds._END

B_5_C_10_38
BEGIN_पाणिभ्याम् च कुचौ काचित् सुवर्ण कलश उपमौ |उपगूह्य अबला सुप्ता निद्रा बल पराजिता || ५-१०-४७_END
BEGIN_Another woman slept hugging her breasts resembling golden pots by her hands, overcome with sleep._END

B_5_C_11_31
BEGIN_पर दार अवरोधस्य प्रसुप्तस्य निरीक्षणम् || ५-११-३७इदम् खलु मम अत्यर्थम् धर्म लोपम् करिष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_"My seeing sleeping house of other people's wives will do a great deficit to dharma."_END

B_5_C_1_109
BEGIN_
त्वं हि देववरिष्ठस्य मारुतस्य महात्मनः |
पुत्रस्तस्यैव वेगेन सदृशः कपिकुञ्जर || ५-१-१२१_END
BEGIN_
"O best among vanaras! You are the son of the great Vayu - the God of wind, who is
best in speed among the Devas. In speed you are equal to him alone."_END

B_5_C_12_3
BEGIN_विरूप रूपा विकृता विवर्चसो |महा आनना दीर्घ विरूप दर्शनाः |समीक्ष्य सा राक्षस राज योषितो 
|भयाद् विनष्टा जनक ईश्वर आत्मजा|| ५-१२-४_END
BEGIN_"That daughter of King Janaka died of fear seeing the wives of Ravana with crooked appearances 
- horrible ones without radiance with great faces with long and crooked eyes."_END

B_5_C_9_46
BEGIN_
हंस कारण्डव आकीर्णाः चक्र वाक उपशोभिताः |
आपगा इव ता रेजुर् जघनैः पुलिनैर् इव || ५-९-५१_END
BEGIN_
Those women with buttocks resembling sand dunes, shone like rivers filled with swans
and birds called Karandas and decorated by Chakravaka birds._END

B_5_C_10_39
BEGIN_अन्या कमल पत्र अक्षी पूर्ण इन्दु सद्र्श आनना |अन्याम् आलिन्ग्य सुश्रोणी प्रसुप्ता मद विह्वला 
|| ५-१०-४८_END
BEGIN_Another woman with eyes like lotus petals, with her face resembling full moon, overcome with lust 
slept hugging another woman with a beautiful hip region._END

B_5_C_1_110
BEGIN_
पूजिते त्वयि धर्मज्ञ पूजां प्राप्नोति मारुतः |
तस्मात्त्वं पूजनीयो मे शृणु चाप्यत्र कारणम् || ५-१-१२२_END
BEGIN_
"O knower of Dharma! If you are worshipped, Vayu also gets worship. For that reason
you are to be worshipped by me. Also listen to another reason in this matter."_END

B_5_C_11_32
BEGIN_न हि मे पर दाराणाम् दृष्टिर् विषय वर्तिनी ||५-११-३८अयम् च अत्र मया दृष्टः पर दार परिग्रहः 
|_END
BEGIN_"My sight is indeed not in the matter of other wives here. These other's wives have been seen by 
me."_END

B_5_C_12_4
BEGIN_सीताम् अद्ऱ्ष्ट्वा हि अनवाप्य पौरुषम् |विह्ऱ्त्य कालम् सह वानरैः चिरम् |न मे अस्ति 
सुग्रीव समीपगा गतिः |सुतीक्ष्ण दण्डो बलवामः च वानरः || ५-१२-५_END
BEGIN_"Without seeing Seetha, not obtaining destiny and wandering for a long time together with Vanaras, 
to me there is not a path to go near Sugreeva. Sugreeva has a sharp punishment and also is strong."_END

B_5_C_9_47
BEGIN_
किन्किणी जाल सम्काशाः ता हेम विपुल अम्बुजाः |
भाव ग्राहा यशः तीराः सुप्ता नद्य इव आबभुः || ५-९-५२_END
BEGIN_
Those sleeping women shone like rivers with their smiles as flower buds, with golden
jewellery as big lotuses, with their behaviours as crocodiles, with fame as banks._END

B_5_C_10_40
BEGIN_आतोद्यानि विचित्राणि परिष्वज्य वर स्त्रियः |निपीड्य च कुचैः सुप्ताः कामिन्यः कामुकान् 
इव || ५-१०-४९_END
BEGIN_Some excellent women slept hugging strange instruments and pressing them with breasts as though 
lustful woman with lusty men._END

B_5_C_1_111
BEGIN_
पूर्वं कृतयुगे तात पर्वताः पक्षिणोऽभवन् |
ते हि जग्मुर्दिशः सर्वा गरुडानिलवेगिनः || ५-१-१२३_END
BEGIN_
"O son! Earlier in the Krita yuga, mountains had wings. With speed equal to that of
Garuda and Vayu, they went in all directions."_END

B_5_C_11_33
BEGIN_तस्य प्रादुर् अभूच् चिन्ता पुनर् अन्या मनस्विनः || ५-११-३९निश्चित एक अन्त चित्तस्य कार्य 
निश्चय दर्शिनी |_END
BEGIN_To that Hanuma with an excellent mind, with a fixed and concentrated mind, was born another thought 
again, showing a fixed resolve in the task at hand._END

B_5_C_12_5
BEGIN_दृष्टम् अन्तः पुरम् सर्वम् दृष्ट्वा रावण योषितः |न सीता दृश्यते साध्वी वृथा जातो मम श्रमः 
|| ५-१२-६_END
BEGIN_"All inner city has been seen. Women of Ravana have been seen. The chaste Seetha has not been seen. 
My effort became wastefull."_END

B_5_C_9_48
BEGIN_
मृदुष्व् अन्गेषु कासांचित् कुच अग्रेषु च संस्थिताः |
बभूवुर् भूषणानि इव शुभा भूषण राजयः || ५-९-५३_END
BEGIN_
Auspicious lines of decoration which were on smooth parts of some other women and on
nipples, were like jewellery._END

B_5_C_10_41
BEGIN_तासाम् एक अन्त विन्यस्ते शयानाम् शयने शुभे |ददर्श रूप सम्पन्नाम् अपराम् स कपिः स्त्रियम् 
|| ५-१०-५०_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saw among those women a very beautiful woman sleeping on an auspicious couch arranged 
alone at a side._END

B_5_C_1_112
BEGIN_
ततस्तेषु प्रयातेषु देवसंघः सहर्षिभिः |
भूतानि च भयं जग्मुस्तेषां पतनशङ्कया|| ५-१-१२४_END
BEGIN_
"After that when those mountains were thus flying freely, Devas and living creatures
together with sages obtained fear in the doubt that those mountains might fall down."_END

B_5_C_11_34
BEGIN_कामम् दृष्ट्वा मया सर्वा विश्वस्ता रावण स्त्रियः || ५-११-४०न तु मे मनसः किंचिद् वैकृत्यम् 
उपपद्यते |_END
BEGIN_"All Ravana's women who were in faith could have been seen by me; to my mind there indeed was not 
even a little disturbance"._END

B_5_C_12_6
BEGIN_किम् नु माम् वानराः सर्वे गतम् वक्ष्यन्ति सम्गताः |गत्वा तत्र त्वया वीर किम् कृतम् तद् 
वदस्व नः || ५-१२-७_END
BEGIN_"To me who has gone back all Vanaras after meeting what they would say? O strong one! Going there, 
what has been done by you? Tell that to us."_END

B_5_C_9_49
BEGIN_
अंशु कान्ताः च कासांचिन् मुख मारुत कम्पिताः |
उपरि उपरि वक्त्राणाम् व्याधूयन्ते पुनः पुनः || ५-९-५४_END
BEGIN_
Edges of clothing (worn by them) disturbed by air from breathing of some other
women, were being fluttered again and again on their faces._END

B_5_C_10_42
BEGIN_मुक्ता मणि समायुक्तैर् भूषणैः सुविभूषिताम् |विभूषयन्तीम् इव च स्व श्रिया भवन उत्तमम् || 
५-१०-५१गौरीम् कनक वर्ण आभाम् इष्टाम् अन्तः पुर ईश्वरीम् |कपिर् मन्द उदरीम् तत्र शयानाम् चारु रूपिणीम् 
|| ५-१०-५२_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Mandodari with a beautiful form together with diamonds and pearls, well decorated by 
jewellery and with her self radiance as though decorating that great building with a fair complexion and with 
a radiance like golden colour, who was dear to her husband the lady of women in that gynaeceum sleeping there._END

B_5_C_1_113
BEGIN_
ततः क्रुद्धः सहस्राअक्षः पर्वतानां शतक्रतुः |
पक्षान् चिच्छेद वज्रेण तत्र तत्र सहस्रशः ||५-१-१२५_END
BEGIN_
"Then the angry Devendra who performed a hundred Asvamedha rituals, cut off the
wings of thousands of mountains by his weapon vajra then and there."_END

B_5_C_11_35
BEGIN_मनो हि हेतुः सर्वेषाम् इन्द्रियाणाम् प्रवर्तते || ५-११-४१शुभ अशुभास्व् अवस्थासु तच् च 
मे सुव्यवस्थितम् |_END
BEGIN_"Among auspicious or inauspicious states in the behavior of all senses mind is the reason. My that 
mind is very steady."_END

B_5_C_12_7
BEGIN_अदृष्ट्वा किम् प्रवक्ष्यामि ताम् अहम् जनक आत्मजाम् |ध्रुवम् प्रायम् उपेष्यन्ति कालस्य 
व्यतिवर्तने || ५-१२-८_END
BEGIN_"Without seeing that Seetha what can I say? Due to passing of time, definitely they will obtain 
fire."_END

B_5_C_9_50
BEGIN_
ताः पाताका इव उद्धूताः पत्नीनाम् रुचिर प्रभाः |
नाना वर्ण सुवर्णानाम् वक्त्र मूलेषु रेजिरे || ५-९-५५_END
BEGIN_
Those edges of clothes with various beautiful colours, shone at the base of Ravana's
wives' throats like hoisted flags of beautiful shine._END

B_5_C_10_43
BEGIN_स ताम् दृष्ट्वा महा बाहुर् भूषिताम् मारुत आत्मजः |तर्कयाम् आस सीता इति रूप यौवन सम्पदा 
|| ५-१०-५३हर्षेण महता युक्तो ननन्द हरि यूथपः |_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma with great arms seeing the woman well decorated, out of logic thought thus: "This is 
Seetha by the wealth of her appearance and her youth". That warrior of Vanaras was delighted together with great 
pleasure._END

B_5_C_13_0
BEGIN_विमानात् तु सुसम्क्रम्य प्राकारम् हरि यूथपः |हनूमान् वेगवान् आसीद् यथा विद्युद् घन अन्तरे 
|| ५-१३-१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma the leader of Vanaras crossed from pushpaka toward the fort wall and became with speed like 
lighting in the middle of a cloud._END

B_5_C_1_114
BEGIN_
स मामुपागतः क्रुद्धो वज्रमुद्यम्य देवराट् |
ततोऽहं सहसा क्षिप्तः स्वसनेन महात्मना || ५-१-१२६_END
BEGIN_
"That Devendra angrily reached me with raised vajra. Then I was thrown away
immediately by the great Vayu."_END

B_5_C_11_36
BEGIN_न अन्यत्र हि मया शक्या वैदेही परिमार्गितुम् || ५-११-४२स्त्रियो हि स्त्रीषु द्ऱ्श्यन्ते 
सदा सम्परिमार्गणे |_END
BEGIN_"By me it is not possible to search Seetha at another place. Always during search women will be 
seen among other women."_END

B_5_C_12_8
BEGIN_किम् वा वक्ष्यति व्ऱ्द्धः च जाम्बवान् अन्गदः च सः |गतम् पारम् समुद्रस्य वानराः च समागताः 
|| ५-१२-९_END
BEGIN_"To me who had gone for the other shore of the ocean what will the old Jambavan say? What would 
that Angada and vanaras who meet say?"_END

B_5_C_9_51
BEGIN_
ववल्गुः च अत्र कासांचित् कुण्डलानि शुभ अर्चिषाम् |
मुख मारुत संसर्गान् मन्दम् मन्दम् सुयोषिताम् || ५-९-५६_END
BEGIN_
Here ear-rings of some beautiful women with a good glory, also moved lightly due to
the air from breathing of those women._END

B_5_C_10_44
BEGIN_आश्पोटयाम् आस चुचुम्ब पुच्चम् |ननन्द चिक्रीड जगौ जगाम|स्तम्भान् अरोहन् निपपात भूमौ 
|निदर्शयन् स्वाम् प्रक्र्तिम् कपीनाम् || ५-१०-५४_END
BEGIN_He clasped his arms, kissed his tail he was delighted, he was playful, sang, paced showing his 
simian nature, climbed pillars and fell down on land._END

B_5_C_13_1
BEGIN_सम्परिक्रम्य हनुमान् रावणस्य निवेशनान् |अदृष्ट्वा जानकीम् सीताम् अब्रवीद् वचनम् कपिः || 
५-१३-२_END
BEGIN_The simian Hanuma went far from the house of Ravana and not seeing Seetha, the daughter of King 
Janaka, said these words:_END

B_5_C_11_37
BEGIN_यस्य सत्त्वस्य या योनिः तस्याम् तत् परिमार्ग्यते || ५-११-४३न शक्यम् प्रमदा नष्टा मृगीषु 
परिमार्गितुम् |_END
BEGIN_"To an animal of whatever race that animal is searched in that race; a woman missing is not possible 
to be searched among female deer."_END

B_5_C_1_115
BEGIN_
अस्मिन्लवणतोये च प्रक्षिप्तः प्लवगोत्तम |
गुप्तपक्षसमग्रश्च तव पित्राभिरक्षितः || ५-१-१२७_END
BEGIN_
"O best among vanaras! With saved full wings, being thrown down into this salt
ocean, I have been protected by your father."_END

B_5_C_12_9
BEGIN_अनिर्वेदः श्रियो मूलम् अनिर्वेदः परम् सुखम् |अनिर्वेदो हि सततम् सर्व अर्थेषु प्रवर्तकः 
|| ५-१२-१०_END
BEGIN_"Non-depression is root of development. Absence of despondency is the greatest comfort. Self reliance 
always is indeed the promoter in all matters."_END

B_5_C_9_52
BEGIN_
शर्कर आसव गन्धः स प्रक्ऱ्त्या सुरभिः सुखः |
तासाम् वदन निह्श्वासः सिषेवे रावणम् तदा || ५-९-५७_END
BEGIN_
Then comforting breath from the faces of those women, by nature fragrant with the
smell of liquor made of Sarkara, served Ravana._END

B_5_C_13_2
BEGIN_भूयिष्ठम् लोडिता लन्का रामस्य चरता प्रियम् |न हि पश्यामि वैदेहीम् सीताम् सर्व अन्ग शोभनाम् 
|| ५-१३-३_END
BEGIN_"The city of Lanka has been mostly explored by me attempting for the pleasure of Rama. But I am 
unable to see Seetha, beautiful in all limbs, and the daughter of Videha."_END

B_5_C_1_116
BEGIN_
ततोऽहं मानयामि त्वां मान्यो हि मम मारुतः |
त्वया मे ह्येष संबन्धः कपिमुख्य महागुणः || ५-१-१२८_END
BEGIN_
"O chief among vanaras! Vayu is thus indeed respectable to me. For that reason I am
respecting you. My this relationship with you has great virtues."_END

B_5_C_11_38
BEGIN_तद् इदम् मार्गितम् तावत् शुद्धेन मनसा मया || ५-११-४४रावण अन्तः पुरम् सरम् दृश्यते न च 
जानकी |_END
BEGIN_"For that reason all this Ravana's house has been search by me with a pure mind Seetha alone cannot 
be seen."_END

B_5_C_12_10
BEGIN_करोति सफलम् जन्तोः कर्म यच् च करोति सः |तस्माद् अनिर्वेद क्ऱ्तम् यत्नम् चेष्टे अहम् उत्तमम् 
|| ५-१२-११अदृष्टामः च विचेष्यामि देशान् रावण पालितान् |_END
BEGIN_"Whatever action a human does that action of man is made to be successful by non-depression. For 
that reason I will perform a best effort together with non-depression. I will search all those regions ruled by 
Ravana not yet seen."_END

B_5_C_9_53
BEGIN_
रावण आनन शन्काः च काश्चिद् रावण योषितः |
मुखानि स्म सपत्नीनाम् उपाजिघ्रन् पुनः पुनः || ५-९-५८_END
BEGIN_
Some women of Ravana smelled co-wives' faces again and again imagining them to be
face of Ravana._END

B_5_C_1_117
BEGIN_
अस्मिन्नेवंगते कार्ये सागरस्य ममैव च |
प्रीतिं प्रीतमनाः कर्तुं त्वमर्हसि महाकपे || ५-१-१२९_END
BEGIN_
"O great Vanara! Because this matter is like this, you are suitable to make myself
and Sagara happy, with a gladdened heart."_END

B_5_C_13_3
BEGIN_पल्वलानि तटाकानि सरांसि सरितः तथा |नद्यो अनूपवन अन्ताः च दुर्गाः च धरणी धराः || ५-१३-४
लोडिता वसुधा सर्वा न च पश्यामि जानकीम् |_END
BEGIN_"All earth consisting of pools, ponds, lakes and streams, rivers and forest areas filled with water, 
mountains difficult of access have been explored but I did not see Seetha."_END

B_5_C_11_39
BEGIN_देव गन्धर्व कन्याः च नाग कन्याः च वीर्यवान् || ५-११-४५अवेक्षमाणो हनुमान् न एव अपश्यत जानकीम् 
|_END
BEGIN_The strong Hanuma observing girls from devas, gandharvas and girls from nagas did not see Janaki._END

B_5_C_12_11
BEGIN_आपान शाला विचिताः तथा पुष्प गृहाणि च || ५-१२-१२चित्र शालाः च विचिता भूयः क्रीडा गृहाणि 
च |निष्कुट अन्तर रथ्याः च विमानानि च सर्वशः || ५-१२-१३_END
BEGIN_"Bars have been searched; in the same way flower houses, art houses have been searched; again pleasure 
houses, pathways in the middle of gardens, buildings in all directions have been searched."_END

B_5_C_9_54
BEGIN_
अत्यर्थम् सक्त मनसो रावणे ता वर स्त्रियः |
अस्वतन्त्राः सपत्नीनाम् प्रियम् एव आचरमः तदा || ५-९-५९_END
BEGIN_
Those best women with greatly devoted mind in Ravana, then not being on own will,
brought delight only to their co-wives._END

B_5_C_13_4
BEGIN_इह सम्पातिना सीता रावणस्य निवेशने || ५-१३-५आख्याता गृध्र राजेन न च पश्यामि ताम् अहम् |_END
BEGIN_"It has been said by the eagle King Sampati that Seetha is here in the house of Ravana. I am unable 
to see her."_END

B_5_C_1_118
BEGIN_
श्रमं मोक्षय पूजां च गृहाण कपिसत्तम |
प्रीतिं च बहुमन्यस्व प्रीतोऽस्मि तव दर्शनात् || ५-१-१३०_END
BEGIN_
"O best among Vanaras! Reduce your fatigue. Accept our worship also. Respect our
love. I am happy by your manifestation."_END

B_5_C_11_40
BEGIN_ताम् अपश्यन् कपिः तत्र पश्यमः च अन्या वर स्त्रियः || ५-११-४६अपक्रम्य तदा वीरः प्रध्यातुम् 
उपचक्रमे |_END
BEGIN_The powerful Hanuma not seeing Her there and seeing other best women then started to think deeply 
going far from there._END

B_5_C_12_12
BEGIN_इति संचिन्त्य भूयो अपि विचेतुम् उपचक्रमे |भूमी गृहामः चैत्य गृहान् गृह अतिगृहकान् अपि 
|| ५-१२-१४_END
BEGIN_Thus thinking Hanuma began to search again undergrounds, houses at the beginning of street intersections 
and also small houses faraway from the main houses._END

B_5_C_9_55
BEGIN_
बाहून् उपनिधाय अन्याः पारिहार्य विभूषिताः |
अंशुकानि च रम्याणि प्रमदाः तत्र शिश्यिरे || ५-९-६०_END
BEGIN_
Some other women slept there, making as pillows their arms decorated with bracelets
and beautiful clothes._END

B_5_C_13_5
BEGIN_किम् नु सीता अथ वैदेही मैथिली जनक आत्मजा || ५-१३-६उपतिष्ठेत विवशा रावणम् दुष्ट चारिणम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise Seetha belonging to Videha born in Mithila and daughter of king Janaka - Can she be 
helplessly together with the evil minded Ravana."_END

B_5_C_1_119
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तः कपिश्रेष्ठस्तं नगोत्तममब्रवीत् |
प्रीतोऽस्मि कृतमातिथ्यं मन्युरेषोऽपनीयताम् || १५-१-१३१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma listening to the best mountain's words, spoke thus : "I am happy. Hospitality
has been done. Let this ill feeling be removed."_END

B_5_C_11_41
BEGIN_स भूयस्तु परम् श्रीमान् मारुतिर्यत्नमास्थितः || ५-११-४७अपानभूमिमुत्सृज्य तद्विचेतुम् प्रचक्रमे 
|_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma the glorious one adopting a great task again left that bar and began to search that 
house._END

B_5_C_12_13
BEGIN_उत्पतन् निपतमः च अपि तिष्ठन् गच्चन् पुनः क्वचित् |अपावृण्वमः च द्वाराणि कपाटानि अवघट्टयन् 
|| ५-१२-१५प्रविशन् निष्पतमः च अपि प्रपतन्न् उत्पतन्न् अपि |सर्वम् अपि अवकाशम् स विचचार महा कपिः || ५-१२-१६_END
BEGIN_The great Hanuma flying again and again and jumping down, standing up, walking, opening doors, 
pushing doors and entering inside, coming out, climbing down, climbing up wandered all opportunity._END

B_5_C_9_56
BEGIN_
अन्या वक्षसि च अन्यस्याः तस्याः काचित् पुनर् भुजम् |
अपरा त्व् अन्कम् अन्यस्याः तस्याः च अपि अपरा भुजौ || ५-९-६१_END
BEGIN_
Another woman slept on another's bosom, again another woman slept on her shoulder,
another woman slept on another woman's thigh and another slept on her breasts._END

B_5_C_13_6
BEGIN_क्षिप्रम् उत्पततो मन्ये सीताम् आदाय रक्षसः || ५-१३-७बिभ्यतो राम बाणानाम् अन्तरा पतिता 
भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"I think while Ravana fearing Rama's arrows flew quickly carrying Seetha, she might have fallen 
down in the middle of the journey."_END

B_5_C_1_120
BEGIN_
त्वरते कार्यकालो मे अहश्चाप्यतिवर्तते |
प्रतिज्ञा च मया दत्ता न स्थातव्यमिहान्त्तरे || ५-१-१३२_END
BEGIN_
"The time to perform my duty is hastening me. The day too is passing. A promise has
also been given by me. I should not stand here in the middle neglecting my duty."_END

B_5_C_12_14
BEGIN_चतुर् अन्गुल मात्रो अपि न अवकाशः स विद्यते |रावण अन्तः पुरे तस्मिन् यम् कपिर् न जगाम सः 
|| ५-१२-१७_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma in that city of Ravana - whatever region he did not go that region was not there even 
for four angulas._END

B_5_C_9_57
BEGIN_
ऊरु पार्श्व कटी प्ऱ्ष्ठम् अन्योन्यस्य समाश्रिताः |
परस्पर निविष्ट अन्ग्यो मद स्नेह वश अनुगाः || ५-९-६२_END
BEGIN_
Overcome with heat and friendship, they resorted to thighs, sides, waist and back of
one another, with mutual limbs placed on one another._END

B_5_C_14_0
BEGIN_स मुहूर्तम् इव ध्यत्वा मनसा च अधिगम्य ताम् |अवप्लुतो महा तेजाः प्राकारम् तस्य वेश्मनः 
|| ५-१४-१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma with great resplendence thought for a moment, obtained that Ashoka garden by mind and 
jumped from the compound wall of that house._END

B_5_C_13_7
BEGIN_अथवा ह्रियमाणायाः पथि सिद्ध निषेविते || ५-१३-८मन्ये पतितम् आर्याया हृदयम् प्रेक्ष्य सागरम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Or I think the heart of the noble Seetha being stolen in the path served by Siddhas must have 
sunk at the site of the ocean."_END

B_5_C_1_121
BEGIN_
इत्युक्त्वा पाणिना शैलमालभ्य हरिपुङ्गवः |
जगामाकाशमाविश्य वीर्यवान् प्रहसन्निव || ५-१-१३३_END
BEGIN_
The courageous Hanuma saying thus, touched the mountain with His hand, entered the
sky and flew on with a smile._END

B_5_C_12_15
BEGIN_प्राकर अन्तर रथ्याः च वेदिकः चैत्य संश्रयाः |श्वभ्राः च पुष्करिण्यः च सर्वम् तेन अवलोकितम् 
|| ५-१२-१८_END
BEGIN_Streets between fort walls, platforms together with the intersection of four streets, wells, lakes 
all these had been seen by him._END

B_5_C_9_58
BEGIN_
अन्योन्यस्य अन्ग संस्पर्शात् प्रीयमाणाः सुमध्यमाः |
एकी क्ऱ्त भुजाः सर्वाः सुषुपुः तत्र योषितः
अन्योन्य भुज सूत्रेण स्त्री माला ग्रथिता हि सा |
माला इव ग्रथिता सूत्रे शुशुभे मत्त षट्पदा || ५-९-६३_END
BEGIN_
That garland of women tied with the rope of each other's shoulders shone like a
flower garland with dragon flies on it tied in thread._END

B_5_C_14_1
BEGIN_स तु सम्हृष्ट सर्व अन्गः प्राकारस्थो महा कपिः |पुष्पित अग्रान् वसन्त आदौ ददर्श विविधान् 
द्रुमान् || ५-१४-२सालान् अशोकान् भव्यामः च चम्पकामः च सुपुष्पितान् |उद्दालकान् नाग वृक्षामः चूतान् कपि 
मुखान् अपि || ५-१४-३_END
BEGIN_That great Hanuma with joyful limbs, being on enclosure wall saw various trees such as Sal, beautiful 
Ashoka, Champaka full of flowers, Uddalaka, Naga, mango trees with their fruit in the colour of the snout of a 
monkey, in full blossom at the start of the spring._END

B_5_C_13_8
BEGIN_रावणस्य ऊरु वेगेन भुजाभ्याम् पीडितेन च || ५-१३-९तया मन्ये विशाल अक्ष्या त्यक्तम् जीवितम् 
आर्यया |_END
BEGIN_"I think due to great speed of Ravana and due to the torture of Ravana's shoulders the life has 
been given up by that noble one with wide eyes."_END

B_5_C_1_122
BEGIN_
स पर्वतसमुद्राभ्यां बहुमानादवेक्षितः |
पूजितश्चोपपन्नाभिराशीर्भिरनिलात्मजः || ५-१-१३४_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma was thus seen with great respect by the ocean and the mountain, and also
worshipped with suitable blessings._END

B_5_C_12_16
BEGIN_राक्षस्यो विविध आकारा विरूपा विकृताः तथा |दृष्टा हनूमता तत्र न तु सा जनक आत्मजा || ५-१२-१९_END
BEGIN_Rakshasa women of various forms, with crooked forms and horrific forms had been seen there by Hanuma 
but not that Seetha._END

B_5_C_14_2
BEGIN_अथ आम्र वण संचन्नाम् लता शत समावृताम् |ज्या मुक्त इव नाराचः पुप्लुवे वृक्ष वाटिकाम् || 
५-१४-४_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Hanuma flew like a Naracha arrow released from bow string, toward the garden covered 
by mango trees and surrounded by hundreds of creepers._END

B_5_C_9_59
BEGIN_
लतानाम् माधवे मासि फुल्लानाम् वायु सेवनात् |
अन्योन्य माला ग्रथितम् संसक्त कुसुम उच्चयम् || ५-९-६४
व्यतिवेष्टित सुस्कन्थम् अन्योन्य भ्रमर आकुलम् |
आसीद् वनम् इव उद्धूतम् स्त्री वनम् रावणस्य तत् || ५-९-६५_END
BEGIN_
That group of women of Ravana, tied by each other as garland with mixed group of
flowers, with beautiful shoulders entwined promiscuously, hair like an exalted garden with a flower
garland tied together of creepers in bloom due to the caress of the lord of wind in the vernal in
the month of Vaisakha, with entwined beautiful trees._END

B_5_C_13_9
BEGIN_उपरि उपरि वा नूनम् सागरम् क्रमतः तदा || ५-१३-१०विवेष्टमाना पतिता समुद्रे जनक आत्मजा |_END
BEGIN_"Then while being flown upon the surface of the ocean, Seetha definitely fell down in the ocean 
while wriggling."_END

B_5_C_1_123
BEGIN_
अथोर्ध्वं दूरमुत्प्लुत्य हित्वा शैलमहार्णवौ |
पितुः पन्थानमास्थाय जगाम विमलेऽम्बरे || १-५-१३५_END
BEGIN_
After that leaving the mountain and the great ocean, and flying up far into the
clear sky, Hanuma followed the path of his father._END

B_5_C_12_17
BEGIN_रूपेण अप्रतिमा लोके वरा विद्या धर स्त्रियः |दृटा हनूमता तत्र न तु राघव नन्दिनी || ५-१२-२०_END
BEGIN_The best Vidhyadhara women incomparable by beauty in the world had been seen there by Hanuma, but 
not Seetha._END

B_5_C_14_3
BEGIN_स प्रविष्य विचित्राम् ताम् विहगैर् अभिनादिताम् |राजतैः कान्चनैः चैव पादपैः सर्वतो वृताम् 
|| ५-१४-५विहगैर् मृग सम्घैः च विचित्राम् चित्र काननाम् |उदित आदित्य सम्काशाम् ददर्श हनुमान् कपिः || ५-१४-६
वृताम् नाना विधैर् वृक्षैः पुष्प उपग फल उपगैः |कोकिलैर् भृन्ग राजैः च मत्तैर् नित्य निषेविताम् || ५-१४-७
प्रहृष्ट मनुजे कले मृग पक्षि समाकुले |मत्त बर्हिण सम्घुष्टाम् नाना द्विज गण आयुताम् || ५-१४-८_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma the simian, saw on entering that garden filled with happy humans, animals and birds 
with varied hues during spring, resounded by birds, with trees made of silver, made of gold, surrounded everywhere 
by birds and groups of animals; wonderful with wonderful trees equaling the Sun at sunrise together with trees 
of various kinds which obtained flowers and fruits, served daily by Cuckoos and by dragon flies, resounded by 
peacocks in heat and with groups of birds of various kinds._END

B_5_C_9_60
BEGIN_
उचितेष्व् अपि सुव्यक्तम् न तासाम् योषिताम् तदा |
विवेकः शक्य आधातुम् भूषण अन्ग अम्बर स्रजाम् || ५-९-६६_END
BEGIN_
Then it was not possible to make clear the knowledge of jewellery, body parts and
clothes of those women even for those used to them._END

B_5_C_13_10
BEGIN_आहो क्षुद्रेण च अनेन रक्षन्ती शीलम् आत्मनः || ५-१३-११अबन्धुर् भक्षिता सीता रावणेन तपस्विनी 
|_END
BEGIN_"Or has the austere Seetha been eaten by this Ravana, the evil minded one while she was protecting 
her chastity without any relatives near her."_END

B_5_C_1_124
BEGIN_
भूयश्चोर्ध्वं गतिं प्राप्य गिरिं तमवलोकयन् |
वायुसूनुर्निरालम्बे जगाम विमलेऽम्बरे || १-५-१३६_END
BEGIN_
The son of Vayu obtained the speed to fly still higher into the sky and seeing that
mountain below, went in the clear sky which had no support._END

B_5_C_12_18
BEGIN_नाग कन्या वर आरोहाः पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ आननाः |दृष्टा हनूमता तत्र न तु सीता सुमध्यमा || ५-१२-२१_END
BEGIN_Naaga women with beautiful buttocks, with faces equaling full moon had been seen by Hanuma there, 
but not Seetha with a beautiful waist._END

B_5_C_14_4
BEGIN_मार्गमाणो वर आरोहाम् राज पुत्रीम् अनिन्दिताम् |सुख प्रसुप्तान् विहगान् बोधयाम् आस वानरः 
|| ५-१४-९_END
BEGIN_Hanuma searching the royal daughter Seetha with excellent limbs and without blame, woke up birds 
in comfortable sleep._END

B_5_C_9_61
BEGIN_
रावणे सुख सम्विष्टे ताः स्त्रियो विविध प्रभाः |
ज्वलन्तः कान्चना दीपाः प्रेक्षन्त अनिमिषा इव || ५-९-६७_END
BEGIN_
While Ravana slept comfortably, golden lamps shining brilliant, were as though
seeing without closing eyes, those women of various glows._END

B_5_C_13_11
BEGIN_अथवा राक्षस इन्द्रस्य पत्नीभिर् असित ईक्षणा || ५-१३-१२अदुष्टा दुष्ट भावाभिर् भक्षिता सा 
भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise not being evil with black eyes, She may have been eaten by the wives of Ravana with 
evil thoughts."_END

B_5_C_1_125
BEGIN_
तद्द्वितीयं हनुमतो दृष्ट्वा कर्म सुदुष्करम् |
प्रश्शंसुः सुराः सर्वे सिद्धाश्च परमर्षयः || १-५-१३७_END
BEGIN_
Seeing Hanuma perform that very difficult second task (first one being the flight
over ocean), all Devas, Siddhas and great sages praised Him._END

B_5_C_12_19
BEGIN_प्रमथ्य राक्षस इन्द्रेण नाग कन्या बलाद्द् हृताः |दृष्टा हनूमता तत्र न सा जनक नन्दिनी || 
५-१२-२२_END
BEGIN_Naaga women who had been stolen forcefully, being defeated by Ravana had been seen there by Hanuma, 
not that Seetha_END

B_5_C_14_5
BEGIN_उत्पतद्भिर् द्विज गणैः पक्षैः सालाः समाहताः |अनेक वर्णा विविधा मुमुचुः पुष्प वृष्टयः || 
५-१४-१०_END
BEGIN_Trees hit by wings of groups of birds in flight shed showers of flowers of various colours and 
of various kinds._END

B_5_C_9_62
BEGIN_
राज ऱ्षि पित्ऱ् दैत्यानाम् गन्धर्वाणाम् च योषितः |
रक्षसाम् च अभवन् कन्याः तस्य काम वशम् गताः || ५-९-६८_END
BEGIN_
Women of royal sages, brahmanas and demons and of Gandharvas, of Rakshasas - all
those unmarried girls surrendered from lust to Ravana._END

B_5_C_13_12
BEGIN_सम्पूर्ण चन्द्र प्रतिमम् पद्म पत्र निभ ईक्षणम् || ५-१३-१३रामस्य ध्यायती वक्त्रम् पन्चत्वम् 
कृपणा गता |_END
BEGIN_"The pitiable Seetha equaling full moon, with eyes equaling lotus petals must have obtained death 
while meditating upon Rama's face."_END

B_5_C_1_126
BEGIN_
देवताश्चाभवन् हृष्टास्तत्रस्थास्तस्य कर्मणा |
काञ्चनस्य सुनाभस्य सहस्राक्षश्च वासवः || १-५-१३८_END
BEGIN_
Devas and the thousand eyed Devendra who were there, became happy by the task of
that golden hued Mainaka._END

B_5_C_12_20
BEGIN_सो अपश्यमः ताम् महा बाहुः पश्यमः च अन्या वर स्त्रियः |विषसाद महा बाहुर् हनूमान् मारुत 
आत्मजः || ५-१२-२३_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma with great arms, the wise one, the son of Vayu not seeing that Seetha and seeing other 
women became depressed again and again._END

B_5_C_14_6
BEGIN_पुष्प अवकीर्णः शुशुभे हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः |अशोक वनिका मध्ये यथा पुष्पमयो गिरिः || ५-१४-११_END
BEGIN_The son of Lord Vayu, Hanuma sprinkled with flowers shone like a mountain of flowers in the middle 
of Ashoka garden._END

B_5_C_9_63
BEGIN_
युद्धकामेन ताः सर्वा रावणेन हृताः स्त्रियः |
समदा मदनेनैव मोहिताः काश्चिदागताः || ५-९-६९_END
BEGIN_
All those women had been stolen by Ravana with a desire for war, some together with
heat of youth obtained Ravana being desired by god of love._END

B_5_C_13_13
BEGIN_हा राम लक्ष्मण इति एव हा अयोध्येति च मैथिली || ५-१३-१४विलप्य बहु वैदेही न्यस्त देहा भविष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_"The daughter of Videha, Seetha. �O Rama!' �O Lakshmana!' �O Ayodhya!', thus weeping greatly may 
have given up her body."_END

B_5_C_1_127
BEGIN_
उवाच वचनं धीमान् परितोषात्सगद्गदम् |
सुनाभं पर्वतश्रेष्ठं स्वयमेव शचीपतिः || १-५-१३९_END
BEGIN_
The wise Devendra himself spoke these words through faltering tones due to extreme
happiness, to Mainaka, the best among mountains._END

B_5_C_12_21
BEGIN_उद्योगम् वानर इन्द्राणम् प्लवनम् सागरस्य च |व्यर्थम् वीक्ष्य अनिल सुतः चिन्ताम् पुनर् 
उपागमत् || ५-१२-२४_END
BEGIN_Seeing the effort of the best Vanaras and the crossing of ocean as being wasted, Hanuma got depression 
again._END

B_5_C_14_7
BEGIN_दिशः सर्व अभिदावन्तम् वृक्ष षण्ड गतम् कपिम् |द्ऱ्ष्ट्वा सर्वाणि भूतानि वसन्त इति मेनिरे 
|| ५-१४-१२_END
BEGIN_Seeing Hanuma running in all directions and being in the middle of trees, all living creatures 
thought Him to be Vasanta, the lord of spring._END

B_5_C_9_64
BEGIN_
न तत्र काचित् प्रमदा प्रसह्य |
वीर्य उपपन्नेन गुणेन लब्धा |
न च अन्य कामा अपि न च अन्य पूर्वा |
