विना वर अर्हाम् जनक आत्मजाम् तु || ५-९-७०_END
BEGIN_
There, even one woman had not been obtained forcefully by the strong Ravana, except
for that daughter of Janaka, Seetha. Every other woman had been obtained by her character alone and
there was no woman who had desire in another man, and there also was none with another lover._END

B_5_C_13_14
BEGIN_अथवा निहिता मन्ये रावणस्य निवेशने || ५-१३-१५नूनम् लालप्यते मन्दम् पन्जरस्था इव शारिका 
|_END
BEGIN_"I think otherwise being put in the house of Ravana Seetha is definitely crying like a caged myna."_END

B_5_C_1_128
BEGIN_
हिरण्यनाभ शैलेन्द्र परितुष्टोऽस्मि ते भृशम् |
अभयं ते प्रयच्छामि तिष्ठ सौम्य यथासुखम् || ५-१-१४०_END
BEGIN_
"O Mainaka, the king of mountains! I am very happy with you. O gentle one! I am
giving protection to you. Proceed according to your comfort."_END

B_5_C_12_22
BEGIN_अवतीर्य विमानाच् च हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |चिन्ताम् उपजगाम अथ शोक उपहत चेतनः || ५-१२-२५_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the son of Vayu Hanuma got down from Pushpaka, obtained thought with a mind overcome 
with grief._END

B_5_C_15_0
BEGIN_स वीक्षमाणः तत्रस्थो मार्गमाणः च मैथिलीम् |अवेक्षमाणः च महीम् सर्वाम् ताम् अन्ववैक्षत 
	|| ५-१५-१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma being there, seeing and searching for Seetha, observing all that land, explored 
	the garden._END

B_5_C_14_8
BEGIN_वृक्षेभ्यः पतितैः पुष्पैर् अवकीर्णा पृथग् विधैः |रराज वसुधा तत्र प्रमदा इव विभूषिता || 
५-१४-१३_END
BEGIN_There the Earth sprinkled by flowers of various kinds which fell down from trees shone like a well 
decorated woman._END

B_5_C_9_65
BEGIN_
न च अकुलीना न च हीन रूपा |
न अदक्षिणा न अनुपचार युक्ता |
भार्या अभवत् तस्य न हीन सत्त्वा |
न च अपि कान्तस्य न कामनीया || ५-९-७१_END
BEGIN_
And there was no wife of his without a good lineage, there was no one with less
beauty, no one without skill, no one without service, none with low intellect, no one without
causing desire to lover._END

B_5_C_13_15
BEGIN_जनकस्य कुले जाता राम पत्नी सुमध्यमा || ५-१३-१६कथम् उत्पल पत्र अक्षी रावणस्य वशम् व्रजेत् 
|_END
BEGIN_"How can the daughter of King Janaka, Rama's wife Seetha with a beautiful waist, with eyes like 
black lotus petals obtain Ravana's capture."_END

B_5_C_1_129
BEGIN_
साह्यं ते सुमहद्विक्रान्तस्य हनूमतः |
क्रमतो योजनशतं निर्भयस्य भये सति || ५-१-१४१_END
BEGIN_
To the dauntless Hanuma crossing hundred yojanas, who is fearless even when there is
reason to be afraid, a great help has been done by you._END

B_5_C_15_1
BEGIN_सन्तान कलताभिः च पादपैर् उपशोभिताम् |दिव्य गन्ध रस उपेताम् सर्वतः समलम्कृताम् || ५-१५-२
	ताम् स नन्दन सम्काशाम् मृग पक्षिभिर् आवृताम् |हर्म्य प्रासाद सम्बाधाम् कोकिल आकुल निह्स्वनाम् || ५-१५-३
	कान्चन उत्पल पद्माभिः वापीभिः उपशोभिताम् |बह्व आसन कुथा उपेताम् बहु भूमि गृह आयुताम् || ५-१५-४सर्व 
	ऋतु कुसुमैः रम्यैः फलवद्भिः च पादपैः |पुष्पितानाम् अशोकानाम् श्रिया सूर्य उदय प्रभाम् || ५-१५-५प्रदीप्ताम् 
	इव तत्रस्थो मारुतिः समुदैक्षत |निष्पत्र शाखाम् विहगैः क्रियमाणाम् इव असकृत् || ५-१५-६विनिष्पतद्भिः 
	शतशः चित्रैः पुष्प अवतंसकैः |आमूल पुष्प निचितैर् अशोकैः शोक नाशनैः || ५-१५-७पुष्प भार अतिभारैः च स्पृशद्भिर् 
	इव मेदिनीम् |कर्णिकारैः कुसुमितैः किंशुकैः च सुपुष्पितैः || ५-१५-८_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma being there observed closely that Ashoka garden shone by Santanaka creepers, Santana 
	trees with heavenly aroma and juice, well decorated in all directions equalling the garden of Nandana, surrounded 
	by animals and birds, congested with mansions and palaces, resounded with the notes of cuckoos, decorated 
	with wells having golden water lilies, lotuses and with many chairs and carpets; with many sub-terrain houses, 
	beautiful trees, with trees with flowers of all seasons and with fruit, with the radiance of raising sun, 
	by the glory of ashoka trees in bloom, as though radiant as though being made to be with branches without 
	leaves, by hundreds of birds perching again and again, Ashoka trees with wonderful flowers as head decoration, 
	with flowers spread till the roots destroying leaves, with weight of groups of flowers as touching the earth 
	with karnolaara trees; in blossom with Kimkusa trees in full blossom._END

B_5_C_14_9
BEGIN_तरस्विना ते तरवः तरसा अभिप्रकम्पिताः |कुसुमानि विचित्राणि सस्ऱ्जुः कपिना तदा || ५-१४-१४_END
BEGIN_Then those trees, shaken by the might of Hanuma the mighty one, showered wonderful flowers._END

B_5_C_9_66
BEGIN_
बभूव बुद्धिः तु हरि ईश्वरस्य |
यदि ईद्ऱ्शी राघव धर्म पत्नी |
इमा यथा राक्षस राज भार्याः |
सुजातम् अस्य इति हि साधु बुद्धेः || ५-९-७२_END
BEGIN_
Following thought occurred to Hanuma with a pious mind : "It would have been good
for this Ravana if the virtuous wife of Rama had been left happy with her husband in the same such
manner as these wives of the king of rakshasas."_END

B_5_C_13_16
BEGIN_विनष्टा वा प्रनष्टा वा मृता वा जनक आत्मजा || ५-१३-१७रामस्य प्रिय भार्यस्य न निवेदयितुम् 
क्षमम् |_END
BEGIN_"It is not fair to let know Rama who has a dear wife if Seetha is lost or is not to be seen or 
has died."_END

B_5_C_1_130
BEGIN_
रामस्यैष हितायैव याति दाशरथेर्हरिः |
सत्क्रियां कुर्वता तस्य तोषितोऽस्मि दृढं त्वया || ५-१-१४२_END
BEGIN_
This Vanara Hanuma is going for the benefit of Sri Rama, the son of Dasaratha. I am
very happy with you who is doing respect to Him._END

B_5_C_15_2
BEGIN_स देशः प्रभया तेषाम् प्रदीप्त इव सर्वतः |पुम्नागाः सप्त पर्णाः च चम्पक उद्दालकाः तथा 
	|| ५-१५-९विवृद्ध मूला बहवः शोभन्ते स्म सुपुष्पिताः |_END
BEGIN_By the radiance of those trees that region was as though lit in all directions. Punnaaga trees 
	with flatted roots and in full blossom, Saptaparna trees Campaka and Uddalaka trees were shining._END

B_5_C_14_10
BEGIN_निर्धूत पत्र शिखराः शीर्ण पुष्प फल द्रुमाः |निक्षिप्त वस्त्र आभरणा धूर्ता इव पराजिताः 
|| ५-१४-१५_END
BEGIN_The trees with their branches, removed leaves with fallen down fruits and flowers were like defeated 
gamblers with their clothes and jewellery kept down._END

B_5_C_9_67
BEGIN_
पुनः च सो अचिन्तयद् आर्त रूपो |
ध्रुवम् विशिष्टा गुणतो हि सीता |
अथ अयम् अस्याम् क्ऱ्तवान् महात्मा |
लन्का ईश्वरः कष्टम् अनार्य कर्म || ५-९-७३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma became gloomy and thought thus: "Seetha is definitely the best by virtues;
then this lord of Lanka even though being great otherwise, did an evil and an un-gentlemanly deed
with her._END

B_5_C_13_17
BEGIN_निवेद्यमाने दोषः स्याद् दोषः स्याद् अनिवेदने || ५-१३-१८कथम् नु खलु कर्तव्यम् विषमम् प्रतिभाति 
मे |_END
BEGIN_"To be let known becomes an error; not to let know becomes an error how to perform the duty? To 
me this seems dire situation."_END

B_5_C_1_131
BEGIN_
ततः प्रहर्षमगमद्विपुलं पर्वतोत्तमः |
देवतानां पतिं दृष्ट्वा परितुष्टं शतक्रतुम् || ५-१-१४३_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, the best among mountains obtained great happiness on seeing Devendra,
the lord of Devas being happy._END

B_5_C_15_3
BEGIN_शात कुम्भ निभाः केचित् केचिद् अग्नि शिख उपमाः || ५-१५-१०नील अन्जन निभाः केचित् तत्र 
	अशोकाः सहस्रशः |_END
BEGIN_There in that garden of Ashoka there were thousands of Ashoka trees some equalling gold, some 
	equalling fire, some equalling the precious stone Niila and Anjana._END

B_5_C_14_11
BEGIN_हनूमता वेगवता कम्पिताः ते नग उत्तमाः |पुष्प पर्ण फलानि आशु मुमुचुः पुष्प शालिनः || ५-१४-१६_END
BEGIN_The excellent trees shining with best flowers fell down instantly flowers, leaves and fruits._END

B_5_C_13_18
BEGIN_अस्मिन्न् एवम् गते कर्ये प्राप्त कालम् क्षमम् च किम् || ५-१३-१९भवेद् इति मतिम् भूयो हनुमान् 
प्रविचारयन् |_END
BEGIN_"This task while it goes this way the time is approaching. What becomes appropriate" thus Hanuma 
thought again this view point._END

B_5_C_1_132
BEGIN_
स वै दत्तवरः शैलो बभूवावस्थितस्तदा |
हनुमांश्च मुहूर्तेन व्यतिचक्राम सागरम् || ५-१-१४४_END
BEGIN_
Then that mountain with a given boon from Devendra stood still there. Hanuma also
leaped over that part of the ocean in an instant._END

B_5_C_15_4
BEGIN_नन्दनम् विविध उद्यानम् चित्रम् चैत्ररथम् यथा || ५-१५-११अतिवृत्तम् इव अचिन्त्यम् दिव्यम् 
	रम्यम् श्रिया वृतम् |द्वितीयम् इव च आकाशम् पुष्प ज्योतिर् गण आयुतम् || ५-१५-१२पुष्प रत्न शतैः चित्रम् 
	पन्चमम् सागरम् यथा |सर्व ऋतु पुष्पैर् निचितम् पादपैर् मधु गन्धिभिः || ५-१५-१३नाना निनादैः उद्यानम् 
	रम्यम् मृग गणैर् द्विजैः |अनेक गन्ध प्रवहम् पुण्य गन्धम् मनो रमम् || ५-१५-१४_END
BEGIN_Like the garden of Nandana, a celestial garden, wonderful like Caitraratham, a garden of Kubera, 
	surpassing all, unfathomable, an excellent one, a beautiful one consisting of glory together with flowers 
	like clusters of stars, like a second sky wonderful with flowers, like hundreds of diamonds, like a second 
	ocean with flowers of all seasons, spread with trees having the smell of honey, beautiful with groups of animals 
	of various sounds, diffused with many smells with an auspicious soul pleasing smell._END

B_5_C_14_12
BEGIN_विहम्ग सम्घैर् हीनाः ते स्कन्ध मात्र आश्रया द्रुमाः |बभूवुर् अगमाः सर्वे मारुतेन इव निर्धुताः 
|| ५-१४-१७_END
BEGIN_All those trees losing groups of birds became being a resort to branches only like trees shook 
by wind._END

B_5_C_13_19
BEGIN_यदि सीताम् अदृष्ट्वा अहम् वानर इन्द्र पुरीम् इतः || ५-१३-२०गमिष्यामि ततः को मे पुरुष अर्थो 
भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"If I go towards Sugreeva's city from here without seeing Seetha from that to what avail will this 
effort be?"_END

B_5_C_1_133
BEGIN_
ततो देवाः सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाश्च परमर्षयः |
अब्रूवन् सूर्यसंकाशां सुरसां नागमातरम् || ५-१-१४५_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, Devas together with Gandharvas, Siddhas and great sages spoke thus to
Surasa, the mother of Nagas, equal to the Sun in brilliance._END

B_5_C_15_5
BEGIN_शैल इन्द्रम् इव गन्ध आढ्यम् द्वितीयम् गन्ध मादनम् |अशोक वनिकायाम् तु तस्याम् वानर 
	पुम्गवः || ५-१५-१५स ददर्श अविदूरस्थम् चैत्य प्रासादम् ऊर्जितम् |मध्ये स्तम्भ सहस्रेण स्थितम् कैलास 
	पाण्डुरम् || ५-१५-१६प्रवाल कृत सोपानम् तप्त कान्चन वेदिकम् |मुष्णन्तम् इव चक्षूम्षि द्योतमानम् इव 
	श्रिया || ५-१५-१७विमलम् प्रांशु भावत्वाद् उल्लिखन्तम् इव अम्बरम् |_END
BEGIN_That monkey warrior Hanuma saw not far away in that Ashoka garden, in the middle, a lofty temple 
	filled with fragrance like a second Gandhamadana Mountain, standing by a thousand pillars, white like Mount 
	Kailaasa with stairs made of corals with platforms made of refined gold as though radiant with glory, clear 
	and because of being tall as though scraping the sky._END

B_5_C_14_13
BEGIN_विधूत केशी युवतिर् यथा मृदित वर्णिका |निष्पीत शुभ दन्त ओष्ठी नखैर् दन्तैः च विक्षता || 
५-१४-१८तथा लान्गूल हस्तैः च चरणाभ्याम् च मर्दिता |बभूव अशोक वनिका प्रभग्न वर पादपा || ५-१४-१९_END
BEGIN_Hit by Hanuma's tail, hands and feet, Ashoka garden with broken best trees became like a young 
woman with disturbed hair, with effaced sandal paste, with her auspicious teeth and lips drunk from and wounded 
by nails and by teeth._END

B_5_C_13_20
BEGIN_मम इदम् लन्घनम् व्यर्थम् सागरस्य भविष्यति || ५-१३-२१प्रवेशः चिव लन्काया राक्षसानाम् च 
दर्शनम् |_END
BEGIN_"My crossing of the ocean entering the city of Lanka the site of rakshasas - all this will become 
waste."_END

B_5_C_1_134
BEGIN_
अयं वातात्मजः श्रीमान्प्लवते सागरोपरि |
हनुमान्नाम तस्य त्वं मुहूर्तं विघ्नमाचर || ५-१-१४६
राक्षसं रूपमास्थाय सुघोरं पर्वतोपमम् |
दंष्ट्रकराळं पिङ्गाक्षं वक्त्रं कृत्वा नभःसमम् || ५-१-१४७_END
BEGIN_
"This glorious son of Vayu, going by the name of Hanuma is flying over the ocean.
You obtain a horrible mountain like demonic appearance and make a face with fearful tusks,
red-brown eyes and as vast as the sky, and create an obstacle to Him for an instant."_END

B_5_C_15_6
BEGIN_ततो मलिन सम्वीताम् राक्षसीभिः समावृताम् || ५-१५-१८उपवास कृशाम् दीनाम् निह्श्वसन्तीम् 
	पुनः पुनः |ददर्श शुक्ल पक्ष आदौ चन्द्र रेखाम् इव अमलाम् || ५-१५-१९_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Hanuma saw Seetha wearing a soiled garment, surrounded by rakshasa women, emaciated 
	due to fasting, looking miserable, sighing again and again, like the pure crescent moon at the beginning of 
	a bright fortnight._END

B_5_C_14_14
BEGIN_महा लतानाम् दामानि व्यधमत् तरसा कपिः |यथा प्रावृषि विन्ध्यस्य मेघ जालानि मारुतः || ५-१४-२०_END
BEGIN_Hanuma broke circles of great creepers by His might like the wind during rainy season, breaking 
the groups of clouds of mountain Vindhya._END

B_5_C_13_21
BEGIN_किम् वा वक्ष्यति सुग्रीवो हरयो व समागताः || ५-१३-२२किष्किन्धाम् समनुप्राप्तौ तौ वा दशरथ 
आत्मजौ |_END
BEGIN_"To me reaching Kishkindha what would Sugreeva say or Vanaras there or those sons of Dasharatha 
what would they say?"_END

B_5_C_1_135
BEGIN_
बलमिच्छामहे ज्ञातुं भूयश्चास्य पराक्रमम् |
त्वां विजेष्यत्युपायेन विषादं वा गमिष्यति || ५-१-१४८_END
BEGIN_
"We are desiring to find out if by His strength and also courage and intelligence He
can win over you or obtain sorrow."_END

B_5_C_16_0
BEGIN_प्रशस्य तु प्रशस्तव्याम् सीताम् ताम् हरि पुम्गवः |गुण अभिरामम् रामम् च पुनः चिन्ता परो 
अभवत् || ५-१६-१_END
BEGIN_The best among vanaras praising that Seetha who is fit to be praised, and also praising Sri Rama 
pleasing with His virtues, became immersed in thought again._END

B_5_C_15_7
BEGIN_मन्द प्रख्यायमानेन रूपेण रुचिर प्रभाम् |पिनद्धाम् धूम जालेन शिखाम् इव विभावसोः || 
	५-१५-२०_END
BEGIN_With a form that slowly came out like a tongue of fire, of beautiful radiance covered by smoke._END

B_5_C_14_15
BEGIN_स तत्र मणि भूमीः च राजतीः च मनो रमाः |तथा कान्चन भूमीः च विचरन् ददृशे कपिः || ५-१४-२१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma pacing there saw diamond studded floors, silver inlaid floors, and beautiful gold inlaid 
floors._END

B_5_C_13_22
BEGIN_गत्वा तु यदि काकुत्स्थम् वक्ष्यामि परम् अप्रियम् || ५-१३-२३न दृष्टा इति मया सीता ततः त्यक्ष्यन्ति 
जीवितम् |_END
BEGIN_"Going there by me for Rama, �Seetha has not been seen' - thus if I say a very unpleasant word 
thereafter Rama will give up life."_END

B_5_C_1_136
BEGIN_
एवमुक्ता तु सा देवी दैवतैरभिसत्कृता |
समुद्रमध्ये सुरसा बिभ्रती राक्षसं वपुः || ५-१-१४९
विकृतं च विरूपं च सर्वस्य च भयावहम् |
प्लवमानं हनूमन्तमावृत्येदमुवाच ह || ५-१-१५०_END
BEGIN_
That Goddess Surasa, thus spoken to by Devas and also being respected by them,
wearing a horrible disfigured appearance of a demon in the middle of the ocean which caused fear to
all, and stopping Hanuma who was flying, spoke these words._END

B_5_C_16_1
BEGIN_स मुहूर्तम् इव ध्यात्वा बाष्प पर्याकुलेक्षणः |सीताम् आश्रित्य तेजस्वी हनुमान् विललाप ह 
|| ५-१६-२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma the radiant one thinking for a moment, cried about Seetha and became with eyes tormented 
with tears._END

B_5_C_15_8
BEGIN_पीतेन एकेन सम्वीताम् क्लिष्टेन उत्तम वाससा |सपन्काम् अनलम्काराम् विपद्माम् इव पद्मिनीम् 
	|| ५-१५-२१_END
BEGIN_Covered by a single best cloth of yellow colour, which was wrinkled, without any decorations 
	like a lotus plant without lotuses, together with mud._END

B_5_C_14_16
BEGIN_वापीः च विविध आकाराः पूर्णाः परम वारिणा |महा अर्हैर् मणि सोपानैर् उपपन्नाः ततः ततः || 
५-१४-२२मुक्ता प्रवाल सिकता स्फटिक अन्तर कुट्टिमाः |कान्चनैः तरुभिः चित्रैः तीरजैर् उपशोभिताः || ५-१४-२३
फुल्ल पद्म उत्पल वनाः चक्र वाक उपकूजिताः |नत्यूह रुत सम्घुष्टा हंस सारस नादिताः || ५-१४-२४दीर्घाभिर् द्रुम 
युक्ताभिः सरिद्भिः च समन्ततः |अम्ऱ्त उपम तोयाभिः शिवाभिर् उपसंस्कृताः || ५-१४-२५लता शतैर् अवतताः सन्तानक 
समावृताः |नाना गुल्म आवृत वनाः कर वीर कृत अन्तराः || ५-१४-२६_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw ponds filled with the best waters, together there and there with stairs embedded with 
diamonds of great value, with pearls and corals as sand, with bottoms made of crystal and precious stones, shone 
by trees of golden hue and of wonderful hue at banks containing beds of lotuses in full blossom and lilies, resounded 
by chakravaka birds nearby, sounded by water fowls, resounded by swans and cranes, together with tall trees, with 
nectar like waters, with hundreds of auspicious creepers, covered by the flowers of santaana trees, surrounded 
by various shrubs with middle regions of karaveera and also wells and in various shapes._END

B_5_C_13_23
BEGIN_परुषम् दारुणम् क्रूरम् तीक्ष्णम् इन्द्रिय तापनम् || ५-१३-२४सीता निमित्तम् दुर्वाक्यम् 
श्रुत्वा स न भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing bad word belonging to Seetha that is harsh, horrible, cruel, sharp, sense agonizing, He 
will not exist."_END

B_5_C_1_137
BEGIN_
मम भक्षः प्रदिष्टस्त्वमीश्वरैर्वानरर्षभ |
अहं त्वा भक्षयिष्यामि प्रविशेदं ममाननम् || ५-१-१५१_END
BEGIN_
"O best among Vanaras! You have been given by Devas as my food. I will eat you.
Enter inside my mouth."_END

B_5_C_16_2
BEGIN_मान्या गुरु विनीतस्य लक्ष्मणस्य गुरु प्रिया |यदि सीता अपि दुह्ख आर्ता कालो हि दुरतिक्रमः 
|| ५-१६-३_END
BEGIN_"Respectable to Lakshmana, instructed by teachers, Seetha is also dear to teachers; if She is stricken 
with grief, destiny is indeed difficult to withstand."_END

B_5_C_15_9
BEGIN_व्रीडिताम् दुह्ख सम्तप्ताम् परिम्लानाम् तपस्विनीम् |ग्रहेण अन्गारकेण एव पीडिताम् इव 
	रोहिणीम् || ५-१५-२२_END
BEGIN_Bashful, tortured by sorrow worn out in a pitiable condition like the constellation Rohini, 
	pressed by the planet mars._END

B_5_C_14_17
BEGIN_ततो अम्बु धर सम्काशम् प्रव्ऱ्द्ध शिखरम् गिरिम् |विचित्र कूटम् कूटैः च सर्वतः परिवारितम् 
|| ५-१४-२७शिला गृहैर् अवततम् नाना वृक्षैः समावृतम् |ददर्श कपि शार्दूलो रम्यम् जगति पर्वतम् || ५-१४-२८_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the monkey warrior Hanuma saw a mountain which was a beautiful mountain in the world, 
equaling cloud with high peaks, with wonderful peaks surrounded in all directions by peaks, spread by caves and 
covered by different trees._END

B_5_C_13_24
BEGIN_तम् तु कृच्च्र गतम् दृष्ट्वा पन्चत्व गत मानसम् || ५-१३-२५भृश अनुरक्तो मेधावी न भविष्यति 
लक्ष्मणः |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing that Rama being with troubles, being with a heart towards death, Lakshmana, one with great 
love and an intellectual will not exist."_END

B_5_C_1_138
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तः सुरसया प्राञ्जलिर्वानरर्षभः |
प्रहृष्टवदनः श्रीमानिदं वचनमब्रवीत् || १-५-१५२_END
BEGIN_
Thus spoken to by Surasa, the glorious Hanuma, with a happy face and with folded
hands, spoke these words to Surasa._END

B_5_C_16_3
BEGIN_रामस्य व्यवसायज्ञा लक्ष्मणस्य च धीमतः |न अत्यर्थम् क्षुभ्यते देवी गन्गा इव जलद आगमे || 
५-१६-४_END
BEGIN_"Knowing the effort of Sri Rama and of sagacious Lakshmana, Seetha is not worried a lot, like Ganga 
in the rainy season."_END

B_5_C_15_10
BEGIN_अश्रु पूर्ण मुखीम् दीनाम् कृशाम् अननशेन च |शोक ध्यान पराम् दीनाम् नित्यम् दुह्ख परायणाम् 
	|| ५-१५-२३_END
BEGIN_With a face full of tears in a pitiable condition, emaciated due to not taking food, immersed 
	in thought with gloom, always in a pitiable state, surrendering to sorrow._END

B_5_C_14_18
BEGIN_ददर्श च नगात् तस्मान् नदीम् निपतिताम् कपिः |अन्काद् इव समुत्पत्य प्रियस्य पतिताम् प्रियाम् 
|| ५-१४-२९जले निपतित अग्रैः च पादपैर् उपशोभिताम् |वार्यमाणाम् इव क्रुद्धाम् प्रमदाम् प्रिय बन्धुभिः || 
५-१४-३०पुनर् आव्ऱ्त्त तोयाम् च ददर्श स महा कपिः |प्रसन्नाम् इव कान्तस्य कान्ताम् पुनर् उपस्थिताम् || ५-१४-३१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw river which fell down from the mountain like a beloved (young wife) who fell down after 
jumping from the lap of a loved one shone by trees whose ends fell down in water or like a woman in anger being 
detained by her near and dear. That great Hanuma again saw that river with water, turning back like a beloved 
woman reaching her beloved again, being reconciled to her beloved one._END

B_5_C_13_25
BEGIN_विनष्टौ भ्रातरौ श्रुत्वा भरतो अपि मरिष्यति || ५-१३-२६भरतम् च मृतम् दृष्ट्वा शत्रुघ्नो 
न भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing brothers to be dead, Bharata also will die. Seeing the dead Bharata, Shatrughana also 
will not exist."_END

B_5_C_1_139
BEGIN_
रामो दाशरथिर्नाम प्रविष्टो दण्डकावनम् |
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा वैदेह्या चापि भार्यया || ५-१-१५३_END
BEGIN_
"The son of Dasaratha, with the name of Rama entered the forest of Dandaka together
with His brother Lakshmana and wife Seetha."_END

B_5_C_16_4
BEGIN_तुल्य शील वयो वृत्ताम् तुल्य अभिजन लक्षणाम् |राघवो अर्हति वैदेहीम् तम् च इयम् असित ईक्षणा 
|| ५-१६-५_END
BEGIN_"Sri Rama is suited to Seetha with Her well matched character, age and conduct; with well matched 
pedigree and characteristics this black-eyed Seetha is also suited to Him."_END

B_5_C_15_11
BEGIN_प्रियम् जनम् अपश्यन्तीम् पश्यन्तीम् राक्षसी गणम् |स्व गणेन मृगीम् हीनाम् श्व गण अभिवृताम् 
	इव || ५-१५-२४_END
BEGIN_Not seeing dear people, seeing groups of demonesses, like a female deer loosing her own herd 
	surrounded by group of hounds._END

B_5_C_14_19
BEGIN_तस्य अदूरात् स पद्मिन्यो नाना द्विज गण आयुताः |ददर्श कपि शार्दूलो हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः 
|| ५-१४-३२_END
BEGIN_The best among vanaras and the son of Vayu, that Hanuma saw near to that mountain, lotus ponds 
together with many groups of birds._END

B_5_C_13_26
BEGIN_पुत्रान् मृतान् समीक्ष्य अथ न भविष्यन्ति मातरः || ५-१३-२७कौसल्या च सुमित्रा च कैकेयी च 
न संशयः |_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter seeing sons to be dead the mothers Kausalya, Sumitra and Kaikeyi will not exist - there 
is no doubt."_END

B_5_C_1_140
BEGIN_
अन्यकार्यविषक्तस्य बद्धवैरस्य राक्षसैः |
तस्य सीत हृता भार्या रावणेन यशस्विनी || ५-१-१५४_END
BEGIN_
"When that Sri Rama, with a bitter enmity towards Rakshasas, was diverted in another
task, His famed wife Seetha had been taken away by Ravana."_END

B_5_C_16_5
BEGIN_ताम् दृष्ट्वा नव हेम आभाम् लोक कान्ताम् इव श्रियम् |जगाम मनसा रामम् वचनम् च इदम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ५-१६-६_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Seetha with the radiance of new gold, like the goddess Laksmi, delightful to the world, 
Hanuma went by heart to Sri Rama spoke these words also._END

B_5_C_15_12
BEGIN_नील नाग आभया वेण्या जघनम् गतया एकया |नीलया नीरदापाये वनराज्या महीमिव || ५-१५-२५
	सुख अर्हाम् दुह्ख सम्तप्ताम् व्यसनानाम् अकोदिवाम् |_END
BEGIN_With a braid with the radiance of a single black serpent reaching hinder part, like the earth 
	with dark green groups of trees during the end of rainy season, deserving of comforts, tormented by grief, 
	not accustomed to calamities._END

B_5_C_14_20
BEGIN_कृत्रिमाम् दीर्घिकाम् च अपि पूर्णाम् शीतेन वारिणा |मणि प्रवर सोपानाम् मुख्ता सिकत शोभिताम् 
|| ५-१४-३३विविधैर् मृग सम्घैः च विचित्राम् चित्र काननाम् |प्रासादैः सुमहद्भिः च निर्मितैर् विश्व कर्मणा 
|| ५-१४-३४काननैः कॄत्रिमैः च अपि सर्वतः समलम्कृताम् |_END
BEGIN_He also saw an artificial pond filled with cold water, with steps embedded with best diamonds, 
shone by the sand of pearls, wonderful forest with very big buildings made by Vishwakarma, with groups of artificial 
trees decorated in all directions._END

B_5_C_13_27
BEGIN_कृतज्ञः सत्य संधः च सुग्रीवः प्लवग अधिपः || ५-१३-२८रामम् तथा गतम् दृष्ट्वा ततः त्यक्ष्यन्ति 
जीवितम् |_END
BEGIN_"Grateful, true to pledge Sugreeva, the leader of Vanaras, seeing Rama the leader of Vanaras seeing 
Rama die in that way will give up life thereafter."_END

B_5_C_1_141
BEGIN_
तस्याः सकाशं दूतोऽहं गमिष्ये रामकारणात् |
कर्तुमर्हसि रामस्य साह्यं विषयवासिनि || ५-१-१५५_END
BEGIN_
"I am going for Rama's sake as a messenger to find Her presence. O subject of Sri
Rama! You are suited to help Rama."_END

B_5_C_16_6
BEGIN_अस्या हेतोर् विशाल अक्ष्या हतो वाली महा बलः |रावण प्रतिमो वीर्ये कबन्धः च निपातितः || 
५-१६-७_END
BEGIN_"For the sake of this Seetha, the wide eyed one, Vali of great strength has been killed, Kabanda 
also equalling Ravana in strength has been felled."_END

B_5_C_15_13
BEGIN_ताम् समीक्ष्य विशाल अक्षीम् अधिकम् मलिनाम् कृशाम् || ५-१५-२६तर्कयाम् आस सीता इति कारणैः 
	उपपादिभिः |_END
BEGIN_Observing that woman with wide eyes, very untidy, emaciated, Hanuma thought that this is indeed 
	Seetha on logical grounds._END

B_5_C_14_21
BEGIN_ये केचित् पादपाः तत्र पुष्प उपग फल उपगाः || ५-१४-३५सच् चत्राः सवितर्दीकाः सर्वे सौवर्ण 
वेदिकाः |_END
BEGIN_There whatever trees were there with flowers and fruits, all those were together with umbrellas, 
together with big platforms and with smaller golden platforms._END

B_5_C_13_28
BEGIN_दुर्मना व्यथिता दीना निरानन्दा तपस्विनी || ५-१३-२९पीडिता भर्तृ शोकेन रुमा त्यक्ष्यति जीवितम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Being tortured by the sorrow of husband, made sad by a gloomy heart, disconsolate without happiness, 
to be pitied, Ruma will give up life."_END

B_5_C_1_142
BEGIN_
अथवा मैथिलीं दृष्ट्वा रामं चाक्लिष्टकारिणम् |
आगमिष्यामि ते वक्त्रं सत्यं प्रतिशृणोमि ते || ५-१-१५६_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise after seeing Seetha and informing that to Sri Rama who makes Seetha
without troubles, I will obtain your mouth. I am promising truthfully to you."_END

B_5_C_16_7
BEGIN_विराधः च हतः सम्ख्ये राक्षसो भीम विक्रमः |वने रामेण विक्रम्य महा इन्द्रेण इव शम्बरः || 
५-१६-८_END
BEGIN_"In the forest during war Virada of horrible prowess has been killed by Rama by valour, like Sambara 
by Mahendra."_END

B_5_C_15_14
BEGIN_ह्रियमाणा तदा तेन रक्षसा काम रूपिणा || ५-१५-२७यथा रूपा हि दृष्टा वै तथा रूपा इयम् 
	अन्गना |_END
BEGIN_Then, while being abducted by that rakshasa with the ability to assume desired form in whatever 
	way, She was seen, this woman has the same form._END

B_5_C_14_22
BEGIN_लता प्रतानैः बहुभिः पर्णैः च बहुभिर् व्ऱ्ताम् || ५-१४-३६काञ्चनीम् शिंशुपाम् एकाम् ददर्श 
स महा कपिः |वृताम् हेममयूभिस्तु वेदिकाभिः समन्ततः || ५-१४-३७_END
BEGIN_The monkey warrior Hanuma saw one shimshupaa tree golden in colour covered with many groups of 
creepers and with many leaves surrounded everywhere with platforms made of gold._END

B_5_C_13_29
BEGIN_वालिजेन तु दुह्खेन पीडिता शोक कर्शिता || ५-१३-३०पन्चत्व गमने राज्ञः तारा अपि न भविष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_"Being distressed from the sorrow of Vali, being emaciated from grief, Tara also will not exist 
while the king Sugreeva is obtaining death."_END

B_5_C_1_143
BEGIN_
एवमुक्ता हनुमता सुरसा कामरूपिणी |
अब्रवीन्नातिवर्तेत कश्चिदेष वरो मम || ५-१-१५७_END
BEGIN_
Thus being spoken to by Hanuma, Surasa with power to take desired form, spoke thus:
"No one can overcome me. This is my boon."_END

B_5_C_16_8
BEGIN_चतुर् दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |निहतानि जन स्थाने शरैर् अग्नि शिख उपमैः || ५-१६-९_END
BEGIN_"At Janastaana fourteen thousands of rakshasas of terrible deed have been killed by arrows equalling 
tongues of fires."_END

B_5_C_15_15
BEGIN_पूर्ण चन्द्र आननाम् सुभ्रूम् चारु वृत्त पयो धराम् || ५-१५-२८कुर्वन्तीम् प्रभया देवीम् 
	सर्वा वितिमिरा दिशः |ताम् नील केशीम् बिम्ब ओष्ठीम् सुमध्याम् सुप्रतिष्ठिताम् || ५-१५-२९सीताम् पद्म 
	पलाश अक्षीम् मन्मथस्य रतिम् यथा |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Seetha with a face like full moon, with beautiful eyebrows, with graceful rounded 
	breasts, by the radiance making all directions without darkness, goddess like with black hair, with lips like 
	bimba fruit, with a good waist, very firm, with eyes like lotus petals, like Rati the consort of god of love._END

B_5_C_14_23
BEGIN_सो अपश्यद् भूमि भागामः च गर्त प्रस्रवणानि च |सुवर्ण वृक्षान् अपरान् ददर्श शिखि सम्निभान् 
|| ५-१४-३८_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw lands, mountain springs, and some other golden trees equal to fire._END

B_5_C_13_30
BEGIN_माता पित्रोर् विनाशेन सुग्रीव व्यसनेन च || ५-१३-३१कुमारो अपि अन्गदः कस्माद् धारयिष्यति 
जीवितम् |_END
BEGIN_"The young Angada also from the death of mother and father, from the grief of Sugreeva - why will 
he retain life?"_END

B_5_C_1_144
BEGIN_
तं प्रयान्तं समुद्वीक्ष्य सुरसा वाक्यमब्रवीत् |
बलं जिज्ञासमाना वै नागमाता हनूमतः || ५-१-१५८_END
BEGIN_
Mother of Nagas, Surasa, desiring to know the strength of Hanuma, spoke these words
on seeing Him going away._END

B_5_C_16_9
BEGIN_करः च निहतः सम्ख्ये त्रिशिराः च निपातितः |दूषणः च महा तेजा रामेण विदित आत्मना || ५-१६-१०_END
BEGIN_"By Rama with a famed mind, Khara has been killed, Trisira also has been fell down, Duushana with 
great glory also has been killed in war."_END

B_5_C_15_16
BEGIN_इष्टाम् सर्वस्य जगतः पूर्ण चन्द्र प्रभाम् इव || ५-१५-३०भूमौ सुतनुम् आसीनाम् नियताम् 
	इव तापसीम् |_END
BEGIN_As the light of full moon, dear to all world, like an ascetic woman leading austere life sitting 
	on bare ground with a good body._END

B_5_C_14_24
BEGIN_तेषाम् द्रुमाणाम् प्रभया मेरोर् इव महा कपिः |अमन्यत तदा वीरः कान्चनो अस्मि इति वानरः || 
५-१४-३९_END
BEGIN_Then the courageous Hanuma thought thus: "Like the sun by the radiance of Mount Meru, by the radiance 
of those trees, I am of golden colour."_END

B_5_C_13_31
BEGIN_भर्तृजेन तु शोकेन अभिभूता वन ओकसः || ५-१३-३२शिरांसि अभिहनिष्यन्ति तलैर् मुष्टिभिर् एव 
च |_END
BEGIN_"Vanaras being rejected by the sorrow due to their lord will strike their heads with palms and 
fists."_END

B_5_C_1_145
BEGIN_
प्रविश्य वदनं मेऽद्य गन्तव्यं वानरोत्तम |
वर एष पुरा दत्तो मम धात्रेति सत्वरा || ५-१-१५९
व्यादाय विपुलं वक्त्रं स्थिता सा मारुतेः पुरः |_END
BEGIN_
"O best among Vanaras! You are bound to go only after entering my mouth. This boon
had been given to me long ago by Brahma." - speaking thus, with quickness she opened her wide mouth
and stood before Hanuma._END

B_5_C_16_10
BEGIN_ऐश्वर्यम् वानराणाम् च दुर्लभम् वालि पालितम् |अस्या निमित्ते सुग्रीवः प्राप्तवान् लोक सत्कृतम् 
|| ५-१६-११_END
BEGIN_"For Her sake Sugreeva obtained wealth of vanaras ruled by Vali difficult to be obtained and worshiped 
by the world."_END

B_5_C_15_17
BEGIN_निःश्वास बहुलाम् भीरुम् भुजग इन्द्र वधूम् इव || ५-१५-३१शोक जालेन महता विततेन न राजतीम् 
	|_END
BEGIN_Sighing a lot like the consort of lord of serpents in fright, not radiant by sorrow which was 
	great and extensive._END

B_5_C_14_25
BEGIN_ताम् कान्चनैः तरु गणैर् मारुतेन च वीजिताम् |किन्किणी शत निर्घोषाम् दृष्ट्वा विस्मयम् आगमत् 
|| ५-१४-४०_END
BEGIN_Seeing that shimshupaa tree with groups of trees of golden colour blown by the wind, with the sound 
of hundreds of tinkle bells, Hanuma got surprised._END

B_5_C_1_146
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तः सुरसया क्रुद्धो वानरपुञ्गवः || ५-१-१६०
अब्रवीत्कुरु वै वक्त्रं येन मां विषहिष्यसे |_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma speaking thus to Surasa, became angry and became ten yojanas long and
ten yojanas wide._END

B_5_C_13_32
BEGIN_सान्त्वेन अनुप्रदानेन मानेन च यशस्विना || ५-१३-३३लालिताः कपि राजेन प्राणामः त्यक्ष्यन्ति 
वानराः |_END
BEGIN_"Vanaras loved by the famous king Sugreeva through good words, through small gifts, through respect 
will give up lives."_END

B_5_C_16_11
BEGIN_सागरः च मया क्रान्तः श्रीमान् नद नदी पतिः |अस्या हेतोर् विशाल अक्ष्याः पुरी च इयम् निरीक्षिता 
|| ५-१६-१२_END
BEGIN_"For the sake of Her, with wide eyes, the ocean, lord of rivers and streams, has been crossed by 
me; this city also has been explored."_END

B_5_C_15_18
BEGIN_संसक्ताम् धूम जालेन शिखाम् इव विभावसोः || ५-१५-३२ताम् स्मृतीम् इव संदिघ्दाम् ऋद्धिम् 
	निपतिताम् इव |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Her like a tongue of fire mixed with column of smoke, like an intellect together 
	with doubts, like a cast away treasure._END

B_5_C_14_26
BEGIN_स पुष्पित अग्राम् रुचिराम् तरुण अन्कुर पल्लवाम् |ताम् आरुह्य महा वेगः शिंशपाम् पर्ण सम्व्ऱ्ताम् 
|| ५-१४-४१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma with great arms climbing up that shimshupaa tree with well flowered ends, beautiful tree, 
mature with young shoots and leaves and covered by leaves (thought thus)._END

B_5_C_16_12
BEGIN_यदि रामः समुद्रान्ताम् मेदिनीम् परिवर्तयेत् |अस्याः कृते जगत् च अपि युक्तम् इति एव मे 
मतिः || ५-१६-१३_END
BEGIN_"If Sri Rama for Her sake turns upside down the earth with the ocean at the end, and the entire 
universe it is fair, this is my opinion."_END

B_5_C_13_33
BEGIN_न वनेषु न शैलेषु न निरोधेषु वा पुनः || ५-१३-३४क्रीडाम् अनुभविष्यन्ति समेत्य कपि कुन्जराः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Best among Vanaras will not enjoy together sport in forest, not on mountains, not again in covered 
places."_END

B_5_C_1_147
BEGIN_
प्रविश्य वदनं मेऽद्य ग्न्तव्यं वानरोत्तम |
वर एष पुरा दत्तो ममम् ध्रात्रेति सत्वरा || ५-१-१६१
व्यादाय विपुलं वक्त्रं स्थिता सा मरुतेः पुरः |_END
BEGIN_
Seeing Hanuma, who looked like a cloud, being ten yojanas long, Surasa also made her
mouth twenty yojanas long._END

B_5_C_15_19
BEGIN_विहताम् इव च श्रद्धाम् आशाम् प्रतिहताम् इव || ५-१५-३३स उपसर्गाम् यथा सिद्धिम् बुद्धिम् 
	सकलुषाम् इव |_END
BEGIN_Like shattered faith, like frustrated hope, like success together with obstacles, like an impure 
	mind._END

B_5_C_14_27
BEGIN_इतो द्रक्ष्यामि वैदेहीम् राम दर्शन लालसाम् |इतः च इतः च दुह्ख आर्ताम् सम्पतन्तीम् यद्ऱ्च्चया 
|| ५-१४-४२_END
BEGIN_"I will see by God's grace, Seetha who is interested in the sight of Sri Rama while she is moving 
here and there with grief."_END

B_5_C_16_13
BEGIN_राज्यम् वा त्रिषु लोकेषु सीता वा जनक आत्मजा |त्रैलोक्य राज्यम् सकलम् सीताया न आप्नुयात् 
कलाम् || ५-१६-१४_END
BEGIN_"Among three worlds, if it is a choice between kingdom or Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, all the 
kingdom of three worlds will not approach a sixteenth part of Seetha."_END

B_5_C_13_34
BEGIN_सपुत्र दाराः सामात्या भर्तृ व्यसन पीडिताः || ५-१३-३५शैल अग्रेभ्यः पतिष्यन्ति समेत्य विषमेषु 
च |_END
BEGIN_"Together with wife and children and together with ministers being tortured by grief of their lord, 
they will fall down from top of mountains on to flat lands and on to rugged lands."_END

B_5_C_1_148
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा मेघसंकाशं दशयोजनमायतम् || ५-१-१६२
चकार सुरसा चास्यं विंशद्योजनमायतम् |_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, Hanuma got angry and became thirty yojanas long. Surasa made her mouth
forty yojanas high. The courageous Hanuma then became fifty yojanas high._END

B_5_C_15_20
BEGIN_अभूतेन अपवादेन कीर्तिम् निपतिताम् इव || ५-१५-३४राम उपरोध व्यथिताम् रक्षो हरण कर्शिताम् 
	|_END
BEGIN_Like fame that has fallen down by a false scandal, tortured by the obstruction caused to Rama, 
	emaciated due to the abduction by Ravana._END

B_5_C_14_28
BEGIN_अशोक वनिका च इयम् दृढम् रम्या दुरात्मनः |चम्पकैः चन्दनैः च अपि बकुलैः च विभूषिता || ५-१४-४३_END
BEGIN_This Ashoka garden of evil-souled Ravana is definitely beautiful; it is well decorated by Champaka 
trees, by sandal trees and by Vakula trees._END

B_5_C_13_35
BEGIN_विषम् उद्बन्धनम् वा अपि प्रवेशम् ज्वलनस्य वा || ५-१३-३६उपवासम् अथो शस्त्रम् प्रचरिष्यन्ति 
वानराः |_END
BEGIN_"Vanaras will perform death by taking poison or getting hanged or entering fire or fasting or a 
weapon."_END

B_5_C_16_14
BEGIN_इयम् सा धर्म शीलस्य जनकस्य महात्मनः |सुता मैथिलराजस्य सीता भर्तृदृढ व्रता || ५-१६-१५_END
BEGIN_"This She is that Seetha, the daughter of king Janaka of Mithila, the great soul, and noble one 
with a firm resolution towards husband."_END

B_5_C_1_149
BEGIN_
हनुमांस्तु ततः क्रुद्धस्त्रिंशद्योजनमायतः || ५-१-१६३
चकार सुरसा वक्त्रं चत्वारिंशत्तथोच्छ्रितम् |
बभूव हनुमान्वीरः पञ्चाशद्योजनोच्छ्रितः || ५-१-१६४_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, Hanuma got angry and became thirty yojanas long. Surasa made her mouth
forty yojanas high. The courageous Hanuma then became fifty yojanas high._END

B_5_C_15_21
BEGIN_अबलाम् मृग शाव अक्षीम् वीक्षमाणाम् ततः ततः || ५-१५-३५बाष्प अम्बु प्रतिपूर्णेन कृष्ण 
	वक्त्र अक्षि पक्ष्मणा |वदनेन अप्रसन्नेन निह्श्वसन्तीम् पुनः पुनः || ५-१५-३६_END
BEGIN_With eyes like those of a young doe full of tears, with black and oblique eye-brows, with a 
	cheerless countenance, seeing there and there, being helpless, sighing again and again._END

B_5_C_14_29
BEGIN_इयम् च नलिनी रम्या द्विज सम्घ निषेविता |इमाम् सा राम महिषी नूनम् एष्यति जानकी || ५-१४-४४_END
BEGIN_"This pond also served by groups of birds is beautiful; that wife of Sri Rama definitely will come 
for this pond."_END

B_5_C_13_36
BEGIN_घोरम् आरोदनम् मन्ये गते मयि भविष्यति || ५-१३-३७इक्ष्वाकु कुल नाशः च नाशः चैव वन ओकसाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"While I am going I think about the destruction of Ikshvaaku dynasty and destruction of Vanaras 
and there will be a terrible wail."_END

B_5_C_1_150
BEGIN_
चकार सुरसा वक्त्रं षष्टियोजनमायतम् |
तथैव हनुमान्वीरः सप्ततीयोजिनोच्छ्रितः || ५-१-१६५_END
BEGIN_
Surasa then made her mouth sixty yojanas long. The mighty Hanuma in the same
fashion, became seventy yojanas high._END

B_5_C_16_15
BEGIN_उत्थिता मेदिनीम् भित्त्वा क्षेत्रे हल मुख क्षते |पद्म रेणु निभैः कीर्णा शुभैः केदार पांसुभिः 
|| ५-१६-१६_END
BEGIN_"While a field was being ploughed She rose up splitting the earth covered by auspicious dust of 
field equalling pollen."_END

B_5_C_15_22
BEGIN_मल पन्क धराम् दीनाम् मण्डन अर्हाम् अमण्डिताम् |प्रभाम् नक्षत्र राजस्य काल मेघैः इव 
	आवृताम् || ५-१५-३७_END
BEGIN_Wearing a coat of dust, pitiable one, although suited for decorations undecorated, like the 
	radiance of the moon, the lord of stars, covered by black clouds._END

B_5_C_14_30
BEGIN_सा राम राम महिषी राघवस्य प्रिया सदा |वन संचार कुशला नूनम् एष्यति जानकी || ५-१४-४५_END
BEGIN_"The wife of Sri Rama dear to Sri Rama, a chaste wife, soul captivating one, expert at moving in 
forest, that Janaki will definitely come."_END

B_5_C_13_37
BEGIN_सो अहम् न एव गमिष्यामि किष्किन्धाम् नगरीम् इतः || ५-१३-३८न हि शक्ष्यामि अहम् द्रष्टुम् 
सुग्रीवम् मैथिलीम् विना |_END
BEGIN_"I will not go from here to the Kishkindha city. I am not capable to see Sugreeva without Seetha."_END

B_5_C_1_151
BEGIN_
चकार सुरसा व्क्त्रंशीतीयोजनोच्छ्रितम् |
हनुमानचलप्रख्यो नवतीयोजनोच्छ्रितः || ५-१-१६६_END
BEGIN_
Surasa made her mouth eighty yojanas high. The mountain-like Hanuma then became
ninety yojanas high._END

B_5_C_16_16
BEGIN_विक्रान्तस्य आर्य शीलस्य सम्युगेषु अनिवर्तिनः |स्नुषा दशरथस्य एषा ज्येष्ठा राज्ञो यशस्विनी 
|| ५-१६-१७_END
BEGIN_"She is the famed eldest daughter-in-law of king Dasaratha the valorous one, not turning back in 
the battle."_END

B_5_C_15_23
BEGIN_तस्य संदिदिहे बुद्धिः मुहुः सीताम् निरीक्ष्य तु |आम्नायानाम् अयोगेन विद्याम् प्रशिथिलाम् 
	इव || ५-१५-३८_END
BEGIN_Seeing Seetha like knowledge in ruin for want of repeated study, that Hanuma's mind got repeatedly 
	doubtful._END

B_5_C_14_31
BEGIN_अथवा मृग शाव अक्षी वनस्य अस्य विचक्षणा |वनम् एष्यति सा च इह राम चिन्ता अनुकर्शिता || ५-१४-४६_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise one with the eyes of a deer, emaciated by the thought of Sri Rama, that noble one will 
come for this garden."_END

B_5_C_13_38
BEGIN_मयि अगच्चति च इहस्थे धर्म आत्मानौ महा रथौ || ५-१३-३९आशया तौ धरिष्येते वनराः च मनस्विनः 
|_END
BEGIN_"I while not going, being here those virtuous ones, those great warriors those two Rama and Lakshmana 
will live by hope. Vanaras also who are agile will live."_END

B_5_C_1_152
BEGIN_
तद्दृष्ट्वा व्यादितं त्वास्यं वायुपुत्रः सुबुद्धिमान् |
दीर्घजिह्वं सुरसया सुघोरं नरकोपमम् || ५-१-१६७
सुसंक्षिप्यात्मनः कायं बभूवाञ्गुष्ठमात्रकः |_END
BEGIN_
The great wise Hanuma seeing that mouth with a long tongue which was horrible and
equal to hell being opened by Surasa, greatly reduced His own body and became the size of a
thumb._END

B_5_C_16_17
BEGIN_धर्मज्ञस्य कृतज्ञस्य रामस्य विदित आत्मनः |इयम् सा दयिता भार्या राक्षसी वशम् आगता || ५-१६-१८_END
BEGIN_"This She the dear wife of Rama the righteous one, grateful one, knower of Self has obtained capture 
of demonesses."_END

B_5_C_15_24
BEGIN_दुह्खेन बुबुधे सीताम् हनुमान् अनलम्कृताम् |संस्कारेण यथा हीनाम् वाचम् अर्थ अन्तरम् 
	गताम् || ५-१५-३९_END
BEGIN_Hanuma recognized with great sorrow Seetha not decorated, like a sentence which got a different 
	meaning being devoid of culture._END

B_5_C_14_32
BEGIN_राम शोक अभिसम्तप्ता सा देवी वाम लोचना |वन वास रता नित्यम् एष्यते वन चारिणी || ५-१४-४७_END
BEGIN_"Tortured by grief for Sri Rama, with beautiful eyes, interested always living in the garden, that 
Devi moving about in the garden will come."_END

B_5_C_13_39
BEGIN_हस्त आदानो मुख आदानो नियतो वृक्ष मूलिकः || ५-१३-४०वानप्रस्थो भविष्यामि अदृष्ट्वा जनक आत्मजाम् 
|सागर अनूपजे देशे बहु मूल फल उदके || ५-१३-४१_END
BEGIN_"Without seeing Seetha subsisting on whatever falls on hand, whatever comes to mouth, being self 
restrained I will become a hermit living on trees and herbs at a region near ocean which has many roots, fruits 
and much water."_END

B_5_C_1_153
BEGIN_
सोऽभिपत्याशु तद्वक्त्रं निष्पत्य च महाजवः |
अन्तरिक्षे स्थितः श्रीमानिदं वचनमब्रवीत् || ५-१-१६८_END
BEGIN_
The glorious Hanuma with great speed, quickly entered Surasa's mouth and came out of
it and standing in the sky spoke these words to Surasa._END

B_5_C_16_18
BEGIN_सर्वान् भोगान् परित्यज्य भर्तृ स्नेह बलात् कृता |अचिन्तयित्वा दुह्खानि प्रविष्टा निर्जनम् 
वनम् || ५-१६-१९सम्तुष्टा फल मूलेन भर्तृ शुश्रूषणा परा |या पराम् भजते प्रीतिम् वने अपि भवने यथा || ५-१६-२०
सा इयम् कनक वर्ण अन्गी नित्यम् सुस्मित भाषिणी |सहते यातनाम् एताम् अनर्थानाम् अभागिनी || ५-१६-२१_END
BEGIN_"Whoever Seetha abandoning all comforts, forced by the love towards husband not thinking about 
sorrows, entering forest unpopulated with humans, being happy with fruits and roots, devoted to the service of 
Her husband, even in forest is getting great happiness like in a palace, the one with golden limbs, always with 
a smiling talk, not suited to misfortunes - that this Seetha is bearing all this suffering."_END

B_5_C_15_25
BEGIN_ताम् समीक्ष्य विशाल अक्षीम् राज पुत्रीम् अनिन्दिताम् |तर्कयाम् आस सीता इति कारणैः 
	उपपादयन् || ५-१५-४०_END
BEGIN_Seeing that princess, the wide eyed one, blameless one, Hanuma reasoned her to be Seetha for 
	the following reasons._END

B_5_C_14_33
BEGIN_वने चराणाम् सततम् नूनम् स्पृहयते पुरा |रामस्य दयिता भार्या जनकस्य सुता सती|| ५-१४-४८_END
BEGIN_"The beloved wife of Sri Rama, the daughter of king Janaka, the chaste wife, earlier always was 
interested the denizens of the garden. This is true."_END

B_5_C_1_154
BEGIN_
प्रविष्टोऽस्मि हि ते वक्त्रं दाक्षायणि नमोऽस्तु ते |
गमिष्ये यत्र वैदेही सत्यं चासीद्वरस्तव ||५-१-१६९_END
BEGIN_
"O daughter of Daksha! I indeed entered your mouth. My regards to you. I will now go
where Seetha is. Your boon also came true."_END

B_5_C_13_40
BEGIN_चिताम् कृत्वा प्रवेक्ष्यामि समिद्धम् अरणी सुतम् |उपविष्टस्य वा सम्यग् लिन्गिनम् साधयिष्यतः 
|| ५-१३-४२शरीरम् भक्षयिष्यन्ति वायसाः श्वापदानि च |_END
BEGIN_"Or I will enter fire which is glowing after making a funeral pile or while sitting performing 
fasting onto death my body will be eaten by crows and by beasts of prey."_END

B_5_C_15_26
BEGIN_वैदेह्या यानि च अन्गेषु तदा रामो अन्वकीर्तयत् |तानि आभरण जालानि गात्र शोभीनि अलक्षयत् 
	|| ५-१५-४१सुकृतौ कर्ण वेष्टौ च श्व दम्ष्ट्रौ च सुसंस्थितौ |मणि विद्रुम चित्राणि हस्तेष्व् आभरणानि 
	च || ५-१५-४२श्यामानि चिर युक्तत्वात् तथा संस्थानवन्ति च |_END
BEGIN_Then Hanuma saw whatever groups of jewellery of Seetha on various parts Rama spoke, those charming 
	Her limbs, well made earrings, well fitting Svadamstras and ornaments wonderful with diamonds on the limbs 
	of Her hands, belonging to body for long time, blackened and making marks on body._END

B_5_C_16_19
BEGIN_इमाम् तु शील सम्पन्नाम् द्रष्टुम् इच्चति राघवः |रावणेन प्रमथिताम् प्रपाम् इव पिपासितः 
|| ५-१६-२२_END
BEGIN_"Sri Rama likes to see this Seetha who is endowed with excellent character and tormented by Ravana, 
like a thirsty one for a place where water is available freely."_END

B_5_C_14_34
BEGIN_संध्या काल मनाः श्यामा ध्रुवम् एष्यति जानकी |नदीम् च इमाम् शिव जलाम् संध्या अर्थे वर वर्णिनी 
|| ५-१४-४९_END
BEGIN_"The ever youthful one with the best complexion, Seetha interested in the rites of Sandhya time 
will definitely come to this river with the auspicious water for Sandhya rite."_END

B_5_C_1_155
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा वदनान्मुक्तं चन्द्रं राहुमुखादिव |
अब्रवीत्सुरसा देवी स्वेन रूपेण वानरम् || ५-१-१७०_END
BEGIN_
Seeing that Vanara being released from her mouth like the moon from the mouth of
Rahu, goddess Surasa spoke these words assuming her normal form._END

B_5_C_13_41
BEGIN_इदम् अपि ऋषिभिर् दृष्टम् निर्याणम् इति मे मतिः || ५-१३-४३सम्यग् आपः प्रवेक्ष्यामि न चेत् 
पश्यामि जानकीम् |_END
BEGIN_"This way to giving up body has been seen by sages. This is my opinion if I do not see Seetha, 
I will enter lot of water."_END

B_5_C_15_27
BEGIN_तानि एव एतानि मन्ये अहम् यानि रामो अन्वकीर्तयत् || ५-१५-४३तत्र यानि अवहीनानि तानि 
	अहम् न उपलक्षये |यानि अस्या न अवहीनानि तानि इमानि न संशयः || ५-१५-४४_END
BEGIN_"I think all these to be same about which Rama spoke; among them whatever have been worn out 
	those I will not see; whatever jewels of Her are not worn out these are they - no doubt."_END

B_5_C_16_20
BEGIN_अस्या नूनम् पुनर् लाभाद् राघवः प्रीतिम् एष्यति |राजा राज्य परिभ्रष्टः पुनः प्राप्य इव 
मेदिनीम् || ५-१६-२३_END
BEGIN_"By Her gain again Sri Rama definitely will get happiness like a king who lost kingdom getting 
back the land."_END

B_5_C_17_0
BEGIN_ततः कुमुदषण्डाभो निर्मलम् निर्मलोदयः |प्रजगाम नभश्चन्द्रो हंसो नीलमिवोदकम् || ५-१७- १_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the moon with a peaceful rise, with radiance equaling that of a group of lotuses, obtained 
the clear sky like a swan obtaining blue water._END

B_5_C_14_35
BEGIN_तस्याः च अपि अनुरूपेयम् अशोक वनिका शुभा |शुभा या पार्थिव इन्द्रस्य पत्नी रामस्य सम्मिता 
|| ५-१४-५०_END
BEGIN_"Whoever Seetha, the auspicious wife, a dear one of Sri Rama, the king of kings, to that Seetha 
this Ashoka garden, an auspicious one, is well suited also."_END

B_5_C_1_156
BEGIN_
अर्थसिद्ध्यै हरिश्रेष्ठ गच्छ सौम्य यथासुखम् |
समानयस्व वैदेहीं राघवेण महात्मना || ५-१-१७१_END
BEGIN_
"O gentle Hanuma! Go according to your comfort to achieve the desired task. Bring
Seetha together with the great Sri Rama."_END

B_5_C_13_42
BEGIN_सुजात मूला सुभगा कीर्ति माला यशस्विनी || ५-१३-४४प्रभग्ना चिर रात्री इयम् मम सीताम् अपश्यतः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Not seeing Seetha, my garland of glory of long time with a strong foundation, beautiful one together 
with fame has been destroyed."_END

B_5_C_15_28
BEGIN_पीतम् कनक पट्ट आभम् स्रस्तम् तद् वसनम् शुभम् |उत्तरीयम् नग आसक्तम् तदा दृष्टम् प्लवम् 
	गमैः || ५-१५-४५_END
BEGIN_That upper garment yellow with a shine like a golden plate, auspicious one, being dropped had 
	been seen caught in a tree then by vanaras._END

B_5_C_16_21
BEGIN_काम भोगैः परित्यक्ता हीना बन्धु जनेन च |धारयति आत्मनो देहम् तत् समागम कान्क्षिणी || ५-१६-२४_END
BEGIN_"Left by coveted enjoyments, lacking relatives also Seetha is keeping body desirous of meeting 
with Sri Rama."_END

B_5_C_17_1
BEGIN_साचिव्यमिव कुर्वन् स प्रभया निर्मलप्रभः |चन्द्रमा रश्मभिः शीतैः सिषेवे पवनात्मजम् || ५-१७-२_END
BEGIN_That moon with a peaceful glow served Hanuma with cool rays as though performing help with radiance._END

B_5_C_14_36
BEGIN_यदि जिवति सा देवी तारा अधिप निभ आनना |आगमिष्यति सा अवश्यम् इमाम् शिव जलाम् नदीम् || ५-१४-५१_END
BEGIN_"That Devi with the face like that of the moon, if alive, she definitely will come for this river 
with auspicious water."_END

B_5_C_1_157
BEGIN_
तत्तृतीयं हनुमतो दृष्ट्वा कर्म सुदुष्करम् |
साधु साध्विति भूतानि प्रश्शंसुस्तदा हरिम् || ५-१-१७२_END
BEGIN_
Seeing that third very difficult task of Hanuma, all the creatures then praised
Hanuma saying "Good! Good!"._END

B_5_C_13_43
BEGIN_तापसो वा भविष्यामि नियतो वृक्ष मूलिकः || ५-१३-४५न इतः प्रतिगमिष्यामि ताम् अदृष्ट्वा असित 
ईक्षणाम् |_END
BEGIN_"I will become a hermit who is self restrained resorting to trees and herbs, I will not go from 
here not seeing Seetha with black eyes."_END

B_5_C_15_29
BEGIN_भूषणानि च मुख्यानि दृष्टानि धरणी तले |अनया एव अपविद्धानि स्वनवन्ति महान्ति च || ५-१५-४६_END
BEGIN_"Dropped on the earth by Her, ornaments also great and important, those making sound have been 
	seen."_END

B_5_C_16_22
BEGIN_न एषा पश्यति राक्षस्यो न इमान् पुष्प फल द्रुमान् |एकस्थ हृदया नूनम् रामम् एव अनुपश्यति 
|| ५-१६-२५_END
BEGIN_"She is not seeing demonesses, not flowers, fruits or trees and with a single heart is meditating 
only on Sri Rama - this is sure."_END

B_5_C_17_2
BEGIN_स ददर्श ततः सीताम् पूर्णचन्द्रनिभाननाम् |शोकभारैरिव न्यस्तां भारैर्नावमिवाम्भसि || ५-१७-३_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Hanuma saw Seetha with a face like a full moon, put down by the weight of grief, like 
a ship sinking down in water due to weight._END

B_5_C_14_37
BEGIN_एवम् तु मत्वा हनुमान् महात्मा |प्रतीक्षमाणो मनुज इन्द्र पत्नीम् ||अवेक्षमाणः च ददर्श 
सर्वम् |सुपुष्पिते पर्ण घने निलीनः || ५-१४-५२_END
BEGIN_The great-souled Hanuma thus thinking being concealed in the mass of well flowered leaves saw everything 
observing everywhere._END

B_5_C_1_158
BEGIN_
स सागरमनाधृष्यमभ्येत्य वरुणालयम् |
जगामाकाशमाविश्य वेगेन गरुडोपमः || ५-१-१७३_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma, equal to Garuda in speed, neared the ocean which is the abode of
Varuna, entered the sky and went in His original path._END

B_5_C_13_44
BEGIN_यदि इतः प्रतिगच्चामि सीताम् अनधिगम्य ताम् || ५-१३-४६अन्गदः सहितैः सर्वैर् वानरैर् न भविष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_"If I go back from here without knowing that Seetha, there will not be Angada together with all 
those Vanaras."_END

B_5_C_15_30
BEGIN_इदम् चिर गृहीतत्वाद् वसनम् क्लिष्टवत्तरम् |तथा हि नूनम् तद् वर्णम् तथा श्रीमद् यथा 
	इतरत् || ५-१५-४७_END
BEGIN_"This cloth being worn for a long time has worn out a lot, even then definitely it is of the 
	same colour, like the other upper garment; in the same way this is glorious."_END

B_5_C_16_23
BEGIN_भर्ता नाम परम् नार्या भूषणम् भूषणाद् अपि |एषा हि रहिता तेन शोभन अर्हा न शोभते || ५-१६-२६_END
BEGIN_"Husband is indeed the greatest adornment for a woman greater than jewellery; this Seetha though 
deserving of decoration, is not looking charming without Sri Rama."_END

B_5_C_17_3
BEGIN_दिदृक्षमाणो वैदेहीम् हनुमान् मारुतात्मजः |स ददर्शाविदूरस्था राक्षसीर्घोरदर्शनाः || ५-१७-४
एकाक्षीमेककर्णाम् च कर्णप्रावरणाम् तथा |अकर्णाम् शङ्कुकर्णाम् च मस्तकोच्छ्वासनासिकाम् || ५-१७-५अतिकायोत्तमाङ्गीं 
च तनुदीर्घशिरोधराम् |ध्वस्तकेशीम् तथाकेशीम् केशकम्बलधारिणीम् || ५-१७-६लम्बकर्णललाटाम् च लम्बोदरपयोधराम् 
|लम्बोष्ठीं चुबुकोष्ठीं च लम्बास्याम् लम्बजानुकाम् || ५-१७-७ह्रस्वाम् दीर्घाम् च कुब्जाम् विकटाम् वामनां 
तथा |करालाम् भुग्नवक्त्राम् च पिङ्गाक्षीम् विकृताननाम् || ५-१७-८_END
BEGIN_Hanuma wanting to see Seetha saw nearby ogresses with horrible appearance - one with one eye; one 
with a single ear and also one with ears as covering; one with conch shell like ears; one with fattened nose up 
to head; one with lean and long neck; one with disheveled hair and also one without hair; one with blanket like 
hair; one with hanging stomach and breasts; one with hanging face; one with lips at chin; one with hanging face; 
one with hanging knees; one who is short; one who is tall and also hunch backed one; one who is distorted; a dwarf 
one and also one with high teeth and one with crooked mouth, one with green eyes and one with a horrible face._END

B_5_C_1_159
BEGIN_
चरिते कैशिकाचार्यैरैरावतनिषेविते || ५-१-१७४
सिंहकुञ्जरशार्दूलपतगोरगवाहनैः |
विमानैः संपतद्भिश्च विमलैः समलंकृते || ५-१-१७५
वज्राशनिसमाघातैः पावकैरुपशोभिते |
कृतपुण्यैर्महाभागैः स्वर्गजिद्भिरलंकृते || ५-१-१७६
वहता हव्यमत्यर्थं सेविते चित्रभानुना |
ग्रहनक्षत्रचन्द्रार्कतारागणविभूषिते || ५-१-१७७
महर्षिगणगन्धर्वनागयक्षसमाकुले |
विविक्ते विमले विश्वे विश्वावसुनिषेविते || ५-१-१७८
देवराजगजाक्रान्ते चन्द्रसूर्यपथे शिवे |
विताने जीवलोकस्य वितते ब्रह्मनिर्मिते || ५-१-१७९
बहुशः सेविते वीरैर्विद्याधरगणैर्वरैः |
जगाम वायुमार्गे तु गरुत्मानिव मारुतिः || ५-१-१८०_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma went, like Garuda, in the sky served by clouds (or streams of water), served
also by birds, tread by masters of music Tumbura and other Gandharvas, served by Airavata, borne by
lions, elephants, tigers, birds and serpents, decorated by clear Vimanas moving with great speed,
shone by fires with thunderous jolt equal to that of Vajra - the weapon of Devendra, decorated by
people with good deeds, people with great luck who conquered the heavens, served by the God of fire
carrying great quantities of oblations, shone by planets, stars, moon, sun and starlets, occupied
by groups of great sages, Gandharvas, Nagas, Yakshas but unpopulated by humans, clear and all
pervasive, served by the gandharva king Vishvaavasu, roamed by elephants of Devendra, the path of
the moon and the sun, the auspicious one, a wide canopy of the earth constructed by Brahma, served
in various ways by excellent courageous groups of Vidyadharas._END

B_5_C_13_45
BEGIN_विनाशे बहवो दोषा जीवन् प्राप्नोति भद्रकम् || ५-१३-४७तस्मात् प्राणान् धरिष्यामि ध्रुवो 
जीवति सम्गमः |_END
BEGIN_"There are lots of blemishes in dying; one who is alive sees auspicious things. For that reason 
I will keep my life. It is definite for the meeting of people who are alive."_END

B_5_C_15_31
BEGIN_इयम् कनक वर्ण अन्गी रामस्य महिषी प्रिया |प्रनष्टा अपि सती यस्य मनसो न प्रणश्यति || 
	५-१५-४८_END
BEGIN_"This She of golden colour is indeed Rama's dear wife; who ever Seetha the chaste one, even 
	though not seen, is not gone from Rama's heart."_END

B_5_C_16_24
BEGIN_दुष्करम् कुरुते रामो हीनो यद् अनया प्रभुः |धारयति आत्मनो देहम् न दुह्खेन अवसीदति || ५-१६-२७_END
BEGIN_"Sri Rama although bereft of Her that Lord Rama is doing an impossible task by retaining His body 
and not being depressed by sorrow."_END

B_5_C_17_4
BEGIN_विकृताः पिङ्गलाः कालीः क्रोधनाः कलहप्रियाः |कालायसमहाशूलकूटमुद्गधारिणीः || ५-१७-९वराहमृगशार्दूलमहिषाजशिवामुखीः 
|गजोष्ट्र हयपादीश्च निखातशिरसोपराः || ५-१७-१०एकहस्तैकपादाश्च खरकर्ण्यश्वकर्णिकाः |गोकर्णीर्हस्तिकर्णीईश्च 
हरिकर्णीस्तथापराः || ५-१७-११अतिनासाश्च तिर्यङ्नासा अनासिकाः |गजनन्निभनासाश्च ललाटोच्च्वासनासिकाः || ५-१७-१२
हस्तिपादा महापादा गोपादाः पादचूळिकाः |अतिमात्रशिरोग्रीवा अतिमात्रकुचोदरीः || ५-१७-१३अतिमात्रस्यनेत्राश्च 
दीर्घजिह्वानखास्तथा |अजामुखीर्हस्तिमुखीर्गोमुखाः सूकरीमुखीः || ५-१७-१४हयोष्ट्रखरवक्त्राश्च राक्षसीर्घोरदर्शनाः 
|शूलमुद्गरहस्ताश्च क्रोधनाः कलहप्रियाः || ५-१७-१५कराळा धूम्रकेशीश्च राक्षसीर्विकृताननाः |पिबन्तीः 
सततं पानं सदा मां ससुराप्रियाः || ५-१७-१६मांसशोणितदिग्धाङ्गीर्मांसशोणितभोजनाः |ता ददर्श कपिश्रेष्ठो रोमहर्षणदर्शनाः 
|| ५-१७-१७स्कन्धवन्तमुपासीनाः परिवार्य वनस्पतिम् |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw horrible ogresses, dark complexioned ones, angry ones, those who like quarrels, ones 
wearing big darts, mallets and clubs of iron, with faces like those of pigs, deer, tigers, buffaloes, goats, she-foxes, 
with feet like those of elephants, camels, horses, with heads sunk into bodies, with single hand and single foot, 
those ears like that of donkeys and horses, those with cow ears, those with elephant ears, those with monkey ears, 
and some others without nose, those with horizontal nose, those with crooked nose, those with elephant-like nose, 
toes with nose fixed in forehead, with feet like those of elephant, those with big feet, those with cow like feet, 
those with hair on their feet, those with big heads and necks, those with big nipples and big stomach, those with 
big eyes and mouths, with long tongues and nails, and also the a face like that of a she-goat, those with elephant 
like face, those with face like that of a cow, those with face of a she-pig, those with faces like those of horses, 
camels, donkeys, those with horrible appearance, ogresses carrying pikes and clubs in their hand, angry ones, 
those who like quarrels, those with high teeth, with hair color like that of smoke, with horrible faces, always 
drinking liquor, always desiring meat and liquor, with body smeared by meat and blood, with meat and blood as 
food, whose appearance made hair to stand up, sitting around a great tree with huge trunk._END

B_5_C_13_46
BEGIN_एवम् बहु विधम् दुह्खम् मनसा धारयन् मुहुः || ५-१३-४८न अध्यगच्चत् तदा पारम् शोकस्य कपि कुन्जरः 
|_END
BEGIN_Hanuma carrying in mind sorrow of various kinds again and again did not get then the crossing of 
sorrow._END

B_5_C_1_160
BEGIN_
प्रदृश्यमानः सर्वत्र हनुमान्मारुतात्मजः |
भेजेऽम्बरं निरालम्बं लम्बपक्ष इवाद्रिराट् || ५-१-१८१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the son of Vayu, visible everywhere, obtained the sky without support, like
the king of birds with long wings._END

B_5_C_15_32
BEGIN_इयम् सा यत् कृते रामः चतुर्भिः परितप्यते |कारुण्येन आनृशंस्येन शोकेन मदनेन च || ५-१५-४९
	स्त्री प्रनष्टा इति कारुण्याद् आश्रिता इति आनृशंस्यतः |पत्नी नष्टा इति शोकेन प्रियेति मदनेन च || ५-१५-५०_END
BEGIN_"This is She for whose sake Rama tormented in four ways from compassion from pity from grief 
	from love; (thinking that) a woman has disappeared from compassion, depending on him from pity, wife has been 
	lost from grief, a dear one from love."_END

B_5_C_16_25
BEGIN_इमाम् असित केश अन्ताम् शत पत्र निभ ईक्षणाम् |सुख अर्हाम् दुःखिताम् ज्~आत्वा मम अपि व्यथितम् 
मनः || ५-१६-२८_END
BEGIN_"Knowing Her with black ended hairs, with lotus like eyes, deserving of comforts, and in sorrow, 
my mind also is gloomy."_END

B_5_C_17_5
BEGIN_तस्याधस्ताच्च ताम् देवीम् राजपुत्रीमनिन्दिताम् || ५-१७-१८लक्षयामास लक्ष्मीवान् हनुमान् 
जन्कात्मजाम् |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma the glorious one saw that Seetha, the princess, daughter of Janaka, unblemished one below 
that tree._END

B_5_C_18_0
BEGIN_तथा विप्रेक्षमाणस्य वनम् पुष्पितपादपम् |विचिन्वतश्च वैदेहीम् किंचिच्चेषा निशाभवत् || ५-१८-१_END
BEGIN_A little of the night was left while Hanuma was searching like that for Seetha in the garden with 
flowers in blossom._END

B_5_C_13_47
BEGIN_रावणम् वा वधिष्यामि दशग्रीवम् महा बलम् || ५-१३-४९कामम् अस्तु हृता सीता प्रत्याचीर्णम् 
भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise I will kill Ravana with ten heads, with great prowess. Whatever happened to the stolen 
Seetha, this will be revenge to that."_END

B_5_C_1_161
BEGIN_
प्लवमानं तु तं दृष्ट्वा सिंहिका नाम राक्षसी |
मनसा चिन्तयामास प्रवृद्धा कामरूपिणी || ५-१-१८२_END
BEGIN_
A demoness by the name of Simhika with the power to assume desired form, saw Hanuma
flying, increased in size and thought thus in her mind._END

B_5_C_16_26
BEGIN_क्षिति क्षमा पुष्कर सम्निभ अक्षी |या रक्षिता राघव लक्ष्मणाभ्याम् |सा राक्षसीभिर् विकृत 
ईक्षणाभिः |सम्रक्ष्यते सम्प्रति वृक्ष मूले || ५-१६-२९_END
BEGIN_"Whoever Seetha with earth-like patience, with eyes resembling lotuses, was protected by Sri Rama 
and Lakshmana, that Seetha now is being guarded by ogresses with crooked eyes at the base of a tree."_END

B_5_C_15_33
BEGIN_अस्या देव्या यथा रूपम् अन्ग प्रत्यन्ग सौष्ठवम् |रामस्य च यथा रूपम् तस्य इयम् असित 
	ईक्षणा || ५-१५-५१_END
BEGIN_"In whatever way is this lady's appearance, elegance of major and minor limbs, in the same 
	way is Rama's. In whatever way His appearance, in the same way is this black-eyed one's appearance."_END

B_5_C_17_6
BEGIN_निष्प्रभाम् षोकसन्तप्ताम् मलसम्कुलमूर्धजाम् || ५-१७-१९क्षीणपुण्याम् च्युताम् भूमौ ताराम् 
निपतितामिव |_END
BEGIN_She was lack luster being tormented by grief, with hair covered by dirt, with merits exhausted, 
like star fallen from heavens onto ground._END

B_5_C_13_48
BEGIN_अथवा एनम् समुत्क्षिप्य उपरि उपरि सागरम् || ५-१३-५०रामाय उपहरिष्यामि पशुम् पशु पतेर् इव 
|_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise carrying this Ravana over the surface of ocean I will take him to Rama like an animal 
to the lord of animals."_END

B_5_C_1_162
BEGIN_
अद्य दीर्ग़्हस्य कालस्य भविष्याम्यहामाशिता |
इदं हि मे महत्सत्त्वं चिरस्य वशमागतम् || ५-१-१८३_END
BEGIN_
"After a long time, this great animal came into my grasp. After long time, today I
will enjoy my meal."_END

B_5_C_18_1
BEGIN_षडङ्गवेदविदुषाम् क्रतुप्रवरयाजिनाम् |शुश्राव ब्रह्मघोषान् स विरात्रे ब्रह्मरक्षसाम् || 
५-१८-२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma heard Vedic sounds early in the morning of Brahma Rakshasas well versed in six parts 
of Vedas and those who performed excellent sacrifices._END

B_5_C_16_27
BEGIN_हिम हत नलिनी इव नष्ट शोभा |व्यसन परम्परया निपीड्यमाना |सह चर रहिता इव चक्र वाकी |
जनक सुता कृपणाम् दशाम् प्रपन्ना || ५-१६-३०_END
BEGIN_"With lost glory like a lotus plant hit by snow, being tormented by a series of calamities, Seetha 
obtained a pitiable condition like a chakravaka bird without a companion."_END

B_5_C_15_34
BEGIN_अस्या देव्या मनः तस्मिमः तस्य च अस्याम् प्रतिष्ठितम् |तेन इयम् स च धर्म आत्मा मुहूर्तम् 
	अपि जीवति || ५-१५-५२_END
BEGIN_"This lady's heart is in Rama, His heart is firmly in Her, for that reason She and that noble 
	Rama are able to live even for a moment."_END

B_5_C_17_7
BEGIN_चारित्रव्यपदेशाड्यां भर्तृदर्शनदुर्गताम् || ५-१७-२०भूषणैरुत्तमोर्हीनाम् भर्तृवात्सल्यभूषणाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_She was rich with fame of lofty character, poor due to not seeing husband, lacking excellent ornaments, 
with husband's love as ornament._END

B_5_C_13_49
BEGIN_इति चिन्ता समापन्नः सीताम् अनधिगम्य ताम् || ५-१३-५१ध्यान शोका परीत आत्मा चिन्तयाम् आस 
वानरः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma not seeing that Seetha thus begetting sorrow, thought with a mind cluttered with thoughts 
and sorrow._END

B_5_C_1_163
BEGIN_
इति संचिन्त्य मनसा छायामस्य समाक्षिपत् |
छायायां गृह्यमाणायां चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-१-१८४_END
BEGIN_
Thinking thus in her mind, Simhika attracted His shadow. While the shadow was thus
being grasped, Hanuma thought thus._END

B_5_C_18_2
BEGIN_अथ मङ्गलवादित्रशब्दैः श्रुतिमनोहरैः |प्रबुध्यत महाबाहुर्दशग्रीवो महाबलः || ५-१८-३_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Ravana with great arms and great prowess was woken by the sounds of various auspicious 
musical instruments pleasing to the ear._END

B_5_C_16_28
BEGIN_अस्या हि पुष्प अवनत अग्र शाखाः |शोकम् दृढम् वै जनयति अशोकाः |हिम व्यपायेन च शीतरश्मिः 
|रभ्युत्थितो न एक सहस्र रश्मिः || ५-१६-३१_END
BEGIN_"Ashoka trees with bent branches due to flowers are giving rise to gloom a lot to Her; Due to melting 
of snow the risen up moon also with thousands of rays is causing grief."_END

B_5_C_15_35
BEGIN_दुष्करम् कुरुते रामो इमाम् मत्त काशिनीम् |सीताम् विना महा बाहुः मुहूर्तम् अपि जीवति 
	|| ५-१५-५३_END
BEGIN_"Lord Rama losing Her has done an impossible task in that He still preserved His body, in that 
	He did not die from grief."_END

B_5_C_17_8
BEGIN_राक्षसाधिपसम्रुद्धाम् बन्धुभिश्च विना कृताम् || ५-१७-२१वियूथाम् सिम्हसम्रुद्धाम् बद्धाम् 
गजवधूमिव |_END
BEGIN_Being held captive by Ravana, without any relatives, She was like a she-elephant without herd, 
being detained by a lion._END

B_5_C_13_50
BEGIN_यावत् सीताम् न पश्यामि राम पत्नीम् यशस्विनीम् || ५-१३-५२तावद् एताम् पुरीम् लन्काम् विचिनोमि 
पुनः पुनः |_END
BEGIN_"To wherever I see Seetha, the wife of Sri Rama and one with fame, till there I will search the 
city of Lanka again and again."_END

B_5_C_1_164
BEGIN_
समाक्षिप्तोऽस्मि तरसा पञूकृतपराक्रमः |
प्रतिलोमेन वातेन महानौरिव सागरे || ५-१-१८५_END
BEGIN_
"Like a great boat in the ocean with opposing winds, I am being pulled back
forcefully, with disabled power."_END

B_5_C_18_3
BEGIN_विबुध्य तु यथाकालम् राक्षसेन्द्रः प्रतापवान् |स्रस्तमाल्याम्बरधरो वैदेहीमन्वचिन्तयात् 
|| ५-१८-४_END
BEGIN_The king of rakshasas with great might woke up at the appropriate hour wearing slippery flower 
garlands remembered about Seetha._END

B_5_C_16_29
BEGIN_इति एवम् अर्थम् कपिर् अन्ववेक्ष्य |सीता इयम् इति एव निविष्ट बुद्धिः |संश्रित्य तस्मिन् 
निषसाद वृक्षे |बली हरीणाम् ऋषभः तरस्वी || ५-१६-३२_END
BEGIN_The mighty one, the best among vanaras, quick one, Hanuma thus observed the subject: "This is Seetha!" 
- thus with a firm mind sat at that tree, leaning against it._END

B_5_C_15_36
BEGIN_एवम् सीताम् तदा दृष्ट्वा हृष्टः पवन सम्भवः |जगाम मनसा रामम् प्रशशंस च तम् प्रभुम् 
	|| ५-१५-५४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, then seeing Seetha became happy thus and went by mind to Rama and also praised that 
	Lord._END

B_5_C_17_9
BEGIN_चन्द्ररेखाम् पयोदान्ते शारदाब्रैरिवावृताम् || ५-१७-२२क्लिष्टरूपामसंस्पर्शादयुक्तामिव वल्लकीम् 
|_END
BEGIN_She was like moon being covered by clouds at the end of rainy season with an appearance lacking 
lustre due to lack of contact with husband, was like an unplucked Veena._END

B_5_C_13_51
BEGIN_सम्पाति वचनाच् च अपि रामम् यदि आनयामि अहम् || ५-१३-५३अपश्यन् राघवो भार्याम् निर्दहेत् 
सर्व वानरान् |_END
BEGIN_"Based on words of Sampati if I bring Sri Rama then Sri Rama not seeing wife will burn all Vanaras."_END

B_5_C_1_165
BEGIN_
तिर्यगूर्ध्वमधश्चैव वीक्षिमाणस्ततः कपिः |
ददर्श स महत्सत्त्वमुत्थितं लवणाम्भसि || ५-१-१८६_END
BEGIN_
After that, Hanuma looking sideways, upwards and downwards, saw a big animal raised
up in the salty ocean._END

B_5_C_18_4
BEGIN_भृशं नियुक्तस्तस्याम् च मदनेन मदोत्कटः |न स तं राक्षसः कामं शशाकात्मनि गूहितुम् || ५-१८-५_END
BEGIN_In that Seetha's matter, directed a lot by the god of love and excited by passion, that Rakshasa 
was not capable to suppress in self that desire._END

B_5_C_17_10
BEGIN_स ताम् भर्तवशे युक्तामयुक्ताम् राक्षसीवशे || ५-१७-२३अशोकवनिकामध्ये शोकसागरमाप्लुताम् |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Seetha being suited to be with her husband, in the custody of ogresses, in the middle 
of Ashoka garden being immersed in an ocean of grief_END

B_5_C_1_166
BEGIN_
छाय्तद्धृष्ट्वा चिन्तयामास मारुतिर्विकृताननम् |
कपिराजेन कथितं सत्त्वमद्भुतदर्शनम् || ५-१-१८७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma saw that animal with a horrible face and thought: "This animal with a strange
appearance, with great strength attracting shadow, is indeed the animal that had been told by
Sugriva. There is no doubt in that."_END

B_5_C_13_52
BEGIN_इह एव नियत आहारो वत्स्यामि नियत इन्द्रियः || ५-१३-५४न मत् कृते विनश्येयुः सर्वे ते नर 
वानराः |_END
BEGIN_"With limited food and with restrained senses, I live here itself. By my deed those men and vanaras 
- let they not be destroyed."_END

B_5_C_18_5
BEGIN_स सर्वाभरणैर्युक्तो बिभच्छ्रियमनुत्तमाम् |तां नगैर्बहुभिर्जुष्टाम् सर्वपुष्पफलोपगैः || 
५-१८-६_END
BEGIN_Together with all ornaments wearing great glory that Ravana entered that Ashoka garden having a 
lot of trees with all fruits and flowers._END

B_5_C_19_0
BEGIN_तस्मिन्नेव ततः काले राजपुत्री त्वनिन्दिता |रूपयौवनसम्पन्नं भूषणोत्तमभूषितम् || ५-१९-१
ततो दृष्ट्वैव वैदेही रावणम् राक्षसाधिपम् |प्रावेपत वरारोहा प्रवाते कदली यथा || ५-९-२_END
BEGIN_Thereafter at that time Seetha a princess without any blame of excellent limbs shook like a plantain 
tree in wind on seeing Ravana the king of rakshasas endowed with beauty and youth adorned with excellent ornaments._END

B_5_C_17_11
BEGIN_ताभिः परिवृताम् तत्र सग्रहामिव रोहिणीम् || ५-१७-२४ददर्श हनुमान् देवीम् लतामकुसुमामिव |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Seetha there surrounded by those ogresses, like Rohini with planets, like a creeper 
without flowers._END

B_5_C_13_53
BEGIN_अशोक वनिका च अपि महती इयम् महा द्रुमा || ५-१३-५५इमाम् अभिगमिष्यामि न हि इयम् विचिता मया 
|_END
BEGIN_"Whatever this Ashoka garden with great trees is being seen this I will obtain. This has not been 
searched by me."_END

B_5_C_1_167
BEGIN_
आग्राहि महावीर्यं तदिदं नात्र संशयः |
स तां बुद्ध्वार्थतत्त्वेन सिंहिकां मतिमान्कपिः |
व्यवर्धत महाकायः प्रवृषीव वलाहकः || ५-१-१८८_END
BEGIN_
That wise Hanuma recognizing that animal correctly as Simhika, increased His body
greatly, like a cloud in rainy season._END

B_5_C_18_6
BEGIN_वृतां पुष्करिणीभिश्च नानापुष्पोपशोभिताम् |सदामदैश्च विहगैर्विचित्राम् परमाद्भुताम् || 
५-१८-७_END
BEGIN_Ravana entered that great wonderful Ashoka garden together with lakes, shone by various flowers, 
brilliant with birds always in rut._END

B_5_C_19_1
BEGIN_आच्छाद्योदरमूरुभ्यां बाहुभ्यां च पयोधरौ |उपविष्टा विशालाक्षी रुदन्ती वरवर्णिनी || ५-१९-३_END
BEGIN_The wide eyed Seetha with excellent color covering stomach with thighs and breasts with hands sat 
down crying._END

B_5_C_17_12
BEGIN_सा मलेन च दिग्धाङ्गीवपुषा चाप्यलंकृता || ५-१७-२५मृणाली पङ्कदिग्धेव विभाति च न भाति च |_END
BEGIN_With body smeared with dirt, being graced by Her body, that Seetha shone and also did not shine, 
like a lotus-fibre covered with dirt._END

B_5_C_13_54
BEGIN_वसून् रुद्रामः तथा आदित्यान् अश्विनौ मरुतो अपि च || ५-१३-५६नमः कृत्वा गमिष्यामि रक्षसाम् 
शोक वर्धनः |_END
BEGIN_"Saluting the eight Vasus, Rudras and Adityas, the two Aswinis, seven Maruts, I will go to increase 
the grief of Rakshasas."_END

B_5_C_1_168
BEGIN_
तस्य सा कायमुद्वीक्ष्य वर्धमानं महाकपेः || ५-१-१८९
वक्त्रं प्रसारयामास पाताळान्तरसन्निभम् |_END
BEGIN_
That Simhika seeing the growing body of the great monkey Hanuma, spread her mouth to
be equal to the middle of Patala._END

B_5_C_18_7
BEGIN_ईहामृगैश्च विविधैर्जुष्टां डृष्टिमनोहरैः |वीथीः संप्रेक्षमाणश्च मणिकाञ्चनतोरणाः || ५-१८-८
नानामृगगणाकीर्णां फलैः प्रपतितैर्वृताम् |अशोकवनकामेव प्राविशत्संततद्रुमाम् || ५-१८-९_END
BEGIN_Ravana entered Ashoka garden seeing archways of gold and gems crowded by artificial deer of various 
kinds ravishing eyes and mind, filled with animals of various kinds, together with fallen fruits and full of trees._END

B_5_C_19_2
BEGIN_दशग्रीवस्तु वैदेहीम् रक्षितां राक्षसीगणैः |ददर्श दीनाम् दुःखार्तां नावं सन्नामिवार्णवे 
|| ५-१९-४_END
BEGIN_Ravana saw Seetha protected by batches of ogres looking miserable being struck with grief like 
a ship in danger in the sea._END

B_5_C_17_13
BEGIN_मलिनेन तु वस्त्रेण परिक्लिष्टेन भामिनीम् || ५-१७-२६संवृताम् मृगशाबाक्षीं ददर्श हनुमान् 
कपिः |ताम् देवीं दीनवदनामदीनां भर्तृतेजसा || ५-१७-२७रक्षिताम् स्वेन शीलेन सीतामसितलोचनाम् |_END
BEGIN_The monkey Hanuma saw that Seetha with great beauty with black eyes, covered by a cloth which was 
creased and dirty, with eyes of a deer, with a pitiful face, not depressed due to the brilliance of her husband, 
protected by her own character._END

B_5_C_13_55
BEGIN_जित्वा तु राक्षसान् देवीम् इक्ष्वाकु कुल नन्दिनीम् || ५-१३-५७सम्प्रदास्यामि रामाया यथा 
सिद्धिम् तपस्विने |_END
BEGIN_"Defeating all rakshasas, I will give Seetha, who gives happiness to Ikshvaaku dynasty to Sri Rama 
as the fruit of austerity to an ascetic."_END

B_5_C_1_169
BEGIN_
घनराजीव गर्जन्ती वानरं सम्भिद्रवत् || ५-१-१९०
स ददर्श ततस्तस्या विवृतं सुमहन्मुखम् |
कायमात्रं च मेधावी मर्माणि च महाकपिः || ५-१-१९१_END
BEGIN_
Roaring like a dense cloud, she ran towards the Vanara. Then the wise Hanuma saw her
opened very big mouth equal to His own body and also her internal organs._END

B_5_C_18_8
BEGIN_अङ्गनाशतमात्रं तु तं व्रजन्तमनुव्रजत् |महेन्द्रमिव पौलस्त्यम्ं देवगन्धर्वयोषितः || ५-१८-१०_END
BEGIN_While He was going only a hundred of women followed that Ravana like Deva and Gandharva women following 
Indra._END

B_5_C_19_3
BEGIN_असंवृतायामासीनाम् धरण्याम् संशितव्रताम् |चिनां प्रपतितां भूमौ शाखामिव वनस्पतेः || ५-१९-५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Seetha sitting down on uncovered land, with a firm resolve, like a branch of a tree 
fallen down on earth being torn from the tree._END

B_5_C_17_14
BEGIN_ताम् दृष्ट्वा हनुमान् सीताम् मृगशाबनिभेक्षणाम् |मृगकन्यामिव त्रस्ताम् वीक्षमाणाम् समन्ततः 
|| ५-१७-२८दहन्तीमिव निःश्वासैर्वृक्षान् पल्लवधारिणः |सम्घातमिव शोकानाम् दुःखस्योर्मिमिवोथिताम् || ५-१७-२९_END
BEGIN_Hanuma became happy on seeing Seetha with eyes of a fawn, fearful like a she-deer, seeing trees 
with young shoots, as though being burnt by sighs, like a bundle of grief, with a wave of sorrow risen up._END

B_5_C_13_56
BEGIN_स मुहूर्तम् इव ध्यात्वा चिन्ता विग्रथित इन्द्रियः || ५-१३-५८उदतिष्ठन् महा बाहुर् हनूमान् 
मारुत आत्मजः |_END
BEGIN_The gloried son of Vayu that Hanuma got up with his senses tied by grief._END

B_5_C_1_170
BEGIN_
स तस्या विवृते वक्त्रे वज्रसंहननः कपिः |
संक्षिप्य मुहुरात्मानं निष्पपात महाबलः || ५-१-१९२_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma with great strength and with a body equal to a diamond, repeatedly
contracted His body and fell into her opened mouth._END

B_5_C_18_9
BEGIN_दीपिकाः काञ्चनीः काश्चिज्जगृहुस्तत्र योषितः |वालव्यजनहस्ताश्च तालवृन्तानि चापराः || ५-१८-११_END
BEGIN_There some women bore lamps of gold; some others carried chowries; some others had fans of Palmyra 
leaves in their hands._END

B_5_C_19_4
BEGIN_मलमण्डनचित्राङ्गीम् मण्डनार्हाममण्डिताम् |मृणाली पङ्कदिग्धेव विभाति न विभाति च || ५-१९-६_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Seetha with a stange body with dirt as ornament, who although suited to decorate with 
ornaments was without ornaments. Although She was shining like a lotus stem covered with mud, She was not shining 
also._END

B_5_C_17_15
BEGIN_ताम् क्षमां सुविभक्ताङ्गीं विनाभरणशोभिनीम् |प्रहर्षमतुलम् लेभे मारुतिः प्रेक्ष्य मैथिलीम् 
|| ५-१७-३०_END
BEGIN_Hanuma the son of wind god on seeing Seetha that Seetha like the goddess earth, with well divided 
body parts shining eve without ornaments, obtained great joy._END

B_5_C_13_57
BEGIN_नमो अस्तु रामाय सलक्ष्मणाय |देव्यै च तस्यै जनक आत्मजायै |नमो अस्तु रुद्र इन्द्र यम 
अनिलेभ्यो |नमो अस्तु चन्द्र अर्क मरुद् गणेभ्यः || ५-१३-५९_END
BEGIN_"Let there be salutations to Sri Rama together with Lakshmana, also to that, who is divine let 
there be salutations. To Rudra, Indra, Yama and Vaayu let there be salutations."_END

B_5_C_1_171
BEGIN_
आस्ये तस्या निमज्जन्तं ददृशुः सिद्धचारणाः |
ग्रस्यमानं यथा चन्द्रं पूर्णं पर्वणि राहुणा || ५-१-१९३_END
BEGIN_
Siddhas and Charanas saw Hanuma sinking in her mouth, like the full moon on a full
moon day being swallowed by Rahu._END

B_5_C_18_10
BEGIN_काञ्चनैरपि भृङ्गारैर्जह्रुः सलिलमग्रतः |मण्डलागान् ब्रुसींश्चापि गृह्यान्याः पृष्ठतो ययुः 
|| ५-१८-१२_END
BEGIN_Some women carried water in small vessels of gold; some others followed in the back taking pillows 
with circular ends._END

B_5_C_19_5
BEGIN_समीपम् राजसिम्हस्य रामस्य विदितात्मनः |सङ्कल्पहयसम्युक्तैर्यान्तीमिव मनोरथैः || ५-१९-७_END
BEGIN_Seetha was as though going near to Rama a lion among kings with a famous personality with desires 
as chariot tied with thoughts as horses._END

B_5_C_17_16
BEGIN_हर्षजानि च सोऽश्रूणि ताम् दृष्ट्वा मदिरेक्षणाम् |मुमुचे हनुमांस्तत्र नमश्चक्रे च राघवम् 
|| ५-१७-३१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma on seeing Seetha there with intoxicating eyes shed tears of joy and also paid obeisance 
to Sri Rama._END

B_5_C_13_58
BEGIN_स तेभ्यः तु नमः कृत्वा सुग्रीवाय च मारुतिः |दिशः सर्वाः समालोक्य अशोक वनिकाम् प्रति || 
५-१३-६०_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saluting to all those and also to Sugreeva, observing all directions went towards Ashoka 
garden._END

B_5_C_1_172
BEGIN_
ततस्तस्या नखैस्तीक्णैर्मर्माण्युत्कृत्य वानरः |
उत्पपाताथ वेगेन मनः संपातविक्रमः || ५-१-१९४_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma rend her internal organs with His sharp nails and after that flew up
with a speed equal to that of thought._END

B_5_C_18_11
BEGIN_काचिद्रत्नमयीं स्थालीं पूर्णां पानस्य ब्राजतम् |दक्षिणा दक्षिणेनैव तदा जग्राह पाणिना || 
५-१८-१३_END
BEGIN_One woman to the right of Ravana held with her right hand a vessel with gem stones filled with 
liqour._END

B_5_C_19_6
BEGIN_शुष्यन्तीम् रुदतीमेकां ध्यानशोकपरायणाम् |दुःखस्यान्तमपश्यन्तीं रामां राममनुव्रताम् || 
५-१९-८_END
BEGIN_Seetha a pleasant one, was emaciated, was crying, being alone having surrendered to Her thoughts 
and sorrow not seeing the end of grief, following the will of Rama._END

B_5_C_17_17
BEGIN_नमस्कृत्वा रामाय लक्ष्मणाय च वीर्यवान् |सीतादर्शनसम्हृष्टो हनुमान् सम्वृतोऽभवत् || ५-१७-३२_END
BEGIN_Being joyful on seeing Seetha, Hanuma the mighty one paid obeisance to Sri Rama and to Lakshmana 
and became covered with leaves._END

B_5_C_20_0
BEGIN_स ताम् परिवृतां दीनां निरानन्दां तपस्विनीम् |साकारैर्मधुरैर्वाक्यैर्न्यदर्शयत रावणः || 
५-२०-१_END
BEGIN_Ravana conveyed in significant words to that Seetha who was surrounded by ogresses, wretched, without 
happiness and pitiable._END

B_5_C_13_59
BEGIN_स गत्वा मनसा पूर्वम् अशोक वनिकाम् शुभाम् |उत्तरम् चिन्तयाम् आस वानरो मारुत आत्मजः || ५-१३-६१_END
BEGIN_The son of Vayu, that Vanara went by mind before itself toward that Ashoka garden. The auspicious 
one pondered the task to be done later._END

B_5_C_1_173
BEGIN_
तां तु दृष्ट्वा च धऋत्या च दाक्षिण्येन निपात्य च |
स कपिप्रवरो वेगाद्ववृधे पुनरात्मवान् || ५-१-१९५_END
BEGIN_
That wise Hanuma felling Simhika down with His vision, courage and ability,
developed again by speed._END

B_5_C_18_12
BEGIN_राजहंसप्रतीकाशं चत्रं पूर्णशशिप्रभम् |सौवर्णदण्डमपरा गृहीत्वा पृष्ठतो ययौ || ५-१८-१४_END
BEGIN_Another woman went at back taking an umbrella equalling a royal swan with the radiance of full 
moon with a golden handle._END

B_5_C_19_7
BEGIN_चेष्टमानां तथाविष्टां पन्नगेन्द्रवधूमिव |धूप्यमानाम् ग्रहेणेव रोहिणीं धूमकेतुना || ५-१९-९_END
BEGIN_And also Seetha was like a great she-serpant writhing under the spell of an incantation. She was 
like Rohini being fumigated by a smoke colored planet called Ketu._END

B_5_C_20_1
BEGIN_मां दृष्ट्वा नागनासोरु गूहमाना स्तनोदरम् |अदर्शनमिवात्मानं भयान्नेतुं त्वमिच्चसि || ५-२०-२_END
BEGIN_"You are with thighs like the trunk of an elephant. Seeing me covering your breasts and belly, 
you desire obtaining disappearance of self due to fear._END

B_5_C_13_60
BEGIN_ध्रुवम् तु रक्षो बहुला भविष्यति वन आकुला |अशोक वनिका चिन्त्या सर्व संस्कार संस्कृता || 
५-१३-६२_END
BEGIN_"The Ashoka garden definitely will be with many rakshasas, filled with trees, adorned with various 
cultures and sacred."_END

B_5_C_1_174
BEGIN_
हृतहृत्सा हनुमता पपात विधुराम्भसि |
तां हतां वानरेणाशु पतितां वीक्ष्य सिंहिकाम् || ५-१-१९६
भूतान्याकाशचारीणी तमूचुः प्लवगोत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
That Simhika with heart rend by Hanuma fell in water with sorrow. Seeing Simhika
killed by Hanuma, creatures roaming in the sky spoke thus to that best among Vanaras._END

B_5_C_18_13
BEGIN_निद्रामदपरीताक्ष्यो रावनस्योत्तमाः स्त्रियः |अनुजग्मुः पतिं वीरम् घनम् विद्युल्लता इव 
|| ५-१८-१५_END
BEGIN_With sleepy eyes best women of Ravana followed mighty husband like lightning following a cloud._END

B_5_C_19_8
BEGIN_वृत्तशीलकुले जातामाचारवति धार्मिके |पुनः संस्कारमापन्नां जातामिव च दुष्कुले || ५-१९-१०_END
BEGIN_Being born in a virtuous traditional family with good conduct and character and getting married, 
Seetha appeared as if She was born in a bad family._END

B_5_C_20_2
BEGIN_कामये त्वाम् विशालाक्षि बहुमन्यस्व मां प्रिये |सर्वाङ्गगुणसम्पन्ने सर्वलोकमनोहरे || ५-२०-३_END
BEGIN_"O wide eyed one! You are endowed with bodily excellencies, pleasing to all people. I desire you. 
O lovable one! respect me."_END

B_5_C_13_61
BEGIN_रक्षिणः च अत्र विहिता नूनम् रक्षन्ति पादपान् |भगवान् अपि सर्व आत्मा न अतिक्षोभम् प्रवायति 
|| ५-१३-६३सम्क्षिप्तो अयम् मया आत्मा च राम अर्थे रावणस्य च |_END
BEGIN_"There definitely guards will be protecting assigned, trees, omnipresent Lord Vayu also will be 
blowing by without force, and by me this body has been made small for the sake of Sri Rama and to avoid Ravana."_END

B_5_C_18_14
BEGIN_व्याविद्धहारकेयूराः समामृदितवर्णकाः |समागळितकेशान्ताः सस्वेदवदनास्तथा || ५-१८-१६घोर्णन्त्यो 
मदशेषेण निद्रया च शुभाननाः |स्वेदक्लिष्टाङ्गकुसुमाः सुमाल्याकुलमूर्धजाः || ५-१८-१७प्रयान्तं नैरृतपतिं 
नार्यो मदिरलोचनाः |बहुमानाच्च कामाच्च प्रिया भार्यास्तमन्वयुः || ५-१८-१८_END
BEGIN_With displaced necklaces and armlets, with effaced cover of sandal-paste, with dishevelled hair, 
and also with sweaty faces, staggering due to surviving trace of liquor and due to sleepiness, with shrivelled 
flowers on perspiring bodies, with dishevelled hair along with good garlands, with intoxicating eyes, women who 
were dear wives followed that king of Rakshasas who was going due to respect and due to love._END

B_5_C_1_175
BEGIN_
भीममद्य कृतं कर्म महत्सत्त्वं त्वया हतम् || ५-१-१९७
साधयार्थमभिप्रेतमरिष्टं प्लवतां वर |_END
BEGIN_
"O best among Vanaras! A huge animal has been killed by you. A great task has been
done. Perform the task dear to you auspiciously."_END

B_5_C_19_9
BEGIN_अभूतेनापवादेन कीर्तीम् निपतितामिव |अम्नायानामयोगेन विद्यां प्रशिथिलामिव || ५-१९-११_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like fame fallen down due to false blame. She was like education ruined due to lack 
of learning by heart._END

B_5_C_20_3
BEGIN_नेह केचिन्मनुष्या वा राक्षसाः कामरूपिणः |व्यपसर्पतु ते सीते भयम् मत्तः समुत्थितम् || ५-२०-४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Here there are no humans or ogres with ability to change form. Let your fear caused 
due to me be removed."_END

B_5_C_13_62
BEGIN_सिद्धिम् मे सम्विधास्यन्ति देवाः सर्षि गणाः त्व् इह || ५-१३-६४ब्रह्मा स्वयम्भूर् भगवान् 
देवाः चैव दिशन्तु मे |सिद्धिम् अग्निः च वायुः च पुरु हूतः च वज्रधृत् || ५-१३-६५वरुणः पाश हस्तः च सोम आदित्यै 
तथैव च |अश्विनौ च महात्मानौ मरुतः सर्व एव च || ५-१३-६६सिद्धिम् सर्वाणि भूतानि भूतानाम् चैव यः प्रभुः |
दास्यन्ति मम ये च अन्ये अदृष्टाः पथि गोचराः || ५-१३-६७_END
BEGIN_"Devas together with ascetics will make success to me here, self born Brahma the divine one and 
devas and Agni and Vaayu, Devendra wearing the weapon of Vajra and Varuna with Pasha in hand and also the Sun 
and the moon and the aswinis. The great ones Maruts and Eshwara may give my success. Whoever is the lord of all 
living creatures among all living beings others who being unseen exist in the path may give success to me."_END

B_5_C_18_15
BEGIN_स च कामपराधीनः पतिस्तासां महाबलः |सीतासक्तमना मन्दो मन्दाञ्चितगतिर्बभौ || ५-१८-१९_END
BEGIN_Husband of those women, of great might, who was surrendered to lust, that Ravana also who was dull 
witted, with his mind interested in Seetha shone with a slow and beautiful gait._END

B_5_C_1_176
BEGIN_
यस्य त्वेतानि चत्वारि वानरेन्द्र यथा तव || ५-१९८
धृतिर्दृष्टिर्मतिर्दाक्ष्यं स कर्मसु न सीदति |_END
BEGIN_
"O best among Vanaras! Whoever has the four qualities of courage, vision, intellect
and skill, all these four virtues like you, such a person will not fail in any task."_END

B_5_C_19_10
BEGIN_सन्नामिव महाकीर्तिं श्रद्धामिव विमानिताम् |प्रज्ञामिव परिक्षीणामाशां प्रतिहतामिव || ५-१९-१२_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like deteriorated great fame,like insulted faith,like an understanding grown feeble, 
like dulled hope._END

B_5_C_20_4
BEGIN_स्वधर्मो रक्षसां भीरु सर्वथैव न संशयः |गमनं वा परस्त्रीणाम् हरणम् सम्प्रमथ्य वा || ५-२०-५_END
BEGIN_"O one with fear! Obtaining women belonging to others or abducting by force is the righteous deed 
for ogres by all means. There is no doubt in this."_END

B_5_C_13_63
BEGIN_तद् उन्नसम् पाण्डुर दन्तम् अव्रणम् |शुचि स्मितम् पद्म पलाश लोचनम् |द्रक्ष्ये तद् आर्या 
वदनम् कदा न्व् अहम् |प्रसन्न तारा अधिप तुल्य दर्शनम् || ५-१३-६८_END
BEGIN_"When will I see that noble face with a high nose, with white teeth without any injuries with a
