bright smile, with eyes resembling lotus petals with sight equaling the splendor of clear full moon?"_END

B_5_C_18_16
BEGIN_ततः काञ्चीनिनादं च नूपुराणाम् च निस्वनम् |शुश्राव परमस्त्रीणां स कपिर्मारुतात्मजः || ५-१८-२०_END
BEGIN_Thereafter that Hanuma, the son of wind-god heard the sound of waist-bands and the sound of anklets 
of those excellent women._END

B_5_C_1_177
BEGIN_
स तैः संभावितः पूज्यः प्रतिपन्नप्रयोजनः || ५-१-१९९
जगामाकाशमाविश्य पन्नगाशनवत्कपिः |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma the respectable one, thus respected by them, entered the sky and went
like the Garuda with a determined goal._END

B_5_C_19_11
BEGIN_आयतीमिव विध्वस्तामाज्ञां प्रतिहतामिव |दीप्तामिव दिशं काले पूजामपहृतामिव || ५-१९-१३_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like an expectation destroyed, like an order flouted; like a blazing quarter during 
a period of destruction, like a worship stolen._END

B_5_C_20_5
BEGIN_एवं चैतदकामां तु न त्वां स्प्रक्ष्यामि मैथिलि |कामम् कामः शरीरे मे यथाकामं प्रार्तताम् 
|| ५-२०-६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! It is like this. desire very much may behave in whatever way it likes in my body. But 
I will not touch you without lust."_END

B_5_C_13_64
BEGIN_क्षुद्रेण पापेन नृशंस कर्मणा |सुदारुण अलाम्कृत वेष धारिणा|बल अभिभूता अबला तपस्विनी 
|कथम् नु मे दृष्ट पथे अद्य सा भवेत् || ५-१३-६९_END
BEGIN_"How that powerless Seetha, a helpless one, forcefully taken away by the mean vile Ravana with 
a cruel action, with a horribly decorated form will fall in the range of my sight today."_END

B_5_C_18_17
BEGIN_तं चाप्रतिमकर्माणमचिन्त्यबलपौरुषम् |द्वारदेशमनुप्राप्तं ददर्श हनुमान् कपिः || ५-१८-२१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma the monkey saw that Ravana also, performer of deeds without an equal, with unfathomable 
might and virility, reaching the entrance region._END

B_5_C_1_178
BEGIN_
प्राप्तभूयिष्ठपारस्तु सर्वतः प्रतिलोकयन् || ५-१-२००
योजनानां शतस्यान्ते वनराजिं ददर्श सः |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma after almost reaching the other shore, looked in all directions and saw a
series of trees at the end of his journey of hundred yojanas._END

B_5_C_19_12
BEGIN_पद्मिनीमिव विध्वस्तां हतशूरां चमूमिव |प्रभामिव तमोध्वस्तामुपक्षीणामिवापगाम् || ५-१९-१४_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like a lotus destroyed, like an army with killed warriors, like light destroyed by darkness, 
like vanished river._END

B_5_C_20_6
BEGIN_देवि नेह भयम् कार्यम् मयि विश्वसिहि प्रिये |प्रणयस्व च तत्वएन मैवम् भूः शिकलालसा || ५-२०-७_END
BEGIN_"O queen of my heart! In this matter fear is not to be made. O love! Believe in me. Truly become 
with love. Do not become absorbed in sorrow like this."_END

B_5_C_21_0
BEGIN_तस्य तद्वचनम् श्रुत्वा सीता रौद्रस्य रक्षसः |आर्ता दीनस्वरा दीनम् प्रत्युवाच ततः शनैः 
|| ५-२१-१_END
BEGIN_Seetha listening to that horrible ogre's word, being tormented spoke in reply with a pitiable voice, 
pitifully and slowly._END

B_5_C_18_18
BEGIN_दीपिकाभिरनेकाभिः समन्तादवभासितम् |गन्धतैलावसिक्ताभिर्द्रियमाणाभिरग्रतः || ५-१८-२२_END
BEGIN_Wettened by fragrant oil, being carried in front of Ravana, Hanuma saw Ravana being shone in all 
directions by many lamps._END

B_5_C_1_179
BEGIN_
ददर्श च पतन्नेव विविधद्रुमभूषितम् || ५-१-२०१
द्वीपं शाखामृगश्रेष्ठो मलयोपवनानि च |_END
BEGIN_
The best among Vanaras, Hanuma, immediately after getting down also saw an island
decorated by a variety of trees and also the forests in the region of Malaya._END

B_5_C_19_13
BEGIN_वेदीमिव परामृष्टां शान्तामग्निशिखामिव |पौर्णमासीमिव निशां राहुग्रस्तेन्दुमण्डलाम् || ५-१९-१५_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like an altar desecrated, like a tongue of fire gone out, like a full moon night with 
moon devoured by Rahu._END

B_5_C_20_7
BEGIN_एकवेणी धराशय्या ध्यानं मलिनमम्बरम् |अस्थानेऽप्युपवासश्च नैतान्यौपयिकानि ते || ५-२०-८_END
BEGIN_"Single plait, the bed of ground,mediation,dirty cloth,fasting at an inappropriate time - all these 
are not useful to you."_END

B_5_C_21_1
BEGIN_दुःखार्ता रुदती सीता वेपमाना तपस्विनी |चिन्तयन्ती वरारोह पतिमेव पतिव्रता || ५-२१-२
तृणमन्तरतः कृत्वा प्रत्युवाच शुचिस्मिता |_END
BEGIN_Being tormented by grief, in a pitiful state, with excellent limbs, devoted to husband, thinking 
about husband alone, with pleasant smiles Seetha was sobbing, shivering and placing a straw in between herself 
and Ravana spoke thus in reply._END

B_5_C_18_19
BEGIN_कामदर्पमदैर्युक्तं जिह्मताम्रायतेक्षणम् |समक्षमिव कन्दर्पमपविद्धशरासनम् || ५-१८-२३_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Ravana together with lust, vanity and intoxication, with wide red eyes which were slanted, 
like the god of love in person with bow kept at a distance._END

B_5_C_1_180
BEGIN_
सागरं सागरानूपं सागरानूपजान् द्रुमान् || ५-१-२०२
सागरस्य च पत्नीनां मुखान्यपि विलोकयन् |
स महामेघसंकाशं समीक्ष्यात्मानमात्मवान् || ५-१-२०३
निरुन्धन्तमिवाकाशं चकार मतिमान् मतिम् |_END
BEGIN_
That Hanuma with controlled senses and with good thoughts looked at the ocean, the
bay and the trees born in the bay, and also the faces of the wives of the ocean (rivers are
considered wives of ocean), observed Himself to be equal in size to a great cloud as though
stopping the sky, and thought thus._END

B_5_C_19_14
BEGIN_उत्कृष्टपर्णकमलां वित्रासितविहङ्गमाम् |हस्तिहस्तपरामृष्टमाकुलां पद्मिनीमिव || ५-१९-१६_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like a lotus pond agitated with torned out leaves and lotuses, being roughly traeated 
by the trunk of an elephant._END

B_5_C_20_8
BEGIN_विचित्राणि च माल्यानि चन्दनान्यगरूणि च |विविधानि च वासांसि द्व्यान्याभरणानि च || ५-२०-९
महार्हणि च पानानि शयनान्यासनानि च |गीतम् नृत्तं च वाद्यं च लभ मं प्राप्य मैथिलि || ५-२०-१०_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! After getting me gain wonderful garlands, sandals, Agallochums, a variety of cloths 
and best ornaments, the best drinks, beds and seats, song and dance and musical instrument."_END

B_5_C_21_2
BEGIN_निवर्तय मनो मत्तः स्वजने क्रियतां मनः || ५-२१-३न मां प्रार्थयितुं युक्तं सुसिद्धिमिव पापकृत् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Turn your mind back from me. Let your mind be made on your own wives. Like best emancipation for 
a sinner, it is not appropriate to pray me."_END

B_5_C_1_181
BEGIN_
कायवृद्धिं प्रवेगं च मम दृष्ट्वव राक्षसाः || ५-१-२०४
मयि कौतूहलं कुर्युरिति मेने महाकपिः |_END
BEGIN_
"After seeing my huge body and the speed, Rakshasas will become curious." - thus
thought the great Hanuma._END

B_5_C_18_20
BEGIN_मथितामृतफेनाभमरजोवस्त्रमुत्तमम् |सलीलमनुकर्षन्तं विमुक्तं सक्तमङ्गदे || ५-१८-२४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Ravana playfully readjusting his excellent upper garment with the luster of churned 
nectar froth, without stain,slipping being entangled in armlet._END

B_5_C_19_15
BEGIN_पतिशोकातुरां शुष्कां नदीं विस्रावितामिव |परया मृजया हीनाम् कृष्णपक्षनिशामिव || ५-१९-१७_END
BEGIN_Grieved for husband, Seetha was like a river which has dried uo with water caused to flow out lacking 
best washing, was like a new moon night._END

B_5_C_20_9
BEGIN_स्त्रीरत्नमसि मैवम् भूः कुरु गात्रेषु भूषणम् |मां प्राप्य हि कथम् नु स्यास्त्वमनर्हा सुविग्रहे 
|| ५-२०-११_END
BEGIN_"You are a gem among women. Do not be like this. Make decoration on your limbs. O one with a good 
body! Getting me how will you become unsuited for luxuries?"_END

B_5_C_21_3
BEGIN_अकार्यम् न मया कार्यमेकपत्न्या विगर्हितम् || ५-२१-४कुलम् सम्प्राप्तया पुण्यम् कुले महति 
जातया |_END
BEGIN_"I was born in a great family. Getting such family, having one husband, a bad deed which is blameable 
is not to be made by me."_END

B_5_C_1_182
BEGIN_
ततः शरीरं संक्षिप्य तन्महीधरसन्निभम्|| ५-१-२०५
पुनः प्रकृतिमापेदे वीतमोह इवात्मवान् |_END
BEGIN_
For that reason, Hanuma reduced His mountain-like body and obtained the nature of
one who reached self-realization, free from infatuations._END

B_5_C_18_21
BEGIN_तं पत्रविटपे लीनः अत्रपुष्पघनावृतह् |समीपमिव संक्रान्तं निध्यातुमुपचक्रमे || ५-१८-२५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma blended in a branch full of leaves covered by groups of leaves and flowers started to see 
that Ravana as though coming near Him._END

B_5_C_19_16
BEGIN_सुकुमारीम् सुजाताङ्गीं रत्न गर्भगृहोचिताम् |तप्यमानामिवोष्णेन मृणालीमचिरोद्धृताम् || ५-१९-१८_END
BEGIN_Seetha was a delicate one with well built limbs, accustomed to houses full of diamonds, being tormented 
by heat, like a lotus fibre uprooted short time back._END

B_5_C_20_10
BEGIN_इदम् ते चारु सम्जातम् यौवनम् व्यतिवर्तते |यदतीतं पुनर्नैति स्रोतः शीघ्रमपामिव || ५-२०-१२_END
BEGIN_"This your youth born beautifully is passing away, whichever youth is quickly passing away will 
not come back again like the flow of water."_END

B_5_C_21_4
BEGIN_एवमुक्त्वा तु वैदेही रावणम् तम् यशस्विनी || ५-२१-५रावणम् पृष्ठतः कृत्वा भूयो वचनम्ब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_Seetha with renown thus speaking to that Ravana, turned back and spoke words again._END

B_5_C_1_183
BEGIN_
तद्रूपमतिसंक्षिप्य हनुमान् प्रकृतौ स्थितः || ५-१-२०६
त्रीन् क्रमानिव विक्रम्य बलिवीर्यहरो हरिः |_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma greatly reducing His size became normal in nature regaining His original
form, like Vishnu who mitigated the strength of Bali by taking three strides._END

B_5_C_18_22
BEGIN_अवेक्षमाणस्तु ततो ददर्श कपिकुञ्जरः |रूपयौवनसंपन्ना रावणस्य वरस्तियः || ५-१८-२६_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Hanuma, the best among Vanaras looking in all directions saw best women of Ravana full 
of beauty and youth._END

B_5_C_19_17
BEGIN_गृहीतामाळितां स्तम्भे यूथपेन विनाकृताम् |निःश्वसन्तीं सुदुःखार्तां गजराजवधूमिव || ५-१९-१९_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like a she-elephant captured and tied to a pillar, made to be without the leader of 
herd, sighing, very much tormented by grief._END

B_5_C_20_11
BEGIN_त्वां कृत्वोपरतो मन्ये रूपकर्ता स विश्वसृक् |न हि रूपोपमा त्वन्या तवास्ति शुभदर्शने || 
५-२०-१३_END
BEGIN_"O one with auspicious appearance! The creator of form, that creator of the world, Lord Brahma 
has made you and stopped - I think thus. There is not another who is equal to your appearance."_END

B_5_C_21_5
BEGIN_वाहमौपयिकी भार्या परभार्या सती तव || ५-२१-६साधु धर्ममवेक्षस्व साधु साधुव्रतम् चर |_END
BEGIN_"I who am wife of another and devoted to husband am not suitable wife to you. Observe righteousness 
well. Follow well course of conduct of virtuous."_END

B_5_C_1_184
BEGIN_
स चारुनानाविधरूपधारी |
परं समासाद्य समुद्रतीरम् |
परैरशक्यः प्रतिपन्नरूपः |
समीक्षितात्मा समवेक्षितार्थः || ५-१-२०७_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma capable of assuming many different beautiful forms, who cannot be defeated by
enemies, obtained the other side of ocean and being cognizant of Himself restored His own form and
became with a decided mission._END

B_5_C_18_23
BEGIN_ताभिः परिवृतो राजा सुरूपाभिर्महायशाः |तस्मृगद्विजसम्घष्टं प्रविष्टः प्रमदावनम् || ५-१८-२७_END
BEGIN_King of great fame, Ravana, together with those women with good appearance entered that garden 
resounded by animals and birds._END

B_5_C_19_18
BEGIN_एकया दीर्घया वेण्या शोभमानामयत्नतः |नीलया नीरदापाये वनराज्या महीमिव || ५-१९-२०_END
BEGIN_With a long single plait, shining without effort, Seetha was like the earth with dark groups of 
trees at the end of rainy season._END

B_5_C_20_12
BEGIN_त्वाम् समाअसाद्य वैदेहि रूपयौवनशालिनीम् |कः पुमानतिवर्तेत साक्षादपि पितामहः || ५-२०-१४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Obtaining you endowed with beauty and youth, which man even if he is Lord Brahma himself 
will disregard (leave) you."_END

B_5_C_21_6
BEGIN_यथा तव तथान्येषां दारा रक्ष्या विशाचर || ५-२१-७आत्मानमुपमां कृत्वा स्वेषु दारेषु रम्यताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"O Ogre! How your wives are to be protected, in the same way others' wives are to be protected. 
Making yourself as an example enjoy your own wives."_END

B_5_C_1_185
BEGIN_
ततः स लम्बस्य गिरेः समृद्धे |
विचित्रकूटे निपपात कूटे |
सकेतकोद्दालकनाळिकेरे |
महाभ्रकूटप्रतिमो महात्मा || ५-१-२०८_END
BEGIN_
After that great one who looked like a huge mass of clouds, alighted on the mountain
peak of Lamba with wonderful lower peaks, abundant with various things and filled with Ketaka,
Uddalaka and coconut trees._END

B_5_C_18_24
BEGIN_क्षीबो विचित्राभरणः शङ्कुकर्णो महाबलः |तेन विश्रवसः पुत्रः स दृष्टो राक्षसाधिपः || ५-१८-२८
वृतः परमनारीभिस्ताराभिरिव चन्द्रामाः |तं ददर्श महातेजास्तेजोवन्तं महाकपिः || ५-१८-२९_END
BEGIN_That king of Rakshasas who was intoxicated with wonderful ornaments, with pointed ears, son of 
Visravasa was like the moon together with stars, together with best women was seen by Hanuma. That great Vanara 
with great brilliance saw that Ravana with glory._END

B_5_C_19_19
BEGIN_उपवासेन शोकेन ध्यानेन च भयेन च |परिक्षीणां कृशां दीनामल्पाहारां तपोधनाम् || ५-१९-२१_END
BEGIN_Wasted, emaciated due to fasting, due to sorrow, due to thought and due to fear, Seetha was with 
limited food and with austerity as wealth._END

B_5_C_22_0
BEGIN_सीताय वचनं श्रुत्वा परुषं राक्षसेश्वरः |प्रत्युवाच ततः सीतां विप्रियं प्रियदर्शनम् || 
५-२२-१_END
BEGIN_Ravana listening to Seetha's words which were harsh thereafter replied to Seetha unpleasant words 
which are seen to be pleasant._END

B_5_C_20_13
BEGIN_यद्यत्पश्यामि ते गात्रम् शीतांशुसदृशानने |तस्मिंस्तस्मिन् पृधुश्रोणि चक्षुर्मम निबध्यते 
|| ५-२०-१५_END
BEGIN_"O one with face like that of moon! O one with broad hips! Your whichever limb I see, my eye is 
getting tied in that that limb."_END

B_5_C_21_7
BEGIN_अतुष्टं स्वेषु दारेषु चपलम् चलितेन्द्रियम् || ५-२१-८नयन्ति निकृतिप्रज्ञं परदाराः पराभवम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"One who is not satisfied in own wives, a fickle-minded one with disturbed senses, mean minded 
one, to such a man, others' wives will lead to humilation."_END

B_5_C_1_186
BEGIN_
ततस्तु संप्राप्य समुद्रतीरं |
समीक्ष्य लङ्कां गिरिवर्यमूर्ध्नि |
कपिस्तु तस्मिन्निपपात पर्वते |
विधूय रूपं व्यथयन्म्ऱृगद्विजान् || ५-१-२०९_END
BEGIN_
After that Hanuma for His part obtained the ocean shore, observed the city of Lanka
from the top of the mountain, leaving His original form, tormenting animals and birds, alighted on
that mountain._END

B_5_C_18_25
BEGIN_रावणोऽयम् महाबाहुरिति संचिन्त्य वानरः |अवप्लुतो महातेजा हनुमान्मारुतात्मजः || ५-१८-३०_END
BEGIN_The son of god of wind Vanara Hanuma of great brilliance thinking thus "This long armed one is 
Ravana", jumped down._END

B_5_C_19_20
BEGIN_आयाचमानाम् दुःखार्तां प्राञ्जलिं देवतामिव |भावेन रघुमुख्यस्य दशग्रीवपराभवम् || ५-१९-२२_END
BEGIN_Seetha was like a celestial being, tormented by grief and by thought with joined palms, desiring 
the defeat of Ravana at the hands of Sri Rama_END

B_5_C_22_1
BEGIN_यथा यथा सान्त्वयिता वश्यः स्त्रीणां तथा तथा |यथा यथा प्रियम् वक्ता परिBहूतस्तथा तहा || 
५-२२-२_END
BEGIN_"In whatever way gentle language is used to women in that way they will be under control. In whatever 
way men speak dear words, in that way they will be rejected."_END

B_5_C_20_14
BEGIN_भव मैथिलि भाया मे मोहमेनम् विसर्जय |बह्वीनामुत्तमस्त्रीणामाहृतानामितस्ततः || ५-२०-१६
सर्वापामेव भद्रं ते ममाग्रमहिषी भव |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Become my wife. Leave this ignorance. In all my many best women brought from here and 
there, become foremost consort. Let there be auspicious to you."_END

B_5_C_21_8
BEGIN_इह सन्तो न वा सन्ति सतो वा नानुवर्तसे || ५-२१-९तथाहि विपरीता ते बुद्धिराचारवर्जिता |_END
BEGIN_"Here are there not good people? Or are you not following those who are good? It must be like that 
because your mind, devoid of traditions is perverse."_END

B_5_C_1_187
BEGIN_
स सागरं दानवपन्नगायुतं |
बलेन विक्रम्य महोर्मिमालिनम् |
निपत्य तीरे च महोदधेस्तदा |
ददर्श लङ्काममरावतीमिव || ५-१-२१०_END
BEGIN_
Having tranersed, by the dint of his strength over the ocean which was infested with
demons and reptiles and endowed with series of huge waves, and alighting on the shore of the great
sea, Hanuma then saw the City of Lanka having a resemblance of Amaravati, the capital City of
Indra._END

B_5_C_18_26
BEGIN_स तथाप्युग्रतेजाः सन्निर्धूतस्तस्य तेजसा |पत्रगुह्यान्तरे सक्तो हनुमान् संवृतोऽभवत् || 
५-१८-३१_END
BEGIN_Thus Hanuma although of terrible energy was overshadowed by Ravana's brilliance and became rooted 
behind a group of leaves and was concealed._END

B_5_C_19_21
BEGIN_समीक्षमाणां रुदतीमनिन्दितां |सुपक्ष्मताम्रायतशुक्ललोचनाम् |अनुव्रतां राममतीव मैथिलीं 
|प्रलोभयामास वधाय रावणः || ५-१९-२३_END
BEGIN_Ravana was trying to allure and threatening death to Seetha who was looking at every direction, 
crying, without blame, with good eye lids and reddish and white eyes, with an excessive vow to follow Sri Rama._END

B_5_C_22_2
BEGIN_संनियच्चति मे क्रोधं त्वयि कामः समुत्थितः |द्रवतोऽमार्गमासाद्य हयानिव सुसारथिः || ५-२२-३_END
BEGIN_"In your matter desire which has risen up is subdueing my anger like horses running obtaining a 
bad path being subdued by a good charioteer."_END

B_5_C_20_15
BEGIN_लोकेभो यानि रत्नानि सम्प्रमथ्याहृतानि वै || ५-२०-१७तानि मे भीरु सर्वाणि राज्यम् चैतदहं 
च ते |_END
BEGIN_"O timid one! Whatever gems that have been brought by force, all those, my this kingdom and also 
myself belong to you."_END

B_5_C_21_9
BEGIN_वचो मिथ्याप्रणीतात्मा पथ्यमुक्तं विचक्षणैः || ५-२१-१०राक्षसानामभावाय त्वम् वा न व्रतिपद्यसे 
|_END
BEGIN_"You who is being led by mind towards unreal is not taking wholesome words being said by righteous 
onesfor the destruction of ogres."_END

B_5_C_18_27
BEGIN_स तामसितकेशान्तां सुश्रोणीं संहतस्तनीम् |दिदृक्षुरसितापाङ्गमुपावर्तत रावणः || ५-१८-३२_END
BEGIN_That Ravana neared Seetha with black hair, with charming limbs with well knit breasts, with black 
corners of eyes, wishing to see Her._END

B_5_C_22_3
BEGIN_वामः कामो मनुष्याणाम् यस्मिन् किल निबध्यते |जने तस्मिंस्त्वनुक्रोशः स्नेहश्च किल जायते 
|| ५-२२-४_END
BEGIN_"Desire of men is unfavourable. In which man desire is tied up, in that man there is compassion 
and fondness."_END

B_5_C_20_16
BEGIN_विजित्य पृथिवीं सर्वां नानानगरमालिनीम् || ५-२०-१८जनकाय प्रदास्यामि तव हेतोर्विलासिनि |_END
BEGIN_"O charmful lady! Conquering the entire earth together with chain of various cities for your sake, 
I can give to king Janaka._END

B_5_C_21_10
BEGIN_आकृतात्मानमासाद्य राजानमनये रतम् || ५-२१-११समृद्धानि विनश्यन्ति राष्ट्राणि नगराणि च |
तथेयम् त्वाम् समासाद्य लङ्का रत्नौघसम्कुला || ५-२१-१२अपराधात्तवैकस्य वचिराद्विनशिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"After getting a king who has uncontrolled mind, interested in a bad path, wealthy states and cities 
also will be destroyed. After getting you like that this Lanka filled with best things in a short while will be 
destroyed due to your one sin."_END

B_5_C_22_4
BEGIN_एतस्मात्कारणान्न त्वां घातयामि वरानने |वधार्हमवमानार्हां मिथ्याप्रव्रजिते रताम् || ५-२२-५_END
BEGIN_"O one with a beautiful face! For this reason although you are suitable to be killed and suitable 
to be humilaited, interested in Rama who is in sham exile, I am not killing you."_END

B_5_C_20_17
BEGIN_नेह पश्यामि लोकेऽन्यम् यो मे प्रतिबलो भवेत् || ५-२०-१९पश्य मे सुमहद्वीर्यमप्रतिद्वन्द्वमाहवे 
|_END
BEGIN_"In this world I do not see another one who is equally matched to me. See my very great power."_END

B_5_C_21_11
BEGIN_स्वकृतैर्हन्यमानस्य आवणादीर्घदर्शिनः || ५-२१-१३अभिनन्दन्ति भूतानि विनाशे पापकर्मणः |_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana! When there is destruction of a short sighted one being hit by his own deeds, a sinner, 
living beings will be happy."_END

B_5_C_23_0
BEGIN_इत्युक्त्वा मैथिलीं राजा रावणः शत्रुरावणः |संदिश्य च ततः सर्वा राक्षसीर्निर्जगाम ह || 
५-२३-१_END
BEGIN_The king Ravana who makes enemies to cry thus speaking to Seetha thereafter also ordering all ogre 
women went away._END

B_5_C_22_5
BEGIN_परुषाणीह वाक्यानि यानि यानि ब्रवीषि माम् |तेषु तेषु वधो युक्तस्तव मैथिलि दारुणः || ५-२२-६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Here whatever harsh words you are speaking about me, because of those words, you are 
suitable to be horribly slayed."_END

B_5_C_20_18
BEGIN_असकृत्सम्युगे भग्ना मया विमृदितध्वजाः || ५-२०-२०अशक्ताः प्रत्यनीकेषु स्थातुं मम सुरासुराः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Suras and Asuras defeated with broken flags by me in war many times are powerless to stand in 
an army against me."_END

B_5_C_21_12
BEGIN_एवं त्वां पापकर्माणम् वक्ष्यन्ति निकृता जनाः || ५-२१-१४दिष्ट्यैतद् व्यसनं प्राप्तो रौद्र 
इत्येव हर्षिताः |_END
BEGIN_"About you who is a sinner thus being destroyed, people who have been humiliated by you being happy 
will speak thus: 'The cruel Ravana by God's grace has got this danger' "._END

B_5_C_23_1
BEGIN_निष्क्रन्ते राक्षसेन्द्र तु पुनरन्तःपुरं गते |राक्षस्यो भीमरूपास्ताः सीतां समभिदुद्रुवुः 
|| ५-२३-२_END
BEGIN_After Ravana left and obtained gynaeceum, those ogres with horrible appearances went running to 
Seetha._END

B_5_C_22_6
BEGIN_एकमुक्त्वा तु विअदेशीं रावणो राक्षसाधिपः |क्रोधसंरम्भसम्युक्तः सीतामुत्तरमब्रवीत् || ५-२२-७_END
BEGIN_The king of ogres Ravana speaking thus to Seetha, full of anger and fury spoke subsequent word 
to Seetha._END

B_5_C_20_19
BEGIN_इच्छ मां क्रियतामद्य प्रतिकर्म तवोत्तमम् || ५-२०-२१सप्रभाण्यवसज्यन्तां तवांगे भूषणानि 
च |साधु पश्यामि ते रूपम् सम्युक्तं प्रतिकर्मणा || ५-२०-२२_END
BEGIN_"Desire me! Now let your best decoration be made. On your body let ornaments also with great brilliance 
be fit. I will see well your form together with decoration."_END

B_5_C_21_13
BEGIN_शक्या लोभयितुं नाहमैश्वर्येण धनेन वा || ५-२१-१५अनन्या राघवेणाहं भास्करेण प्रभा यथा |_END
BEGIN_"I am not capable to be tempted by wealth or by money. I am not separate with Raghava like the 
sun-shine with the sun."_END

B_5_C_23_2
BEGIN_ततः सीतामुपागम्य राक्षस्यः क्रोधमूर्चिताः |परं पुरुषया वाचा वैदेहीमिदमब्रवन् || ५-२३-३_END
BEGIN_Thereafter reaching Seetha ogre women swooned with anger and with a very harsh speech spoke these 
words to Seetha._END

B_5_C_22_7
BEGIN_द्वौ मासौ रक्षितव्यौ मे योऽवधिस्ते मया कृतः |ततः शयनमारोह मम त्वं वरवर्णिनि || ५-२२-८_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with best complexion! Whatever limit has been made by me to you, those two months are 
protectable to me. Thereafter ascend my bed."_END

B_5_C_20_20
BEGIN_प्रतिकर्माभिसम्युक्ता दाक्षिण्येन वरानने |भुम्क्ष्व भोगान्यथाकामं पिब भीरु रमस्व च || 
५-२०-२३_END
BEGIN_"O one with best face! O timid one! With consideration enjoy luxuries according to your desire 
together with decoration. Drink. Rejoice."_END

B_5_C_21_14
BEGIN_उपधाय भुजम् तस्य लोकनाथस्य सत्कृतम् || ५-२१-१६कथम् नामोपधास्यामि भुजमन्यस्य कस्य चित् 
|_END
BEGIN_"After making as a pillow that worshipped shoulder of that lord of the world, of that Rama, how 
can I make as pillow some other one's shoulder?"_END

B_5_C_23_3
BEGIN_पौलस्त्यस्य वरिष्ठस्य रावणस्य महात्मनः |दशग्रीवस्य भार्यात्वं सीते न बहुमन्यसे || ५-२३-४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! You are not respscting becoming wife of Ravana born in the family of Paulastya, best 
among men, a great soul with ten heads."_END

B_5_C_22_8
BEGIN_ऊर्ध्वं द्वाभ्यां तु मासाभ्यां भर्तारम् मामनिच्चतीम् |मम त्वां प्रातराशार्थमालभन्ते महानसे 
|| ५-२२-९_END
BEGIN_"Above two months you not desiring me as husband will be killed in my kitched for my breakfast."_END

B_5_C_21_15
BEGIN_अहमौपयीकी भार्या तस्यैव वसुधापतेः || ५-२१-१७व्रतस्नातस्य विप्रस्य विद्येव विदितात्मनः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Like the education of a brahmin with a famous mind, initiated in religious vow, I am suitable 
wife to that Rama alone the lord of earth."_END

B_5_C_20_21
BEGIN_यथेच्छम् च प्रयच्छ त्वं पृथिवीम् वा धनानि च |ललस्व मयि विस्रब्धा धृष्टमाज्ञापयस्व च || 
५-२०-२४_END
BEGIN_"You donate land and wealth according to your wish. With confidence behave freely in my matter. 
Fearlessly order also."_END

B_5_C_23_4
BEGIN_ततस्वएकजटा नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् |अमन्त्य्र क्रोधताम्राक्षी सीतां करतलोदरीम् || ५-२३-५_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Ekajata with red eyes sue to anger calling Seetha with stomach that 
can be held by palm of the hand, spoke these words._END

B_5_C_22_9
BEGIN_तां तर्ज्यमानां सम्प्रेक्ष्य राक्षसेन्द्रेण जानकीम् |देवगन्धर्वकन्यास्ता विषेदुर्विकृतेक्षणाः 
|| ५-२२-१०_END
BEGIN_Seeing Seetha being frightened by Ravana those Deva and Gandharva maidens grieved with troubled 
eyes._END

B_5_C_20_22
BEGIN_मत्र्पसादाल्ललन्त्याश्च ललन्तां बान्धवास्तव |बुद्धिं ममानुपश्य त्वम् श्रियम् भद्रे यशश्च 
मे || ५-२०-२५_END
BEGIN_" By my grace with your sporting, tour relatives will also sport. O auspicious one! You see my 
wealth and my fame."_END

B_5_C_21_16
BEGIN_साधु रावण रामेण मां समानय दुःखिताम् || ५-२१-१८वने वाशितया सार्थम् करेण्वेव गजाधिपम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana! Let me meet together with Rama like a female elephant with a male elephant in a forest."_END

B_5_C_23_5
BEGIN_प्रजापतीनाम् षण्णं तु चतुर्थो यः प्रजापतिः |मानसो ब्रह्मणः पुत्रः पुलस्त्य इति विश्रुतः 
|| ५-२३-६_END
BEGIN_"Among th six Prajapatis, whichever son, the fourth Prajapati, born by the thought of Lord Brahma 
,he is famous as Paulastya."_END

B_5_C_22_10
BEGIN_औष्ठप्रकारैरपरा वक्त्रनेत्रैस्तथापराः |सीतामाश्वासयामासुस्तर्जितां तेन रक्षसा || ५-२२-११_END
BEGIN_Some in the way of lips and in like manner some others with faces and eyes consoled that Seetha 
frightened by that ogre._END

B_5_C_20_23
BEGIN_किं करिष्यसि रामेण सुभगे चीरवाससा |निक्षिप्तविजयो रामो गतश्रीर्वनगोचरः || ५-२०-२६व्रती 
स्थण्डिलशायी च शङ्के जीवति वा न वा |_END
BEGIN_"O beautiful one! What can you do with Rama clad in tatters, with lost hope of victory, with gone 
fortune. Roaming in forests, observing austerities and also sleeping on floor, I doubt if Rama is alive or not."_END

B_5_C_21_17
BEGIN_मित्रमौपयिकम् कर्तुम् रामः स्थानम् परीप्सता || ५-२१-१९वधम् चानिच्छता घोरं त्वयासौ पुरुषर्षभः 
|_END
BEGIN_"It is suited that this Rama, best among men, is made to be a friend by you who is desiring continued 
existence and not desiring a horrible slaying."_END

B_5_C_23_6
BEGIN_पुलस्त्यस्य तु तेजस्वी महार्षिर्मानसः सुतः |नाम्ना स विश्रवा नाम प्रजापतिसमप्रभः || ५-२३-७_END
BEGIN_By the name, famous as Visrava, with a radiance equalling that of Lord Brahmathat glorious sage 
is the son born from the thought of Pulastya._END

B_5_C_22_11
BEGIN_ताभिराश्वासिता सीता रावणम् राक्षसाधिपम् |उवाचात्महितं वाक्यं वृत्तशौण्डीर्यगर्वितम् || 
५-२२-१२_END
BEGIN_Consoled by them Seetha proud of virtuous conduct spoke words beneficial to self to the king of 
ogres Ravana._END

B_5_C_20_24
BEGIN_न हि वैदेहि रांस्त्वां द्रष्टुं वा प्युपलस्स्यते || ५-२०-२७पुरोबलाकैरसितैर्मे घोर्ज्योत्स्नामिवावृताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha, Rama indeed does not get opportunity even to see you like moonlight covered by dark 
clous with cranes at the front."_END

B_5_C_21_18
BEGIN_विदितः स हि धर्मज्ञः शरणागतवत्सलः || ५-२१-२०तेन मैत्री भवतु ते यदि जीवितुमिच्चसि |_END
BEGIN_"Rama the righteous one is indeed known as one who loves those who seek protection. If you desire 
to live. let there be friendship between you and Rama."_END

B_5_C_23_7
BEGIN_तस्य पुत्रो विशालाक्षि रावणः शत्रुरावणः |तस्य त्वं राक्षसेन्द्रस्य भार्या भवितुमर्हसि 
|| ५-२३-८मयोक्तं चारुसर्वाङ्गि वाक्यम् किं नाममन्यसे |_END
BEGIN_"O wide eyed one! Ravana who makes enemies to cry, is Visrava's son. You are suited to become Ravana's 
wife. O one with all beautiful limbs! Why will you not agree words spoken by me."_END

B_5_C_22_12
BEGIN_नूनम् न ते जनः कश्चिदस्ति निःश्रेयसे स्थितः |निवारयति यो न त्वां कर्मणोऽस्माद्विगर्हितात् 
|| ५-२२-१३_END
BEGIN_"Whoever prevents you from these actions which are blameable, such a person interested in your 
welfare there is none. This is definite."_END

B_5_C_20_25
BEGIN_न चापि मम हस्तात्त्वां प्राप्तुमर्हति राघवः || ५-२०-२८हिरण्यकशिपुः कीर्तिमिन्द्रहस्तगतामिव 
|_END
BEGIN_"Like Keerthi got by Hiranyakasipu from Indra's hand, Rama is not suited to get you from my hands."_END

B_5_C_21_19
BEGIN_प्रसादयस्व त्वं चनं शरणागतवत्सलम् || ५-२१-२१मां चास्मै नियतो भूत्वा निर्यातयितुमर्हसि 
|_END
BEGIN_"You seek graciousness of this Rama who loves those who seek protection. Becoming piously disposed, 
you are suited to return me to this Rama."_END

B_5_C_24_0
BEGIN_ततः सीतामुपागम्य राक्षस्यो विकृताननाः |परुषं परुषा नार्य ऊचुस्तां वाक्यमप्रियम् || ५-२४-१_END
BEGIN_Thereafter ogre women with a cruel nature, with crooked faces neared that Seetha and spoke unpleasant 
words harshly._END

B_5_C_23_8
BEGIN_ततो हरिजटा नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् || ५-२३-९विवर्त्य नयने कोपान्मार्जारसदृशेक्षणा |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Harijata with eyes like those of a cat turned around eyes due to 
anger and spoke these words._END

B_5_C_22_13
BEGIN_मां हि धर्मात्मनः पत्नीं शचीमिव शचीपतेः |त्वदन्यस्त्रिषु लोकेषु प्रार्थयेन्मनसापि कः || 
५-२२-१४_END
BEGIN_"In all the three worlds except you who even by heart will desire me who am the wife of virtuous 
Rama like Sachi the wife of Indra."_END

B_5_C_20_26
BEGIN_चारुस्मिते चारुदति चारुनेत्रे विलासिनि || ५-२०-२९मनो हरसि मे भीरु सुपर्णः पन्न्गं यथा 
|_END
BEGIN_"O one with a beautiful smile! O one with beautiful teeth!O one with beautiful eyes! O charmful 
one! O timid one! You are stealing my heart like a serpent stolen by Garuda._END

B_5_C_21_20
BEGIN_एवम् हि ते भवेत्स्वस्ति सम्प्रदाय रघूत्तमे || ५-२१-२२अन्यथा त्वम् हि कुर्वणो वधम् प्राप्स्यसि 
रावण |_END
BEGIN_"In this way giving me to Rama will become fortunate to you. O Ravana! If you do in a different 
way, you will get slayed."_END

B_5_C_24_1
BEGIN_किं त्वमन्तःपुरे सीते सर्वभूतमनोहरे |महार्हशयनोपेते न वासमनुमन्यसे || ५-२४-२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Why are you not agreeing to stay in the gynaeceum pleasing to all beings together with 
very best beds."_END

B_5_C_23_9
BEGIN_येन देवास्त्रायस्त्रिंशद्देवराजश्च निर्जताः || ५-२३-१०तस्य त्वं राक्षसेन्द्रस्य भार्या 
भवितुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_"By whom thirty three Devas and the king of Devas have been conquered, you are suited to become 
the wife of that lord of ogres._END

B_5_C_22_14
BEGIN_राक्षसाधम रामस्य भार्याममिततेजसः |उक्तवानसि यत्पापं क्व गतस्तस्य मोक्ष्यसे || ५-२२-१५_END
BEGIN_"O vile ogre! Whatever sinful word you spoke to me who is the wife of the great resplendent Rama, 
from that word where will you go to be released?"_END

B_5_C_20_27
BEGIN_क्लिष्टकौशेयवसनाम् तन्वीमप्यनलम्कृताम् || ५-२०-३०त्वां दृष्ट्वा स्वेषु दारेषु रतिं नोपलभाम्यहम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"You are Wearing a silk cloth in a bad condition. You are emaciated. Even though you have not decorated, 
seeing you I am not getting happiness in my wives."_END

B_5_C_21_21
BEGIN_वर्जयेद्वज्रमुत्सृष्टं वर्जयेदन्तकश्चिरम् || ५-२१-२३त्वद्विधम् तु न स क्रुद्धो लोकनाथः 
स राघवः |_END
BEGIN_"Drawn out Vajrayudha, the weapon of Indra may spare some one like you. Lord of death may spare 
you for a long time. That Rama the lord of worlds greatly enraged will not spare you."_END

B_5_C_24_2
BEGIN_मानुषी मानुषस्यैव भार्यात्वं बहुमन्यसे |प्रत्याहर मनो रामान्न त्वं जातु भविष्यसि || ५-२४-३_END
BEGIN_"You who are a human are thinking highly about the wifehood of a human being. Withdraw your mind 
from Rama. Otherwise you will not exist at all."_END

B_5_C_23_10
BEGIN_ततस्तु प्रघसा नाम राक्षसी क्रोधमूर्छिता || ५-२३-११भर्त्सयनी तदा घोरमिदं वचनमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre named Praghasa swooning with anger and then frightening Seetha, spoke this horrible 
word._END

B_5_C_22_15
BEGIN_यथा दृप्तश्च मातङ्गः शशश्च सहितौ वने |तथा द्विरदवद्रामस्त्वं नीच शशवत् स्मृतः || ५-२२-१६_END
BEGIN_"Like an elephant in rut and a hare at war in the forest, in the same way O vile one! Rama is like 
an elephant and you are said to be like a hare."_END

B_5_C_20_28
BEGIN_अन्तः पुरविनासिन्यः स्त्रियः सर्वगुणान्विताः || ५-२०-३१यावन्त्यो मम सर्वासामैश्वरम् कुरु 
जानकि |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! whoever women living in gynaeceum endowed with all virtues, have sovereignty on all 
of them."_END

B_5_C_21_22
BEGIN_रामस्य धनुषः शब्दं श्रोष्यसि त्वं महास्वनम् || ५-२१-२४शतक्रतुविसृष्टस्य निर्घोषमशनेरिव 
|_END
BEGIN_"Like the great sound of Vajrayudha hurled by Indra, you will hear a loud sound which is sonorous 
of Rama's bow."_END

B_5_C_24_3
BEGIN_त्रैलोक्यवसुभोक्तारं रावणं राक्षसेश्वरम् |भर्तारमुपसंगम्य विहरस्व यथासुखम् || ५-२४-४_END
BEGIN_"Sport according to your comfort coming together with the king of ogres Ravana enjoying luxuries 
of the three worlds and taking him as husband._END

B_5_C_23_11
BEGIN_वीर्योत्सिक्तस्य शूरस्य सम्ग्रामे न निवर्तिनः || ५-२३-१२बलिनो वीर्ययुक्तस्य भार्यात्वम् 
किं न लप्स्यसे |_END
BEGIN_"Why will you not get wifehood of Ravana who is proud of his might, valiant, who will not turn 
back in wars, who is strong together with valour."_END

B_5_C_22_16
BEGIN_स त्वमिक्ष्वाकुनाथम् वै क्षिपन्निह न लज्जसे |चक्षुषोर्विषयम् तस्य न तावदुपगच्छसि || ५-२२-१७_END
BEGIN_"Such you are not shameful abusing the lord of Ikshvaku dynasty Rama. You are not getting Rama's 
matter so much."_END

B_5_C_21_23
BEGIN_इह शीग्रं सुपर्वाणो ज्वलितास्य इवोरगाः || ५-२१-२५इषवो निपतिष्यन्ति रामलक्ष्मणलक्षणाः |_END
BEGIN_"Arrows with good nodes, with blazing tips, like snakes, with characteristic signs of Rama and 
Lakshmana will fall down soon here in Lanka."_END

B_5_C_20_29
BEGIN_मम ह्यसितकेशान्ते त्रैलोक्यप्रवराः स्त्रियः || ५-२०-३२तास्त्वां परिचरिष्यन्ति श्रियमप्सरसो 
यथा |_END
BEGIN_"O one with black hair! My those women and apsarasas who are the best among the three worlds will 
serve you like the goddess of wealth."_END

B_5_C_24_4
BEGIN_मानुषी मानुषं तं तु राममिच्छसि शोभने |राज्याद्भ्राष्टमसिद्धार्थं विक्लबं त्वमनिन्दिते 
|| ५-२४-५_END
BEGIN_"O beautiful one! O irrreproachable one! But being a human you are desiring that Rama who is a 
human, banished from kingdom, unsuccessful and gloomy."_END

B_5_C_23_12
BEGIN_प्रियां बहुमतां भार्यां त्यक्त्वा राजा महाबलः || ५-२३-१३सर्वासां च महाभागां त्वामुपैष्यति 
रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"The mighty Ravana can leave dear respectable wife who among all wives is most fortunate and can 
obtain you."_END

B_5_C_22_17
BEGIN_इवे ते नयने क्रूते विरूपे कृष्णपिङ्गले |क्षितौ न पतिते कस्मान्मामनार्य निरीक्षतः || ५-२२-१८_END
BEGIN_"O ignoble one! your these eyes which are cruel, crooked, which are black and reddish brown, which 
are seeing me, for what reason are they not falling down."_END

B_5_C_21_24
BEGIN_रक्षांसि परिनिघ्नस्तः पुर्यामस्यां समन्ततः || ५-२१-२६असम्पातं करिष्यन्ति पतन्तः कङ्कवाससः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Arrows tied with the plumes of an eagle will hit ogres everywhere in this city and will cover 
the city without space."_END

B_5_C_20_30
BEGIN_यानि वैश्रवणे सुभ्रु रत्नानि च धनानि च || ५-२०-३३तानि लोकांश्च सुश्रोणि मां च भुम्क्ष्व 
यथासुखम् |_END
BEGIN_"O one with beautiful hips! O one with beuatiful eyebrows! Enjoy according to your comfort whatever 
gems and wealth belonging to Kubera, all those three worlds and me."_END

B_5_C_23_13
BEGIN_समृद्धम् स्त्रीसहस्रेण नानारत्नोपशोभितम् || ५-२३-१४अन्तःपुरं समुत्सृज्य त्वामुपैष्यति 
रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"Ravana leaving gynaeceum filled with thousand women and shone by various best things can obtain 
you._END

B_5_C_24_5
BEGIN_राक्षसीनां वचः श्रुत्वा सीता पद्मनिभेक्षणा |नेत्राभ्यामश्रुपूर्णाभ्यामिदं वचनमब्रवीत् 
|| ५-२४-६_END
BEGIN_Seetha with eyes like lotuses hearing the words of ogre women spoke these words with eyes filled 
with tears._END

B_5_C_22_18
BEGIN_तस्य धर्मात्मनः पत्नीं स्नुषां दशरथस्य च |कथं व्याहरतो मां ते न जिह्वा व्यवशीर्यते || 
५-२२-१९_END
BEGIN_"Thus speaking about me who am the wife of virtuous Rama and the daughter-in-law of Dasaratha how 
your tongue did not fall off."_END

B_5_C_21_25
BEGIN_राक्षसेन्द्रमहासर्पान् स रामगरुडो महान् || ५-२१-२७उद्धरिष्यति वेगेन वैनतेय इवोरगान् |_END
BEGIN_"That Garuda called Rama speedily will pluck the great serpants called ogres like Vainateya plucking 
the serpants."_END

B_5_C_20_31
BEGIN_न रामस्तपसा देवि न बलेन विक्रमैः || ५-२०-३४न धनेन मया तुल्यस्तेजसा यशसापि वा |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Rama is not equal to me by austerity, not equal by might; not equal by strength, not 
equal by wealth, by brilliance and by fame."_END

B_5_C_25_0
BEGIN_अथ तासां वदन्तीनां परुषं दारुणं बहु |राक्षसीनामसौम्यानां रुरोद जनकात्मजा || ५-२५-१_END
BEGIN_As those ogre woman with a cruel nature were speaking a lot harshly and horribly, Seetha cried._END

B_5_C_24_6
BEGIN_यदिदम् लोकविद्विष्टमुदाहरथ संगताः |नैतन्मनसि वाक्यं मे किल्बिषं प्रतिभाति वः || ५-२४-७_END
BEGIN_"All of you coming together whatever words which are hated in the world you spoke in my matter, 
this does it not seem sinful in your mind?"_END

B_5_C_23_14
BEGIN_अन्या तु विकटा नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् || ५-२३-१५असकृद्देवता युद्धे नागगन्धर्वदानवाः 
|निर्जिताः समरे येन सते पार्श्वमुपागतः || ५-२३-१६_END
BEGIN_Another ogre woman named Vikata spoke these words: "By whom a number of times in war Devas, in 
war Nagas, Gandharvas and Danavas have been conquered that Ravana has come to your side."_END

B_5_C_22_19
BEGIN_असंदेशात्तु रामस्य तपसश्चामपालनात् |न त्वां कुर्मि दशग्रीव भस्म भर्मार्ह तेजसा || ५-२२-२०_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana! Although you are suited to be burnt into ashes, not having the mandate of Rama and preserving 
austerity, I am not reducing you into ashes with my glory."_END

B_5_C_20_32
BEGIN_पिब विहर रमस्व भुंक्ष्व भोगान् |धननिचौअम् प्रदिशामि मेदिनीम् च |मयि लल ललने यथासुखम् 
त्वम् |त्वयि च समेत्य ललन्तु बान्धव्वस्ते || ५-२०-३५_END
BEGIN_"O playful one! I will give hordes of wealth and land. You drink. Roam freely and play. Enjoy luxuries. 
Sport according to comfort in me. Your relatives may sport together in you."_END

B_5_C_21_26
BEGIN_अपनेष्यति मां भर्ता त्वत्तः शीघ्रमरिन्दमः || ५-२१-२८असुरेभ्यः श्रियं दीप्तां विष्णुस्त्रिभिरिव 
क्रमैः |_END
BEGIN_"My husband who is a destroyer of foes will take me away from you like Lord Vishnu with three steps 
taking away the brilliant prosperity from Asuras."_END

B_5_C_25_1
BEGIN_एवमुक्ता तु वैदेही राक्षसीभिर्मनस्विनी |उवाच परमत्रस्ताबाष्पगद्गदया गिरा || ५-२५-२_END
BEGIN_Thus being spoken to by ogre women, Seetha with a good mind being frightened a lot spoke as follows 
with a voice indistinct due to tears._END

B_5_C_23_15
BEGIN_तस्य सर्वसमृद्धस्य रावणस्य महात्मनः |किमद्य राक्षसेन्द्रस्य भार्यात्वं नेच्छऽधमे || ५-२३-१७_END
BEGIN_"O vile one! Why are you not desiring wifehood of such Ravana, fulfilled in all respects, who is 
a great soul and lord of ogres._END

B_5_C_24_7
BEGIN_न मानुषी राक्षसस्य भार्या भवितुमर्हति |कामं खादत मां सर्वा न करिष्यामि वो वचः || ५-२४-८_END
BEGIN_"Human woman is not waited to become wife of an ogre. All of you freely eat me. I will not honour 
your words."_END

B_5_C_22_20
BEGIN_नापहर्तुमहं शक्या त्वया रामस्य धीमतः |विधिस्तव वधार्थाय विहितो नात्र संशयः || ५-२२-२१_END
BEGIN_"Wise Rama's I am not capable of being abducted by you. This act has been made for your slaying. 
In this there is no doubt."_END

B_5_C_20_33
BEGIN_कनकविमलहारभूषिताङ्गी |विहर मया सह भीरु काननानि || ५-२०-३६_END
BEGIN_"O timid one! With body decorated with gold colored, pure garlands, roam with me in forests born 
at sea shore filled with groups of flowered trees and with humble bees."_END

B_5_C_21_27
BEGIN_जनस्थाने हतस्थाने निहते रक्षसां बले || ५-२१-२९अशक्तेन त्वया रक्षः कृतमेतदसाधु वै |_END
BEGIN_"O ogre! While the army of ogres was being killed at Janasthana which became the land of dead, 
this bad deed has been done by you being powerless."_END

B_5_C_25_2
BEGIN_न मानुषी राक्षसस्य भार्या भवितुमर्हति |कामं खादत मां सर्वा न करिष्यामि वो वचः || ५-२५-३_END
BEGIN_"A human woman is not suited to become a wife of an ogre. All of you eat me according to your desire. 
I will not do according to your words."_END

B_5_C_23_16
BEGIN_ततस्तु दुर्मुखी नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् |यस्य सूर्यो न तपति भीतो यस्य च मारुतः || ५-२३-१८
न वाति स्मायतापाङ्गे किं त्वं तस्य न तिष्ठसि |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Durmukhi spoke these words: " O one with long eyes! Fearing whom 
the sun will not comsume by heat, fearing whom the win will not blow, to that one why are you not favourable."_END

B_5_C_24_8
BEGIN_दीनो वा राज्यहीनो वा यो मे भर्ता स मे गुरुः |तं नित्यमनुरक्तास्मि यथा सूर्यं सुवर्चला 
|| ५-२४-९_END
BEGIN_"Although wretched or without kingdom, whoever is my husband, He alone is my master. Like Suvarchala 
with the Sun God, I am fond of Him always."_END

B_5_C_22_21
BEGIN_शूरेण धनदभ्रात्रा बलैः समुदितेन च |अपिह्य रामं कस्माद्धि दारचौर्यं त्वया कृतम् || ५-२२-२२_END
BEGIN_"By you who is strong, brother of Kubera possessed of army, removing Rama for what reason abduction 
of wife has been done."_END

B_5_C_21_28
BEGIN_अश्रमम् तु तयोः शून्यं प्रविश्य नरसिम्हयोः || ५-२१-३०गोचरं गतयोर्र्भात्रोरपनीता त्वयाधम 
|_END
BEGIN_"O lowest one! When those brothers were gone out, entering hermitage without them, I have been 
abducted by you."_END

B_5_C_25_3
BEGIN_सा राक्षसीमध्यगता सीता सुरसुतोपमा |न शर्म लेभे दुःखार्ता रावणेन च तर्जिता || ५-२५-४_END
BEGIN_Being in the middle of ogre women, being frightened by Ravana also, like a daughter of gods, that 
Seetha did not get comfort being tormented by grief._END

B_5_C_23_17
BEGIN_पुष्टवृष्टं च तरवो मुमुचुर्यस्य वै भयात् || ५-२३-१९शैलाश्च सुभ्रु पानीयम् जलदाश्च यदेच्छति 
|तस्य नैरृतराजस्य राजराजस्य भामिनि || ५-२३-२०किं त्वं न कुरुषे बुद्धिं भार्यार्थे रावणस्य हि |_END
BEGIN_"O one with good eyebrows! O Seetha! By the fear of whom trees shed a shower of flowers, whenever 
Ravana desired mountains and clouds will shed water, why you are not making mind to be the wife of such Ravana, 
who is the king of ogres and king of kings."_END

B_5_C_22_22
BEGIN_सीताया वचनं श्रुत्वा रावणो राक्षसाधिपः |विनृत्य नयने क्रूरे जानकीमन्ववैक्षत || ५-२२-२३_END
BEGIN_King of rakshasas Ravana listening to Seetha's words turned around his cruel eyes and saw Seetha._END

B_5_C_24_9
BEGIN_यथा शची महाभागा शक्रं समुपतिष्ठति |अरुन्धती वसिष्ठं च रोहिणी शशिनं यथा || ५-२४-१०लोपामुद्रा 
यथागस्त्यं सुकन्याच्यवनं यथा |सावित्री सत्यवन्तं च कपिलं श्रीमती यथा || ५-२४-११सौदासं मदयन्तीव केशिनी 
सगरं यथा |नैषधं दमयन्तीव भैमी पतिमनुव्रता || ५-२४-१२तथाहमिक्ष्वाकुवरं रामं पतिमनुव्रता |_END
BEGIN_"Like the highly fortunate Sachi who waits upon Indra, like Arundhati on Vasishta, like Rohini 
on the Moon God, like Lopamudra on Agastya, like Sukanya on Chyavana, like Savitri on Satyavanta, like Srimati 
on Kapila, like Madayanti on Saudasa, like Kesini on Sagara, like Damayanti the daughter of Bhima, devoted to 
husband Nala, in the same way I am devoted to my husband Rama, the best in Ikshvaku dynasty."_END

B_5_C_21_29
BEGIN_न हि गन्धमुपाघ्राय रामलक्ष्मणयोस्त्वया || ५-२१-३१शक्यं संदर्शने स्थातुं शुना शार्दूलयोरिव 
|_END
BEGIN_"Like tiger by dog, smelling the scent of Rama and Lakshmana it is indeed not possible by you to 
stand in their view."_END

B_5_C_25_4
BEGIN_वेपते स्माधिकं सीता विशन्ती वाङ्गमात्मनः |वने यथा परिभ्रष्टा मृगी कोकैरिवार्दिता || ५-२५-५_END
BEGIN_Like a fawn in a forest lost from its herd and tormented by wolves, Seetha was as though sinking 
into own body and shook a lot._END

B_5_C_23_18
BEGIN_साधु ते तत्त्वतो देवि कथितं साधु भामिनि || ५-२३-२१गृहाण सुस्मिते वाक्यमन्यथा न भविष्यसि 
|_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with a good smile! O princess! Understand kind words spoken to you well and truly."_END

B_5_C_22_23
BEGIN_नीलजीमूतसम्काशो महाभुजशिरोधरः |सिंहसत्त्वगतिः श्रीमान् दीप्त जिह्वग्रलोचनः || ५-२२-२४_END
BEGIN_Ravana was qual to a black cloud, with big shoulders and neck with the strength and gait of a lion, 
glorious with radiant tip of tongue and eyes._END

B_5_C_24_10
BEGIN_सीताया वचनं श्रुत्वा राक्षस्यः क्रोधमूर्चिताः || ५-२४-१३भर्त्सयन्ति स्म परुषैर्वाक्यै 
रावणचोदिताः |_END
BEGIN_Ogre women incited by Ravana listening to the words of Seetha, swooned with anger and frightened 
Her with harsh words._END

B_5_C_21_30
BEGIN_तस्य ते विग्रहे ताभ्यां युगग्रहणमस्थिरम् || ५-२१-३२वृत्रस्येवेन्द्रबाहुभ्यां बाहोरेकस्य 
विग्रहे |_END
BEGIN_"To you like that, enmity with those two is like the enmity of one hand of Vruttasura with two 
hands of Indra and it is not persevering for you to be an opponent with them."_END

B_5_C_25_5
BEGIN_सा त्वशोकस्य विपुलां शाखामालम्ब्य पुष्पिताम् |चिन्तयामास शोकेन भर्तारं भग्नमानसा || ५-२५-६_END
BEGIN_That Seetha with a broken heart due to grief, held a wide flowering branch of Ashoka tree and thought 
about Her husband._END

B_5_C_24_11
BEGIN_अवलीनः स निर्वाक्यो हनुमान् शिंशुपाद्रुमे || ५-२४-१४सीतां संतर्जयन्तीस्ता राक्ससीरशृणोत् 
कपिः |_END
BEGIN_That monkey Hanuma not talking and hiding in the Simsupa tree listened to those ogre women frightening 
Seetha._END

B_5_C_22_24
BEGIN_चलाग्रमकुटप्रांशुश्चित्रमाल्यानुलेपनः |रक्तमाल्याम्बरधरस्तप्ताङ्गदविभूषणः || ५-२२-२५_END
BEGIN_He was tall with moving front portion of crown, with excellent garlands and anointments, wearing 
red garlands and clothes, with ornaments made of refined gold._END

B_5_C_21_31
BEGIN_क्षिप्रं तव स नाथो मे रामः सौमित्रिणा सह || ५-२१-३३तोयमल्पमिवादित्यः प्रानानादास्यते शरैः 
|_END
BEGIN_"My husband that Rama together with Lakshmana will take away with His arrows your life quickly 
like the sun drying up shallow water."_END

B_5_C_25_6
BEGIN_सा स्नापयन्ती विपुलौ स्तनौ नेत्रजलस्रवैः |चिन्तयन्ती न शोकस्य तदान्तमधिगच्छति || ५-२५-७_END
BEGIN_Then that Seetha washing Her wide breasts with a flow of tears from eyes and thinking, did not 
get end of sorrow._END

B_5_C_24_12
BEGIN_तामभिक्रम्य संक्रुद्दा वेपमानां समन्ततः || ५-२४-१५भृशं संलिलिहुर्दीप्तान् प्रलब्मन् दशनच्छदान् 
|_END
BEGIN_Nearing that Seetha shaking with fear in all directions, those ogres being angry licked a lot shining 
and hanging lips._END

B_5_C_22_25
BEGIN_श्रोणिसूत्रेण महता मेचकेन सुसम्वृतः |अमृतोत्पादनद्धेन भुजगेनेव मन्दरः || ५-२२-२६_END
BEGIN_Like Mount Mandara tied by Vasuki for producing nectar, Ravana was well tied by a black big thread._END

B_5_C_21_32
BEGIN_गिरिं कुबेरस्य गतोऽथवालयम् |सभां गतो वा वरुणस्य राज्ञः |असंशयं दाशरथेर्न मोक्ष्यसे 
|महाद्रुमः कालहतोऽशनेरिव || ५-२१-३४_END
BEGIN_"Killed by time even if you go to the mountain of Kubera or to his house or if you go to the assembly 
of King Varuna, without doubt you will not be relased from Rama like a great tree from thunderbolt."_END

B_5_C_26_0
BEGIN_प्रसक्ताश्रुमुखी त्वेवं ब्रुवती जनकात्मजा |अधोगतमुखी बाला विलप्तुमुपचक्रमे || ५-२६-१_END
BEGIN_With a face continually shedding tears, Seetha an young woman, thus speaking with a downward face, 
started to weep._END

B_5_C_25_7
BEGIN_सा वेपमाना पतिता प्रवाते कदळी यथा |राक्षसीनां भयत्रस्ता विवर्णवदनाभवत् || ५-२५-८_END
BEGIN_That Seetha was shaking like a plantain tree fallen down in an exceedingly windy place, trembling 
with fear of the ogre women, and became with a pale face._END

B_5_C_24_13
BEGIN_ऊचुश्च परमक्रुद्धाः प्रगृह्याशु परश्वधान् || ५-२४-१६नेयमर्हति भर्तारं रावणं राक्षसाधिपम् 
|_END
BEGIN_Being angry a lot and grasping axes quickly spoke as follows: "This woman is not suited to have 
the king of ogres Ravana as husband."_END

B_5_C_22_26
BEGIN_ताभ्यां स परिपूर्णाभ्यां भुजाभ्यां राक्षसेश्वरः |शुशुभेऽचलसंकाशः शृङ्गाभ्यामिव मन्दरः 
|| ५-२२-२७_END
BEGIN_Equalling a mountain the king of ogres shone with those perfect shoulders like Mount Mandara with 
its peaks._END

B_5_C_26_1
BEGIN_उन्मत्तेव प्रमत्तेव भ्रान्तचित्तेव शोचती |उपावृत्ता किशोरीव विवेष्टन्ती महीतले || ५-२६-२_END
BEGIN_Seetha was crying like a mad one, like an intoxicated one, with a deluded mind. Like a female horse 
rolling on ground, Seetha rolled on the ground._END

B_5_C_25_8
BEGIN_तस्याः सा दीर्घविपुला वेपन्त्या सीतया तदा |ददृशे कम्पिनी वेणी व्याळीव परिसर्पती || ५-२५-९_END
BEGIN_That moving plait, which was wide and long, of that best woman was seen to be like a serpant in 
motion._END

B_5_C_24_14
BEGIN_सा भर्तस्यमाना भीमाभी राक्षसीभिर्वरानना || ५-२४-१७सबाष्पमपसर्पन्ती शिंशुपां तामुपागमत् 
|_END
BEGIN_Being frightened by ogre women who were horrible that Seetha with best face with tears in eyes 
and moving from there reached that Simsupa tree._END

B_5_C_22_27
BEGIN_तरुणादित्यवर्णाभ्यां कुण्डलाभ्यां विभूषितः |रक्तपल्लवपुष्पाभ्यामशोकाभ्यामिवाचलः || ५-२२-२८_END
BEGIN_With the color of just risen sun, decorated by earrings, he was like a mountain with Ashoka trees 
with red flowers and shoots._END

B_5_C_26_2
BEGIN_राघवस्य प्रमत्तस्य रक्षसा कामरूपिणा |रावणेन प्रमथ्याहमानीता क्रोशती बलात् || ५-२६-३_END
BEGIN_"While Rama was heedless (taken away by Mareecha), I who have been crying was forcibly brought 
overpowered by the ogre Ravana who can wear desired form."_END

B_5_C_25_9
BEGIN_सा निःश्वसन्ती दुःखार्ता शोकोपहतचेतना |आर्ता व्यसृजदश्रूणि मैथिली विललाप च || ५-२५-१०_END
BEGIN_That Seetha tormented by grief, with a mind hit by sorrow, struck by calamity was sighing and let 
down tears and also cried._END

B_5_C_24_15
BEGIN_ततस्तां शिंशुपां सीता राक्षसीभिः समावृता || ५-२४-१८अभिगम्य विशालाक्षी तस्थौ शोकपरिप्लुता 
|_END
BEGIN_Thereafter the wide eyed Seetha nearing that Simsupa tree being surrounded by ogre women was situated 
there with gloom._END

B_5_C_22_28
BEGIN_स कल्पवृक्षप्रतिमो वसन्त इव मूर्तिमान् |श्मशानचैत्यप्रतिमो भूषितोऽपि भयम्करः || ५-२२-२९_END
BEGIN_Equalling a Kalpavriksha he was like the embodiment of spring season. Like a funeral mound in a 
grave-yard was horrible even though decorated._END

B_5_C_26_3
BEGIN_राक्षसीवशमापन्ना भर्त्स्यमाना सुदारुणम् |चिन्तयन्ती सुदुःखार्ता नाहं जीवितुमुत्सहे || 
५-२६-४_END
BEGIN_"Being under the control of ogresses, being frightened very horribly, thinking and being tormented 
by grief, I do not desire to live."_END

B_5_C_25_10
BEGIN_हा रामेति च दुःखार्ता हा पुनर्लक्ष्मणेति च |हा श्वश्रु मम कौसल्ये हा सुमित्रेति भामिनी 
|| ५-२५-११_END
BEGIN_Seetha being tormented by grief said : "Oh! Rama!" and again "Oh! Lakshmana!","Oh! Kausalya!, my 
mother-in-law" "Oh! Sumitra!"_END

B_5_C_24_16
BEGIN_तां कृशां दीनवदनां मलिनाम्बरधारिणीम् || ५-२४-१९भर्त्सयांचक्रिरे सीतां राक्षस्यस्ताम् समन्ततः 
|_END
BEGIN_Those ogres frightened from all directions that Seetha who was emaciated with a pitiful face and 
wearing dirty garments._END

B_5_C_22_29
BEGIN_अवेक्षमाणो वैदेहीं कोपसम्रक्तलोचनः |उवाच रावणः सीतां भुजङ्ग इव निःश्वसन् || ५-२२-३०_END
BEGIN_With red eyes due to anger Ravana was looking at Seetha sighing like a serpant and spoke to Seetha._END

B_5_C_26_4
BEGIN_न हि मे जीविते नार्थो नै वार्थैर्न च भूषणैः |वसन्त्या राक्षसीमध्ये विना रामं महारथम् || 
५-२६-५_END
BEGIN_"Without Rama, a great car-warrior, living in the midst of ogresses, there is no use with life 
to me; not with wealth, not with ornaments."_END

B_5_C_25_11
BEGIN_लोकप्रवादः सत्योऽयं पण्डितैः समुदाहृतः |अकाले दुर्लभो मृत्युः स्त्रिया वा पुरुषस्य वा 
|| ५-२५-१२यदाहमेवं क्रूराभी राक्षसीभिरिहार्दिता |जीवामि हीना रामेण मुहूर्तमपि दुःखिता || ५-२५-१३_END
BEGIN_"I thus being tormented by cruel ogre women here lacking Rama, being tormented by grief, when I 
am living even for a moment,' death at wrong time to woman or to a man is hard' - thus being said this popular 
saying in the world is true."_END

B_5_C_24_17
BEGIN_ततस्तां विनता नाम राक्षसी भीमदर्शना || ५-२४-२०अब्रवीत्कुपिताकारा कराळा निर्णतोदरी |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Vinata with a horrible appearance with an angry form, crooked, having 
a prominent belly spoke to Her._END

B_5_C_22_30
BEGIN_अनयेनाभिसम्पन्नमर्थहीनमनुव्रते |नाशयाम्यहमद्य त्वां सूर्यः सन्ध्यामिवौजसा || ५-२२-३१_END
BEGIN_O foloower of Rama posessing bad conduct, without wealth! Now I will destroy you like sun destroying 
morning twilight with light._END

B_5_C_26_5
BEGIN_अश्मसारमिदं नूनथवाप्यजरामरम् |हृदयं मम येनेदं न दुःखेनावशीर्यते || ५-२६-६_END
BEGIN_"Or my this heart truly is made of iron. It is undecaying and without death. By what reason is 
it not destroying with sorrow?"_END

B_5_C_25_12
BEGIN_एषाल्पपुण्या कृपणा विनशिष्याम्यनाथवत् |समुद्रमथ्ये नौः पूर्णा वायुवेगैरिवाहता || ५-२५-१४_END
BEGIN_"This me with small merit,wreched, like an orphan, will perish like a ship in the middle of the 
ocean being hit by the speed of wind."_END

B_5_C_24_18
BEGIN_सीते पर्याप्तमेतावद्भर्तुः स्नेहो निदर्शितः || ५-२४-२१सर्वात्रातिकृतं भद्रे व्यसनायोपकल्पते 
|_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! You have showed love of husband. This much is enough. O auspicious one! At all times 
doing something excessively serves as vice."_END

B_5_C_22_31
BEGIN_इत्युक्त्वा मैथिलीम् राजा रावणः शत्रुरावणः |संदिदेश ततः सर्वा राक्षसीर्गोरदर्शनाः || ५-२२-३२_END
BEGIN_The king Ravana who causes enemies to cry thus speaking to Seetha, thereafter ordered all ogre 
women with horrible appearances._END

B_5_C_26_6
BEGIN_धिङ्मामनार्यामसतीं याहं तेन विना कृता |मुहूर्तमपि रक्षामि जीवितं पापजीविता || ५-२६-७_END
BEGIN_"Whoever I with a sinful life made to be without Rama, protecting life even for a moment, to such 
me who am ignoble, who am bad wife, shame on me."_END

B_5_C_25_13
BEGIN_भर्तारं तमपश्यन्ती राक्षसीवशमागता |सीदामि खलु शोकेन कूलं तोयहतं यथा || ५-२५-१५_END
BEGIN_"Not seeing my husband that Rama and obtaining control of ogre women like a bank hit by water I 
am verily perishing with sorrow."_END

B_5_C_24_19
BEGIN_परितुष्टास्मि भद्रं ते मानुषस्ते कृतो विधिः || ५-२४-२२ममापि तु वचः पथ्यं ब्रुवन्त्याः 
कुरु मैथिलि |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! I am happy. Human duty has been done by you. Let there be fortune to you. Do also according 
to my wholesome words being told."_END

B_5_C_22_32
BEGIN_एकाक्षीमेककर्णां च कर्णप्रावरणां तथा |गोकर्णीं हस्तिकर्णीम् च लम्बकर्णीमकर्णिकाम् || ५-२२-३३
हस्तिपाद्यश्वपाद्यौ च गोपादीं पादचूळिकाम् |एकाक्षीमेकपादीं च पृथुपादीमपादिकाम् || ५-२२-३४अतिमात्रशिरोग्रीवामतिमात्रकुचोदरीम् 
|अतिमात्रास्यनेत्राम् च दीर्घजिह्वमजिह्विकाम् || ५-२२-३५अनासिकां सिम्हमुखीं गोमुखीम् सूकरीमुखीम् |_END
BEGIN_Ravana ordered one with a single eye, one with a single ear and one with ears as covering, one 
with cow's wars, one with ears of an elephant, one with dangling ears, one without ears and one with the feet 
of an elephant and one with the feet of a horse, one with feet of a cow,one with hair over feet, one with a single 
eye and one with a single foot, one with big feet, one without feet, one with a big head and neck,one with big 
breasts and stomach, and one with big mouth and eyes, one with a long tongue, one without tongue, one without 
nose, one with the face of a lion, one with the face of a cow,one with the face of a pig._END

B_5_C_26_7
BEGIN_का च मे जीविते श्रद्धा सुखे वा तं प्रियं विना |भर्तारं सागरान्ताया वसुधायाः प्रियंवदम् 
|| ५-२६-८_END
BEGIN_"Without husband Rama who is the lord of the earth with ocean at the end, a pleasant talker, what 
is the interest to me in life or in comfort."_END

B_5_C_25_14
BEGIN_तं पद्मदळपत्राक्षं सिंहविक्रान्तगामिनम् |धन्याः पश्यन्ति मे नाथं कृतज्ञं प्रियवादिनम् 
|| ५-२५-१६_END
BEGIN_"Only fortunate see that my husband with eyes like petals of an expanded lotus, walking with the 
gait of a lion, correct in conduct and a pleasant talker."_END

B_5_C_24_20
BEGIN_रावणं भ्ज भर्तारं भर्तारं सर्वरक्षसाम् || ५-२४-२३विक्रान्तं रूपवन्तं च सुरेशमिव वासवम् 
|दक्षिणं त्यागशीलं च सर्वस्य प्रियदर्शनम् || ५-२४-२४_END
BEGIN_"Obtain as husband Ravana who is the lord of al l ogres, bold and handsome, like Indra the lord 
of Devas, able one and liberal with a pleasing appearance to all."_END

B_5_C_22_33
BEGIN_यथा मद्वशगा सीता क्ष्प्रं भवति जानकी || ५-२२-३६तथा कुरुत राक्षस्यः सर्वाः क्षिप्रं समेत्य 
च |_END
BEGIN_"O ogres! How the daughter of Janaka, Seetha becomes under my control quickly, thus all of you 
together do that task."_END

B_5_C_26_8
BEGIN_भिद्यतां भक्ष्यतां वापि शरीरं विसृजाम्यहम् |न चाप्यहं चिरं कुःखं सहेयं प्रियवर्जिता || 
५-२६-९_END
BEGIN_"I will leave the body. Let it be split into pieces or let it be eaten. I without husband will 
not tolerate sorrow for a long time."_END

B_5_C_25_15
BEGIN_सर्वथा तेन हीनाया रामेण विदितात्मना |तीक्ष्णंविषमिवास्वाद्यदुर्लभं मम जीवितम् || ५-२५-१७_END
BEGIN_"To me lacking that Rama with a famous soul, like after eating a pungent poison life in all ways 
is hard."_END

B_5_C_24_21
BEGIN_मानुषं कृपणं रामं त्यक्त्वा रावणमाश्रय |दिव्याङ्गरागा वैदेहि दिव्याभरणभूषिता || ५-२४-२५
अद्यप्रभृति सर्वेषां लोकनामीश्वरी भव |_END
BEGIN_"Leaving Rama who is a human and miserable, seek refuge in Ravana. O Seetha! With best unguents 
to the body and decorated with best ornaments, become mistress of all the worlds from today."_END

B_5_C_22_34
BEGIN_प्रतिलोमानुलोमैश्च सामदानादिभेदनैः || ५-२२-३७अवर्जयत वैदेहीं दण्डस्योद्यमनेन च |_END
BEGIN_"With hostile and favourable tasks, with kind words, with gifts and dividing words and exertion 
of punishment, bring Seetha under my possession."_END

B_5_C_26_9
BEGIN_चरणेनापि सव्येन न स्पृशेयं निशाचरम् |रावणं किं पुनरहं कावयेयं विगर्हतम् || ५-२६-१०_END
BEGIN_"I will not touch even with my left foot Ravana an ogre of reprehensible conduct. What to say of 
desiring him."_END

B_5_C_25_16
BEGIN_कीदृशं तु महापापं मया जन्मान्तरे कृतम् |येनेदं प्राप्यते दुःखं मया घोरं सुदारुणं || ५-२५-१८_END
BEGIN_"By what this horrible and very dreadful grief is obtained by me, what kind of great sin had been 
done by me in another life."_END

B_5_C_24_22
BEGIN_अग्नेः स्वाहा यथा देवी शिची वेन्द्रस्य शोभने || ५-२४-२६किं ते रामेण वैदेहि कृपणेन गतायिषा 
|_END
BEGIN_"O auspicious one! Like Svaha the wife of the Fire God, like Sachi the wife of Indra become mistress 
of all worlds. O Seetha! What is the use with Rama who is miserable and with gone vigour."_END

B_5_C_22_35
BEGIN_इति प्रतिसमादिश्य राक्षसेन्द्रः पुनः पुनः || ५-२२-३८काममन्युपरीतात्मा जानकीं पर्यतर्जयत् 
|_END
BEGIN_Ravana thus ordered again and again with a mind full of lust and anger frightened Seetha._END

B_5_C_26_10
BEGIN_प्रत्याख्यातं न जानाति नात्मानं नात्मनः कुलम् |यो नृशंसस्वभावेन मां प्रार्थयितुमिच्छति 
|| ५-२६-११_END
BEGIN_"Whoever Ravana with a cruel nature is desiring to solicit me, that Ravana does not know him to 
be refused; he does not know his race."_END

B_5_C_25_17
BEGIN_जीवितं त्यक्तुंइच्छामि शोकेन महता वृता |राक्षसीभिश्च रक्ष्यन्त्या रामो नासाद्यते मया || 
५-२५-१९_END
BEGIN_"Together with great grief, I desire to give away my life. This desire is not obtainable by me. 
I am well protected by ogre women."_END

B_5_C_24_23
BEGIN_एतदुक्तं च मे वाक्यं यदि त्वं न करिष्यपि || ५-२४-२७अस्मिन्मुहूर्ते सर्वास्त्वां भक्षयिष्यामहे 
वयम् |_END
BEGIN_If you do not do my this spoken word, all of us in this moment will eat you._END

B_5_C_22_36
BEGIN_उपगम्य ततः शीघ्रं राक्षसी धान्यमालिनी || ५-२२-३९परिष्वज्य दशग्रीवमिदं वचनमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre named Dhanyamalini quickly neared Ravana, embraced him and spoke these words._END

B_5_C_26_11
BEGIN_चिन्ना भिन्ना विभक्ता वा दीप्तेवाग्नौ प्रदीपिता |रावणं नोपतिष्ठेयं किं प्रलापेन वश्चिरम् 
|| ५-२६-१२_END
BEGIN_"Even if cut or if divided into parts in blazing fire, I will not reach Ravana. What is the use 
with your prattling for a long time?"_END

B_5_C_25_18
BEGIN_धिगस्तु खलु मानुष्यं धिगस्तु परवश्यताम् |न शक्यं यत्परित्यक्तुमात्मच्छन्देन जीवितम् || 
५-२५-२०_END
BEGIN_"Fie upon human condition! Fie upon being in the control of others. By what reason it is not possible 
according to own desire to give up life."_END

B_5_C_24_24
BEGIN_अन्या तु विकटा नाम लबमानपयोधरा || ५-२४-२८अब्रवीत्कुपिता सीतां मुष्टिमुद्यम्य गर्जती |_END
BEGIN_Another ogre named Vikata with hanging breasts raising fist and roaring with anger spoke to Seetha._END

B_5_C_22_37
BEGIN_मया क्रीड महाराज सीतया किं तवानया || ५-२२-४०विवर्णया कृपणया मानुष्या राक्षसेश्वर |_END
BEGIN_"O king! Sport with me. O lord of ogres! Of what use to you is this Seetha who is colorless and 
a wreched human."_END

B_5_C_26_12
BEGIN_ख्यातः प्राज्ञः कृतज्ञ्शश्च राघवः |सद्वृत्तो निरनुक्रोशः शङ्के मद्भाग्यसंक्षयात् || ५-२६-१३_END
BEGIN_"Rama is famous, is a wise man, is compassionate with a good conduct. Due to the deterioration 
of my fortune, I doubt He became hard hearted."_END

B_5_C_24_25
BEGIN_बहून्य्प्रियरूपाणि वचनानि सुदुर्मते || ५-२४-२९अनुक्रोशान्मऋदुत्वाच्च सोढानि तव मैथिलि 
|_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with an evil mind! Your many words which are unpleasant have been tolerated due to pity 
and due to softness."_END

B_5_C_22_38
BEGIN_नूनमस्या महाराज न दिव्यान् भोगसत्तमान् || ५-२२-४१विदधात्यमरश्रेष्ठस्तव बाहुबलार्जितान् 
|_END
BEGIN_"O king! Lord Barhma did not assign to Her wonderful best luxuries earned by the might of your 
arms. This is definite."_END

B_5_C_26_13
BEGIN_राक्षसानां सहस्राणि जनस्थाने चतुर्दश |येनैकेन निरस्तानि स मां किं नाभिपद्यते || ५-२६-१४_END
BEGIN_"By whom alone fourteen thousand of ogres have been destroyed, why is that Rama not saving me."_END

B_5_C_22_39
BEGIN_अकामां कामयानस्य शरीरमुपतप्यते || ५-२२-४२इच्छन्तीं कामयानस्य प्रीतिर्भवति शोभना |_END
BEGIN_"The body of one who desires a woman without desire suffers pain. Good happiness will occur to 
one who loves a woman who desires him."_END

B_5_C_24_26
BEGIN_न च नः कुरुषे वाक्यं हितं कालपुरुस्कृतम् || ५-२४-३०अनीतासि समुद्रस्य पारमन्यैर्दुरासदम् 
|रावणान्तःपुरं घोरं प्रविष्टा चासि मैथिलि || ५-२४-३१_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! You are not doing according to our word which is respected by time and wholesome. You 
have been brought to this bank of the ocean not obtainable by others. You have entered the terrible gynaeceum 
of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_26_14
BEGIN_निरुद्धा रावणेनाहमल्पवीर्येण रक्षसा |समर्थः खलु मे भर्ता रावणं हन्तुमाहवे || ५-२६-१५_END
BEGIN_"I am withheld by the ogre Ravana with little strength. My husband is indeed capable of killing 
Ravana in a war."_END

B_5_C_22_40
BEGIN_एवमुक्तस्तु राक्षस्या समुत्क्षिप्तस्ततो बली || ५-२२-४३प्रहसन्मेघसम्काशो राक्षसः स न्यवर्तत 
|_END
BEGIN_Thus spoken to by that ogre that Ravana who was strong equalling a cloud, thereafter being taken 
away turned back laughing."_END

B_5_C_24_27
BEGIN_रावणस्य गृहे रुद्धामस्माभिस्तु सुरक्षिताम् |न त्वां शक्तः परित्रातुमपि साक्षात्पुरन्दरः 
|| ५-२४-३२_END
BEGIN_"Withheld in the house of Ravana well protected by us, even Devendra himself is not capable to 
protect you."_END

B_5_C_26_15
BEGIN_विराधो दण्डकारण्ये येन राक्षसपुङ्गवः |रणे रामेण निहतः स मां किं नाभिपद्यते || ५-२६-१६_END
BEGIN_"By which Rama Viradha, best among ogres, has been killed in Dandaka forest in a war, why is that 
He not saving me?"_END

B_5_C_24_28
BEGIN_कुरुष्व हितवादिन्या वचनं मम मैथिलि |अलमश्रुप्रपातेन त्यज शोकमन्र्थकम् || ५-२४-३३_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Do according to my word, which is beneficial. Discharge of tears is enough. Leave worthless 
gloom."_END

B_5_C_22_41
BEGIN_प्रस्थितः स दशग्रीवः कम्पयन्निव मेदिनीम् || ५-२२-४४ज्वलद्भास्करवर्णाभम् प्रविवेश निवेशनम् 
|_END
BEGIN_That Ravana departing was as though shaking the earth and entered his house with the lustre of 
blazing sun shine._END

B_5_C_26_16
BEGIN_कामं मध्ये समुद्रस्य लङ्केयं दुष्प्रधर्षणा |न तु राघवबाणानां गतिरोधो भविष्यति || ५-२६-१७_END
BEGIN_"This city of Lanka being in the middle of ocean is difficult to be attacked. But there will not 
be an obstacle to flying of Rama's arrows."_END

B_5_C_24_29
BEGIN_भज प्रीतिं च हर्षं च त्यजैतां नित्यदैन्यताम् |सीते राक्षसराजेन सह क्रीड यथासुखम् || ५-२४-३४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Have love and happiness. Leave this daily gloom. Sport according to comfort with the 
king of ogres."_END

B_5_C_22_42
BEGIN_देवगन्धर्वकन्याश्च नागकन्याश्च सर्वतः || ५-२२-४५परिवार्य दशग्रीवं विविशुस्तं गृहोत्तमम् 
|_END
BEGIN_Deva and Gandharva maidens and Naga maidens surrounding Ravana in all directions entered that best 
among houses._END

B_5_C_26_17
BEGIN_किं नु तत्कारणं येन रामो दृढपराक्रमः |रक्षसापहृतां भार्यामिष्टां नाभ्यवपद्यते || ५-२६-१८_END
BEGIN_"What now is that reason by which Rama with a firm courage is not protecting His dear wife stolen 
by an ogre."_END

B_5_C_24_30
BEGIN_जानासि हि यथा भीरु स्त्रीणां यौवनमध्रुवम् |यावन्न ते व्यतिक्रामेत्तावत्सुखमवाप्नुहि || 
५-२४-३५_END
BEGIN_"O timid one! You know how youth of women is not lasting. As long as your youth will not pass away, 
so long get comfort."_END

B_5_C_22_43
BEGIN_स मैथिलीं ध्रम परामवस्थितां |प्रवेपमानां परिभर्स्य रावणः |विहाय सीतां मदनेन मोहितः 
|स्वमेव वेश्म प्रविवेश भास्वरम् || ५-२२-४६_END
BEGIN_That Ravana frightening Seetha who was steadfastly intent on virtue and who was shaking, leaving 
Seetha, infatuated by love, entered his own house which was shining._END

B_5_C_26_18
BEGIN_इहस्थां मां न जानीते शङ्के लक्ष्मणपूर्वजः |जानन्नपि स तेजस्वी धर्षणं मर्षयिष्यति || ५-२६-१९_END
BEGIN_"I doubt that Rama elder to Laksmana does not know me to be here. After knowing will that glorious 
Rama tolerate this outrage?"_END

B_5_C_24_31
BEGIN_उद्यानानि च रम्याणि पर्वतोपवनानि च |सह राक्षसराजेन चर त्वं मदिरेक्षणे || ५-२४-३६_END
BEGIN_"O one with intoxicating eyes! You along with king of ogres roam beautiful groves, mountains and 
nearby forests._END

B_5_C_26_19
BEGIN_हृतेति योऽधिगत्वा मां राघवाय निवेदयेत् |गृध्रारजोऽपि स रणे रावणेन निपातितः || ५-२६-२०_END
BEGIN_"Whoever Jatayu nearing Rama will have let known to Rama that Seetha was stolen, that king of vultures 
has been killed by Ravana in war."_END

B_5_C_24_32
BEGIN_स्त्रीसहस्राणि ते सप्त वशे स्थास्यन्ति सुन्दरि |रावणं भज भर्तारं भ्र्तारं सर्वरक्षसाम् 
|| ५-२४-३७_END
BEGIN_"O beautiful one! seven thousand women will be in your control. Have as husband Ravana the lord 
of all ogres."_END

B_5_C_26_20
BEGIN_कृतं कर्म महत्तेन मां तथाभ्यवपद्यता |तिष्ठता रावणद्वन्द्वे वृद्धेनापि जटायुषा || ५-२६-२१_END
BEGIN_"A great deed has been done by that Jatayu, thus protecting me, although of old age, standing in 
a dual combat with Ravana."_END

B_5_C_24_33
BEGIN_उत्पाट्य वा ते हृदयं भक्षयिष्यामि मैथिलि |यदि मे व्याहृतं वाक्यं न यथावत्करिष्यसि || ५-२४-३८_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! If you do not do according to my spoken word as is, I will eat your heart indeed by 
plucking it out."_END

B_5_C_26_21
BEGIN_यदि मामिह जानीयाद्वर्तमानां स राघवः |अद्य बाणैरभिक्रुद्धः कुर्याल्लोकमराक्षसम् || ५-२६-२२_END
BEGIN_"If that Rama knows me to be living here, with anger He will make the world to be without ogres 
with His arrows now."_END

B_5_C_24_34
BEGIN_ततश्चण्डोदरी नाम राक्षसी क्रोधमूर्छिता |भ्रामयन्ती महच्चूलमिदं वचनम्ब्रवीत् || ५-२४-३९_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Chandodari swooning with anger, turning around a big spike spoke 
this word._END

B_5_C_26_22
BEGIN_विधमेच्च पुरीं लङ्कां शोषयेच्च महोदधिम् |रावणस्य च नीचस्य कीर्तिं नाम च नाशयेत् || ५-२६-२३_END
BEGIN_"Rama will blow away the city of Lanka, will dry up the great ocean, will destroy the name and 
fame of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_24_35
BEGIN_इमां हरिणलोलाक्षीं त्रासोत्कम्पिपयोधरां |रावणेन हृतां दृष्ट्वा दौहृदो मे महानभूत् || ५-२४-४०_END
BEGIN_"Seeing this woman with eyes like that of a deer, with moving breasts due to fear, abducted by 
Ravana, there occured to me a great desire."_END

B_5_C_26_23
BEGIN_ततो निहतनाथानां राक्षसीनां गृहे गृहे |यथाहमेवं रुदती तथा भुयो न संशयः || ५-२६-२४_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter how I am crying in this way, in the same way, in very house, ogresses with killed husbands 
will cry again and again. There is no doubt in this."_END

B_5_C_24_36
BEGIN_यकृत्ल्पीहमथोत्पीडं हृदयं च सबन्धनम् |अन्त्राण्यपि तथा शीर्षं खादेयमिति मे मतिः || ५-२४-४१_END
BEGIN_"It is my mind to eat the liver, the spleen, flesh above heart and heart together with muscle and 
entrails and the head."_END

B_5_C_26_24
BEGIN_अन्विष्य रक्षसां लङ्कां कुर्याद्रामः सलक्ष्मणः |न हि ताभ्यां रिपुर्दृष्टो मुहूर्तमपि जीवति 
|| ५-२६-२५_END
BEGIN_"Rama together will Lakshmana will search the city of Lanka belonging to ogres. An enemy seen by 
those two will indeed not live even for a moment."_END

B_5_C_24_37
BEGIN_ततस्तु प्रघसा नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् |कण्ठमस्या नृशंसायाः पीडयाम किमास्यते || ५-२४-४२_END
BEGIN_An ogre woman named Pragasa spoke these words : "Squeeze the neck of this cruel woman. Why do we 
delay?"_END

B_5_C_26_25
BEGIN_चिताधुमाकुलपथा गृध्रमण्डलसंकुला |अचिरेण तु लङ्केयं श्मशानसदृशी भवेत् || ५-२६-२६_END
BEGIN_"This Lanka shortly will become like a graveyard, with paths agitated with smoke of funeral pyres, 
crowded with a group of vultures."_END

B_5_C_24_38
BEGIN_निवेद्यतां ततो राज्ञे मानुषी सा मृतेति ह |नात्र कश्चन संदेहः खादतेति स वक्ष्यति || ५-२४-४३_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter let it be known to the king that that human woman has died. He will say thus : "Eat.". 
There is no doubt in this matter."_END

B_5_C_26_26
BEGIN_अचिरेणैव कालेन प्राप्स्याम्येव मनोरथम् |दुष्प्रस्थानोऽयमाख्याति सर्वेषाम् वो विपर्ययम् 
|| ५-२६-२७_END
BEGIN_"In a short time only I will attain my desire. This evil course is telling of destruction of you 
all."_END

B_5_C_24_39
BEGIN_ततस्त्वजामुखी नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् |विशस्येमां ततः सर्वाः समान् कुरुत पीलुकान् || 
५-२४-४४_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Ajamukhi spoke these words : "All of you killing this woman thereafter 
do equal pieces."_END

B_5_C_26_27
BEGIN_यादृशानीह दृशन्ते लङ्कायामशुभानि वै |अचिरेणैव कालेन भविष्यति हतप्रभा || ५-२६-२८_END
BEGIN_"Here in Lanka whatever inauspicious things are being seen, from those, in a short while Lanka 
will become deprived of glory."_END

B_5_C_24_40
BEGIN_विभजाम ततः सर्वा विवादो मे न रोचते |पेयमानीयतां क्षिप्रं लेह्यमुच्चावचं बहु || ५-२४-४५_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter all of us will divide. Quarrel is not desirable to me. Liquor, many kinds and a lot 
of lickables be brought quickly."_END

B_5_C_26_28
BEGIN_नूनं लङ्का हते पापे रावणे राक्षसाधमे |शोषं यास्यति दुर्धर्षा प्रमदा विधव यथा || ५-२६-२९_END
BEGIN_"While the sinful, vile ogre Ravana is being killed, Lanka which is unconquerable till now, definitely 
will get drying up like a woman who lost husband."_END

B_5_C_24_41
BEGIN_ततः शूर्पणखा नाम राक्षसी वाक्यमब्रवीत् |अजामुख्या यदुक्तं हि तदेव मम रोचते || ५-२४-४६_END
BEGIN_Thereafter an ogre woman named Surpanakha spoke these words: "That which was spoken by Ajamukhi, 
is desirable to me."_END

B_5_C_26_29
BEGIN_पुण्योत्सव समृद्धा च नष्टभर्र्ती सराक्षसी |भविष्यति पुरी लङ्का नष्टभर्त्री यथाङ्गना || 
५-२६-३०_END
BEGIN_"Now abounding in pious festivities, the city of Lanka with lost lord together with ogresses will 
become like a woman with lost husband."_END

B_5_C_24_42
BEGIN_सुरा चानीयतां क्षिप्रं सर्वशोकविनाशिनी |मानुषं मां समास्वाद्य नृत्यामोथ निकुम्भिलाम् || 
५-२४-४७_END
BEGIN_"Liquor which is the destroyer of all sorrow be brought quickly. Eating human flesh afterwards, 
we will dance for propitiating Nikumbila."_END

B_5_C_24_43
BEGIN_एवं संभर्त्स्यमाना सा सीता सुरसुतोपमा |राक्षसीभिः सुघोराभिर्धैर्यमुत्सृज्य रोदिति || ५-२४-४८_END
BEGIN_Thus being frightened by horrible ogres, that Seetha equalling a daughter of gods, abandoning fortitude, 
was crying._END

B_5_C_26_30
BEGIN_नूनं राक्षसकन्यानां रुदन्तीनां गृहे गृहे |श्रोष्यामि नचिरादेव दुःखार्तानामिह ध्वनिम् || 
५-२६-३१_END
BEGIN_"In a short while here in every house I can definitely hear the sound of ogresses crying being 
tormented by grief."_END

B_5_C_27_0
BEGIN_इत्युक्ताह् सीतया घोरं राक्षस्यः क्रोधमूर्छिताः |काश्चिज्जग्मुस्तदाख्यातुं रावणस्य दुरात्मनः 
|| ५-२७-१_END
BEGIN_Thus spoken to by Seetha, ogresses swooned with anger terribly. Some went to tell that to Ravana 
the evil minded one._END

B_5_C_26_31
BEGIN_सान्धकारा हतद्योता हतराक्षसपुङ्गवा |भविष्यति पुरी लङ्का निर्दग्धा रामसायकैः || ५-२६-३२_END
BEGIN_"The city of Lanka will become burnt by Rama's arrows together with darkness, with destroyed luster 
with killed best ogres."_END

B_5_C_27_1
BEGIN_ततः सीतामुपागम्य राक्षस्यो घोरदर्शनाः |पुनः पुरुषमेकार्थमनर्थार्थमथाब्रुवन् || ५-२७-२_END
BEGIN_Therafter ogresses with a terrible appearance neared Seetha and ten agin spoke words of evil purpose, 
with a single meaning and which were harsh._END

B_5_C_26_32
BEGIN_यदि नाम स शूरो मां रामो रक्तान्तालोचनः |जानीयद्वर्तमानां हि रावणस्य निवेशने || ५-२६-३३_END
BEGIN_"Will that Rama who is a strong man with red eye corners know me to be in the house of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_27_2
BEGIN_अद्येदानीं तवानार्ये सीते पापविनिश्चये |राक्षस्यो भक्षयिष्यन्ति मांसमेतद्यथासुखम् || ५-२७-३_END
BEGIN_"O ignoble one! O one with a sinful resolve! O Seetha! Today at this moment ogreeses will eat this 
your flesh according to comfort."_END

B_5_C_27_3
BEGIN_सीतां ताभिरनार्याभिर्दृष्ट्वा संतर्जितां तदा |राक्षसी त्रिजटा वृद्धा शयाना वाक्यमब्रवीत् 
|| ५-२७-४_END
BEGIN_Then, seeing Seetha frightened by those evil ones, an ogress named Trijata, sleeping till then, 
spoke these words._END

B_5_C_26_33
BEGIN_अनेन तु नृशंसेन रावणेनाधमेन मे |समयो यस्तु निर्दिष्टस्तस्य कालोऽयमागतः || ५-२६-३४स 
च मे विहितो मृत्युरस्मिन् दुष्टे न वर्तते |_END
BEGIN_"Whatever time has been ordered by this cruel and vilest of men Ravana, this time has come to me. 
That death decreed to me does not hold good to this evil one (Ravana)."_END

B_5_C_27_4
BEGIN_आत्मानं खादतानार्या न सीतां भक्षयिष्यथ |जनकस्य सुतामिष्टां सुन्नषां दशरथस्य च || ५-२७-५_END
BEGIN_"O evil ones! Eat your selves. You will not eat Seetha who is the dear daughter of king Janaka 
and daughter-in-law of king Dasaratha."_END

B_5_C_26_34
BEGIN_अकार्यं ये न जानन्ति नैरृताः पापकारिणः || ५-२६-३५अधर्मात्तु महोत्पातो भविष्यति हि सांप्रतम् 
|नैते धर्मं विजानन्ति राक्षसाः पिशिताशनाः || ५-२६-३६_END
BEGIN_"Whoever sinful ogres who do not know what should not be done, due to their unrighteousness now 
there will be a great calamity. These meat eating ogres do not know virtue."_END

B_5_C_27_5
BEGIN_स्वप्नो ह्यद्य मया दृष्टो दारुनो रोमहर्षणः |राक्षसानामभावाय भर्तुरस्या भवाय च || ५-२७-६_END
BEGIN_"Now a dream which is terrible, causing the hairs to stand erect for the destruction of ogres and 
for the welfare of Her husband, has been seen by me."_END

B_5_C_26_35
BEGIN_ध्रुवं मां प्रातराशार्थे राक्षसः कल्पयिस्यति |साहं कथं करिष्यामि तं विना प्रियदर्शनम् 
|| ५-२६-३७रामम् रक्तान्तनयनमपश्यन्ती सुकुःखिता |_END
BEGIN_"An ogre will definitely eat me for breakfast. What should such I do without Rama with pleasing 
appearance? I am grieving a lot not seeing Rama with red eye corners."_END

B_5_C_27_6
BEGIN_एवमुक्टास्त्रिजटया राक्षस्यः क्रोधमूर्छिताः |सर्वा एवाब्रुवन्भीतास्त्रिजटां तामिदं वचः 
|| ५-२७-७_END
BEGIN_Thus spoken to by Trijata all ogresses were frightened and spoke to that Trijata these words._END

B_5_C_26_36
BEGIN_यदि कश्चित् प्रदाता मे विषस्याद्य भवेदिह || ५-२६-३८क्षिप्रं वैवस्वतं देवं पश्येयं पतिना 
विना |_END
BEGIN_"Now if there exists any one who is a giver of poison here, I without husband quickly will see 
the god Yama."_END

B_5_C_27_7
BEGIN_कथयस्व त्वया दृष्टः स्वप्नोऽयं कीदृशो निशि |तासां श्रुत्वा तु वचनं राक्षसीनां मुखाच्य्चुतम् 
|| ५-२७-८उवाच वचनं काले त्रिजटा स्वप्नसंश्रितम् |_END
BEGIN_"Of what kind is this dream seen by you. Tell us". Listening to this utterance that came forth 
from the mouths of those ogresses, Trijata spoke at that time this word relating to the dream._END

B_5_C_26_37
BEGIN_नाजानाज्जिवतीं रामः स मां लक्ष्मणपूर्वजः || ५-२६-३९जानन्तौ तौ न कुर्यातां नोर्य्वां हि 
मम मार्गणम् |_END
BEGIN_"That Rama elder to Lakshmana may not know me to be alive. If those two know me to be alive, then 
it cannot be said that they will not do my search on earth."_END

B_5_C_28_0
BEGIN_सा राक्षसेन्द्रस्य वचो निशम्य |तद्रावणस्याप्रियमप्रियार्ता |सीता वितत्रास यथा वनान्ते 
|सिंहाभिपन्ना गजराजकन्या || ५-२८-१_END
BEGIN_That Seetha, hearing those unpleasant words of Ravana, tormented by grief, was frightened like 
a tiny female-elephant overpowered by a lion in the middle of a forest._END

B_5_C_27_8
BEGIN_गजदन्तमयीं दिव्यां शिबिकामन्तरिक्षगाम् || ५-२७-९युक्तां हंससह्रेण स्वयमास्थाय राघवः |
शुक्लमाल्याम्बरधरो लक्ष्मणेन सहागतः || ५-२७-१०_END
BEGIN_"Rama wearing white garlands and clothes passing through the sky, Himself ascending a palanquin 
made of ivory tied with a thousand swans, arrived along with Lakshmana."_END

B_5_C_26_38
BEGIN_नूनं ममैव शोकेन स नीरो लक्ष्मणाग्रजः || ५-२६-४०देवलोकमितो यातस्त्यक्त्वा देहं महीतले |_END
BEGIN_"That valiant Rama who is the elder brother of Lakshmana due to grief of me, leaving the body on 
earth has gone to celestial world. This is certain."_END

B_5_C_28_1
BEGIN_सा राक्षसीमध्यगता च भीरु |र्वाग्भिर्भृशं रावणतर्जिता च |कान्तारमध्ये विजने विसृष्टा 
|बालेव कन्या विललाप सीता || ५-२८-२_END
BEGIN_That fearful Seetha, who was situated in the middle of female-demons and also threatened by Ravana 
with his words galore, lamented (as follows) like a young virgin who was left lonely in the midst of a forest._END

B_5_C_27_9
BEGIN_स्वप्ने चाद्य मया दृष्टा सीता शुक्लाम्बरावृता |सागरेण परिक्षिप्तं स्वेतं पर्वतमास्थिता 
|| ५-२७-११_END
BEGIN_"Now it has been seen by me in the dream that Seetha also wearing white clothes was sitting on 
a white mountain surrounded by the ocean."_END

B_5_C_26_39
BEGIN_धन्या देवाह् सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाश्च परमर्षयः || ५-२६-४१मम पश्यन्ति ये नाथं रामं राजीवलोचनम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Whoever is seeing my husband Rama with eyes resembling a lotus flower such Devas, Siddhas together 
with Gandharvas and great sages are fortunate."_END

B_5_C_28_2
BEGIN_सत्यं बतेदं प्रवदन्ति लोके |नाकालमृत्युर्भवतीति सन्तः |यत्राहमेवं परिभर्त्स्यमाना 
|जीवामि दीना क्षणमप्यपुण्या || ५-२८-३_END
BEGIN_"Truly the saints affirm that untimely death does not come in the world, as I being impure am surviving 
even for an instant, though being threatened in this way."_END

B_5_C_27_10
BEGIN_रामेण संगता सीता भास्करेण प्रभा यथा |राघवश्च मया दृष्टश्च तुर्दंष्ट्रं महागजम् || ५-२७-१२_END
BEGIN_"Seetha came together with Rama like the light with the Sun. Rama also was seen by me to be mounted 
on a great elephant with four tusks and equalling a mountain and Rama wandered together with Lakshmana."_END

B_5_C_26_40
BEGIN_अथवा न हि तस्यार्थो द्कर्मकामस्य धीमतः || ५-२६-४२मया रामस्य राजर्षेर्भार्यया परमात्मनः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Or to that Rama with a desire in virtuousness, who is intelligent, a sage-king, the supreme spirit, 
there is no use with me, his wife."_END

B_5_C_28_3
BEGIN_सुखाद्विहीनं बहुदुःखपूर्ण |मिदं तु नूनं हृदयं स्थिरं मे |विशीर्यते यन्न सहस्रधाद्य 
|वज्राहतं शृङ्गमिवाचलस्य || ५-२८-४_END
BEGIN_"Though devoid of happiness and frequently full of sorrow, my heart must be hard indeed, in that 
it does not break into a thousand pieces today like a mountain-top struck by lightning."_END

B_5_C_27_11
BEGIN_ततस्तौ नरशार्दूलौ दीप्यमानौ स्वतेजसा || ५-२७-१३शुक्लमाल्याम्बरधरौ जानकीं पर्युपस्थितौ 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter shining with their own radiance, wearing white garlands and clothes, those two best 
among men Rama and Laksmana neared Seetha."_END

B_5_C_26_41
BEGIN_दृश्यमाने भवेत्प्रीतिः सौहृदं नास्त्यपश्यतः || ५-२६-४३नाशयन्ति कृतघ्नास्तु न रामो नाशयिष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_"Friendly disposition will occur in what is being seen. There is no friendship to one who does 
not see. Ungrateful ones destroy frindship. But Rama will not destroy friendship."_END

B_5_C_28_4
BEGIN_वैवास्ति दोषो मम नूनमत्र |वध्याहमस्याप्रियदर्शनस्य |भावं न चास्याहमनुप्रदातु |
मलं द्विजो मन्त्रमिवाद्विजाय || ५-२८-५_END
BEGIN_"There is no fault of mine in this matter. I have become killable at the hands of this demon of 
disagreeable perception. I am not able to give him my affection any more than a member of the twice-born classes 
would offer a mystical verse to one not belonging to the twice-born classes."_END

B_5_C_26_42
BEGIN_किं नु मे न गुणाः केचित्किं वा भाग्यक्षयो मम || ५-२६-४४याहं सीदामि रामेण हीना मुख्येन 
भामिनी |_END
BEGIN_"I who is a woman who is perishing without the chief Rama to such me are there no good qualities 
or has my fortune diminished."_END

B_5_C_27_12
BEGIN_ततस्तस्य नगस्याग्रे ह्याकाशस्थस्य दन्तिनः || ५-२७-१४भर्त्रा परिगृहीतस्य जानकी स्कन्धमाश्रिता 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter Seetha rested on the upper part of back of elephant in the sky; taken by Her husband 
Rama to the front of that mountain."_END

B_5_C_28_5
BEGIN_नूनं ममाङ्गान्यचिरादनार्यः |शस्त्रैः शितै श्छेत्स्यति राक्षसेन्द्रः |तस्मिन्ननागच्छति 
लोकनाथे |गर्भस्थजन्तोरिव शल्यकृन्तः || ५-२८-६_END
BEGIN_"If Rama the Ruler of the world does not come here, the evil Ravana, the king of Demons will cut 
off my limbs with his sharpened weapons, even as a surgeon would cut the limbs of a lifeless feotus."_END

B_5_C_26_43
BEGIN_श्र्यो हि हीवितान्मर्तुं विहीनाया महात्मनः || ५-२६-४५रामादक्लिष्टचारित्राच्छूराच्छत्रुनिबर्हणात् 
|_END
BEGIN_"To me who is deprived of Rama with untroubled reputation, a warrior, annihilator of enemies, a 
great soul, more than living, death is good."_END

B_5_C_27_13
BEGIN_भर्तुरङ्कात्समुत्पत्य ततः कमललोचना || ५-२७-१५चन्द्रसूर्यौ मया दृष्टा पाणिना परिमार्जती 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter it has been seen by me that Seetha with eyes like lotuses has risen up from the lap 
of Her husband and gently touched the Moon and the Sun with Her hand."_END

B_5_C_28_6
BEGIN_दुःखं बतेदं मम दुःखिताया |मासौ चिरायाधिगमिष्यतो द्वौ |बद्धस्य वध्यस्य तथा निशान्ते 
|राजापराधादिव तस्करस्य || ५-२८-७_END
BEGIN_"To me lamenting, two months will go up to a long time, as at the end of a night a thief imprisoned 
and to be capitally punished under the detention orders of a king. Alas! This is painful."_END

B_5_C_26_44
BEGIN_अथवा न्यस्तशस्त्रौ तौ वने मूलफलाशिनौ || ५-२६-४६भ्रातरौ हि नरश्रेष्ठौ संवृत्तौ वनगोचरौ 
|_END
BEGIN_"Or those two brothers who are best among men giving up weapons in the forest may have become dwellers 
of forest eating roots and fruits."_END

B_5_C_27_14
BEGIN_ततस्ताभ्यां कुमाराभ्यामास्थितः स गजोत्तमः || ५-२७-१६सीतया च विशालाक्ष्या लङ्काया उपरिस्थितः_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter that best elephant ascended by those princes Rama and Lakshmana and by Seetha with 
wide eyes stood on the top of Lanka."_END

B_5_C_28_7
