BEGIN_हा राम हा लक्ष्मण हा सुमित्रे |हा राममातः सह मे जनन्या |एषा विपद्याम्यहमल्पभाग्या 
|महार्णवे नौरिव मूढवाता || ५-२८-८_END
BEGIN_"O Rama, O Lakshmana, O Sumitra, O Kausalya! O mother! I, of a scanty fortune, am going to be destroyed, 
like a ship driven out of its course by a strong wind in a mighty ocean."_END

B_5_C_26_45
BEGIN_अथवा राक्षसेन्द्रेण रावणेन दुरात्मना || ५-२६-४७चद्मना घातितौ शूरौ भ्रातरौ रामलक्ष्मणौ 
|_END
BEGIN_"Or Rama and Lakshmana the warrior brothers may have been killed by the evil soul king of ogres 
Ravana by deceit."_END

B_5_C_27_15
BEGIN_पाण्डुरर्षभयुक्तेन रथेनाष्टयुजा स्वयम् || ५-२७-१७इहोपयातः काकुथ्सः सीतया सह भार्य या |_END
BEGIN_"Rama together with wife Seetha, Himself came here in a chariot tied with eight white bulls."_END

B_5_C_28_8
BEGIN_तरस्विनौ धारयता मृगस्य |सत्त्वेन रूपं मनुजेन्द्रपुत्रौ |नूनं विशस्तौ मम कारणात्तौ 
|सिंहर्षभौ द्वाविव वैद्युतेन || ५-२८-९_END
BEGIN_"In the disguise of a deer, those two energetic sons of Dasaratha were surely killed for my sake, 
as two excellent lions killed by a flashing thunderbolt."_END

B_5_C_26_46
BEGIN_साहमेवंगते काले मर्तुमिच्छामि सर्वथा || ५-२६-४८न च मे विहितो मृत्युरस्मिन् दुःखेऽपि वर्तते 
|_END
BEGIN_"Under such circumstances and time, such I in all ways am desiring to die. Even in this grief, 
death is not bestowed on me."_END

B_5_C_27_16
BEGIN_लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा सीतया सह वीर्यवान् || ५-२७-१८आरुह्य पुष्पकं दिव्यं विमानं सूर्यसन्निभम् 
|उत्तरां दिशमालोक्य जगाम पुरुष्त्तमः || ५-२७-१९_END
BEGIN_"The valorous best among men Rama together with brother Lakshmana and with Seetha ascended wonderful 
Pushpaka aeroplane equalling the Sun, went in the northern direction."_END

B_5_C_28_9
BEGIN_नूनं स कालो मृगरूपधारी |मामल्पभाग्यां लुलुभे तदानीम् |यत्रार्यपुत्रं विससर्ज मूढा 
|रामानुजं लक्ष्मणपूर्वजं च || ५-२८-१०_END
BEGIN_"Certainly that Time-spirit, assuming the guise of a deer, allured me, a woman of poor fortune 
at that time and to whom I, a stupid woman, sent forth (far away) Lakshmana and the noble prince Rama the elder 
brother of Lakshmana."_END

B_5_C_26_47
BEGIN_धन्याः खलु महात्मानो मुनयस्त्यक्तकिल्बिषाः || ५-२६-४९जितात्मनो महाभागा येषां न स्तः प्रियाप्रिये 
|_END
BEGIN_"Great souled ones with abandoned sins, with a conquered mind, those with great fortune, sages 
are indeed fortunate to whom there is no pleasure and displeasure."_END

B_5_C_27_17
BEGIN_एवं स्वप्ने मया दृष्टो रामो विष्णुपराक्रमः |लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा सीतया सह राघवः || ५-२७-२०_END
BEGIN_"Rama with strength equalling that of Lord Vishnu, born in Raghu's dynasty together with brother 
Lakshmana and with Seetha has been seen by me thus in the dream."_END

B_5_C_28_10
BEGIN_हा राम सत्यव्रत दीर्घबाहो |हा पूर्णचन्द्रप्रतिमानवक्त्र |हा जीवलोकस्य हितः प्रियश्च 
|वध्यां न मां वेत्सि हि राक्षसानाम् || ५-२८-११_END
BEGIN_"O Rama, the strictly truthful man and the long-armed, O the man whose face resembles the full-moon! 
You, who are well-disposed of the world of living beings, do not indeed know me to have been sentenced to death 
by the demons."_END

B_5_C_26_48
BEGIN_प्रियान्न संभवेद्दुःखमप्रियादधिकं भयम् || ५-२६-५०ताभ्यां हि ये वियुज्यन्ते नमस्तेषां महात्मनाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"From pleasure sorrow and from displeasure great fear do not occur to great souls. Whoever are 
separated from pleasure and displeasure, my obeisance to such great souls."_END

B_5_C_27_18
BEGIN_न हि रामो महातेजाः शोक्यो जेतुं सुरासुरैः |राक्षसैर्वापि चान्यैर्वा स्वर्गः पापजनैरिव 
|| ५-२७-२१_END
BEGIN_"Rama with great glory is not possible to be defeated by Suras or by ogres or by others like heaven 
not being conquerable by sinners."_END

B_5_C_28_11
BEGIN_अनन्यदैवत्वमियं क्षमा च |भूमौ च शय्या नियमश्च धर्मे |पतिव्रतात्वं विफलं ममेदम् |
कृतं कृतघ्नेष्विव मानुषाणाम् || ५-२८-१२_END
BEGIN_"My not having a deity (other than my husband), this patience, my reposing on the floor, my restriction 
in righteousness, my devotion to the husband - all this has become a waste, like a good act done by men to ungrateful 
men becoming waste"._END

B_5_C_26_49
BEGIN_साहंत्युक्ता प्रियेणैव रामेन विदितात्मना || ५-२६-५१प्राणांस्त्यक्ष्यामि पापस्य रावनस्य 
गता वशम् |_END
BEGIN_"Left by dear Rama with a well known mind coming under the control of sinful Ravana, such I will 
leave breath of life."_END

B_5_C_27_19
BEGIN_रावणश्च मया दृष्टः क्षितौ तैलसमुक्षितः |रक्तवासाह् पिबन् मत्तः करवीरकृतस्रजः|| ५-२७-२२_END
BEGIN_"Ravana also was seen by me on earth sprinkled with oil, with red clothes, with garlands tied with 
Oleander flowers, drinking oil and intoxicated."_END

B_5_C_28_12
BEGIN_मोघो हि धर्मश्चरितो मयायं |तथैकपत्नीत्वमिदं निरर्थम् |या त्वां न पश्यामि कृशा विवर्णा 
|हीना त्वया संगमने निराशा || ५-२८-१३_END
BEGIN_"For me who is not seeing you, who is bereft of you, who is not hopeful of coming into contact 
with you, who is emaciated and pale in complexion this righteous act performed by me has indeed become a waste. 
Likewise, this state of my being only one wife to you has become useless.."_END

B_5_C_27_20
BEGIN_विमानात्पुष्पकादद्य रावणः पतितो भुवि |कृष्यमाणः स्त्रिया दृष्टो मुण्डः कृष्णाम्बरः पुनः 
|| ५-२७-२३_END
BEGIN_"Now Ravana fallen down on to earth from Pushpaka aeroplane having the head shaved, wearing black 
clothes again was seen to be pulled by a woman."_END

B_5_C_28_13
BEGIN_पितुर्निदेशं नियमेन कृत्वा वनान्निवृत्तश्चरितव्रतश्च |स्त्रीभिस्तु मन्ये विपुलेक्षणाभिस्त्वं 
रंस्यसे वीतभयः कृतार्थः || ५-२८-१४_END
BEGIN_"Having fulfilled your father's command as per the order of his words and observed your vow, you 
return from the forest fearlessly and having accomplished your purpose, I think you will enjoy carnally with large-eyed 
women."_END

B_5_C_27_21
BEGIN_रथेन खरयुक्तेन रक्तमाल्यानुलेपनः |पिबंस्तैलं हसन्नृतन् भ्रान्तचित्ताकुलेन्द्रियः || ५-२७-२४_END
BEGIN_"Wearing red garlands and unguents, drinking oil, laughing, dancing, with a confused mind, with 
agitated senses, Ravana went by a chariot tied by donkeys."_END

B_5_C_28_14
BEGIN_अहं तु राम त्वयि जातकामा चिरं विनाशाय निबद्धभावा |मोघं चरित्वाथ तपो व्रतञ्च त्यक्ष्यामि 
धिग्जीवितमल्पभाग्याम् || ५-२८-१५_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! Having performed austerity and vow in vain, I for myself who has fallen in love with you 
and in whose was confined an affection for you for a long time, for my own destruction, I can lose my life. Woe 
to me of my little fortune!"_END

B_5_C_27_22
BEGIN_गर्दभेन ययौ शीग्रं दक्षिणां दिशमास्थितः |पुनरेव मया दृष्टो रावणो राक्षसेश्वरः || ५-२७-२५
पतितोऽवाक्छिरा भूमौ गर्दभाद्भयमोहितः |_END
BEGIN_"Undertaking southern direction, Ravana went quickly by a donkey.Again it was seen by me that the 
king of ogres Ravana stupefied with fear, fell down from the donkey with head down."_END

B_5_C_28_15
BEGIN_सा जीवितं क्षिप्रमहं त्यजेयं |विषेण शस्त्रेण शितेन वापि |विषस्य दाता न हि मेऽस्ति 
कश्चि |च्छस्त्रस्य वा वेश्मनि राक्षसस्य || ५-२८-१६_END
BEGIN_"I as such will abandon quickly my life by poison or by a sharp weapon. To me, none is there, who 
is a giver either of a poison or of a sharp weapon in the house of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_27_23
BEGIN_सहसोत्थाय संभ्रान्तो भयार्तो मदविह्वलः || ५-२७-२६उन्मत्त इव दिग्वासा दुर्वाक्यं प्रलपन् 
बहु |दुर्गन्धं दुस्सहं घोरं तिमिरं नरकोपमम् || ५-२७-२७मलपङ्कं प्रविश्याशु मग्नस्तत्र स रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"That Ravana rising up quickly, together with perplexity, distressed with fear, excited by passion, 
being naked, like a mad man, prattling many bad words, entering dirt with a bad smell, which was intolerable, 
horrible, dark, like the hell and quickly sank in that."_END

B_5_C_27_24
BEGIN_कण्ठे बद्ध्वा दशग्रीवं प्रमदा रक्तवासिनी || ५-२७-२८काळी कर्दमलिप्ताङ्गी दिशं याम्यां प्रकर्षति 
|_END
BEGIN_"A woman with red clothes, who was black, with body smeared with dirt, tying Ravana by the throat, 
was pulling hiim in southern direction."_END

B_5_C_28_16
BEGIN_इतीव देवी बहुधा विलप्य |सर्वात्मना राममनुस्मरन्ती |प्रवेपमाना परिशुष्कवक्त्रा |
नगोत्तमं पुष्पितमाससाद || ५-२८-१७_END
BEGIN_Thus lamenting in several ways, Seetha was recollecting Rama in all spirits and trembling with 
and emaciated face, approached that excellent tree in bloom._END

B_5_C_28_17
BEGIN_सा शोकतप्ता बहुधा विचिन्त्य |सीताथ वेण्युद्ग्रथनं गृहीत्वा |उद्भुध्य वेण्युद्ग्रथनेन 
श्रीघ्र |महं गमिष्यामि यमस्य मूलम् || ५-२८-१८_END
BEGIN_Seetha, who was tormented with grief, thus thinking in various ways and thereafter holding her 
braid of hair looking like a hanging rope (now thought within herself) "I shall go to the presence of Yama the 
God of Death by tying my neck quickly with my braid of hair looking like a hanging rope"_END

B_5_C_27_25
BEGIN_एवं तत्र मया दृष्टह् कुम्भकर्णो निशाचरः || ५-२७-२९रावणस्य सुताः सर्वे दृष्टास्तैलसमुक्षिताः 
|_END
BEGIN_"In that dream the ogre Kumbhakarna has been seen thus by me. All Ravana's sons have been seen 
to be sprinkled with oil."_END

B_5_C_28_18
BEGIN_उपस्थिता सा मृदुसर्वगात्री |शाखां गृहीत्वाथ नगस्य तस्य |तस्यास्तु रामं प्रविचिन्तयन्त्या 
|रामानुजं स्वं च कुलं शुभाङ्ग्याः || ५-२८-१९शोकानिमित्तानि तथा बहूनि |धैर्यार्जितानि प्रवराणि लोके 
|प्रादुर्निमित्तानि तदा बभूवुः |पुरापि सिद्धान्युपलक्षितानि || ५-२८-२०_END
BEGIN_Thereafter Seetha with all her soft limbs stood seizing a branch of that tree. To her having handsome 
limbs, who was thinking of Rama, Lakshmana and her own race, then appeared many omens, which were not having adequate 
occasion for grief, which procured courage in the world, which were excellent and which were seen earlier also 
as thoroughly efficacious._END

B_5_C_27_26
BEGIN_वराहेण दशग्रीवः शिंशुमारेण चेन्द्रजित् || ५-२७-३०उष्ट्रेण कुम्भकर्णश्च प्रयाता दक्षिणां 
दिशम् |_END
BEGIN_"Ravana by a pig, Indrajit by a porpoise, Kumbhakarna by a camel set out in southern direction."_END

B_5_C_27_27
BEGIN_एकस्तत्र मया दृष्टः श्वेतच्छत्रो विभीसणः || ५-२७-३१शुक्लमाल्याम्बरधरः शुक्लगन्धानुलेपनः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Among those Vibhishana is the only one who has been seen by me to be having a white umbrella, 
wearing white garlands and clothes and anointing body with white unguents."_END

B_5_C_27_28
BEGIN_शङ्खदुन्दुभिनिर्घोषैर्नृत्तगीतैरलङ्कृतः || ५-२७-३२आरुह्य शैलसंकाशं मेघस्तनितनिस्वनम् |
चतुर्धन्तं गजं दिव्यमास्ते तत्र विभीषणः || ५-२७-३३चतुर्भिः सचिवैः सार्धं वहायसमुपस्थितः |_END
BEGIN_"Vibhishana is there adorned with the sound of conch shells and kettledrums, with dances and songs, 
ascended a best elephant equalling a mountain with the sound of a thundering cloud, with four tusks. He approached 
the sky together with four ministers"_END

B_5_C_27_29
BEGIN_समाजश्च मया दृष्टो गीतवादित्रनिःस्वनः || ५-२७-३४पिबतां रक्तमाल्यानां रक्षसां रक्तवाससाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"An assembly also of ogres drinking oil and wearing red garlands, with red clothes, with the sound 
of songs and musical instruments has been seen by me."_END

B_5_C_27_30
BEGIN_लङ्का चेयं पुरी रम्या सवाजिरथकुञ्जरा || ५-२७-३५सागरे पतिता दृष्टा भग्नगोपुरतोरणा |_END
BEGIN_"This beautiful city of Lanka has also been seen together with horses and elephants with broken 
gates and arches fallen down in the ocean."_END

B_5_C_27_31
BEGIN_लङ्का दृष्टा मया स्वप्ने रावणेनाभिरक्षिता || ५-२७-३६दग्धा रामस्य दूतेन वानरेण तरस्विना 
|_END
BEGIN_"Lanka protected by Ravana has been seen by me in the dream to be burnt by a quick Vanara who is 
a messenger of Rama."_END

B_5_C_27_32
BEGIN_सीत्वा तैलं प्रनृत्ताश्च प्रहसन्त्यो महास्वनाः || ५-२७-३७लङ्कायाण् भस्मरूक्षायां सर्वा 
राक्षसयोषितः |_END
BEGIN_"In Lanka horrible with ash, all ogresses were drinking oil, laughing heartily with a great noise 
and also dancing a lot."_END

B_5_C_27_33
BEGIN_कुम्भकर्णादयश्चेमे सर्वे राक्षसपुङ्गवाः || ५-२७-३८रक्तं निवसनं गृह्य प्रविष्टा गोमयह्रदे 
|_END
BEGIN_"All these best among ogres such as Kumbhakarna and others taking a red cloth entered a hole filled 
with cow dung."_END

B_5_C_27_34
BEGIN_अपगच्छत नश्यध्वं सीतामाप्नोति राघवः || ५-२७-३९घातयेत्परमामर्षी युष्मान् सार्धं हि राक्षनैः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Go away! Be destroyed! Rama will get Seetha. With a great anger He will get you killed together 
with other ogres."_END

B_5_C_27_35
BEGIN_प्रियां बहुमतां भार्यां वनवासमनुव्रताम् || ५-२७-४०भर्त्सितां तर्जितां वापि नानुमंस्यति 
राघवः |_END
BEGIN_"Rama will not approve frightening ot threatening His dear wife who is highly valued by Him, who 
followed Him to live in the forest."_END

B_5_C_27_36
BEGIN_तदलं क्रूरवाक्यैश्च सान्त्वमेवाभिधीयताम् || ५-२७-४१अभियाचाम वैदेहीमेतद्धि मम रोचते |_END
BEGIN_"For that reason, enough of cruel words. Gentle words indeed be said. Let us request Seetha. This 
is agreeable to me."_END

B_5_C_27_37
BEGIN_यस्यामेवंविधः स्वप्नो दुःखितायां प्रदृश्यते || ५-२७-४२सा दुःखैर्विविधैर्मुक्ता प्रियं 
प्राप्नोत्यनुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_"Which woman while being sorrowful, such type of dream has been seen, that woman being released 
from various sorrows, will get unsurpassed pleasure."_END

B_5_C_27_38
BEGIN_भर्त्सितामपि याचध्वं राक्सस्यः किं विवक्षया || ५-२७-४३राघवाद्धि भयं घोरं राक्षसानामुपस्थितम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"O ogresses! Entreat Seetha who has been frightened. What is the use with a desire to speak. From 
Rama a horrible fear has come to ogres."_END

B_5_C_27_39
BEGIN_प्रणिपातप्रसन्ना हि मैथिली जनकात्मजा || ५-२७-४४अलमेषा परित्रारुं राक्षस्यो महातो भयात् 
|अपि चास्या विशालाक्ष्या न किंचिदुपलक्षये || ५-२७-४५विरूपमपि चाङ्गेषु सुसूक्ष्ममपि लक्षणम् |_END
BEGIN_"O ogresses! This Seetha daughter of Janaka, pleased with prostration is competent to protect us 
from great danger. And also I do not see in Her who is wide eyed, in Her limbs even a minute misshapen characteristic, 
even insignificant one."_END

B_5_C_27_40
BEGIN_चायावैगुण्यमात्रं तु शङ्के दुःखमुपस्थितम् || ५-२७-४६अदुःखार्हमिमां देवीं वैहायसमुपस्थिताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"I see an imperfection in complexion alone. I doubt that this princess who came near an aeroplane 
in my dream, who is not suited to sorrows received sorrow."_END

B_5_C_27_41
BEGIN_अर्थसिद्धिं तु वैदेह्याः पश्याम्यहमुपस्थिताम् || ५-२७-४७राक्षसेन्द्रविनाशं च विजयं राघवस्य 
च |_END
BEGIN_"I am seeing Seetha coming near accomplishment of motive. I also see the destruction of Ravana 
also and victory of Rama coming near."_END

B_5_C_27_42
BEGIN_निमित्तभूतमेतत्तु श्रोतुमस्या महत्प्रियम् || ५-२७-४८दृश्यते च स्फुरच्चक्षुः पद्मपत्रमिवायतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Being a cause to listen to a great pleasure of Her, this throbbing eye long like a lotus petal 
is being seen my me."_END

B_5_C_27_43
BEGIN_ईषच्च हृषितो वास्या दक्षिणाया ह्यदक्षिणः || ५-२७-४९अकस्मादेव वैदेह्या बहुरेकः प्रकम्पते 
|_END
BEGIN_"One left arm of this strightforward Seetha suddenly has become erect and is slightly trembling."_END

B_5_C_27_44
BEGIN_करेणुहस्तप्रतिमः सव्यश्चोरुरनुत्तमः || ५-२७-५०वेपमानः सूचयति राघवं पुरतः स्थितम् |_END
BEGIN_"Seetha's best left thigh equal to an elephant's trunk is trembling indicating Rama's standing 
in front of Her."_END

B_5_C_27_45
BEGIN_पक्षी च शाखानिलयं प्रविष्टः |पुनः पुनश्चोत्तमसान्त्ववादी |सुस्वागतं वाचमुदीरयानः |
पुनः पुनश्चोदयतीव हृष्टः || ५-२७-५१_END
BEGIN_"A bird also entering its dwelling place on a branch again and again speaking best consolating 
words, is telling heartily welcoming words being delighted again and again, as though impelling Seetha."_END

B_5_C_29_0
BEGIN_तथा गताम् ताम् व्यथिताम् अनिन्दिताम् |व्यपेत हर्षाम् परिदीन मानसाम् |शुभाम् निमित्तानि 
शुभानि भेजिरे |नरम् श्रिया जुष्टम् इव उपजीविनः || ५-२९-१_END
BEGIN_To her who was in such circumstances, who was in distress, who was irraproachable, devoid of joy 
and dejected but virtuous, was bestowed with auspicious omens, as a prosperous man is bestowed with dependent 
servants._END

B_5_C_29_1
BEGIN_तस्याः शुभम् वामम् अराल पक्ष्म |राजी वृतम् कृष्ण विशाल शुक्लम् |प्रास्पन्दत एकम् नयनम् 
सुकेश्या |मीन आहतम् पद्मम् इव अभिताम्रम् || ५-२९-२_END
BEGIN_The beautifully haired Seetha's left eye, which was auspicious, whose surrounding row of eye-lashes 
were curved, which was black, wide and bright-looking; was predominantly quivering, like a red lotus quivered 
by the blow of a fish._END

B_5_C_29_2
BEGIN_भुजः च चार्व् अन्चित पीन वृत्तः |पर अर्ध्य काल अगुरु चन्दन अर्हः |अनुत्तमेन अध्युषितः 
प्रियेण |चिरेण वामः समवेपत आशु || ५-२९-३_END
BEGIN_Her left shoulder, which was pretty, distinguished beefy and round, which deserved to be applied 
with excellent black aloe and sandalwood paste, which had been used_END

B_5_C_29_3
BEGIN_गज इन्द्र हस्त प्रतिमः च पीनः |तयोः द्वयोः सम्हतयोः सुजातः |प्रस्पन्दमानः पुनः ऊरुः 
अस्या |रामम् पुरस्तात् स्थितम् आचचक्षे || ५-२९-४_END
BEGIN_Of her two thighs kept together, the left tigh which was beefy and well born, which resembled the 
trunk of a princely elephant was predominantly quivering, spoke indistinctly of existenc of Rama in front._END

B_5_C_29_4
BEGIN_शुभम् पुनः हेम समान वर्णम् |ईषत् रजो ध्वस्तम् इव अमल अक्ष्याः |वासः स्थितायाः शिखर 
अग्र दन्त्याः |किंचित् परिस्रंसत चारु गात्र्याः || ५-२९-५_END
BEGIN_Again, the clothing of Seetha standing there, of spotless eyes and charming limbs, having teeth 
resembling the buds of jasmine, which was of golden shade and was slightly soiled as it were with dust, glited 
down, which appeared auspicious (for her)._END

B_5_C_30_0
BEGIN_हनुमान् अपि विक्रान्तः सर्वम् शुश्राव तत्त्वतः |सीतायाः त्रिजटायाः च राक्षसीनाम् च तर्जनम् 
|| ५-३०-१_END
BEGIN_The valiant Hanuma also heard truly all those words of Seetha, Trijata and the threatening words 
of the female demons._END

B_5_C_29_5
BEGIN_एतैः निमित्तैः अपरैः च सुभ्रूः |सम्बोधिता प्राग् अपि साधु सिद्धैः |वात आतप क्लान्तम् 
इव प्रनष्टम् |वर्षेण बीजम् प्रतिसम्जहर्ष || ५-२९-६_END
BEGIN_Bolstered by these and some other omens which straight explained that they were fruitful on the 
earlier occasion also, Seetha of beautiful eyebrows disclosed a great joy, even as a seed vanished and withered 
by the wind and the sun, got sprouted by rain._END

B_5_C_30_1
BEGIN_अवेक्षमाणः ताम् देवीम् देवताम् इव नन्दने |ततो बहु विधाम् चिन्ताम् चिन्तयामास वानरः || 
५-३०-२_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, seeing that Seetha as a divine lady in the garden of Nandana, Hanuma echoed his thought 
in various ways._END

B_5_C_29_6
BEGIN_तस्याः पुनः बिम्ब फल उपम ओष्ठम् |स्वक्षि भ्रु केश अन्तम् अराल पक्ष्म |वक्त्रम् बभासे 
सित शुक्ल दम्ष्ट्रम् |राहोः मुखाच् चन्द्र इव प्रमुक्तः || ५-२९-७_END
BEGIN_Moreover, having the lips resembling Bimba fruit, having beautiful eyes and eyebrows, whose eye 
lids are curved, having charming white teeth, her face shone like the moon liberated from the mouth of the demon 
Rahu._END

B_5_C_30_2
BEGIN_याम् कपीनाम् सहस्राणि सुबहूनि अयुतानि च |दिक्षु सर्वासु मार्गन्ते सा इयम् आसादिता मया 
|| ५-३०-३_END
BEGIN_"Which Seetha is being searched in all directions by many thousands and myriads of monkeys, the 
same Seetha has been found by me."_END

B_5_C_29_7
BEGIN_सा वीत शोका व्यपनीत तन्द्री |शान्त ज्वरा हर्ष विबुद्ध सत्त्वा |अशोभत आर्या वदनेन शुक्ले 
|शीत अन्शुना रात्रिः इव उदितेन || ५-२९-८_END
BEGIN_Free from sorrow, her weariness removed, her mental affliction alleviated and her consciousness 
awakened with exaltation, that esteemed lady (Seetha) looked handsome with her countenance, as a night with the 
moon appears during the bright fortnight._END

B_5_C_30_3
BEGIN_चारेण तु सुयुक्तेन शत्रोः शक्तिम् अवेक्षिता |गूढेन चरता तावत् अवेक्षितम् इदम् मया || ५-३०-४_END
BEGIN_"By me, employed thoughtfully (by my Master) as a secret agent and gone about secretly with a view 
to ascertain the enemy's strength, this has been perceived._END

B_5_C_30_4
BEGIN_राक्षसानाम् विशेषः च पुरी च इयम् अवेक्षिता |राक्षस अधिपतेः अस्य प्रभावो रावणस्य च || ५-३०-५_END
BEGIN_"The characteristics of demons, this town and the power of the king of demons, Ravana, have been 
perceived by me."_END

B_5_C_31_0
BEGIN_एवम् बहु विधाम् चिन्ताम् चिन्तयित्व महाकपिः |संश्रवे मधुरम् वाक्यम् वैदेह्या व्याजहार 
ह || ५-३१-१_END
BEGIN_Thus reflecting on many kinds of thought, Hanuma spoke the following sweet words within the hearing 
range of Seetha._END

B_5_C_30_5
BEGIN_युक्तम् तस्य अप्रमेयस्य सर्व सत्त्व दयावतः |समाश्वासयितुम् भार्याम् पतिदर्शन कान्क्षिणीम् 
|| ५-३०-६_END
BEGIN_"It is proper for me to console the wife of Rama, desirous of seeing her husband who is compassionate 
towards all beings and who is of immeasurable might."_END

B_5_C_31_1
BEGIN_राजा दशरथो नाम रथ कुन्जर वाजिनाम् |पुण्य शीलो महाकीर्तिः ऋजुः आसीन् महायशाः || ५-३१-२_END
BEGIN_"There was a king named Dasaratha who was very glorious among the kings of Ikshvaku dynasty and 
had a virtuous disposition. He owned chariots, elephants and horses, becoming very famous._END

B_5_C_30_6
BEGIN_अहम् आश्वासयामि एनाम् पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ आननाम् |अदृष्ट दुह्खाम् दुह्खस्य न हि अन्तम् अधिगच्छतीम् 
|| ५-३०-७_END
BEGIN_"I shall console this woman, whose face resembles a full moon, who is having an unforeseen affliction, 
who is tormented by grief and who is not attaining the end to her affliction."_END

B_5_C_31_2
BEGIN_राजर्षीणां गुणश्रेष्ठस्तपसा चर्षिभिः समः |चक्र वर्ति कुले जातः पुरम् दर समो बले || ५-३१-३_END
BEGIN_"He was excellent in virtues among royal sages. He was equal to the seven sages in austerity. He 
was born in the lineage of emperors and was equivalent to Indra in prowess."_END

B_5_C_30_7
BEGIN_यदि हि अहम् इमाम् देवीम् शोक उपहत चेतनाम् |अनाश्वास्य गमिष्यामि दोषवत् गमनम् भवेत् || 
५-३०-८_END
BEGIN_"If I return without consoling this Seetha, the wife of Rama, even though her mind is tormented 
by grief, my departure becomes blemished."_END

B_5_C_31_3
BEGIN_अहिंसा रतिः अक्षुद्रो घृणी सत्य पराक्रमः |मुख्यः च इक्ष्वाकु वंशस्य लक्ष्मीवाम्ल् लक्ष्मि 
वर्धनः || ५-३१-४_END
BEGIN_"He was keen on harmlessness. He was not vulgar. He was compassionate. He was truly mighty. He 
was an eminent king in Ikshvaku race. He was endowed with prosperity and was causing to increase prosperity."_END

B_5_C_30_8
BEGIN_गते हि मयि तत्र इयम् राज पुत्री यशस्विनी |परित्राणम् अविन्दन्ती जानकी जीवितम् त्यजेत् 
|| ५-३०-९_END
BEGIN_"Not finding a rescue when I return to Kishkindha, the illustrious princess Seetha may give up 
her life."_END

B_5_C_31_4
BEGIN_पार्थिव व्यञ्जनैः युक्तः पृथु श्रीः पार्थिव ऋषभः |पृथिव्याम् चतुः अन्तयाम् विश्रुतः सुखदः 
सुखी || ५-३१-५_END
BEGIN_"The king Dasaratha was endowed with royal characteristics, highly prosperous, excellent among 
kings and highly prosperous, excellent among kings and famous on earth with its four borders. He was happy man 
and gave happiness to others."_END

B_5_C_30_9
BEGIN_मया च स महाबाहुः पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ आननः |समाश्वासयितुम् न्याय्यः सीता दर्शन लालसः || ५-३०-१०_END
BEGIN_"That long-armed Rama having the countenance of a full moon, eagerly longing to see Seetha, is 
fit to be consoled by me."_END

B_5_C_32_0
BEGIN_ततः शाखा अन्तरे लीनम् दृष्ट्वा चलित मानसा |वेष्टितार्जुनवस्त्रम् तं विद्युत्सम्घातपिङ्गलम् 
|| || ५-३२-१_END
BEGIN_Then, seeing Hanuma, who was tawny coloured like a series of flashing thunderbolts wrapped up in 
a white cloth and hiding behind the branches of a tree, Seetha had her mind shaken._END

B_5_C_31_5
BEGIN_तस्य पुत्रः प्रियो ज्येष्ठः तारा अधिप निभ आननः |रामो नाम विशेषज्ञः श्रेष्ठः सर्व धनुष्मताम् 
|| ५-३१-६_END
BEGIN_"There was an eldest son named Rama to that Dasaratha. Rama was beloved having a moon-like face. 
He, knows the distinctions among humans and others. He was excellent among all the wielders of the bow."_END

B_5_C_30_10
BEGIN_निशा चरीणाम् प्रत्यक्षम् अक्षमम् च अभिभाषणम् |कथम् नु खलु कर्तव्यम् इदम् कृच्छ्र गतो हि 
अहम् || ५-३०-११_END
BEGIN_"It is not proper to speak with her within the sight of these female-demons. How indeed is this 
to be done? I am indeed perplexed."_END

B_5_C_32_1
BEGIN_सा ददर्श कपिम् तत्र प्रश्रितम् प्रिय वादिनम् |पुल्लाशोकोत्कराभासम् तप्तचामिकरेक्षणम् || 
|| ५-३२-२_END
BEGIN_Seetha beheld there a monkey, beaming like a cluster of Ashoka flowers wide opened, with his eyes 
resembling regined gold, humble and speaking agreeable words._END

B_5_C_31_6
BEGIN_रक्षिता स्वस्य वृत्तस्य स्व जनस्य अपि रक्षिता |रक्षिता जीव लोकस्य धर्मस्य च परम् तपः || 
५-३१-७_END
BEGIN_"That Rama who annihilates enemies, is a protector of his own mode of life, a protector of his 
own people, a protector of every living being and a protector of righteousness."_END

B_5_C_30_11
BEGIN_अनेन रात्रि शेषेण यदि न आश्वास्यते मया |सर्वथा न अस्ति संदेहः परित्यक्ष्यति जीवितम् || 
५-३०-१२_END
BEGIN_"If she is not consoled by me during the rest of this night, she will forsake her life by all means. 
There is no doubt about it."_END

B_5_C_32_2
BEGIN_मैथिली चिन्तयामास स्वप्नो अयम् इति भामिनी |अहो भीममिदं रूपं वानरस्य दुरासदम् || ५-३२-३
दुर्निरीक्षमिति ज्ञात्वा पुनरेव मुमोह सा |_END
BEGIN_Seetha got a great surprise and thought (as follows): "Alas! This monkey is hard to be approached, 
fearful and difficult to be looked at." Thus thinking, she was bewildered again._END

B_5_C_31_7
BEGIN_तस्य सत्य अभिसंधस्य वृद्धस्य वचनात् पितुः |सभार्यः सह च भ्रात्रा वीरः प्रव्रजितो वनम् 
|| ५-३१-८_END
BEGIN_"By the command of that Dasaratha, his old father and true-speaking man, that Rama a brave man 
went on exile to a forest along with his wife and brother."_END

B_5_C_30_12
BEGIN_रामः च यदि पृच्छेन् माम् किम् माम् सीता अब्रवीत् वचः |किम् अहम् तम् प्रतिब्रूयाम् असम्भाष्य 
सुमध्यमाम् || ५-३०-१३_END
BEGIN_"If Rama enquires of me as to what words did Seetha speak about him, what can I say to Rama without 
speaking now to this Seetha, the slender-waisted lady?"_END

B_5_C_32_3
BEGIN_विललाप भृशं सीता करुणम् भयमोहिता || ५-३२-४रामरामेति दुःखार्ता लक्ष्मणेति च भामिनी |
रुरोद बहुधा सीता मन्दम् मन्दस्वरा सती || ५-३२-५_END
BEGIN_The splendid woman Seetha, bewildered by fear and afflicted with grief, lamented most piteously 
saying "O, Rama! O, Rama! and "O Lakshmana!". Seetha wept faintly in a low voice in many ways._END

B_5_C_31_8
BEGIN_तेन तत्र महाअरण्ये मृगयाम् परिधावता |राक्षसा निहताः शूरा बहवः कामरूपिणः || ५-३१-९_END
BEGIN_"While hunting in that forest, that Rama killed many demons who were valiant and who could assume 
any form at will."_END

B_5_C_30_13
BEGIN_सीता संदेश रहितम् माम् इतः त्वरया गतम् |निर्दहेत् अपि काकुत्स्थः क्रुद्धः तीव्रेण चक्षुषा 
|| ५-३०-१४_END
BEGIN_"To me returning in haste from here without carrying Seetha's message Rama may get irritated and 
burn me up with his pungent eyes."_END

B_5_C_32_4
BEGIN_सा तम् दृष्ट्वा हरिश्रेष्ठं विनीतवदुपस्थितम् |मैथिली चिन्तयामास स्वप्नोऽयमिति भामिनी || 
५-३२-६_END
BEGIN_Seeing that excellent monkey appraching humbly, that splendid woman Seetha thought it as a dream._END

B_5_C_31_9
BEGIN_जन स्थान वधम् श्रुत्वा हतौ च खर दूषणौ |ततः तु अमर्ष अपहृता जानकी रावणेन तु || ५-३१-१०
वञ्चयित्वा वने रामं मृगरूपेण मायया |_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, hearing about the killing of demons in Janasthana, a part of Dandaka forest, in addition 
to killing of Khara and Dushana the demons, the enraged Ravana took away, Seetha, by deceiving Rama in creating 
an illusive image of deer in the forest."_END

B_5_C_30_14
BEGIN_यदि चेत् योजयिष्यामि भर्तारम् राम कारणात् |व्यर्थम् आगमनम् तस्य ससैन्यस्य भविष्यति || 
५-३०-१५_END
BEGIN_"Even if I instigate my master Sugreeva to do his best in the cause of Rama, his arrival here with 
an army will be futile."_END

B_5_C_32_5
BEGIN_सा वीक्षमाणा पृथुभुग्नवक्त्रं शाखामृगेन्द्रस्य यथोक्तकारम् |ददर्श पिङ्गप्रवरं महार्हं 
वातात्मजं बुद्धिमतां वरिष्ठम् || ५-३२-७_END
BEGIN_Seetha, looking hither and thither, saw Hanuman, who was having a wide and curved mouth, doing 
acts as told by sugreeva the king of monkeys, the foremost of monkeys, greatly adored and the best among the inelligent._END

B_5_C_31_10
BEGIN_स मार्गमाणस्ताम् देवीम् रामः सीतामन्न्दिताम् || ५-३१-११आससाद वने मित्रम् सुग्रीवम् नाम 
वानरम् |_END
BEGIN_"Searching for Seetha the irreproachable lady, that Rama met a monkey called Sugreeva as his friend 
in the forest."_END

B_5_C_30_15
BEGIN_अन्तरम् तु अहम् आसाद्य राक्षसीनाम् इह स्थितः |शनैः आश्वासयिष्यामि सम्ताप बहुलाम् इमाम् 
|| ५-३०-१६_END
BEGIN_"Staying here itself and getting hold of an opportunity even in the midst of the female-demons 
(when they are in attentive), I shall slowly console Seetha who is very much in distress."_END

B_5_C_32_6
BEGIN_सा तम् समीक्ष्य एव भृशम् विसम्ज्ञा गत असु कल्पा इव बभूव सीता |चिरेण सम्ज्ञाम् प्रतिलभ्य 
चैव चैव विचिन्तयामास विशाल नेत्रा || ५-३२-८_END
BEGIN_As soon as seeing Hanuma Seetha lost her consciousness very much and became seemingly lifeless. 
Regaining her consciousness after a long time the wide eyed Seetha moreover thought (as follows)_END

B_5_C_33_0
BEGIN_सोऽवतीर्य द्रुमात्तस्माद्विद्रुमप्रतिमाननः |विनीतवेषः कृपणः प्रणिपत्योपसृत्य च || ५-३३-१
ताम् अब्रवीन् महातेजा हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |शिरसि अञ्जलिम् आधाय सीताम् मधुरया गिरा || ५-३३-२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, with coral-coloured face, very bright, the son of wind-god, wearing a humble and feeble 
look, approached Seetha by stepping down from the tree and offered her his salutation by keeping his joined palms 
on his head and spoke the following sweet words:_END

B_5_C_31_11
BEGIN_ततः स वालिनम् ह्त्वा रामः परपुरम्जयः || ५-३१-१२प्रायच्छत्कपिराज्यम् तत्सुग्रीवाय महाबलः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, Rama the conqueror of enemy's cities and very strong man, killed Vali and gave away 
that kingdom of monkeys to Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_30_16
BEGIN_अहम् हि अतितनुः चैव वनरः च विशेषतः |वाचम् च उदाहरिष्यामि मानुषीम् इह संस्कृताम् || ५-३०-१७_END
BEGIN_"However, I am very small in stature, particularly as a monkey and can speak now Sanskrit, the 
human language too."_END

B_5_C_32_7
BEGIN_स्वप्नो मया अयम् विकृतो अद्य दृष्टः शाखा मृगः शास्त्र गणैः निषिद्धः |स्वस्ति अस्तु रामाय 
सलक्ष्मणाय तथा पितुः मे जनकस्य राज्ञः || ५-३२-९_END
BEGIN_"Today, I saw an ugly monkey in my dream, which is forbidden according to a body of scriptures. 
May it be well with Rama together with Lakshmana and with my father, King Janaka._END

B_5_C_33_1
BEGIN_का नु पद्म पलाश अक्षी क्लिष्ट कौशेय वासिनी |द्रुमस्य शाखाम् आलम्ब्य तिष्ठसि त्वम् अनिन्दिता 
|| ५-३३-३_END
BEGIN_"O Lady with your eyes resembling lotus leaves, wearing a worn out silken cloth! O, the irreproachable 
one! You have stood, holding by the hand a branch of the tree who are you?"_END

B_5_C_30_17
BEGIN_यदि वाचम् प्रदास्यामि द्विजातिः इव संस्कृताम् |रावणम् मन्यमाना माम् सीता भीता भविष्यति 
|| ५-३०-१८वानरस्य विशेषेण कथं स्यादभिभाषणम्म् |_END
BEGIN_"If I use Sanskrit language like a brahmin, Seetha will get frightened, thinking me as Ravana. 
Especially, how can a monkey speak it?"_END

B_5_C_31_12
BEGIN_सुग्रीवेणापि संदिष्टा हरयः कामरूपिणः || ५-३१-१३दिक्षु सर्वासु ताम् देवीम् विचिन्न्वन्ति 
सहस्रशः |_END
BEGIN_"As commanded and sent by Sugreeva, thousands of monkeys capable of assuming form at their will, 
are searching for that lady Seetha in all quarters of the earth."_END

B_5_C_32_8
BEGIN_स्वप्नो अपि न अयम् न हि मे अस्ति निद्रा |शोकेन दुह्खेन च पीडितायाः |सुखम् हि मे न 
अस्ति यतो अस्मि हीना |तेन इन्दु पूर्ण प्रतिम आननेन || ५-३२-१०_END
BEGIN_"This is not a dream. To me, tormented by sorrow and grief, there is indeed no sleep. To me, separated 
from Rama whose countenance resembles a full moon, there is no happiness indeed!"_END

B_5_C_33_2
BEGIN_किम् अर्थम् तव नेत्राभ्याम् वारि स्रवति शोकजम् |पुण्डरीक पलाशाभ्याम् विप्रकीर्णम् इव उदकम् 
|| ५-३३-४_END
BEGIN_"Tears of sorrow are gushing down from your eyes, as water is scattered down from two lotus-petals. 
Why?"_END

B_5_C_30_18
BEGIN_अवश्यम् एव वक्तव्यम् मानुषम् वाक्यम् अर्थवत् || ५-३०-१९मया सान्त्वयितुम् शक्या न अन्यथा 
इयम् अनिन्दिता |_END
BEGIN_"Certainly, meaningful words of a human being are to be spoken by me. Otherwise, the virtuous Seetha 
cannot be consoled."_END

B_5_C_31_13
BEGIN_अहम् सम्पातिवचनाच्छतयोजनमायतम् || ५-३१-१४अस्या हेतोर्विशालाक्ष्याः सागरं वेगवान् प्लुतः 
|_END
BEGIN_"By the words of Sampati, I a swift monkey crossed the ocean having a length of one hundred yojanas 
for the sake of this broad eyed Seetha."_END

B_5_C_32_9
BEGIN_रामेति रामेति सदैव बुद्ध्या विचिन्त्या वाचा ब्रुवती तमेव |तस्यानुरूपं च कथां तदर्था मेवं 
प्रपश्यामि तथा शृणोमि || ५-३२-११_END
BEGIN_"Since I am pondering with my mind about that Rama only, and always saying 'Rama! Rama!' thus, 
confomably I am seeing and hearing a story thus corresponding to he same thought."_END

B_5_C_33_3
BEGIN_सुराणाम् असुराणाम् च नाग गन्धर्व रक्षसाम् |यक्षाणाम् किम्नराणाम् च का त्वम् भवसि शोभने 
|| ५-३३-५_END
BEGIN_"O auspicious lady! In whom are you born-whether in celestials or in ogres or in serpent-demons 
or in celestial musicians or in demons or in semi-divine beings or in mythical beings?"_END

B_5_C_30_19
BEGIN_सा इयम् आलोक्य मे रूपम् जानकी भाषितम् तथा || ५-३०-२०रक्षोभिः त्रासिता पूर्वम् भूयः त्रासम् 
गमिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"Looking at my figure and the language, Seetha who was already frightened previously by the demons, 
will get frightened again."_END

B_5_C_31_14
BEGIN_यथा रूपाम् यथा वर्णाम् यथा लक्ष्मीम् विनिश्चिताम् || ५-३१-१५अश्रौषम् राघवस्य अहम् सा इयम् 
आसादिता मया |_END
BEGIN_"This Seetha has been found by me according to the same comeliness, complexion and the bodily marks 
as I had heard from Rama."_END

B_5_C_32_10
BEGIN_अहम् हि तस्य अद्य मनो भवेन सम्पीडिता तत् गत सर्व भावा |विचिन्तयन्ती सततम् तम् एव तथैव 
पश्यामि तथा शृणोमि || ५-३२-१२_END
BEGIN_"Tormented as I am today by manmatha god of love longing for Rama, my whole feelings directed towards 
him and constantly thinking of him alone, in the like manner I am seeing him and in the like manner i am hearing 
of him alone."_END

B_5_C_33_4
BEGIN_का त्वम् भवसि रुद्राणाम् मरुताम् वा वर आनने |वसूनाम् वा वर आरोहे देवता प्रतिभासि मे || 
५-३३-६_END
BEGIN_"O lovely-faced woman! Who are you among eleven Rudras who bestow strength, or among Maruts the 
storm-gods or among eight Vasus the beneficent gods? O Handsome lady with fine hips! You appear to me as a deity."_END

B_5_C_30_20
BEGIN_ततो जात परित्रासा शब्दम् कुर्यान् मनस्विनी || ५-३०-२१जानमाना विशाल अक्षी रावणम् काम रूपिणम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, this large-eyed Seetha who is full of mind, thinking me as Ravana who can assume any 
form at will, may shout loudly, engendered by fear."_END

B_5_C_31_15
BEGIN_विरराम एवम् उक्त्वा असौ वाचम् वानर पुम्गवः || ५-३१-१६जानकी च अपि तत् श्रुत्वा विस्मयम् 
परमम् गता |_END
BEGIN_Having spoken these words, Hanuma kept quiet. Hearing those words, Seetha too got a great surprise._END

B_5_C_32_11
BEGIN_मनो रथः स्यात् इति चिन्तयामि |तथा अपि बुद्ध्या च वितर्कयामि |किम् कारणम् तस्य हि न 
अस्ति रूपम् |सुव्यक्त रूपः च वदति अयम् माम् || ५-३२-१३_END
BEGIN_"I am imagining that my wish will be fulfilled. Likewise, I am reasoning my wish by my intellect 
also. There is no concrete form indeed for my wish. He, with a well manifested form is speaking to me. for what 
reason?"_END

B_5_C_33_5
BEGIN_किम् नु चन्द्रमसा हीना पतिता विबुध आलयात् |रोहिणी ज्योतिषाम् श्रेष्ठा श्रेष्ठा सर्व गुण 
अन्विता || ५-३३-७_END
BEGIN_"Are you Rohini, endowed with all the best qualities, fallen from heaven, left behind by moon and 
excellent among stars."_END

B_5_C_31_16
BEGIN_ततः सा वक्र केश अन्ता सुकेशी केश सम्वृतम् || ५-३१-१७उन्नम्य वदनम् भीरुः शिंशपा वृक्षम् 
ऐक्षत |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, that Seetha whose consciousness was enshrouded by affliction, whose hair-ends were 
curved and who was of a fearful nature, lifted her face and looked towards Shimshupa tree._END

B_5_C_30_21
BEGIN_सीतया च कृते शब्दे सहसा राक्षसी गणः || ५-३०-२२नाना प्रहरणो घोरः समेयात् अन्तक उपमः |_END
BEGIN_"As soon as Seetha shouts loudly, a troop of female-demons, wielding various kinds of weapons and 
appearing dreadful as Yama the Lord of Death, may assemble here."_END

B_5_C_32_12
BEGIN_नमो अस्तु वाचः पतये सवज्रिणे स्वयम्भुवे चैव हुत अशनाय |अनेन च उक्तम् यत् इदम् मम अग्रतो 
वन ओकसा तच् च तथा अस्तु न अन्यथा || ५-३२-१४_END
BEGIN_"My salutation to Brihaspati the Lord of eloquence, together with Indra the wielder of a thunderbolt, 
to Brahma the self-existent Lord and to the Lord of Fire eating the oblations! Let whatever words spoken by this 
monkey be true! Let them not be untrue!"_END

B_5_C_33_6
BEGIN_कोपात् वा यदि वा मोहात् भर्तारम् असित ईक्षणा || ५-३३-८वसिष्ठम् कोपयित्वा त्वम् न असि कल्याणि 
अरुन्धती |_END
BEGIN_"O dark-eyed lady! Are you not the auspicious Arundhati, who irritated her husband, Vasishta the 
sage either by anger or by error?"_END

B_5_C_31_17
BEGIN_निशम्य सीता वचनम् कपेश्च |दिशश्च सर्वाः प्रदिशश्च वीक्ष्य |स्वयम् प्रहर्षं परमं जगाम 
|सर्वात्मना राममनुस्मरन्ती || ५-३१-१८_END
BEGIN_Hearing Hanuma's words and looking at all quarters and sub-quarters, Seetha was recollecting Rama 
in all ways and obtained a great joy._END

B_5_C_30_22
BEGIN_ततो माम् सम्परिक्षिप्य सर्वतो विकृत आननाः || ५-३०-२३वधे च ग्रहणे चैव कुर्युः यत्नम् यथा 
बलम् |_END
BEGIN_"Then those ugly faced female-demons may encircle me from all sides and try to catch and kill me 
with all their might."_END

B_5_C_34_0
BEGIN_तस्याः तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा हनूमान् हरि यूथपः |दुह्खात् दुह्ख अभिभूतायाः सान्तम् उत्तरम् 
अब्रवीत् || ५-३४-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Seetha who was overthrown from one grief to another, Hanuma the best of 
monkeys gave the following reply in a kindly and affectionate manner._END

B_5_C_33_7
BEGIN_को नु पुत्रः पिता भ्रात भर्ता वा ते सुमध्यमे || ५-३३-९अस्माल् लोकात् अमुम् लोकम् गतम् 
त्वम् अनुशोचसि |_END
BEGIN_"O the slender waisted lady! You seem to be lamenting over someone who died is he your son, or 
father or brother or husband."_END

B_5_C_31_18
BEGIN_सा तिर्यग् ऊर्ध्वम् च तथा अपि अधस्तान् |निरीक्षमाणा तम् अचिन्त्य बुद्धिम् |ददर्श पिन्ग 
अधिपतेः अमात्यम् |वात आत्मजम् सूर्यम् इव उदयस्थम् || ५-३१-१९_END
BEGIN_Looking at sides, up and down, that Seetha saw that Hanuman, the sun of wind-god, having an unimaginable 
intelligence, the minister of Sugreeva and looking like the sun behind an eastern mountain._END

B_5_C_30_23
BEGIN_गृह्य शाखाः प्रशाखाश्च स्कन्धांश्चोत्तमशाखिनाम् || ५-३०-२४दृष्ट्वा विपरिधावन्तं भवेयुर्भयशङ्किताः 
|_END
BEGIN_"Then, seeing me running hither and thither, seizing big branches, twigs and trunks of excellent 
trees, they may get alarmed with fear."_END

B_5_C_34_1
BEGIN_अहम् रामस्य संदेशात् देवि दूतः तव आगतः |वैदेहि कुशली रामः त्वाम् च कौशलम् अब्रवीत् || 
५-३४-२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the daughter of the king of Videha Kingdom! I have come here as your messenger on Rama's 
directions. The virtuous Rama enquired about your welfare too."_END

B_5_C_33_8
BEGIN_रोदनादतिनिःश्वासाद्भूमिसंस्पर्शनादपि || ५-३३-१०न त्वाम् देवीमहम् मन्ये राज्ञः संज्ञावधारणात् 
|_END
BEGIN_"You are lamenting. You are sighing a lot. You are touching the earth. You have royal insignia 
in you. According to these things, I do not consider you as a divine woman."_END

B_5_C_30_24
BEGIN_मम रूपम् च सम्प्रेक्ष्य वनम् विचरतो महत् || ५-३०-२५राक्षस्यो भय वित्रस्ता भवेयुः विकृत 
आननाः |_END
BEGIN_"The ugly faced female-demons will be frightened with fear, after seeing my huge figure wandering 
in the grove."_END

B_5_C_34_2
BEGIN_यो ब्राह्मम् अस्त्रम् वेदान् च वेद वेदविदाम् वरः |स त्वाम् दाशरथी रामो देवि कौशलम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ५-३४-३_END
BEGIN_"O Divine Lady! Rama the son of Dasaratha, who is excellent among the knowers of Veda and who knows 
Brahma's missile (a mythical weapon which deals infallible destruction) and Vedas the sacred knowledge, enquired 
about your welfare."_END

B_5_C_33_9
BEGIN_व्यञ्जनानि हि ते यानि लक्षणानि च लक्षये || ५-३३-११महिषी भूमि पालस्य राज कन्या असि मे मता 
|_END
BEGIN_"Based on the marks on your person and your bodily characteristics, I believe you to be a queen 
of an emperor and the daughter of a king."_END

B_5_C_30_25
BEGIN_ततः कुर्युः समाह्वानम् राक्षस्यो रक्षसाम् अपि || ५-३०-२६राक्षस इन्द्र नियुक्तानाम् राक्षस 
इन्द्र निवेशने |_END
BEGIN_"Then those female-demons may call the other demons too retained by Ravana in his house."_END

B_5_C_34_3
BEGIN_लक्ष्मणः च महातेजा भर्तुः ते अनुचरः प्रियः |कृतवान् शोक सम्तप्तः शिरसा ते अभिवादनम् || 
५-३४-४_END
BEGIN_"Also the greatly splendourous Lakshmana, the favourite brother and the follower of your husband, 
himself tormented with grief, performed salutation to you by bowing his head."_END

B_5_C_30_26
BEGIN_ते शूल शर निस्त्रिंश विविध आयुध पाणयः || ५-३०-२७आपतेयुः विमर्दे अस्मिन् वेगेन उद्विग्न 
कारिणः |_END
BEGIN_"Those female-demons with an element of turbulence and rapidity may rush into a battle with various 
kinds of weapons like spears lances and swords."_END

B_5_C_33_10
BEGIN_रावणेन जन स्थानात् बलात् अपहृता यदि || ५-३३-१२सीता त्वम् असि भद्रम् ते तन् मम आचक्ष्व 
पृच्छतः |_END
BEGIN_"If you are Seetha stolen per force by Ravana from Janasthana, tell it to me who is asking if you 
please!"_END

B_5_C_34_4
BEGIN_सा तयोः कुशलम् देवी निशम्य नर सिम्हयोः |प्रीति सम्हृष्ट सर्व अन्गी हनूमान्तम् अथ अब्रवीत् 
|| ५-३४-५_END
BEGIN_Hearing that news of welfare of Rama and Lakshmana the excellent of men, the divine lady, with 
all her limbs thrilled with joy, spoke to Hanuma (as follows):_END

B_5_C_30_27
BEGIN_सम्क्रुद्धः तैः तु परितो विधमन् रक्षसाम् बलम् || ५-३०-२८शक्नुयम् न तु सम्प्राप्तुम् परम् 
पारम् महाउदधेः |_END
BEGIN_"Surrounded on all sides by them, I may not be able to reach the other shore of the great ocean, 
while destroying the army of demons."_END

B_5_C_33_11
BEGIN_यथा हि तव वैदैन्यम् रूपम् चाप्यतिमानुषम् || ५-३३-१३तपसा चान्वितो वेषस्त्वं राममहिषी ध्रुवम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"According to your miserable state, the super-human beautiful figure and your costume endowed with 
austerity, surely you are Rama's wife."_END

B_5_C_34_5
BEGIN_कल्याणी बत गथा इयम् लौकिकी प्रतिभाति मे |एहि जीवन्तम् आनदो नरम् वर्ष शतात् अपि || ५-३४-६_END
BEGIN_" 'Joy rushes to surviving man even though (it be) as the end of a hundred years' - this popular 
adage appears true and and auspicious for me."_END

B_5_C_30_28
BEGIN_माम् वा गृह्णीयुः आप्लुत्य बहवः शीघ्र कारिणः || ५-३०-२९स्यात् इयम् च अगृहीत अर्था मम च 
ग्रहणम् भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"Or having jumped up (over me) many demons operating speedily may capture me. Then, Seetha may 
not be able to know the occurrence of my arrival. Even I may get captured too."_END

B_5_C_33_12
BEGIN_सा तस्य वचनम् श्रुत्वा राम कीर्तन हर्षिता || ५-३३-१४उवाच वाक्यम् वैदेही हनूमन्तम् द्रुम 
आश्रितम् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing his words, Seetha was delighted of Rama's mention and spoke the following words to Hanuma, 
who was dwelling on a tree._END

B_5_C_34_6
BEGIN_तयोः समागमे तस्मिन् प्रीतिः उत्पादिता अद्भुता |परस्परेण च आलापम् विश्वस्तौ तौ प्रचक्रतुः 
|| ५-३४-७_END
BEGIN_Seetha showed wonderful friendly disposition towards Hanuma who approached her. Both of them also 
conversed with each other in full confidence._END

B_5_C_30_29
BEGIN_हिंसा अभिरुचयो हिंस्युः इमाम् वा जनक आत्मजाम् || ५-३०-३०विपन्नम् स्यात् ततः कार्यम् राम 
सुग्रीवयोः इदम् |_END
BEGIN_"Or the violent minded demons may kill this Seetha. Consequently this work of Rama and Sugreeva 
will be ruined."_END

B_5_C_33_13
BEGIN_पृथिव्यां राजसिंहानां मुख्यस्य विदितात्मनः || ५-३३-१५स्नुषा दशरथस्याहम् शत्रुसैन्यप्रतापिनः 
|_END
BEGIN_"I am the daughter-in-law of Dasaratha, eminent among the excellent kings on earth, who understands 
the nature of the spirit and who torments the army of the adversary."_END

B_5_C_34_7
BEGIN_तस्याः तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा हनूमान् हरि यूथपः |सीतायाः शोक दीनायाः समीपम् उपचक्रमे || ५-३४-८_END
BEGIN_Hearing that reply of Seetha who was afflicted with grief, Hanuma the army-chief of monkeys endeavoured 
to draw nearer to her._END

B_5_C_33_14
BEGIN_दुहिता जनकस्य अहम् वैदेहस्य महात्मनः || ५-३३-१६सीता च नाम नाम्ना अहम् भार्या रामस्य धीमतः 
|_END
BEGIN_"I am the daughter of the noble-natured Janaka, the king of Videha kingdom. I am know._END

B_5_C_30_30
BEGIN_उद्देशे नष्ट मार्गे अस्मिन् राक्षसैः परिवारिते || ५-३०-३१सागरेण परिक्षिप्ते गुप्ते वसति 
जानकी |_END
BEGIN_"Seetha is residing in this secret place, with a concealed access, surrounded by demons and encircled 
by an ocean."_END

B_5_C_34_8
BEGIN_यथा यथा समीपम् स हनूमान् उपसर्पति |तथा तथा रावणम् सा तम् सीता परिशन्कते || ५-३४-९_END
BEGIN_In as much as that Hanuma drew nearer to her, in the same way, that Seetha suspected him as Ravana._END

B_5_C_35_0
BEGIN_ताम् तु राम कथाम् श्रुत्वा वैदेही वानर ऋषभात् |उवाच वचनम् सान्त्वम् इदम् मधुरया गिरा || 
५-३५-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing that narration about Rama from Hanuma the excellent of monkeys, Seetha in a sweet voice 
spoke the following gentle words:_END

B_5_C_33_15
BEGIN_समा द्वादश तत्र अहम् राघवस्य निवेशने || ५-३३-१७भुन्जाना मानुषान् भोगान् सर्व काम समृद्धिनी 
|_END
BEGIN_"I stayed in Rama's house there for twelve years, enjoying the worldly pleasures belonging to human 
kind and fulfilling all my desires."_END

B_5_C_30_31
BEGIN_विशस्ते वा गृहीते वा रक्षोभिः मयि सम्युगे || ५-३०-३२न अन्यम् पश्यामि रामस्य सहायम् कार्य 
साधने |_END
BEGIN_"If I am killed in the battle or got captured by the demons, I do not see any other companion for 
Rama who can fulfill this work (of searching for Seetha)."_END

B_5_C_34_9
BEGIN_अहो धिग् धिग् कृतम् इदम् कथितम् हि यत् अस्य मे |रूप अन्तरम् उपागम्य स एव अयम् हि रावणः 
|| ५-३४-१०_END
BEGIN_"O shame! It was my guilt to tell him all this to him. He is indeed that Ravana, who obtained another 
guise."_END

B_5_C_35_1
BEGIN_क्व ते रामेण संसर्गः कथम् जानासि लक्ष्मणम् |वानराणाम् नराणाम् च कथम् आसीत् समागमः || ५-३५-२_END
BEGIN_"Where was your contact with Rama? How do you know Lakshmana? How did the union between monkeys 
and men arise?"_END

B_5_C_30_32
BEGIN_विमृशन् च न पश्यामि यो हते मयि वानरः || ५-३०-३३शत योजन विस्तीर्णम् लन्घयेत महाउदधिम् |_END
BEGIN_"Even after due reflection, I do not see any monkey who can transgress the ocean with a breadth 
of one hundred Yojanas, in case I am killed."_END

B_5_C_33_16
BEGIN_ततः त्रयोदशे वर्षे राज्येन इक्ष्वाकु नन्दनम् || ५-३३-१८अभिषेचयितुम् राजा स उपाध्यायः प्रचक्रमे 
|_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, in the thirteenth year, King Dasaratha along with his preceptors started to perform 
anointment of the kingdom to Rama, a celebrity of Ikshvaku dynasty."_END

B_5_C_34_10
BEGIN_ताम् अशोकस्य शाखाम् सा विमुक्त्वा शोक कर्शिता |तस्याम् एव अनवद्य अन्गी धरण्याम् समुपाविशत् 
|| ५-३४-११_END
BEGIN_That Seetha, having faultless limbs, leaving that branch of Ashoka tree and as emaciated with grief, 
sat down on that ground itself._END

B_5_C_35_2
BEGIN_यानि रामस्य लिन्गानि लक्ष्मणस्य च वानर |तानि भूयः समाचक्ष्व न माम् शोकः समाविशेत् || ५-३५-३_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! What are the characteristics of Rama and Lakshmana? Narrate them to me, so that sorrow 
will not take possession of me again."_END

B_5_C_30_33
BEGIN_कामम् हन्तुम् समर्थो अस्मि सहस्राणि अपि रक्षसाम् || ५-३०-३४न तु शक्ष्यामि सम्प्राप्तुम् 
परम् पारम् महाउदधेः |_END
BEGIN_"I am competent to kill even thousands of demons. I am quite sure. But, after doing such a large 
battle, I may not be capable of reaching the other shore of the ocean."_END

B_5_C_33_17
BEGIN_तस्मिन् सम्भ्रियमाणे तु राघवस्य अभिषेचने || ५-३३-१९कैकेयी नाम भर्तारम् देवी वचनम् अब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_"While that anointment of Rama was being arranged, a queen called Kaikeyi spoke the following words 
to Dasaratha, her husband._END

B_5_C_34_11
BEGIN_हनुमानपि दुःखार्तां तां दृष्ट्वा भयमोहिताम् |अवन्दत महाबाहुः ततः ताम् जनक आत्मजाम् || 
५-३४-१२सा च एनम् भय वित्रस्ता भूयो न एव अभ्युदैक्षत |_END
BEGIN_Seeing Seetha afflicted with grief and deluded with fear, the great armed Hanuma also then simply 
saluted her. She too, trembling with fear, did not look towards him again._END

B_5_C_35_3
BEGIN_कीदृशम् तस्य संस्थानम् रूपम् रामस्य कीदृशम् |कथम् ऊरू कथम् बाहू लक्ष्मणस्य च शंस मे || 
५-३५-४_END
BEGIN_"Of what kind was the appearance of that Rama and of Lakshmana? Of what kind was their form? How 
were the thighs? How were the arms? Tell me."_END

B_5_C_30_34
BEGIN_असत्यानि च युद्धानि संशयो मे न रोचते || ५-३०-३५कः च निह्संशयम् कार्यम् कुर्यात् प्राज्ञः 
ससंशयम् |_END
BEGIN_'Conflicts are unreal too and to me, there is no desire for uncertainty. which intellectual will 
do an assured act with an apprehension?"_END

B_5_C_33_18
BEGIN_न पिबेयम् न खादेयम् प्रत्यहम् मम भोजनम् || ५-३३-२०एष मे जीवितस्य अन्तो रामो यदि अभिषिच्यते 
|_END
BEGIN_"If Rama gets anointed for the kingdom, from now onwards, I shall neither drink water nor take 
my food daily. This is the end to my life."_END

B_5_C_34_12
BEGIN_तम् दृष्ट्वा वन्दमानम् तु सीता शशि निभ आनना || ५-३४-१३अब्रवीत् दीर्घम् उच्छ्वस्य वानरम् 
मधुर स्वरा |_END
BEGIN_Seetha, with her countenance resembling the moon, seeing Hanuma saluting her, had a deep sigh and 
spoke to Hanuma in a sweet-sounding voice (as follows)_END

B_5_C_35_4
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः तु वैदेह्या हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |ततो रामम् यथा तत्त्वम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे 
|| ५-३५-५_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Seetha, Hanuma, the son of wind-god, then started to describe Rama according 
to his actual state (as follows):_END

B_5_C_30_35
BEGIN_एष दोषो महान् हि स्यान् मम सीता अभिभाषणे || ५-३०-३६प्राण त्यागः च वैदेह्या भवेत् अनभिभाषणे 
|_END
BEGIN_"If I do not talk, there will be Seetha's death. If I talk to Seetha, this great lapse will occur."_END

B_5_C_33_19
BEGIN_यत् तत् उक्तम् त्वया वाक्यम् प्रीत्या नृपति सत्तम || ५-३३-२१तच् चेन् न वितथम् कार्यम् 
वनम् गच्छतु राघवः |_END
BEGIN_"O the excellent king! If that word of pledge was uttered affectionately by you and if it is not 
going to be a waste, let Rama go to the forest."_END

B_5_C_34_13
BEGIN_मायाम् प्रविष्टो मायावी यदि त्वम् रावणः स्वयम् || ५-३४-१४उत्पादयसि मे भूयः सम्तापम् तन् 
न शोभनम् |_END
BEGIN_"If you are Ravana, who made use of an illusive guise and yourself a conjurer, you are causing 
me a further agony. It is no good."_END

B_5_C_35_5
BEGIN_जानन्ती बत दिष्ट्या माम् वैदेहि परिपृच्छसि |भर्तुः कमल पत्र अक्षि सम्ख्यानम् लक्ष्मणस्य 
च || ५-३५-६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha having eyes resembling lotus leaves! By my fortune, you are enquiring about the appearance 
of Rama your husband and Lakshmana, eventhough you know about them. Alas! what a pleasure!"_END

B_5_C_30_36
BEGIN_भूताः च अर्था विनश्यन्ति देश काल विरोधिताः || ५-३०-३७विक्लवम् दूतम् आसाद्य तमः सूर्य उदये 
यथा |_END
BEGIN_"Actions which are going to be accomplished shortly, get spoiled at the hands of a accomplished 
shortly, get spoiled at the hands of a confused messenger, when the actions are set in opposition to time and 
space, even as darkness disappears at sun rise."_END

B_5_C_33_20
BEGIN_स राजा सत्य वाग् देव्या वर दानम् अनुस्मरन् || ५-३३-२२मुमोह वचनम् श्रुत्वा कैकेय्याः क्रूरम् 
अप्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the cruel and the disagreeable words of Kaikeyi and recollecting the boon given to the 
queen, King Dasaratha who was true to his word, fell unconscious._END

B_5_C_34_14
BEGIN_स्वम् परित्यज्य रूपम् यः परिव्राजक रूपधृत् || ५-३४-१५जन स्थाने मया दृष्टः त्वम् स एव असि 
रावणः |_END
BEGIN_'You are indeed the same Ravana, who, abandoning your real form, appeared to me in the guise of 
a vagrant religious mendicant in Janasthana."_END

B_5_C_35_6
BEGIN_यानि रामस्य चिह्नानि लक्ष्मणस्य च यानि वै |लक्षितानि विशाल अक्षि वदतः शृणु तानि मे || 
५-३५-७_END
BEGIN_"O the large eyed Seetha! I tell the characteristics of Rama and Lakshmana as I recognized them; 
hear them from me."_END

B_5_C_30_37
BEGIN_अर्थ अनर्थ अन्तरे बुद्धिः निश्चिता अपि न शोभते || ५-३०-३८घातयन्ति हि कार्याणि दूताः पण्डित 
मानिनः |_END
BEGIN_"Even if a decision is taken, regarding what is worthy and what is worthless, it does not yield 
good results. Messengers boasting themselves to be learned, thus indeed ruin those actions."_END

B_5_C_33_21
BEGIN_ततः तु स्थविरो राजा सत्य धर्मे व्यवस्थितः || ५-३३-२३ज्येष्ठम् यशस्विनम् पुत्रम् रुदन् 
राज्यम् अयाचत |_END
BEGIN_"Then, the aged king, who was firmly established in truth and righteousness, regretfully asked 
his illustrious eldest son to give back the kingdom, which he bestowed him earlier."_END

B_5_C_36_0
BEGIN_भूय एव महातेजा हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
अब्रवीत् प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् सीता प्रत्यय कारणात् || ५-३६-१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the highly energetic son of wind-god, with an inducement to obtain confidence 
from Seetha, again modestly spoke the following words:_END

B_5_C_34_15
BEGIN_उपवास कृशाम् दीनाम् काम रूप निशा चर || ५-३४-१६सम्तापयसि माम् भूयः सम्तापम् तन् न शोभनम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"O demon who can assume any form at your will! It is no good that again you are causing agony to 
me, emaciated because of fasting and feeling very miserable."_END

B_5_C_35_7
BEGIN_रामः कमल पत्र अक्षः सर्व भूत मनो हरः |रूप दाक्षिण्य सम्पन्नः प्रसूतो जनक आत्मजे || ५-३५-८_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the daughter of Janaka! Rama has his eyes resembling the petals of a lotus. He has a 
handsomeness, attracting the hearts of all living beings. He is endowed with grace and dexterity, by birth."_END

B_5_C_33_22
BEGIN_स पितुः वचनम् श्रीमान् अभिषेकात् परम् प्रियम् || ५-३३-२४मनसा पूर्वम् आसाद्य वाचा प्रतिगृहीतवान् 
|_END
BEGIN_"That glorious Rama first admitted his father's words in mind, considering them more dearer than 
his anointment to the kingdom and accepted them with his word."_END

B_5_C_30_38
BEGIN_न विनश्येत् कथम् कार्यम् वैक्लव्यम् न कथम् भवेत् || ५-३०-३९लन्घनम् च समुद्रस्य कथम् नु 
न वृथा भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"How does not my work get spoiled? How should I avoid my feebleness? Also how does not my leaping 
across the sea become vain?"_END

B_5_C_36_1
BEGIN_वानरो अहम् महाभागे दूतो रामस्य धीमतः |
राम नाम अन्कितम् च इदम् पश्य देवि अन्गुलीयकम् || ५-३६-२_END
BEGIN_"O illustrious lady! I am a monkey and a messenger of the wise Rama. O princess! Look 
at this ring too, marked with Rama's name."_END

B_5_C_34_16
BEGIN_अथवा नैतदेवं हि यन्मया परिशङ्कितम् || ५-३४-१७मनसो हि मम प्रीतिरुत्पन्ना तव दर्शनात् |_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise, whatever is suspected by me is not indeed true because in my mind, a pleasurable sensation 
indeed occurred by reason of your audience."_END

B_5_C_35_8
BEGIN_तेजसा आदित्य सम्काशः क्षमया पृथिवी समः |बृहस्पति समो बुद्ध्या यशसा वासव उपमः || ५-३५-९_END
BEGIN_"He is equal to the sun in splendour, earth in endurance, Brihaspati in intelligence and Indra 
in fame."_END

B_5_C_33_23
BEGIN_दद्यान् न प्रतिगृह्णीयान् न ब्रूयत् किंचित् अप्रियम् || ५-३३-२५अपि जीवित हेतोः हि रामः 
सत्य पराक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_"The truly courageous Rama always gives anything to others and does not take anything from others. 
He does not speak just a little of a disagreeable word even for the cause of his life."_END

B_5_C_30_39
BEGIN_कथम् नु खलु वाक्यम् मे शृणुयान् न उद्विजेत च || ५-३०-४०इति संचिन्त्य हनुमान् चकार मतिमान् 
मतिम् |_END
BEGIN_"How can Seetha hear my words without fear?" Thinking in this way, the wise Hanuma made up his 
mind (as follows):_END

B_5_C_36_2
BEGIN_प्रत्ययार्थम् तवानीतम् तेन दत्तम् महात्मना |
समाश्वसिहि भद्रम् ते क्षीण दुह्ख फला हि असि || ५-३६-३_END
BEGIN_"I brought this ring given by the high souled Rama, for the purpose of gaining your confidence. 
Get consoled indeed. Happiness to you! You are now free from the object of your grief."_END

B_5_C_34_17
BEGIN_यदि रामस्य दूतः त्वम् आगतो भद्रम् अस्तु ते || ५-३४-१८पृच्छामि त्वाम् हरि श्रेष्ठ प्रिया 
राम कथा हि मे |_END
BEGIN_"If you have come as Rama's messenger, may you be blessed! O the best of monkeys! Rama's anecdote 
is very pleasurable for me. Hence, I am requesting you to narrate it."_END

B_5_C_35_9
BEGIN_रक्षिता जीव लोकस्य स्व जनस्य च रक्षिता |रक्षिता स्वस्य वृत्तस्य धर्मस्य च परम् तपः || 
५-३५-१०_END
BEGIN_"Rama the tormentator of his adversaries, is a protector of the world of beings, further protecting 
his own people. He is the protector of his own behaviour and righteousness._END

B_5_C_33_24
BEGIN_स विहाय उत्तरीयाणि महाअर्हाणि महायशाः || ५-३३-२६विसृज्य मनसा राज्यम् जनन्यै माम् समादिशत् 
|_END
BEGIN_"Leaving behind his greatly valuable outer garments and wearing garments made of bark, that highly 
illustrious Rama gave up his kingdom willingly and assigned me to his mother."_END

B_5_C_30_40
BEGIN_रामम् अक्लिष्ट कर्माणम् स्व बन्धुम् अनुकीर्तयन् || ५-३०-४१न एनाम् उद्वेजयिष्यामि तत् बन्धु 
गत मानसाम् |_END
BEGIN_"If I eulogize Rama, who is unwearied in action and a good relation, I shall not frighten her, 
whose mind is directed towards that relation."_END

B_5_C_36_3
BEGIN_गृहीत्वा प्रेक्षमाणा सा भर्तुः कर विभूषणम् |
भर्तारम् इव सम्प्राप्ता जानकी मुदिता अभवत् || ५-३६-४_END
BEGIN_"I brought this ring given by the high souled Rama, for the purpose of gaining your confidence. 
Get consoled indeed. Happiness to you! You are now free from the object of your grief."_END

B_5_C_34_18
BEGIN_गुणान् रामस्य कथय प्रियस्य मम वानर || ५-३४-१९चित्तम् हरसि मे सौम्य नदी कूलम् यथा रयः |_END
BEGIN_"O monkey! Narrate the qualities of my beloved Rama. O gentle one! You are eroding my mind as a 
rapid course of stream erodes a river bank."_END

B_5_C_35_10
BEGIN_रामो भामिनि लोकस्य चातुर्वर्ण्यस्य रक्षिता |मर्यादानाम् च लोकस्य कर्ता कारयिता च सः || 
५-३५-११_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Rama is the protector of the four castes of the world. He is the doer and also the agent 
for the people's propriety of conduct."_END

B_5_C_33_25
BEGIN_सा अहम् तस्य अग्रतः तूर्णम् प्रस्थिता वन चारिणी || ५-३३-२७न हि मे तेन हीनाया वासः स्वर्गे 
अपि रोचते |_END
BEGIN_"To me bereft of him, residing even in heaven does not indeed give pleasure. I, as such, decided 
to proceed to the forest and soon was ready to start even ahead of Rama."_END

B_5_C_30_41
BEGIN_इक्ष्वाकूणाम् वरिष्ठस्य रामस्य विदित आत्मनः || ५-३०-४२शुभानि धर्म युक्तानि वचनानि समर्पयन् 
|श्रावयिष्यामि सर्वाणि मधुराम् प्रब्रुवन् गिरम् || ५-३०-४३श्रद्धास्यति यथा हि इयम् तथा सर्वम् समादधे |_END
BEGIN_"Offering auspicious and righteous words about Rama the most excellent prince Ikshvaku dynasty 
who possesses a learned soul and myself speaking in a sweet voice, I shall make everything intelligible so that 
Seetha rightly believes everything."_END

B_5_C_36_4
BEGIN_चारु तत् वदनम् तस्याः ताम्र शुक्ल आयत ईक्षणम् |
अशोभत विशालाक्ष्या राहु मुक्त इव उडु राट् || ५-३६-५
ततः सा ह्रीमती बाला भर्तुः संदेश हर्षिता |
परितुट्षा प्रियम् श्रुत्वा प्राशंसत महाकपिम् || ५-३६-६_END
BEGIN_The countenance of that large-eyed Seetha, which appeared charming with red and white 
eyes shone like a moon the king of stars liberated by Rahu the demon. Then, that young Seetha, gladdened 
by the message of her husband, became shy and message of her husband, became shy and well-pleased. Uttering 
delightful words, she praised Hanuma the great monkey (as follows):_END

B_5_C_34_19
BEGIN_अहो स्वप्नस्य सुखता या अहम् एवम् चिर आहृता || ५-३४-२०प्रेषितम् नाम पश्यामि राघवेण वन ओकसम् 
|_END
BEGIN_"I, who was taken away long ago, is seeing a monkey sent by Rama in this way. Alas! How delightful 
this dream is!'_END

B_5_C_35_11
BEGIN_अर्चिष्मान् अर्चितो अत्यर्थम् ब्रह्म चर्य व्रते स्थितः |साधूनाम् उपकारज्ञः प्रचारज्ञः 
च कर्मणाम् || ५-३५-१२_END
BEGIN_"Rama is a resplendent man. He is respected exceedingly. He is established in a vow of chastity. 
He knows how to do good to virtuous people. He knows the application and advantage of his actions."_END

B_5_C_33_26
BEGIN_प्राग् एव तु महाभागः सौमित्रिः मित्र नन्दनः || ५-३३-२८पूर्वजस्य अनुयात्रा अर्थे द्रुम 
चीरैः अलम्कृतः |_END
BEGIN_"Adorned with clothes of bark, the illustrious Lakshmana, the rejoice of his friends, got ready 
to follow his elder brother even before (me)."_END

B_5_C_30_42
BEGIN_इति स बहु विधम् महाअनुभावो |जगति पतेः प्रमदाम् अवेक्षमाणः |मधुरम् अवितथम् जगाद वाक्यम् 
|द्रुम विटप अन्तरम् आस्थितो || ५-३०-४४_END
BEGIN_The noble-minded Hanuman, abiding in the midst of the twigs of the trees and seeing Seetha, spoke 
the following words of many kinds which were not futile._END

B_5_C_36_5
BEGIN_विक्रान्तः त्वम् समर्थः त्वम् प्राज्ञः त्वम् वानर उत्तम |
येन इदम् राक्षस पदम् त्वया एकेन प्रधर्षितम् || ५-३६-७_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the best of monkeys! You have singly overpowered this place infested by demons. 
You are valiant. You are competent. You are intelligent."_END

B_5_C_34_20
BEGIN_स्वप्नेऽपि यद्यहम् वीरं राघवम् सहलक्ष्मणम् || ५-३४-२१पश्येयम् नावसीदेयम् स्वप्नोऽपि मम 
मत्सरी |_END
BEGIN_"If I have seen the eminent Rama together with Lakshmana, I would not have disheartened. In my 
case, even my dream is wicked!"_END

B_5_C_35_12
BEGIN_राज विद्या विनीतः च ब्राह्मणानाम् उपासिता |श्रुतवान् शील सम्पन्नो विनीतः च परम् तपः || 
५-३५-१३_END
BEGIN_"He is well trained in statesmanship. He honours brahmins, the priestly class. He possesses sacred 
knowledge. He is endowed with good conduct. He is a modest man. He torments his adversaries."_END

B_5_C_33_27
BEGIN_ते वयम् भर्तुः आदेशम् बहु मान्य दृढ व्रताः || ५-३३-२९प्रविष्टाः स्म पुरात् दृष्टम् वनम् 
गम्भीर दर्शनम् |_END
BEGIN_"Obeying respectfully the command of Lord Dasaratha, we as such with a firm resolution, entered 
the forest, which we have never seen before and which was deep and profound in appearance."_END

B_5_C_36_6
BEGIN_शत योजन विस्तीर्णः सागरो मकर आलयः |
विक्रम श्लाघनीयेन क्रमता गोष्पदी कृतः || ५-३६-८_END
BEGIN_"You, with an acclaimable gallantry, crossed the ocean having a width of one hundred 
Yojanas and an asylum of crocodiles, making it as a small puddle."_END

B_5_C_34_21
BEGIN_न अहम् स्वप्नम् इमम् मन्ये स्वप्ने दृष्ट्वा हि वानरम् || ५-३४-२२न शक्यो अभ्युदयः प्राप्तुम् 
प्राप्तः च अभ्युदयो मम |_END
BEGIN_"I do not deem it as a dream. Seeing a monkey in a dream does not bring about prosperity But prosperity 
has come to me!"_END

B_5_C_37_0
BEGIN_सा सीता तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ आनना |
हनूमन्तम् उवाच इदम् धर्म अर्थ सहितम् वचः || ५-३७-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing Hanuma's words, Seetha whose face resembled the full moon, spoke the following 
words braced with justice and utility, to Hanuma._END

B_5_C_35_13
BEGIN_यजुः वेद विनीतः च वेदविद्भिः सुपूजितः |धनुः वेदे च वेदे च वेद अन्गेषु च निष्ठितः || ५-३५-१४_END
BEGIN_"He got trained in Yajurveda, the sacrificial Veda. He is highly honoured by those well-versed 
in Vedas. He is skilled in Dhanurveda, the science of archery, other Vedas and the six limbs* of Vedangas."_END

B_5_C_33_28
BEGIN_वसतो दण्डक अरण्ये तस्य अहम् अमित ओजसः || ५-३३-३०रक्षसा अपहृता भार्या रावणेन दुरात्मना 
|_END
BEGIN_While Rama of great vigour was dwelling in the forest of Dandaka, the evil-minded demon, Ravana 
took me, Rama's wife, away."_END

B_5_C_36_7
BEGIN_न हि त्वाम् प्राकृतम् मन्ये वनरम् वनर ऋषभ |
यस्य ते न अस्ति सम्त्रासो रावणान् न अपि सम्भ्रमः || ५-३६-९_END
BEGIN_"O excellent of monkeys! For you there is no fear nor even bewilderment from Ravana. 
Hence, I do not consider you as an ordinary monkey."_END

B_5_C_34_22
BEGIN_किम् नु स्याच् चित्त मोहो अयम् भवेत् वात गतिः तु इयम् || ५-३४-२३उन्मादजो विकारो वा स्यात् 
इयम् मृग तृष्णिका |_END
BEGIN_"How possibly is it a delusion of my mind? Is it an impending course of flatulence or changing 
mental condition of madness? Is it a looming mirage?"_END

B_5_C_37_1
BEGIN_अमृतम् विष संसृष्टम् त्वया वानर भाषितम् |
यच् च न अन्य मना रामो यच् च शोक परायणः || ५-३७-२_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! The words spoken by you viz. that Rama is not having any other thoughts (than 
on me) and is fully overwhelmed by sorrow are like ambrosia mixed with poisons."_END

B_5_C_35_14
BEGIN_विपुल अंसो महाबाहुः कम्बु ग्रीवः शुभ आननः |गूढ जत्रुः सुताम्र अक्षो रामो देवि जनैः श्रुतः 
|| ५-३५-१५_END
BEGIN_"O princess! Rama is a broad shouldered and a long-armed man. He has a shell-like neck. He has 
a handsome countenance. He has a hidden collar-bone. He has beautiful red eyes. His fame is heard about by people."_END

B_5_C_33_29
BEGIN_द्वौ मासौ तेन मे कालो जीवित अनुग्रहः कृतः || ५-३३-३१ऊर्ध्वम् द्वाभ्याम् तु मासाभ्याम् 
ततः त्यक्ष्यामि जीवितम् |_END
BEGIN_"A period of two months of survival-benefit has been given to me by him. For that reason, after 
the said two months, I shall give up my life."_END

B_5_C_36_8
BEGIN_अर्हसे च कपि श्रेष्ठ मया समभिभाषितुम् |
यदि असि प्रेषितः तेन रामेण विदित आत्मना || ५-३६-१०_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! If you are sent by that Rama, who knows the nature of his self, 
you are worthy of talking to me well."_END

B_5_C_34_23
BEGIN_अथवा न अयम् उन्मादो मोहो अपि उन्माद लक्ष्मणः || ५-३४-२४सम्बुध्ये च अहम् आत्मानम् इमम् 
च अपि वन ओकसम् |_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise, it is neither madness nor even a delusion, which is a symptom of madness. Because I 
am knowing about myself as also about this monkey."_END

B_5_C_37_2
BEGIN_ऐश्वर्ये वा सुविस्तीर्णे व्यसने वा सुदारुणे |
रज्ज्वा इव पुरुषम् बद्ध्वा कृत अन्तः परिकर्षति || ५-३७-३_END
BEGIN_"Destiny drags out a man into a very extensive fortune or into a very dreadful adversity, 
as if being dragged, tied with ropes."_END

B_5_C_35_15
BEGIN_दुन्दुभि स्वन निर्घोषः स्निग्ध वर्णः प्रतापवान् |समः सम विभक्त अन्गो वर्णम् श्यामम् समाश्रितः 
|| ५-३५-१६_END
BEGIN_"He has a voice like the sound of a kettle-drum. He has a shining skin. He is full of splendour. 
He is square-built. His limbs are built symmetrically. He is endowed with a dark-brown complexion."_END

B_5_C_36_9
BEGIN_प्रेषयिष्यति दुर्धर्षो रामो न हि अपरीक्षितम् |
पराक्रमम् अविज्ञाय मत् सकाशम् विशेषतः || ५-३६-११_END
BEGIN_"The indomitable Rama must not have sent you indeed, especially to me, without knowing 
your enterprise and without testing you in advance."_END

B_5_C_34_24
BEGIN_इति एवम् बहुधा सीता सम्प्रधार्य बल अबलम् || ५-३४-२५रक्षसाम् काम रूपत्वान् मेने तम् राक्षस 
अधिपम् |_END
BEGIN_Thus deliberating upon the strengths and weaknesses in several ways, Seetha finally imagined him 
to be Ravana, as demons can change their forms at will._END

B_5_C_37_3
BEGIN_विधिः नूनम् असम्हार्यः प्राणिनाम् प्लवग उत्तम |
सौमित्रिम् माम् च रामम् च व्यसनैः पश्य मोहितान् || ५-३७-४_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the best of monkeys! For living beings, destiny is surely irresistible. See 
how Lakshmana, myself and Rama are baffled by misfortunes."_END

B_5_C_35_16
BEGIN_त्रिस्थिरः त्रिप्रलम्बः च त्रिसमः त्रिषु च उन्नतः |त्रिवलीवान् त्र्यवनतः चतुः व्यन्गः 
त्रिशीर्षवान् || ५-३५-१७_END
BEGIN_"He is ever firm in three limbs (viz. the breast, waist and fist), long in three (viz. the breast, 
waist and fist), long in three (viz. the eyebrows, arms and soles), uniform in three (viz. his locks, testical 
and knees, elevated in three (viz. his breast, rim of his navel and lower abdomen), coppery in three of the navel 
and the lower abdomen), coppery in three (viz. the rims of his eyes, nails, palms and soles), soft in three (viz. 
the lines on his soles, hair and the end of the membrane virile) and always deep in three (viz. the voice, gait 
and the navel)."_END

B_5_C_36_10
BEGIN_दिष्ट्या च कुशली रामो धर्म आत्मा धर्म वत्सलः |
लक्ष्मणः च महातेजाः सुमित्र आनन्द वर्धनः || ५-३६-१२_END
BEGIN_"Rama the righteous man who is true to his promise and Lakshmana of great splendour who 
enriches the joy of Sumitra are fortunately safe."_END

B_5_C_34_25
BEGIN_एताम् बुद्धिम् तदा कृत्वा सीता सा तनु मध्यमा || ५-३४-२६न प्रतिव्याजहार अथ वानरम् जनक आत्मजा 
|_END
BEGIN_Then, that slender waisted Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, thus having made up her mind, did not 
reply in return anything further to Hanuman._END

B_5_C_37_4
BEGIN_शोकस्य अस्य कदा पारम् राघवो अधिगमिष्यति |
प्लवमानः परिश्रान्तो हत नौः सागरे यथा || ५-३७-५_END
BEGIN_"When will Rama reach the end of this grief any more than a thoroughly fatigued man, 
having suffered a ship wreck is swimming in the middle of the sea?"_END

B_5_C_35_17
BEGIN_त्रिवलीवांस्त्र्यवनतश्चतुर्व्यङ्गस्त्रिशीर्षवान् |चतुष्कलश्चतुर्लेखश्चतुष्किष्कुश्चतुःसमः 
|| ५-३५-१८_END
BEGIN_"He has three folds in the skin of his neck and belly. He is depressed at three places (viz. the 
middle of his soles, the lines on his soles and the nipples). He is undersized at four places (viz. the neck, 
membran virile, the back and the shanks). He is endowed with three spirals in the hair of his head. He has four 
lines at the root of his thumb (denoting his proficiency in the four Vedas). He has four lines on his forehead 
(indicating longevity). He is four cubits high (96 inches). He has four pairs of limbs (viz. the cheeks, arms, 
shanks and knees) equally matched."_END

B_5_C_36_11
BEGIN_कुशली यदि काकुत्स्थः किम् नु सागर मेखलाम् |
महीम् दहति कोपेन युग अन्त अग्निः इव उत्थितः || ५-३६-१३_END
BEGIN_"If Rama is safe, with his anger why is he not scorching the earth with ocean as its 
belt, like rising fire at the end of the world?"_END

B_5_C_34_26
BEGIN_सीतायाः चिन्तितम् बुद्ध्वा हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-३४-२७श्रोत्र अनुकूलैः वचनैः तदा ताम् 
सम्प्रहर्षयत् |_END
BEGIN_Understanding the contemplation of Seetha, Hanuma the son of wind-god then brought about a great 
joy in her with his words most favourable to her ears (as follows):_END

B_5_C_37_5
BEGIN_राक्षसानाम् क्षयम् कृत्वा सूदयित्वा च रावणम् |
लन्काम् उन्मूलिताम् कृत्वा कदा द्रक्ष्यति माम् पतिः || ५-३७-६_END
BEGIN_"When will my husband see me, after annihilation of the demons, killing of Ravana and 
making the City of Lanka debacled?."_END

B_5_C_35_18
BEGIN_चतुष् कलः चतुः लेखः चतुष् किष्कुः चतुः समः |चतुर्दश सम द्वन्द्वः चतुः दष्टः चतुः गतिः 
|| ५-३५-१९_END
BEGIN_"He has fourteen other pairs of limbs (viz. the eye brows, nostrils, eyes, ears, lips, nipples, 
elbows, wrists, knees testicles, lions, hands, feet and thighs) equally matched. The four large teeth at both 
the ends of his upper and lower jaws are very sharp. He walks in four gaits (resembling the walks of a lion, a 
tiger, an elephant and a bull). He is endowed with excellent lips, chin and nose. He has five glossy limbs (viz. 
the hair, eyes, teeth, skin and soles). He has eight long limbs (viz. the arms, fingers and toes, eyes and ears, 
thighs and shanks)._END

B_5_C_36_12
BEGIN_अथवा शक्तिमन्तौ तौ सुराणाम् अपि निग्रहे |
मम एव तु न दुह्खानाम् अस्ति मन्ये विपर्ययः || ५-३६-१४_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise, Rama and Lakshmana are capable of holding down even the celestials. But I 
think there is no end indeed to my troubles."_END

B_5_C_34_27
BEGIN_आदित्य इव तेजस्वी लोक कान्तः शशी यथा || ५-३४-२८राजा सर्वस्य लोकस्य देवो वैश्रवणो यथा |
विक्रमेण उपपन्नः च यथा विष्णुः महायशाः || ५-३४-२९_END
BEGIN_"Rama has a great splendour like that of the sun. He is pleasing to all like the moon. As Kubera 
the Lord of wealth, he is a lord to the entire world. Like Vishnu, he is greatly renowned and endowed with valour."_END

B_5_C_37_6
BEGIN_स वाच्यः सम्त्वरस्व इति यावत् एव न पूर्यते |
अयम् सम्वत्सरः कालः तावद्त् हि मम जीवितम् || ५-३७-७_END
BEGIN_"Till the current period of one year is not completed, that Rama is to be told to make 
haste to save me; since my life will be lasting till such time only."_END

B_5_C_35_19
BEGIN_दश पद्मो दश बृहत् त्रिभिः व्याप्तो द्वि शुक्लवान् |षड् उन्नतो नव तनुः त्रिभिः व्याप्नोति 
राघवः || ५-३५-२०_END
BEGIN_"Rama has ten lotus-like limbs (viz. the countenance, the mouth, the eyes, the tongue, lips, palate, 
breasts, nails, the hands and the feet). He has ten ample limbs (viz. the chest, the head, the forehead, the neck, 
the arms, the heart, the mouth the feet, the back and the ears). He is spread through by reason of three (viz. 
splendour, renown and glory). He is doubly pure (on father's and mother's side). He is elevated in six limbs (viz. 
the flanks, the abdomen, the breast, the nose, the shoulders and the forehead). He is small, thin, fine or sharp 
in nine (viz. the hair, the moustaches and the beard, nails the hair on the body, the skin, the finger-joints, 
the membrum virile, acumen and perception). He pursues religious merit, worldly riches and the sensuous delight 
in three periods (viz. the forenoon, midday and afternoon)._END

B_5_C_36_13
BEGIN_कच्चिच् च व्यथते रामः कच्चिन् न परिपत्यते |
उत्तराणि च कार्याणि कुरुते पुरुष उत्तमः || ५-३६-१५_END
BEGIN_"Is not Rama getting perturbed? Is he not tormented with grief? Is Rama the best of men 
now doing the right acts to annihilate the enemies?"_END

B_5_C_34_28
BEGIN_सत्य वादी मधुर वाग् देवो वाचस्पतिः यथा |रूपवान् सुभगः श्रीमान् कन्दर्प इव मूर्तिमान् || 
५-३४-३०_END
BEGIN_"Rama is a speaker of truth. Like Lord Brihaspati, he has a sweet voice. He is a handsome man, 
possessing good fortune and a royal dignity. He is a personified Manmadha, the lord of love."_END

B_5_C_37_7
BEGIN_वर्तते दशमो मासो द्वौ तु शेषौ प्लवम्गम |
रावणेन नृशंसेन समयो यः कृतो मम || ५-३७-८_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Out of the time-limit given to me by the cruel Ravana for my survival, the 
tenth month is now running. Only two months are left out."_END

B_5_C_35_20
BEGIN_सत्य धर्म परः श्रीमान् सम्ग्रह अनुग्रहे रतः |देश काल विभागज्ञः सर्व लोक प्रियम् वदः || 
५-३५-२१_END
BEGIN_"Rama is engrossed in truth and righteousness. He is a prosperous man. He is interested in reception 
and facilitation. He knows how to apportion place and time. He speaks affectionately with all."_END

B_5_C_36_14
BEGIN_कच्चिन् न दीनः सम्भ्रान्तः कार्येषु च न मुह्यति |
कच्चिन् पुरुष कार्याणि कुरुते नृपतेः सुतः || ५-३६-१६_END
BEGIN_"Is Rama the prince miserable and confused? Is he even mistaken in his actions? I hope 
he is doing all acts which require human effort."_END

B_5_C_34_29
BEGIN_स्थान क्रोध प्रहर्ता च श्रेष्ठो लोके महारथः |बाहुच् चायाम् अवष्टब्धो यस्य लोको महात्मनः 
|| ५-३४-३१_END
BEGIN_"Rama gets anger only at right time. He strikes a befitting person at a right time. He is an excellent 
chariot-warrior. The world is resting under the shelter of arms of this high souled man."_END

B_5_C_37_8
BEGIN_विभीषणेन च भ्रात्रा मम निर्यातनम् प्रति |
अनुनीतः प्रयत्नेन न च तत् कुरुते मतिम् || ५-३७-९_END
BEGIN_"Even when humbly entreated with continued exertion by Vibhishana his brother about my 
restoration (to Rama), Ravana is not making up his mind to do so."_END

B_5_C_35_21
BEGIN_भ्राता च तस्य द्वैमात्रः सौमित्रिः अपराजितः |अनुरागेन रूपेण गुणैः चैव तथा विधः || ५-३५-२२_END
BEGIN_"The invincible Lakshmana, the son of Rama's step-mother and Rama's brother, is resembling Rama 
in appearance, affection and in qualities."_END

B_5_C_38_0
BEGIN_ततः स कपि शार्दूलः तेन वाक्येन हर्षितः |
सीताम् उवाच तत् श्रुत्वा वाक्यम् वाक्य विशारदः || ५-३८-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Seetha, the eloquent Hanuma was very much pleased and spoke to 
Seetha (as follows):_END

B_5_C_36_15
BEGIN_द्विविधम् त्रिविध उपायम् उपायम् अपि सेवते |
विजिगीषुः सुहृत् कच्चिन् मित्रेषु च परम् तपः || ५-३६-१७_END
BEGIN_"Is Rama the annihilator of enemies as per necessity resorting to the two strategies 
viz., conciliatory and partaking approaches and even the three strategies viz., partaking, sowing dissension 
and open assault? Is he kind-hearted towards friends, with a wish to conquer the enemies?"_END

B_5_C_37_9
BEGIN_मम प्रतिप्रदानम् हि रावणस्य न रोचते |
रावणम् मार्गते सम्ख्ये मृत्युः काल वशम् गतम् || ५-३७-१०_END
BEGIN_"My restoration is not agreeable to Ravana. In the battle, death lies in wait for Ravana, 
who has become subject to the power of Time."_END

B_5_C_34_30
BEGIN_अपकृश्ष्य आश्रम पदान् मृग रूपेण राघवम् |शून्ये येन अपनीता असि तस्य द्रक्ष्यसि यत् फलम् 
|| ५-३४-३२_END
BEGIN_"Showing an illusory antelope, Ravana detracted Rama and took you away from a deserted hermitage. 
You will see later, the consequence Ravana will get for this act."_END

B_5_C_38_1
BEGIN_युक्त रूपम् त्वया देवि भाषितम् शुभ दर्शने |
सदृशम् स्त्री स्वभावस्य साध्वीनाम् विनयस्य च || ५-३८-२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha, the beautiful princess! Whatever you spoke is befitting. It is in keeping 
with woman's nature and humility of a chaste women."_END

B_5_C_35_22
BEGIN_तावुभौ नरशार्डूलौ त्वद्दर्शनसमुत्सुकौ |विचिन्वनौ महीम् कृत्स्नामस्माभिरभिसम्गातौ || ५-३५-२३_END
BEGIN_"Rama and Lakshmana, the two tigers among men, very anxiously desirous of seeing you and searching 
all over the earth, came in contact with us."_END

B_5_C_36_16
BEGIN_कच्चिन् मित्राणि लभते मित्रैः च अपि अभिगम्यते |
कच्चित् कल्याण मित्रः च मित्रैः च अपि पुरः कृतः || ५-३६-१८_END
BEGIN_"Is he getting friends? Has he been approached for friendship by others? I hope he is 
having good friends and even so honoured by them."_END

B_5_C_37_10
BEGIN_ज्येष्ठा कन्या अनला नम विभीषण सुता कपे |
तया मम एतत् आख्यातम् मात्रा प्रहितया स्वयम् || ५-३७-११_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Nala, the eldest maiden daughter of Vibhishana, when she was sent personally 
to me by her mother, told me about this."_END

B_5_C_34_31
BEGIN_नचिरात् रावणम् सम्ख्ये यो वधिष्यति वीर्यवान् |रोष प्रमुक्तैः इषुभिः ज्वलद्भिः इव पावकैः 
|| ५-३४-३३तेन अहम् प्रेषितो दूतः त्वत् सकाशम् इह आगतः |त्वत् वियोगेन दुह्ख आर्तः स त्वाम् कौशलम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ५-३४-३४_END
BEGIN_"Which valiant Rama with arrows strongly shining like sparkles released with anger, by the same 
Rama I was sent here as a messenger and I arrived at your presence. That Rama, agonised by your separation wishes 
to enquire of your welfare."_END

B_5_C_38_2
BEGIN_स्त्रीत्वम् न तु समर्थम् हि सागरम् व्यतिवर्तितुम् |
माम् अधिष्ठाय विस्तीर्णम् शत योजनम् आयतम् || ५-३८-३_END
BEGIN_"It is indeed not fit for a woman to mount on my back and traverse an extensive ocean, 
which is having a width of one hundred yojanas."_END

B_5_C_35_23
BEGIN_त्वाम् एव मार्गमाणो तौ विचरन्तौ वसुम् धराम् |ददर्शतुः मृग पतिम् पूर्वजेन अवरोपितम् || 
५-३५-२४ऋश्यमूकस्य पृष्ठे तु बहु पादप सम्कुले |भ्रातुः भार्य आर्तम् आसीनम् सुग्रीवम् प्रिय दर्शनम् || ५-३५-२५_END
BEGIN_"Those two brothers Rama and Lakshmana, wandering only in search of you all over the earth, saw 
Sugreeva the Lord of monkeys, sitting on the top of Rishyamuka mountain, filled with several trees, having been 
dethroned by his elder brother, oppressed with fear, but who was pleasant to the sight."_END

B_5_C_36_17
BEGIN_कच्चित् आशास्ति देवानाम् प्रसादम् पार्थिव आत्मजः |
कच्चित् पुरुष कारम् च दैवम् च प्रतिपद्यते || ५-३६-१९_END
BEGIN_"Is Rama the prince wishing the grace of the gods? Is he equally aware of the role of 
human endeavour and the role of fate?"_END

B_5_C_34_32
BEGIN_लक्ष्मणः च महातेजाः सुमित्र आनन्द वर्धनः |अभिवाद्य महाबाहुः सो अपि कौशलम् अब्रवीत् || 
५-३४-३५_END
BEGIN_"That long-armed Lakshmana too, having a great splendour and who augments the happiness of Sumitra 
his mother, saluted you and enquired about your welfare."_END

B_5_C_37_11
BEGIN_आशंस इति हरि श्रेष्ठ क्षिप्रम् माम् प्राप्स्यते पतिः |
अन्तः आत्मा हि मे शुद्धः तस्मिन् च बहवो गुणाः || ५-३७-१२_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the excellent of monkeys! Rama, my husband, will soon regain me without any 
doubt. Because my heart is pure and in Rama also, there are many good qualities existing."_END

B_5_C_38_3
BEGIN_द्वितीयम् कारणम् यच् च ब्रवीषि विनय अन्विते |
रामात् अन्यस्य न अर्हामि संस्पर्शम् इति जानकि || ५-३८-४
एतत् ते देवि सदृशम् पत्न्याः तस्य महात्मनः |
का हि अन्या त्वाम् ऋते देवि ब्रूयात् वचनम् ईदृशम् || ५-३८-५_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha endowed with modesty! The second reason you mentioned that you would not be 
touching any one else other then Rama is befitting of you, the wife of that high soled Rama. O princess! 
which other lady except you can speak of such sweet words?"_END

B_5_C_35_24
BEGIN_वयम् तु हरि राजम् तम् सुग्रीवम् सत्य सम्गरम् |परिचर्यामहे राज्यात् पूर्वजेन अवरोपितम् 
|| ५-३५-२६_END
BEGIN_"We for one are serving that Sugreeva, the Lord of monkeys, who was true to his promise, but was 
dethroned from the kingdom from his elder brother."_END

B_5_C_36_18
BEGIN_कच्चिन् न विगत स्नेहो विवासान् मयि राघवः |
कच्चिन् माम् व्यसनात् अस्मान् मोक्षयिष्यति वानरः || ५-३६-२०_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Is Rama not losing affection in me because of my staying away from home? Will 
he release me from this evil predicament?"_END

B_5_C_34_33
BEGIN_रामस्य च सखा देवि सुग्रीवो नाम वानरः |राजा वानर मुख्यानाम् स त्वाम् कौशलम् अब्रवीत् || 
५-३४-३६_END
BEGIN_"O princess! That monkey called Sugreeva, a companion of Rama and the king of the excellent monkeys, 
asked about your welfare."_END

B_5_C_37_12
BEGIN_उत्साहः पौरुषम् सत्त्वम् आनृशंस्यम् कृतज्ञता |
विक्रमः च प्रभावः च सन्ति वानर राघवे || ५-३७-१३_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! In Rama are figured, pesseverence, manliness, courage, non-mischievousness, 
gratitude, prowess and energy."_END

B_5_C_38_4
BEGIN_श्रोष्यते चैव काकुत्स्थः सर्वम् निरवशेषतः |
चेष्टितम् यत् त्वया देवि भाषितम् मम च अग्रतः || ५-३८-६_END
BEGIN_"O princess! I can completely inform Rama of all that you have done and of all that you 
have spoken before me."_END

B_5_C_35_25
BEGIN_ततः तौ चीर वसनौ धनुः प्रवर पाणिनौ |ऋश्यमूकस्य शैलस्य रम्यम् देशम् उपागतौ || ५-३५-२७_END
BEGIN_"In the meanwhile, those two brothers Rama and Lakshmana, wearing clothes made of bark and arming 
the best bows, came to the charming place of Rishyamuka mountain."_END

B_5_C_36_19
BEGIN_सुखानाम् उचितो नित्यम् असुखानाम् अनूचितः |
दुह्खम् उत्तरम् आसाद्य कच्चित् रामो न सीदति || ५-३६-२१_END
BEGIN_"Is Rama, who is habituated always to pleasures and not habituated to pains, not sinking 
into despondency by now getting this great pain?"_END

B_5_C_37_13
BEGIN_चतुर्दश सहस्राणि राक्षसानाम् जघान यः |
