जन स्थाने विना भ्रात्रा शत्रुः कः तस्य न उद्विजेत् || ५-३७-१४_END
BEGIN_"Which Rama, who without the help of Lakshmana his brother, killed fourteen thousand 
demos in Janasthana (part of the forest), what adversary will not have fear of such a man?"_END

B_5_C_34_34
BEGIN_नित्यम् स्मरति रामः त्वाम् ससुग्रीवः सलक्ष्मणः |दिष्ट्या जीवसि वैदेहि राक्षसी वशम् आगता 
|| ५-३४-३७_END
BEGIN_"Rama, together with Sugreeva and Lakshmana, is always recollecting you. O Seetha! Eventhough coming 
into the control female-demons, you are somehow surviving by your good luck!"_END

B_5_C_38_5
BEGIN_कारणैः बहुभिः देवि राम प्रिय चिकीर्षया |
स्नेह प्रस्कन्न मनसा मया एतत् समुदीरितम् || ५-३८-७_END
BEGIN_"O princess! All this was told by me because of several reasons, being desirous of doing 
good to Rama ad with my mind moistened with affection towards him."_END

B_5_C_35_26
BEGIN_स तौ दृष्ट्वा नर व्याघ्रौ धन्विनौ वानर ऋषभः |अभिप्लुतो गिरेः तस्य शिखरम् भय मोहितः || 
५-३५-२८_END
BEGIN_"Seeing Rama and Lakshmana, the excellent of men, coming with bows in hand, that Sugreeva the best 
of monkeys was deluded with fear and jumped over to the hill-top of that mountain."_END

B_5_C_36_20
BEGIN_कौसल्यायाः तथा कच्चित् सुमित्रायाः तथैव च |
अभीक्ष्णम् श्रूयते कच्चित् कुशलम् भरतस्य च || ५-३६-२२_END
BEGIN_"Are you constantly hearing the news of safety of Kausalya, Sumitra and Bharata?"_END

B_5_C_37_14
BEGIN_न स शक्यः तुलयितुम् व्यसनैः पुरुष ऋषभः |
अहम् तस्य अनुभावज्ञा शक्रस्य इव पुलोमजा || ५-३७-१५_END
BEGIN_"Rama, the excellent among men, is not compelled to be moved by troubles. I now well 
the energy of Rama, as Shachi the wife of Indra knows the energy of Indra the Lord of celestials."_END

B_5_C_38_6
BEGIN_लन्काया दुष्प्रवेशत्वात् दुस्तरत्वान् महाउदधेः |
सामर्थ्यात् आत्मनः चैव मया एतत् समुदाहृतम् || ५-३८-८_END
BEGIN_"I spoke this because of the unassailability of Lanka, its great ocean so difficult to 
be crossed and also my capacity of taking you."_END

B_5_C_34_35
BEGIN_नचिरात् द्रक्ष्यसे रामम् लक्ष्मणम् च महारथम् |मध्ये वानर कोटीनाम् सुग्रीवम् च अमित ओजसम् 
|| ५-३४-३८_END
BEGIN_"Within a few days, you will see Rama, the mighty Lakshmana and the highly splendorous Sugreeva, 
in the presence of crores of monkeys."_END

B_5_C_35_27
BEGIN_ततः स शिखरे तस्मिन् वानर इन्द्रो व्यवस्थितः |तयोः समीपम् माम् एव प्रेषयामास सत्वरः || 
५-३५-२९_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, stationed on that hill-top, that Sugreeva the lord of monkeys, very soon sent me only, 
to approach those two brothers."_END

B_5_C_36_21
BEGIN_मन् निमित्तेन मान अर्हः कच्चित् शोकेन राघवः |
कच्चिन् न अन्य मना रामः कच्चिन् माम् तारयिष्यति || ५-३६-२३_END
BEGIN_"Is Rama worthy of honour, suffering from pain just because of me? Will he liberate me 
from my sorrow, without fixing his mind on something else?"_END

B_5_C_37_15
BEGIN_शर जाल अंशुमान् शूरः कपे राम दिवा करः |
शत्रु रक्षोमयम् तोयम् उपशोषम् नयिष्यति || ५-३७-१६_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! The powerful Rama like the sun, with his multitude of ray-like arrows, will 
dry up the water in the form of hostile adversaries."_END

B_5_C_38_7
BEGIN_इच्छामि त्वाम् समानेतुम् अद्य एव रघु बन्धुना |
गुरु स्नेहेन भक्त्या च न अन्यथा तत् उदाहृतम् || ५-३८-९_END
BEGIN_"Because of my great affection and devotion towards you, I wish to carry you well now 
itself to Rama your hushand. These words were not spoken by me with any other motive."_END

B_5_C_34_36
BEGIN_अहम् सुग्रीव सचिवो हनूमान् नाम वानरः |प्रविष्टो नगरीम् लन्काम् लन्घयित्वा महाउदधिम् || 
५-३४-३९_END
BEGIN_"I am a monkey, the minister of Sugreeva, called Hanuma. I entered the city of Lanka, by traversing 
the great ocean."_END

B_5_C_35_28
BEGIN_ताव् अहम् पुरुष व्याघ्रौ सुग्रीव वचनात् प्रभू |रूप लक्षण सम्पन्नौ कृत अञ्जलिः उपस्थितः 
|| ५-३५-३०_END
BEGIN_"On that command of Sugreeva, I reached saluting those two brothers, Rama and Lakshmana the excellent 
and capable men, endowed with good form and characteristics."_END

B_5_C_36_22
BEGIN_कच्चित् अक्षाउहिणीम् भीमाम् भरतो भ्रातृ वत्सलः |
ध्वजिनीम् मन्त्रिभिः गुप्ताम् प्रेषयिष्यति मत् कृते || ५-३६-२४_END
BEGIN_"I hope Bharata, having a brotherly affection, will send for my sake, an army furnished 
with banners, guarded by the ministers, consisting of ten anikinis (21870 elephants, 21870 chariots, 
65610 horses and 109350 foot soldiers) which were terrific in appearance."_END

B_5_C_38_8
BEGIN_यदि न उत्सहसे यातुम् मया सार्धम् अनिन्दिते |
अभिज्ञानम् प्रयच्छ त्वम् जानीयात् राघवो हि यत् || ५-३८-१०_END
BEGIN_"O faultless Seetha! If you are not willing to go with me, give me a token of remembrance 
which Rama can recognise."_END

B_5_C_37_16
BEGIN_इति सम्जल्पमानाम् ताम् राम अर्थे शोक कर्शिताम् |
अश्रु सम्पूर्ण वदनाम् उवाच हनुमान् कपिः || ५-३७-१७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma spoke the following words to Seetha, who was thus talking with grief for Rama 
and with her eyes full of tears."_END

B_5_C_34_37
BEGIN_कृत्वा मूर्ध्नि पद न्यासम् रावणस्य दुरात्मनः |त्वाम् द्रष्टुम् उपयातो अहम् समाश्रित्य 
पराक्रमम् || ५-३४-४०_END
BEGIN_"Asserting my strength and putting down my feet on the head of the evil minded Ravana, I have come 
to see you."_END

B_5_C_35_29
BEGIN_तौ परिज्ञात तत्त्व अर्थौ मया प्रीति समन्वितौ |पृष्ठम् आरोप्य तम् देशम् प्रापितौ पुरुष 
ऋषभौ || ५-३५-३१_END
BEGIN_"Those two brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, the excellent among men, were fully endowed with kindness, 
after knowing the exact position about Sugreeva. Then, I made Rama and Lakshmana to ascend on my back and took 
them to Sugreeva's place."_END

B_5_C_39_0
BEGIN_मणिम् दत्त्वा ततः सीता हनूमन्तम् अथ अब्रवीत् |
अभिज्ञानम् अभिज्ञातम् एतत् रामस्य तत्त्वतः || ५-३९-१_END
BEGIN_Then, after giving the jewel for head, Seetha spoke to Hanuma as follows: "This token 
of remembrance is actually known to Rama."_END

B_5_C_36_23
BEGIN_वानर अधिपतिः श्रीमान् सुग्रीवः कच्चित् एष्यति |
मत् कृते हरिभिः वीरैः वृतो दन्त नख आयुधैः || ५-३६-२५_END
BEGIN_"The glorious Sugreeva the lord of monkeys will indeed come for my sake along with his 
valiant monkeys, who have their tusks and nails as their weapons."_END

B_5_C_38_9
BEGIN_एवम् उक्ता हनुमता सीता सुर सुत उपमा |
उवाच वचनम् मन्दम् बाष्प प्रग्रथित अक्षरम् || ५-३८-११
इदम् श्रेष्ठम् अभिज्ञानम् ब्रूयाः त्वम् तु मम प्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing Hanuma's words, Seetha like the daughter of a god, slowly spoke the following 
words, strung together with alphabets of tears: "You tell this (following) excellent thing as a token 
of remembrance to my beloved husband."_END

B_5_C_37_17
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा एव तु वचो मह्यम् क्षिप्रम् एष्यति राघवः |
चमूम् प्रकर्षन् महतीम् हरि ऋक्ष गण सम्कुलाम् || ५-३७-१८_END
BEGIN_"Soon after hearing my words, Rama will soon come, engaging a great army comprising of 
a multitude of monkeys and bears with him."_END

B_5_C_34_38
BEGIN_न अहम् अस्मि तथा देवि यथा माम् अवगच्छसि |विशन्का त्यज्यताम् एषा श्रद्धत्स्व वदतो मम || 
५-३४-४१_END
BEGIN_"O Princess! I am not so, as you comprehend me (as Ravana). Let your suspicion be given up. Believe 
me as I say it."_END

B_5_C_35_30
BEGIN_निवेदितौ च तत्त्वेन सुग्रीवाय महात्मने |तयोः अन्योन्य सम्भाषात् भृशम् प्रीतिः अजायत || 
५-३५-३२_END
BEGIN_"I informed the high-souled Sugreeva about the true position of Rama and Lakshmana. After a mutual 
conversation between those two brothers and Sugreeva, a great friendship developed among them."_END

B_5_C_39_1
BEGIN_मणिम् तु दृष्ट्वा रामो वै त्रयाणाम् संस्मरिष्यति |
वीरो जनन्या मम च राज्ञो दशरथस्य च || ५-३९-२_END
BEGIN_"By seeing this jewel, the heroic Rama can recollect three of us, viz. my mother, myself 
and the king Dasaratha."_END

B_5_C_36_24
BEGIN_कच्चिच् च लक्ष्मणः शूरः सुमित्रा आनन्द वर्धनः |
अस्त्रवित् शर जालेन राक्षसान् विधमिष्यति || ५-३६-२६_END
BEGIN_"Lakshmana, the strong man, who augments the joy of Sumitra and who is an expert in weaponry, 
will indeed destroy the demons by the multitude of his arrows."_END

B_5_C_38_10
BEGIN_शैलस्य चित्र कूटस्य पादे पूर्व उत्तरे तदा || ५-३८-१२
तापस आश्रम वासिन्याः प्राज्य मूल फल उदके |
तस्मिन् सिद्ध आश्रमे देशे मन्दाकिन्या अदूरतः || ५-३८-१३
तस्य उपवन षण्डेषु नाना पुष्प सुगन्धिषु |
विहृत्य सलिल क्लिन्ना तव अन्के समुपाविशम् ||
पर्यायेण प्रसुप्तः च मम अन्के भरत अग्रजः || ५-३८-१४_END
BEGIN_"There is a place inhabited by sages at a hillock in the north-eastern It was bountiful 
with roots fruits and water. In that place, while we were residing in a hermitage of sages, on a day 
long ago, we were strolling in water in parts of groves with various kinds of flowers of perfume in 
that hillock. Your thereupon became wet and sat at my proximity."_END

B_5_C_37_18
BEGIN_अथवा मोचयिष्यामि ताम् अद्य एव हि राक्षसात् |
अस्मात् दुह्खात् उपारोह मम पृष्ठम् अनिन्दिते || ५-३७-१९_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with a charming face! Or rather, I shall relieve you from this grief now itself. 
O irreproachable lady! Ascend my back. I shall take you to Rama."_END

B_5_C_35_31
BEGIN_ततस्तौ प्रीतिसंपन्नौ हरि ईश्वर नर ईश्वरौ |परस्पर कृत आश्वासौ कथया पूर्व वृत्तया || ५-३५-३३_END
BEGIN_"Thus endowed with friendship, Sugreeva the lord of monkeys and Rama the best of men, by talking 
together of their earlier occurrences, developed mutual confidence."_END

B_5_C_39_2
BEGIN_स भूयः त्वम् समुत्साहे चोदितो हरि सत्तम |
अस्मिन् कार्य समारम्भे प्रचिन्तय यत् उत्तरम् || ५-३९-३_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the excellent among monkeys! Driven by your enthusiasm again, think what remains 
to be done in undertaking this task."_END

B_5_C_36_25
BEGIN_रौद्रेण कच्चित् अस्त्रेण रामेण निहतम् रणे |
द्रक्ष्यामि अल्पेन कालेन रावणम् ससुहृज् जनम् || ५-३६-२७_END
BEGIN_"Within a short time, I hope see Ravana killed along with his companions in the battle-field 
by terrific weapons burning brightly."_END

B_5_C_35_32
BEGIN_तम् ततः सान्त्वयामास सुग्रीवम् लक्ष्मण आग्रजः |स्त्री हेतोः वालिना भ्रात्रा निरस्तम् उरु 
तेजसा || ५-३५-३४_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, that Rama the elder brother of Lakshmana, through the extremely effulgent Vali the 
brother of Sugreeva, consoled Sugreeva who was earlier expelled from the kingdom; (by Vali), for the sake of Ruma 
a woman."_END

B_5_C_37_19
BEGIN_त्वम् हि पृष्ठ गताम् कृत्वा सम्तरिष्यामि सागरम् |
शक्तिः अस्ति हि मे वोढुम् लन्काम् अपि सरावणाम् || ५-३७-२०_END
BEGIN_"I shall cause you sit on my back and cross the ocean. I have indeed capacity to carry 
even Lanka together with Ravana."_END

B_5_C_38_11
BEGIN_ततो मांस समायुक्तो वायसः पर्यतुण्डयत् |
तम् अहम् लोष्टम् उद्यम्य वारयामि स्म वायसम् || ५-३८-१५_END
BEGIN_"Then, a crow, yearning for meat, began to peck me. Picking up a clod of earth, I prevented 
the crow from its act."_END

B_5_C_39_3
BEGIN_त्वम् अस्मिन् कार्य निर्योगे प्रमाणम् हरि सत्तम |
हनुमन् यत्नमास्थाय दुःखक्षयकरो भव || ५-३९-४
तस्य चिन्तय यो यत्नो दुह्ख क्षय करो भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the best among monkeys! You are capable of fulfilling this task. O Hanuma! 
Become the one who can remove my misfortunes, by employing your effort. If you think of it carefully, 
your effort will become the one which can remove my misfortunes."_END

B_5_C_36_26
BEGIN_कच्चिन् न तद्त् हेम समान वर्णम् |
तस्य आननम् पद्म समान गन्धि |
मया विना शुष्यति शोक दीनम् |
जल क्षये पद्मम् इव आतपेन || ५-३६-२८_END
BEGIN_"That face of Rama with its golden and with the fragrance of a lotus may be looking miserable 
as bereft of me and getting dehydrated too. I hope it is not parched by the sun, like a louts."_END

B_5_C_35_33
BEGIN_ततः त्वन् नाशजम् शोकम् रामस्य अक्लिष्ट कर्मणः |लक्ष्मणो वानर इन्द्राय सुग्रीवाय न्यवेदयत् 
|| ५-३५-३५_END
BEGIN_"Then, Lakshmana informed Sugreeva the king of monkeys about the sadness of Rama, (who is unwearied 
in action), born out of your disappearance."_END

B_5_C_37_20
BEGIN_अहम् प्रस्रवणस्थाय राघवाय अद्य मैथिलि |
प्रापयिष्यामि शक्राय हव्यम् हुतम् इव अनलः || ५-३७-२१_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Now itself, I shall cause you to reach Rama who is staying at Prasravana Mountain, 
even as fire-god hands over the oblations offered in the sacrifices to Indra the Lord of celestials."_END

B_5_C_38_12
BEGIN_दारयन् स च माम् काकः तत्र एव परिलीयते |
न च अपि उपरमन् मांसात् भक्ष अर्थी बलि भोजनः || ५-३८-१६_END
BEGIN_"Pecking me again and again, the crow was hiding there only. That crow, yearning for 
food, did not resig from meat."_END

B_5_C_39_4
BEGIN_स तथा इति प्रतिज्ञाय मारुतिः भीम विक्रमः || ५-३९-५
शिरसा आवन्द्य वैदेहीम् गमनाय उपचक्रमे |_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma of terrific prowess, having promised 'so be it', offered salutation to Seetha 
by bowing his head to her and was set off to go._END

B_5_C_36_27
BEGIN_धर्म अपदेशात् त्यजतः च राज्याम् |
माम् च अपि अरण्यम् नयतः पदातिम् |
न आसीत् व्यथा यस्य न भीः न शोकः |
कच्चित् स धैर्यम् हृदये करोति || ५-३६-२९_END
BEGIN_"Which Rama left the kingdom as an indication of his righteousness and to whom there 
was neither disturbance nor fear nor sorrow even while taking me to the forest by foot, I hope that 
the same Rama is maintaining boldness in his heart."_END

B_5_C_35_34
BEGIN_स श्रुत्वा वानर इन्द्रः तु लक्ष्मणेन ईरितम् वचः |तदा आसीन् निष्प्रभो अत्यर्थम् ग्रह ग्रस्त 
इव अंशुमान् || ५-३५-३६_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the words of Lakshmana, Sugreeva then became highly dim-witted, as the sun becomes dim 
when overpowered by an eclipse."_END

B_5_C_38_13
BEGIN_उत्कर्षन्त्याम् च रशनाम् क्रुद्धायाम् मयि पक्षिणे |
स्रंसमाने च वसने ततो दृष्टा त्वया हि अहम् || ५-३८-१७_END
BEGIN_"While I was angry with that bird, my skirt was slipping and I was pulling its string 
(so as to tighten it). I was seen by you then."_END

B_5_C_37_21
BEGIN_द्रक्ष्यसि अद्य एव वैदेहि राघवम् सह लक्ष्मणम् |
व्यवसाय समायुक्तम् विष्णुम् दैत्य वधे यथा || ५-३७-२२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Now itself, you can see Rama together with Lakshmana, getting ready for a 
strenuous effort to annihilate the demons, as Vishnu the Lord of Preservation getting ready for killing 
of demons."_END

B_5_C_39_5
BEGIN_ज्ञात्वा सम्प्रस्थितम् देवी वानरम् मारुत आत्मजम् || ५-३९-६
बाष्प गद्गदया वाचा मैथिली वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_Getting to know Hanuma ready to set out, Seetha the princess spoke the following words 
with her voice choked by tears._END

B_5_C_36_28
BEGIN_न च अस्य माता न पिता न च अन्यः न |
स्नेहात् विशिष्टो अस्ति मया समो वा |
तावद्त् हि अहम् दूत जिजीविषेयम् |
यावत् प्रवृत्तिम् शृणुयाम् प्रियस्य || ५-३६-३०_END
BEGIN_"To Rama, in the matter of affection, neither his mother nor his father nor any body 
else is equal to or more than me. O Hanuma the messenger! I wish to survive only as long as I hear the 
activity of my beloved."_END

B_5_C_35_35
BEGIN_ततः त्वत् गात्र शोभीनि रक्षसा ह्रियमाणया |यानि आभरण जालानि पातितानि मही तले || ५-३५-३७
तानि सर्वाणि रामाय आनीय हरि यूथपाः |सम्हृष्टा दर्शयाम् आसुः गतिम् तु न विदुः तव || ५-३५-३८_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, all those multitude of ornaments which adorned your body, which were being tried to 
be be snatched away by Ravana and which were dropped on to the earth, were brought by monkey-leaders joyfully 
and shown to Rama. But the monkey-leaders did not know the further course of your movement."_END

B_5_C_37_22
BEGIN_त्वत् दर्शन कृत उत्साहम् आश्रमस्थम् महाबलम् |
पुरंदरम् इव आसीनम् नाग राजस्य मूर्धनि || ५-३७-२३_END
BEGIN_"The mighty Rama, with a gusto to see you, is staying in a hermitage, even as Indra the 
destroyer of strong-holds sitting on the back of Airavata the elephant."_END

B_5_C_38_14
BEGIN_त्वया विहसिता च अहम् क्रुद्धा सम्लज्जिता तदा |
भक्ष्य गृद्धेन कालेन दारिता त्वाम् उपागता || ५-३८-१८_END
BEGIN_"Moved by anger, I felt abashed for being laughed at by you. Torn down by the crow, which 
was yearning for food, I sought shelter with you."_END

B_5_C_40_0
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा तु वचनम् तस्य वायु सूनोः महात्मनः |
उवाच आत्म हितम् वाक्यम् सीता सुर सुत उपमा || ५-४०-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of that high-souled Hanuma, Seetha who resembled the daughter of god, 
spoke the following words beneficial to herself._END

B_5_C_39_6
BEGIN_कुशलम् हनुमन् ब्रूयाः सहितौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ५-३९-७
सुग्रीवम् च सह अमात्यम् वृद्धान् सर्वान् च वानरान् |
ब्रुयस्त्वाम् वानरश्रेष्ठ कुशलम् धर्मसम्हितम् || ५-३९-८_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma, the excellent among monkeys! Ask about the welfare of both Rama and Lakshmana 
together. You also ask, according to our usage, about the welfare of Sugreeva together with his ministers 
and of all the monkeys who are elder."_END

B_5_C_36_29
BEGIN_इति इव देवी वचनम् महाअर्थम् |
तम् वानर इन्द्रम् मधुर अर्थम् उक्त्वा |
श्रोतुम् पुनः तस्य वचो अभिरामम् |
राम अर्थ युक्तम् विरराम रामा || ५-३६-३१_END
BEGIN_Uttering thus those greatly meaningful and sweetly worthwhile words, Seetha the princess 
further abstained from talking so as to hear Hanuma's delightful words describing the matters pertaining 
to Rama._END

B_5_C_35_36
BEGIN_तानि रामाय दत्तानि मया एव उपहृतानि च |स्वनवन्ति अवकीर्णन्ति तस्मिन् विहत चेतसि || ५-३५-३९_END
BEGIN_"I indeed brought those ornaments near to Rama and gave them to him. Then, soon after receiving 
them, Rama lost his consciousness and the resounding ornaments were scattered all over."_END

B_5_C_38_15
BEGIN_आसीनस्य च ते श्रान्ता पुनः उत्सन्गम् आविशम् |
क्रुध्यन्ती च प्रहृष्टेन त्वया अहम् परिसान्त्विता || ५-३८-१९_END
BEGIN_"Feeling tired, I again settled on your lap. As though angry, I was consoled by you and 
I was fully delighted."_END

B_5_C_37_23
BEGIN_पृष्ठम् आरोह मे देवि मा विकान्क्षस्व शोभने |
योगम् अन्विच्छ रामेण शश अन्केन इव रोहिणी || ५-३७-२४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the auspicious princess! Mount on my back. Do not have any hesitation. Be inclined 
of joining Rama even as Rohini, moon's favourite wife, joined the moon."_END

B_5_C_40_1
BEGIN_त्वाम् दृष्ट्वा प्रिय वक्तारम् सम्प्रहृष्यामि वानर |
अर्ध सम्जात सस्य इव वृष्टिम् प्राप्य वसुम् धरा || ५-४०-२_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Seeing you speaking pleasant words, I am as overjoyed, as a field with half-sprouted 
crop of grain is thrilled by receiving a rain."_END

B_5_C_39_7
BEGIN_यथा च स महाबाहुः माम् तारयति राघवः |
अस्मात् दुह्ख अम्बु सम्रोधात् त्वम् समाधातुम् अर्हसि || ५-३९-९_END
BEGIN_"You deserve to evolve a strategy through which the long-armed Rama can make me to cross 
over this ocean of misfortunes."_END

B_5_C_36_30
BEGIN_सीताया वचनम् श्रुत्वा मारुतिः भीम विक्रमः |
शिरसि अञ्जलिम् आधाय वाक्यम् उत्तरम् अब्रवीत् || ५-३६-३२_END
BEGIN_Hearing Seetha's words, Hanuma of terrific prowess, keeping his joined palms on his head, 
spoke the following words in reply._END

B_5_C_38_16
BEGIN_बाष्प पूर्ण मुखी मन्दम् चक्षुषी परिमार्जती |
लक्षिता अहम् त्वया नाथ वायसेन प्रकोपिता || ५-३८-२०_END
BEGIN_"Slowly wiping my eyes, my face filled with tears, I was seen by you, O Lord, as having 
been annoyed by the crow."_END

B_5_C_35_37
BEGIN_तानि अन्के दर्शनीयानि कृत्वा बहु विधम् ततः |तेन देव प्रकाशेन देवेन परिदेवितम् || ५-३५-४०_END
BEGIN_"That Lord Rama looking like god, kept those beautiful ornaments of yours in his flank and lamented 
in many ways."_END

B_5_C_37_24
BEGIN_कथयन्ति इव चन्द्रेण सूर्येण इव सुवर्चला |
मत् पृष्ठम् अधिरुह्य त्वम् तर आकाश महाअर्णवम् || ५-३७-२५_END
BEGIN_"You ascend my back and cross the ocean by journeying through the sky, as though speaking 
to the greatly resplendent sun and to the moon."_END

B_5_C_40_2
BEGIN_यथा तम् पुरुष व्याघ्रम् गात्रैः शोक अभिकर्शितैः |
संस्पृशेयम् सकामा अहम् तथा कुरु दयाम् मयि || ५-४०-३_END
BEGIN_"With my limbs emaciated with grief, I have a desire to touch that Rama the tiger among 
men. Show mercy on me and fulfill my desire."_END

B_5_C_39_8
BEGIN_जीवन्तीम् माम् यथा रामः सम्भावयति कीर्तिमान् |
तत् त्वया हनुमन् वाच्यम् वाचा धर्मम् अवाप्नुहि || ५-३९-१०_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Tell, in whatever manner, by which the illustrious Rama can console me, even 
while I am still surviving. Reap righteousness, by helping me through your word."_END

B_5_C_36_31
BEGIN_न त्वाम् इहस्थाम् जानीते रामः कमल लोचनः |
तेन त्वामिहस्थाम् जानीते रामः कमललोचने || ५-३६-३३_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha having lotus eyes! Rama does not know that you are here. For that reason, he 
did not take you back soon, as Indra the destroyer of strong holds did not take back Sachi, his wife."_END

B_5_C_37_25
BEGIN_न हि मे सम्प्रयातस्य त्वाम् इतो नयतो अन्गने |
अनुगन्तुम् गतिम् शक्ताः सर्वे लन्का निवासिनः || ५-३७-२६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! While I am taking you from here, no body staying in Lanka is competent to 
come along with me."_END

B_5_C_35_38
BEGIN_पश्यतः तस्या रुदतः ताम्यतः च पुनः पुनः |प्रादीपयन् दाशरथेः तानि शोक हुत अशनम् || ५-३५-४१_END
BEGIN_"While seeing those ornaments, Rama was lamenting and getting suffocated again and again. Thus, 
those ornaments ignited the fire of Rama's grief."_END

B_5_C_38_17
BEGIN_परिश्रमात्प्रसुप्ता च राघवाङ्के ऽप्य्हम् चिरम् |
पर्याय़ेण प्रसुप्तश्च ममाङ्के भरताग्रजः ५-३८-२१_END
BEGIN_"I even slept for a long time on Rama's lap because of my fatigue. In his turn, Rama 
the elder brother of Bharata, slept in my arms."_END

B_5_C_40_3
BEGIN_अभिज्ञानम् च रामस्य दत्तम् हरि गण उत्तम |
क्षिप्ताम् ईषिकाम् काकस्य कोपात् एक अक्षि शातनीम् || ५-४०-४_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the excellent one among the troops of monkeys! Present the story of the blade 
of grass called Ishika hurled with anger and thereby one eye of the crow destroyed by Rama (as a signal 
remembrance)."_END

B_5_C_39_9
BEGIN_नित्यम् उत्साह युक्ताः च वाचः श्रुत्वा मया ईरिताः |
वर्धिष्यते दाशरथेः पौरुषम् मत् अवाप्तये || ५-३९-११_END
BEGIN_"Constantly hearing the words endowed with energy spoken by you, Rama's manly strength 
will be intensified to recover me."_END

B_5_C_36_32
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा एव तु वचो मह्यम् क्षिप्रम् एष्यति राघवः |
चमूम् प्रकर्षन् महतीम् हरि ऋष्क गण सम्कुलाम् || ५-३६-३४_END
BEGIN_"Soon after hearing my words, Rama will come soon, drawing forth a large army, consisting 
of a multitude of monkeys and bears."_END

B_5_C_37_26
BEGIN_यथा एव अहम् इह प्राप्तः तथैव अहम् असंशयम् |
यास्यामि पश्य वैदेहि त्वाम् उद्यम्य विहायसम् || ५-३७-२७_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! In what manner I reached here, in the same manner, I shall move through the 
sky, taking you along with me. See, there is no doubt."_END

B_5_C_35_39
BEGIN_शयितम् च चिरम् तेन दुह्ख आर्तेन महात्मना |मया अपि विविधैः वाक्यैः कृच्छ्रात् उत्थापितः 
पुनः || ५-३५-४२_END
BEGIN_"That grief-stricken mighty man was thus lying on the floor for a long time. Then, with great difficulty, 
I made him to get up by telling several consoling words."_END

B_5_C_38_18
BEGIN_स तत्र पुनरे वाथ वायसः समुपागमत् |
ततः सुप्तप्रबुद्धाम् माम् रामस्याङ्कात्समुत्थिताम् || ५-३८-२२
वायसः सहसागम्य विददार स्तनान्तरे |
पुनः पुनर्थोत्पत्य विददार स मां भृशम् || ५-३८-२३_END
BEGIN_"Meanwhile, the same crow appeared there. Descending all of a sudden, the crow clawed 
me at the space between the breasts, even as I awoke from my sleep and rose from the lap of Rama. Flying 
up again, it tore me up a lot."_END

B_5_C_40_4
BEGIN_मनः शिलायाः तिकलो गण्ड पार्श्वे निवेशितः |
त्वया प्रनष्टे तिलके तम् किल स्मर्तुम् अर्हसि || ५-४०-५_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! You ought surely to recollect that while a mark on my forehead had got effaced 
once, another mark with realgar was indeed painted by you on the side of my cheek."_END

B_5_C_39_10
BEGIN_मत् संदेश युता वाचः त्वत्तः श्रुत्वा एव राघवः |
पराक्रम विधिम् वीरो विधिवत् सम्विधास्यति || ५-३९-१२_END
BEGIN_'Hearing the words containing my message from you, the valiant Rama will duly set his 
heart in exercising his strength."_END

B_5_C_36_33
BEGIN_विष्टम्भयित्वा बाण ओघैः अक्षोभ्यम् वरुण आलयम् |
करिष्यति पुरीम् लन्काम् काकुत्स्थः शान्त राक्षसाम् || ५-३६-३५_END
BEGIN_"Rama will paralyze the imperturbable ocean with his flood of arrows and make the City 
of Lanka extinguished of demons."_END

B_5_C_37_27
BEGIN_मैथिली तु हरि श्रेष्ठात् श्रुत्वा वचनम् अद्भुतम् |
हर्ष विस्मित सर्व अन्गी हनूमन्तम् अथ अब्रवीत् || ५-३७-२८_END
BEGIN_Hearing those astonishing words from Hanuma, Seetha with her entire limbs flowered with 
joy, thereafter spoke to Hanuma (as follows):_END

B_5_C_35_40
BEGIN_तानि दृष्ट्वा महाअर्हाणि दर्शयित्वा मुहुः मुहुः |राघवः सह सौमित्रिः सुग्रीवे स न्यवेदयत् 
|| ५-३५-४३_END
BEGIN_"That long-armed Rama, along with Lakshmana, after seeing those ornaments, examined them, again 
and again. He later gave them to Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_40_5
BEGIN_स वीर्यवान् कथम् सीताम् हृताम् समनुमन्यसे |
वसन्तीम् रक्षसाम् मध्ये महाइन्द्र वरुण उपम || ५-४०-६_END
BEGIN_"How are you, the valiant man equal to Indra the Lord of celestials and Varuna the King 
of Universe, ignore Seetha who was taken away and now staying in the midst of these demons?"_END

B_5_C_38_19
BEGIN_ततः समुक्षितो रामो मुक्तैः शोणितबिन्दुभिः |
वयसेन ततस्तेन बलवत्क्लिश्यमानया || ५-३८-२४
स मया बोधितः श्रीमान् सुखसुप्तः परम्तपः |_END
BEGIN_"Then, Rama got wet by the discharged drops of blood. Thereafter, that splendorous Rama, 
the annihilator of enemies, who was in a pleasant slumber, was woken up by that crow and by me who was 
grievously tormented by the crow."_END

B_5_C_39_11
BEGIN_सीतायाः तत् वचः श्रुत्वा हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
शिरसि अञ्जलिम् आधाय वाक्यम् उत्तरम् अब्रवीत् || ५-३९-१३_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Seetha, Hanuma the son of wind-god, having placed his open hands 
side by side, slightly shallowed on his head in salutation), spoke the following words in reply._END

B_5_C_36_34
BEGIN_तत्र यदि अन्तरा मृत्युः यदि देवाः सह असुराः |
स्थास्यन्ति पथि रामस्य स तान् अपि वधिष्यति || ५-३६-३६_END
BEGIN_"If the goddess of Death along with demons or celestials stand firmly in the way of Rama 
at that time, he will kill them also."_END

B_5_C_37_28
BEGIN_हनूमन् दूरम् अध्वनम् कथम् माम् वोढुम् इच्छसि |
तत् एव खलु ते मन्ये कपित्वम् हरि यूथप || ५-३७-२९_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! How are you wishing to carry me for such a long distance? O chief of monkeys! 
I consider this indeed as your apishness!"_END

B_5_C_35_41
BEGIN_स तव अदर्शनात् आर्ये राघवः परितप्यते |महता ज्वलता नित्यम् अग्निना इव अग्नि पर्वतः || ५-३५-४४_END
BEGIN_"O the kind mistress! As you were being unseen, Rama was tormented forever with a great flaming 
fire of grief, like a volcano."_END

B_5_C_40_6
BEGIN_एष चूडा मणिः दिव्यो मया सुपरिरक्षितः |
एतम् दृष्ट्वा प्रहृष्यामि व्यसने त्वाम् इव अनघ || ५-४०-७_END
BEGIN_"O faultless Rama! This wonderful jewel for the head head has been protected well by 
me. Seeing this in my distress, I have been getting delighted, as though I have seen you."_END

B_5_C_38_20
BEGIN_स माम् दृष्ट्वा महाबाहुर्वितुन्नाम् स्तनयोस्तदा || ५-३८-२५
आशी विष इव क्रुद्धः श्वसान् वाक्यम् अभाषथाः |_END
BEGIN_"That long-armed Rama, seeing me pierced violently on the breasts, then spoke the following 
words, hissing like an angry serpant._END

B_5_C_39_12
BEGIN_क्षिप्रम् एष्यति काकुत्स्थो हरि ऋक्ष प्रवरैः वृतः |
यस्ते युधि विजित्य अरीन् शोकम् व्यपनयिष्यति || ५-३९-१४_END
BEGIN_"Coming soon together with valiant monkeys and bears, Rama after defeating the enemies 
in battle, will eliminate your sorrow."_END

B_5_C_41_0
BEGIN_स च वाग्भिः प्रशस्ताभिः गमिष्यन् पूजितः तया |
तस्मात् देशात् अपक्रम्य चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-४१-१_END
BEGIN_Seetha honoured Hanuma, who was ready to go, with good words. Hanuma, having gone to 
a distance from that place, thought within himself (as follows):_END

B_5_C_36_35
BEGIN_तव अदर्शनजेन आर्ये शोकेन स परिप्लुतः |
न शर्म लभते रामः सिम्ह अर्दित इव द्विपः || ५-३६-३७_END
BEGIN_"O noble lady! Being full of grief caused by your non-appearance, that Rama is not obtaining 
happiness, like an elephant tornmented by a lion."_END

B_5_C_37_29
BEGIN_कथम् वा अल्प शरीरः त्वम् माम् इतो नेतुम् इच्छसि |
सकाशम् मानव इन्द्रस्य भर्तुः मे प्लवग ऋषभ || ५-३७-३०_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the best of monkeys! With such a small seized body, how do you wish to take 
me from here to the presence of my husband, Rama the Lord of human beings?"_END

B_5_C_35_42
BEGIN_त्वत् कृते तम् अनिद्रा च शोकः चिन्ता च राघवम् |तापयन्ति महात्मानम् अग्नि अगारम् इव अग्नयः 
|| ५-३५-४५_END
BEGIN_"For your sake, insomnia, grief and worry were tormenting that great souled Rama, as flames torment 
a burning house."_END

B_5_C_40_7
BEGIN_एष निर्यातितः श्रीमान् मया ते वारि सम्भवः |
अतः परम् न शक्ष्यामि जीवितुम् शोक लालसा || ५-४०-८_END
BEGIN_"This splendid jewel, produced in water, has been sent to you. Absorbed in grief, I shall 
not be able to survive henceforth."_END

B_5_C_38_21
BEGIN_केन ते नाग नास ऊरु विक्षतम् वै स्तन अन्तरम् || ५-३८-२६
कः क्रीडति सरोषेण पन्च वक्त्रेण भोगिना |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the round-thighed woman! Who has wounded the space between your breasts? who 
is playing with a fire-faced serpent filled with fury?"_END

B_5_C_39_13
BEGIN_न हि पश्यामि मर्त्येषु न अमरेष्व् असुरेषु वा |
यस्तस्य ष्खिपतो बाणान् स्थातुम् उत्सहते अग्रतः || ५-३९-१५_END
BEGIN_"While discharging his arrows, none can be seen either in men or in monkeys or in celestials 
who are able to stand before Rama in battle."_END

B_5_C_41_1
BEGIN_अल्प शेषम् इदम् कार्यम् दृष्टा इयम् असित ईक्षणा |
त्रीन् उपायान् अतिक्रम्य चतुर्थ इह दृश्यते || ५-४१-२_END
BEGIN_"I have seen this black-eyed Seetha. There is only a little that remains to be done by 
me. Abandoning the three strategies for success viz. sowing dissension, negotiation and bribery, I have 
to implement here the fourth strategy viz. open assault."_END

B_5_C_36_36
BEGIN_दर्दरेण च ते देवि शपे मूल फलेन च |
मलयेन च विन्ध्येन मेरुणा मन्दरेण च || ५-३६-३८
यथा सुनयनं वल्गु बिम्बौष्ठं चारुकुण्डलम् |
मुखं द्रक्ष्यसि रामस्य पूर्णचन्द्रमिवोदितम् || ५-३६-३९_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! I swear and tell you by the mountains Malaya, Vindhya, Meru and 
Dardura as well as by our staple food of roots and fruits, that you will soon see Rama's face, having 
good eyes, handsome, having lips with the colour of a bright-red gourd (fruit of Momordica monodelpha) 
and with its charming look like a rising full moon."_END

B_5_C_37_30
BEGIN_सीताया वचनम् श्रुत्वा हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
चिन्तयामास लक्ष्मीवान् नवम् परिभवम् कृतम् || ५-३७-३१_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Seetha, the illustrious Hanuma, the son of wind-god thought it to 
be the first insult was caused to him._END

B_5_C_35_43
BEGIN_तव अदर्शन शोकेन राघवः प्रविचाल्यते |महता भूमि कम्पेन महान् इव शिला उच्चयः || ५-३५-४६_END
BEGIN_"By the grief caused by your not being seen, Rama is trembled with grief, as a high mountain is 
trembled by a great earthquake."_END

B_5_C_40_8
BEGIN_असह्यानि च दुह्खानि वाचः च हृदयच् चिदः |
राक्षसीनाम् सुघोराणाम् त्वत् कृते मर्षयामि अहम् || ५-४०-९_END
BEGIN_"With a hope of your coming here at any time, I am enduring these unbearable hardships 
and also the words of horrible female demons; which pierce my heart."_END

B_5_C_38_22
BEGIN_वीक्षमाणः ततः तम् वै वायसम् समवैक्षथाः || ५-३८-२७
नखैः सरुधिरैः तीक्ष्णैः माम् एव अभिमुखम् स्थितम् |_END
BEGIN_'Then, throwing a glance around, Rama saw that crow with its sharp claws moistened iwth 
blood and sitting in front of me alone."_END

B_5_C_39_14
BEGIN_अपि अर्कम् अपि पर्जन्यम् अपि वैवस्वतम् यमम् |
स हि सोढुम् रणे शक्तः तव हेतोः विशेषतः || ५-३९-१६_END
BEGIN_"That Rama is capable of enduring even the sun-god, even Indra the god of rain or even 
Yama the god of death, son of the sun-god a battle-field especially for your sake."_END

B_5_C_41_2
BEGIN_न साम रक्षह्सु गुणाय कल्पते |
न दनम् अर्थ उपचितेषु वर्तते |
न भेद साध्या बल दर्पिता जनाः |
पराक्रमः तु एष मम इह रोचते || ५-४१-३_END
BEGIN_"In the case of demons, the strategy of negotiation is not practicable. For those persons 
having abundant wealth, the strategy of bribery is not suitable. For persons who are proud of their 
strength, the strategy of sowing dissension is not amenable. Prowess alone is agreeable for me here."_END

B_5_C_36_37
BEGIN_क्षिप्रं द्रक्ष्यसि वैदेहि रामं प्रस्रवणे गिरौ |
शतक्रतुमिवासीनं नाकपृष्ठस्य मूर्धनि || ५-३६-४०_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! You will see soon Rama on the Prasravana mountain, like Indra the Lord of 
celestials seated on the back of Airavata, the chief of elephants."_END

B_5_C_37_31
BEGIN_न मे जानाति सत्त्वम् वा प्रभावम् वा असित ईक्षणा |
तस्मात् पश्यतु वैदेही यत् रूपम् मम कामतः || ५-३७-३२_END
BEGIN_(Hanuma said to himself); "The black-eyed Seetha is not aware of my strength or power. 
That is why, let her see the form I can assume at will."_END

B_5_C_40_9
BEGIN_धारयिष्यामि मासम् तु जीवितम् शत्रु सूदन |
मासात् ऊर्ध्वम् न जीविष्ये त्वया हीना नृप आत्मज || ५-४०-१०_END
BEGIN_"O Rama the prince, the annihilator of enemies! I shall hold my life only for a month. 
I will not survive without you, after a month."_END

B_5_C_35_44
BEGIN_कानानानि सुरम्याणि नदी प्रस्रवणानि च |चरन् न रतिम् आप्नोति त्वम् अपश्यन् नृप आत्मजे || 
५-३५-४७_END
BEGIN_"O princess! In not seeing you, Rama is not obtaining delight, even while moving in quite charming 
forests, encompassing rivers and water-falls."_END

B_5_C_38_23
BEGIN_पुत्रः किल स शक्रस्य वायसः पतताम् वरः || ५-३८-२८
धरा अन्तर चरः शीघ्रम् पवनस्य गतौ समः |_END
BEGIN_"That crow, the best among birds, seems to be the son of Indra the Lord of celestials, 
staying in mountains and moving with a peed equal to the wind."_END

B_5_C_39_15
BEGIN_स हि सागर पर्यन्ताम् महीम् शासितुम् ईहते |
त्वन् निमित्तो हि रामस्य जयो जनक नन्दिनि || ५-३९-१७_END
BEGIN_"Rama is indeed worthwhile to master the entire earth bounded by the ocean. O Seetha! 
Rama's victory is indeed for your sake."_END

B_5_C_41_3
BEGIN_न च अस्य कार्यस्य पराक्रमात् ऋते |
विनिश्चयः कश्चित् इह उपपद्यते |
हृत प्रवीराः तु रणे हि राक्षसाः |
कथंचित् ईयुः यत् इह अद्य मार्दवम् || ५-४१-४_END
BEGIN_"Except showing of valour, no strategy in accomplishing this task is adequate in these 
circumstances, for the demons can adopt a weak attitude in the ensuring combat, if their foremost heroes 
are somehow killed here and now."_END

B_5_C_36_38
BEGIN_न मांसं राघवो भुङ्क्ते न चापि मधुसेवते |
वन्यं सुविहितं नित्यं भक्तमश्नाति पञ्चमम् || ५-३६-४१_END
BEGIN_"Rama is not eating meat, nor indulging even in spirituous liquor. Everyday, in the evening, 
he is eating the food existing in the forest, well arranged for him."_END

B_5_C_37_32
BEGIN_इति संचिन्त्य हनुमान् तदा प्लवग सत्तमः |
दर्शयामास वैदेह्याः स्वरूपम् अरि मर्दनः || ५-३७-३३_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the best of monkeys and the annihilator of enemies, thinking in this way, then 
showed his peculiarity to Seetha._END

B_5_C_40_10
BEGIN_घोरो राक्षस राजो अयम् दृष्टिः च न सुखा मयि |
त्वाम् च श्रुत्वा विपद्यन्तम् न जीवेयम् अहम् क्षणम् || ५-४०-११_END
BEGIN_"This Ravana, the king of demons, is terrible. In my instance, his glance is not pleasant. 
Hearing that you are causing a delay, I will not survive even for a moment."_END

B_5_C_35_45
BEGIN_स त्वाम् मनुज शार्दूलः क्षिप्रम् प्राप्स्यति राघवः |समित्र बान्धवम् हत्वा रावणम् जनक आत्मजे 
|| ५-३५-४८_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the daughter of Janaka! That Rama the excellent of men will receive you, soon after, 
killing Ravana along with Ravana's friends and relatives."_END

B_5_C_38_24
BEGIN_ततः तस्मिन् महाबाहुः कोप सम्वर्तित ईक्षणः || ५-३८-२९
वायसे कृतवान् क्रूराम् मतिम् मतिमताम् वर |_END
BEGIN_"Then, the long-armed Rama, the best among wise men, swirling his eyes in anger, made 
a resolve in the matter of that ferocious crow."_END

B_5_C_39_16
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा सम्यक् सत्यम् सुभाषितम् |
जानकी बहु मेने अथ वचनम् च इदम् अब्रवीत् || ५-३९-१८_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Hanuma, spoken rightly and truly well, Seetha held him in great 
respect and proceeded to speak (the following) words:_END

B_5_C_41_4
BEGIN_कार्ये कर्मणि निर्दिष्टः यो बहूनि अपि साधयेत् |
पूर्व कार्य विरोधेन स कार्यम् कर्तुम् अर्हति || ५-४१-५_END
BEGIN_"He alone can accomplish his purpose, who implements many (secondary) tasks even after 
the initial task has been carried through, without impairing the previous achievement."_END

B_5_C_36_39
BEGIN_न एव दंशान् न मशकान् न कीटान् न सरी सृपान् |
राघवो अपनयेत् गत्रात् त्वत् गतेन अन्तः आत्मना || ५-३६-४२_END
BEGIN_"With his mind wholly devoted to you, Rama is not even driving away forest-flies from 
his body, nor mosquitoes nor insects nor reptiles from his body."_END

B_5_C_37_33
BEGIN_स तस्मात् पादपात् धीमान् आप्लुत्य प्लवग ऋषभः |
ततो वर्धितुम् आरेभे सीता प्रत्यय कारणात् || ५-३७-३४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the intelligent and the excellent of monkeys, leaped down from that tree and 
then, to create confidence in Seetha, started to increase his body-form._END

B_5_C_40_11
BEGIN_वैदेह्या वचनम् श्रुत्वा करुणम् स अश्रु भाषितम् |
अथ अब्रवीन् महातेजा हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४०-१२_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Seetha, spoken pitiably with tears, Hanuma the son of wind-god, 
with a great splendour, spoke (as follows):_END

B_5_C_35_46
BEGIN_सहितौ राम सुग्रीवाव् उभाव् अकुरुताम् तदा |समयम् वालिनम् हन्तुम् तव च अन्वेषणम् तथा || 
५-३५-४९_END
BEGIN_"That day when Rama and Sugreeva were together, both of them made an agreement that Rama would 
annihilate Vali and Sugreeva would arrange for a search of you."_END

B_5_C_38_25
BEGIN_स दर्भ संस्तरात् गृह्य ब्रह्मणो अस्त्रेण योजयः || ५-३८-३०
स दीप्त इव काल अग्निः जज्वाल अभिमुखो द्विजम् |_END
BEGIN_"Taking a blade of Kusa grass from his bed ( made of Kusa grass), Rama employed it to 
work with Brahma's missile (a mythical weapon which deals with infallible destruction). That blazing 
shoot of grass, resembling a fire destroying the world, flared up in front of that bird."_END

B_5_C_39_17
BEGIN_ततः तम् प्रस्थितम् सीता वीक्षमाणा पुनः पुनः |
भर्तुः स्नेह अन्वितम् वाक्यम् सौहार्दात् अनुमानयत् || ५-३९-१९_END
BEGIN_Thereupon, looking again and again towards that Hanuma who was going away, Seetha kind-heartedly 
adored his words endowed with friendliness for her husband._END

B_5_C_41_5
BEGIN_न हि एकः साधको हेतुः स्वल्पस्य अपि इह कर्मणः |
यो हि अर्थम् बहुधा वेद स समर्थो अर्थ साधने || ५-४१-६_END
BEGIN_'There is indeed no single exclusive method to accomplish a purpose however small a task 
may be. On the other hand, whoever knows to do a task in many ways, he alone is capable of achieving 
that task."_END

B_5_C_36_40
BEGIN_नित्यम् ध्यान परो रामो नित्यम् शोक परायणः |
न अन्यच् चिन्तयते किंचित् स तु काम वशम् गतः || ५-३६-४३_END
BEGIN_"Rama always cogitates on something or the other. He is forever engaged in sorrow. He 
is enamoured with the god of love and thinks of nothing else."_END

B_5_C_40_12
BEGIN_त्वत् शोक विमुखो रामो देवि सत्येन ते शपे |
रामे शोक अभिभूते तु लक्ष्मणः परितप्यते || ५-४०-१३
कथंचित् भवती दृष्टा न कालः परिशोचितुम् |
इमम् मुहूर्तम् दुह्खानाम् अन्तम् द्रक्ष्यसि भामिनि || ५-४०-१४
ताव् उभौ पुरुष व्याघ्रौ राज पुत्राव् अनिन्दितौ |
त्वत् दर्शन कृत उत्साहौ लन्काम् भस्मी करिष्यतः || ५-४०-१५
हत्वा तु समरे क्रूरम् रावणम् सह बान्धवम् |
राघवौ त्वाम् विशाल अक्षि स्वाम् पुरीम् प्रापयिष्यतः || ५-४०-१६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! Rama has grown averse to everything else, caused by grief towards 
you. I sear it to you truly. when Rama is overpowered by grief, Lakshmana too gets tormented with grief." 
"O lady! Somehow or other, you have been discovered by me. This is not the time to lament. You will 
see the end of your sorrow shortly." "Those two princes, the excellent among men, the annihilator of 
enemies and who are eager to see you, will surely reduce Lanka to ashes. "O large-eyed Seetha! Killing 
the cruel Ravana along with his relatives, Rama and Lakshmana will take you to their own city."_END

B_5_C_37_34
BEGIN_मेरु मन्दार सम्काशो बभौ दीप्त अनल प्रभः |
अग्रतो व्यवतस्थे च सीताया वानर ऋषभः || ५-३७-३५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the foremost of monkeys, flashed like Meru and Mandara mountains, shining brightly 
like a blazing fire. He thus stood too in front of Seetha._END

B_5_C_35_47
BEGIN_ततस्ताभ्याम् कुमाराभ्याम् वीराभ्याम् स हरीश्वरः |किष्किन्धाम् समूपागम्य वाली युद्धे निपातितः 
|| ५-३५-५०_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, Rama and Lakshmana the two valiant princes reached Kishkindha. Rama killed Vali the 
king of monkeys there in a combat."_END

B_5_C_38_26
BEGIN_स तम् प्रदीप्तम् चिक्षेप दर्भम् तम् वायसम् प्रति || ५-३८-३१
ततस्तम् वायसम् दर्भः सोम्बरेऽनुजगाम ह |_END
BEGIN_"As Rama threw that blazing blade of Kusa grass towards that crow, that blade of grass 
went chasing that crow in the sky."_END

B_5_C_41_6
BEGIN_इह एव तावत् कृत निश्चयो हि अहम् |
यदि व्रजेयम् प्लवग ईश्वर आलयम् |
पर आत्म सम्मर्द विशेष तत्त्ववित् |
ततः कृतम् स्यान् मम भर्तृ शासनम् || ५-४१-७_END
BEGIN_'If I go to the abode of Sugreeva the Lord of monkeys, having ascertained the truth as 
to who will predominate in an encounter between the adversary and ourselves here itself, then will the 
command of my master have been carried out by me."_END

B_5_C_39_18
BEGIN_यदि वा मन्यसे वीर वस एक अहम् अरिम् दम |
कस्मिंश्चित् सम्वृते देशे विश्रान्तः श्वो गमिष्यसि || ५-३९-२०_END
BEGIN_"O valiant monkey, the annihilator of enemies! If you are agreeable, stay for a day at 
any one secret place. After taking rest, you can go tomorrow."_END

B_5_C_36_41
BEGIN_अनिद्रः सततम् रामः सुप्तो अपि च नर उत्तमः |
सीतेति मधुराम् वाणीम् व्याहरन् प्रतिबुध्यते || ५-३६-४४_END
BEGIN_"Rama mostly does not have sleep. Even if that best of men sleeps, he keeps awake uttering 
sweet words like "lo! Behold! Seetha!"_END

B_5_C_40_13
BEGIN_यत् तु रामो विजानीयात् अभिज्ञानम् अनिन्दिते |
प्रीति सम्जननम् तस्य भूयः त्वम् दातुम् अर्हसि || ५-४०-१७_END
BEGIN_"O faultless Seetha! Be pleased to give another token of remembrance, which Rama will 
recognise and which creates pleasure to him."_END

B_5_C_37_35
BEGIN_हरिः पर्वत सम्काशः ताम्र वक्त्रो महाबलः |
वज्र दम्ष्ट्र नखो भीमो वैदेहीम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ५-३७-३६_END
BEGIN_The mighty Hanuma, resembling a mountain, having a red face, having teeth and nails as 
hard as adamant and terrific in appearance, spoke the following words to Seetha._END

B_5_C_38_27
BEGIN_अनुसृष्टः तदा कालो जगाम विविधाम् गतिम् || ५-३८-३२
त्राण काम इमम् लोकम् सर्वम् वै विचचार ह |_END
BEGIN_"Then, while that blade of grass came chasing, that crow went flying in many a way. Seeking 
protection, it roamed all over the world."_END

B_5_C_35_48
BEGIN_ततो निहत्य तरसा रामो वालिनम् आहवे |सर्व ऋष्क हरि सम्घानाम् सुग्रीवम् अकरोत् पतिम् || ५-३५-५१_END
BEGIN_"After killing Vali in combat by means of his strength, Rama made Sugreeva the king for the entire 
multitude of bears and monkeys."_END

B_5_C_41_7
BEGIN_कथम् नु खल्व् अद्य भवेत् सुख आगतम् |
प्रसह्य युद्धम् मम राक्षसैः सह |
तथैव खल्व् आत्म बलम् च सारवत् |
समानयेन् माम् च रणे दश आननः || ५-४१-८_END
BEGIN_"How can my combat with the demons now will prove to be a happy one? And, how will my 
strength become fruitful? How indeed will that Ravana applaud me in battle?"_END

B_5_C_39_19
BEGIN_मम चेत् अल्प भाग्यायाः साम्निध्यात् तव वीर्यवान् |
अस्य शोकस्य महतो मुहूर्तम् मोक्षणम् भवेत् || ५-३९-२१_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Because of your vicinity, there may be a relief for a moment to this great 
sorrow of me, who is less fortunate."_END

B_5_C_36_42
BEGIN_दृष्ट्वा फलम् वा पुष्पम् वा यच् च अन्यत् स्त्री मनो हरम् |
बहुशो हा प्रियेति एवम् श्वसन् त्वाम् अभिभाषते || ५-३६-४५_END
BEGIN_"When he happens to see a fruit or a flower or any other beautiful object, he recollects 
of you and says 'O beloved!' many times and breathes a sigh."_END

B_5_C_40_14
BEGIN_सा अब्रवीत् दत्तम् एव इह मया अभिज्ञानम् उत्तमम् |
एतत् एव हि रामस्य दृष्ट्वा मत् केश भूषणम् || ५-४०-१८
श्रद्धेयम् हनुमन् वाक्यम् तव वीर भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_Seetha said, " An excellent token of remembrance was indeed given by me. Seeing this 
jewel for my hair, Rama will trust your words."_END

B_5_C_37_36
BEGIN_सपर्वत वन उद्देशाम् साट्ट प्राकार तोरणाम् |
लन्काम् इमाम् सनथाम् वा नयितुम् शक्तिः अस्ति मे || ५-३७-३७_END
BEGIN_"To me, there is capability to carry this Lanka along with its hills, forest-areas, market-places, 
defensive walls and arches together with its Lord Ravana himself."_END

B_5_C_38_28
BEGIN_स पित्रा च परित्यक्तः सुरैः सर्वैः महर्षिभिः || ५-३८-३३
त्रीन् लोकान् सम्परिक्रम्य त्वाम् एव शरणम् गतः |_END
BEGIN_"Roaming the three worlds in search of a saviour, that crow was abandoned by Indra; its 
father, the celestials and the sages. Finally, it sought refuge in the same Rama."_END

B_5_C_35_49
BEGIN_राम सुग्रीवयोः ऐक्यम् देवि एवम् समजायत |हनूमन्तम् च माम् विद्धि तयोः दूतम् इह आगतम् || 
५-३५-५२_END
BEGIN_"O princess! A friendship was held well in such a manner between Rama and Sugreeva. Know me as 
Hanuma, who came here as a messenger on behalf of both of them."_END

B_5_C_41_8
BEGIN_ततः समासाद्य रणे दशाननं |
समन्त्रिवर्गम् सबलप्रयायिनम् |
हृदि स्थितम् तस्य मतम् बलं च वै |
सुखेन मत्त्वाऽहमितः पुनर्व्रजे || ५-४१-९_END
BEGIN_"Then meeting Ravana with his troop of ministers, his army and his followers in battle 
as well as knowing his designs and strength, I will go back from here happily."_END

B_5_C_39_20
BEGIN_गते हि हरि शार्दूल पुनः आगमनाय तु |
प्राणानाम् अपि संदेहो मम स्यान् न अत्र संशयः || ५-३९-२२_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the lion among the monkeys! If after that, there is any doubt about your return, 
there is a doubt even for my survival too. There is no suspicion about this matter."_END

B_5_C_36_43
BEGIN_स देवि नित्यम् परितप्यमानः |
त्वाम् एव सीतेति अभिभाषमाणः |
धृत व्रतो राज सुतो महात्मा |
तव एव लाभाय कृत प्रयत्नः || ५-३६-४६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! Rama the magnanimous prince is always lamenting, speaking just 
about you, recollecting "Seetha, Seetha!". Being firm in his vow, he makes effort to find you only."_END

B_5_C_40_15
BEGIN_स तम् मणि वरम् गृह्य श्रीमान् प्लवग सत्तमः || ५-४०-१९
प्रणम्य शिरसा देवीम् गमनाय उपचक्रमे |_END
BEGIN_Taking that excellent jewel, the illustrious Hanuma, the best among monkeys, offered 
salutation to Seetha by bowing his head and has set off to go._END

B_5_C_37_37
BEGIN_तत् अवस्थाप्य ताम् बुद्धिः अलम् देवि विकान्क्षया |
विशोकम् कुरु वैदेहि राघवम् सह लक्ष्मणम् || ५-३७-३८_END
BEGIN_"O princess! For this reason, leave your suspicion and keep you mind steady. Come along 
with me and make Rama and Lakshmana bereft of grief."_END

B_5_C_38_29
BEGIN_स तम् निपतितम् भूमौ शरण्यः शरणा गतम् || ५-३८-३४
वध अर्हम् अपि काकुत्स्थ कृपया पर्यपालयः |_END
BEGIN_"That Rama, who affords protection, was compassionate and protected that crow, which 
fell on the ground (in salutation to Rama) and sought for protection, eventhough it was apt to be killed."_END

B_5_C_35_50
BEGIN_स्व राज्यम् प्राप्य सुग्रीवः समनीय महाहरीन् |त्वत् अर्थम् प्रेषयामास दिशो दश महाबलान् 
|| ५-३५-५३_END
BEGIN_"Having got his own kingdom, Sugreeva summoned for mighty as well as capable monkeys and sent them 
to ten different directions in search of you."_END

B_5_C_41_9
BEGIN_इदम् अस्य नृशंसस्य नन्दन उपमम् उत्तमम् |
वनम् नेत्र मनः कान्तम् नाना द्रुम लता युतम् || ५-४१-१०_END
BEGIN_"This excellent grove of this cruel Ravana, with its various kinds of trees and creepers, 
which is pleasing to the eyes and the mind, is looking like Nandana, Indra's paradise."_END

B_5_C_39_21
BEGIN_तव अदर्शनजः शोको भूयो माम् परितापयेत् |
दुह्खात् दुह्ख परामृष्टाम् दीपयन्न् इव वानर || ५-३९-२३_END
BEGIN_'O Hanuma! To me, who is tormented by one grief after another grief, my sorrow due to 
your disappearance will further torment me, like a burning flame."_END

B_5_C_36_44
BEGIN_सा राम सम्कीर्तन वीत शोका |
रामस्य शोकेन समान शोका |
शरन् मुखेन अम्बुद शेष |
निशा इव वैदेह सुता बभूव || ५-३६-४७_END
BEGIN_"That Seetha, who has the same amount of grief as that of Rama, became worn out of her 
grief upon hearing the adoration of Rama, like a night with the moon obscured by the remnant clouds 
at the commencement of autumn."_END

B_5_C_40_16
BEGIN_तम् उत्पात कृत उत्साहम् अवेक्ष्य हरि पुम्गवम् || ५-४०-२०
वर्धमानम् महावेगम् उवाच जनक आत्मजा |
अश्रु पूर्ण मुखी दीना बाष्प गद्गदया गिरा || ५-४०-२१_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Hanuma, the best among monkeys, possessed of energy to jump up with great 
speed and expanding, Seetha spoke (as follows) in her voice choked with tears and looking miserable 
in her face filled with tears._END

B_5_C_37_38
BEGIN_तम् दृष्ट्वा अचल सम्काशम् उवाच जनक आत्मजा |
पद्म पत्र विशाल अक्षी मारुतस्य औरसम् सुतम् || ५-३७-३९_END
BEGIN_Seetha, with her large eyes resembling lotus-petals, spoke to that terrific Hanuma, the 
son of wind-god (as follows)_END

B_5_C_38_30
BEGIN_परिद्यूनम् विषण्णम् च स त्वम् आयान्तम् उक्तवान् || ५-३८-३५
मोघम् कर्तुम् न शक्यम् तु ब्राह्मम् अस्त्रम् तत् उच्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing that crow, coming exhausted and dejected, Rama said to it: 'It is not possible 
to make Brahma missile a waste. For this reason, tell me what to do now."_END

B_5_C_35_51
BEGIN_आदिष्टा वानर इन्द्रेण सुग्रीवेण महाओजसः |अद्रि राज प्रतीकाशाः सर्वतः प्रस्थिता महीम् || 
५-३५-५४_END
BEGIN_"As commanded by Sugreeva of a great splendour and the king of monkeys, those monkeys resembling 
Himalayan mountains, started out on all directions of the earth."_END

B_5_C_41_10
BEGIN_इदम् विध्वंसयिष्यामि शुष्कम् वनम् इव अनलः |
अस्मिन् भग्ने ततः कोपम् करिष्यति स रावणः || ५-४१-११_END
BEGIN_"I will destroy this grove like fire scorching a dried up forest. While this grove gets 
demolished, Ravana will then be angry."_END

B_5_C_39_22
BEGIN_अयम् च वीर संदेहः तिष्ठति इव मम अग्रतः |
सुमहान् त्वत् सहायेषु हरि ऋक्षेषु हरि ईश्वर || ५-३९-२४_END
BEGIN_"O best among the monkeys! O valiant one! In the matter of monkeys and bears who are 
your helpmates, this highly great doubt is lingering before me."_END

B_5_C_40_17
BEGIN_हनूमन् सिम्ह सम्काशौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |
सुग्रीवम् च सह अमात्यम् सर्वान् ब्रूया अनामयम् || ५-४०-२२_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Enquire about the welfare of Rama and Lakshmana, the brothers looking like 
lions, of Sugreeva together with his ministers and of all other."_END

B_5_C_37_39
BEGIN_तव सत्त्वम् बलम् चैव विजानामि महाकपे |
वायोः इव गतिम् च अपि तेजः च अग्निः इव अद्भुतम् || ५-३७-४०_END
BEGIN_"O great monkey! I know fully well your courage, strength, your power of movement like 
that of the wind and your wonderful brilliance like that of the fire."_END

B_5_C_38_31
BEGIN_हिनस्तु दक्षिणाक्षित्वच्छर इत्यथ सोऽब्रवीत् || ५-३८-३६
ततः तस्य अक्षि काकस्य हिनस्ति स्म स दक्षिणम् |
दत्त्वा स दक्षिणम् नेत्रम् प्राणेभ्यः परिरक्षितः || ५-३८-३७_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, that crow said "Let your arrow shoot my right eye." Then that blade of Kusa 
grass shooted the right eye of that crow. By giving away its right eye in that way, the crow saved its 
life."_END

B_5_C_35_52
BEGIN_ततस्ते मार्गमाणा वै सुग्रीववचनातुराः |चरन्ति वसुधाम् कृत्स्नाम् वयमन्ये च वानराः || ५-३५-५५_END
BEGIN_"Then, we along with other monkeys too who are eager to fulfill the command of Sugreeva, are wandering 
the entire earth in search of you."_END

B_5_C_41_11
BEGIN_ततो महत् साश्व महारथ द्विपम् |
बलम् समानेष्व् अपि राक्षस अधिपः |
त्रिशूल काल आयस पट्टिश आयुधम् |
ततो महत् युद्धम् इदम् भविष्यति || ५-४१-१२_END
BEGIN_"Thereupon Ravana will order for an army consisting of horses, great chariots and elephants 
and armed with weapons like great tridents and spears made of iron. Then, a great combat will follow."_END

B_5_C_42_0
BEGIN_ततः पक्षि निनादेन वृक्ष भन्ग स्वनेन च |
बभूवुः त्रास सम्भ्रान्ताः सर्वे लन्का निवासिनः || ५-४२-१_END
BEGIN_At the screaming sound of birds and at the sound of the crash of falling trees, all the 
inhabitants of Lanka then became trembled with fear._END

B_5_C_39_23
BEGIN_कथम् नु खलु दुष्पारम् तरिष्यन्ति महाउदधिम् |
तानि हरि ऋक्ष सैन्यानि तौ वा नर वर आत्मजौ || ५-३९-२५_END
BEGIN_"How indeed can those troops of monkeys and bears or Rama and Lakshmana can cross that 
great insurmountable ocean?"_END

B_5_C_40_18
BEGIN_यथा च स महाबाहुः माम् तारयति राघवः |
अस्मात् दुह्ख अम्बु सम्रोधात् तत् समाधातुम् अर्हसि || ५-४०-२३_END
BEGIN_"Be pleased to make that long-armed Rama deliver me from this ocean of sorrow."_END

B_5_C_37_40
BEGIN_प्राकृतो अन्यः कथम् च इमाम् भूमिम् आगन्तुम् अर्हति |
उदधेः अप्रमेयस्य पारम् वानर पुम्गव || ५-३७-४१_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! How can any other common person cross this unfathomable ocean 
and reach this place?"_END

B_5_C_35_53
BEGIN_अन्गदो नाम लक्ष्मीवान् वालि सूनुः महाबलः |प्रस्थितः कपि शार्दूलः त्रिभाग बल सम्वृतः || 
५-३५-५६_END
BEGIN_"An excellent monkey named Angada, possessed of fortune, son of Vali and having great strength, 
taking one third of army along with him, set out in search of you."_END

B_5_C_38_32
BEGIN_स रामाय नमस्कृत्वा राज्ञे दशरथाय च |
विसृष्टस्तेन वीरेण प्रतिपेदे स्वमालयम् || ५-३८-३८_END
BEGIN_"After offering salutations to Rama and King Dasaratha and being discharged by that valiant 
Rama, the crow returned to its own abode."_END

B_5_C_41_12
BEGIN_अहम् तु तैः सम्यति चण्ड विक्रमैः |
समेत्य रक्षोभिः असम्ग विक्रमः |
निहत्य तत् रावण चोदितम् बलम् |
सुखम् गमिष्यामि कपि ईश्वर आलयम् || ५-४१-१३_END
BEGIN_"Attacking those demons of terrific prowess, I too with my unbearable prowess, will kill 
that army instigated by Ravana and return to the place of Sugreeva happily."_END

B_5_C_42_1
BEGIN_विद्रुताः च भय त्रस्ता विनेदुः मृग पक्षुणः |
रक्षसाम् च निमित्तानि क्रूराणि प्रतिपेदिरे || ५-४२-२_END
BEGIN_Made to run to-and-fro and getting frightened, beasts and birds began to scream. Atrocious 
omens made their appearance before the demons._END

B_5_C_39_24
BEGIN_त्रयाणाम् एव भूतानाम् सागरस्य इह लन्घने |
शक्तिः स्यात् वैनतेयस्य तव वा मारुतस्य वा || ५-३९-२६_END
BEGIN_"Three beings viz. Garuda the eagle, or yourself or the wind-god only have the capacity 
of crossing this ocean."_END

B_5_C_40_19
BEGIN_इमम् च तीव्रम् मम शोक वेगम् |
रक्षोभिः एभिः परिभर्त्सनम् च |
ब्रूयाः तु रामस्य गतः समीपम् |
शिवः च ते अध्वा अस्तु हरि प्रवीर || ५-४०-२४_END
BEGIN_"O valiant monkey! After approaching Rama, appraise him of this terrific gush of my grief 
and also about the threatening attitude of these female-demons. Have a happy journey!"_END

B_5_C_37_41
BEGIN_जानामि गमने शक्तिम् नयने च अपि ते मम |
अवश्यम् साम्प्रधार्य आशु कार्य सिद्धिः इह आत्मनः || ५-३७-४२_END
BEGIN_"I know your capacity of carrying and taking me from here. However, we have to determine 
soon whether the accomplishment of work by the high souled Rama would not thus get spoiled."_END

B_5_C_35_54
BEGIN_तेषाम् नो विप्रनष्टानाम् विन्ध्ये पर्वत सत्तमे |भृशम् शोक परीतनाम् अहो रात्र गणा गताः 
|| ५-३५-५७_END
BEGIN_"A number of days and nights passed, filled as we were with grief, having got lost our way intensely 
in a mountain-range called Vindhya."_END

B_5_C_38_33
BEGIN_मत् कृते काक मात्रे अपि ब्रह्म अस्त्रम् समुदीरितम् |
कस्मात् यो माम् हरत् त्वत्तः क्षमसे तम् मही पते || ५-३८-३९_END
BEGIN_"O lord of the earth! For my sake you hurled a Brahma's missile even at a crow. Why are 
you forgiving the one who has taken me away from you?"_END

B_5_C_41_13
BEGIN_ततो मारुतवत् क्रुद्धो मारुतिः भीम विक्रमः |
ऊरु वेगेन महता द्रुमान् क्षेप्तुम् अथ आरभत् || ५-४१-१४_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, Hanuma of terrific prowess, getting angry, started then to throw away trees 
by a highly violent jerk of his thighs akin to the jerk of a wind._END

B_5_C_42_2
BEGIN_ततो गतायाम् निद्रायाम् राक्षस्यो विकृत आननाः |
तत् वनम् ददृशुः भग्नम् तम् च वीरम् महाकपिम् || ५-४२-३_END
BEGIN_Then, the ugly-faced female-demons, whose sleep has vanished, found that grove demolished 
and saw that great heroic monkey._END

B_5_C_39_25
BEGIN_तत् अस्मिन् कार्य निर्योगे वीर एवम् दुरतिक्रमे |
किम् पश्यसि समाधानम् त्वम् हि कार्यविदाम् वरः || ५-३९-२७_END
BEGIN_"O valiant monkey! That is why, what strategy are you visualizing to fulfill this act, 
which is thus impassable? You are indeed excellent of those who know how to accomplish a task._END

B_5_C_40_20
BEGIN_स राज पुत्र्या प्रतिवेदित अर्थः |
कपिः कृत अर्थः परिहृष्ट चेताः |
तत् अल्प शेषम् प्रसमीक्ष्य कार्यम् |
दिशम् हि उदीचीम् मनसा जगाम || ५-४०-२५_END
BEGIN_Having been appraised of the matter by Seetha the princess, having accomplished his object, 
having his mind filled with joy and having perceived that only a little remained to be done, Hanuma 
intellectually sought the northern direction._END

B_5_C_35_55
BEGIN_ते वयम् कार्य नैराश्यात् कालस्य अतिक्रमेण च |भयाच् च कपि राजस्य प्राणान् त्यक्तुम् व्यवस्थिताः 
|| ५-३५-५८_END
BEGIN_"We were determined to forsake our lives because of despair in our non-fulfillment of work, in 
our overstepping of time-limit given by Sugreeva and in fear of the King Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_37_42
BEGIN_अयुक्तम् तु कपि श्रेष्ठ मया गन्तुम् त्वया सह |
वायु वेग सवेगस्य वेगो माम् मोहयेत् तव || ५-३७-४३_END
BEGIN_"O the faultless one! O the excellent of monkeys! It is not befitting of me to go with 
you. For, your speed resembling the winds speed, may bewilder my mind."_END

B_5_C_38_34
BEGIN_स कुरुष्व महाउत्साहम् कृपाम् मयि नर ऋषभ |
त्वया नाथवती नाथ ह्यनाथा इव दृश्यते || ५-३८-४०_END
BEGIN_"O Rama the best among men! You, with great strength, annihilate the enemy and bestow 
your mercy on me. O Lord! She who has a protector in you, actually looks like one without any protector."_END

B_5_C_41_14
BEGIN_ततः तद्त् हनुमान् वीरो बभन्ज प्रमदा वनम् |
मत्त द्विज समाघुष्टम् नाना द्रुम लता युतम् || ५-४१-१५_END
BEGIN_Then, the valiant Hanuma laid waste the royal garden attached to the gynaecium resonant 
with cries of birds in heat and endowed with various kinds of trees and creepers._END

B_5_C_42_3
BEGIN_स ता दृष्ट्व महाबाहुः महासत्त्वो महाबलः |
चकार सुमहत् रूपम् राक्षसीनाम् भय आवहम् || ५-४२-४_END
BEGIN_Seeing those female-demons, the mighty armed Hanuma endowed with a great courage and 
might, assumed a gigantic form which created a terror to the female-demons._END

B_5_C_39_26
BEGIN_कामम् अस्य त्वम् एव एकः कार्यस्य परिसाधने |
पर्याप्तः पर वीरघ्न यशस्यः ते बल उदयः || ५-३९-२८_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the annihilator of hostile enemies! You, as one alone, is capable of fulfilling 
this task. Your act of fulfilling the result is well-known."_END

B_5_C_35_56
BEGIN_विचित्य वन दुर्गाणि गिरि प्रस्रवणानि च |अनासाद्य पदम् देव्याः प्राणान् त्यक्तुम् व्यवस्थिताः 
|| ५-३५-५९_END
BEGIN_"Having searched in places difficult of access in forests, at mountains and at cascades and not 
obtaining any indication of you the princess, we were ready to give up our lives."_END

B_5_C_37_43
BEGIN_अहम् आकाशम् आसक्ता उपरि उपरि सागरम् |
प्रपतेयम् हि ते पृष्ठात् भयात् वेगेन गच्छतः || ५-३७-४४_END
BEGIN_"Reaching the sky high above the sea, I will fall down out of fear from your back even 
as you sweep with speed."_END

B_5_C_38_35
BEGIN_आनृशंस्यम् परो धर्मः त्वत्त एव मया श्रुतः |
जानामि त्वाम् महावीर्यम् महाउत्साहम् महाबलम् || ५-३८-४१
अपार पारम् अक्षोभ्यम् गाम्भीर्यात् सागर उपमम् |
भर्तारम् ससमुद्राया धरण्या वासव उपमम् || ५-३८-४२_END
BEGIN_"You yourself told me that kindness is the best righteousness. I know you, having a great 
prowess, a great energy, and a great strength. I know your non-acquiescence, imperturbability, profoundness 
like an ocean, as Lord of the earth including the oceans and as equal to Indra the Lord of celestials."_END

B_5_C_41_15
BEGIN_तत् वनम् मथितैः वृक्षैः भिन्नैः च सलिल आशयैः |
चूर्णितैः पर्वत अग्रैः च बभूव अप्रिय दर्शनम् || ५-४१-१६_END
BEGIN_Hanuma damaged trees in that grove, destroyed the ponds and crushed the tops of pleasure 
hills to powder. Thus, that grove became nasty at sight._END

B_5_C_42_4
BEGIN_ततः तम् गिरि सम्काशम् अतिकायम् महाबलम् |
राक्षस्यो वानरम् दृष्ट्वा पप्रच्छुः जनक आत्मजाम् || ५-४२-५_END
BEGIN_Beholding that mighty monkey having a gigantic body similar to a mountain, the female-demons 
then asked Seetha (as follows):_END

B_5_C_39_27
BEGIN_बलैः समग्रैः यदि माम् रावणम् जित्य सम्युगे |
विजयी स्व पुरम् यायात् तत् तु मे स्यात् यशः करम् || ५-३९-२९_END
BEGIN_"If Rama defeats Ravana with his entire army in battle and as a champion takes me back 
to his own city, it will be quite worthy of him."_END

B_5_C_35_57
BEGIN_दृष्ट्वा प्रायोपविष्टांश्च सर्वान्वानरपुङ्गवान् |भृशम् शोक अर्णवे मग्नः पर्यदेवयत् अन्गदः 
|| ५-३५-६०तव नाशम् च वैदेहि वालिनः च तथा वधम् |प्राय उपवेशम् अस्माकम् मरणम् च जटायुषः || ५-३५-६१_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Seeing all the excellent monkeys sitting down and calmly awaiting for the approach of 
death, Angada was very much immerssed in the ocean of sorrow and lamented about your loss, the killing of Vali, 
the death of Jatayu and our practice of calmly awaiting for the approach of death in simply sitting down."_END

B_5_C_38_36
BEGIN_एवम् अस्त्रविदाम् श्रेष्ठः सत्त्ववान् बलवान् अपि |
किम् अर्थम् अस्त्रम् रक्षह्सु न योजयसि राघव || ५-३८-४३_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! Eventhough you are strong, excellently skilled in archery and a truthful man, 
why are you not utilizing your arrow on demons?"_END

B_5_C_37_44
BEGIN_पतिता सागरे च अहम् तिमि नक्र झष आकुले |
भयेयम् आशु विवशा यादसाम् अन्नम् उत्तमम् || ५-३७-४५_END
BEGIN_"Having fallen insensible into the sea, which is filled with sharks, crocodiles and giant 
fish, I may become the best food soon for the aquatic creatures."_END

B_5_C_41_16
BEGIN_नानाशकुन्तविरुतैः प्रभिन्नैः सलिलाशयैः |
ताम्रैः किलसयैः क्लान्तैः क्लान्तद्रुमलतायितम् || ५-४१-१७
न बभौ तद्वनम् तत्र दावानलहतम् यथा |
व्याकुलावरणा रेजुर्विह्वला इव ता लताः || ५-४१-१८_END
BEGIN_With its trees and creepers dried up, with the howls of various birds, with its ponds 
destroyed, with its copper-coloured sprouts dried up there, that grove did not look bright, as though 
it had been destroyed by a wild fire. Those creepers with their bars of support displaced, fell down 
like distressed woman._END

B_5_C_42_5
BEGIN_को अयम् कस्य कुतो वा अयम् किम् निमित्तम् इह आगतः |
कथम् त्वया सह अनेन सम्वादः कृत इति उत || ५-४२-६_END
BEGIN_"Who is he? Whose messenger is he? From where and for what purpose he has come here? 
Wherefore a conversation was held by him with you?"_END

B_5_C_39_28
BEGIN_शरैस्तु सम्कुलाम् कृत्वा लन्काम् पर बल अर्दनः |
माम् नयेत् यदि काकुत्स्थः तत् तस्य सदृशम् भवेत् || ५-३९-३०_END
BEGIN_"If Rama, the destroyer of rival army, fills the entire Lanka with his arrows and takes 
me home, it will be quite worthy of him."_END

B_5_C_35_58
BEGIN_तेषाम् नः स्वामि संदेशान् निराशानाम् मुमूर्षताम् |कार्य हेतोः इव आयातः शकुनिः वीर्यवान् 
महान् || ५-३५-६२_END
BEGIN_"For us who lost all our hopes on our lives and willing to give up our lives as per the command 
of Sugreeva, as though for the sake of our need alone, a great valiant bird came there."_END

B_5_C_38_37
BEGIN_न नागा न अपि गन्धर्वा न असुरा न मरुत् गणाः |
रामस्य समरे वेगम् शक्ताः प्रति समाधितुम् || ५-३८-४४_END
BEGIN_"Neither the serpent-demons, nor the divine musicians nor the demons nor the storm-gods 
are able to resist the onrush of Rama in battle."_END

B_5_C_37_45
BEGIN_न च शक्ष्ये त्वया सार्धम् गन्तुम् शत्रु विनाशन |
कलत्रवति संदेहः त्वयि अपि स्यात् असंशयम् || ५-३७-४६_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the annihilator of enemies! It is not possible for me to go with you. There 
will also be a risk for you, having me a lady additionally to protect. There is no doubt."_END

B_5_C_41_17
BEGIN_लता गृहैः चित्र गृहैः च नाशितैः |
महाउरगैः व्याल मृगैः च निर्धुतैः |
शिला गृहैः उन्मथितैः तथा गृहैः |
प्रनष्ट रूपम् तत् अभून् महत् वनम् || ५-४१-१९_END
BEGIN_"With its arbours and picture-galleries destroyed, its great serpents and wild animals 
emitting cries of distress, its grottos and other structures demolished, that grove became defaced._END

B_5_C_42_6
BEGIN_आचक्ष्व नो विशाल अक्षि मा भूत् ते सुभगे भयम् |
सम्वादम् असित अपान्गे त्वया किम् कृतवान् अयम् || ५-४२-७_END
BEGIN_"O large-eyed Seetha! Tell us. Let there be no fear for you, O fortunate lady! What did 
he speak to you? O lady having black outer eye-corners!"_END

B_5_C_39_29
BEGIN_तत् यथा तस्य विक्रान्तम् अनुरूपम् महात्मनः |
भवेत् आहव शूरस्य तथा त्वम् उपपादय || ५-३९-३१_END
BEGIN_"For that reason, you act in such a way, that Rama the high-souled man, valiant in battle, 
may exhibit the prowess befitting of him."_END

B_5_C_35_59
BEGIN_गृध्र राजस्य सोदर्यः सम्पातिः नाम गृध्र राट् |श्रुत्वा भ्रातृ वधम् कोपात् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ५-३५-६३_END
BEGIN_"Hearing about the killing of his brother, the vulture-king Sampati the brother of slain Jatayu 
the King of vultures spoke (the following) words in anger:_END

B_5_C_38_38
BEGIN_तस्या वीर्यवतः कश्चित् यदि अस्ति मयि सम्भ्रमः |
किम् अर्थम् न शरैः तीक्ष्णैः क्षयम् नयति राक्षसान् || ५-३८-४५_END
BEGIN_"If the valiant Rama has any haste in my case, why does he not destroy the demons with 
his sharp arrows?!_END

B_5_C_37_46
BEGIN_ह्रियमाणाम् तु माम् दृष्ट्वा राक्षसा भीम विक्रमाः |
अनुगच्छेयुः आदिष्टा रावणेन दुरात्मना || ५-३७-४७_END
BEGIN_"Seeing me being taken away by you, the demons of terrific prowess, incited by the evil-minded 
Ravana, will follow you."_END

B_5_C_42_7
BEGIN_अथ अब्रवीत् तदा साध्वी सीता सर्व अन्ग शोभना |
रक्षसाम् काम रूपाणाम् विज्ञाने मम का गतिः || ५-४२-८_END
BEGIN_Thereupon Seetha the virtuous lady, having a complete beauty of all limbs, spoke as follows: 
"Where is the ability for me to know about the demons of a terrific form?"_END

B_5_C_41_18
BEGIN_साविह्वलाऽशोकलताप्रताना |
वनस्थली शोकलताप्रताना |
जाता दशास्यप्रमदावनस्य |
कपेर्बलाद्धि प्रमदावनस्य || ५-४१-२०_END
BEGIN_"That woody land of that pleasure-garden which afforded shelter to the women-folk of 
Ravana and which has clusters of Ashoka creepers became a jumble of creepers of sorrow for the distressed 
women; by the violence of Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_39_30
BEGIN_तत् अर्थ उपहितम् वाक्यम् सहितम् हेतु सम्हितम् |
निशम्य हनुमान् शेषम् वाक्यम् उत्तरम् अब्रवीत् || ५-३९-३२_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words, which were meaningful humble and attended with reason, Hanuma gave 
his final reply (as follows)_END

B_5_C_35_60
BEGIN_यवीयान् केन मे भ्राता हतः क्व च विनाशितः |एतत् आख्यातुम् इच्छामि भवद्भिः वानर उत्तमाः 
|| ५-३५-६४_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! Tell me who, where and how my younger brother Jabali was killed and made 
to fall."_END

B_5_C_38_39
BEGIN_भ्रातुः आदेशम् आदाय लक्ष्मणो वा परम् तपः |
कस्य हेतोः न माम् वीरः परित्राति महाबलः || ५-३८-४६_END
BEGIN_"For what reason, even Lakshmana the tormentator of enemies, the mighty man and the valiant 
man does not protect me, by taking the command of his elder brother?'_END

B_5_C_37_47
BEGIN_तैः त्वम् परिवृतः शूरैः शूलम् उद्गर पाणिभिः |
भवेः त्वम् संशयम् प्राप्तो मया वीर कलत्रवान् || ५-३७-४८_END
BEGIN_"O brave monkey! Those valiant demons wielding darts and clubs in their hands will surround 
you. Accompanied by a lady in me, you will be at a risk."_END

B_5_C_42_8
BEGIN_यूयम् एव अस्य जानीत यो अयम् यत् वा करिष्यति |
अहिः एव अहेः पादान् विजानाति न संशयः || ५-४२-९_END
BEGIN_"You alone can recognise who he is and what he does. A serpent only can recognise the 
feet of another serpent. There is no doubt about it."_END

B_5_C_41_19
BEGIN_स तस्य कृत्वा जगतीपतेर्महा |
न्महत् व्यलीकम् मनसो महात्मनः |
युयुत्सुः एको बहुभिः महाबलैः |
श्रिया ज्वलन् तोरणम् आश्रितः कपिः || ५-४१-२१_END
BEGIN_Creating a great displeasure to the mind of that high-souled Ravana, the Lord of the 
land of Lanka; that Hanuma decided to fight alone against many mighty demons and stayed_END

B_5_C_39_31
BEGIN_देवि हरि ऋक्ष सैन्यानाम् ईश्वरः प्लवताम् वरः |
सुग्रीवः सत्त्व सम्पन्नः तव अर्थे कृत निश्चयः || ५-३९-३३_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! Sugreeva, the Lord of the troops of monkeys and bears and the 
premost among the monkeys, who is endowed with strength, is firmly determined in your cause."_END

B_5_C_35_61
BEGIN_अन्गदो अकथयत् तस्य जन स्थाने महत् वधम् |रक्षसा भीम रूपेण त्वाम् उद्दिश्य यथा तथम् || ५-३५-६५_END
BEGIN_"Then, Angada told Sampati a detailed account of events which led tot he killing of that great 
bird at Janasthana, by a demon of terrific form, for your sake."_END

B_5_C_38_40
BEGIN_यदि तौ पुरुष व्याघ्रौ वाय्व् इन्द्र सम तेजसौ |
सुराणाम् अपि दुर्धर्षो किम् अर्थम् माम् उपेक्षतः || ५-३८-४७_END
BEGIN_Those two tigers among men, Rama and Lakshmana, with a sharpness equal to that of wind 
and fire, even if they are unconquerable by demons too, why are they neglecting me?"_END

B_5_C_37_48
BEGIN_सायुधा बहवो व्योम्नि राक्षसाः त्वम् निरायुधः |
कथम् शक्ष्यसि सम्यातुम् माम् चैव परिरक्षितुम् || ५-३७-४९_END
BEGIN_"Many demons will come with their weapons, in the sky. You will be alone without any 
weapon. How can you continue your travel, while protecting me?"_END

B_5_C_42_9
BEGIN_अहम् अपि अस्य भीता अस्मि न एनम् जानामि को अन्वयम् |
वेद्मि राक्षसम् एव एनम् काम रूपिणम् आगतम् || ५-४२-१०_END
BEGIN_"By seeing him, I too get frightened. I do not know who he is. I only know him as a demon, 
able to assume any form at his will, who arrived here."_END

B_5_C_39_32
BEGIN_स वानर सहस्राणाम् कोटीभिः अभिसम्वृतः |
क्षिप्रम् एष्यति वैदेहि राक्षसानाम् निबर्हणः || ५-३९-३४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! That Sugreeva, endowed with thousands and crores of monkeys, will come soon 
to destroy the demons."_END

B_5_C_35_62
BEGIN_जटायोः तु वधम् श्रुत्वा दुह्हितः सो अरुण आत्मजः |त्वाम् आह स वर आरोहे वसन्तीम् रावण आलये 
|| ५-३५-६६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with an excellent waist! Hearing about the slaughter of Jatayu, that Sampati the son 
of Aruna was very much pained and said that you were staying in Ravana's house."_END

B_5_C_38_41
BEGIN_मम एव दुष्कृतम् किंचिन् महत् अस्ति न संशयः |
समर्थाव् अपि तौ यन् माम् न अवेक्षेते परम् तपौ || ५-३८-४८_END
BEGIN_"There is not doubt that I would have committed a great sin, for which reason those two 
brothers Rama and Lakshmana the tormentators of enemies, even when capable , are neglecting me."_END

B_5_C_37_49
BEGIN_युध्यमानस्य रक्षोभिः ततः तैः क्रूर कर्मभिः |
प्रपतेयम् हि ते पृष्ठत् भय आर्ता कपि सत्तम || ५-३७-५०_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! While you will be resorting to battle with those demons, who 
perform cruel acts, I, stricken with fear, may fall down from your back."_END

B_5_C_42_10
BEGIN_वैदेह्या वचनम् श्रुत्वा राक्षस्यो विद्रुता द्रुतम् |
स्थिताः काश्चित् गताः काश्चित् रावणाय निवेदितुम् || ५-४२-११_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Seetha some female-demons fled to different directions. Some stayed 
back. Some others went to Ravana to inform about the matter._END

B_5_C_39_33
BEGIN_तस्य विक्रम सम्पन्नाः सत्त्ववन्तो महाबलाः |
मनः सम्कल्प सम्पाता निदेशे हरयः स्थिताः || ५-३९-३५_END
BEGIN_"So many monkeys, endowed with prowess, perseverance, great strength and who can rush 
to any place as they wish are intensely committed to Sugreeva's command._END

B_5_C_43_0
BEGIN_ततः स किम्करान् हत्वा हनूमान् ध्यानम् आस्थितः |
वनम् भग्नम् मया चैत्य प्रासादो न विनाशितः || ५-४३-१
तस्मात् प्रासादम् अपि एवम् इमम् विध्वंसयामि अहम् |
इति संचिन्त्य हनुमान् मनसा दर्शयन् बलम् || ५-४३-२
चैत्य प्रासादम् आप्लुत्य मेरु शृन्गम् इव उन्नतम् |
आरुरोह हरि श्रेष्ठो हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४३-३_END
BEGIN_After killing the Kinkaras, that Hanuma thought to himself (as follows): "The grove was 
damaged by me. The lofty palatial mansion of the sanctuary (sacred to the guardian-deity of the demons) 
has not been destroyed. For that reason, I will cause this mansion to crumble down in the same way." 
Thus thinking himself, Hanuma the best among monkeys, son of the wind-god having large jaws, by showing 
his strength, bounced up and ascended the lofty palatial mansion of the sanctuary, which was as high 
as a mountain-top of Meru._END

B_5_C_35_63
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा सम्पातेः प्रीति वर्धनम् |अन्गद प्रमुखाः सर्वे ततः सम्प्रस्थिता 
वयम् || ५-३५-६७_END
BEGIN_"Hearing those delightful words of Sampati, we with our Chief Angada started soon from there."_END

B_5_C_38_42
BEGIN_वैदेह्या वचनम् श्रुत्वा करुणम् साशुभाषितम् |
अथाब्रवीन्महातेजा हनुमान् मारुतात्मजः || ५-३८-४९_END
BEGIN_Hearing the pitiable appeal Seetha with tears, Hanuma of great splendour and the son 
of wind-god spoke (as follows)_END

B_5_C_37_50
BEGIN_अथ रक्षांसि भीमानि महान्ति बलवन्ति च |
कथंचित् साम्पराये त्वाम् जयेयुः कपि सत्तम || ५-३७-५१_END
BEGIN_"O excellent of monkeys! Then the powerful and terrific demons with their giant bodies 
will conquer you in battle, somehow or other."_END

B_5_C_42_11
BEGIN_रावणस्य समीपे तु राक्षस्यो विकृत आननाः |
विरूपम् वानरम् भीमम् आख्यतुम् उपचक्रमुः || ५-४२-१२_END
BEGIN_After approaching Ravana, the female demons of ugly faces started to tell (as follows) 
of the monstrous and terrific monkey._END

B_5_C_39_34
BEGIN_येषाम् न उपरि न अधस्तान् न तिर्यक् सज्जते गतिः |
न च कर्मसु सीदन्ति महत्स्व् अमित तेजसः || ५-३९-३६_END
BEGIN_"There is no hindrance to their movement either in the sky or in the ground or in any 
horizontal region (between the sky and the ground) with unlimited splendour are not indolent in performing 
any great task."_END

B_5_C_43_1
BEGIN_आरुह्य गिरिसम्काशम् प्रासादम् हरियूथपः |
बभौ स सुमहातेजाः प्रतिसूर्य इवोदितः || ५-४३-४_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, an army-chief of monkeys, possessing a very great splendour, ascending the 
lofty palatial mansion similar to a mountain shone like a second rising sun._END

B_5_C_35_64
BEGIN_विन्ध्यादुत्थाय सम्प्राप्ताः सागरस्यान्तमुत्तरम् |त्वत् दर्शन कृत उत्साहा हृष्टाः तुष्टाः 
प्लवम्गमाः || ५-३५-६८_END
BEGIN_"The monkeys were very much delighted and satisfied. They were making up their energy to see you, 
rose up from Vindhya mountain and reached the northern shore of the ocean."_END

B_5_C_38_43
BEGIN_त्वच्छोकविमुखो रामो देवि सत्येन ते शपे |
रामे दुःखाभिपन्ने च लक्ष्मणः परितप्यते || ५-३८-५०_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! Rama has grown averse to everything else, caused by grief towards you. I swear 
it to you by truth. When Rama is overpowered by grief; Lakshmana too gets tormented by grief."_END

B_5_C_37_51
BEGIN_अथवा युध्यमानस्य पतेयम् विमुखस्य ते |
पतिताम् च गृहीत्वा माम् नयेयुः पाप राक्षसाः || ५-३७-५२_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise, if you are indifferent of me and resort to battle, I may eventually fall 
down. Then, the wicked demons, catching hold of me fallen, may take me again to Lanka."_END

B_5_C_42_12
BEGIN_अशोक वनिका मध्ये राजन् भीम वपुः कपिः |
सीतया कृत सम्वादः तिष्ठति अमित विक्रमः || ५-४२-१३_END
BEGIN_"O king! A monkey having a terrific body and a boundless prowess, is stationed in the 
middle of Ashoka grove and made a conversation with Seetha."_END

B_5_C_39_35
BEGIN_असकृत् तैः महाउत्सहैः ससागर धरा धरा |
प्रदक्षिणी कृता भूमिः वायु मार्ग अनुसारिभिः || ५-३९-३७_END
BEGIN_"The earth with its oceans and mountains has been circumambulated clockwise many times 
by those monkeys, who are highly energetic and who follow the aerial path."_END

B_5_C_43_2
BEGIN_सम्प्रधृष्य च दुर्धर्षः चैत्य प्रासादम् उन्नतम् |
हनूमान् प्रज्वलम्ल् लक्ष्म्या पारियात्रा उपमो अभवत् || ५-४३-५_END
BEGIN_Overpowering the lofty and inviolable of the sanctuary, Hanuma blazing mansion his splendour, 
meta morposed into a towering sized body equal to that of Pariyatra mountain._END

B_5_C_35_65
BEGIN_अङ्गदप्रमुखाः सर्वे वेलोपान्तमुपस्थिताः |चिन्ताम् जग्मुः पुनर्भीतास्त्वद्दर्शनसमुत्सुकाः 
|| ५-३५-६९_END
BEGIN_"All the monkeys with their Chief Angada, in their anxiety to see you, reached the ocean. They 
were frightened after seeing the ocean there and they were again worried."_END

B_5_C_38_44
BEGIN_कथम् चिद्भवती दृष्टा न कालः परिदेवितुम् |
इमम् मुहूर्तम् दुःखानाम् द्रक्ष्यस्यन्तमनिन्दिते || ५-३८-५१_END
BEGIN_"O faultless Seetha! Somehow or other, you have been discovered by me. This is not the 
time to lament. Your will see the end of your sorrow within a short time."_END

B_5_C_37_52
BEGIN_माम् वा हरेयुः त्वद्त् हस्तात् विशसेयुः अथ अपि वा |
अव्यवस्थौ हि दृश्येते युद्धे जय पराजयौ || ५-३७-५३_END
BEGIN_"Or they may take me away from your hand, or may even kill me. In battle, victory and 
defeat are perceived as uncertain."_END

B_5_C_39_36
BEGIN_मत् विशिष्टाः च तुल्याः च सन्ति तत्र वन ओकसः |
मत्तः प्रत्यवरः कश्चिन् न अस्ति सुग्रीव सम्निधौ || ५-३९-३८_END
BEGIN_"In them, some of the monkeys are superior to me and some are even equal to me. No one 
in the vicinity of Sugreeva is inferior to me."_END

B_5_C_42_13
BEGIN_न च तम् जानकी सीता हरिम् हरिण लोचणा |
अस्माभिः बहुधा पृष्टा निवेदयितुम् इच्छति || ५-४२-१४_END
BEGIN_"Eventhough questioned in many ways by us, Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, having eyes 
similar to those of a doe, is not inclined to tell about the monkey."_END

B_5_C_43_3
BEGIN_स भूत्वा तु महाकायो हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
धृष्टम् आस्फोटयामास लन्काम् शब्देन पूरयन् || ५-४३-६_END
BEGIN_Enhancing his body to a very big size by dint of his distinction, Hanuma clapped on his 
arms strongly, filling the City of Lanka with sound._END

B_5_C_35_66
BEGIN_अथ अहम् हरि सैन्यस्य सागरम् दृश्य सीदतः |व्यवधूय भयम् तीव्रम् योजनानाम् शतम् प्लुतः || 
५-३५-७०_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, seeing the ocean, I removed the serious fears of the army of monkeys who were worrying 
and crossed hundred Yojanas across the sea."_END

B_5_C_38_45
BEGIN_तावुभौ पुरुषव्याघ्रौ राजपुत्रौ महाबलौ |
त्वद्दर्शनकृतोत्साहौ लङ्काम् भस्मीकरिष्यतः || ५-३८-५२_END
BEGIN_"Those two mighty princes, the excellent among men, are eager to see you and they will 
reduce Lanka to ashes."_END

B_5_C_37_53
BEGIN_अहम् वा अपि विपद्येयम् रक्षोभिः अभितर्जिता |
त्वत् प्रयत्नो हरि श्रेष्ठ भवेन् निष्फल एव तु || ५-३७-५४_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! Or while I am frightened by the demons, I may get into a mishap. 
Thus, your effort may become futile indeed!"_END

B_5_C_42_14
BEGIN_वासवस्य भवेत् दूतो दूतो वैश्रवणस्य वा |
प्रेषितो वा अपि रामेण सीता अन्वेषण कान्क्षया || ५-४२-१५_END
BEGIN_"He may be a messenger of Indra the Lord of celestials, or the messenger of Kubera the 
king of riches or even a messenger sent by Rama to search for Seetha."_END

B_5_C_39_37
BEGIN_अहम् तावत् इह प्राप्तः किम् पुनः ते महाबलाः |
न हि प्रकृष्टाः प्रेष्यन्ते प्रेष्यन्ते हि इतरे जनाः || ५-३९-३९_END
BEGIN_"When I have arrived here, why to talk about the mighty ones? Generally, superior ones 
are not sent for errands. Only others are indeed sent."_END

B_5_C_43_4
BEGIN_तस्य आस्फोटित शब्देन महता श्रोत्र घातिना |
पेतुर्विहङ्गमास्तत्र चैत्यपालाश्च मोहिताः || ५-४३-७_END
BEGIN_By the great deafening noise, made by clapping on his arms, the birds and also the guards 
protecting the sanctuary unconsciously fell down._END

B_5_C_35_67
BEGIN_लन्का च अपि मया रात्रौ प्रविष्टा राक्षस आकुला |रावणः च मया दृष्टः त्वम् च शोक निपीडिता 
|| ५-३५-७१_END
BEGIN_"Entering even Lanka, filled with demons in the night, I saw Ravana and you too who were immersed 
in grief."_END

B_5_C_38_46
BEGIN_हत्वा च समरे क्रूतम् रावणम् सहबान्धवम् |
राघवस्त्वाम् विशालाक्षि नेष्यति स्वाम् पुरीम् प्रति || ५-३८-५३_END
BEGIN_"O large-eyed Seetha! Killing the cruel Ravana along with his relatives in battle, Rama 
will take you back to his own city."_END

B_5_C_37_54
BEGIN_कामम् त्वम् अपि पर्याप्तो निहन्तुम् सर्व राक्षसान् |
राघवस्य यशो हीयेत् त्वया शस्तैः तु राक्षसैः || ५-३७-५५_END
BEGIN_"You may be surely able to kill all the demons. But if you alone kill all the demons, 
Rama's celebrity will be lowered."_END

B_5_C_42_15
BEGIN_तेन त्वत् भूत रूपेण यत् तत् तव मनो हरम् |
नाना मृग गण आकीर्णम् प्रमृष्टम् प्रमदा वनम् || ५-४२-१६_END
BEGIN_"He, having a wonderful form, has wiped off your grove, attached to the gynaecium, which 
is fascinating and extending with many kinds of animal-flock."_END

B_5_C_39_38
BEGIN_तत् अलम् परितापेन देवि शोको व्यपैतु ते |
एक उत्पातेन ते लन्काम् एष्यन्ति हरि यूथपाः || ५-३९-४०_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! Enough of your lamentation. Take away your sorrow. Those leaders 
of monkeys will reach Lanka by one single leap."_END

B_5_C_43_5
BEGIN_अस्त्रविज्जयताम् रामो लक्ष्मणः च महाबलः |
राजा जयति सुग्रीवो राघवेन अभिपालितः || ५-४३-८
दासो अहम् कोसल इन्द्रस्य रामस्य अक्लिष्ट कर्मणः |
हनुमान् शत्रु सैन्यानाम् निहन्ता मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४३-९
न रावण सहस्रम् मे युद्धे प्रतिबलम् भवेत् |
शिलाभिः तु प्रहरतः पादपैः च सहस्रशः || ५-४३-१०
अर्दयित्वा पुरीम् लन्काम् अभिवाद्य च मैथिलीम् |
समृद्ध अर्थो गमिष्यामि मिषताम् सर्व रक्षसाम् || ५-४३-११_END
BEGIN_"Long live Rama, skilled in archery and the powerful Lakshmana! Long lie the King Sugreeva, 
protected by Rama! I am Hanuma, the destroyer of the army of adversaries and the son of wind-god. I 
am the servent of Rama, the king of Kosala kingdom, who is unwearied in action. Even a thousand of Ravanas 
will not be matching equally with me, who is capable of striking with thousnads of rocks and trees in 
battle. Here, before the eyes of all the demons, I will annihilate the City of Lanka and after offering 
salutation to Seetha, I will go back duly completing my task."_END

B_5_C_35_68
BEGIN_एतत् ते सर्वम् आख्यातम् यथा वृत्तम् अनिन्दिते |अभिभाषस्व माम् देवि दूतो दाशरथेः अहम् || 
५-३५-७२_END
BEGIN_"O the faultless princess! I told you all this as actually occurred. I am the messenger of Rama. 
Talk to me."_END

B_5_C_38_47
BEGIN_ब्रूहि यद्राघवो वाच्यो लक्ष्मणश्च महाबलः |
सुग्रीवो वापि तेजस्वी हरयोऽपि समागताः || ५-३८-५४_END
BEGIN_"Tell me what to be expressed to Rama or to the mighty Lakshmana or to the splendourous 
Sugreeva or even to the other monkeys assembled there."_END

B_5_C_37_55
BEGIN_अथवा आदाय रक्षांसि न्यस्येयुः सम्वृते हि माम् |
यत्र ते न अभिजानीयुः हरयो न अपि राघवः || ५-३७-५६_END
BEGIN_"Otherwise, the demons may take me away and hide me in any secret place that will not 
be known by those monkeys or even Rama and Lakshmana."_END

B_5_C_42_16
BEGIN_न तत्र कश्चित् उद्देशो यः तेन न विनाशितः |
यत्र सा जानकी सीता स तेन न विनाशितः || ५-४२-१७_END
BEGIN_"There is no place whatsoever in that grove, which was not destroyed by him. Only that
