place, where Seetha the daughter of Janaka was sitting, was not destroyed by him."_END

B_5_C_39_39
BEGIN_मम पृष्ठ गतौ तौ च चन्द्र सूर्याव् इव उदितौ |
त्वत् सकाशम् महासत्त्वौ नृसिम्हाव् आगमिष्यतः || ५-३९-४१_END
BEGIN_"Rama and Lakshmana, those two lions among men also of great strength, ascending on my 
shoulders, can come to you, like the rising sun and the moon."_END

B_5_C_38_48
BEGIN_इत्युक्तवति तस्मिंस्तु सीता सुरसुतोपमा |
उवाच शोकसंतप्ता हनुमन्तं प्लवंगमम् || ५-३८-५५_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Hanuma, Seetha, like the daughter of a sage, tormented with grief, 
spoke to Hanuma the monkey (as follows):_END

B_5_C_43_6
BEGIN_एवम् उक्त्वा विमानस्थः चैत्यस्थान् हरि पुम्गवः |
ननाद भीम निर्ह्रादो रक्षसाम् जनयन् भयम् || ५-४३-१२_END
BEGIN_Thus uttering to those guards protecting the sanctuary, roared terribly, making a noise 
and creating a terror to the demons._END

B_5_C_35_69
BEGIN_त्वम् माम् राम कृत उद्योगम् त्वन् निमित्तम् इह आगतम् |सुग्रीव सचिवम् देवि बुध्यस्व पवन 
आत्मजम् || ५-३५-७३_END
BEGIN_"O princess! I made an effort on Rama's behalf and came here for your sake. I am Sugreeva's minister. 
I am the son of wind-god. Know me, as such."_END

B_5_C_42_17
BEGIN_जानकी रक्षण अर्थम् वा श्रमात् वा न उपलभ्यते |
अथवा कः श्रमः तस्य सा एव तेन अभिरक्षिता || ५-४२-१८_END
BEGIN_"It is not known whether to protect Seetha or because of fatigue, he has left that place 
undestroyed, or else, what fatigue is there for him? He has done it to protect Seetha."_END

B_5_C_37_56
BEGIN_आरम्भः तु मत् अर्थो अयम् ततः तव निरर्थकः |
त्वया हि सह रामस्य महान् आगमने गुणः || ५-३७-५७_END
BEGIN_"Then your effort taken for my sake will become futile. That is why there is a great 
merit in Rama's coming here along with you."_END

B_5_C_39_40
BEGIN_तौ हि वीरौ नर वरौ सहितौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |
आगम्य नगरीम् लन्काम् सायकैः विधमिष्यतः || ५-३९-४२_END
BEGIN_"Coming together, Rama and Lakshmana the valiant and the excellent among men, can destroy 
the City of Lanka with their arrows."_END

B_5_C_44_0
BEGIN_संदिष्टो राक्षस इन्द्रेण प्रहस्तस्य सुतो बली |
जम्बु माली महादम्ष्ट्रो निर्जगाम धनुः धरः || ५-४४-१
रक्त माल्य अम्बर धरः स्रग्वी रुचिर कुण्डलः |
महान् विवृत्त नयनः चण्डः समर दुर्जयः || ५-४४-२
धनुः शक्र धनुः प्रख्यम् महत् रुचिर सायकम् |
विस्फारयाणो वेगेन वज्र अशनि सम स्वनम् || ५-४४-३_END
BEGIN_Jambumali, the demon with great tusks, wielding a bow, donning crimson garlands and clothes, 
wearing beautiful chaplet and charming ear-rings, possessing a gigantic body, having round and open 
eyes, the demon causing diseases, unconquerable in battle, a strong demon and the son of Prahasta, commanded 
by Ravana, started stretching with rashness his big bow resembling a rain bow garnished splendorous 
arrows and which brilliance was similar to that of a lightening and produced a sound like that of a 
thunder._END

B_5_C_38_49
BEGIN_कौसल्या लोक भर्तारम् सुषुवे यम् मनस्विनी |
तम् मम अर्थे सुखम् पृच्छ शिरसा च अभिवादय || ५-३८-५६_END
BEGIN_"On my behalf, salute by bowing your head and ask about the welfare of Rama, the Lord 
of the worlds, whom the magnanimous Kausalya gave birth."_END

B_5_C_43_7
BEGIN_तेन शब्देन महता चैत्य पालाः शतम् ययुः |
गृहीत्वा विविधान् अस्त्रान् प्रासान् खड्गान् परश्वधान् || ५-४३-१३
विसृजन्तो महाक्सया मारुतिम् पर्यवारयन् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing that loud noise, hundreds of guards protecting the sanctuary went, taking many 
kinds of weapons, spears, swords and axes. Those Kinkaras with huge bodies surrounded Hanuma, duly discharging 
those weapons._END

B_5_C_35_70
BEGIN_कुशली तव काकुत्स्थः सर्व शस्त्रभृताम् वरः |गुरोः आराधने युक्तो लक्ष्मणः च सुलक्षणः || 
५-३५-७४_END
BEGIN_"You Rama, the excellent man among all the wielders of bow, is safe. Lakshmana, who is engaged 
in the service of his elder brother and possessing good characteristics, is also safe."_END

B_5_C_42_18
BEGIN_चारु पल्लव पत्र आढ्यम् यम् सीता स्वयम् आस्थिता |
प्रवृद्धः शिंशपा वृक्षः स च तेन अभिरक्षितः || ५-४२-१९_END
BEGIN_"That well-grown Simsupa tree, abounding in charming sprouts and flowers, under which 
Seetha herself took shelter, has been spared by him."_END

B_5_C_37_57
BEGIN_मयि जीवितम् आयत्तम् राघवस्य महात्मनः |
भ्रातृऋणाम् च महाबाहो तव राज कुलस्य च || ५-३७-५८_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the long-armed! The survival of the high souled Rama, his brothers, of yourself 
and of your royal family (of Sugreeva) is dependent on me."_END

B_5_C_39_41
BEGIN_सगणम् रावणम् हत्वा राघवो रघु नन्दनः |
त्वाम् आदाय वर आरोहे स्व पुरम् प्रतियास्यति || ५-३९-४३_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha with a good waist! Rama, the delight of Raghu dynasty, killing Ravana together 
with his troops, will return to his town, duly taking you with him."_END

B_5_C_44_1
BEGIN_तस्य विस्फार घोषेण धनुषो महता दिशः |
प्रदिशः च नभः चैव सहसा समपूर्यत || ५-४४-४_END
BEGIN_The tumultuous sound created out of the twanging of that bow, soon filled up the quarters, 
intermediate points and the sky._END

B_5_C_38_50
BEGIN_स्रजः च सर्व रत्नानि प्रिया याः च वर अन्गनाः |
ऐश्वर्यम् च विशालायाम् पृथिव्याम् अपि दुर्लभम् || ५-३८-५७
पितरम् मातरम् चैव सम्मान्य अभिप्रसाद्य च |
अनुप्रव्रजितो रामम् सुमित्रा येन सुप्रजाः || ५-३८-५८_END
BEGIN_(On my behalf, ask about the welfare of ) Lakshmana, that good child of Sumitra who, 
having renounced the wreaths of flowers, all the riches, pleasant and beautiful girls and even the prosperity 
difficult to be obtained in this extensive world, offered his profound respects to and pacified his 
father and mother, followed Rama to exile."_END

B_5_C_43_8
BEGIN_ते गदाभिर्विचित्राभिः परिघैः काञ्चनाङ्गदैः || ५-४३-१४
अजघ्नर्वानरश्रेष्ठं शरैश्चादित्यसन्निभैः |
आवर्त इव गन्गायाः तोयस्य विपुलो महान् || ५-४३-१५
परिक्षिप्य हरि श्रेष्ठम् स बभौ रक्षसाम् गणः |_END
BEGIN_They banged Hanuma with various kinds of maces, iron bludgeons plated with gold and arrows 
shining like the sun. That troop of demons surrounding Hanuma the best among monkeys, shone like a greatly 
extensive whirlpool in the waters of River Ganga._END

B_5_C_35_71
BEGIN_तस्य वीर्यवतो देवि भर्तुः तव हिते रतः |अहम् एकः तु सम्प्राप्तः सुग्रीव वचनात् इह || ५-३५-७५_END
BEGIN_"O princess! I, who am interested in the welfare of the valiant Rama, your husband, came here alone 
on the command of Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_42_19
BEGIN_तस्य उग्र रूपस्य उग्रम् त्वम् दण्डम् आज्ञातुम् अर्हसि |
सीता सम्भाषिता येन तत् वनम् च विनाशितम् || ५-४२-२०_END
BEGIN_To that terribly looking monkey by whom Seetha was spoken to and that grove destroyed you to order a terrible punishment._END

B_5_C_37_58
BEGIN_तौ निराशौ मत् अर्थे तु शोक सम्ताप कर्शितौ |
सह सर्व ऋक्ष हरिभिः त्यक्ष्यतः प्राण सम्ग्रहम् || ५-३७-५९_END
BEGIN_"Those two men Rama and Lakshmana who are emaciated by grief and anguish along with all 
bears and monkeys, losing their hope, will abandon their lives."_END

B_5_C_39_42
BEGIN_तत् आश्वसिहि भद्रम् ते भव त्वम् काल कान्क्षिणी |
नचिरात् द्रक्ष्यसे रामम् प्रज्वजन्तम् इव अनिलम् || ५-३९-४४_END
BEGIN_"For that reason, console yourself indeed! Happiness to you! If you wait for some time, 
you shall see, within a short time, Rama like a blazing fire."_END

B_5_C_44_2
BEGIN_रथेन खर युक्तेन तम् आगतम् उदीक्ष्य सः |
हनूमान् वेग सम्पन्नो जहर्ष च ननाद च || ५-४४-५_END
BEGIN_Seeing him, arriving by a chariot yoked with donkeys, that Hanuma who was endowed with 
swiftness, was thrilled with joy and made a noise too._END

B_5_C_43_9
BEGIN_ततो वात आत्मजः क्रुद्धो भीम रूपम् समास्थितः || ५-४३-१६
प्रासादस्य महान् तस्य स्तम्भम् हेम परिष्कृतम् |
उत्पाटयित्वा वेगेन हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४३-१७
ततः तम् भ्रामयामास शत धारम् महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_Thereupon, the enraged Hanuma assumed a terrific form. Hanuma possessing a gigantic body 
and the son of wind-god, uprooting a pillar with a hundred edges and decorated with gold in that edifice, 
then speedily whirled it around._END

B_5_C_35_72
BEGIN_मया इयम् असहायेन चरता काम रूपिणा |दक्षिणा दिग् अनुक्रान्ता त्वन् मार्ग विचय एषिणा || ५-३५-७६_END
BEGIN_"I, who can change my form at will, desirous of finding out your access, wandering alone without 
any helper, came to this southern direction."_END

B_5_C_38_51
BEGIN_आनुकूल्येन धर्म आत्मा त्यक्त्वा सुखम् अनुत्तमम् |
अनुगच्छति काकुत्स्थम् भ्रातरम् पालयन् वने || ५-३८-५९_END
BEGIN_"Renouncing a great comfort, the righteous Lakshmana, acting in an affectionate manner 
towards Rama, followed him, watching over him in the forest."_END

B_5_C_37_59
BEGIN_भर्तुः भक्तिम् पुरः कृत्य रामात् अन्यस्य वानर |
न अहम् स्प्रष्टुम् पदा गात्रम् इच्छेयम् वानर उत्तम || ५-३७-६०_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma, the best of monkeys! Honouring the devotion to my husband, I cannot touch 
the body of any man other that of Rama."_END

B_5_C_39_43
BEGIN_निहते राक्षस इन्द्रे च सपुत्र अमात्य बान्धवे |
त्वम् समेष्यसि रामेण शश अन्केन इव रोहिणी || ५-३९-४५_END
BEGIN_"When this king of demons is killed along with his sons, ministers and relatives, you 
will meet Rama, as Rohini* met the moon."_END

B_5_C_42_20
BEGIN_मनः परिगृहीताम् ताम् तव रक्षो गण ईश्वर |
कः सीताम् अभिभाषेत यो न स्यात् त्यक्त जीवितः || ५-४२-२१_END
BEGIN_"O chief of the demons-troops! Who would dare to talk to that Seetha, who has been mentally 
accepted by you, except perhaps he who is ready to abandon his life?"_END

B_5_C_44_3
BEGIN_तम् तोरण विटन्कस्थम् हनूमन्तम् महाकपिम् |
जम्बु माली महाबाहुः विव्याध निशितैः शरैः || ५-४४-६_END
BEGIN_The long-armed Jambumali transfixed sharp arrows into that great monkey, Hanuma who was 
standing on the top of the archy door-way._END

B_5_C_35_73
BEGIN_दिष्ट्या अहम् हरि सैन्यानाम् त्वन् नाशम् अनुशोचताम् |अपनेष्यामि सम्तापम् तव अभिगम शंसनात् 
|| ५-३५-७७_END
BEGIN_"I shall remove the anguish of the army of monkeys who are lamenting because of your disappearance 
by informing them about my coming close to you because of my good fortune!"_END

B_5_C_38_52
BEGIN_सिम्ह स्कन्धो महाबाहुः मनस्वी प्रिय दर्शनः |
पितृवत् वर्तते रामे मातृवन् माम् समाचरन् || ५-३८-६०_END
BEGIN_"Lakshmana, who has broad shoulders like that ofa lion, mighty-armed, steady-minded and 
having pleasant looks, behaves towards Rama as towards his father and looks to me as his own mother."_END

B_5_C_43_10
BEGIN_तत्र चाग्निः समभवत्प्रासादश्चाप्यदह्यत || ५-४३-१८
दह्यमानं ततो दृष्ट्वा प्रासादं हरियूथपः |
स राक्षस शतम् हत्वा वज्रेण इन्द्र इव असुरान् || ५-४३-१९
अन्तरिक्ष स्थितः श्रीमान् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_Fire was also generated there (due to friction with other pillars) The edifice was then 
consumed by fire. Seeing the edifice burning, that Hanuma killing those hundred demons, like Indra killing 
demons with his thunderbolt and gloriously staying in the sky, spoke (the following) words:_END

B_5_C_37_60
BEGIN_यत् अहम् गात्र संस्पर्शम् रावणस्य गता बलात् |
अनीशा किम् करिष्यामि विनाथा विवशा सती || ५-३७-६१_END
BEGIN_"That I got, by force, the touch of Ravana's body, was because being helpless, having 
lost control of myself and without a protector, I could not do anything."_END

B_5_C_39_44
BEGIN_क्षिप्रम् त्वम् देवि शोकस्य पारम् यास्यसि मैथिलि |
रावणम् चैव रामेण निहतम् द्रक्ष्यसे अचिरात् || ५-३९-४६_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! You shall see the end of your sorrow soon. Within a short time, 
you will also see the end of Ravana, as destroyed by Rama."_END

B_5_C_42_21
BEGIN_राक्षसीनाम् वचः श्रुत्वा रावणो राक्षस ईश्वरः |
हुत अगिः इव जज्वाल कोप सम्वर्तित ईक्षणः || ५-४२-२२_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of the female-demons, Ravana the lord of demons flared up like a funeral 
fire, his eyes spinning with anger._END

B_5_C_44_4
BEGIN_अर्ध चन्द्रेण वदने शिरसि एकेन कर्णिना |
बाह्वोः विव्याध नाराचैः दशभिः तम् कपि ईश्वरम् || ५-४४-७_END
BEGIN_He transfixed Hanuma the leader of monkeys in the face with an arrow with a crescent-shaped 
head, on the head with an arrow having an ear-shaped top and in the arms with ten steel arrows._END

B_5_C_35_74
BEGIN_दिष्ट्या हि न मम व्यर्थम् देवि सागर लन्घनम् |प्राप्स्यामि अहम् इदम् दिष्ट्या त्वत् दर्शन 
कृतम् यशः || ५-३५-७८_END
BEGIN_"O princess! By my fortune, my crossing of ocean has not gone in vain. I can get this fame of having 
seen you because of my good luck."_END

B_5_C_38_53
BEGIN_प्रियमाणाम् तदा वीरो न तु माम् वेद लक्ष्मणः |
वृद्ध उपसेवी लक्ष्मीवान् शक्तो न बहु भाषिता || ५-३८-६१
राज पुत्रः प्रिय श्रेष्ठः सदृशः श्वशुरस्य मे |_END
BEGIN_"The valiant Lakshmana, on that day of occurrence, did not know that I was being taken 
away by Ravana. He serves elders. He possesses a splendour. Though capable, he does not talk much. To 
Dasaratha, my father-in-law, he is his replica a beloved and the best prince."_END

B_5_C_43_11
BEGIN_मादृशानाम् सहस्राणि विसृष्टानि महात्मनाम् || ५-४३-२०
बलिनाम् वानर इन्द्राणाम् सुग्रीव वश वर्तिनाम् |
अटन्ति वसुधाम् कृत्स्नाम् वयमये च वानराः || ५-४३-२१_END
BEGIN_"Thousands of monkeys like me, possessing gigantic bodies of strength, were sent on the 
orders of Sugreeva. We and other monkeys are now roaming the entire earth."_END

B_5_C_37_61
BEGIN_यदि रामो दशग्रीवम् इह हत्वा सराक्षसम् |
माम् इतो गृह्य गच्छेत तत् तस्य सदृशम् भवेत् || ५-३७-६२_END
BEGIN_"If Rama kills Ravana here along with his relatives and departs taking me from here, 
it would be proper for him"_END

B_5_C_42_22
BEGIN_तस्य क्रुद्धस्य नेत्राभ्याम् प्रापतन्नस्रबिन्दवः |
दीप्ताभ्यामिव जज्वाल कोपसंवर्तितेक्षणः || ५-४२-२३_END
BEGIN_Tears dropped from Ravana's enraged eyes, like drops of oil dripping from resplendent 
lamps._END

B_5_C_39_45
BEGIN_एवम् आश्वस्य वैदेहीम् हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
गमनाय मतिम् कृत्वा वैदेहीम् पुनः अब्रवीत् || ५-३९-४७_END
BEGIN_Thus consoling Seetha, Hanuma the son of wind-god made up his mind to go back and spoke 
to Seetha again as follows:_END

B_5_C_44_5
BEGIN_तस्य तत् शुशुभे ताम्रम् शरेण अभिहतम् मुखम् |
शरदि इव अम्बुजम् फुल्लम् विद्धम् भास्कर रश्मिना || ५-४४-८_END
BEGIN_That crimson face of Hanuma, hit by an arrow, shone like a full-blown lotus touched by 
a sun's ray in autumn._END

B_5_C_45_0
BEGIN_ततः ते राक्षस इन्द्रेण चोदिता मन्त्रिणः सुताः |
निर्ययुः भवनात् तस्मात् सप्त सप्त अर्चि वर्चसः || ५-४५-१
महाबल परीवारा धनुष्मन्तो महाबलाः |
कृत अस्त्रा अस्त्रविदाम् श्रेष्ठाः परस्पर जय एषिणः || ५-४५-२
हेम जाल परिक्षिप्तैः ध्वजवद्भिः पताकिभिः |
तोयद स्वन निर्घोषैः वाजि युक्तैः महारथैः || ५-४५-३
तप्त कान्चन चित्राणि चापानि अमित विक्रमाः |
विस्फारयन्तः सम्हृष्टाः तडिद्वन्त इव अम्बुदाः || ५-४५-४_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, those seven sons of his chief minister having a lustre similar to that of 
fire, surrounded by a great army, wielding their respective bows, possessing a great strength, well-trained 
in archery and the best among knower of weapons, wishing a victory reciprocally, having an immense prowess 
each, and as directed by Ravana, started highly delighted from that palace, in great chariots yoked 
with horses. Those chariots were having a noise similar to that of an autumnal cloud, overlaid with 
a protective armour of gold, surmounted by banners and decorated with smaller flags. They were stretching 
their bows inlaid with refined gold and looking colourful like clouds accompanied by flashes of lightning._END

B_5_C_35_75
BEGIN_राघवः च महावीर्यः क्षिप्रम् त्वाम् अभिपत्स्यते |समित्र बान्धवम् हत्वा रावणम् राक्षस अधिपम् 
|| ५-३५-७९_END
BEGIN_"The highly valiant Rama, by killing Ravana the Lord of demons along with his friends and relatives, 
will obtain you soon."_END

B_5_C_38_54
BEGIN_मत्तः प्रियतरो नित्यम् भ्राता रामस्य लक्ष्मणः || ५-३८-६२
नियुक्तो धुरि यस्याम् तु ताम् उद्वहति वीर्यवान् |_END
BEGIN_"Lakshmana, the younger brother of Rama is the one who is dearer to me always. That energetic 
Lakshmana carries out well, whatever load of work is entrusted to him"_END

B_5_C_43_12
BEGIN_दशनागबलाः केचित्केचिद्दशगुणोत्तराः |
केचिन्नागसहस्रस्य बभूवुस्तुल्यविक्रमाः || ५-४३-२२_END
BEGIN_"Some of the monkeys are having a strength of ten elephants. Some are having a strength 
of a hundred elephants. Some are having a prowess equal to that of a thousand elephants."_END

B_5_C_37_62
BEGIN_श्रुता हि दृष्टाः च मया पराक्रमा |
महात्मनः तस्य रण अवमर्दिनः |
न देव गन्धर्व भुजम्ग राक्षसा |
भवन्ति रामेण समा हि सम्युगे || ५-३७-६३_END
BEGIN_"I have not only heard but seen myself about the strength of the high souled Rama destroying 
enemies in battle. Neither the celestials nor the divine musicians nor the serpent-gods nor the demons 
are equal to Rama in combat."_END

B_5_C_42_23
BEGIN_आत्मनः सदृशान् शूरान् किम्करान् नाम राक्षसान् |
व्यादिदेश महातेजा निग्रह अर्थम् हनूमतः || ५-४२-२४_END
BEGIN_Ravana, with a great splendour, sent demons with a valiance equal to him, called Kinkaras, 
in order to catch hold of Hanuma._END

B_5_C_39_46
BEGIN_तम् अरिघ्नम् कृत आत्मानम् क्षिप्रम् द्रक्ष्यसि राघवम् |
लक्ष्मणम् च धनुष् पाणिम् लन्का द्वारम् उपस्थितम् || ५-३९-४८_END
BEGIN_"That Rama the annihilator of enemies, who firmly decided to destroy his adversaries 
and Lakshmana wielding a bow in his hand will soon reach the entrance of Lanka and you will see them."_END

B_5_C_44_6
BEGIN_तत्तस्य रक्तम् रक्तेन रञ्जितम् शुशुभे मुखम् |
यथाकाशे महापद्मं सिक्तं चन्दनबिन्दुभिः || ५-४४-९_END
BEGIN_That face of Hanuma, which was naturally crimson in colour, smeared with blood, beamed 
like a large lotus in the sky sprinkled with drops of sandal._END

B_5_C_45_1
BEGIN_जनन्यः ताः ततः तेषाम् विदित्वा किम्करान् हतान् |
बभूवुः शोक सम्भ्रान्ताः सबान्धव सुहृत् जनाः || ५-४५-५_END
BEGIN_Coming to know that Kimkaras themselves were killed their mothers together with their 
relatives and friends were tormented with grief._END

B_5_C_43_13
BEGIN_सन्ति चौघबलाः केचित्केचिद्वायुबलोपमाः |
अप्रमेयबलाश्चान्ये तत्रासन् हरियूथपाः || ५-४३-२३_END
BEGIN_"Some are having the strength of a strong stream. Some have strength equal to that of 
wind. Some other army-chiefs of monkeys even cannot be measured."_END

B_5_C_35_76
BEGIN_कौरजो नाम वैदेहि गिरीणाम् उत्तमो गिरिः |ततो गच्छति गो कर्णम् पर्वतम् केसरी हरिः || ५-३५-८०_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! There is a mountain called Malyavan, which is the best among mountains. From there, 
a monkeys called Kesari went to another mountain called Gokarna."_END

B_5_C_38_55
BEGIN_यम् दृष्ट्वा राघवो न एव वृद्धम् आर्यम् अनुस्मरत् || ५-३८-६३
स मम अर्थाय कुशलम् वक्तव्यो वचनान् मम |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing whom, Rama ceases to recollect his deceased father, that Lakshmana is to be asked 
about his well-being, as my word and on my behalf."_END

B_5_C_37_63
BEGIN_समीक्ष्य तम् सम्यति चित्र कार्मुकम् |
महाबलम् वासव तुल्य विक्रमम् |
सलक्ष्मणम् को विषहेत राघवम् |
हुत अशनम् दीप्तम् इव अनिल ईरितम् || ५-३७-६४_END
BEGIN_"Who can withstand seeing in battle that mighty Rama, dazzling like fire fanned by wind, 
wielding his conspicuous bow and having prowess equal to that of Indra the Lord of celestials, together 
with Lakshmana?"_END

B_5_C_42_24
BEGIN_तेषाम् अशीति साहस्रम् किम्कराणाम् तरस्विनाम् |
निर्ययुः भवनात् तस्मात् कूट मुद्गर पाणयः || ५-४२-२५
महाउदरा महादम्ष्ट्रा घोर रूपा महाबलाः |
युद्ध अभिमनसः सर्वे हनूमत् ग्रहण उन्मुखाः || ५-४२-२६_END
BEGIN_He ordered for eighty thousand of those Kinkaras who were strong. All those mighty Kinkaras 
with their large bellies, long tusks and terrible forms, longing to fight with iron mallets and clubs 
in hand, in eagerness to lay hold on Hanuma, started from that place._END

B_5_C_39_47
BEGIN_नख दम्ष्ट्र आयुधान् वीरान् सिम्ह शार्दूल विक्रमान् |
वानरान् वारण इन्द्र आभान् क्षिप्रम् द्रक्ष्यसि सम्गतान् || ५-३९-४९_END
BEGIN_"You can see soon those valiant monkeys, with their claws and tusks as weapons, having 
the prowess of lions and tigers and looking like lordly elephants, coming together."_END

B_5_C_44_7
BEGIN_चुकोप बाण अभिहतो राक्षसस्य महाकपिः |
ततः पार्श्वे अतिविपुलाम् ददर्श महतीम् शिलाम् || ५-४४-१०_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, struck by those arrows, was enraged with that demon and then saw by his side, 
a big rock of a very large measure._END

B_5_C_45_2
BEGIN_ते परस्पर सम्घर्षाः तप्त कान्चन भूषणाः |
अभिपेतुः हनूमन्तम् तोरणस्थम् अवस्थितम् || ५-४५-६_END
BEGIN_Those sons of chief minister, wearing ornaments made of pure gold, rushed towards Hanuma, 
who was ready for battle and who stood on the archy gate-way motionless._END

B_5_C_43_14
BEGIN_ईदृग्विधैस्तु हरिभिर्वऋतो दन्तनखायुधैः |
शतैः शत सहस्रैः च कोटीभिः अयुतैः अपि || ५-४३-२४
आगमिष्यति सुग्रीवः सर्वेषाम् वो निषूदनः |_END
BEGIN_"Surrounded by hundreds, myriads, lakhs and crores of such monkeys having their teeth 
and nails as their weapons, Sugreeva, who is capable of destroying you all, will come."_END

B_5_C_35_77
BEGIN_स च देव ऋषिभिः दृष्टः पिता मम महाकपिः |तीर्थे नदी पतेः पुण्ये शम्ब सादनम् उद्धरत् || ५-३५-८१_END
BEGIN_"As prayed by gods and seers, that great monkey called Kesari, my father killed a demon named Shambasadana 
at a sacred shrine near the sea-shore."_END

B_5_C_38_56
BEGIN_मृदुः नित्यम् शुचिः दक्षः प्रियो रामस्य लक्ष्मणः || ५-३८-६४
यथा हि वानरश्रेष्ठ दुःखक्षयकरो भवेत् |
त्वमस्मिन् कार्यनिर्योगे प्रमाण हरिसत्तम || ५-३८-६५_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma, the excellent of monkeys and the best of monkeys! you are the model for fulfilling 
this act of addressing him in such a way that Lakshmana, the mild, every-pure and clever darling of 
Rama may bring my sorrows to an end."_END

B_5_C_37_64
BEGIN_सलक्ष्मणम् राघवम् आजि मर्दनम् |
दिशा गजम् मत्तम् इव व्यवस्थितम् |
सहेत को वानर मुख्य सम्युगे |
युग अन्त सूर्य प्रतिमम् शर अर्चिषम् || ५-३७-६५_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! In battle, who can endure Rama resembling the sun at noon-time, 
with his arrows resembling its rays, the destroyer in battle, stationed like a mythical elephant in 
rut, along with Lakshmana?_END

B_5_C_42_25
BEGIN_ते कपिम् तम् समासाद्य तोरणस्थम् अवस्थितम् |
अभिपेतुः महावेगाः पतन्गा इव पावकम् || ५-४२-२७_END
BEGIN_Approaching Hanuma who was standing near the arched doorway, they rushed towards him 
with a great speed, like locusts rushing towards a fire._END

B_5_C_39_48
BEGIN_शैल अम्बुद निकाशानाम् लन्का मलय सानुषु |
नर्दताम् कपि मुख्यानाम् आर्ये यूथानि अनेकशः || ५-३९-५०_END
BEGIN_"O venerable lady! You shall see many troops of excellent monkeys resembling hills and 
clouds, thundering on the peaks of Malaya mountain in Lanka."_END

B_5_C_44_8
BEGIN_तरसा ताम् समुत्पाट्य चिक्षेप बलवत् बली |
ताम् शरैः दशभिः क्रुद्धः ताडयामास राक्षसः || ५-४४-११_END
BEGIN_Uplifting that rock with strength, the athletic Hanuma hurled it with force. The enraged 
demon then struck back that rock with ten arrows._END

B_5_C_45_3
BEGIN_सृजन्तो बाण वृष्टिम् ते रथ गर्जित निह्स्वनाः |
वृष्टिमन्त इव अम्भोदा विचेरुः नैरृत ऋषभाः || ५-४५-७_END
BEGIN_Those demons looking like clouds, diffusing thunder-like sounds of their chariots and 
discharging a shower of arrows, moved in different directions resembling rainy clouds in the monsoon._END

B_5_C_43_15
BEGIN_न इयम् अस्ति पुरी लन्का न यूयम् न च रावणः || ५-४३-२५
यस्मात् इक्ष्वाकु नाथेन बद्धम् वैरम् महात्मना |_END
BEGIN_"You hold enmity with the high souled Rama. For this, the City of Lanka will not be there. 
Neither you, nor even Ravana will survive."_END

B_5_C_35_78
BEGIN_तस्य अहम् हरिणः क्षेत्रे जातो वातेन मैथिलि |हनूमान् इति विख्यातो लोके स्वेन एव कर्मणा 
|| ५-३५-८२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! I am born in the womb of the wife of that Kesari the monkey, by the grace of the wind-god. 
By my activity alone, I am renowned as Hanuma in this world."_END

B_5_C_38_57
BEGIN_राघवस्त्वत्समारम्भान्मयि यत्नपरो भवेत् |
इदम् ब्रूयाः च मे नाथम् शूरम् रामम् पुनः पुनः || ५-३८-६६_END
BEGIN_"Depending on your effort, Rama will be more active with his effort the following words 
again and again to Rama, my Lord and the hero:"_END

B_5_C_42_26
BEGIN_ते गदाभिः विचित्राभिः परिघैः कान्चन अन्गदैः |
आजघ्नुः वानर श्रेष्ठम् शरैः आदित्य सम्निभैः || ५-४२-२८_END
BEGIN_They banged Hanuma with various kinds of maces, iron bludgeons plated with gold and arrows 
shining like the sun._END

B_5_C_37_65
BEGIN_स मे हरि श्रेष्ठ सलक्ष्मणम् पतिम् |
सयूथपम् क्षिप्रम् इह उपपादय |
चिराय रामम् प्रति शोक कर्शिताम् |
कुरुष्व माम् वानर मुख्य हर्षिताम् || ५-३७-६६_END
BEGIN_"O the excellent of monkeys! You, as such, soon bring my husband here along with Lakshmana, 
and the chiefs of army. O the best of monkeys! I am emaciated with grief about Rama since long. Make 
me now joyful."_END

B_5_C_39_49
BEGIN_स तु मर्मणि घोरेण ताडितो मन्मथ इषुणा |
न शर्म लभते रामः सिम्ह अर्दित इव द्विपः || ५-३९-५१_END
BEGIN_"Hit in the vitals by the darts of venerable Manmatha the god of love, Rama is not obtaining 
happiness, as an elephant gets tormented by a lion."_END

B_5_C_44_9
BEGIN_विपन्नम् कर्म तत् दृष्ट्वा हनूमान् चण्ड विक्रमः |
सालम् विपुलम् उत्पाट्य भ्रामयामास वीर्यवान् || ५-४४-१२_END
BEGIN_Seeing that work in vain, the powerful Hanuma of terrific prowess, uprooted a very large 
sal tree and whirled it around._END

B_5_C_45_4
BEGIN_अवकीर्णः ततः ताभिः हनूमान् शर वृष्टिभिः |
अभवत् सम्वृत आकारः शैल राड् इव वृष्टिभिः || ५-४५-८_END
BEGIN_Thus covered by those showers of arrows, Hanuma became invisible even as a mountain-king 
is concealed by incessant showers._END

B_5_C_35_79
BEGIN_विश्वासार्थम् तु वैदेहि भर्तुरुक्ता मया गुणाः |विश्वास अर्थम् तु वैदेहि भर्तुः उक्ता मया 
गुणाः || ५-३५-८३_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! I described the qualities of Rama, your husband, to cause trust in you. O the faultless 
princess! Rama will take you from here within a short time."_END

B_5_C_38_58
BEGIN_जीवितम् धारयिष्यामि मासम् दशरथ आत्मज |
ऊर्ध्वम् मासान् न जीवेयम् सत्येन अहम् ब्रवीमि ते || ५-३८-६७_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! I shall hold my life for a month. I cannot survive after a month I am telling 
you the truth."_END

B_5_C_42_27
BEGIN_मुद्गरैः पट्टिसैः शूलैः प्रासतोमरशक्तिभिः |
परिवार्य हनूमन्तं सहसा तस्थुरग्रतः || ५-४२-२९_END
BEGIN_Quickly surrounding Hanuma with clubs, sharp edged spears, iron pikes, lances, javelins 
and swords, they stood in front of him._END

B_5_C_39_50
BEGIN_मा रुदो देवि शोकेन मा भूत् ते मनसो अप्रियम् |
शची इव पथ्या शक्रेण भर्त्रा नाथवती हि असि || ५-३९-५२_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! Do not weep with grief. Let your mind be without any unpleasantness. 
You are indeed having Rama your husband as your protector like Shachi having Indra her husband as a 
protector."_END

B_5_C_44_10
BEGIN_भ्रामयन्तम् कपिम् दृष्ट्वा साल वृक्षम् महाबलम् |
चिक्षेप सुबहून् बाणान् जम्बु माली महाबलः || ५-४४-१३_END
BEGIN_Seeing the mighty Hanuma, whirling around the sal tree, the exceedingly strong Jambumali 
discharged numerous arrows._END

B_5_C_45_5
BEGIN_स शरान् वन्चयामास तेषाम् आशु चरः कपिः |
रथ वेगान् च वीराणाम् विचरन् विमले अम्बरे || ५-४५-९_END
BEGIN_Roaming about in a cloudless sky, that fast-footed monkey made the arrows and the speedy 
chariots of those virile demons, useless._END

B_5_C_35_80
BEGIN_एवम् विश्वासिता सीता हेतुभिः शोक कर्शिता |उपपन्नैः अभिज्ञानैः दूतम् तम् अवगच्छति || ५-३५-८४_END
BEGIN_Thus inspired by confidence because of the above reasons, Seetha emaciated with grief, by adequate 
clues served as proof._END

B_5_C_42_28
BEGIN_हनूमान् अपि तेजस्वी श्रीमान् पर्वत सम्निभः |
क्षिताव् आविध्य लान्गूलम् ननाद च महास्वनम् || ५-४२-३०_END
BEGIN_The highly splendorous and illustrious Hanuma too, looking like a mountain, hurled his 
tail on the ground, making a thunderous noise._END

B_5_C_38_59
BEGIN_रावणेन उपरुद्धाम् माम् निकृत्या पाप कर्मणा |
त्रातुम् अर्हसि वीर त्वम् पातालात् इव कौशिकीम् || ५-३८-६८_END
BEGIN_"O valiant man! You are required to rescue me, detained (as I am) by Ravana the criminal 
and subjected to humiliation, as you (as Lord Vishnu) earlier protected Indra the Lord of celestials 
and Lakshmi the goddess of prosperity from the abode of servants and demons."_END

B_5_C_39_51
BEGIN_रामात् विशिष्टः को अन्यो अस्ति कश्चित् सौमित्रिणा समः |
अग्नि मारुत कल्पौ तौ भ्रातरौ तव संश्रयौ || ५-३९-५३_END
BEGIN_"Who else is there greater than Rama or who else equal to Lakshmana? Those two brothers, 
like fire and wind, are supportive to you."_END

B_5_C_44_11
BEGIN_सालम् चतुर्भिः चिच्छेद वानरम् पन्चभिः भुजे |
उरसि एकेन बाणेन दशभिः तु स्तन अन्तरे || ५-४४-१४_END
BEGIN_He splitted sal tree with four arrows and struck the arms of Hanuma with five arrows, 
in the chest with one arrow and in the space between the breast wit ten arrows._END

B_5_C_35_81
BEGIN_अतुलम् च गता हर्षम् प्रहर्षेण तु जानकी |नेत्राभ्याम् वक्र पक्ष्माभ्याम् मुमोच आनन्दजम् 
जलम् || ५-३५-८५_END
BEGIN_Seetha obtained unequal delight. She released tears of joy from her eyes having curved eye-lashes, 
with a thrill of delight._END

B_5_C_45_6
BEGIN_स तैः क्रीडन् धनुष्मद्भिः व्योम्नि वीरः प्रकाशते |
धनुष्मद्भिः यथा मेघैः मारुतः प्रभुः अम्बरे || ५-४५-१०_END
BEGIN_Playing with those demons wielding a bow each in the sky, that hero shone like the Lord 
of Wind, playing with clouds brandishing a rain bow._END

B_5_C_42_29
BEGIN_स भूत्वा सुमहाकायो हनुमान् मारुतात्मजः |
धृष्टमास्फोटयामास लङ्काम् शब्देन पूरयन् || ५-४२-३१_END
BEGIN_The highly splendourous and illustrious Hanuma too, looking like a mountain, hurled his 
tail on the ground, making a thunderous noise._END

B_5_C_38_60
BEGIN_ततो वस्त्र गतम् मुक्त्वा दिव्यम् चूडा मणिम् शुभम् |
प्रदेयो राघवाय इति सीता हनुमते ददौ || ५-३८-६९_END
BEGIN_Then, untying the bright devine jewel for her head tied in her garment, Seetha gave it 
to Hanuma, saying that it might be handed over to Rama._END

B_5_C_39_52
BEGIN_न अस्मिन् चिरम् वत्स्यसि देवि देशे |
रक्षो गणैः अध्युषितो अतिरौद्रे |
न ते चिरात् आगमनम् प्रियस्य |
क्षमस्व मत् साम्गम काल मात्रम् || ५-३९-५४_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha the princess! You will not stay for long at this place, which is very terrific 
and occupied with a multitude of demons. The arrival of your husband will not be delayed. Be patient 
till the moment of my meeting with Rama on my return."_END

B_5_C_44_12
BEGIN_स शरैः पूरित तनुः क्रोधेन महता वृतः |
तम् एव परिघम् गृह्य भ्रामयामास वेगितः || ५-४४-१५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, with his body full of arrows, was highly enraged and taking the same iron rod 
as well as clasping it swiftly, whirled it around._END

B_5_C_45_7
BEGIN_स कृत्वा निनदम् घोरम् त्रासयन् ताम् महाचमूम् |
चकार हनुमान् वेगम् तेषु रक्षह्सु वीर्यवान् || ५-४५-११_END
BEGIN_Making a terrific roar and frightening that great army, the valiant Hanuma rushed on 
those demons._END

B_5_C_35_82
BEGIN_चारु तच् च आननम् तस्याः ताम्र शुक्ल आयत ईक्षणम् |अशोभत विशाल अक्ष्या राहु मुक्त इव उडु 
राट् || ५-३५-८६_END
BEGIN_The countenance of that large-eyed Seetha, who is beautiful, whose eyes are red white and long 
is shining like a moon, the king of stars liberated from Rahu the demon._END

B_5_C_42_30
BEGIN_तस्यस्फोटितशब्देन महता सानुनादिना |
पेतुर्विहङ्गा गगनादुच्चैश्चेदमघोयत् || ५-४२-३२_END
BEGIN_By that great sound made by Hanuma through clapping on his arms together with a resound, 
birds fell down from the sky. Hanuma also then cried aloud with a clamorous voice (as follows):_END

B_5_C_38_61
BEGIN_प्रतिगृह्य ततो वीरो मणि रत्नम् अनुत्तमम् |
अन्गुल्या योजयामास न हि अस्या प्राभवत् भुजः || ५-३८-७०_END
BEGIN_Taking the excellent jewel, the valiant Hanuma thereupon fitted it to his finger, since 
his arm (eventhough he had assumed his former tiny form), was not fitting to it properly._END

B_5_C_44_13
BEGIN_अतिवेगो अतिवेगेन भ्रामयित्वा बल उत्कटः |
परिघम् पातयामास जम्बु मालेः महाउरसि || ५-४४-१६_END
BEGIN_Spinning the iron rod with a great speed, Hanuma, richly endowed with strength and highly 
agitated, threw it on the broad chest of Jamubumali._END

B_5_C_45_8
BEGIN_तलेन अभिहनत् कांश्चित् पादैः कांश्चित् परम् तपः |
मुष्टिना अभ्यहनत् कांश्चिन् नखैः कांश्चित् व्यदारयत् || ५-४५-१२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, the annihilator of enemies, struck some with his palms, some with his feet 
and some others with his fists. He tore down some others with his nails._END

B_5_C_35_83
BEGIN_हनूमन्तम् कपिम् व्यक्तम् मन्यते न अन्यथा इति सा |अथ उवाच हनूमान् ताम् उत्तरम् प्रिय दर्शनाम् 
|| ५-३५-८७_END
BEGIN_Seetha considered Hanuma clearly as a monkey and not otherwise. Thereafter Hanuma replied to her 
who is pleasant to the sight (as follows)_END

B_5_C_42_31
BEGIN_जयत्यतिबलो रामो लक्ष्मणश्च महाबलः |
राजा जयति सुग्रीवो राघवेणाभिपालितः || ५-४२-३३_END
BEGIN_"Long live the mighty Rama and the powerful Lakshmana! Long live the King Sugreeva, protected 
by Rama!"_END

B_5_C_38_62
BEGIN_मणि रत्नम् कपि वरः प्रतिगृह्य अभिवाद्य च |
सीताम् प्रदक्षिणम् कृत्वा प्रणतः पार्श्वतः स्थितः || ५-३८-७१_END
BEGIN_Receiving that jewel, Hanuma the best among the monkeys, offered his salutation to seetha, 
by engaging himself in circumambulation and stood aside with humbleness._END

B_5_C_44_14
BEGIN_तस्य चैव शिरो न अस्ति न बाहू न च जानुनी |
न धनुः न रथो न अश्वाः तत्र अदृश्यन्त न इषवः || ५-४४-१७_END
BEGIN_That Jambumali's head was not there, nor his arms, nor his knees, nor his bow, nor his 
chariot and nor his horses were seen nor his arrows._END

B_5_C_45_9
BEGIN_प्रममाथ उरसा कांश्चित् ऊरुभ्याम् अपरान् कपिः |
केचित् तस्य एव नादेन तत्र एव पतिता भुवि || ५-४५-१३_END
BEGIN_Hanuma crushed some with his chest and some others with his thighs. Some fell down there 
itself on the ground, just by the roar made by Hanuma._END

B_5_C_35_84
BEGIN_एतत्ते सर्वमाख्यातम् समाश्वसिहि मैथिलि |किम् करोमि कथम् वा ते रोचते प्रतियाम्यहम् || ५-३५-८८_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! I told you indeed all this please be consoled. Tell me what I can do for you and also 
what is agreeable to you. I am going back now."_END

B_5_C_42_32
BEGIN_दासोऽहम् कोसलेन्द्रस्य रामस्याक्लिष्टकर्मणः |
हनुमान् शत्रुसैन्यानाम् निहन्ता मारुतात्मजः || ५-४२-३४_END
BEGIN_"I am Hanuma, the destroyer of the army of adversaries and the son of wind-god. I am 
the servant of Rama, the king of Kosala Kingdom, who is unwearied in action."_END

B_5_C_38_63
BEGIN_हर्षेण महता युक्तः सीता दर्शनजेन सः |
हृदयेन गतो रामम् शरीरेण तु विष्ठितः || ५-३८-७२_END
BEGIN_Filled with a great delight, born out of Seetha's discovery by him, that Hanuma mentally 
sought (the presence) of Rama but stood there with just his physical body._END

B_5_C_44_15
BEGIN_स हतः तरसा तेन जम्बु माली महारथः |
पपात निहतो भूमौ चूर्णित अन्ग विभूषणः || ५-४४-१८_END
BEGIN_Thus struck by Hanuma, the mighty Jambumali, with his limbs and ornaments crushed to 
powder, was instantly killed and fell dead on the ground._END

B_5_C_35_85
BEGIN_हते असुरे सम्यति शम्ब सादने |कपि प्रवीरेण महर्षि चोदनात् |ततो अस्मि वायु प्रभवो हि 
मैथिलि |प्रभावतः तत् प्रतिमः च वानरः || ५-३५-८९_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! As provoked by the sages, Kesari, the valiant monkey killed a demon called Shambasadana 
in battle. I am a monkey born through wind-god and through his influence I am equal to the wind-god in strength."_END

B_5_C_45_10
BEGIN_ततः तेष्व् अवपन्नेषु भूमौ निपतितेषु च |
तत् सैन्यम् अगमत् सर्वम् दिशो दश भय अर्दितम् || ५-४५-१४_END
BEGIN_Seeing those demons dying and falling on the ground, all the remaining army, afflicted 
with fear, fled in ten different directions._END

B_5_C_38_64
BEGIN_मणि वरम् उपगृह्य तम् महाअर्हम् |
जनक नृप आत्मजया धृतम् प्रभावात् |
गिरि वर पवन अवधूत मुक्तः |
सुखित मनाः प्रतिसम्क्रमम् प्रपेदे || ५-३८-७३_END
BEGIN_Taking that excellent and highly venerable jewel, worn by Seetha and by its influence 
resembling one who was shaken by a blast coming from the top of a huge mountain, Hanuma was mentally 
pleased and set out for crossing the ocean in his return journey._END

B_5_C_42_33
BEGIN_न रावणसहस्रम् मे युद्धे प्रतिबलं भवेत् |
शिलाभिस्तु प्रहरतः पादपैश्च सहस्रशः || ५-४२-३५_END
BEGIN_"Even a thousand of Ravanas will not be matching equally with me, who is capable of striking 
with thousands of rocks and trees in battle."_END

B_5_C_46_0
BEGIN_हतान् मन्त्रि सुतान् बुद्ध्वा वानरेण महात्मना |
रावणः सम्वृत आकारः चकार मतिम् उत्तमाम् || ५-४६-१_END
BEGIN_Coming to know that the chief minister's sons were killed by the high souled who had 
cleverly concealed the expression made an excellent thought._END

B_5_C_44_16
BEGIN_जम्बु मालिम् च निहतम् किम्करान् च महाबलान् |
चुक्रोध रावणः श्रुत्वा कोप सम्रक्त लोचनः || ५-४४-१९_END
BEGIN_Hearing Jambumali having been killed, as also the mighty Kimkaras, Ravana was angry with 
his red enraged eyes._END

B_5_C_45_11
BEGIN_विनेदुः विस्वरम् नागा निपेतुः भुवि वाजिनः |
भग्न नीड ध्वजच् चत्रैः भूः च कीर्णा अभवत् रथैः || ५-४५-१५_END
BEGIN_Their elephants trumpeted with a wrong accent. Horses fell down on the ground. Even the 
earth was filled with chariots which had their seats, banners and canopies broken._END

B_5_C_42_34
BEGIN_अर्दयित्वा पुरीम् लङ्कामभिवाद्य च मैथिलीम् |
समृद्धार्थो गमिष्यामि मिषताम् सर्वरक्षसाम् || ५-४२-३६_END
BEGIN_"Here, before the eyes of all the demons, I will annihilate the City of Lanka and after 
offering salutation to Seetha, I will go back after fully completing my task."_END

B_5_C_46_1
BEGIN_स विरूप अक्ष यूप अक्षौ दुर्धरम् चैव राक्षसम् |
प्रघसम् भास कर्णम् च पन्च सेना अग्र नायकान् || ५-४६-२
संदिदेश दशग्रीवो वीरान् नय विशारदान् |
हनूमत् ग्रहणे व्यग्रान् वायु वेग समान् युधि || ५-४६-३_END
BEGIN_That Ravana ordered (as follows) five foremost leaders of the army viz. Virupaksha, Yupaksha, 
Durdhara the demon, Praghasa and Bhasakarna, all of them brave demons, skilled in strategy, eager to 
capture Hanuma and equal to the speed of wind in battle._END

B_5_C_44_17
BEGIN_स रोष सम्वर्तित ताम्र लोचनः |
प्रहस्त पुत्रे निहते महाबले |
अमात्य पुत्रान् अतिवीर्य विक्रमान् |
समादिदेश आशु निशा चर ईश्वरः || ५-४४-२०_END
BEGIN_Since the mighty son of Prahasta was killed, that Ravana rolling his red eyes with rage, 
immediately ordered the sons of ministers possessing high strength and prowess, to go to the battle._END

B_5_C_45_12
BEGIN_स्रवता रुधिरेणाथ स्रवन्त्यो दर्शिताः पथि |
विविधैश्च स्वरैर्लङ्का ननाद विकृतम् तदा || ५-४५-१६_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, streams flowing with blood were seen on the way. Lanka resounded with various 
kinds of horrible voices._END

B_5_C_42_35
BEGIN_तस्य सन्नाद शब्देन ते अभवन् भय शन्किताः |
ददृशुः च हनूमन्तम् संध्या मेघम् इव उन्नतम् || ५-४२-३७_END
BEGIN_Those demons became frightened by the clamorous voice of Hanuma cried aloud and saw him 
to be as high as a twilight rain-cloud._END

B_5_C_46_2
BEGIN_यात सेना अग्रगाः सर्वे महाबल परिग्रहाः |
सवाजि रथ मातन्गाः स कपिः शास्यताम् इति || ५-४६-४_END
BEGIN_He ordered as follows: "March, all of you O generals, taking a large army together that 
mokey be punished."_END

B_5_C_45_13
BEGIN_स तान् प्रवृद्धान् विनिहत्य राक्षसान् |
महाबलः चण्ड पराक्रमः कपिः |
युयुत्सुः अन्यैः पुनः एव राक्षसैः |
तत् एव वीरो अभिजगाम तोरणम् तत् || ५-४५-१७_END
BEGIN_That heroic and mighty Hanuma having a terrible prowess, killing those arrogant demons 
and being desirous of a combat with the other demons, again reached that archy door way itself._END

B_5_C_42_36
BEGIN_स्वामि संदेश निह्शन्काः ततः ते राक्षसाः कपिम् |
चित्रैः प्रहरणैः भीमैः अभिपेतुः ततः ततः || ५-४२-३८_END
BEGIN_Not feeling apprehended because of the orders of their king, those demons thereafter 
rushed towards Hanuma, with their terrific and amazing weapons._END

B_5_C_46_3
BEGIN_यत् तैः च खलु भाव्यम् स्यात् तम् आसाद्य वन आलयम् |
कर्म च अपि समाधेयम् देश काल विरोधितम् || ५-४६-५_END
BEGIN_"Approaching that monkey, you ought to become diligent. Action should be taken by you 
which is not out of accord with time and space."_END

B_5_C_42_37
BEGIN_स तैः परिवृतः शूरैः सर्वतः स महाबलः |
आससाद आयसम् भीमम् परिघम् तोरण आश्रितम् || ५-४२-३९_END
BEGIN_Surrounded on all sides by those strong demons, that Hanuma endowed with a great strength 
seized a huge iron bar belonging to the arched gate._END

B_5_C_46_4
BEGIN_न हि अहम् तम् कपिम् मन्ये कर्मणा प्रतितर्कयन् |
सर्वथा तन् महत् भूतम् महाबल परिग्रहम् || ५-४६-६_END
BEGIN_"Judging him by his actions, I do not think him as a mere monkey. By all means, he may 
be an evil spirit, putting on an extraordinary might."_END

B_5_C_42_38
BEGIN_स तम् परिघम् आदाय जघान रजनी चरान् |
स पन्नगम् इव आदाय स्फुरन्तम् विनता सुतः || ५-४२-४०
विचचार अम्बरे वीरः परिगृह्य च मारुतिः |_END
BEGIN_Taking that iron rod, Hanuma killed the demons. That violent Hanuma strolled in the sky, 
taking that iron rod in his hand, as Garuda the eagle would carrying a serpent in its claws._END

B_5_C_46_5
BEGIN_भवेत् इन्द्रेण वा सृष्टम् अस्मत् अर्थम् तपो बलात् |
सनाग यक्ष गन्धर्वा देव असुर महर्षयः || ५-४६-७
युष्माभिः सहितैः सर्वैः मया सह विनिर्जिताः |
तैः अवश्यम् विधातव्यम् व्यलीकम् किंचित् एव नः || ५-४६-८
तत् एव न अत्र संदेहः प्रसह्य परिगृह्यताम् |
न अवमन्यो भवद्भिः च हरिः क्रूर पराक्रमः || ५-४६-९_END
BEGIN_"This evil spirit may be some being evolved for our sake by Indra the Lord of celestials 
with a strength of his askesis. Celestials, demons, sages along with Nagas the serpent-demons, Yakshas 
the spirits and Gandharvas the celestials musicians were conquered by my along with you all together. 
Even same offensive surely, will be effected to us by them. It is such an evil spirit created by Indra. 
There is no doubt about it. Let it be captured forcibly. This monkey of a great prowess should not be 
despised by you."_END

B_5_C_42_39
BEGIN_स हत्वा राक्षसान् वीरः किम्करान् मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४२-४१
युद्ध आकान्क्षी पुनः वीरः तोरणम् समुपस्थितः |_END
BEGIN_Killing the valiant demons called Kinkaras, that heroic Hanuma wishing to fight again, 
arrived at the archy gate way._END

B_5_C_46_6
BEGIN_दृष्टा हि हरयः शीघ्रा मया विपुल विक्रमाः |
वाली च सह सुग्रीवो जाम्बवान् च महाबलः || ५-४६-१०
नीलः सेना पतिः चैव ये च अन्ये द्विविद आदयः |
न एव तेषाम् गतिः भीमा न तेजो न पराक्रमः || ५-४६-११
न मतिः न बल उत्साहो न रूप परिकल्पनम् |_END
BEGIN_"Earlier, I saw the monkeys of a great prowess like Vali and Sugreeva, the mighty Jambavan, 
Nila the Chief of army and so on like Dvivida. their scheme of performance is not so fearful as this; 
nor their efficacy, nor their prowess, nor their intellect, nor this capacity to change their form or 
energy at will."_END

B_5_C_42_40
BEGIN_ततः तस्मात् भयान् मुक्ताः कतिचित् तत्र राक्षसाः || ५-४२-४२
निहतान् किम्करान् सर्वान् रावणाय न्यवेदयन् |_END
BEGIN_Some demons, who somehow escaped from that terror, went to Ravana and informed him that 
all the Kinkaras have been killed._END

B_5_C_47_0
BEGIN_सेना पतीन् पन्च स तु प्रमापितान् |
हनूमता सानुचरान् सवाहनान् |
समीक्ष्य राजा समर उद्धत उन्मुखम् |
कुमारम् अक्षम् प्रसमैक्षत अक्षतम् || ५-४७-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing and sustaining that the five army-generals along with their followers and vehicles 
were disposed off by Hanuma, Ravana looked at Aksha, his son, violent in combat and who was inclined 
to fighting as well as sitting in front of him._END

B_5_C_46_7
BEGIN_महत् सत्त्वम् इदम् ज्ञेयम् कपि रूपम् व्यवस्थितम् || ५-४६-१२
प्रयत्नम् महत् आस्थाय क्रियताम् अस्य निग्रहः |_END
BEGIN_"Keeping in view that it is a great evil spirit standing in the form of a monkey, exert 
a great effort and capture it."_END

B_5_C_42_41
BEGIN_स राक्षसानाम् निहतम् महाबलम् |
निशम्य राजा परिवृत्त लोचनः |
समादिदेश अप्रतिमम् पराक्रमे |
प्रहस्त पुत्रम् समरे सुदुर्जयम् || ५-४२-४३_END
BEGIN_Hearing of large army of demons having been killed, that Ravana with his eyes rolling 
rapidly (with anger), ordered Jambumali, son of Prahasta, who was unequal in prowess and admirably unconquerable 
in battle._END

B_5_C_47_1
BEGIN_स तस्य दृष्टि अर्पण सम्प्रचोदितः |
प्रतापवान् कान्चन चित्र कार्मुकः |
समुत्पपात अथ सदसि उदीरितो |
द्विजाति मुख्यैः हविषा इव पावकः || ५-४७-२_END
BEGIN_Goaded by the looks of Ravana, the energetic Aksha, wielding a golden dotted bow, quickly 
sprang up, like a fire switched up by the foremost of brahmins in a sacrificial fire, by offering oblations 
to it._END

B_5_C_46_8
BEGIN_कामम् लोकाः त्रयः स इन्द्राः ससुर असुर मानवाः || ५-४६-१३
भवताम् अग्रतः स्थातुम् न पर्याप्ता रण अजिरे |_END
BEGIN_"The three worlds including Indra, celestials, demons and humans are not fit to stand 
before you in the battle-field."_END

B_5_C_47_2
BEGIN_ततो महत् बाल दिवा कर प्रभम् |
प्रतप्त जाम्बू नद जाल सम्ततम् |
रथाम् समास्थाय ययौ स वीर्यवान् |
महाहरिम् तम् प्रति नैरृत ऋषभः || ५-४७-३_END
BEGIN_Mounting a great chariot, having a splendour of a newly risen sun and overlaid with a 
protective armour of highly refined gold, that valiant cheif of demons sallied forth towards that mighty 
monkey._END

B_5_C_46_9
BEGIN_तथा अपि तु नयज्ञेन जयम् आकान्क्षता रणे || ५-४६-१४
आत्मा रक्ष्यः प्रयत्नेन युद्ध सिद्धिः हि चन्चला |_END
BEGIN_"Even then, the one who is skilled in strategy, desirous of a victory in a battle is 
to protect himself. Victory in a battle is indeed unreliable."_END

B_5_C_47_3
BEGIN_ततः तपः सम्ग्रह संचय अर्जितम् |
प्रतप्त जाम्बू नद जाल शोभितम् |
पताकिनम् रत्न विभूषित ध्वजम् |
मनो जव अष्ट अश्व वरैः सुयोजितम् || ५-४७-४_END
BEGIN_Aksha's chariot was earned through many kinds of his penances. It was shining with a 
protective armour of highly refined gold, adorned with a flag on a flag-staff studded with gems and 
yoked well with eight excellent horses, having speed equal to that of a mind._END

B_5_C_46_10
BEGIN_ते स्वामि वचनम् सर्वे प्रतिगृह्य महाओजसः || ५-४६-१५
समुत्पेतुः महावेगा हुत अश सम तेजसः |
रथैः च मत्तैः नागैः च वाजिभिः च महाजवैः || ५-४६-१६
शस्त्रैः च विविधैः तीक्ष्णैः सर्वैः च उपचिता बलैः |_END
BEGIN_All of them, having a great strength and a blaze equal to that of fire, accepting the 
orders of their king and augmenting their strength with chariots, elephants in rut, horses of extra 
ordinary swiftness and various kinds of sharp weapons, sallied forth with a great speed._END

B_5_C_47_4
BEGIN_सुर असुर अधृष्यम् असम्ग चारिणम् |
रवि प्रभम् व्योम चरम् समाहितम् |
सतूणम् अष्ट असि निबद्ध बन्धुरम् |
यथा क्रम आवेशित शक्ति तोमरम् || ५-४७-५_END
BEGIN_That chariot was unassailable by celestials or demons. It moved without hindrance to 
any place. It shone like a sun and could move within the sky. It was well-conceived with a quiver, eight 
swords and tied with bells. It was orderly arranged with spears and lances in their respective places._END

B_5_C_46_11
BEGIN_ततः तम् ददृशुः वीरा दीप्यमानम् महाकपिम् || ५-४६-१७
रश्मिमन्तम् इव उद्यन्तम् स्व तेजो रश्मि मालिनम् |
तोरणस्थम् महावेगम् महासत्त्वम् महाबलम् || ५-४६-१८_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, those valiant demons saw that Hanuma the great monkey, encircled by his rays 
of splendour like a rising sun, shining, standing on the archy door-way, possessing enormous energy, 
strong mental disposition and colossal strength._END

B_5_C_47_5
BEGIN_विराजमानम् प्रतिपूर्ण वस्तुना |
सहेम दाम्ना शशि सूर्य वर्वसा |
दिवा कर आभम् रथम् आस्थितः ततः |
स निर्जगाम अमर तुल्य विक्रमः || ५-४७-६_END
BEGIN_Then, Aksha having a prowess equal to that of celestials, came forth, mounting that chariot 
decorated with golden wreaths, having a brilliance of moon and sun, filled with every right thing and 
shining like rays of sun._END

B_5_C_46_12
BEGIN_महामतिम् महाउत्साहम् महाकायम् महाबलम् |
तम् समीक्ष्य एव ते सर्वे दिक्षु सर्वास्व् अवस्थिताः || ५-४६-१९
तैः तैः प्रहरणैः भीमैः अभिपेतुः ततः ततः |_END
BEGIN_Immediately on seeing that Hanuma of great intellect, of great swiftness and of a gigantic 
body, all those demons, stationed in all quarters, attacked him with their terrific weapons from every 
side._END

B_5_C_47_6
BEGIN_स पूरयन् खम् च महीम् च साचलाम् |
तुरम्ग मतन्ग महारथ स्वनैः |
बलैः समेतैः स हि तोरण स्थितम् |
समर्थम् आसीनम् उपागमत् कपिम् || ५-४७-७_END
BEGIN_Aksha, filling the sky earth and its mountains with sounds of horses elephants and chariots, 
together with his army, approached the efficient Hanuma the great monkey, standing at the archy door-way._END

B_5_C_46_13
BEGIN_तस्य पन्च आयसाः तीक्ष्णाः सिताः पीत मुखाः शराः || ५-४६-२०
शिरस्ति उत्पल पत्र आभा दुर्धरेण निपातिताः |_END
BEGIN_Durdhara discharged five sharp and fierce steel arrows with a lustre of black lily-petals 
and yellow tops to descend into Hanuma's head._END

B_5_C_47_7
BEGIN_स तम् समासाद्य हरिम् हरि ईक्षणो |
युग अन्त काल अग्निम् इव प्रजा क्षये |
अवस्थितम् विस्मित जात सम्भ्रमः |
समैक्षत अक्षो बहु मान चक्षुषा || ५-४७-८_END
BEGIN_Approaching that Hanuma, standing there readily to destroy mortals, similar to a fire 
that is to destroy the world, the yellow-eyed Aksha was bewildered, born of a surprise and looked to 
him with a great esteem._END

B_5_C_46_14
BEGIN_स तैः पन्चभिः आविद्धः शरैः शिरसि वानरः || ५-४६-२१
उत्पपात नदन् व्योम्नि दिशो दश विनादयन् |_END
BEGIN_Pierced in the head by those fire arrows, Hanuma leapt roaring in the sky, making the 
roar reverberating in all directions._END

B_5_C_48_0
BEGIN_ततस्तु रक्षोधितिर्महात्म |
हनूमताक्षे निहते कुमारे |
मनः समाधाय स देवकल्पम् |
समादिदेशेन्द्रजितम् सरोषः || ५-४८-१_END
BEGIN_Filled with anger on his son Aksha having been killed by Hanuma, yet reconciling his 
mind, the high-minded Ravana the king of demons for his part then instructed Indrajit (his eldest son) 
possessing the qualities of god (as follows):_END

B_5_C_47_8
BEGIN_स तस्य वेगम् च कपेः महात्मनः |
पराक्रमम् चारिषु पार्ह्तिव आत्मजः |
विचारयन् खम् च बलम् महाबलो |
हिम क्षये सूर्य इव अभिवर्धते || ५-४७-९_END
BEGIN_That Aksha, the mighty prince, assessing the swiftness of that high-souled Hanuma and 
his prowess with regard to his adversaries as also his own strength, increased his body more and more 
like the sun when the frost is faded away._END

B_5_C_46_15
BEGIN_ततः तु दुर्धरो वीरः सरथः सज्ज कार्मुकः || ५-४६-२२
किरन् शर शतैः नैकैः अभिपेदे महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_Then the mighty and the valiant Durdhara leapt into the sky with his chariot. Stretching 
his bow and throwing hundreds of sharp arrows, he attacked Hanuma._END

B_5_C_48_1
BEGIN_त्वमस्त्रविच्छस्त्रविदाम् वरिष्ठः |
सुरासुराणामपि शोकदाता |
सुरेषु सेन्द्रेषु च दृष्टकर्मा |
पितामहाराधनसंचितास्त्रः || ५-४८-२_END
BEGIN_"You are well acquainted with mystic missiles. You are the foremost among those who are 
conversant with weapons. You cause anguish even to celestials and demons. Indra and other celestials 
perceived your performance with your missiles acquired by propitiating Brahma the creator."_END

B_5_C_47_9
BEGIN_स जात मन्युः प्रसमीक्ष्य विक्रमम् |
स्थिरः स्थितः सम्यति दुर्निवारणम् |
समाहित आत्मा हनुमन्तम् आहवे |
प्रचोदयामास शरैः त्रिभिः शितैः || ५-४७-१०_END
BEGIN_Understanding Hanuma's prowess to be unrestrainable and stable in battle, that Aksha, 
exhibiting anger initially, became stable and mentally composed and incited Hanuma to battle by discharging 
three sharp arrows towards him._END

B_5_C_46_16
BEGIN_स कपिः वारयामास तम् व्योम्नि शर वर्षिणम् || ५-४६-२३
वृष्टिमन्तम् पयोदान्ते पयोदम् इव मारुतः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma warded him off from showering the arrows on him in the sky, as the wind wards 
off a rainy cloud from raining at the end of a monsoon._END

B_5_C_48_2
BEGIN_तवास्त्रबलमासाद्य ससुराः समरुद्गणाः |
न शेकुः समरे स्थातुम् सुरेश्वरसमाश्रिताः || ५-४८-३_END
BEGIN_"Celestials together with troops of storm-gods joining Indra the lord of celestials were 
not able to endure the strength of your missiles in battle."_END

B_5_C_47_10
BEGIN_ततः कपिम् तम् प्रसमीक्ष्य गर्वितम् |
जित श्रमम् शत्रु पराजयोः जितम् |
अवैक्षत अक्षः समुदीर्ण मानसः |
सबाण पाणिः प्रगृहीत कार्मुकः || ५-४७-११_END
BEGIN_Recognizing that Hanuma, as a haughty monkey, after having gallantly conquered his adversaries 
and accustomed to fatigue, that Aksha, graspign the bow and arrows his hand, saw him with an excited 
mind._END

B_5_C_46_17
BEGIN_अर्द्यमानः ततः तेन दुर्धरेण अनिल आत्मजः || ५-४६-२४
चकार निनदम् भूयो व्यवर्धत च वेगवान् |_END
BEGIN_Thus afflicted by that Durdhara, Hanuma then emitted a roar once again and swiftly expanded 
his body._END

B_5_C_48_3
BEGIN_न कश्चित्त्रिषु लोकेषु सम्युगे न गतश्रमः |
भुजवीर्याभिगुप्तश्च तपसा चाभिरक्षितः || ५-४८-४
देशकालविभागज्ञस्त्वमेव मतिसत्तमः |_END
BEGIN_"In a battle against you, every one in the three worlds gets exhausted. You are protected 
yourself by your great intellect and strong arms. You are guarded by your penance. You are aware of 
apportioning place and time properly."_END

B_5_C_46_18
BEGIN_स दूरम् सहसा उत्पत्य दुर्धरस्य रथे हरिः || ५-४६-२५
निपपात महावेगो विद्युत् राशिः गिराव् इव |_END
BEGIN_Like a mass of lightning on a mountain, Hanuma instantaneously fell on Durdhara's chariot, 
by jumping up from far above with great speed._END

B_5_C_47_11
BEGIN_स हेम निष्क अन्गद चारु कुण्डलः |
समाससाद आशु पराक्रमः कपिम् |
तयोः बभूव अप्रतिमः समागमः |
सुर असुराणाम् अपि सम्भ्रम प्रदः || ५-४७-१२_END
BEGIN_Having a glden chain, a pair of armlets and charming ear-rings, Aksha of a swift prowess, 
approached Hanuma. Their unmatched get-together in combat became a baffle to even the celestials and 
demons._END

B_5_C_48_4
BEGIN_न तेऽस्त्यशक्यम् समरेषु कर्मणा |
न तेऽस्त्यकार्यम् मतिपूर्वमन्त्रणे |
न सोऽस्ति कश्चित्त्रिषु सम्ग्रहेषु वै |
न वेद यस्तेऽस्त्रबलम् बलम् च ते || ५-४८-५_END
BEGIN_"There is nothing impossible for you in your acts of war. With your purposeful thinking, 
everything is possible for you. There is none in the three worlds, who does not know the force of missiles 
as also your (physical) strength."_END

B_5_C_46_19
BEGIN_ततः तम् मथित अष्ट अश्वम् रथम् भग्न अक्ष कूवरम् || ५-४६-२६
विहाय न्यपतत् भूमौ दुर्धरः त्यक्त जीवितः |_END
BEGIN_Losing his chariot whose axle and pole had been broken and all his eight horses destroyed, 
Durdhara then dropped down, losing his life, to the ground._END

B_5_C_47_12
BEGIN_ररास भूमिः न तताप भानुमान् |
ववौ न वायुः प्रचचाल च अचलः |
कपेः कुमारस्य च वीक्ष्य सम्युगम् |
ननाद च द्यौः उदधिः च चुक्षुभे || ५-४७-१३_END
BEGIN_Seeing that battle between Hanuma and Aksha, the earth uproared. The sun did not shine 
brightly. The wind ceased to blow. The mountain shook. The sky made a reverberant sound. The ocean too 
was agitated._END

B_5_C_48_5
BEGIN_ममानुरूपम् तपसो बलम् च ते |
पराक्रमश्चास्त्रबलम् च सम्युगे |
न त्वाम् समासाद्य रणावमर्दे |
मनः श्रमं गच्छति निश्चितार्थम् || ५-४८-६_END
BEGIN_"The strength of your penance as also your prowess and strength in battle resemble mine. 
Admitting you in the squeeze of battle, my mind does not get fatigues because of the re-assurance."_END

B_5_C_46_20
BEGIN_तम् विरूप अक्ष यूप अक्षौ दृष्ट्वा निपतितम् भुवि || ५-४६-२७
सम्जात रोषौ दुर्धर्षाव् उत्पेततुः अरिम् दमौ |_END
BEGIN_Engrossed in anger to see his fallen on the ground, the inviolable virupaksha and Yupaksha, 
the annihilators of enemies, jumped up into the air._END

B_5_C_47_13
BEGIN_ततः स वीरः सुमुखान् पतत्रिणः |
सुवर्ण पुन्खान् सविषान् इव उरगान् |
समाधि सम्योग विमोक्ष तत्त्ववित् |
शरान् अथ त्रीन् कपि मूर्ध्नि अपातयत् || ५-४७-१४_END
BEGIN_Then, that eminent demon, who correctly knew how to fix his gaze on the target, to fit 
an arrow to the bow and to discharge it, hurled on Hanuma's head, three arrows which were well-painted, 
having golden shafts and feathers and which resembled venomous serpants._END

B_5_C_48_6
BEGIN_निहताः किम्कराः सर्वे जम्बुमाली च राक्षसः |
अमात्यपुत्रा वीराश्च पञ्च सेनाग्रयायिनः || ५-४८-७
बलानि सुसमृद्धानि साश्वनागरथानि च |_END
BEGIN_"All the Kimkaras, a demon called Jambumali, the heroic sons of ministers and the five 
chiefs of army have been killed, as also the army together with highly abundant number of horses, elephants 
and chariots."_END

B_5_C_46_21
BEGIN_स ताभ्याम् सहसा उत्पत्य विष्ठितो विमले अम्बरे || ५-४६-२८
मुद्गराभ्याम् महाबाहुः वक्षसि अभिहतः कपिः |_END
BEGIN_Jumping up in the air all of a sudden those two demons struck in the chest with their 
clubs that long-armed Hanuma standing in clear sky._END

B_5_C_47_14
BEGIN_स तैः शरैः मूर्ध्नि समम् निपातितैः |
क्षरन्न् असृग् दिग्ध विवृत्त लोचनः |
नव उदित आदित्य निभः शर अंशुमान् |
व्यराजत आदित्य इव अंशु मालिकः || ५-४७-१५_END
BEGIN_Oozing the blood from his wound caused by those arrows descended into his head (by Aksha), 
looking like the newly risen sun, his eyes bathed in blood rolling rapidly, Hanuma shone brightly like 
the sun surrounded by a circle of rays, having the arrows as its rays._END

B_5_C_48_7
BEGIN_सहोदरस्ते दयितः कुमारोऽक्षश्च सूदितः || ५-४८-८
न हि तेष्वेव मे सारो यस्त्व य्यरिनिषूदन |_END
BEGIN_"Your beloved brother Aksha the prince also has been killed. O annihilator of enemies! 
The strength which is in me or in you, is indeed not there in them at all."_END

B_5_C_46_22
BEGIN_तयोः वेगवतोः वेगम् विनिहत्य महाबलः || ५-४६-२९
निपपात पुनः भूमौ सुपर्ण सम विक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_Striking down the swiftness of those violent demons, the mighty Hanuma whose prowess 
is equal to that of Garuda the eagle, again descended on to the ground._END

B_5_C_47_15
BEGIN_ततः स पिन्ग अधिप मन्त्रि सत्तमः |
समीक्ष्य तम् राज वर आत्मजम् रणे |
उदग्र चित्र आयुध चित्र कार्मुकम् |
जहर्ष च आपूर्यत च आहव उन्मुखः || ५-४७-१६_END
BEGIN_Seeing in the battle that Aksha the prince, with his marvellous weapons and picturesque 
bow, that Hanuma the excellent one among Sugree's counsellors, was rejoiced and with an inclination 
to fight, grew in size._END

B_5_C_48_8
BEGIN_इदम् हि दृष्ट्वा मतिमन् महाद्बलम् |
कपेः प्रभावम् च पराक्रमम् च |
त्वमात्मनश्चापि समीक्ष्य सारं |
कुरुष्व वेगम् स्वबलानुरूपम् || ५-४८-९_END
BEGIN_"O intelligent one! Seeing the great strength, power and prowess of this monkey and keeping 
in view your own strength, exhibit your valour accordingly."_END

B_5_C_46_23
BEGIN_स साल वृक्षम् आसाद्य समुत्पाट्य च वानरः || ५-४६-३०
ताव् उभौ राक्षसौ वीरौ जघान पवन आत्मजः |_END
BEGIN_Approaching a sala tree and uprooting it, that Hanuma the monkey killed those two valiant 
demons._END

B_5_C_47_16
BEGIN_स मन्दर अग्रस्थ इव अंशु माली |
विवृद्ध कोपो बल वीर्य सम्युतः |
कुमारम् अक्षम् सबलम् सवाहनम् |
ददाह नेत्र अग्नि मरीचिभिः तदा || ५-४७-१७_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, endowed with strength and prowess, resembling the sun appearing on a peak 
of Mandara muntain and whose anger was increased, then burnt the prince Aksha along with his army and 
vehicles, by the rays of fire emnating from his eyes._END

B_5_C_48_9
BEGIN_बलावमर्दस्वयि सम्निकृष्टे |
यथा गते शाम्यति शान्तशत्रौ |
तथा समीक्ष्यात्मबलम् परम् च |
समारभस्वास्त्रविदाम् वरिष्ठ || ५-४८-१०_END
BEGIN_"Keeping in view your own strength and of the army, O the foremost among those employing 
missiles, exert yourself in such a way, that further destruction of our army may stop, the moment you, 
whose enemies have died, have arrived near Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_46_24
BEGIN_ततः तान् त्रीन् हतान् ज्ञात्वा वानरेण तरस्विना || ५-४६-३१
अभिपेदे महावेगः प्रसह्य प्रघसो हरिम् |
भास कर्णः च सम्क्रुद्धः शूलम् आदाय वीर्यवान् || ५-४६-३२_END
BEGIN_Getting to know all those mighty three killed by Hanuma, Praghasa with a great alacrity, 
forcefully attacked Hanuma. The valiant Bhasakarna, highly enraged, attacked taking a spear in his hand._END

B_5_C_47_17
BEGIN_ततः स बाण आसन शक्र कार्मुकः |
शर प्रवर्षो युधि राक्षस अम्बुदः |
शरान् मुमोच आशु हरि ईश्वर अचले |
बलाहको वृष्टिम् इव अचल उत्तमे || ५-४७-१८_END
BEGIN_That demon in the form of a cloud, raining down arrows, then wielding a bow in the form 
of a rain-bow, soon discharged arrows on Hanuma standing in the form of a mountain, like a cloud showering 
rain on a high mountain._END

B_5_C_48_10
BEGIN_न वीरसेना गणशोच्य (प्य) वन्ति |
न वज्रमादाय विशालसारम् |
न मारुतस्यास्य गतेः प्रमाणम् |
न चाग्निकल्पः करणेन हन्तुम् || ५-४८-११_END
BEGIN_"O hero! The armies cannot protect you, even if they are in multitudes. There is no use 
taking a weapon like a strong thunder bolt against the monkey. There is no limit to the strength of 
Hanuma the son of wind-god. It is not possible to kill him, who resembles fire, by means of any weapon."_END

B_5_C_46_25
BEGIN_एकतः कपि शार्दूलम् यशस्विनम् अवस्थितौ |
पट्टिशेन शित अग्रेण प्रघसः प्रत्यपोथयत् || ५-४६-३३
भास कर्णः च शूलेन राक्षसः कपि सत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_The two generals stood by the side of the illustrious Hanuma. Praghasa pierced Hanuma 
with a sharp-pointed spear and Bhasakarna attacked him with a dart._END

B_5_C_47_18
BEGIN_ततः कपिः तम् रण चण्ड विक्रमम् |
विवृद्ध तेजो बल वीर्य सायकम् |
कुमारम् अक्षम् प्रसमीक्ष्य सम्युगे |
ननाद हर्षात् घन तुल्य विक्रमः || ५-४७-१९_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Aksha the prince, possessing an impetuous valour, endowed with enhanced splendour 
strength and vigour with a capacity to move within the sky like a cloud, coming to the battle, Hanuma 
roared with joy._END

B_5_C_48_11
BEGIN_तमेवमर्थम् प्रसमीक्ष्य सम्यक् |
स्वकर्मसाम्याद्धि समाहितात्म |
स्मरंश्च दिव्यम् धनुषोऽस्त्रवीर्यम् |
व्रजाक्षतम् कर्म समारभस्व || ५-४८-१२_END
BEGIN_"Perceiving well the fact in this way and with your mind composed by the thought that 
success can be achieved by your own effort, and remembering the strength of arrows of your wonderful 
bow, go and duly proceed with your work, without any hindrance."_END

B_5_C_46_26
BEGIN_स ताभ्याम् विक्षतैः गात्रैः असृग् दिग्ध तनू रुहः || ५-४६-३४
अभवत् वानरः क्रुद्धो बाल सूर्य सम प्रभः |_END
BEGIN_With his limbs wounded by those two demons, that Hanuma with his body-hair anointed by 
blood, became enraged, with his blaze similar to that of a rising sun._END

B_5_C_47_19
BEGIN_स बाल भावात् युधि वीर्य दर्पितः |
प्रवृद्ध मन्युः क्षतज उपम ईक्षणः |
समाससाद अप्रतिमम् रणे कपिम् |
गजो महाकूपम् इव आवृतम् तृणैः || ५-४७-२०_END
BEGIN_Boastful of his valour in battle because of his childish attitude, Aksha wit an enhanced 
fury and red-blood eyes, approached Hanuma who was incomparable in battle, as an elephant approaching 
a well covered with heaps of straw._END

B_5_C_48_12
BEGIN_न खल्वियम् मतिः श्रेष्ठा यत्त्वाम् सम्प्रेषयाम्यहम् |
इयम् च राजधर्माणाम् क्षत्रियस्य मतिर्मता || ५-४८-१३_END
BEGIN_"This thought of my sending you is not indeed the best option. But, this decision is 
said to be according to the duties of a king and is the commendation of a warrior-class."_END

B_5_C_46_27
BEGIN_समुत्पाट्य गिरेः शृन्गम् समृग व्याल पादपम् || ५-४६-३५
जघान हनुमान् वीरो राक्षसौ कपि कुन्जरः |_END
BEGIN_Having plucked up the top of a mountain with its various animals serpents and trees, 
the heroic Hanuma the best among monkeys, killed those two demons._END

B_5_C_47_20
BEGIN_स तेन बाणैः प्रसभम् निपातितैः |
चकार नादम् घन नाद निह्स्वनः |
समुत्पपात आशु नभः स मारुतिः |
भुज ऊरु विक्षेपण घोर दर्शनः || ५-४७-२१_END
BEGIN_As Aksha forcefully discharged his arrows, Hanuma roared a sound of thunder and bounced 
quickly to the sky assuming a terrible sight, stretching out his arms and thighs._END

B_5_C_48_13
BEGIN_नानाशस्त्रेषु सम्ग्रामे वैशारद्यमरिंदम् |
अवश्यमेव बोद्धव्यम् काम्यश्च विजयो रणे || ५-४८-१४_END
BEGIN_"O destroyer of enemies! You have to learn surely the skill to employ various weapons 
in battle. You have to aspire for a victory too in battle."_END

B_5_C_46_28
BEGIN_ततः तेष्व् अवसन्नेषु सेना पतिषु पन्चसु || ५-४६-३६
बलम् तत् अवशेषम् तु नाशयामास वानरः |_END
BEGIN_When those five army-generals have been killed, Hanuma then destroyed that remaining 
army._END

B_5_C_47_21
BEGIN_समुत्पतन्तम् समभिद्रवत् बली |
स राक्षसानाम् प्रवरः प्रतापवान् |
रथी रथ श्रेष्ठतमः किरन् शरैः |
पयो धरः शैलम् इव अश्म वृष्टिभिः || ५-४७-२२_END
BEGIN_That strong and valiant Aksha, the foremost among the demons, and the best among car 
warriors, went chasing Hanuma who was flying upwards, difusing arrows like a cloud showering hail-stones 
on a mountian._END

B_5_C_48_14
BEGIN_ततः पितुस्तद्वचनम् निशम्य |
प्रदक्षिणम् कक्षसुतप्रभावः |
चकार भर्तारमदीनसत्त्वो |
रणाय वीरः प्रतिपन्नबुद्धिः || ५-४८-१५_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of his father, Indrajit the strong demon, possessing a power similar 
to that of gods, with an undepressed mind and with his intellect resolved to fight, performed a circumambulation 
in honour of Ravana the lord._END

B_5_C_46_29
BEGIN_अश्वैः अश्वान् गजैः नागान् योधैः योधान् रथै रथान् || ५-४६-३७
स कपिः नाशयामास सहस्र अक्ष इव असुरान् |_END
BEGIN_Like Indra the thousand-eyed god destroying the demons, Hanuma destroyed the horses by 
striking them with horses, the elephants with elephants, the warriors with warriors and the chariots 
with chariots._END

B_5_C_47_22
BEGIN_स तान् शरान् तस्य विमोक्षयन् कपिः |
चचार वीरः पथि वायु सेविते |
शर अन्तरे मारुतवत् विनिष्पतन् |
मनो जवः सम्यति चण्ड विक्रमः || ५-४७-२३_END
BEGIN_That valiant Hanuma, whose swiftness was equal to the mind and possessing impetuous valour 
in battle, rushing forth like wind in the space between one arrow and another and thus escaping Aksha's 
arrows, moved in the path visited by wind (the sky)._END

B_5_C_48_15
BEGIN_ततसैः स्वगणैरिष्टैरिन्द्रजित् प्रतिपूजितः |
यद्धोद्धतः कृतोत्साहः सम्ग्रामम् प्रत्यपद्यत || ५-४८-१६_END
BEGIN_Acclaimed by the beloved people of his own class, Indrajit who was violent in battle 
then entered the battle-field with an accomplished enthusiasm._END

B_5_C_46_30
BEGIN_हतैः नागैः च तुरगैः भग्न अक्षैः च महारथैः || ५-४६-३८
हतैः च राक्षसैः भूमी रुद्ध मार्गा समन्ततः |_END
BEGIN_The earth had its path-ways blocked on all sides with the elephants and the horses killed, 
with the demons killed and with the big chariots which had their axles broken._END

B_5_C_49_0
BEGIN_ततः स कर्मणा तस्य विस्मितो भीम विक्रमः |
हनुमान् रोष ताम्र अक्षो रक्षो अधिपम् अवैक्षत || ५-४९-१_END
BEGIN_Then, Hanuma with a terrific prowess, was enraged (at his capture and his being dragged) 
and saw Ravana with his red hot eyes. He was surprised by that deed of Indrajit._END

B_5_C_47_23
BEGIN_तम् आत्त बाण आसनम् आहव उन्मुखम् |
खम् आस्तृणन्तम् विविधैः शर उत्तमैः |
अवैक्षत अक्षम् बहु मान चक्षुषा |
जगाम चिन्ताम् च स मारुत आत्मजः || ५-४७-२४_END
BEGIN_With a respectful faculty of sight, Hanuma saw that Aksha who was wielding his bow and 
readily inclined to fight, covering the entire sky with excellent arrows with various types of tops 
and became thoughful._END

B_5_C_48_16
BEGIN_श्रीमान् पद्मपलाशाक्षो राक्षसाधिपतेः सुतः |
निर्जगाम महातेजाः समुद्र इव पर्वसु || ५-४८-१७_END
BEGIN_Indrajit, the illustrious son of Ravana, having eyes like lotus-petals and endowed with 
extra ordinary energy, rushed forth like an ocean on full-moon days._END

B_5_C_46_31
BEGIN_ततः कपिः तान् ध्वजिनी पतीन् रणे |
निहत्य वीरान् सबलान् सवाहनान् |
तत् एव वीरः परिगृह्य तोरणम् |
कृत क्षणः काल इव प्रजा क्षये || ५-४६-३९_END
BEGIN_Like Yama the Time-spirit waiting for the right moment for the destruction of the mortals, 
the heroic Hanuma, killing the eminent demons and the army-generals with their troops and vehicles in 
the combat, waited for the right moment at the arch-way._END

B_5_C_49_1
BEGIN_भ्राजमानम् महाअर्हेण कान्चनेन विराजता |
मुक्ता जाल आवृतेन अथ मुकुटेन महाद्युतिम् || ५-४९-२_END
BEGIN_Ravana was endowed with a great splendor and shone with a glittering and precious diadem 
of gold as also encircled with strings of pearls._END

B_5_C_47_24
BEGIN_ततः शरैः भिन्न भुज अन्तरः कपिः |
कुमार वर्येण महात्मना नदन् |
महाभुजः कर्म विशेष तत्त्ववित् |
विचिन्तयामास रणे पराक्रमम् || ५-४७-२५_END
BEGIN_Then, the mighty armed Hanuma, who knew how to act under particular circumstances, roaring 
when pierced in the breast with shafts by the high souled heroic, Aksha, reflected on the prowess of 
his adversary in battle._END

B_5_C_48_17
BEGIN_स पक्षिराजोपमतुल्यवेगै |
र्व्याळैश्चतुर्भिः सिततीक्ष्णदम्ष्ट्रैः |
रथम् समायुक्तमसम्गवेगम् |
समारुरोहेन्द्रजिदिन्द्रकल्पः || ५-४८-१८_END
BEGIN_That Indrajit, alike Indra the lord of celestials, ascended a chariot with unchecked 
speed and yoked with four sharp-toothed tigers, having their swiftness similar to Garuda the king of 
eagles._END

B_5_C_49_2
BEGIN_वज्र सम्योग सम्युक्तैः महाअर्ह मणि विग्रहैः |
हैमैः आभरणैः चित्रैः मनसा इव प्रकल्पितैः || ५-४९-३_END
BEGIN_That Ravana was adorned with bright-coloured gold ornaments, inlaid with diamonds and 
decorated with worthy gems, which appeared as though they were prepared with the mind._END

B_5_C_47_25
BEGIN_अबालवत् बाल दिवा कर प्रभः |
करोति अयम् कर्म महन् महाबलः |
न च अस्य सर्व आहव कर्म शोभिनः |
प्रमापणे मे मतिः अत्र जायते || ५-४७-२६_END
BEGIN_"The mighty Aksha, possessing the lustre of a rising sun, is performing a great act, 
as a mature youth. My mind is not conceding here to kill him, who is distinguished in all acts of war-fare."_END

B_5_C_48_18
BEGIN_स रथी धन्विनाम् श्रेष्ठः शस्त्रज्ञोऽस्त्रविदाम् वरः |
रथेनाभिययौ क्षिप्रम् हनुमान्यत्र सोऽभवत् || ५-४८-१९_END
BEGIN_That Indrajit, the chariot-warrior, best among the wielders of bow, skilled in the use 
of weapons and excellent among those proficient in the use of missiles, went swiftly in his chariot 
to where Hanuma was._END

B_5_C_49_3
BEGIN_महाअर्ह क्षौम सम्वीतम् रक्त चन्दन रूषितम् |
स्वनुलिप्तम् विचित्राभिः विविधभिः च भक्तिभिः || ५-४९-४_END
BEGIN_Ravana was attired in very costly silk and his body was smeared with red-sandal paste 
and well painted with various brightly coloured designs._END

B_5_C_47_26
BEGIN_अयम् महात्मा च महान् च वीर्यतः |
समाहितः च अतिसहः च सम्युगे |
असंशयम् कर्म गुण उदयात् अयम् |
सनाग यक्षैः मुनिभिः च पूजितः || ५-४७-२७_END
BEGIN_"He possesses a great intellect and is also prominent by his valour. He is well-composed 
and highly tolerant in battle. Due to his eminent deeds and virtues, he is undoubtedly adored by saints, 
Nagas the serpent-demons and Yakshas the semi-dviine being."_END

B_5_C_48_19
BEGIN_स तस्य रथनिर्घोषम् ज्यास्वनम् कार्मुकस्य च |
निशम्य हरिवीरोऽसौ सम्प्रह्ऱ्^ष्टतरोऽभवत् || ५-४८-२०_END
BEGIN_Hearing the rattling sound of Indrajit's chariot and a twang of his bow, the heroic Hanuma 
became more thrilled with delight._END

B_5_C_49_4
BEGIN_विपुलैः दर्शनीयैः च रक्ष अक्षैः भीम दर्शनैः |
दीप्त तीक्ष्ण महादम्ष्ट्रैः प्रलम्ब दशनच् चदैः || ५-४९-५
शिरोभिः दशभिः वीरम् भ्राजमानम् महाओजसम् |
नाना व्याल समाकीर्णैः शिखरैः इव मन्दरम् || ५-४९-६_END
BEGIN_Ravana looked strange with his ten heads, having terrible-looking yet good-looking pair 
of red eyes each, with brilliant sharp enormous teeth and protruding lips, like a daring demon endowed 
with extra ordinary vigour, shining brightly as Mount Mandara with its peaks and infested with snakes 
of different varieties._END

B_5_C_47_27
BEGIN_पराक्रम उत्साह विवृद्ध मानसः |
समीक्षते माम् प्रमुख आगतः स्थितः |
पराक्रमो हि अस्य मनांसि कम्पयेत् |
सुर असुराणाम् अपि शीघ्र कारिणः || ५-४७-२८_END
BEGIN_"He is standing very much before me and looks me straight in the eyes, reassured as he 
is, by his prowess and enthusiasm. His swift-moving prowess trembles even the minds of celestials and 
demons."_END

B_5_C_48_20
BEGIN_सुमहाच्चापमादाय शितशल्यांश्च सायकान् |
हनुमन्तमभिप्रेत्य जगाम रणपण्डितः || ५-४८-२१_END
BEGIN_Indrajit, skilled in warfare, taking a very big bow with pointed arrows, went aiming 
towards Hanuma._END

B_5_C_49_5
BEGIN_नील अञ्जन चय प्रख्यम् हारेण उरसि राजता |
पूर्ण चन्द्र आभ वक्त्रेण सबलाकम् इव अम्बुदम् || ५-४९-७_END
BEGIN_Ravana was having a pearl necklace casting its splendor on his bosom. He was looking 
like a mass of blue antimony, but with his countenance shining like the full moon and appearing like 
a cloud illumined by the rising sun._END

B_5_C_47_28
BEGIN_न खल्व् अयम् न अभिभवेत् उपेक्षितः |
पराक्रमो हि अस्य रणे विवर्धते |
प्रमापणम् तु एव मम अस्य रोचते |
न वर्धमानो अग्निः उपेक्षितुम् क्षमः || ५-४७-२९_END
BEGIN_'If neglected, he would undoubtedly overpower me. His prowess is getting augmented in 
battle. The only option left out for me is to kill him now. It is not proper to neglect a spreadin fire."_END

B_5_C_48_21
BEGIN_तस्मिंस्ततः सम्यति जातहर्षे |
रणाय निर्गच्छति चापपाणौ |
दिशश्च सर्वाः कलुषा बभूवु |
र्मृगाश्च रौद्रा बहुधा विनेदुः || ५-४८-२२_END
BEGIN_While that Indrajit who was energetic in battle, was going ahead to the combat, with 
a bow in his hand, all the quarters became gloomy and ferocious animals howled in many ways._END

B_5_C_49_6
BEGIN_बाहुभिः बद्ध केयूरैः चन्दन उत्तम रूषितैः |
भ्राजमान अन्गदैः पीनैः पन्च शीर्षैः इव उरगैः || ५-४९-८_END
BEGIN_Ravana was distinguished by (twenty) arms, adorned with bracelets, smeared with excellent 
sandal-paste and decked with shining Angadas another variety of bracelets and looking like large five-hooded 
serpents._END

B_5_C_47_29
BEGIN_इति प्रवेगम् तु परस्य तर्कयन् |
स्व कर्म योगम् च विधाय वीर्यवान् |
चकार वेगम् तु महाबलः तदा |
मतिम् च चक्रे अस्य वधे महाकपिः || ५-४७-३०_END
BEGIN_The valiant and te mighty Hanuma, reflecting thus about the swiftness of the adersary 
and determining his own couse of action, then acquired a course of action, then acquired a momentum 
and also made up his mind to kill him._END

B_5_C_48_22
BEGIN_समागतास्तत्र तु नागयक्षा |
महर्षयश्चक्रचराश्च सिद्धाः |
नभः समावृत्य च पक्षिसम्घा |
विनेदुरुच्चैः परमप्रहृष्टाः || ५-४८-२३_END
BEGIN_Nagas and Yakshas, great sages moving in astronomical circles, Siddhas and a multitude 
of birds going around the sky, gathered there and clamoured loudly with a great rejoice._END

B_5_C_49_7
BEGIN_महति स्फाटिके चित्रे रत्न सम्योग संस्कृते |
उत्तम आस्तरण आस्तीर्णे उपविष्टम् वर आसने || ५-४९-९_END
BEGIN_He was comfortably seated on a big excellent throne of crystal, rendered picturesque 
by being embedded with jewels and overspread with an exquisite covering._END

B_5_C_47_30
BEGIN_स तस्य तान् अष्ट हयान् महाजवान् |
समाहितान् भार सहान् विवर्तने |
जघान वीरः पथि वायु सेविते |
तल प्रहालैः पवन आत्मजः कपिः || ५-४७-३१_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, the heroic son of wind, killed using the blows of his palm, those eight 
horses posessing a great speed in the path of sky with alertness as also having a capacity to bear burden 
while turning to different directions._END

B_5_C_48_23
BEGIN_आयान्तम् सरथम् द्ऱ्^ष्ट्वा तूर्णमन्द्रिजितम् कपिः |
विननाद महानादम् व्यवर्धत च वेगवान् || ५-४८-२४_END
BEGIN_Seeing Indrajit coming swiftly with the chariot, Hanuma made a noise with great resonance 
and grew up his body speedily._END

B_5_C_49_8
BEGIN_अलम्कृताभिः अत्यर्थम् प्रमदाभिः समन्ततः |
वाल व्यजन हस्ताभिः आरात् समुपसेवितम् || ५-४९-१०_END
BEGIN_He was duly waited upon at close quarters on all sides by young ladies, well-adorned 
and with whisks in their hands._END

B_5_C_47_31
BEGIN_ततः तलेन अभिहतो महारथः |
स तस्य पिन्ग अधिप मन्त्रि निर्जितः |
स भग्न नीडः परिमुक्त कूबरः |
पपात भूमौ हत वाजिः अम्बरात् || ५-४७-३२_END
BEGIN_Then, the great chariot of Aksha, thus struck by the palm and subdued by Hanuma the counsellor 
of Sugreeva, had its interior broken, its carriage pole loosened and its horses dead and fallen from 
the sky to the ground._END

B_5_C_48_24
BEGIN_इन्द्रजित्तु रथम् दिव्यमास्थितश्चित्रकार्मुकः |
धनुर्विष्फारयामास तटिदूर्जितनिस्स्वनम् || ५-४८-२५_END
BEGIN_Ascending on his wonderful chariot and wielding a colourful bow, Indrajit on his part, 
stretched his bow, which made a glaring sound like that accompanying a stroke lightning._END

B_5_C_49_9
BEGIN_दुर्धरेण प्रहस्तेन महापार्श्वेन रक्षसा |
मन्त्रिभिः मन्त्र तत्त्वज्ञैः निकुम्भेन च मन्त्रिणा || ५-४९-११
उप उपविष्टम् रक्षोभिः चतुर्भिः बल दर्पितैः |
कृत्स्नैः परिवृतम् लोकम् चतुर्भिः इव सागरैः || ५-४९-१२_END
BEGIN_He was proud of his might and had four counselors sitting nearby, all belonging to the 
demonical race and who knew the secret of good counsel, viz. Durdhara, Prahasta, Mahaparshva the demon 
and the counselor Nikumbha and looked like the entire terrestrial globe enclosed by four oceans._END

B_5_C_47_32
BEGIN_स तम् परित्यज्य महारथो रथम् |
सकार्मुकः खड्ग धरः खम् उत्पतत् |
तपो अभियोगात् ऋषिः उग्र वीर्यवान् |
विहाय देहम् मरुताम् इव आलयम् || ५-४७-३३_END
BEGIN_Leaving the chariot, wielding the bow and sword, that Aksha the chariot-warrior leapt 
to the sky. Having a terrible power of penance and leaving his body like a sage, he then was seen departing 
to heaven because of his Yogic penance._END

B_5_C_48_25
BEGIN_ततः समेतावतितीक्ष्णवेगौ |
महाबलौ तौ रणनिर्विशङ्कौ |
कपिश्च रक्षोधिपतेस्तनूजः |
सुरासुरेन्द्रनिव बद्धवैरौ || ५-४८-२६_END
BEGIN_Those two warriors, Hanuma and Indrajit, possessing great velocity and a great strength 
as also fearless in combat, confronted in the battle like Indra the Lord of celestials and Ravana the 
Lord of demons who tightened hostility with each other._END

B_5_C_49_10
BEGIN_मन्त्रिभिः मन्त्र तत्त्वज्ञैः अन्यैः च शुभ बुद्धिभिः |
अश्वास्यमानम् सचिवैः सुरैः इव सुर ईश्वरम् || ५-४९-१३_END
BEGIN_He was being reassured by counselors knowing the secret of good counsel and other demons 
with auspicious minds, as Indra the lord of celestials is reassured by celestials._END

B_5_C_47_33
BEGIN_ततः कपिः तम् विचरन्तम् अम्बरे |
पतत्रि राजा अनिल सिद्ध सेविते |
समेत्य तम् मारुत वेग विक्रमः |
क्रमेण जग्राह च पादयोः दृढम् || ५-४७-३४_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, Hanuma with his prowess equal to that of wind, approaching Aksha moving in 
the sky, which is often frequented by Garuda the eagle, the wind and Siddhas the ascetics endowed with 
supernatural powers, slowly grasped his feet firmly._END

B_5_C_48_26
BEGIN_स तस्य वीरस्य महारथस्य |
धनुष्मतः सम्यति सम्मतस्य |
शरप्रवेगम् व्यहनत्प्रवृद्ध |
श्चचार मार्गे पितुरप्रमेयः || ५-४८-२७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, of immeasurable strength, having expanded his body, aborted the swiftness of 
arrows of that Indrajit, the great chariot-warrior, the wielder of a bow and well-renowned in battle. 
Hanuma wheeled about in the path of wind-god, his father._END

B_5_C_49_11
BEGIN_अपश्यत् राक्षस पतिम् हनूमान् अतितेजसम् |
विष्ठितम् मेरु शिखरे सतोयम् इव तोयदम् || ५-४९-१४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma saw Ravana with a great splendor, sitting on the throne, looking like a rainy 
cloud on the peak of Mount Meru._END

B_5_C_47_34
BEGIN_स तम् समाविध्य सहस्रशः कपिः |
महाउरगम् गृह्य इव अण्डज ईश्वरः |
मुमोच वेगात् पितृ तुल्य विक्रमो |
मही तले सम्यति वानर उत्तमः || ५-४७-३५_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, with a prowess equal to that of wind-god, his father, and the excellent 
one among monkeys, spigning round Aksha like grasping a great serpent an eagle for a thousand times 
in the battle, hurled him down to the floor rapidly._END

B_5_C_48_27
BEGIN_ततः श्रानायततीक्ष्णशल्यान् |
सुपत्रिणः काञ्चनचित्रपुङ्खान् |
मुमोच वीरः परवीरहन्ता |
सुनन्नतान् वज्रनिपातवेगान् || ५-४८-२८_END
BEGIN_Then, the heroic Indrajit, the destroyer of strong enemies, discharged long and sharp-pointed 
arrows, having beautiful feathers, provided with picturesque golden shafts, with good inclination and 
as swift as lightning._END

B_5_C_49_12
BEGIN_स तैः सम्पीड्यमानो अपि रक्षोभिः भीम विक्रमैः |
विस्मयम् परमम् गत्वा रक्षो अधिपम् अवैक्षत || ५-४९-१५_END
BEGIN_Though tortured by the demons that Hanuma, of terrific prowess, experiencing a great 
surprise, looked attentively at Ravana._END

B_5_C_47_35
BEGIN_स भग्न बाहु ऊरु कटी शिरो धरः |
क्षरन्न् असृन् निर्मथित अस्थि लोचनः |
स भिन्न संधिः प्रविकीर्ण बन्धनो |
हतः क्षितौ वायु सुतेन राक्षसः || ५-४७-३६_END
BEGIN_With his arms, thighs, hips and neck broken, blood dripping, his bones and eyes crushed, 
his joints displaced and his sinews shattered, that demon was killed by Hanuma._END

B_5_C_48_28
BEGIN_ततः स तत्स्यन्दननिःस्वनम् च |
मृदङ्गभेरीपटहस्वनम् च |
विकृष्यमाणस्य च कार्मुकस्य |
निशम्य घोषम् पुनरुत्पपात || ५-४८-२९_END
BEGIN_Hearing the rattling sound of the chariot and the sound of wooden tomtoms, kettledrums 
and war-drums as also the sound of the bow-string being plucked, Hanuma sprang up again._END

B_5_C_49_13
BEGIN_भ्राजमानम् ततो दृष्ट्वा हनुमान् राक्षस ईश्वरम् |
मनसा चिन्तयामास तेजसा तस्य मोहितः || ५-४९-१६_END
BEGIN_Seeing the glittering Ravana, the king of demons, Hanuma was bewildered by his splendor 
and thought in his mind as follows:_END

B_5_C_47_36
BEGIN_महाकपिः भूमि तले निपीड्य तम् |
चकार रक्षो अधिपतेः महत् भयम् |
महर्षिभिः चक्र चरैः महाव्रतैः |
समेत्य भूतैः च सयाक्ष पन्नगैः |
सुरैः च स इन्द्रैः भृश जात विस्मयैः |
हते कुमारे स कपिः निरीक्षितः || ५-४७-३७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, having crushed him on the ground, created a great fear to Ravana. Aksha, thus 
having been killed, Hanuma was gazed on with excessive astonishment by great sages who move everywhere 
without obstruction and having great voes as also by spirits Yakshas the semidivine beings, Pannagas 
the serpent-demons and by celestials with Indra the lord of celestials._END

B_5_C_48_29
BEGIN_शराणामन्तरेष्वाशु व्यवर्तत महाकपिः |
हरिस्तस्याभिलक्ष्यस्य मोघयन् लक्ष्यसम्ग्रहम् || ५-४८-३०_END
BEGIN_Making the total target of Indrajit who was skilled in hitting his target useless, Hanuma 
the great monkey swiftly wheeled about between the arrows._END

B_5_C_49_14
BEGIN_अहो रूपम् अहो धैर्यम् अहो सत्त्वम् अहो द्युतिः |
अहो राक्षस राजस्य सर्व लक्षण युक्तता || ५-४९-१७_END
BEGIN_"What figure, what courage, what strength, what splendor and what amalgam of auspicious 
marks, alas, this king of demons has!"_END

B_5_C_47_37
BEGIN_निहत्य तम् वज्र सुत उपम प्रभम् |
कुमारम् अक्षम् क्षतज उपम ईक्षणम् |
तत् एव वीरो अभिजगाम तोरणम् |
कृत क्षणः काल इव प्रजा क्षये || ५-४७-३८_END
BEGIN_Killing that Aksha, possessing a lustre equal to that of Jayanta the son of Indra the 
lord of celestials and having his eyes resembling blood, the heroic Hanuma reached the same archy door 
way again, like Yama the lord of death expecting in a moment any mortal getting destroyed by him._END

B_5_C_48_30
BEGIN_शराणामग्रतस्तस्य पुनः समभिवर्तत |
प्रसार्य हस्तौ हनुमानुत्पपातानिलात्मजः || ५-४८-३१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the son of wind-god, again stayed in front of his arrows and stretching out his 
hands, sprang up._END

B_5_C_49_15
BEGIN_यदि अधर्मो न बलवान् स्यात् अयम् राक्षस ईश्वरः |
