स्यात् अयम् सुर लोकस्य सशक्रस्य अपि रक्षिता || ५-४९-१८_END
BEGIN_"Had this lord of demons perhaps not strong in unrighteousness, he would have been a 
protector of even the world of celestials together with Indra the lord of celestials."_END

B_5_C_48_31
BEGIN_तावुभौ वेगसम्पन्नौ रणकर्मविशारदौ |
सर्वभूतमनोग्राहि चक्रतुर्युद्धमुत्तमम् || ५-४८-३२_END
BEGIN_Those two warriors, full of swiftness and skilled in their war-fare, staged an excellent 
battle, which captivated the minds of all beings._END

B_5_C_49_16
BEGIN_अस्य क्रूरैर्नृशम् सैश्च कर्मभिर्लोककुत्सितैः |
सर्वे बिभ्यति खल्वस्माल्लोकाः सामरदानवाः || ५-४९-१९
अयम् ह्युत्सह्ते क्रुद्धः कर्तुमेकार्णवम् जगत् |_END
BEGIN_"By his cruel and violent acts despised by the world, all people including gods and demons 
indeed remain frightened of him. If enraged he is indeed capable to turn the entire world into a single 
ocean."_END

B_5_C_48_32
BEGIN_हनुमतो वेद न राक्षसोऽन्त्रम् |
न मारुतिस्तस्य महात्मनोऽन्तरम् |
परस्परम् निर्विषहौ बभूवतुः |
समेत तौ देवसमानविक्रमौ || ५-४८-३३_END
BEGIN_Indrajit could not know the weakness of Hanuma, nor did Hanuma know the weakness of high-minded 
Indrajit. Those two warriors, who were equal in prowess to gods, coming into collision with each other, 
became unbearable to each other._END

B_5_C_49_17
BEGIN_इति चिन्ताम् बहु विधाम् अकरोन् मतिमान् कपिः |
दृष्ट्वा राक्षस राजस्य प्रभावम् अमित ओजसः || ५-४९-२०_END
BEGIN_Seeing the power of Ravana the king of demons, who possessed an unlimited vigour, the 
intelligent Hanuma formulated many kinds of thoughts in this way._END

B_5_C_48_33
BEGIN_ततस्तु लक्ष्ये स विहन्यमाने |
शरेष्वमोघेषु च संपतत्सु |
जगाम चिन्ताम् महतीम् महात्मा |
समाधिसम्योगसमाहितात्मा || ५-४८-३४_END
BEGIN_The aim of his arrows getting aborted and even his unfailing arrows falling down, the 
high-minded Indrajit, who was well-known for hitting his target, got hold of a great thought._END

B_5_C_48_34
BEGIN_ततो मतिम् राक्षसराजसूनु |
श्चकार तस्मिन् हरिवीरमुख्ये |
अवध्यताम् तस्य कपेः समीक्ष्य |
कथम् निगच्छेदिति निग्रहार्थम् || ५-४८-३५_END
BEGIN_Keeping in view of that monkey being incapable of being slain, Indrajit, Ravana's son 
then formed an idea as to how to resort to capture of that Hanuma the chief of monkey-warriors._END

B_5_C_48_35
BEGIN_ततः पैतामहम् वीरः सोऽस्त्रमस्त्रविदाम् वरः |
संदधे सुमहातेजास्तम् हरिप्रारम् प्रति || ५-४८-३६_END
BEGIN_That warrior, Indrajit, excellent among the knowers of missiles and possessing a great 
splendor, then fitted to his bow, a missile presided over by Brahma the creator._END

B_5_C_48_36
BEGIN_अवध्योऽयमिति ज्ञात्वा तमस्त्रेणास्त्रतत्त्ववित् |
निजग्राह महाबाहुर्मारुतात्मजमिन्द्रजित् || ५-४८-३७_END
BEGIN_Indrajit, who knows the true nature of missiles, feeling certain that he was incapable 
of being killed, bound that Hanuma, the son of wind-god, by that presided over by Brahma the creator._END

B_5_C_48_37
BEGIN_तेन बद्धस्ततोऽस्त्रेण राक्षसेन स वानरः |
अभवन्निर्विचेष्टश्च पपात स महीतले || ५-४८-३८_END
BEGIN_Fastened with the weapon discharged by the demon, Hanuma became motionless and fell down 
on the ground._END

B_5_C_48_38
BEGIN_ततोऽथ बुद्ध्वा स तदस्त्रबन्धम् |
प्रभोः प्रभावाद्विगतात्मवेगः |
पितामहानुग्रहमात्मनश्च |
विचिन्तयामास हरिप्रवीतः || ५-४८-३९_END
BEGIN_Realizing that he had been bound by a missile presided over by Brahma the Lord of creation 
that Hanuma failing to keep his swiftness, considered it to be a favour of Brahma the creator done to 
him._END

B_5_C_48_39
BEGIN_ततह् स्वायम्भुवैर्मन्रैर्ब्रह्मस्त्रमभिमन्त्रितम् |
हनुमांश्चिन्तयामास वरदानम् पितामहात् || ५-४८-४०_END
BEGIN_Knowing it to be a missile presided over by Brahma the creator and consecrated by spells 
sacred to Brahma, the creator, Hanuma then recollected a boon got by Lord Brahma, the grand father of 
the entire creation._END

B_5_C_48_40
BEGIN_न मेऽस्त्रबन्धस्य च शक्तिरस्ति |
मिमोक्षणे लोकगुरोः प्रभावात् |
इत्येव मत्वा विहितोऽस्त्रबन्धो |
मयात्मयोनेरनुवर्तितव्यः || ५-४८-४१_END
BEGIN_"I have no capacity to liberate from the bondage of the missile due to the power of Brahma 
the father of the world. Thus knowing the bondage, through the missile presided over by Brahma the self-born 
creator imposed by the enemy, it must be obeyed by me."_END

B_5_C_48_41
BEGIN_स वीर्यमस्त्रस्य कपिर्विचार्य |
पितामहानुग्रहमात्मनश्च |
विमोक्षशक्तिम् परिचिन्तयित्वा |
पितामाहाज़्ज़्नामनुवर्तते स्म || ५-४८-४२_END
BEGIN_Thinking of the potency of the missile and the grace of Brahma, the grandfather of the 
entire creation enjoyed by him, and thinking about his capacity to liberate from it (which was going 
to alight on him after a while) that Hanuma obeyed the command of Brahma the grand father of the entire 
creation._END

B_5_C_48_42
BEGIN_अस्त्रेणापि हि बद्धस्य भयम् मम न जायते |
पितामहम् हेन्द्राभ्याम् रक्षितस्यानिलेन च || ५-४८-४३_END
BEGIN_"Since I am being protected by Brahma, Indra and the wind-god, I do not have fear, eventhough 
I am fastened by the missile."_END

B_5_C_48_43
BEGIN_ग्रहणे चापि रक्षोभिर्महन्मे गुणदर्शनम् |
राक्षसेन्द्रेण सम्वादस्तस्माद्गृह्णन्तु माम् परे || ५-४८-४४_END
BEGIN_"Even if I were captured by the demons, a great advantage is foreseen. There will be 
a dialogue with Ravana. Therefore, let the enemies capture me."_END

B_5_C_48_44
BEGIN_स निश्चितार्थः परवीरहन्ता |
समीक्ष्यकारी विनिवृत्तचेष्टः |
परैः प्रसह्याभिगतैर्निगृह्य |
ननाद तैस्तैः परिभर्त्स्यमानः || ५-४८-४५_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, the destroyer of enemies and who acted after fully considering the pros 
and cons, ascertained his objective and stayed motionless. Approached and captured forcibly by the enemies 
as also frightened by them, he made a loud scream._END

B_5_C_48_45
BEGIN_ततस्तम् राक्षसा दृष्ट्वा निर्विचेष्टमरिंदमम् |
बबन्धुः शणवल्कैश्च द्रुमचीरैश्च सम्हतैः || ५-४८-४६_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Hanuma, the destroyer of enemies falling motionless, the demons then tied 
him with plaited chords of hemp and bark of trees._END

B_5_C_48_46
BEGIN_स रोचयामास परैश्च बन्धनम् |
प्रश्य वीरैरभिनिग्रहम् च |
कौरूहलान्माम् यदि राक्षसेन्द्रो |
द्रष्टो व्यवस्येदिति निश्चितार्थः || ५-४८-४७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma approved of being forcibly bound and reviled by the enemies, with an assured feeling 
that Ravana was curious as he was, to see him._END

B_5_C_48_47
BEGIN_स बद्धस्तेन वल्केन विमुक्तोऽस्त्रेण वीर्यवान् |
अस्त्रबन्धः स चान्यम् हि न बन्धमनुवर्तते || ५-४८-४८_END
BEGIN_That powerful Hanuma, tied with those chords of hemp and bark, was relieved of the missile, 
since the bondage of that missile does not indeed coexist with another bondage._END

B_5_C_48_48
BEGIN_अथेन्द्रजित्तु द्रुमचीरबद्धम् |
विचार्य वीरः कपिसत्तमम् तम् |
विमुक्तमस्त्रेण जगाम चिन्ताम् |
नान्येन बद्धो ह्यनुवर्ततेऽस्त्रम् || ५-४८-४९_END
BEGIN_Conceiving that Hanuma the foremost among the monkeys, bound with the bark of trees, 
as having been relieved of the missile, the heroic Indrajit, on his part, then became thoughtful as 
follows: "A person tied with other means cannot indeed be bound again by the missile."_END

B_5_C_48_49
BEGIN_अहो महत्कर्म कृतम् निरर्थकम् |
न राक्षसैर्मन्त्रगतिर्विमृष्टा |
पुनश मन्त्रे विहतेऽस्त्रमन्य |
त्प्रवर्तते संशयिताः स्म सर्वे || ५-४८-५०_END
BEGIN_"Alas! My great exploit has been rendered futile. The scope of the mystic formula has 
not been considered by the demons. Once the spell has been made ineffective, another missile cannot 
be operative. All of us became jeopardized."_END

B_5_C_48_50
BEGIN_अस्त्रेण हनुमान् मुक्तो नात्मानमवबुध्यत |
कृष्यमाणस्तु रक्षोभिस्तैश्च बन्धैर्निपीडितः || ५-४८-५१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, liberated from the missile being dragged away by the demons and afflicted by 
the ties of ropes, could not realize that he was liberated from the missile._END

B_5_C_48_51
BEGIN_हन्यमानस्ततः क्रूरै राक्षसैः काष्ठमुष्टिभिः |
समीपे राक्षसेन्द्रस्य प्राकृष्यत स वानरः || ५-४८-५२_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, then being beaten with sticks and fists by the cruel demons, was dragged 
to the vicinity of Ravana._END

B_5_C_48_52
BEGIN_अथेन्द्रजित्तम् प्रसमीक्ष्य मुक्त |
मस्त्रेण बद्धम् द्रुमचीरसूत्रैः |
व्यदर्शयत्तत्र महाबलम् तम् |
हरिप्रवीरम् सगणाय राज्ञे || ५-४८-५३_END
BEGIN_Then, recognizing that Hanuma, tied with barks of trees and ropes, but liberated by the 
missile, Indrajit slowed that mighty Hanuma the jewel among the monkeys, to Ravana there sitting along 
with a body of his attendants._END

B_5_C_48_53
BEGIN_तम् मत्तमिव मातङ्गम् बद्धम् कपिवरोत्तमम् |
राक्षसा राक्षसेन्द्राय रावणाय न्यवेदयन् || ५-४८-५४_END
BEGIN_The demons showed to Ravana, the king of demons that captured Hanuma, the jewel among 
the foremost of monkeys who looked like an elephant in rut._END

B_5_C_48_54
BEGIN_कोऽयम् कस्य कुतो वात्र किम् कार्यम् को व्यपाश्रयः |
इति राक्षसवीराणाम् तत्र सम्ज्ज्ञिरे कथेः || ५-४८-५५_END
BEGIN_So went round the following conversations from the heroic demons there: "Who is this 
being? Whose savant is he? Where has he come from? What is his pursuit? Who is his alley?"_END

B_5_C_48_55
BEGIN_हन्यताम् दह्यताम् वापि भक्ष्यतामिति चापरे |
राक्षसास्तत्र सम्क्रुद्धाः परस्परमथाब्रुवन् || ५-४८-५६_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, some demons, highly enraged, said to one another as follows: "Let this monkey 
be killed, even roasted alive and devoured."_END

B_5_C_48_56
BEGIN_अत्तित्य मार्गम् सहसा महात्मा |
स तत्र रक्षोधिपपादमूले |
ददर्श राज्ञः परिचारवृद्धान् |
गृहम् महारत्नविभूषितम् च || ५-४८-५७_END
BEGIN_After crossing over the path swiftly, the high-souled Hanuma saw there the palace of 
Ravana, decorated with highly precious stones and his elderly attendants sitting at the feet of Ravana._END

B_5_C_48_57
BEGIN_स ददर्श महातेजा रावणः कपिसत्तमम् |
रक्षोभिर्विकृताकारैः कृष्यमाणमितस्ततः || ५-४८-५८_END
BEGIN_That Ravana, who was endowed with an extraordinary energy, saw Hanuma the foremost of 
monkeys, being dragged hither and thither by demons of ugly countenance._END

B_5_C_48_58
BEGIN_राक्षसाधिपतिम् चापि ददर्श कपिसत्तमः |
तेजोबलसमायुक्तम् तपन्त मिव भास्करम् || ५-४८-५९_END
BEGIN_Hanuma the jewel among the monkeys also saw Ravana the king of demons, charged with luster 
and strength and blazing like the sun._END

B_5_C_50_0
BEGIN_तम् उद्वीक्ष्य महाबाहुः पिन्ग अक्षम् पुरतः स्थितम् |
रोषेण महता आविष्टो रावणो लोक रावणः || ५-५०-१
स राजा रोष ताम्र अक्षः प्रहस्तम् मन्त्रि सत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_That Ravana, the long-armed, who caused people to cry, looking up at that monkey standing 
in front of him, was affected with violent anger, having his mind seized with suspicion, speculated 
(as follows) about Hanuma, the jewel among the monkeys, who was invested with splendour._END

B_5_C_48_59
BEGIN_स रोषसम्वर्तितताम्रदृष्टि |
र्दशाननस्तम् कपिमन्ववेक्ष्य |
अथोपविष्टान् कुलशीलवृद्धन् |
समादिशत्तम् प्रति मन्त्रिमुख्यान् || ५-४८-६०_END
BEGIN_That Ravana, rolling his red-hot eyes with rage by seeing that Hanuma and thereafter 
seeing his important ministers who were elder to his by clan and character sitting there, ordered them 
to interrogate Hanuma._END

B_5_C_50_1
BEGIN_किमेष भगवान्नन्दी भवेत्साक्षादिहागतः || ५-५०-२
येन शप्तोऽस्मि कैलासे मया संचालिते पुरा |
सोऽयम् वानरमूर्तिः स्यात्किंस्विद्बाणो महासुरः || ५-५०-३_END
BEGIN_"When Mount Kailasa was moved by me, is it the same Nandi the divine bull (attendant 
of Siva) which cursed me long ago and came here now in this form or whether he is Bana the great demon 
(son of Bali) came here in the form of a monkey."_END

B_5_C_48_60
BEGIN_यथाक्रमम् तैः स कपिर्विपृष्टः |
कार्यार्थमर्थस्य च मूलमादौ |
निवेदयामास हरीश्वरस्य |
दूतः सकाशादहमागतोऽस्मि || ५-४८-६१_END
BEGIN_Questioned, as per order, by those ministers as to the purpose of his operation and the 
motive of his act, that Hanuma at the outset informed, "I came from Sugreeva as an envoy."_END

B_5_C_50_2
BEGIN_स राजा रोषताम्राक्षः प्रहस्तम् मन्त्रिसत्तमम् |
काल युक्तम् उवाच इदम् वचो विपुलम् अर्थवत् || ५-५०-४_END
BEGIN_That king Ravana, becoming enraged with red hot eyes, spoke the following concise and 
meaningful words relevant to that occasion, to Prahasta, his chief of ministers._END

B_5_C_50_3
BEGIN_दुरात्मा पृच्छ्यताम् एष कुतः किम् वा अस्य कारणम् |
वन भन्गे च को अस्य अर्थो राक्षसीनाम् च तर्जने || ५-५०-५_END
BEGIN_"Ask this wicked monkey from where did he come, for what reason did he come to this place 
and for what purpose did he frighten the female-demons in destroying our garden."_END

B_5_C_50_4
BEGIN_मत्पुरीमप्रधृष्याम् वागमने किं प्रयोजनम् |
आयोधने वाकिं कार्यम् पृच्छ्यतामेष दुर्मतिः ||५-५०-६_END
BEGIN_"Ask this evil-minded monkey as to what really is his purpose in coming over to my invincible 
City and what pursuit he is doing this battle."_END

B_5_C_50_5
BEGIN_रावणस्य वचः श्रुत्वा प्रहस्तो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |
समाश्वसिहि भद्रम् ते न भीः कार्या त्वया कपे || ५-५०-७_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Ravana, Prahasta spoke the following words to Hanuma, "Take courage! 
Happiness to you! You need not get frightened, O monkey!"_END

B_5_C_51_0
BEGIN_तम् समीक्ष्य महासत्त्वम् सत्त्ववान् हारि सत्तमः |
वाक्यम् अर्थवत् अव्यग्रः तम् उवाच दश आननम् || ५-५१-१_END
BEGIN_Seeing that highly energetic Ravana, the courageous Hanuma coolly spoke to him the following 
meaningful words:_END

B_5_C_50_6
BEGIN_यदि तावत् त्वम् इन्द्रेण प्रेषितो रावण आलयम् |
तत्त्वम् आख्याहि मा ते भूत् भयम् वानर मोक्ष्यसे || ५-५०-८_END
BEGIN_"O monkey! If Indra has sent you to the abode of Ravana, tell me the truth. Do not have 
fear. You will be released."_END

B_5_C_51_1
BEGIN_अहम् सुग्रीव संदेशात् इह प्राप्तः तव आलयम् |
राक्षस इन्द्र हरि ईशः त्वाम् भ्राता कुशलम् अब्रवीत् || ५-५१-२_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! By the command of Sugreeva, I came here to your abode. Sugreeva, the 
Lord of monkeys, your brother, asked me to enquire about your welfare._END

B_5_C_50_7
BEGIN_यदि वैश्रवणस्य त्वम् यमस्य वरुणस्य च |
चारु रूपम् इदम् कृत्वा ओरवुष्टो नः पुरीमिमाम् || ५-५०-९
विष्णुना प्रेषितो वा अपि दूतो विजय कान्क्षिणा |_END
BEGIN_"Are you, the one who has entered our city, assuming the guise of a spy, sent by Kubera 
the god of riches or by Yama the god of death or by Varuna the lord of the sea or whether sent by Vishnu 
the lord of preservation, as a messenger, longing for a victory?"_END

B_5_C_51_2
BEGIN_भ्रातुः शृणु समादेशम् सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
धर्म अर्थ उपहितम् वाक्यम् इह च अमुत्र च क्षमम् || ५-५१-३_END
BEGIN_"Hear the righteous and meaningful words, as a following advice, of the high-souled Sugreeva, 
your brother, conducive to good in the world as well as in the other world."_END

B_5_C_50_8
BEGIN_न हि ते वानरम् तेजो रूप मात्रम् तु वानरम् || ५-५०-१०
तत्त्वतः कथयस्व अद्य ततो वानर मोक्ष्यसे |_END
BEGIN_"O monkey! Your form alone is that of a monkey. Your splendour indeed is not that of 
a monkey. Now, tell me the truth. Thereupon, you will be released."_END

B_5_C_51_3
BEGIN_राजा दशरथो नाम रथ कुन्जर वाजिमान् |
पिता इव बन्धुः लोकस्य सुर ईश्वर सम द्युतिः || ५-५१-४_END
BEGIN_"There was a king named Dasaratha, having chariots, elephants and horses, like a father 
to the people and endowed with a splendour equal to that of Indra the lord of celestials."_END

B_5_C_50_9
BEGIN_अनृतम् वदतः च अपि दुर्लभम् तव जीवितम् || ५-५०-११
अथवा यन् निमित्तः ते प्रवेशो रावण आलये |_END
BEGIN_"If you tell a lie, your survival will be difficult. Or else, tell me the purpose of 
your entry into Ravana's abode."_END

B_5_C_51_4
BEGIN_ज्येष्ठः तस्य महाबाहुः पुत्रः प्रिय करः प्रभुः |
पितुः निदेशान् निष्क्रान्तः प्रविष्टो दण्डका वनम् || ५-५१-५
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा सीतया च अपि भार्यया |
रामो नाम महातेजा धर्म्यम् पन्थानम् आश्रितः || ५-५१-६_END
BEGIN_"His eldest son named Rama, having mighty arms, a bestower of affection and our lord, 
by the command of his father, abiding in a righteous path, went out on exile and entered a forest called 
Dandaka along with Lakshmana his brother and Seetha his wife."_END

B_5_C_50_10
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तो हरि वरः तदा रक्षो गण ईश्वरम् || ५-५०-१२
अब्रवीन् न अस्मि शक्रस्य यमस्य वरुणस्य वा |
धनदेन न मे सख्यम् विष्णुना न अस्मि चोदितः || ५-५०-१३
जातिः एव मम तु एषा वानरो अहम् इह आगतः |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Prahasta, Hanuma spoke to Ravana the Lord of demons as follows, 
"I am not a messenger of Indra or Yama or Varuna. I have no friendship with Kubera the god of riches, 
nor am I instigated by Vishnu. This is just my form of existence, by my very birth. I am a monkey who 
came here."_END

B_5_C_51_5
BEGIN_तस्य भार्या वने नष्टा सीता पतिम् अनुव्रता |
वैदेहस्य सुता राज्ञो जनकस्य महात्मनः || ५-५१-७_END
BEGIN_"Seetha, wife of Rama, devoted to her husband and daughter of the high-souled king, named 
Janaka, the head of Videha kingdom, got lost in the forest."_END

B_5_C_50_11
BEGIN_दर्शने राक्षस इन्द्रस्य दुर्लभे तत् इदम् मया || ५-५०-१४
वनम् राक्षस राजस्य दर्शन अर्थे विनाशितम् |_END
BEGIN_"The sight of Ravana the King of demons is difficult to be obtained. Intent on that object 
(of sight of Ravana), the garden was destroyed by me."_END

B_5_C_51_6
BEGIN_स मार्गमाणः ताम् देवीम् राज पुत्रः सह अनुजः |
ऋश्यमूकम् अनुप्राप्तः सुग्रीवेण च सम्गतः || ५-५१-८_END
BEGIN_"That prince, Rama together with his brother, searching that lady, reached Mount Rishyamuka 
and happened to meet Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_50_12
BEGIN_ततः ते राक्षसाः प्राप्ता बलिनो युद्ध कान्क्षिणः || ५-५०-१५
रक्षण अर्थम् च देहस्य प्रतियुद्धा मया रणे |_END
BEGIN_"Then, those strong demons came with a desire to fight with me. Just for protecting my 
body, I had to attack them in battle."_END

B_5_C_51_7
BEGIN_तस्य तेन प्रतिज्ञातम् सीतायाः परिमार्गणम् |
सुग्रीवस्य अपि रामेण हरि राज्यम् निवेदितम् || ५-५१-९_END
BEGIN_"While Sugreeva promised Rama to get Seetha searched, Rama too promised to get the kingdom 
of monkeys to Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_50_13
BEGIN_अस्त्र पाशैः न शक्यो अहम् बद्धुम् देव असुरैः अपि || ५-५०-१६
पितामहात् एव वरो मम अपि एषो अभ्युपागतः |_END
BEGIN_"I am incapable of being bound by missiles and nooses even by celestials and demons. 
This boon came to me also from Brahama only."_END

B_5_C_51_8
BEGIN_ततः तेन मृधे हत्वा राज पुत्रेण वालिनम् |
सुग्रीवः स्थापितो राज्ये हरि ऋक्षाणाम् गण ईश्वरः || ५-५१-१०_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, killing Vali in a combat, Rama installed Sugreeva on the throne as a lord 
of that troop monkeys and bears."_END

B_5_C_50_14
BEGIN_राजानम् द्रष्टु कामेन मया अस्त्रम् अनुवर्तितम् || ५-५०-१७
विमुक्तो अहम् अस्त्रेण राक्षसैः तु अतिपीडितः |
केवचिद्राजकार्येण सम्प्राप्तोऽस्मि तवान्तिकम् || ५-५०-१८_END
BEGIN_With a desire to see you the king, I surrendered to the missile. Soon after bound by 
the demons, I was indeed released from the missile. I came to your presence, prompted by some mission 
of Rama."_END

B_5_C_51_9
BEGIN_त्वया विज्ञातपूर्वश्च वाली वानरपुङ्गवः |
रामेण निहतः संख्ये शरेणैकेन वानरः || ५-५१-११_END
BEGIN_"You may indeed know Vali, the foremost among monkeys, previously. Rama killed that Vali 
with a single arrow in battle."_END

B_5_C_50_15
BEGIN_दूतोऽहमिति विज्ञेयो राघवस्यामितौजसः |
श्रूयताम् चापि वचनम् मम पथ्यमिदम् प्रभो || ५-५०-१९_END
BEGIN_"O, Lord of demons! Know me to be a messenger of Rama who is possessing I am unlimited 
splendour. I am telling you a beneficial word. Listen to it."_END

B_5_C_51_10
BEGIN_स सीता मार्गणे व्यग्रः सुग्रीवः सत्य सम्गरः |
हरीन् सम्प्रेषयामास दिशः सर्वा हरि ईश्वरः || ५-५१-१२_END
BEGIN_"Sugreeva, the lord of monkeys, true to his promise, was intent on searching for Seetha 
and sent his monkeys to all directions."_END

B_5_C_51_11
BEGIN_ताम् हरीणाम् सहस्राणि शतानि नियुतानि च |
दिक्षु सर्वासु मार्गन्ते अधः च उपरि च अम्बरे || ५-५१-१३_END
BEGIN_"Hundreds, thousands and lakhs of monkeys are searching for her in all quarters, as also 
below and above in the sky."_END

B_5_C_52_0
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा वानरस्य महात्मनः |
आज्ञापयत् वधम् तस्य रावणः क्रोध मूर्चितः || ५-५२-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of the high=souled Hanuma, Ravana duly excited with anger, ordered 
for the killing of Hanuma._END

B_5_C_51_12
BEGIN_वैनतेय समाः केचित् केचित् तत्र अनिल उपमाः |
असम्ग गतयः शीघ्रा हरि वीरा महाबलाः || ५-५१-१४_END
BEGIN_"Among those monkeys, some mighty and virile monkeys are similar to Garuda the eagle. 
Some are like wind, swiftly going with an unhindered movement."_END

B_5_C_52_1
BEGIN_वधे तस्य समाज्ञप्ते रावणेन दुरात्मना |
निवेदितवतो दौत्यम् न अनुमेने विभीषणः || ५-५२-२_END
BEGIN_While it was ordered by the evil-natured Ravana for the killing of Hanuma, Vibhishana 
did not agree to the killing of Hanuma, who was entrusted with the functions of a messenger._END

B_5_C_51_13
BEGIN_अहम् तु हनुमान् नाम मारुतस्य औरसः सुतः |
सीतायाः तु कृते तूर्णम् शत योजनम् आयतम् || ५-५१-१५
समुद्रम् लन्घयित्वा एव ताम् दिदृक्षुः इह आगतः |_END
BEGIN_"I am, however, an own son of wind-god and named as Hanuma. I came here even by crossing 
quickly the ocean, which is a hundred yojanas (or eight hundred miles) wide for the sake of Seetha and 
wishing to see her."_END

B_5_C_52_2
BEGIN_तम् रक्षो अधिपतिम् क्रुद्धम् तच् च कार्यम् उपस्थितम् |
विदित्वा चिन्तयामास कार्यम् कार्य विधौ स्थितः || ५-५२-३_END
BEGIN_Seeing Ravana getting enraged and looking to that affair (of killing of an envoy) that 
has arisen, Vibhishana who was firm in accompanying any object, reflected upon an appropriate action 
to be done._END

B_5_C_51_14
BEGIN_भ्रमता च मया दृष्टा गृहे ते जनकात्मजा || ५-५१-१६
तत् भवान् दृष्ट धर्म अर्थः तपः कृत परिग्रहः |
पर दारान् महाप्राज्ञ न उपरोद्धुम् त्वम् अर्हसि || ५-५१-१७_END
BEGIN_"While strolling around in the city of Lanka, I found Seetha in your abode. You know 
about religious merit and wealth. You performed and mastered the austerities. That is why, you ought 
not besiege the wife of another, O great intellectual!"_END

B_5_C_52_3
BEGIN_निश्चित अर्थः ततः साम्ना आपूज्य शत्रुजित् अग्रजम् |
उवाच हितम् अत्यर्थम् वाक्यम् वाक्य विशारदः || ५-५२-४_END
BEGIN_Then, deciding about a right action, Vibhishna, who was silled in communication and a 
conqueror of enemies, spoke softly the following very meaningful and useful words to Ravana, his venerable 
borther._END

B_5_C_51_15
BEGIN_न हि धर्म विरुद्धेषु बह्व् अपायेषु कर्मसु |
मूल घातिषु सज्जन्ते बुद्धिमन्तो भवत् विधाः || ५-५१-१८_END
BEGIN_"Intellectuals like you indeed are not engrossed in acts, which are antagonistic to righteousness, 
which are attended with many dangers and which even ruin the doer at the roots."_END

B_5_C_52_4
BEGIN_क्षमस्व रोषम् त्यज राक्षसेन्द्र |
प्रसीद मद्वाक्यमिदम् शृणुष्व |
वधम् न कुर्वन्ति परावरज्ञा |
दूतस्य सन्तो वसुधाधिपेन्द्राः || ५-५२-५_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! Forgive and give up your anger. Be gracious and hear my words. Virtuous 
kings of excellence, knowing the distant and the near, do not cause killing of an envoy."_END

B_5_C_51_16
BEGIN_कः च लक्ष्मण मुक्तानाम् राम कोप अनुवर्तिनाम् |
शराणाम् अग्रतः स्थातुम् शक्तो देव असुरेष्व् अपि || ५-५१-१९_END
BEGIN_"Who is capable even among celestials and demons, to withstand the arrows discharged 
by Lakshmana, in the wake of the fury of Rama?_END

B_5_C_52_5
BEGIN_राजन् धर्म विरुद्धम् च लोक वृत्तेः च गर्हितम् |
तव च असदृशम् वीर कपेः अस्य प्रमापणम् || ५-५२-६_END
BEGIN_"O hero! Killing of this monkey is against a royal virtue and any universal custom condemns 
it. Hence, it is improper for you also to do it."_END

B_5_C_51_17
BEGIN_न च अपि त्रिषु लोकेषु राजन् विद्येत कश्चन |
राघवस्य व्यलीकम् यः कृत्वा सुखम् अवाप्नुयात् || ५-५१-२०_END
BEGIN_"O king! No one is known in the three worlds, who have gained happiness, by doing harm 
to Rama."_END

B_5_C_52_6
BEGIN_धर्मज्ञ्श्च कृतज्ञ्श्च राजधर्मविशारदः |
परावरज्ञो भूतानाम् त्वमेव परमार्थवित् || ५-५२-७_END
BEGIN_"You are indeed the knower of what is right. You are a person of gratitude. You are well-versed 
in royal virtues. You know both the distant and the near in beings. You know the highest truth."_END

B_5_C_51_18
BEGIN_तत् त्रिकाल हितम् वाक्यम् धर्म्यम् अर्थ अनुबन्धि च |
मन्यस्व नर देवाय जानकी प्रतिदीयताम् || ५-५१-२१_END
BEGIN_"That is why, accede to my words, which are beneficial for all the three divisions of 
time (viz. the past, present and future), resulting in affluence and respectability as well. Let Seetha 
be restored to Rama."_END

B_5_C_52_7
BEGIN_गृह्यन्ते यदि रोषेण त्वादृशोऽपि विपश्चितः |
ततः शास्त्रविपश्चित्त्वम् श्रम एव हि केवलम् || ५-५२-८_END
BEGIN_"If even learned persons like you are seized by anger, then the knowledge of scriptures 
is indeed just a labour in vain."_END

B_5_C_51_19
BEGIN_दृष्टा हि इयम् मया देवी लब्धम् यत् इह दुर्लभम् |
उत्तरम् कर्म यत् शेषम् निमित्तम् तत्र राघवः || ५-५१-२२_END
BEGIN_"I beheld Seetha, the princess. The audience of Seetha is difficult to be achieved and 
it is obtained here. It is for Rama there to decide his remaining task of future consequence."_END

B_5_C_52_8
BEGIN_तस्मात्प्रसीद शत्रुघ्न राक्षसेन्द्र दुरासद |
ततः शास्त्रविपश्चित्त्वम् श्रम एव हि केवल्म् || ५-५२-९_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! O annihilator of enemies, dangerous to be approached! Therefore, be 
graceful. After ascertaining about right and wrong, let appropriate punishment be ordered to the envoy."_END

B_5_C_51_20
BEGIN_लक्षिता इयम् मया सीता तथा शोक परायणा |
गृह्य याम् न अभिजानासि पन्च आस्याम् इव पन्नगीम् || ५-५१-२३_END
BEGIN_"Capturing Seetha, whom you do not recognize as a five-hooded female serpent in your 
abode, has been found by me in that manner, and wholly given over to sorrow."_END

B_5_C_52_9
BEGIN_विभीषणवचः श्रुत्वा रावणो राक्षसेश्वरः |
रोषेण महताविष्टो वाक्यमुत्तरमब्रवीत् || ५-५२-१०_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Vibhishana, Ravana the lord of demons was greatly enraged and replied 
in the following words:_END

B_5_C_51_21
BEGIN_न इयम् जरयितुम् शक्या सासुरैः अमरैः अपि |
विष संसृष्टम् अत्यर्थम् भुक्तम् अन्नम् इव ओजसा || ५-५१-२४_END
BEGIN_"She is incapable of being devoured with one's might even by celestials and demons, any 
more than food mixed with abundant poison could be digested with one's digestive power, if consumed."_END

B_5_C_52_10
BEGIN_न पापानाम् वधे पापम् विद्यते शत्रुसूदन |
तस्मादेनम् वधिष्यामि वानरम् पापचारिणम् || ५-५२-११_END
BEGIN_"O Vibhishana, the annihilator of enemies! There is no sin, even if the sinners are killed. 
So, I shall kill this monkey, who performed sins."_END

B_5_C_51_22
BEGIN_तपः सम्ताप लब्धः ते यो अयम् धर्म परिग्रहः |
न स नाशयितुम् न्याय्य आत्म प्राण परिग्रहः || ५-५१-२५_END
BEGIN_"It is not proper for you to lose your exceptional longevity and that fortune which is 
an outcome of your virtue, both of which have been acquired by you through the practice of austerities."_END

B_5_C_51_23
BEGIN_अवध्यताम् तपोभिः याम् भवान् समनुपश्यति |
आत्मनः सासुरैः देवैः हेतुः तत्र अपि अयम् महान् || ५-५१-२६_END
BEGIN_"You may be thinking that you are immune from death from demons and celestials, because 
of your austerities. But your opinion in that matter is not correct, on account of the following reason._END

B_5_C_52_11
BEGIN_अधर्ममूलम् बहुदोषयुक्त |
मनार्यजुष्टम् वचनम् निशम्य |
उवाच वाक्यम् परमार्थतत्त्वम् |
विभीषणो बुद्धिमताम् वरिष्ठः || ५-५२-१२_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words, rooted in unrighteousness, enveloped in a great anger and accepted 
by the dishonourable, Vibhishana the best among those who weer endowed with understanding, spoke the 
following words, comprising of the highest truth._END

B_5_C_52_12
BEGIN_प्रसीद लङ्केश्वर राक्षसेन्द्र |
धर्मार्थयुक्तम् वचनम् शृणुष्व |
दूतानवध्यान् समयेषु राजन् |
सर्वेषु सर्वत्र वदन्ति सन्तः || ५-५२-१३_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! O lord of Lanka! Be gracious enough. Hear my words endowed with righteousness 
and significance. O king! Sages say that messengers should not be killed at all places and at all times."_END

B_5_C_51_24
BEGIN_सुग्रीवो न हि देवो अयम् न असुरो न च मानुषः |
न दानवो न गन्धर्वो न यक्षो न च पन्नगः || ५-५१-२७
तस्मात् प्राण परित्राणम् कथम् राजन् करिष्यसि |_END
BEGIN_"This Sugreeva is indeed neither a god, nor Asura the chief of evil spirits nor a demon 
nor a child of Danu the demon, nor Gandharva the celestial musician nor Yaksha the semi-divine being 
nor pannaga the serpent-demon. O King! How do you protect your life from him?"_END

B_5_C_52_13
BEGIN_असंशयम् शत्रुः अयम् प्रवृद्धः |
कृतम् हि अनेन अप्रियम् अप्रमेयम् |
न दूत वध्याम् प्रवदन्ति सन्तो |
दूतस्य दृष्टा बहवो हि दण्डाः || ५-५२-१४_END
BEGIN_"There is no doubt that this enemy is arrogant. He has created an unlimited displeasure 
to us. But, sages do not talk about the killing of an envoy There are indeed severeal punishments, intended 
for an envoy."_END

B_5_C_51_25
BEGIN_न तु धर्म उपसम्हारम् अधर्म फल सम्हितम् || ५-५१-२८
तत् एव फलम् अन्वेति धर्मः च अधर्म नाशनः |_END
BEGIN_"The fruit of righteousness does not exist together with the result of unrighteousness 
(eventhough he practices virtue). That consequence of unrighteousness alone follows him. Righteousness 
in abundance destroys unrighteousness."_END

B_5_C_53_0
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा दशग्रीवो महाबलः |
देश काल हितम् वाक्यम् भ्रातुः उत्तमम् अब्रवीत् || ५-५३-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words, which were aprropriate for that place and time, spoken by that hih-souled 
Vibhishana, his brother, Ravana spoke the following words in reply:_END

B_5_C_52_14
BEGIN_वैरूप्याम् अन्गेषु कश अभिघातो |
मौण्ड्यम् तथा लक्ष्मण सम्निपातः |
एतान् हि दूते प्रवदन्ति दण्डान् |
वधः तु दूतस्य न नः श्रुतो अपि || ५-५२-१५_END
BEGIN_"Some of the punishments to an envoy are-deforming the limbs, striking with a whip, shaving 
the head and impressing marks on the body. Indeed, we have not heard at any time of killing a messenger."_END

B_5_C_51_26
BEGIN_प्राप्तम् धर्म फलम् तावत् भवता न अत्र संशयः || ५-५१-२९
फलम् अस्य अपि अधर्मस्य क्षिप्रम् एव प्रपत्स्यसे |_END
BEGIN_"You already obtained the fruit of virtue till now. There is no doubt about it. In no 
time, you will obtain the fruit of unrighteousness also."_END

B_5_C_53_1
BEGIN_सम्यग् उक्तम् हि भवता दूत वध्या विगर्हिता |
अवश्यम् तु वधात् अन्यः क्रियताम् अस्य निग्रहः || ५-५३-२_END
BEGIN_"You have spoken well indeed that killing of an envoy is forbidden. Another punishment 
other than killing needs be certainly meted out to him."_END

B_5_C_52_15
BEGIN_कथम् च धर्म अर्थ विनीत बुद्धिः |
पर अवर प्रत्यय निश्चित अर्थः |
भवत् विधः कोप वशे हि तिष्ठेत् |
कोपम् नियच्छन्ति हि सत्त्ववन्तः || ५-५२-१६_END
BEGIN_"How can a person like you, holding an intellect trained in religious merit and purpose 
and a right judgement on cause and effect, subject to anger? Wise people indeed contain their anger."_END

B_5_C_51_27
BEGIN_जन स्थान वधम् बुद्ध्वा बुद्ध्वा वालि वधम् तथा || ५-५१-३०
राम सुग्रीव सख्यम् च बुध्यस्व हितम् आत्मनः |_END
BEGIN_"Recognizing the killing of demons in the forest of Janasthana, about the killing of 
Vali and about the friendship between Rama and Sugreeva, realize your own interest."_END

B_5_C_53_2
BEGIN_कपीनाम् किल लान्गूलम् इष्टम् भवति भूषणम् |
तत् अस्य दीप्यताम् शीघ्रम् तेन दग्धेन गच्छतु || ५-५३-३_END
BEGIN_"It is said that a tail is possibly a beloved ornament for the monkeys. Let his tail 
be burn immediately. Let him go with a burnt tail."_END

B_5_C_52_16
BEGIN_न धर्म वादे न च लोक वृत्ते |
न शास्त्र बुद्धि ग्रहणेषु वा अपि |
विद्येत कश्चित् तव वीर तुल्यः |
त्वम् हि उत्तमः सर्व सुर असुराणाम् || ५-५२-१७_END
BEGIN_"O hero! There is no one equal to you, who can discuss about the law or duty, none about 
universal custom and none in capturing the essence of scriptures. You are indeed excellent among all 
the celestials and demons in these matter."_END

B_5_C_51_28
BEGIN_कामम् खल्व् अहम् अपि एकः सवाजि रथ कुन्जराम् || ५-५१-३१
लन्काम् नाशयितुम् शक्तः तस्य एष तु विनिश्चयः |_END
BEGIN_"I am indeed, even alone, undoubtedly, destroying Lanka, along with its horses, chariots 
and elephants. However, this is not in accordance with the resolution of Rama."_END

B_5_C_53_3
BEGIN_ततः पश्यन्तु इमम् दीनम् अन्ग वैरूप्य कर्शितम् |
समित्रा ज्ञातयः सर्वे बान्धवाः ससुहृज् जनाः || ५-५३-४_END
BEGIN_"Let all his relatives together with his friends, kinsmen and amicable persons then see 
him miserably injured with his deformed limbs."_END

B_5_C_52_17
BEGIN_शूरेण वीरेण निशाचरेन्द्र |
सुरासुराणामपि दुर्जयेन |
त्वया प्रगल्भाः सुरदैत्यसम्घा |
जिताश्च युद्धेष्वसकृन्नरेन्द्राः || ५-५२-१८_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! You are valiant. You are heroic. Even celestials and demons cannot 
conquer you. You conquered a multitude of proud celestials and demons together with their kings in battles 
several times"_END

B_5_C_51_29
BEGIN_रामेण हि प्रतिज्ञातम् हरि ऋक्ष गण सम्निधौ || ५-५१-३२
उत्सादनम् अमित्राणाम् सीता यैः तु प्रधर्षिता |_END
BEGIN_"For, Rama, indeed, promised in the presence of troops of monkeys and bears, about the 
extermination of enemies, by whom Seetha was actually laid violent hands upon."_END

B_5_C_53_4
BEGIN_आज्ञापयत् राक्षस इन्द्रः पुरम् सर्वम् सचत्वरम् |
लान्गूलेन प्रदीप्तेन रक्षोभिः परिणीयताम् || ५-५३-५_END
BEGIN_Ravana ordered that let the monkey be carried around with his burning tail by the demons 
in the entire city around its cross-roads."_END

B_5_C_52_18
BEGIN_न च अपि अस्य कपेः घाते कंचित् पश्यामि अहम् गुणम् |
तेष्व् अयम् पात्यताम् दण्डो यैः अयम् प्रेषितः कपिः || ५-५२-१९_END
BEGIN_"I do not see any merit in killing this monkey. Let this carnal punishment be employed 
on those by whom this monkey was sent."_END

B_5_C_51_30
BEGIN_अपकुर्वन् हि रामस्य साक्षात् अपि पुरम् दरः || ५-५१-३३
न सुखम् प्राप्नुयात् अन्यः किम् पुनः त्वत् विधो जनः |_END
BEGIN_"Even Indra the Lord of celestials, in person, cannot attain happiness if he does any 
harm to Rama. How much move to another person like you?"_END

B_5_C_53_5
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा राक्षसाः कोप कर्कशाः |
वेष्टन्ते तस्य लान्गूलम् जीर्णैः कार्पासिकैः पटैः || ५-५३-६_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Ravana, the demons, hard-tempered with their wrath, wrapped, up 
old ragged clothes around Hanuma's tail._END

B_5_C_52_19
BEGIN_साधुः वा यदि वा असाधुः परैः एष समर्पितः |
ब्रुवन् पर अर्थम् परवान् न दूतो वधम् अर्हति || ५-५२-२०_END
BEGIN_"He is a person, sent by our enemies, whether he is good or bad. It is not worthy of 
killing him, who is an envoy, who is dependent on others and who talks for the cause of others."_END

B_5_C_51_31
BEGIN_याम् सीता इति अभिजानासि या इयम् तिष्ठति ते वशे || ५-५१-३४
काल रात्री इति ताम् विद्धि सर्व लन्का विनाशिनीम् |_END
BEGIN_"Know her, whom you recognize as Seetha and who stays in your captivity, to be none else 
than Kalaratri (the goddess presiding over and responsible for dissolution), who can destroy the entire 
Lanka."_END

B_5_C_54_0
BEGIN_वीक्षमाणः ततो लन्काम् कपिः कृत मनो रथः |
वर्धमान समुत्साहः कार्य शेषम् अचिन्तयत् || ५-५४-१_END
BEGIN_Then, after fulfilling his heart's wish, Hanuma, looking over Lanka, thought about the 
remaining act to be done, with an augmented energy._END

B_5_C_53_6
BEGIN_सम्वेष्ट्यमाने लान्गूले व्यवर्धत महाकपिः |
शुष्कम् इन्धनम् आसाद्य वनेष्व् इव हुत अशनः || ५-५३-७_END
BEGIN_While his tail was being wrapped around with cotton tatters, Hanuma proliferating, soon 
after catching dry wood in forests._END

B_5_C_52_20
BEGIN_अपि च अस्मिन् हते राजन् न अन्यम् पश्यामि खे चरम् |
इह यः पुनः आगच्छेत् परम् पारम् महाउदधिः || ५-५२-२१_END
BEGIN_"O king! Moreover, If he is killed, I do not find any other person, who can travel through 
the sky and come here again to this shore of the great ocean."_END

B_5_C_54_1
BEGIN_किम् नु खल्व् अविशिष्टम् मे कर्तव्यम् इह साम्प्रतम् |
यत् एषाम् रक्षसाम् भूयः सम्ताप जननम् भवेत् || ५-५४-२_END
BEGIN_"Which act indeed is remaing nowto be done by me here, that may further create anguish 
to these demons?"_END

B_5_C_51_32
BEGIN_तत् अलम् काल पाशेन सीता विग्रह रूपिणा || ५-५१-३५
स्वयम् स्कन्ध अवसक्तेन क्षमम् आत्मनि चिन्त्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_"Therefore, have it enough of this noose of death, in the form of Seetha's personality, 
which has been placed by yourself around your neck. Think well of your safety."_END

B_5_C_53_7
BEGIN_तैलेन परिषिच्य अथ ते अग्निम् तत्र अवपातयन् |
लान्गूलेन प्रदीप्तेन राक्षसान् तान् अपातयत् || ५-५३-८
रोष अमर्ष परीत आत्मा बाल सूर्य सम आननः |_END
BEGIN_The demons sprinkled oil and set out fire on that tail. Then, Hanuma, with his face resembling 
a rising sun with his mind filled with anger and impatience and with his burning tail, threw those demons 
down._END

B_5_C_52_21
BEGIN_तस्मान् न अस्य वधे यत्नः कार्यः पर पुरम् जय |
भवान् स इन्द्रेषु देवेषु यत्नम् आस्थातुम् अर्हति || ५-५२-२२_END
BEGIN_"O conqueror of enemies! Therefore, do not make efforts to kill him. On the other hand, 
you ought to strengthen such effort on celestials including indra."_END

B_5_C_54_2
BEGIN_वनम् तावत् प्रमथितम् प्रकृष्टा राक्षसा हताः |
बल एक देशः क्षपितः शेषम् दुर्ग विनाशनम् || ५-५४-३_END
BEGIN_"I have demolished the garden. I have killed excellent demons. I destroyed a portion 
of the army. The demolition of the fort is still remaining."_END

B_5_C_51_33
BEGIN_सीतायाः तेजसा दग्धाम् राम कोप प्रपीडिताम् || ५-५१-३६
दह्यमनाम् इमाम् पश्य पुरीम् साट्ट प्रतोलिकाम् |_END
BEGIN_"See; (in the immediate future), this city of Lanka, burnt away by the effulgence of 
Seetha and the City too being scorched with its markets and main streets, afflicted by the wrath of 
Rama."_END

B_5_C_52_22
BEGIN_अस्मिन् विनष्टे न हि दूतम् अन्यम् |
पश्यामि यः तौ नर राज पुत्रौ |
युद्धाय युद्ध प्रिय दुर्विनीताव् |
उद्योजयेत् दीर्घ पथ अवरुद्धौ || ५-५२-२३_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana, who is fond of war! If he is dead, I do not find any other hero, who can incite 
those two arrogant princes, who are hindered by a long distance, for war."_END

B_5_C_53_8
BEGIN_लाङ्गूलम् सम्प्रदीप्तम् तु द्रष्टुम् तस्य हनूमतः || ५-५३-९
सहस्त्रीबालवृद्धाश्च जग्मुः प्रीता निशाचराः |_END
BEGIN_To see the burning tail of that Hanuma, the delighted demons together with their women, 
chldren and elders went there._END

B_5_C_54_3
BEGIN_दुर्गे विनाशिते कर्म भवेत् सुख परिश्रमम् |
अल्प यत्नेन कार्ये अस्मिन् मम स्यात् सफलः श्रमः || ५-५४-४_END
BEGIN_"When the fort gets destroyed, the task (of Rama's battle) will be devoid of fatigue. 
Even with a small effort in this task, the work will become fruitful."_END

B_5_C_51_34
BEGIN_स्वानि मित्राणि मन्त्रींश्च ज्ञातीन् भ्रातृन् सुतान् हितान् || ५-५१-३७
भोगान् दारांश्च लङ्काम् च मा विनाशमुपानय |_END
BEGIN_"Do not lead to extermination your own friends, counsellors, kinsmen, brothers, sons, 
well-wishers, enjoyments, wives and Lanka."_END

B_5_C_53_9
BEGIN_स भूयः सम्गतैः क्रूरै राकसैः हरि सत्तमः || ५-५३-१०
निबद्धः कृतवान् वीरः तत् काल सदृशीम् मतिम् |_END
BEGIN_Tied down again by the cruel demons, coming together, the heroic Hanuma the foremost 
among monkeys made up his mind appropriate for that occasion (as follows):_END

B_5_C_52_23
BEGIN_पराक्रम उत्साह मनस्विनाम् च |
सुर असुराणाम् अपि दुर्जयेन |
त्वया मनो नन्दन नैरृतानाम् |
युद्ध आयतिः नाशयितुम् न युक्ता || ५-५२-२४_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana who can gladden the hearts of demons! It is not proper for you, who are difficult 
to be conquered by even celestials and demons having sufficient prowess energy and courage, to crush 
the arrival of a war."_END

B_5_C_54_4
BEGIN_यो हि अयम् मम लान्गूले दीप्यते हव्य वाहनः |
अस्य सम्तर्पणम् न्याय्यम् कर्तुम् एभिः गृह उत्तमैः || ५-५४-५_END
BEGIN_"It is justified to satisfy this blazing flame on my tail, by feeding it to the full, 
with these excellent houses (in the city of Lanka)."_END

B_5_C_51_35
BEGIN_सत्यम् राक्षसराजेन्द्र शृणुष्व वचनम् मम || ५-५१-३८
रामदासस्य दूतस्य वानरस्य विशेषतः |_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! Listen to my truthful words coming as it is from the lips of this 
servant of Rama, his messenger and particularly of this monkey."_END

B_5_C_53_10
BEGIN_कामम् खलु न मे शक्ता निबधस्य अपि राक्षसाः || ५-५३-११
चित्त्वा पाशान् समुत्पत्य हन्याम् अहम् इमान् पुनः |_END
BEGIN_"Though I have been tied down, those demons cannot do whatever they wish to do against 
me. Breaking the ties, I can fly up and kill them."_END

B_5_C_52_24
BEGIN_हिताः च शूराः च समाहिताः च |
कुलेषु जाताः च महागुणेषु |
मनस्विनः शस्त्रभृताम् वरिष्ठाः |
कोटि अग्र शस्ते सुभृताः च योधाः || ५-५२-२५_END
BEGIN_"There are more than a crore of valiant warriors in your charge, well-maintained, who 
desire your welfare, quite devoted, having colossal merits, born in a good tribe, holding high spirits 
and excellent wielders of weapons."_END

B_5_C_54_5
BEGIN_ततः प्रदीप्त लान्गूलः सविद्युत् इव तोयदः |
भवन अग्रेषु लन्काया विचचार महाकपिः || ५-५४-६_END
BEGIN_Then, Hanuma, with his burning tail, strolled over the house-tops of Lanka, like a cloud 
charged with lightning._END

B_5_C_51_36
BEGIN_सर्वान् लोकान् सुसम्हृत्य सभूतान् सचराचरान् || ५-५१-३९
पुनरेव तथा स्रष्टुम् शक्तो रामो महायशाः |_END
BEGIN_"The renowned Rama is capable of totally destroying all the worlds together with its 
five elements, along with its animate and inanimate things and also to create yet again all the worlds 
in like manner as before."_END

B_5_C_53_11
BEGIN_यदिभर्तुर्हतार्थाय चरन्तम् भर्तृशासनात् || ५-५३-१२
बध्नन्त्येते दुरात्मनो न तु मे निष्कृतिः कृता |_END
BEGIN_"If these evil-minded demons fasten me who is acting for the good of Rama my lord, because 
of the command by their lord, no rebuff has been done to me."_END

B_5_C_55_0
BEGIN_संदीप्यमानाम् विध्वस्ताम् त्रस्त रक्षो गणाम् पुरीम् |
अवेक्ष्य हानुमाम्ल् लन्काम् चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-५५-१_END
BEGIN_Seeing the city of Lanka blazing, and frightened with its multitude of demons getting 
alarmed, Hanuma the monkey became thoughtful._END

B_5_C_52_25
BEGIN_तत् एक देशेन बलस्य तावत् |
केचित् तव आदेश कृतो अपयान्तु |
तौ राज पुत्रौ विनिगृह्य मूढौ |
परेषु ते भावयितुम् प्रभावम् || ५-५२-२६_END
BEGIN_"Therefore, let some who follow your command, by talking a portion of your army, subjugate 
those two stupid princes, in order to make your power known to your adversaries."_END

B_5_C_54_6
BEGIN_गृहाद्गृहम् राक्षसानामुद्यानानि च वानरः |
वीक्षमाणो ह्यसम्त्रस्तः प्रासादांश्च चचार सः || ५-५४-७_END
BEGIN_Surveying the gardens and lofty palatial mansions, that Hanuma, without fear, passed 
from one house to another, of the demons._END

B_5_C_51_37
BEGIN_देवासुरनरेन्द्रेषु यक्षरक्षोगणेषु च || ५-५१-४०
विद्याधरेषु सर्वेषु गन्धर्वेषूरगेषु च |
सिद्धेषु किन्नरेन्द्रेषु पतत्रिषु च सर्वतः || ५-५१-४१
सर्वभूतेषु सर्वत्र सर्वकालेषु नास्ति सः |
योरामम् प्रतियुध्येत विष्णुतुल्यपराक्रमम् || ५-५१-४२_END
BEGIN_"The renowned Rama, who is equal in prowess to Vishnu the lord of the preservation and 
among celestials, demons or the foremost of men, or among hordes of Yakshas the semi-divine beings or 
ogres or among all Vidyadharas, a king of super-natural beings or among Gandharvas the celestials musicians 
or among Uragas the semi-divine serpents or among Siddhas the holy personages having super-natural powers 
or among excellent Kinnaras the mythical beings with human figure and head of a horse or among all types 
of birds or among all living beings at all places and at all times."_END

B_5_C_53_12
BEGIN_सर्वेषाम् एव पर्याप्तो राक्षसानाम् अहम् युधि || ५-५३-१३
किम् तु रामस्य प्रीति अर्थम् विषहिष्ये अहम् ईदृशम् |
लन्का चरयितव्या मे पुनः एव भवेत् इति || ५-५३-१४_END
BEGIN_"I am adequate enough to kill all these demons in battle. But, for the delight of Rama, 
such city of Lanka is fit to be espionaged again. For this reason, I am putting up with it."_END

B_5_C_55_1
BEGIN_तस्य अभूत् सुमहान् त्रासः कुत्सा च आत्मनि अजायत |
लन्काम् प्रदहता कर्म किंस्वित् कृतम् इदम् मया || ५-५५-२_END
BEGIN_A great anxiety entered his mind and there arose in him a feeling of self-contempt. He 
said to himself "What an admonitory act has bee done by me in burning Lanka."_END

B_5_C_52_26
BEGIN_निशाचराणामधिपोऽनुजस्य |
विभीषणस्योत्तमवाक्यमिष्टम् |
जग्राह बुद्ध्या सुरलोकशत्रु |
र्महाबलो राक्षसराजमुख्यः || ५-५२-२७_END
BEGIN_Ravana, the mighty and the eminent king of demons as also the lord of ogres and the adversary 
of the world of celestials, understood the cherished and excellent message of Vibhishana his brother 
with his due presence of mind."_END

B_5_C_54_7
BEGIN_अवप्लुत्य महावेगः प्रहस्तस्य निवेशनम् |
अग्निम् तत्र स निक्षिप्य श्वसनेन समो बली || ५-५४-८
ततोऽन्यत्पुप्लुवे वेश्म महापार्श्वस्य वीर्यवान् |
मुमोच हनुमान् अग्निम् काल अनल शिखा उपमम् || ५-५४-९_END
BEGIN_Jumping down on Prahasta's house, the valiant Hanuma, with great swiftness, having strength 
equal to wind, scattering fire on it, jumped over from there, to another house belonging to Mahaparsva. 
Hanuma, with great swiftness, having strength equal to wind, scattering fire on it, jumped over from 
there, to another house belonging to Mahaparsva. Hanuma scattered a fire there resembling a flame of 
fire that is to destroy the world._END

B_5_C_51_38
BEGIN_सर्वलोकेश्वरस्यैवम् कृत्वा विप्रियमुत्तमम् |
रामस्य राजसिम्हस्य दुर्लभम् तव जीवितम् || ५-५१-४३_END
BEGIN_"After doing a great harm in this manner to Rama the lord of all worlds as well as the 
lion among kings, your survival will be difficult."_END

B_5_C_53_13
BEGIN_रात्रौ न हि सुदृष्टा मे दुर्ग कर्म विधानतः |
अवश्यम् एव द्रष्टव्या मया लन्का निशा क्षये || ५-५३-१५_END
BEGIN_"Lanka was not indeed observed well as to the particulars of specifications of the fort, 
when it was seen by me during the night. Surely, it is to be seen by me during the day-time."_END

B_5_C_55_2
BEGIN_धन्याः ते पुरुष श्रेष्ठ ये बुद्ध्या कोपम् उत्थितम् |
निरुन्धन्ति महात्मानो दीप्तम् अग्निम् इव अम्भसा || ५-५५-३_END
BEGIN_"As a burning fire is extinguished with water, blessed indeed are those great-souled 
men of excellence, who in their wisdom, restrain their elevated fury."_END

B_5_C_54_8
BEGIN_वज्रदंष्ट्र स्य च तदा पुप्लुवे स महाकपिः |
शुकस्य च महातेजाः सारणस्य च धीमतः || ५-५४-१०_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, of great splendour, then leapt to the houses of Vajradamshtra, Shuka and 
Sarana, the intelligent._END

B_5_C_51_39
BEGIN_देवाश्च दैत्याश्च निशाचरेन्द्र |
गन्धर्वविद्याधरनागयक्षाः |
रामस्य लोकत्रयनायकस्य |
स्थातुम् न शक्ताः समरेषु सर्वे || ५-५१-४४_END
BEGIN_"O king of demons! Either celestials or demons or Gandharvas the celestial musicians 
or Vidyadharas a king of super-natural beings or Nagas the semi-divine serpents or Yakshas the semi 
divine beings-all of them are not able to stand before Rama the lord of the three worlds."_END

B_5_C_53_14
BEGIN_कामम् बन्धैः च मे भूयः पुच्छस्य उद्दीपनेन च |
पीडाम् कुर्वन्तु रक्षांसि न मे अस्ति मनसः श्रमः || ५-५३-१६_END
BEGIN_"Let the demons tie me down of again and torment me as they wish, by burning my tail. 
There will be no travail to my mind."_END

B_5_C_54_9
BEGIN_तथा चेन्द्रजितो वेश्म ददाह हरियूथपः |
जम्बुमालेः सुमालेश्च ददाह भवनम् ततः || ५-५४-११
रश्मिकेतोश्च भवनम् सूर्यशत्रोस्तथैव च |
ह्रस्वकर्णस्य दंष्ट्रस्य रोमशस्य च रक्षसः || ५-५४-१२
युद्धोन्मत्तस्य मत्तस्य ध्वजग्रीवस्य रक्षसः |
विद्युज्जिह्वस्य घोरस्य तथा हस्तिमुखस्य च || ५-५४-१३
कराळस्य पिशाचस्य शोणिताक्षस्य चैव हि |
कुम्भकर्णस्य भवनम् मकराक्षस्य चैव हि || ५-५४-१४
यज्ञशत्रोश्च भवनम् ब्रह्मशत्रोस्तथैव च|
नरान्तकस्य कुम्भस्य निकुम्भस्य दुरात्मनः || ५-५४-१५
वर्जयित्वा महातेजा विभीषणगृहम् प्रति |
क्रममाणः क्रमेणैव ददाह हरिपुङ्गवः || ५-५४-१६_END
BEGIN_Leaving the house of Vibhishana, Hanuma of great splendour, went successively to the 
houses of Rashmiketu, Surya shatru, Hrasvakarna, Damshtra, Romasha the demon, Yuddhonmatta, Matta, Dhvajagreeva 
the demon, the terrific Vidyujjihva, Hastimukha, Karala, Pishacha, Shonitaaksha, Kumbhakarna, Makaraksha, 
Yajnashatru, Brahmashatru, Narantaka, Kumbha as also the evil-minded Nikumbha and burnt the houses._END

B_5_C_55_3
BEGIN_क्रुद्धः पापम् न कुर्यात्कः क्रुद्धो हन्याद्गुरूनपि |
क्रुद्धः परुषया वाचा नरः साधूनधिक्षिपेत् || ५-५५-४_END
BEGIN_"Which enraged man would not incur a sinful act? An enraged person may even kill his 
elders. An enraged person may insult virtuous men with harsh words."_END

B_5_C_51_40
BEGIN_ब्रह्म स्वयमुभूश्च तुराननो वा |
रुद्रस्त्रिणेत्रस्त्रिपुरान्तको वा |
इन्द्रो महेन्द्रः सुरनायको वा |
त्रातुम् न शक्ता युधि रामवध्यम् || ५-५१-४५_END
BEGIN_"Either Brahma the self-existing god with four faces or Rudra with three eyes and the 
destroyer of Tripura (the city built of gold, silver and iron in the sky, air and earth, by Maya for 
the demons and burnt by Shiva), or Mahendra the god of atmosphere and sky as also the lord of celestials 
would not be able to protect the one to be killed by Rama in battle."_END

B_5_C_53_15
BEGIN_ततः ते सम्वृत आकारम् सत्त्ववन्तम् महाकपिम् |
परिगृह्य ययुः हृष्टा राक्षसाः कपि कुन्जरम् || ५-५३-१७_END
BEGIN_Then, those delighted demons went, seizing Hanuma, who concealed all types of his feelings, 
who was strong and foremost among monkeys._END

B_5_C_54_10
BEGIN_तेषु तेषु महार्हेषु भवनेषु महायशाः |
गृहेष्वृद्धिमतामृद्धिम् ददाह स महाकपिः || ५-५४-१७_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma of great fame burnt away wealth in the mansions of the rich._END

B_5_C_55_4
BEGIN_वाच्यावाच्यम् प्रकुपितो न विजानाति कर्हिचित् |
नाकार्यमस्ति क्रुद्धस्य नावाच्यम् विद्यते क्वचित् || ५-५५-५_END
BEGIN_"An agitated person ever does not know which appropriate words are and which are forbidden 
words to be uttered. For enraged persons, there is neither an improper act nor ever an improper word 
to be spoken."_END

B_5_C_51_41
BEGIN_स सौष्ठव उपेतम् अदीन वादिनः |
कपेः निशम्य अप्रतिमो अप्रियम् वचः |
दश आननः कोप विवृत्त लोचनः |
समादिशत् तस्य वधम् महाकपेः || ५-५१-४६_END
BEGIN_Hearing those unpleasant words endowed with extreme skillfulness and which were spoken 
without fear from Hanuma, that unequalled Ravana ordered for the killing of that Hanuma._END

B_5_C_53_16
BEGIN_शन्ख भेरी निनादैः तैः घोषयन्तः स्व कर्मभिः |
राक्षसाः क्रूर कर्माणः चारयन्ति स्म ताम् पुरीम् || ५-५३-१८_END
BEGIN_Sounding couches and kettle-drums and proclaining the acts of Hanuma like his damaging 
of the pleasure-garden, the demons performing terrible deeds, dragged Hanuma through out that city._END

B_5_C_54_11
BEGIN_सर्वेषाम् समतिक्रम्य राक्षसेन्द्रस्य वीर्यवान् |
आससादाथ लक्ष्मीवान् रावणस्य निवेशनम् || ५-५४-१८_END
BEGIN_Having passed over all the houses, the mighty and glorious Hanuma thereafter approached 
the house of Ravana the king of demons._END

B_5_C_55_5
BEGIN_यः समुत्पतितम् क्रोधम् क्षमयैव निरस्यति |
यथोरगस्त्वचम् जीर्णाम् स वै पुरुष उच्यते || ५-५५-६_END
BEGIN_"As a serpent casts off its slough, whoever casts aside an intense anger sprung up in 
him suddenly by virtue of his endurance, he verily is said to be an excellent man."_END

B_5_C_53_17
BEGIN_अन्वीयमानो रक्षोभिर्ययौ सुखमरिंदमः |
हनुमान् चारयामास राक्षसानाम् महापुरीम् || ५-५३-१९_END
BEGIN_Accompanied by demons, Hanuma the annihilator of enemies, went happily and roamed about 
in that great city of demons._END

B_5_C_54_12
BEGIN_ततस्तस्मिन् गृहे मुख्ये नानारत्नविभूषिते |
मेरुमन्दरसंकाशे सर्वमङ्गळशोभिते || ५-५४-१९
प्रदीप्तमग्निमुत्सृज्य लाङ्गूलाग्रे प्रतिष्ठितम् |
ननाद हनुमान् वीरो युगान्तजलदो यथा || ५-५४-२०_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, scattering a blazing fire located at the tip of his tail, on that principal 
house, decorated with various kinds of precious stones, resembling Mounts Meru and Mandara as also embellished 
with all good work, the valiant Hanuma roared like a cloud thundering at noon-time in a rainy season._END

B_5_C_55_6
BEGIN_धिगस्तु माम् सुदुर्भद्धिम् निर्लज्जम् पापकृत्तमम् |
अचिन्तयित्वा ताम् सीतामग्निदम् स्वामिघातकम् || ५-५५-७_END
BEGIN_"Shame be upon me, the greatest sinner with utter foolishness and impudence, who became 
a fire-brand without giving thought to that Seetha and became hurtful to my master."_END

B_5_C_53_18
BEGIN_अथ अपश्यत् विमानानि विचित्राणि महाकपिः |
सम्वृतान् भूमि भागान् च सुविभक्तान् च चत्वरान् || ५-५३-२०_END
BEGIN_Then, Hanuma saw some wonderful house some wrapped up plots of land and well parted cross 
ways._END

B_5_C_54_13
BEGIN_श्वसनेन च सम्योगात् अतिवेगो महाबलः |
काल अग्निः इव जज्वाल प्रावर्धत हुत अशनः || ५-५४-२१_END
BEGIN_In contact with the wind, the fire escalated with a great speed and intensity, blazing 
like a fire that is to destroy the world._END

B_5_C_55_7
BEGIN_यदि दग्धा तु इयम् लन्का नूनम् आर्या अपि जानकी |
दग्धा तेन मया भर्तुः हतम् कार्यम् अजानता || ५-५५-८_END
BEGIN_"If this whole Lanka for its part has been burnt, the worshipful Seetha too has surely 
been burnt. Thus, I have spolt the purpose of my lord inadvertently."_END

B_5_C_53_19
BEGIN_वीथीश्च गृहसम्बाधाः कपिः शृङ्गटकानि च |
तथा रथ्योपरथ्याश्च तथैव गृहकान्तरान् || ५-५३-२१
गृहांश्च मेघसम्काशान् ददर्श पवनात्मजः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the son of wind-god, saw streets congested with dwellings, places where several 
roads meet, high-ways as also approach-roads, small inner apartments and palaces appearing in multitudes, 
like clouds._END

B_5_C_54_14
BEGIN_प्रदीप्तम् अग्निम् पवनः तेषु वेश्मसु चारयत् |
अभूच्छ्वसनसम्योगादतिवेगो हुताशनः || ५-५४-२२_END
BEGIN_The wind carried the blazing fire to other houses. In conjunction with the wind, the 
fire became very swift._END

B_5_C_55_8
BEGIN_यत् अर्थम् अयम् आरम्भः तत् कार्यम् अवसादितम् |
मया हि दहता लन्काम् न सीता परिरक्षिता || ५-५५-९_END
BEGIN_"That purpose for which all this effort was taken, has been spoilt. At the time of burning 
the city, I have not saved Seetha indeed."_END

B_5_C_53_20
BEGIN_चत्वरेषु चतुष्केषु राज मार्गे तथैव च || ५-५३-२२
घोषयन्ति कपिम् सर्वे चारीक इति राक्षसाः |_END
BEGIN_All the demons proclaimed in cross roads, four-pillared temples and in royal high-ways, 
saying that Hanuma was a spy._END

B_5_C_54_15
BEGIN_तानि कान्चन जालानि मुक्ता मणिमयानि च |
भवनानि अवशीर्यन्त रत्नवन्ति महान्ति च || ५-५४-२३_END
BEGIN_Those large houses, with golden windows, embedded with pearls, gems and precious jewels 
were shattered to pieces._END

B_5_C_55_9
BEGIN_ईषत् कार्यम् इदम् कार्यम् कृतम् आसीन् न संशयः |
तस्य क्रोध अभिभूतेन मया मूल क्षयः कृतः || ५-५५-१०_END
BEGIN_"This task (of burning Lanka) has been fulfilled by me and it has been completed only 
with a small effort. Overpowered as I was with anger, the very root of that fulfillment has been destroyed 
by me. There is no doubt."_END

B_5_C_54_16
BEGIN_सम्जज्ञे तुमुलः शब्दो राक्षसानाम् प्रधावताम् |
स्वग्ऱिहस्य परित्राणे भग्नोत्साहोर्जिअश्रियाम् || ५-५४-२४
नूनेमेषाऽग्निरायातः कपिरूपेण हा इति |_END
BEGIN_The demons, who were running hither and thither to protect their houses and who lost 
their spirits and abundant wealth, created a tumultuous nose, saying "Alas! The fire-god has come really 
in a form of this monkey!"_END

B_5_C_53_21
BEGIN_स्त्रीबालवृद्धा निर्जग्मुस्तत्र तत्र कुतूहलात् || ५-५३-२३
तम् प्रदीपितलाङ्गूलम् हनुमन्तम् दिदृक्षवः |_END
BEGIN_Women, children and old people came out from their respective dwellings, with an eagerness 
to see that Hanuma with his burning tail._END

B_5_C_55_10
BEGIN_विनष्टा जानकी व्यक्तम् न हि अदग्धः प्रदृश्यते |
लन्कायाः कश्चित् उद्देशः सर्वा भस्मी कृता पुरी || ५-५५-११_END
BEGIN_"The entire Lanka has been reduced to ashes. No place is seen unburnt in this City. Therefore, 
Seetha also must have been surely lost."_END

B_5_C_56_0
BEGIN_ततः तु शिंशपा मूले जानकीम् पर्यवस्थिताम् |
अभिवाद्य अब्रवीत् दिष्ट्या पश्यामि त्वाम् इह अक्षताम् || ५-५६-१_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, having offered his salutation to Seetha, who was present at the foot of Ashoka 
tree, Hanuma spoke: "Thank heaven! I am seeing you uninjured here!"_END

B_5_C_54_17
BEGIN_क्रन्दन्त्यः सहसा पेतुः स्तनंधयधराः स्त्रियः || ५-५४-२५
काश्चिरग्निपरीतेभ्यो हर्म्येभ्यो मुक्तमूर्धजाः |
पतन्त्यो रेजिरेऽभ्रेभ्यः सौदामिन्य इवाम्बरात् || ५-५४-२६_END
BEGIN_Some women crying and carrying their suckling's with their hair dishevelled, fell down 
from their houses, which were enveloped with fire, and shone like flashes of lightning falling from 
clouds in the sky._END

B_5_C_53_22
BEGIN_दीप्यमाने ततः तस्य लान्गूल अग्रे हनूमतः || ५-५३-२४
राक्षस्यः ता विरूप अक्ष्यः शंसुः देव्याः तत् अप्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_While the tip of Hanuma's tail was being ignited by the demons there, those female-demons 
with monstrous eyes then informed that unpleasant matter to Seetha, the princess._END

B_5_C_55_11
BEGIN_यदि तत् विहतम् कार्यम् मया प्रज्ञा विपर्ययात् |
इह एव प्राण सम्न्यासो मम अपि हि अतिरोचते || ५-५५-१२_END
BEGIN_"If this task has been spoiled due to my perverted intelligence, it is appropriate even 
for me, here and now itself, to give up my life."_END

B_5_C_56_1
BEGIN_ततः तम् प्रस्थितम् सीता वीक्षमाणा पुनः पुनः |
भर्तृ स्नेह अन्वितम् वाक्यम् हनूमन्तम् अभाषत || ५-५६-२_END
BEGIN_Then, beholding again and again, that Hanuma, who had made ready for his return journey, 
Seetha spoke the following words, filled with affection towards her husband._END

B_5_C_53_23
BEGIN_यः त्वया कृत सम्वादः सीते ताम्र मुखः कपिः || ५-५३-२५
लान्गूलेन प्रदीप्तेन स एष परिणीयते |_END
BEGIN_"O Seetha! That monkey with a red face, who had a conversation with you, is being moved 
around in the city, with his ignited tail."_END

B_5_C_54_18
BEGIN_वज्र विद्रुम वैदूर्य मुक्ता रजत सम्हितान् |
विचित्रान् भवनात् धातून् स्यन्दमानान् ददर्श सः || ५-५४-२७_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma saw molten metals mixed with diamonds, corals, cat's eye-gems, pearls and 
silver, surging from every marvellous house._END

B_5_C_55_12
BEGIN_किम् अग्नौ निपतामि अद्य आहोस्वित् वडवा मुखे |
शरीरम् आहो सत्त्वानाम् दद्मि सागर वासिनाम् || ५-५५-१३_END
BEGIN_"Shall I jump into fire now or into the mouth of a submarine fire? Or shall I give up 
my body as a feed to the marine animals?"_END

B_5_C_56_2
BEGIN_कामम् अस्य त्वम् एव एकः कार्यस्य परिसाधने |
पर्याप्तः पर वीरघ्न यशस्यः ते बल उदयः || ५-५६-३_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma, the annihilator of enemies! You are yourself surely sufficient single-handed 
completion of this task. Your elevated energy is creditable indeed._END

B_5_C_53_24
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा तत् वचनम् क्रूरम् आत्म अपहरण उपमम् || ५-५३-२६
वैदेही शोक सम्तप्ता हुत अशनम् उपागमत् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing that cruel news, which created as much sorrow as when she was carried away by 
Ravana, Seetha was tormented with grief and started to pay homage to the fire-god._END

B_5_C_54_19
BEGIN_न अग्निः तृप्यति काष्ठानाम् तृणानाम् च यथा तथा |
हनूमान् राक्षस इन्द्राणाम् वधे किंचिन् न तृप्यति || ५-५४-२८
न हनूमद्विशस्तानाम् राक्षसानाम् वसुन्धरा |_END
BEGIN_As the fire does not get satisfied with any amount of firewood and straw fed to it, Hanuma 
was not wearied in killing any number of demons. The earth was not then wearied in receiving the number 
of demons killed by Hanuma (in her lap)._END

B_5_C_55_13
BEGIN_कथम् हि जीवता शक्यो मया द्रष्टुम् हरि ईश्वरः |
तौ वा पुरुष शार्दूलौ कार्य सर्व स्व घातिना || ५-५५-१४_END
BEGIN_"By me who has ruined the entire task, how can I, even while remaining alive, see Sugreeva 
the Lord of monkeys or Rama and Lakshmana the best of men?"_END

B_5_C_56_3
BEGIN_शरैस्तुः सम्कुलाम् कृत्वा लन्काम् पर बल अर्दनः |
माम् नयेत् यदि काकुत्स्थः तस्य तत् सादृशम् भवेत् || ५-५६-४_END
BEGIN_"But, it will be appropriate for Rama, who destroys the hostile forces, to take me with 
him, after routing Lanka with his arrows."_END

B_5_C_53_25
BEGIN_मन्गला अभिमुखी तस्य सा तदा आसीन् महाकपेः || ५-५३-२७
उपतस्थे विशाल अक्षी प्रयता हव्य वाहनम् |_END
BEGIN_Then, the large-eyed Seetha, wishing for the welfare of Hanuma, prayed the fire-god with 
her devoted self._END

B_5_C_54_20
BEGIN_क्वचित्किंशुकसम्काशाः क्वचिच्छाल्मलिसन्निभाः || ५-५४-२९
क्वचित्कुङ्कुमसम्काशाः शिखा वह्नेश्चकाशिरे |_END
BEGIN_Flames of fire glittered like Kimshuka flowers at some places, blossoms of Shalmali tree 
at some places and like saffron-flowers at some other places._END

B_5_C_55_14
BEGIN_मया खलु तत् एव इदम् रोष दोषात् प्रदर्शितम् |
प्रथितम् त्रिषु लोकेषु कपितम् अनवस्थितम् || ५-५५-१५_END
BEGIN_"Due to culpability of my anger, I have indeed shown this apishness that is famous for 
instability in the three worlds."_END

B_5_C_56_4
BEGIN_तत् यथा तस्य विक्रान्तम् अनुरूपम् महात्मनः |
भवति आहव शूरस्य तत्त्वम् एव उपपादय || ५-५६-५_END
BEGIN_"Therefore, you act in such a way that the high-souled Rama, valiant in battle, may exhibit 
prowess worthy of him."_END

B_5_C_53_26
BEGIN_यदि अस्ति पति शुश्रूषा यदि अस्ति चरितम् तपः || ५-५३-२८
यदि च अस्ति एक पत्नीत्वम् शीतो भव हनूमतः |_END
BEGIN_"If I have done any service to my husband, if I have performed a penance and if I am 
a faithful wife, please be cool to Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_54_21
BEGIN_हनूमता वेगवता वानरेण महात्मना |
लङ्कापुरम् प्रदग्धम् तद्रुद्रेण त्रिपुरम् यथा || ५-५४-३०_END
BEGIN_The high souled Hanuma, the swift monkey scorched the city of Lanka, as Rudra scorched 
the city of Tripura._END

B_5_C_55_15
BEGIN_धिग् अस्तु राजसम् भावम् अनीशम् अनवस्थितम् |
ईश्वरेण अपि यत् रागान् मया सीता न रक्षिता || ५-५५-१६_END
BEGIN_"Let there be shame upon the passionate way of my thinking, which breeds helplessness 
and instability. fir, eventhough capable as I am, Seetha could not be saved by me due to my exciting 
passion of anger."_END

B_5_C_56_5
BEGIN_तत् अर्थ उपहितम् वाक्यम् प्रश्रितम् हेतु सम्हितम् |
निशम्य हनुमान् तस्या वाक्यम् उत्तरम् अब्रवीत् || ५-५६-६_END
BEGIN_Hearing those humble, reasonable and meaningful words of Seetha, Hanuma spoke the following 
words in reply._END

B_5_C_54_22
BEGIN_ततस्तु लङ्कापुरपर्वताग्रे |
स्मुत्थितो भीमपराक्रमोऽग्निः |
प्रसार्य चूडावलयम् प्रदीप्तो |
हनूमता वेगवता विसृष्टः || ५-५४-३१_END
BEGIN_Then, the fire having a terrific prowess, diffused by the swift Hanuma, stretching out 
a circle of flames, blazed and rose up to the summit of the mountain on which the city of Lanka._END

B_5_C_53_27
BEGIN_यदि कश्चित् अनुक्रोशः तस्य मयि अस्ति धीमतः || ५-५३-२९
यदि वा भाग्य शेषम् मे शीतो भव हनूमतः |_END
BEGIN_"If the wise Rama has even a little of kindness to me and if I have still some good fortune 
remaining to my credit, please be cool to Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_55_16
BEGIN_विनष्टायाम् तु सीतायाम् ताव् उभौ विनशिष्यतः |
तयोः विनाशे सुग्रीवः सबन्धुः विनशिष्यति || ५-५५-१७_END
BEGIN_"If Seetha dies, those two princes, Rama and Lakshmana will die. If their death occurs, 
Sugreeva along with his associates will also die."_END

B_5_C_56_6
BEGIN_क्षिप्रम् एष्यति काकुत्स्थो हरि ऋक्ष प्रवरैः वृतः |
यः ते युधि विजित्य अरीन् शोकम् व्यपनयिष्यति || ५-५६-७_END
BEGIN_"Rama, accompanied by the leaders of monkeys and bears, will come soon and after conquering 
the enemies in battle, will take away your grief."_END

B_5_C_54_23
BEGIN_युगान्तकालानलतुल्यवेगः |
समारुतोऽग्निर्ववृधे दिवस्पृक् |
विधूमरश्मिर्भवनेषु सक्तो |
रक्षः शरीराज्यसमर्पितार्चिः || ५-५४-३२_END
BEGIN_That fire diffused on those buildings, together with the wind picked up a speed equal 
to that of a fire at the time of dissolution of the world. It grew taller, touching the sky with a smokeless 
splendour. Those flames of fire shot up, as inflamed by ghee_END

B_5_C_55_17
BEGIN_एतत् एव वचः श्रुत्वा भरतो भ्रातृ वत्सलः |
धर्म आत्मा सह शत्रुघ्नः कथम् शक्ष्यति जीवितुम् || ५-५५-१८_END
BEGIN_"How can the virtuous Bharata together with Shatrughna, who are affectionate to his brother, 
survive after hearing this news?"_END

B_5_C_53_28
BEGIN_यदि माम् वृत्त सम्पन्नाम् तत् समागम लालसाम् || ५-५३-३०
स विजानाति धर्म आत्मा शीतो भव हनूमतः |_END
BEGIN_"If that virtuous Rama recognises me as one,, who is endowed with a good moral conduct 
and who is ardently desirous of meeting him, please be cool to Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_56_7
BEGIN_एवम् आश्वास्य वैदेहीम् हनूमान् मारुत् आत्मजः |
गमनाय मतिम् कृत्वा वैदेहीम् अभ्यवादयत् || ५-५६-८_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the son of wind-god, thus consoling Seetha and making up his mind to go, saluted 
Seetha with reverence._END

B_5_C_54_24
BEGIN_आदित्यकोटीसदृशः सुतेजा |
लङ्काम् समस्ताम् परिवार्य तिष्ठन् |
शब्दैरनेकैरशनिप्ररूडै |
र्भिन्दन्निवाण्डम् प्रबभौ महाग्निः || ५-५४-३३_END
BEGIN_The great fire persisted, surrounding the entire Lanka, having a good splendour equal 
to that of millions of suns and blazed like a broken-up hemi-sphere of the world, creating many sounds 
of a wide-spread thunderbolt._END

B_5_C_55_18
BEGIN_इक्ष्वाकु वंशे धर्मिष्ठे गते नाशम् असंशयम् |
भविष्यन्ति प्रजाः सर्वाः शोक सम्ताप पीडिताः || ५-५५-१९_END
BEGIN_"When the virtuous Ikshvaku dynasty perishes, all the people will undoubtedly be tormented 
with anguish and affliction."_END

B_5_C_53_29
BEGIN_यदि माम् तारयति आर्यः सुग्रीवः सत्य सम्गरः || ५-५३-३१
अस्मात् दुह्खान् महाबाहुः शीतो भव हनूमतः |_END
BEGIN_"If the venerable Sugreeva, true to his promise, can make me traverse from this ocean 
of sorrow, please be cool to Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_56_8
BEGIN_ततः स कपि शार्दूलः स्वामि संदर्शन उत्सुकः |
आरुरोह गिरि श्रेष्ठम् अरिष्टम् अरि मर्दनः || ५-५६-९_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, that Hanuma the foremost among the monkeys, and the annihilator of enemies, 
with an anxious desire to see his lord, ascended the Mount Arishta of excellence._END

B_5_C_54_25
BEGIN_तत्राम्बरादग्निरतिप्रवृद्धो |
रूक्षप्रभः किंशुकपुष्पचूडाः |
निर्वाणधूमाकुलराजयश्च |
नीलोत्पलाभाः प्रचकाशिरेऽभ्राः || ५-५४-३४_END
BEGIN_The fire with a fierce splendour there, extended fully to the sky, shooting flames like 
Kumshuka flowers. The clouds, bearing the colour of blue lotuses, shone as covered by smoke formed out 
of the extinguished fire._END

B_5_C_55_19
BEGIN_तत् अहम् भाग्य रहितो लुप्त धर्म अर्थ सम्ग्रहः |
रोग दोष परीत आत्मा व्यक्तम् लोक विनाशनः || ५-५५-२०_END
BEGIN_"Therefore, I, the unfortunate being, deprived of the values of duty and interest, with 
my mind filled with culpability of anger, clearly became the destroyer of the world."_END

B_5_C_53_30
BEGIN_ततः तीक्ष्ण अर्चिः अव्यग्रः प्रदक्षिण शिखो अनलः || ५-५३-३२
जज्वाल मृग शाव अक्ष्याः शंसन्न् इव शिवम् कपेः |_END
BEGIN_Then, the fire-god, as though informing the fawn-eyed Seetha about the well-being of 
Hanuma, shone brightly with sharp flames, undisteurbed and shooting out pointed flames towards the right._END

B_5_C_56_9
BEGIN_तुन्ग पद्मक जुष्टाभिः नीलाभिः वन राजिभिः |
सोत्तरीयमिवाम्भोदैः शृम्गान्तरविलम्बिभिः || ५-५६-१०_END
BEGIN_That mountain was covered as it were with dark green rows of gardens inhabited by towery 
elephants with red spots on their skin and with its clouds hanging between its summits, as with an upper 
garment._END

B_5_C_55_20
BEGIN_इति चिन्तयतः तस्य निमित्तानि उपपेदिरे |
पूरम् अपि उपलब्धानि साक्षात् पुनः अचिन्तयत् || ५-५५-२१_END
BEGIN_While thinking thus, Hanuma clearly saw some omens, whose welcome-results had already 
been directly experienced by him and again thought (as follows);_END

B_5_C_54_26
BEGIN_वज्री महेन्द्रस्त्रिदशेश्वरो वा |
साक्षाद्यमो वा वरुणोऽनिलो वा |
रुद्रोग्निरर्को धनदश्च सोमो |
न वानरोऽयम् स्वयमेव कालः | ५-५४-३५_END
BEGIN_"He is not a monkey. He is either Indra the Lord of celestials wielding a thunderbolt, 
or Yama the lord of death of water, or the wind-god or the fire seated in the third eye of Lord Shiva 
or the sun-god or Kubera the lord of riches or the moon-god. He may be Kala (the Time-spirit) himself."_END

B_5_C_53_31
BEGIN_हनुमज्जनकश्चापि पुच्छानलयुतोऽनिलः || ५-५३-३३
ववौ स्वास्थ्यकरो देव्याः प्रालेयानिलशीतलः |_END
BEGIN_Even wind-god, the father of Hanuma, combined with the fire on Hanuma's tail, swept coolly 
like a snow-breeze, creating a solace to Seetha._END

B_5_C_56_10
BEGIN_बोध्यमानमिव प्रीत्या दिवाकरकरैः शुभैः |
उन्मिषन्तिमिवोद्धूतैर्लोचनैरिव धातुभिः || ५-५६-११_END
BEGIN_By metals scattered here and there, looking like eyes drawing up the eye-lids, the mountain 
looked like being awakened, as it were, with love by the bright rays of the sun._END

B_5_C_55_21
BEGIN_अथवा चारु सर्व अन्गी रक्षिता स्वेन तेजसा |
न नशिष्यति कल्याणी न अग्निः अग्नौ प्रवर्तते || ५-५५-२२_END
BEGIN_"Or else, Seetha the auspicious lady, who is completely charming of her limbs and protected 
by her own effulgence, does not get destroyed. Fire does not indeed destroy fire!"_END

B_5_C_53_32
BEGIN_दह्यमाने च लान्गूले चिन्तयामास वानरः || ५-५३-३४
प्रदीप्तो अग्निः अयम् कस्मान् न माम् दहति सर्वतः |_END
BEGIN_While his tail was in flames, Hanuma was reflecting why the fire, which was blazing on 
all sides, was not burning him._END

B_5_C_57_0
BEGIN_सचन्द्र कुमुदम् रम्यम् सार्क कारण्डवम् शुभम् |
	तिष्य श्रवण कदम्बम् अभ्र शैवल शाद्वलम् || ५-५७-१
	पुनर्वसु महामीनम् लोहित अन्ग महाग्रहम् |
	ऐरावत महाद्वीपम् स्वाती हंस विलोडितम् || ५-५७-२
	वात सम्घात जात ऊर्मिम् चन्द्र अंशु शिशिर अम्बुमत् |
	भुजम्ग यक्ष गन्धर्व प्रबुद्ध कमल उत्पलम् || ५-५७-३
	हनुमान् मारुतगतिर्महानौरिव सागरम् |
	अपारमपरिश्रान्तः पुप्लुवे गगनार्णवम् || ५-५७-४_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, with a rush equal to that of wind, withaut a fatigue, leapt across the baundless 
	sea looking analogaus to sky, like a large ship crossing the ocean. In that pleasant and auspiciaus 
	sky-like sea, shone the moon as a white water-like sea, shone having the constellations known by 
	the names of Pushya and Shravana as swans, the clauds as its duck-weeds; the twin constellations 
	the Punarvasus as its large fish, the planet Mars as its large alligator, a large island as Airavata 
	(Indra's elephant), graced with a swan in the form of the constellation, Shwati, having gales as 
	its waves, the moon bea.ns as its cool water and with the Nagas, yakshas and Gandharvas as its full 
	blown lotuses and water-lilies._END

B_5_C_54_27
BEGIN_किम् ब्रह्मण सर्वपितामहस्य |
सर्वस्य धातुश्चतुराननस्य |
इहागतो वानररूपधारी |
रक्षोपसम्हारकरः प्रतापः ५-५४-३६_END
BEGIN_"Whether the rage of four-faced Brahma, the grand father of all and the creator of all 
has arrived here in the guise of a monkey, playing the role of a destroyer of demons?"_END

B_5_C_56_11
BEGIN_तोयौघनिस्वनैर्मन्द्रैः प्राधीतमिव पर्वतम् |
प्रगीतमिव विस्पष्टैर्नानाप्रस्रवणस्व्नै || ५-५६-१२_END
BEGIN_The mountain looked resembling the one which has started reciting the scriptures clearly 
in the form of the deep sound of running streams of water, singing as it were at a high pitch, in the 
form of roaring sound of various cascades._END

B_5_C_55_22
BEGIN_न हि धर्मात् मनः तस्य भार्याम् अमित तेजसः |
स्व चारित्र अभिगुप्ताम् ताम् स्प्रष्टुम् अर्हति पावकः || ५-५५-२३_END


B_5_C_53_33
BEGIN_दृश्यते च महाज्वालः करोति च न मे रुजम् || ५-५३-३५
शिशिरस्य इव सम्पातो लान्गूल अग्रे प्रतिष्ठितः |_END
BEGIN_"It is conspicuous with large flames. But it is not creating any paoin to me, as if a 
snow-ball is kept at the tip of my tail."_END

B_5_C_54_28
BEGIN_किम् वैष्णवम् वा कपिरूपमेत्य |
रक्षोविनाशाय परम् सुतेजः |
अनन्तमव्यक्तमचिन्त्यमेकम् |
स्वमायया साम्प्रतमागतम् वा ५-५४-३७_END
BEGIN_"Or whether a supreme bright energy of Vishnu, the lord of maintenance of the Universe, 
unthinkable, unmanifest, infinite and pearless, arrived now, assuming the form of a monkey for the destruction 
of demons, by virtue of Her extraordinary power?"_END

B_5_C_57_1
BEGIN_ग्रासमान इव आकाशम् तारा अधिपम् इव आलिखन् |
	हरन्न् इव सनक्षत्रम् गगनम् सार्क मण्डलम् || ५-५७-५
	मारुतस्य आलयम् श्रीमान् कपिः व्योम चरो महान् |
	हनूमान् मेघ जालानि विकर्षन्न् इव गच्छति || ५-५७-६_END
BEGIN_While moving in the sky, the illustrious Hanuma, the son of wind-god and the great 
	monkey, appeared as if swallowing the sky, scratching the moon and carrying off the sky with its 
	stars and the disc of the sun and was going as though dragging asunder, a mass of clouds._END

B_5_C_56_12
BEGIN_देवदारुभिरत्युच्चैरूर्ध्वबाहुमिव स्थितम् |
प्रपातजलनिर्घोषैः प्राकृष्टमिव सर्वतः || ५-५६-१३_END
BEGIN_The mountain stood as it were with uplifted arms in the form of very lofty deodars and 
which started crying loudly as it were, on all sides, in the form of the sound of its cascades._END

B_5_C_55_23
BEGIN_नूनम् राम प्रभावेन वैदेह्याः सुकृतेन च |
यन् माम् दहन कर्मा अयम् न अदहद्त् हव्य वाहनः || ५-५५-२४_END
BEGIN_"If this fire with its burning nature is not igniting me, it is surely due to the power 
of Rama and the benevolence of Seetha."_END

B_5_C_54_29
BEGIN_इत्येवमूचुर्बहवो विशिष्टा |
रक्षोगणास्तत्र समेत्य सर्वे |
सप्राणिसम्घां सगृहाम् सवृक्षाम् |
दग्धाम् पुरीम् ताम् सहसा समीक्ष्य || ५-५४-३८_END
BEGIN_Thus spoke all those excellent troops of demons in multitude, gathering together there, 
on seeing that city scorched so soon, with its host of living beings, houses and trees._END

B_5_C_57_2
BEGIN_पाण्डुर अरुण वर्णानि नील मान्जिष्ठकानि च |
	हरित अरुण वर्णानि महाअभ्राणि चकाशिरे || ५-५७-७_END
BEGIN_Dense clauds, with white and red colaurs, blue and yellow colaurs as also green and 
	reddish brown colaurs shone brightly in the sky._END

B_5_C_53_34
BEGIN_अथवा तत् इदम् व्यक्तम् यत् दृष्टम् प्लवता मया || ५-५३-३६
राम प्रभावात् आश्चर्यम् पर्वतः सरिताम् पतौ |_END
BEGIN_"Or, while I was jumping over the ocean, a surprise-alliance was formed with Mount Mainaka 
and through the mountain, with the ocean, because of Rama's power. By this, the reason of the coolness 
is clear."_END

B_5_C_56_13
BEGIN_वेपमानमिव श्यामैः कम्पमानैः शरद्वनैः |
वेणुभिर्मारुतोद्धूतैः कूजन्तमिव कीचकैः || ५-५६-१४_END
BEGIN_The mountain seemed to be trembling in the form of waving dark automnal groves, which 
was piping as it were, in the form of hollow bamboos shaken up by the wind and whistling._END

B_5_C_55_24
BEGIN_त्रयाणाम् भरत आदीनाम् भ्रातृऋणाम् देवता च या |
रामस्य च मनः कान्ता सा कथम् विनशिष्यति || ५-५५-२५_END
BEGIN_"How should that Seetha, who is a godhead for the three brothers (of Rama) starting with 
Bharata and who is dear to the heart of Rama perish?"_END

B_5_C_54_30
BEGIN_ततस्तु लङ्का सहसा प्रदग्धा |
सराक्षसा साश्वरथा सनागा |
सपक्षिसम्घा समृगा सवृक्षा |
रुरोद दीना तुमुलम् सशब्दम् || ५-५४-३९_END
BEGIN_Then, Lanka having been scorched with its demons, horses, chariots, elephants, multitude 
of birds, animals and trees, cried pitiably with tumultuous noise._END

B_5_C_53_35
BEGIN_यदि तावत् समुद्रस्य मैनाकस्य च धीमथ || ५-५३-३७
राम अर्थम् सम्भ्रमः तादृक् किम् अग्निः न करिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_"If such an eagerness was there in the mind of the sea and the wise Mount Mainaka for 
the cause of Rama; will not the fire-god show the same degree of eagerness in making its touch cold?"_END

B_5_C_57_3
BEGIN_प्रविशन्न् अभ्र जालानि निष्क्रमन् च पुनः पुनः |
	प्रच्छन्नः च प्रकाशः च चन्द्रमा इव लक्ष्यते || ५-५७-८_END
BEGIN_Time and again, entering and coming out of the clusters of clouds, Hanuma appeared 
	like the moon becoming visible and invisible again and again._END

B_5_C_56_14
BEGIN_निःश्वसन्तमिवामर्षाद्घोरैराशीविषोत्तमैः |
वीहारकृतगम्भीरैर्ध्यायन्तमिव गह्वरैः || ५-५६-१५_END
BEGIN_The mountain was hissing as it were with fury, in the form of its terrible and most poisonous 
snakes and which sat absorbed in meditation as it were, in the form of its deep caves covered with mist._END

B_5_C_55_25
BEGIN_यत् वा दहन कर्मा अयम् सर्वत्र प्रभुः अव्ययः |
न मे दहति लान्गूलम् कथम् आर्याम् प्रधक्ष्यति || ५-५५-२६_END
BEGIN_"This fire, which spreads everywhere without any hindrance, is not burning my tail. How 
can it burn the venerable Seetha?"_END

B_5_C_53_36
BEGIN_सीतायाः च आनृशंस्येन तेजसा राघवस्य च || ५-५३-३८
पितुः च मम सख्येन न माम् दहति पावकः |_END
BEGIN_"The fire does not burn me, due to kindness of Seetha, powerfulness of Rama and friendlines 
of my father."_END

B_5_C_54_31
BEGIN_हा तात हा पुत्रक कान्त मित्र |
हा जीवितम् भोगयुतम् सुपुण्यम् |
रक्षोभिरेवम् बहुधा ब्रुवद्भिः |
शब्दः कृतो घोररवः सुभीमः || ५-५४-४०_END
BEGIN_Making a very terrific noise with a dreadful sound, the demons cried in various ways 
as follows: "O my dear beloved son! O my beloved husband! O my friend! O my very auspicious life, filled 
with enjoyments!"_END

B_5_C_57_4
BEGIN_विविधाभ्राघनासन्नगोचरो धवळाम्बरः |
	दृश्यादृश्यतनुर्वीरस्तदा चन्द्रयतेऽम्बरे || ५-५७-९_END
BEGIN_The heroic Hanuma, who was clad in white clothes, having faund his way into variaus 
	kinds of dense clauds (and energing again) and having his personlaity becoming visible and invisible, 
	shone like the moon in the sky._END

B_5_C_56_15
BEGIN_मेघपादनिभैः पादैः प्रक्रान्तमिव सर्वतः |
जृम्भमाणमिवाकाशे शिखरैरभ्रामालिभिः || ५-५६-१६_END
BEGIN_The mountain seems to be setting out on a journey on all four sides, with feet of the 
mountain, looking like rising clouds, which with its peaks having a lining of clouds, seemed to stretch 
its limbs in the sky._END

B_5_C_55_26
BEGIN_पुनश्चाचिन्तयत्तत्र हनुमान्विस्मितस्तदा |
हिरण्यनाभस्य गिरेर्जलमध्ये प्रदर्शनम् || ५-५५-२७_END
BEGIN_Hanuma then recalled with wonder the sight of Mount Mainaka (having gold in its cavities) 
in the midst of sea-water there._END

B_5_C_53_37
BEGIN_भूयः स चिन्तयामास मुहूर्तम् कपि कुन्जरः || ५-५३-३९
उत्पपात अथ वेगेन ननाद च महाकपिः |_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, the foremost among the monkeys, reflected agian for a monment, jumped with 
swiftness and roared too._END

B_5_C_54_32
BEGIN_हुताशनज्वालसमावृता सा |
हतप्रवीरा परिवृत्तयोधा |
हनूमतः क्रोधबलाभिभूता |
बभूव शापोपहतेअ लङ्का || ५-५४-४१_END
BEGIN_That Lanka appeared as though afflicted by a curse, as defeated by a strong fury of Hanuma, 
enveloped by flames of fire, with its distinguished heroes killed and with its warriors in retreat._END

B_5_C_57_5
BEGIN_तार्क्ष्यायमाणो गगने बभासे वायुनन्दनः |
	दारयन्मेघबृन्दानि निष्पतंश्च पुनः पुनः || ५-५७-१०_END
BEGIN_Tearing asunder the clusters of clouds again and again as also energing from them 
	and roaring with a big noise, Hanuma the son of wind-god, making a thunderous great sound, shone 
	flying like Garuda the eagle, in the sky._END

B_5_C_56_16
BEGIN_कूटैश्च बहुधा कीर्णै शोभितम् बहुकन्दरैः |
साल ताल अश्व कर्णैः च वंशैः च बहुभिः वृतम् || ५-५६-१७_END
BEGIN_The mountain was embellished with a number of summits and adorned with numerous caves 
scattered at many places and endowed with many sal, palmyrah, karna and bamboo trees._END

B_5_C_55_27
BEGIN_तपसा सत्य वाक्येन अनन्यत्वाच् च भर्तरि |
अपि सा निर्दहेत् अग्निम् न ताम् अग्निः प्रधक्ष्यति || ५-५५-२८_END
BEGIN_"That Seetha can even burn away the fire by her penance, true utterances and undivided 
devotion towards her husband. Fire does not ignite her."_END

B_5_C_53_38
BEGIN_पुर द्वारम् ततः श्रीमान् शैल शृन्गम् इव उन्नतम् || ५-५३-४०
विभक्त रक्षः सम्बाधम् आससाद अनिल आत्मजः |_END
BEGIN_Then, the glorious Hanuma like a mountain-peak, approached the city-gate, which was looking 
high and stood secluded from the crowds of demons._END

B_5_C_57_6
BEGIN_नदन् नादेन महता मेघ स्वन महास्वनः |
	प्रवरान् राक्षसान् हत्वा नाम विश्राव्य चात्मनः || ५-५७-११
	आकुलाम् नगतीम् कृत्वा व्यथयित्वा च रावणम् |
	अर्दयित्वा बलम् घोरम् वैदेहीमभिवाद्य च || ५-५७-१२
	आजगाम महातेजाः पुनः मध्येन सागरम् |_END
BEGIN_Killing the foremost of demons, becoming famaus by is name, making Lanka perplexed, 
	causing anguish to Ravana by tormenting his terrible army, and bidding his adieu to Sheetha, Hanuma 
	returned by flying over the middle of the sea._END

B_5_C_54_33
BEGIN_स सम्भ्रामत्रस्तविषण्णराक्षसां |
समुज्ज्वलज्ज्वालहुताशनाङ्किताम् |
ददर्श लङ्काम् हनुमान् महामानाः |
स्वयम्भूकोपोपहतामिवावनिम् || ५-५४-४२_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, with his great mind, saw Lanka with its dazed, frightened and dejected demons, 
marked by blazing flames of fire and afflicted by the fury of Brahma the creator of the universe._END

B_5_C_56_17
BEGIN_लतावितानैर्विततैः प्ष्पवद्भिरलम्कृतम् |
नानामृगगणाकीर्णम् धातुनिष्यन्दभूषितम् || ५-५६-१८_END
BEGIN_The mountain was adorned with clusters of creepers having plenty of flowers, filled with 
a number of summits and adorned with numerous caves scattered at many places and endowed with many sal, 
palmyrah, karna and bamboo trees._END

B_5_C_55_28
BEGIN_स तथा चिन्तयन् तत्र देव्या धर्म परिग्रहम् |
शुश्राव हनुमान् वाक्यम् चारणानाम् महात्मनाम् || ५-५५-२९_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, who was thus thinking there about the overpowering virtue of Seetha, happened 
to hear the words of the high-souled charanas (heavenly bards)._END

B_5_C_53_39
BEGIN_स भूत्वा शैल सम्काशः क्षणेन पुनः आत्मवान् || ५-५३-४१
ह्रस्वताम् परमाम् प्राप्तो बन्धनानि अवशातयत् |_END
BEGIN_That prudent Hanuma assumed the form of a mountain and immediately within a moment, assumed 
an exceedingly short form, thus becoming free from his tethers._END

B_5_C_57_7
BEGIN_पर्वत इन्द्रम् सुनाभम् च समुपस्पृश्य वीर्यवान् || ५-५७-१३
	ज्या मुक्त इव नाराचो महावेगो अभ्युपागतः |_END
BEGIN_Touching Mount Mainaka, the victorious Hanuma came with a great speed resembling 
	an iron arrow discharged from a bow-string._END

B_5_C_54_34
BEGIN_भम्क्त्वा वनम् पादपरत्नसम्कुलम् |
हत्वा तु रक्षांसि महान्ति सम्युगे |
दग्ध्वा पुरीम् ताम् गृहरत्नमालिनीम् |
तस्थौ हनूमान् पवनात्मजः कपिः || ५-५४-४३_END
BEGIN_After demolishing the garden which was full of excellent trees, killing great demons 
in battle and burning that city endowed with a series of excellent houses, Hanuma the monkey and the 
son of wind-god, stood at ease._END

B_5_C_56_18
BEGIN_बहुप्रस्रवणोपेतम् शिलासंचयसम्कटम् |
महर्षियक्षगन्धर्वकिन्नरोरगसेवितम् || ५-५६-१९_END
BEGIN_The mountain was endowed with many cascades, crowded together with heaps of rocks and 
frequented by great sages, Yakshas, Gandharvas, Kinnaras and celestial serpents._END

B_5_C_53_40
BEGIN_विमुक्तः च अभवत् श्रीमान् पुनः पर्वत सम्निभः || ५-५३-४२
वीक्षमाणः च ददृशे परिघम् तोरण आश्रितम् |_END
BEGIN_The glorious Hanuma, having been free from his bonds, again assumed the form equal to 
a mountain and while looking around, found and iron rod belonging to the arched door-way._END

B_5_C_55_29
