BEGIN_अहो खलु कृतम् कर्म दुर्विषह्यम् हनूमता |
अग्निम् विसृजता अभीक्ष्णम् भीमम् राक्षस सद्मनि || ५-५५-३०_END
BEGIN_"Alas! Hanuma, who hurled a very terrific fire into Ravana's house, has indeed done a 
difficult act."_END

B_5_C_57_8
BEGIN_स किंचित् अनुसम्प्राप्तः समालोक्य महागिरिम् || ५-५७-१४
	महाइन्द्र मेघ सम्काशम् ननाद हरि पुम्गवः |_END
BEGIN_Approaching a bit near and observing Maunt Mahendra, the great mauntain looking like 
	a dense claud, that Hanuma made a laud noise._END

B_5_C_54_35
BEGIN_त्रिकूटशृङ्गाग्रतले विचित्रे |
प्रतिष्ठितो वानरराजसिम्हः |
प्रदीप्तलाङ्गूलकृतार्चिमाली |
व्यराजतादित्य इवांशुमाली || ५-५४-४४_END
BEGIN_Standing there on the wonderful flat summit of Mount Trikuta, Hanuma the foremost leader 
of the monkeys, having a garland of flames formed by his blazing tail, shone like the sun having a garland 
of rays._END

B_5_C_56_19
BEGIN_लतापादपसम्घातम् सिम्हाध्युषितकन्दरम् |
व्याग्रसम्घसमाकीर्णम् स्वादुमूलफलद्रुमम् || ५-५६-२०_END
BEGIN_The mountain was exquisite with creepers and trees, having caves inhabited by lions, 
spread over with a number of tigers and endowed with sweet roots and fruit-trees._END

B_5_C_53_41
BEGIN_स तम् गृह्य महाबाहुः काल आयस परिष्कृतम् || ५-५३-४३
रक्षिणः तान् पुनः सर्वान् सूदयामास मारुतिः |_END
BEGIN_That long-armed Hanuma, again taking taht rod made of iron, killed all those guards._END

B_5_C_55_30
BEGIN_प्रपलायितरक्षः स्त्रीबाल वृद्धसमाकुला |
जनकोलाहलाध्माता क्रन्दन्तीवाद्रिकन्दरैः ||३१_END
BEGIN_"The city of Lanka, full of demons their wives, children and elders running hither and 
thither, as also filled with an uproar of people, appears as if it weeping through its mountain-caves."_END

B_5_C_57_9
BEGIN_स पूरयामास कपिर्दिशो दश समन्ततः || ५-५७-१५
	नदन्नदेव महता मेघस्वनमहास्वनः |_END
BEGIN_Emitting a great roar, that Hanuma, whole loud noise resembled the rumbling of a 
	cloud, filled the whole space in all directions with the noise._END

B_5_C_54_36
BEGIN_स राक्षसांस्तान् सुबहूंश्च हत्वा |
वनम् च भम्क्त्वा बहूपादपम् तत् |
विसृज्य रक्षोभवनेषु चाग्निम् |
जगाम रामम् मनसा महात्मा || ५-५४-४५_END
BEGIN_Killing those multitudes of demons, demolishing that garden endowed with several trees 
and scattering fire on the houses of demons, the high-souled Hanuma sought Rama with his mind._END

B_5_C_56_20
BEGIN_तम् आरुरोह हनुमान् पर्वतम् पवनात्मजः |
राम दर्शन शीघ्रेण प्रहर्षेण अभिचोदितः || ५-५६-२१_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the son of wind-god, in a hurry to see Rama, ascended that mountain, excited 
as he was with an extreme joy._END

B_5_C_53_42
BEGIN_स तान् निहत्वा रण चण्ड विक्रमः |
समीक्षमाणः पुनः एव लन्काम् |
प्रदीप्त लान्गूल कृत अर्चि माली |
प्रकाशत आदित्य इव अंशु माली || ५-५३-४४_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma, having an impetuous valour in combat, destroying those demons and looking 
over Lanka, shone like the sun encircled with rays, with the wreath of flames blazing on his tail._END

B_5_C_55_31
BEGIN_दग्धा इयम् नगरी लन्का साट्ट प्राकार तोरणा |
जानकी न च दग्धा इति विस्मयो अद्भुत एव नः || ५-५५-३२_END
BEGIN_"It is just so surprising a marvel to us that the entire City with its market-places, 
ramparts and arched door-ways, was burnt, but Seetha alone was not burnt."_END

B_5_C_54_37
BEGIN_ततस्तु तम् वानवीरमुख्यम् |
महाबलम् मारुततुल्यवेगम् |
महामतिम् वायुसुतम् वरिष्ठम् |
प्रतुष्टवुर्देवगणाश्च सर्वे || ५-५४-४६_END
BEGIN_Then, all the multitude of celestials enlogised that Hanuma, the principal warrior of 
the monkeys, possessing great strength and swiftness similar to the wind, greatly intelligent and the 
most excellent._END

B_5_C_57_10
BEGIN_स तम् देशमनुप्राप्तः सुहृद्दर्शनलालसः || ५-५७-१६
	ननाद हरिशार्दूलो लाङ्गूलम् चाप्यकम्पयत् |_END
BEGIN_Having reached that place, Hanuma who was ardently desiraus of seeing his friends, 
	roared and waved his tail._END

B_5_C_56_21
BEGIN_तेन पाद तल आक्रान्ता रम्येषु गिरि सानुषु |
सघोषाः समशीर्यन्त शिलाः चूर्णी कृताः ततः || ५-५६-२२_END
BEGIN_Then, the rocks in the charming table-land of the mountain, on which the soles of Hanuma 
lied heavily, were crushed with noise and fallen to pieces._END

B_5_C_55_32
BEGIN_स निमित्तैः च दृष्ट अर्थैः कारणैः च महागुणैः |
ऋषि वाक्यैः च हनुमान् अभवत् प्रीत मानसः || ५-५५-३३_END
BEGIN_That Hanuma became delighted in his mind, by seeing the omens, with their apparent advantages 
in them and very high qualities of their origin as also the words of those sages._END

B_5_C_54_38
BEGIN_भम्क्त्वा वनम् महातेजा हत्वा रक्षांसि सम्युगे |
दग्ध्वा लङ्कापुरीम् रम्याम् रराज स महाकपिः || ५-५४-४७_END
BEGIN_Demolishing the garden, killing the demons in battle, Hanuma of great splendour shone 
brightly, after burning the beautiful City of Lanka._END

B_5_C_57_11
BEGIN_तस्य नानद्यमानस्य सुपर्णचरिते पथि || ५-५७-१७
	फलतीवास्य घोषेण गगनम् सार्कमण्डलम् |_END
BEGIN_The sky, with the disc of the sun, began to crack as it were, due to his roar, even 
	as he repeatedly roared on the path of the sky as followed by Garuda, the eagle endowed with charming 
	wings._END

B_5_C_56_22
BEGIN_स तम् आरुह्य शैल इन्द्रम् व्यवर्धत महाकपिः |
दक्षिणात् उत्तरम् पारम् प्रार्थयम्ल् लवण अम्भसः || ५-५६-२३_END
BEGIN_Desirous of reaching the northern shore from the southern shore of that ocean, Hanuma 
ascended that mountain and enlarged his body._END

B_5_C_55_33
BEGIN_ततः कपिः प्राप्त मनो रथ अर्थः |
ताम् अक्षताम् राज सुताम् विदित्वा |
प्रत्यक्षतः ताम् पुनः एव दृष्ट्वा |
प्रतिप्रयाणाय मतिम् चकार || ५-५५-३४_END
BEGIN_Then, Hanuma, having fulfilled his object of desire by learning that Seetha the princess 
remains uninjured, made up his mind to return only after seeing her personally yet again._END

B_5_C_54_39
BEGIN_तत्र देवाः सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाश्च परमर्ष्यः |
दृष्ट्वा लङ्काम् प्रद्ग्धाम् ताम् विस्मयम् परमम् गताः || ५-५४-४८_END
BEGIN_Seeing that city of Lanka burnt there, celestials, saints and great sages along with 
celestial's musicians, got a colossal surprise._END

B_5_C_57_12
BEGIN_ये तु तत्रोत्तरे तीरे समुद्रस्य महाबलाः | ५-५७-१८
	पूर्वम् सम्विष्ठिताः शूरा वायुपुत्रदिदृक्षवः |
	महतो वातनुन्नस्य तोयदस्येव गर्जितम् || ५-५७-१९
	शुश्रुवुस्ते तदा घोषमूरुवेगम् हनूमतः |_END
BEGIN_Those mighty heroes who were waiting already on the northern shore of the sea, with 
	an eagerness to see Hanuma, heard there at that time, the saund produced by the sweeping motion 
	of Hanuma's thighs, which resembled the reoar of a huge claud propelled by the wind._END

B_5_C_56_23
BEGIN_अधिरुह्य ततो वीरः पर्वतम् पवन आत्मजः |
ददर्श सागरम् भीमम् मीन उरग निषेवितम् || ५-५६-२४_END
BEGIN_Then, the valiant Hanuma after ascending the mountain, saw the terrific ocean inhabited 
by fishes and water-snakes._END

B_5_C_57_13
BEGIN_ते दीनमनसः सर्वे शुश्रुवुः काननौकसः || ५-५७-२०
	वानरेन्द्रस्य निर्घोषम् पर्जन्यनिनदोपमम् |_END
BEGIN_All those monkeys, who were distressed in mind (for not having heard the news of 
	Seetha hitherto), heard Hanuma's roar similar to the roar of a rumbling cloud._END

B_5_C_54_40
BEGIN_तम् दृष्ट्वा वानरश्रेष्ठम् हनुमन्तम् महाकपिम् |
कालाग्निरिति संचिन्त्य सर्वभूतानि तत्रसुः || ५-५४-४९_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Hanuma, the foremost among the monkeys and a mighty monkey, all the created 
beings were frightened, thinking of him as a fire that is to destroy the world._END

B_5_C_56_24
BEGIN_स मारुत इव आकाशम् मारुतस्य आत्म सम्भवः |
प्रपेदे हरि शार्दूलो दक्षिणात् उत्तराम् दिशम् || ५-५६-२५_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, the foremost among the monkeys and the son of the wind-god, entered the sky towards 
northern direction, like a wind, from southern direction._END

B_5_C_54_41
BEGIN_देवाश्च सर्वे मुनिपुङ्गवाश्च |
गन्धर्वविद्याधरनागयक्षाः |
भूतानि सर्वाणि महान्ति तत्र |
जग्मुः पराम् प्रीतिमतुल्यरूपाम् || ५-५४-५०_END
BEGIN_There, all the celestial musicians, Vidyadharas the supernatural beings, Nagas the celestial 
serpents, Yakshas the spirits and all great living beings attained a great joy._END

B_5_C_57_14
BEGIN_निशम्य नदतो नादम् वानराः ते समन्ततः || ५-५७-२१
	बभूवुः उत्सुकाः सर्वे सुहृत् दर्शन कान्क्षिणः |_END
BEGIN_Hearing that roar of Hanuma, who was making the saund, all those mokeys stationed 
	there in all directions, became anxiausly desiraus of seeing their friend._END

B_5_C_56_25
BEGIN_स तदा पीडितः तेन कपिना पर्वत उत्तमः |
ररास सह तैः भूतैः प्राविशत् वसुधा तलम् || ५-५६-२६
कम्पमानैः च शिखरैः पतद्भिः अपि च द्रुमैः |_END
BEGIN_Pressed at that moment by Hanuma, that excellent mountain sank into the bowels of the 
earth along with the various living beings and made a noise with its shaking summits and toppling trees._END

B_5_C_56_26
BEGIN_तस्य ऊरु वेगान् मथिताः पादपाः पुष्प शालिनः || ५-५६-२७
निपेतुः भू तले रुग्णाः शक्र आयुध हता इव |_END
BEGIN_Shaken by the impetus of the thighs of Hanuma, trees in blossom were broken and fell 
down on earth, as though struck by a thunder-bolt._END

B_5_C_57_15
BEGIN_जाम्बवान् स हरि श्रेष्ठः प्रीति सम्हृष्ट मानसः || ५-५७-२२
	उपामन्त्र्य हरीन् सर्वान् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_The Jambavan, the foremot among the monkesy and bears, with his mind thrilled with 
	joy, having summoned all the monkeys, spoke the follwoing words:_END

B_5_C_56_27
BEGIN_कन्दर उदर संस्थानाम् पीडितानाम् महाओजसाम् || ५-५६-२८
सिम्हानाम् निनदो भीमो नभो भिन्दन् स शुश्रुवे |_END
BEGIN_When the lions of great prowess dwelling in the midst of caves were tormented and roared 
terribly, that roaring noise was heard as it was piercing the sky._END

B_5_C_57_16
BEGIN_सर्वथा कृत कार्यो असौ हनूमान् न अत्र संशयः || ५-५७-२३
	न हि अस्य अकृत कार्यस्य नाद एवम् विधो भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"This Hanuma has accoMplished his assignment in all ways. His saund will not indeed 
	be like this, if he has not fulfilled his task. There is not daubt in this matter."_END

B_5_C_56_28
BEGIN_त्रस्त व्याअविद्ध वसना व्याकुली कृत भूषणा || ५-५६-२९
विद्याधर्यः समुत्पेतुः सहसा धरणी धरात् |_END
BEGIN_The females of Vidyadhara class of supernatural beings, with their raiments in disorder 
through fear and their ornaments fallen off, went up all of a sudden from the mountain._END

B_5_C_58_0
BEGIN_ततः तस्य गिरेः शृन्गे महाइन्द्रस्य महाबलाः |
हनुमत् प्रमुखाः प्रीतिम् हरयो जग्मुः उत्तमाम् || ५-५८-१_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, the mighty monkeys, headed by Hanuma and others, experienced a great joy 
on that summit of Mount Mahendra._END

B_5_C_57_17
BEGIN_तस्या बाहु ऊरु वेगम् च निनादम् च महात्मनः || ५-५७-२४
	निशम्य हरयो हृष्टाः समुत्पेतुः ततः ततः |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the sound of the dashing movement of the high souled Hanuma's arms and thighs, 
	the monkeys moved by jumps with joy from their respective places._END

B_5_C_58_1
BEGIN_तम् ततः प्रतिसम्हृष्टः प्रीतिमन्तम् महाकपिम् |
जाम्बवान् कार्य वृत्त अन्तम् अपृच्छत् अनिल आत्मजम् || ५-५८-२_END
BEGIN_Then, Jambavan, thrilling with rapture, asked the delighted Hanuma, the great monkey 
about the particulars of that actual occurrence (of seeing Seetha) as follows_END

B_5_C_56_29
BEGIN_अतिप्रमाणा बलिनो दीप्त जिह्वा महाविषाः || ५-५६-३०
निपीडित शिरो ग्रीवा व्यवेष्टन्त महाहयः |_END
BEGIN_Large poisonous serpents of immense size, possessing vigour and having fiery tongues 
with their hoods and necks severely pressed lay coiled._END

B_5_C_57_18
BEGIN_ते नग अग्रान् नग अग्राणि शिखरात् शिखराणि च || ५-५७-२५
	प्रहृष्टाः समपद्यन्त हनूमन्तम् दिदृक्षवः |_END
BEGIN_Those monkeys with joy, longing to see Hanuma, took off from the top of one tree 
	to the tops of other trees as also from one mauntain-summit to the other summits._END

B_5_C_56_30
BEGIN_किन्नर उरग गन्धर्व यक्ष विद्या धराः तथा || ५-५६-३१
पीडितम् तम् नग वरम् त्यक्त्वा गगनम् आस्थिताः |_END
BEGIN_Then, leaving that tormented mountain of excellence; Kinnaras, Nagas, Gadharvas, Yakshas 
and Vidyadharas ascended to the sky._END

B_5_C_58_2
BEGIN_कथम् दृष्टा त्वया देवी कथम् वा तत्र वर्तते |
तस्याम् वा स कथम् वृत्तः क्रूर कर्मा दश आननः || ५-५८-३_END
BEGIN_"How did you see Seetha? How was she there? How was that Ravana of terrible deeds behaving 
towards her?"_END

B_5_C_57_19
BEGIN_ते प्रीताः पादप अग्रेषु गृह्य शाखाः सुपुष्पिताः || ५-५७-२६
	वासांसि इव प्रकाशानि समाविध्यन्त वानराः |_END
BEGIN_Those monkeys, grasping the boughs at the tops of trees, and standing there firmly, 
	joyously waved the twigs, as if they are their raiments._END

B_5_C_58_3
BEGIN_तत्त्वतः सर्वम् एतन् नः प्रब्रूहि त्वम् महाकपे |
श्रुत अर्थाः चिन्तयिष्यामो भूयः कार्य विनिश्चयम् || ५-५८-४_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Tell us entirely, in truth whatever has occurred. Ascertaining the truth, 
from you, we shall again think about what decision to be taken further."_END

B_5_C_56_31
BEGIN_स च भूमि धरः श्रीमान् बलिना तेन पीडितः || ५-५६-३२
सवृक्ष शिखर उदग्राः प्रविवेश रसा तलम् |_END
BEGIN_Pressed down by that strong Hanuma, that beautiful mountain having its elevated summits 
crowned with trees, entered the bowels of the earth._END

B_5_C_57_20
BEGIN_गिरिगह्वरसम्लीनो यथा गर्जति मारुतः || ५-५७-२७
	एवम् जगर्ज बलवान् हनुमान्मारुतातमजः |_END
BEGIN_The mighty, Hanuma the son of wind-god, roared as thaugh the wind roars while it 
	enters the caves of mauntains._END

B_5_C_58_4
BEGIN_यः च अर्थः तत्र वक्तव्यो गतैः अस्माभिः आत्मवान् |
रक्षितव्यम् च यत् तत्र तत् भवान् व्याकरोतु नः || ५-५८-५_END
BEGIN_"When we go there (to the presence of Rama), having prudence, tell us clearly which matter 
is to be disclosed and which matter is to be kept off from him."_END

B_5_C_56_32
BEGIN_दश योजन विस्तारः त्रिंशत् योजनम् उच्छ्रितः || ५-५६-३३
धरण्याम् समताम् यातः स बभूव धरा धरः |_END
BEGIN_That mountain, with a width of ten yojanas (or eighty miles) and a height of thirty yojanas 
(or two hundred and forty miles) got level with the earth._END

B_5_C_57_21
BEGIN_तम् अभ्र घन संकाशम् आपतन्तम् महाकपिम् || ५-५७-२८
	दृष्ट्वा ते वानराः सर्वे तस्थुः प्रान्जलयः तदा |_END
BEGIN_Seeing that Hanuma then rushing like a dense cloud, all those monkeys stood there, 
	joining their palms in salutation._END

B_5_C_59_0
BEGIN_एतत् आख्यानम् तत् सर्वम् हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
भूयः समुपचक्राम वचनम् वक्तुम् उत्तरम् || ५-५९-१_END
BEGIN_After informing all this, Hanuma the son of wind-god started telling more of the following 
words._END

B_5_C_56_33
BEGIN_स लिलङ्घुयिर्भीमम् सलीलम् लवणार्णवम् || ५-५६-३४
कल्लोलास्फालवेलान्तमुत्पपात नभो हरिः |_END
BEGIN_With a desire to cross easily the terrific ocean, whose shores were being lashed by its 
waves, which Hanuma jumped up into the air._END

B_5_C_58_5
BEGIN_स नियुक्तः ततः तेन सम्प्रहृष्ट तनू रुहः |
नमस्यन् शिरसा देव्यै सीतायै प्रत्यभाषत || ५-५८-६_END
BEGIN_Thus commanded by Jambavan, Hanuma, with his hair standing on end mentally offered his 
salutation to Seetha, the princess, by bowing his head and replied as follows:_END

B_5_C_57_22
BEGIN_ततः तु वेगवान् तस्य गिरेः गिरि निभः कपिः || ५-५७-२९
	निपपात महाइन्द्रस्य शिखरे पादप आकुले |_END
BEGIN_The swift Hanuma, looking like a mauntain, then descended on the summit of that Maunt 
	mahendra, thick with trees._END

B_5_C_59_1
BEGIN_सफलो राघव उद्योगः सुग्रीवस्य च सम्भ्रमः |
शीलम् आसाद्य सीताया मम च प्रवणम् मनः || ५-५९-२_END
BEGIN_"By the power of virtuousness of Seetha, Rama's effort and Sugreeva's zeal are getting 
fulfilled. My mind too is devoted to her."_END

B_5_C_58_6
BEGIN_प्रत्यक्षम् एव भवताम् महाइन्द्र अग्रात् खम् आप्लुतः |
उदधेः दक्षिणम् पारम् कान्क्षमाणः समाहितः || ५-५८-७_END
BEGIN_"With an intention to reach the southern shore of the ocean, I leapt into the sky, indeed 
before your presence, from the summit of Mount Mahendra."_END

B_5_C_57_23
BEGIN_हर्षेणापूर्यमाणोऽसौ रम्ये पर्वतनिर्घरे || ५-५७-३०
	चिन्नपक्ष इवाकाशात्पपात धरणीधरः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma like a mountain with its wings torn off, thrilled with joy, fell from the 
	sky into a charming mountain-torrent._END

B_5_C_59_2
BEGIN_तपसा निर्दहेल्लोकान् स्रुद्धो वा निर्दहेदपि |
सर्वधातिप्रवृद्धोऽसौ रावणो राक्षसाधिपः || ५-५९-३_END
BEGIN_"Ravana, the king of demons, who is strong in all ways, can burn away the three worlds 
by the power of his penance. Even if he is enraged, he can scorch away his adversaries."_END

B_5_C_57_24
BEGIN_ततः ते प्रीत मनसः सर्वे वानर पुम्गवाः || ५-५७-३१
	हनूमन्तम् महात्मानम् परिवार्य उपतस्थिरे |
	परिवार्य च ते सर्वे पराम् प्रीतिम् उपागताः || ५-५७-३२_END
BEGIN_Then, all the foremost of those monkeys, with their pleasing hearts, stood surraunding 
	the high-sauled Hanuma. Having encircled Hanuma, all of them obtained a supreme joy._END

B_5_C_58_7
BEGIN_गच्छतः च हि मे घोरम् विघ्न रूपम् इव अभवत् |
कान्चनम् शिखरम् दिव्यम् पश्यामि सुमनो हरम् || ५-५८-८_END
BEGIN_"While I was going, a terrific hindrance occurred in my way as it was. I saw a golden 
mountain-peak which was so charming and fascinating."_END

B_5_C_59_3
BEGIN_तस्य ताम् स्पृशतो गात्रम् तपसा न विनाशितम् |
न तदग्निशिखा कुर्यात्संस्पृष्टा पाणिना सती || ५-५९-४
जनकस्य सुता कुर्याद्यत्क्रोधकलुषीकृता |_END
BEGIN_"His body, which touched Seetha the daughter of Janaka, was not destroyed because of 
his askesis. Even a flame, when fully touched with one's hand, cannot do that which Seetha would, if 
stirred by anger."_END

B_5_C_58_8
BEGIN_स्थितम् पन्थानम् आवृत्य मेने विघ्नम् च तम् नगम् |
उपसम्गम्य तम् दिव्यम् कान्चनम् नग सत्तमम् || ५-५८-९
कृता मे मनसा बुद्धिः भेत्तव्यो अयम् मया इति च |_END
BEGIN_"I accounted that mountain staying turned towards the path, as an impediment. Approaching 
that excellent charming and golden mountain, I made up my mind to shatter it."_END

B_5_C_57_25
BEGIN_प्रहृष्ट वदनाः सर्वे तम् अरोगम् उपागतम् |
	उपायनानि च आदाय मूलानि च फलानि च || ५-५७-३३
	प्रत्यर्चयन् हरि श्रेष्ठम् हरयो मारुत आत्मजम् |_END
BEGIN_All those mokeys with their delightful faces, taking roots and fruits as their presents, 
	honured Hanuma, the foremost among the monkeys, who came back hale and healthy._END

B_5_C_59_4
BEGIN_जाम्बवत्प्रमुखान् सर्वाननुज्ञाप्य महाहरीन् || ५-५९-५
अस्मिन्नेवम् गते कार्ये भवताम् च निवेदिते |
न्याय्यम् स्म सह वैदेह्या द्रष्टुम् तौ पार्थिवात्मजौ || ५-५९-६_END
BEGIN_"This work (of mine in the form of Seetha's discovery) has been informed to you in this 
way. It is indeed proper to see those two princes (Rama and Lakshmana) along with Seetha, after taking 
permission from all the great monkeys headed by Jambavan._END

B_5_C_58_9
BEGIN_प्रहतम् च मया तस्य लान्गूलेन महागिरेः || ५-५८-१०
शिखरम् सूर्य सम्काशम् व्यशीर्यत सहस्रधा |_END
BEGIN_"As I struck it with my tail, the mountain-peak of that great hill, resembling the sun, 
was broken into a thousand pieces."_END

B_5_C_57_26
BEGIN_हनूमान् तु गुरून् वृद्धान् जाम्बवत् प्रमुखान् तदा || ५-५७-३४
	कुमारम् अन्गदम् चैव सो अवन्दत महाकपिः |_END
BEGIN_Then, Hanuma the excellent one among the monkeys, on his part, offered his salutation 
	to venerable persons and elders like Jambavan in the first place, as also Angada, the prince._END

B_5_C_59_5
BEGIN_अहमेकोऽपि पर्याप्तः सराक्षसगणाम् पुरीम् |
ताम् लङ्काम् तरसा हन्तुम् रावणम् च महाबलम् || ५-५९-७_END
BEGIN_"I am sufficient, even alone; to destroy rapidly that City of Lanka together with those 
troops of demons as also the mighty Ravana."_END

B_5_C_57_27
BEGIN_स ताभ्याम् पूजितः पूज्यः कपिभिः च प्रसादितः || ५-५७-३५
	दृष्टा देवी इति विक्रान्तः संक्षेपेण न्यवेदयत् |_END
BEGIN_Jambavan and Angada honoured that victorious and venerable Hanuma. The other monkeys 
	also made him gracious. Hanuma informed them briefly that he had seen Seetha._END

B_5_C_58_10
BEGIN_व्यवसायम् च मे बुद्ध्वा स ह उवाच महागिरिः || ५-५८-११
पुत्र इति मधुराम् बाणीम् मनः प्रह्लादयन्न् इव |_END
BEGIN_"Understanding my purpose, that great mountain spoke the following sweet words saying, 
'O my son!', As though it was refreshing my mind (once more to proceed further)."_END

B_5_C_59_6
BEGIN_किम् पुनः सहितो वीरैर्बलवद्भिः कृतात्मभिः |
कृतास्त्रैः प्लवगैः शूरैर्भवद्भिर्विजयैषिभिः || ५-५९-८_END
BEGIN_"When accompanied by you, who are strong, whose spirit is disciplined, who are proficient 
in the use of arms, valiant, longing for victory and moving by jumps, how much more is required?"_END

B_5_C_57_28
BEGIN_निषसाद च हस्तेन गृहीत्वा वालिनः सुतम् || ५-५७-३६
	रमणीये वन उद्देशे महाइन्द्रस्य गिरेः तदा |_END
BEGIN_Then, seizing the hand of Angada, Vali's son, Hanuma sat down at a distinct spot 
	in the charming forest of Maunt Mahendra._END

B_5_C_58_11
BEGIN_पितृव्यम् च अपि माम् विद्धि सखा अयम् मातरिश्वनः || ५-५८-१२
मैनाकम् इति विख्यातम् निवसन्तम् महाउदधौ |_END
BEGIN_" 'Know me to be generally called as Mynaa dwelling in this great ocean, as a companion 
of the wind-god and even as your father's brother'."_END

B_5_C_59_7
BEGIN_अहम् तु रावणम् युद्धे ससैन्यम् सपुरःसरम् |
सहपुत्रम् वधिष्यामि सहोदरयुतम् युधि || ५-५९-९_END
BEGIN_"In the battle, I on my part will kill Ravana along with his army, his forerunners, his 
sons and his brothers."_END

B_5_C_57_29
BEGIN_हनूमान् अब्रवीद्त् हृष्टः तदा तान् वानर ऋषभान् || ५-५७-३७
	अशोक वनिका संस्था दृष्टा सा जनक आत्मजा |
	रक्ष्यमाणा सुघोराभी राक्षसीभिः अनिन्दिता || ५-५७-३८
	एक वेणी धरा बाला राम दर्शन लालसा |
	उपवास परिश्रान्ता मलिना जटिला कृशा || ५-५७-३९_END
BEGIN_Then, the pleased Hanuma spoke the following words to those excellent monkeys: "I 
	saw that Seetha, the duaghter of Janaka, who was staying in Ashoka garden, guarded unblemished by 
	highly dreadful female-demons and wearing a single braid, young woman, as she was, longing to see 
	Rama, thoroughly fatigued due to her fasting, with her hair twisted together, wearing soiled clothes 
	and looking emaciated."_END

B_5_C_58_12
BEGIN_पक्ष्ववन्तः पुरा पुत्र बभूवुः पर्वत उत्तमाः || ५-५८-१३
चन्दतः पृथिवीम् चेरुः बाधमानाः समन्ततः |_END
BEGIN_" 'O my son! Long ago, the foremost among the mountains used to have wings. They used 
to wander the entire earth freely, hurting the people!"_END

B_5_C_59_8
BEGIN_ब्रह्ममैन्द्रम् च रौद्रम् च वायव्यम् वारुणम् तथा |
यदि शक्रजोतोऽ स्त्रणि दुर्निरीक्षाणि सम्युगे || ५-५९-१०
तान्यहम् विधष्यामि हनिष्यामि च रावणम् |_END
BEGIN_"In the battle, I can blow out the missiles presided over by Indra the lord of celestials, 
Brahma the creator, Rudra the god of destruction, Vayu the wind-god, Varuna the god of water and even 
those missiles even if they are difficult to be looked at, employed by Indrajit (Ravana's eldest son)._END

B_5_C_57_30
BEGIN_ततो दृष्टा इति वचनम् महाअर्थम् अमृत उपमम् || ५-५७-४०
	निशम्य मारुतेः सर्वे मुदिता वानरा भवन् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing from Hanuma that iMportant and nectar like word to the effect that Sheetha 
	had been seen all the monkeys became delighted._END

B_5_C_58_13
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा नगानाम् चरितम् महाइन्द्रः पाक शासनः || ५-५८-१४
चिच्छेद भगवान् पक्षान् वज्रेण एषाम् सहस्रशः |_END
BEGIN_" 'Hearing that behaviour of those mountains, the venerable Indra the lord of celestials, 
the destroyer of a demon called Paka, chopped their wings into a thousand pieces by using his thunderbolt.' 
"_END

B_5_C_60_0
BEGIN_तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा वालि सूनुः अभाषत |
अयुक्तम् तु विना देवीम् दृष्ट्वद्भिश्च वानराः || ५-६०-१
समीपम् गन्तुमस्माभी राघवस्य महात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Hanuma, Angada the son of Vali spoke as follows: "Even after our 
seeing of Seetha, it is not proper for us to approach the high-souled Rama without taking Seetha with 
us."_END

B_5_C_59_9
BEGIN_भवतामभ्यनुज्ञातो विक्रमो मे रुणद्धि तम् || ५-५९-११
मयातुला विसृष्टा हि शैलवृष्टिर्निरन्तरा |
देवानपि रणे हन्यात्किम् पुनस्तान्निशाचरान् || ५-५९-१२_END
BEGIN_"My prowess, when permitted by you, will frustrate that Ravana. The shower of rocks, 
which will be unequalled and incessant, discharged by me, can kill even celestials. How much more those 
demons?"_END

B_5_C_57_31
BEGIN_क्ष्वेडन्ति अन्ये नदन्ति अन्ये गर्जन्ति अन्ये महाबलाः |
	चक्रुः किल किलाम् अन्ये प्रतिगर्जन्ति च अपरे || ५-५७-४१_END
BEGIN_Some mighty monkeys made a lion's roar. Some were making a sound of approbation. 
	Some were making a sound of thunder. Some others proudced cries expressing joy. Some others were 
	roaring in return._END

B_5_C_58_14
BEGIN_अहम् तु मोक्षितः तस्मात् तव पित्रा महात्मना || ५-५८-१५
मारुतेन तदा वत्स प्रक्षिप्तो अस्मि महाअर्णवे |_END
BEGIN_" 'O child! I, on my part, was hurled into the great ocean by the high-souled wind-god, 
your father and was liberated from the clutches of Indra.' "_END

B_5_C_60_1
BEGIN_दृष्टा देवी न च आनीता इति तत्र निवेदनम् || ५-६०-२
अयुक्तम् इव पश्यामि भवद्भिः ख्यात विक्रमैः |_END
BEGIN_"I perceive it as improper to inform there that Seetha the princess, though seen by you 
of renowned prowess, has not been brought here."_END

B_5_C_59_10
BEGIN_सागरोऽप्यतियाद्वेलाम् मन्दरः प्रचलेदपि |
न जाम्बवन्तम् समरे कम्पयेदरिवाहिनी || ५-५९-१३_END
BEGIN_"The ocean may overflow its shore. Mount Mandara may move from its position. But, in 
battle, no army of adversaries can stagger Jambavan."_END

B_5_C_57_32
BEGIN_केचित् उच्छ्रित लान्गूलाः प्रहृष्टाः कपि कुन्जराः |
	अन्चित आयत दीर्घाणि लान्गूलानि प्रविव्यधुः || ५-५७-४२_END
BEGIN_Shome eminent monkeys, with joy and with their tails lifted up, waved their distended 
	curved tails._END

B_5_C_58_15
BEGIN_रामस्य च मया साह्ये वर्तितव्यम् अरिम् दम || ५-५८-१६
रामो धर्मभृताम् श्रेष्ठो महाइन्द्र सम विक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_" 'O Hanuma the annihilator of enemies! I have to behave in such a way as to help Rama. 
For, Rama, having a prowess equal to that of Indra; is indeed excellent in supporting righteousness.'"_END

B_5_C_60_2
BEGIN_न हि वः प्लवते कश्चिन् न अपि कश्चित् पराक्रमे || ५-६०-३
तुल्यः सामर दैत्येषु लोकेषु हरि सत्तमाः |_END
BEGIN_"O the best of monkeys! No one is equal to us even in our prowess nor indeed anyone who 
can leap like us in the worlds either of celestials or demons."_END

B_5_C_59_11
BEGIN_सर्वराक्षससम्घानाम् राक्षसा ये च महात्मनः |
अलमेको विनाशाय वीरो वालिसुतः कपिः || ५-५९-१४_END
BEGIN_"The heroic Angada, the son of Vali alone, is sufficient to destroy all the troops of 
demons and even the demons who were their progenitors."_END

B_5_C_57_33
BEGIN_अपरे तु हनूमन्तम् वानरा वारण उपमम् |
	आप्लुत्य गिरि शृन्गेभ्यः संस्पृशन्ति स्म हर्षिताः || ५-५७-४३_END
BEGIN_Descending from the mountain-tops; some other monkeys, with delight, fondingly touched 
	Hanuma who resembled an elephant._END

B_5_C_58_16
BEGIN_एतत् श्रुत्वा मया तस्य मैनाकस्य महात्मनः || ५-५८-१७
कार्यम् आवेद्य तु गिरेः उद्धतम् च मनो मम |
तेन च अहम् अनुज्ञातो मैनाकेन महात्मना || ५-५८-१८_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the words of that high-souled Mynaka and after informing my purpose, my mind 
was prepared for a further travel. The high-soled Mynaka also allowed me to depart."_END

B_5_C_60_3
BEGIN_तेष्व् एवम् हत वीरेषु राक्षसेषु हनूमता || ५-६०-४
किम् अन्यत् अत्र कर्तव्यम् गृहीत्वा याम जानकीम् |_END
BEGIN_"Hanuma indeed thus killed all the warriors among the demons. What work is remaining 
to be done by us? We will go, after taking Janaki."_END

B_5_C_59_12
BEGIN_पनसस्योरुवेगेन नीलस्य च महात्मनः |
मन्दरोऽप्यवशीर्येत किम्पुनर्युधि राक्षसाः || ५-५९-१५_END
BEGIN_"By the rapid movement of the thighs of the high-souled Neela and of Panasa, even Mount 
Mandara can be shattered. How much more, the demons in battle?"_END

B_5_C_58_17
BEGIN_स चाप्यन्तर्हितः शैलो मानुषेण वपुष्मता |
शरीरेण महाशैलः शैलेन च महोदधौ || ५-५८-१९_END
BEGIN_"That Mynaka mountain vanished in the guise of a beautiful form of a human being. That 
large mountainous form also later drowned into the great ocean."_END

B_5_C_57_34
BEGIN_उक्त वाक्यम् हनूमन्तम् अन्गदः तु तदा अब्रवीत् |
	सर्वेषाम् हरि वीराणाम् मध्ये वाचम् अनुत्तमाम् || ५-५७-४४_END
BEGIN_After hearing the words of Hanuma, Angada spoke the follwoing excellent words in 
	the midst of those eminent monkeys._END

B_5_C_60_4
BEGIN_तम् एवम् कृत सम्कल्पम् जाम्बवान् हरि सत्तमः || ५-६०-५
उवाच परम प्रीतो वाक्यम् अर्थवत् अर्थवित् |_END
BEGIN_Jambavan, the foremost among the forest-animals, understanding the sense, was very much 
pleased and spoke the following meaningful words to that Angada, who thus formed a resolution._END

B_5_C_59_13
BEGIN_सदेवासुरयक्षेषु गन्धर्वोरगपक्षिषु |
मैन्दस्य प्रतियोद्धारम् शंसत द्विविदस्य वा || ५-५९-१६_END
BEGIN_"Tell me any one who can fight against Mainda or Dvivida, among Gandharvas the celestial 
singers or Uragas the serpents or Pakshis the birds or the celestials or the demons or Yakshas the semi-divine 
beings."_END

B_5_C_58_18
BEGIN_उत्तमम् जवम् आस्थाय शेषम् अध्वानम् आस्थितः |
ततो अहम् सुचिरम् कालम् वेगेन अभ्यगमम् पथि || ५-५८-२०_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, employing an excellent speed and continuing on my course, I proceeded in 
that path speedily for a long time."_END

B_5_C_60_5
BEGIN_न तावत् एषा मतिः अक्षमा नो |
यथा भवान् पश्यति राज पुत्र |
यथा तु रामस्य मतिः निविष्टा |
तथा भवान् पश्यतु कार्य सिद्धिम् || ५-६०-६_END
BEGIN_"O prince! This thought you thus perceive is not incompetent of us. But, you must see 
the way in which Rama's inclination would be, for the accomplishment of the object."_END

B_5_C_57_35
BEGIN_सत्त्वे वीर्ये न ते कश्चित् समो वानर विद्यते |
	यत् अवप्लुत्य विस्तीर्णम् सागरम् पुनः आगतः || ५-५७-४५_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Since you returned here crossing the extensive ocean, none stands equal 
	to you in strength and prowess."_END

B_5_C_59_14
BEGIN_अश्विपुत्रौ महाभागावेतौ प्लवगसत्तमौ |
एतयोः प्रतियोद्धारम् न पश्यामि रणाजिरे || ५-५९-१७_END
BEGIN_"These two illustrious sons of Ashvini Kumaras, Mainda and Dvivida are the foremost among 
the monkeys. In the battle-field, I do not find anyone who can fight against these two monkeys."_END

B_5_C_58_19
BEGIN_ततः पश्यामि अहम् देवीम् सुरसाम् नाग मातरम् |
समुद्र मध्ये सा देवी वचनम् माम् अभाषत || ५-५८-२१_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, I saw Surasa, the mother of serpents in the midst of the sea. That goddess 
spoke the following words to me._END

B_5_C_57_36
BEGIN_अहो स्वामिनि ते भक्तिरहो वीर्यमहो धृतिः |
	दिष्ट्या दृष्टा त्वया देवी राम पत्नी यशस्विनी || ५-५७-४६
	दिष्ट्या त्यक्ष्यति काकुत्स्थः शोकम् सीता वियोगजम् |_END
BEGIN_"What amazing is yaur devotion to the Lord! What a wonderful prowess! What a surprising 
	caurage! By aur good fortune, yau saw the illustriaus Sheetha, Rama's consort. Thank heaven! Rama 
	can give up his sorrow born aut of Sheetha's separataion."_END

B_5_C_61_0
BEGIN_ततो जाम्बवतो वाक्यम् अगृह्णन्त वन ओकसः |
अन्गद प्रमुखा वीरा हनूमान् च महाकपिः || ५-६१-१_END
BEGIN_Thereupon, the heroic monkeys like Angada and others as also Hanuma, the great one among 
the monkeys accepted the words of Jambavan._END

B_5_C_59_15
BEGIN_पितामहवरोत्सेकात्परमम् दर्पमास्थितौ |
अमृतप्राशनावेतौ सर्ववानरसत्तमौ || ५-५९-१८_END
BEGIN_"Proud of having received boons from Brahma the creator and their grandfather and abiding 
in a supreme haughtiness, these two foremost among all the monkeys live on Amrita the nectar."_END

B_5_C_58_20
BEGIN_मम भक्ष्यः प्रदिष्टः त्वम् अमारैः हरि सत्तमम् |
ततः त्वाम् भक्षयिष्यामि विहितः त्वम् चिरस्य मे || ५-५८-२२_END
BEGIN_"O excellent of monkeys! The celestials have shown you as my eatable. Therefore, I will 
eat you since you have been bestowed to me by gods after a long time."_END

B_5_C_57_37
BEGIN_ततो अन्गदम् हनूमन्तम् जाम्बवन्तम् च वानराः || ५-५७-४७
	परिवार्य प्रमुदिता भेजिरे विपुलाः शिलाः |_END
BEGIN_Very much delighted, the monkeys then sat on extensive flat rocks encircling Angada, 
	Hanuma and Jambavan._END

B_5_C_61_1
BEGIN_प्रीतिमन्तः ततः सर्वे वायु पुत्र पुरः सराः |
महाइन्द्र अग्रम् परित्यज्य पुप्लुवुः प्लवग ऋषभाः || ५-६१-२
मेरु मन्दर सम्काशा मत्ता इव महागजाः |
चादयन्त इव आकाशम् महाकाया महाबलाः || ५-६१-३
सभाज्यमानम् भूतैः तम् आत्मवन्तम् महाबलम् |
हनूमन्तम् महावेगम् वहन्त इव दृष्टिभिः || ५-६१-४
राघवे च अर्थ निर्वृत्तिम् भर्तुः च परमम् यशः |
समाधाय समृद्ध अर्थाः कर्म सिद्धिभिः उन्नताः || ५-६१-५
प्रिय आख्यान उन्मुखाः सर्वे सर्वे युद्ध अभिनन्दिनः |
सर्वे राम प्रतीकारे निश्चित अर्था मनस्विनः || ५-६१-६_END
BEGIN_Then, the excellent monkeys, resembling Meru and Mandara mountains, like elephants in 
rut, as if covering the sky, having huge bodies and colossal strength, keeping Hanuma in their front, 
leaving Mount Mahendra, went ahead leaping delightfully. They looked as though conducted by the mind's 
eyes of Hanuma, who is adored by living beings as having good stupendous swiftness, they having resolved 
to fulfill the purpose of Rama and to attain a great glory, having accomplished the purpose and duly 
determined to complete the task. All of them were looking up at narrating the previous pleasant tidings 
and taking delight in war. All of them, in high spirits, were judging rightly the vengeance of Rama 
against the evil-minded Ravana._END

B_5_C_59_16
BEGIN_अश्विनोर्माननार्थम् हि सर्वलोकपितामहः |
सर्वावध्यत्वमतुलमनयोर्दत्तवान् पुरा || ५-५९-१९_END
BEGIN_"Long ago, Brahma the grandfather of all the worlds gave an unequal boon to them in honour 
of Ashvini Kumaras regarding their inviolability."_END

B_5_C_58_21
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः सुरसया प्राञ्जलिः प्रणतः स्थितः |
विवर्ण वदनो भूत्वा वाक्यम् च इदम् उदीरयम् || ५-५८-२३_END
BEGIN_"Hearing Surasa's words, I stood there, offering salutation with my joined palms to her. 
Becoming pale-faced, I spoke the following words:_END

B_5_C_57_38
BEGIN_श्रोतु कामाः समुद्रस्य लन्घनम् वानर उत्तमाः || ५-५७-४८
	दर्शनम् च अपि लन्कायाः सीताया रावणस्य च |
	तस्थुः प्रान्जलयः सर्वे हनूमत् वदन उन्मुखाः || ५-५७-४९_END
BEGIN_Longing to hear abaut crossing of ocean and the seeing of Lanka, Sheetha and Ravana, 
	all those excellent monkeys waited with their joined pal.ns, in anctipation of Hanuma's words._END

B_5_C_61_2
BEGIN_प्लवमानाः खम् आप्लुत्य ततः ते कानन ओक्सकः |
नन्दन उपमम् आसेदुः वनम् द्रुम लता युतम् || ५-६१-७_END
BEGIN_Then, those monkeys, leaping into the sky and floating in the air, reached a garden looking 
like Nandanavana the divine grove filled with trees and creepers._END

B_5_C_59_17
BEGIN_वरोत्सेकेन मत्तौ च प्रमथ्य महतीम् चमूम् |
सुराणाममृतम् वीरौ पीतवन्तौ प्लवम्गमौ || ५-५९-२०_END
BEGIN_"By the pride of those boons, those two heroic monkeys harassed a great army of celestials 
and thereupon drank up nectar, excited as they were with joy."_END

B_5_C_58_22
BEGIN_रामो दाशरथिः श्रीमान् प्रविष्टो दण्डका वनम् |
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा सीतया च परम् तपः || ५-५८-२४_END
BEGIN_" 'Rama, the son of Dasaratha the splendid man and the tormentator of enemies, together 
with Lakshmana, his brother and Seetha entered the forest of Dandaka.'"_END

B_5_C_57_39
BEGIN_तस्थौ तत्र अन्गदः श्रीमान् वानरैः बहुभिः वृतः |
	उपास्यमानो विबुधैः दिवि देव पतिः यथा || ५-५७-५०_END
BEGIN_The auspicious Angada encircled by many monkeys there, waited like Indra the lord 
	of celestials, who was waited upon by celestials in heaven._END

B_5_C_61_3
BEGIN_यत् तन् मधु वनम् नाम सुग्रीवस्य अभिरक्षितम् |
अधृष्यम् सर्व भूतानाम् सर्व भूत मनो हरम् || ५-६१-८_END
BEGIN_They reached, that Madhuvana by name, the garden abounded with honey, which was protected 
grove, unapproachable for all and looking fascinated to the soul of all beings._END

B_5_C_59_18
BEGIN_एतावेन हि सम्क्रुद्धौ सवाजिरथकुम्जराम् |
लङ्काम् नाशयितुम् शक्तौ सर्वे तिष्ठन्तु वानराः || ५-५९-२१_END
BEGIN_"Let all the other monkeys stand aside. Even these Mainda and Dvivida on their part are 
capable of destroying the entire city of Lanka together with its horses, chariots and elephants."_END

B_5_C_58_23
BEGIN_तस्य सीता हृता भार्या रावणेन दुरात्मना |
तस्याः सकाशम् दूतो अहम् गमिष्ये राम शासनात् || ५-५८-२५_END
BEGIN_" 'The evil-minded Ravana took away Seetha, Rama's wife. By the orders of Rama, I am 
going to her as an envoy.' "_END

B_5_C_57_40
BEGIN_हनूमता कीर्तिमता यशस्विना |
	तथा अन्गदेन अन्गद बद्ध बाहुना |
	मुदा तदा अध्यासितम् उन्नतम् महन् |
	मही धर अग्रम् ज्वलितम् श्रिया अभवत् || ५-५७-५१_END
BEGIN_The high and large summit of the mauntain, on which were seated then with delight, 
	the illustriaus Hanuma and the famaus Angada, with bracelets worn on his upper ar.ns, stood blazed 
	with splendaur._END

B_5_C_61_4
BEGIN_यत् रक्षति महावीर्यः सदा दधि मुखः कपिः |
मातुलः कपि मुख्यस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः || ५-६१-९_END
BEGIN_A very powerful monkey called Dadhimukha, who was a high-souled eminent monkey and the 
maternal uncle of Sugreeva always protected that garden._END

B_5_C_59_19
BEGIN_मयैव निहता लङ्का दग्धा भस्मीकृता पुनः |
राजमार्गेषु सर्वत्र नाम विश्रावित मया || ५-५९-२२_END
BEGIN_"I alone burnt and destroyed the City of Lanka. In all its royal high-ways, the name 
(of Rama and others) was proclaimed by me as follows:_END

B_5_C_58_24
BEGIN_कर्तुम् अर्हसि रामस्य साह्यम् विषय वासिनि |
अथवा मैथिलीम् दृष्ट्वा रामम् च अक्लिष्ट कारिणम् || ५-५८-२६
आगमिष्यामि ते वक्त्रम् सत्यम् प्रतिशृणोति मे |_END
BEGIN_"'You, abiding in Rama's country, ought to do a help to Rama. Otherwise, after seeing 
Seetha and Rama, who is unwearied in action, I will come to your mouth. I am thus promising you in truth."_END

B_5_C_61_5
BEGIN_ते तत् वनम् उपागम्य बभूवुः परम उत्कटाः |
वानरा वानर इन्द्रस्य मनः कान्ततमम् महत् || ५-६१-१०_END
BEGIN_Reaching that huge grove, which was very dear to the heart of Sugreeva, those monkeys 
became highly excessive in their behaviour._END

B_5_C_59_20
BEGIN_जयत्यतिबलो रामो लक्ष्मणश्च महाबलः |
राजा जयति सुग्रीवो राघवेणाभिपालितः || ५-५९-२३
अहम् कोसलराजस्य दासः पवनसम्भवः |
हनुमानिति सर्वत्र नाम विश्रावितम् मया || ५-५९-२४_END
BEGIN_"'Victorious is Rama, the exceedingly strong and the mighty Lakshmana too! Victorious 
is King Sugreeva, protected by Rama. I am Hanuma, a servant of Rama and the son of wind-god'. In this 
way, the name (of Rama and others) was heralded by me everywhere."_END

B_5_C_58_25
BEGIN_एवम् उक्ता मया सा तु सुरसा काम रूपिणी || ५-५८-२७
अब्रवीन् न अतिवर्तेत कश्चित् एष वरो मम |_END
BEGIN_Hearing my words, that Surasa who can assume any form at her will said: "No one can violate 
me by unfaithfulness. I have this boon with me."_END

B_5_C_61_6
BEGIN_ततः ते वानरा हृष्टा दृष्ट्वा मधु वनम् महत् |
कुमारम् अभ्ययाचन्त मधूनि मधु पिन्गलाः || ५-६१-११_END
BEGIN_Then, seeing that large Madhuvana, the garden abounded in honey, those monkeys, whose 
colour was as yellow as honey, were delighted and solicited Angada the prince for permission to taste 
the honey._END

B_5_C_59_21
BEGIN_अशोक वनिका मध्ये रावणस्य दुरात्मनः |
अधस्तात् शिंशपा वृक्षे साध्वी करुणम् आस्थिता || ५-५९-२५
राक्षसीभिः परिवृता शोक सम्ताप कर्शिता |
मेघ लेखा परिवृता चन्द्र लेखा इव निष्प्रभा || ५-५९-२६
अचिन्तयन्ती वैदेही रावणम् बल दर्पितम् |_END
BEGIN_"In the midst of Ashoka garden of the evil-minded Ravana and underneath a Shimshupa tree, 
the virtuous Seetha was seen staying dejected, encircled as she was with female-demons, agonized with 
grief and anguish, lusterless like a digit of the moon encircled by a line of clouds and disregarding 
that Ravana who is arrogant of his strength."_END

B_5_C_58_26
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः सुरसया दश योजनम् आयतः || ५-५८-२८
ततो अर्ध गुण विस्तारो बभूव अहम् क्षणेन तु |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the words of Surasa, I, as tall as ten Yojanas (eighty miles), within a moment, 
grew half as much in size (fifteen Yojanas or one hundred twenty miles)."_END

B_5_C_61_7
BEGIN_ततः कुमारः तान् वृद्धान् जाम्बवत् प्रमुखान् कपीन् |
अनुमान्य ददौ तेषाम् निसर्गम् मधु भक्षणे || ५-६१-१२_END
BEGIN_Thereupon, Angada the prince, taking approval from those elders like Jambavan and others, 
gave the monkeys a liberty to drink honey there._END

B_5_C_59_22
BEGIN_पति व्रता च सुश्रोणी अवष्टब्धा च जानकी || ५-५९-२७
अनुरक्ता हि वैदेही रामम् सर्व आत्मना शुभा |
अनन्य चित्ता रामे च पौलोमी इव पुरम् दरे || ५-५९-२८_END
BEGIN_"Seetha, a devoted and virtuous wife, having charming hips, has been placed under restraint. 
The auspicious Seetha is devoted to Rama in all ways, giving her undivided thought to Rama like Shachi 
the goddess, giving her concern to Indra the destroyer of strong holds."_END

B_5_C_58_27
BEGIN_मत् प्रमाण अनुरूपम् च व्यादितम् तन् मुखम् तया || ५-५८-२९
तत् दृष्ट्वा व्यादितम् तु आस्यम् ह्रस्वम् हि अकरवम् वपुः |
तस्मिन् मुहूर्ते च पुनः बभूव अन्गुष्ठ सम्मितः || ५-५८-३०_END
BEGIN_"She opened her mouth so wide as to correspond to the size of my body. Seeing her expanded 
mouth, I assumed a dwarfish form. At that moment, I still became reduced to the size of a human thumb."_END

B_5_C_61_8
BEGIN_ततः च अनुमताः सर्वे सम्प्रहृष्टा वन ओकसः |
मुदिताः च ततः ते च प्रनृत्यन्ति ततः ततः || ५-६१-१३_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, all those monkeys, thus permitted to drink honey, were exceedingly pleased. 
Then, those excited monkeys felt glad and began dancing._END

B_5_C_59_23
BEGIN_तत् एक वासः सम्वीता रजो ध्वस्ता तथैव च |
शोक सम्ताप दीन अन्गी सीता भर्तृ हिते रता || ५-५९-२९_END
BEGIN_"Weaving that single piece of cloth, which she had on her person even while being borne 
away by Ravana, and likewise covered with dust, she was seen by me in a miserable condition with her 
grief and anguish, devoted as she was to the welfare of her husband."_END

B_5_C_62_0
BEGIN_तान् उवाच हरि श्रेष्ठो हनूमान् वानर ऋषभः |
अव्यग्र मनसो यूयम् मधु सेवत वानराः || ५-६२-१
अहमावारयिष्यामि युष्माकम् परिपन्थिनः |_END
BEGIN_Hanuma, like a bull among the monkeys and the foremost among them spoke to them as follows: 
"Cherish the honey with a cool mind, O monkeys! I will keep off your opposer who is standing in your 
way."_END

B_5_C_58_28
BEGIN_अभिपत्य आशु तत् वक्त्रम् निर्गतो अहम् ततः क्षणात् |
अब्रवीत् सुरसा देवी स्वेन रूपेण माम् पुनः || ५-५८-३१_END
BEGIN_"After entering her mouth quickly, I then came out instantly. The divine Surasa, in her 
native form, spoke to me again, as follows:_END

B_5_C_61_9
BEGIN_गायन्ति केचित् प्रणमन्ति केचिन् |
नृत्यन्ति केचित् प्रहसन्ति केचित् |
पतन्ति केचित् विचरन्ति केचित् |
प्लवन्ति केचित् प्रलपन्ति केचित् || ५-६१-१४_END
BEGIN_Some were singing. Some were offering salutations. Some were dancing. Some were laughing 
loudly. Some were falling down. Some were moving in different directions. Some were jumping up. Some 
were talking incoherently._END

B_5_C_59_24
BEGIN_सा मया राक्षसी मध्ये तर्ज्यमाना मुहुः मुहुः |
राक्षसीभिः विरूपाभिः दृष्टा हि प्रमदा वने || ५-५९-३०
एक वेणी धरा दीना भर्तृ चिन्ता परायणा |
अधः शय्या विवर्ण अन्गी पद्मिनी इव हिम आगमे |
रावणात् विनिवृत्त अर्था मर्तव्य कृत निश्चया || ५-५९-३१_END
BEGIN_"I saw Seetha in a royal pleasure garden, amidst some female-demons. Seetha was being 
frightened time and again by those ugly female-demons. That Seetha, wearing a single braid of hair and 
looking depressed, was fully engaged in thinking about her lord. Looking like a lotus with a discoloured 
figure in winter, she had determined to die, utterly averting to do anything with Ravana."_END

B_5_C_62_1
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा हनुमतो वाक्यम् हरीणाम् प्रवरो अन्गदः || ५-६२-२
प्रत्युवाच प्रसन्न आत्मा पिबन्तु हरयो मधु |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Hanuma, the gracious minded Angada the principal among the monkeys 
repeated the words: "Let the monkeys drink the honey."_END

B_5_C_58_29
BEGIN_अर्थ सिद्ध्यै हरि श्रेष्ठ गच्छ सौम्य यथा सुखम् |
समानय च वैदेहीम् राघवेण महात्मना || ५-५८-३२
सुखी भव महाबाहो प्रीता अस्मि तव वानर |_END
BEGIN_"'O gently monkey! O the foremost among monkeys! Go happily for the fulfillment of your 
purpose. Bring back Seetha to the magnanimous Rama. O mighty armed monkey! Be happy. I am pleased with 
you.'"_END

B_5_C_61_10
BEGIN_परस्परम् केचित् उपाश्रयन्ते |
परस्परम् केचित् अतिब्रुवन्ते |
परस्परम् केचिदुपब्रुवन्ते |
परस्परम् केचिदुपारमन्ते || ५-६१-१५_END
BEGIN_Some were leaning against one another. Some were falling upon one another. Some were 
disputing with one another. Some were playing with one another._END

B_5_C_59_25
BEGIN_कथंचिन् मृग शाव अक्षी विश्वासम् उपपादिता || ५-५९-३२
ततः सम्भाषिता चैव सर्वम् अर्थम् च दर्शिता |
राम सुग्रीव सख्यम् च श्रुत्वा प्रीतिम् उपागता || ५-५९-३३_END
BEGIN_"With great difficulty, I created confidence in that fawn-eyed Seetha. Thereafter, I 
talked to her and explained everything to her. She was delighted to hear the companionship cropped up 
between Rama and Sugreeva."_END

B_5_C_62_2
BEGIN_अवश्यम् कृत कार्यस्य वाक्यम् हनुमतो मया || ५-६२-३
अकार्यम् अपि कर्तव्यम् किम् अन्ग पुनः ईदृशम् |_END
BEGIN_"The words, though improper of Hanuma who had accomplished his task, are to be obliged 
certainly by me. Wherefore then, moreover, on such an occasion?"_END

B_5_C_58_30
BEGIN_ततो अहम् साधु साध्वी इति सर्व भूतैः प्रशंसितः || ५-५८-३३
ततो अन्तरिक्षम् विपुलम् प्लुतो अहम् गरुडो यथा |_END
BEGIN_"Then, all living beings praised me! Saying Good! Well done! Bravo! Thereupon, I leapt 
into the extensive sky, like Garuda the eagle, the carrier of Lord Vishnu."_END

B_5_C_61_11
BEGIN_द्रुमात् द्रुमम् केचित् अभिप्लवन्ते |
क्षितौ नग अग्रान् निपतन्ति केचित् |
मही तलात् केचित् उदीर्ण वेगा |
महाद्रुम अग्राणि अभिसम्पतन्ते || ५-६१-१६_END
BEGIN_Some were running from one tree to another. Some were falling down to the ground from 
the tree-tops. Some, with a missile-like speed, were flying towards the tops of gigantic trees from 
the ground._END

B_5_C_59_26
BEGIN_नियतः समुदाचारो भक्तिः भर्तरि च उत्तमा |
यन् न हन्ति दशग्रीवम् स महात्मा कृतागसम् || ५-५९-३४_END
BEGIN_"That high-souled Seetha does not kill Ravana who has committed an offence because she 
conducts herself well with restraint and since supreme is her devotion to her lord."_END

B_5_C_62_3
BEGIN_अन्दगस्य मुखात् श्रुत्वा वचनम् वानर ऋषभाः || ५-६२-४
साधु साध्व् इति सम्हृष्टा वानराः प्रत्यपूजयन् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words coming from the mouth of Angada, those monkeys who were like bulls 
among the monkeys were delighted and answered with reverence, saying 'good, good!'_END

B_5_C_58_31
BEGIN_चाया मे निगृहीता च न च पश्यामि किंचन || ५-५८-३४
सो अहम् विगत वेगः तु दिशो दश विलोकयन् |
न किंचित् तत्र पश्यामि येन मे अपहृता गतिः || ५-५८-३५_END
BEGIN_"In the meanwhile, my shadow was held fast. Yet, I did not perceive anything. My speed 
having been blocked, I surveyed all the ten directions. But I could not discover there, any object by 
which my movement was blocked."_END

B_5_C_61_12
BEGIN_गायन्तम् अन्यः प्रहसन्न् उपैति |
हसन्तम् अन्यः प्रहसन्न् उपैति |
रुदन्तम् अन्यः प्ररुदन्न् उपैति |
नुदन्तम् अन्यः प्रणुदन्न् उपैति || ५-६१-१७_END
BEGIN_While one was singing, another approached him laughing. While one was laughing, another 
approached him weeping. While one was weeping, another approached him pushing. While one was pushing, 
another approached him roaring._END

B_5_C_59_27
BEGIN_निमित्त मात्रम् रामः तु वधे तस्य भविष्यति |
सा प्रकृत्यैव तन्वङ्गी तद्वियोगाच्छ कर्शिता || ५-५९-३५
प्रतिपत्पाअठशीलस्य विद्येव तनुताम् गता |_END
BEGIN_"Rama, on his part, will become mere instrument in killing that Ravana. That Seetha, 
who is by her own nature, on delicate-limbed woman, was emaciated because of separation from her lord. 
She had grown thin like the learning of a scholar continuing his studies even on the first day of lunar 
fortnight (which must be observed as a complete holiday by students."_END

B_5_C_62_4
BEGIN_पूजयित्वा अन्गदम् सर्वे वानरा वानर ऋषभम् || ५-६२-५
जग्मुः मधु वनम् यत्र नदी वेग इव द्रुतम् |_END
BEGIN_Reverencing Angada the foremost among the monkeys, all the monkeys rushed towards Madhuvana, 
the grove abounding in honey, like the rush of a river towards a tree._END

B_5_C_58_32
BEGIN_ततो मे बुद्धिः उत्पन्ना किम् नाम गमने मम |
ईदृशो विघ्न उत्पन्नो रूपम् यत्र न दृश्यते || ५-५८-३६_END
BEGIN_"Then, the thought arose in me: "How I wonder has such a hindrance arose in my journey, 
although no concrete configuration is being seen here?"_END

B_5_C_61_13
BEGIN_समाकुलम् तत् कपि सैन्यम् आसीन् |
मधु प्रपान उत्कट सत्त्व चेष्टम् |
न च अत्र कश्चिन् न बभूव मत्तो |
न च अत्र कश्चिन् न बभूव तृप्तो || ५-६१-१८_END
BEGIN_That army of monkeys, moving in excessively honey-drunken state, became highly excited. 
None in that army was not drunk. None in that army was not satiated._END

B_5_C_59_28
BEGIN_एवम् आस्ते महाभागा सीता शोक परायणा || ५-५९-३६
यत् अत्र प्रतिकर्तव्यम् तत् सर्वम् उपपाद्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_"Thus, the illustrious Seetha remains immersed in grief. Let all that be done, which 
requires to be counteracted by way of a relief in this matter."_END

B_5_C_62_5
BEGIN_ते प्रहृष्टा मधु वनम् पालान् आक्रम्य वीर्यतः || ५-६२-६
अतिसर्गाच् च पटवो दृष्ट्वा श्रुत्वा च मैथिलीम् |
पपुः सर्वे मधु तदा रसवत्फलमाददुः || ५-६२-७_END
BEGIN_Because Hanuma had seen Seetha and others had heard of her and because of the grant of 
permission from Angada, all those gifted monkeys entered Madhuvana the grove, overpowered the guards 
with their prowess, drank honey and the partook juicy fruits there._END

B_5_C_58_33
BEGIN_अधो भागेन मे दृष्टिः शोचता पातिता मया |
ततो अद्राक्षम् अहम् भीमाम् राक्षसीम् सलिले शयाम् || ५-५८-३७_END
BEGIN_"While I was thinking thus, my sight has fallen downward. There, I saw a terrible female-demon 
lying in water."_END

B_5_C_61_14
BEGIN_ततो वनम् तत् परिभक्ष्यमाणम् |
द्रुमान् च विध्वंसित पत्र पुष्पान् |
समीक्ष्य कोपात् दधि वक्त्र नामा |
निवारयामास कपिः कपीन् तान् || ५-६१-१९_END
BEGIN_Seeing that grove, being consumed and the trees stripped off their leaves and flowers 
the monkey named Dadhimukha (who was incharge of the grove) then angrily interrupted those monkeys._END

B_5_C_62_6
BEGIN_उत्पत्य च ततः सर्वे वन पालान् समागताः |
ताडयन्ति स्म शतशः सक्तान् मधु वने तदा || ५-६२-८_END
BEGIN_Then, all those monkeys jumped on the guards of the grove, who came there in hundreds 
together and banged them._END

B_5_C_58_34
BEGIN_प्रहस्य च महानादम् उक्तो अहम् भीमया तया |
अवस्थितम् असम्भ्रान्तम् इदम् वाक्यम् अशोभनम् || ५-५८-३८_END
BEGIN_"Heartily laughing with a great noise, that terrific woman, spoke to me the following 
inauspicious words, firmly and without any bewilderment (as follows):_END

B_5_C_61_15
BEGIN_स तैः प्रवृद्धैः परिभर्त्स्यमानो |
वनस्य गोप्ता हरि वीर वृद्धः |
चकार भूयो मतिम् उग्र तेजा |
वनस्य रक्षाम् प्रति वानरेभ्यः || ५-६१-२०_END
BEGIN_Threatened by those monkeys who were behaving excessively, Dadhimukha who was endowed 
with a terrible energy, the care-taker of the grove and an elderly hero of the monkeys further contemplated 
the means to protect that grove from the monkeys._END

B_5_C_58_35
BEGIN_क्व असि गन्ता महाकाय क्षुधिताया मम ईप्सितः |
भक्षः प्रीणय मे देहम् चिरम् आहार वर्जितम् || ५-५८-३९_END
BEGIN_"O gigantic monkey! Where are you going? You are my requisite food, hungry as I am. Gratify 
my person, who has remained without sustenance for long."_END

B_5_C_62_7
BEGIN_मधूनि द्रोण मात्राणि बहुभिः परिगृह्य ते |
पिबन्ति सहिताः सर्वे भक्षयन्ति तथा अपरे || ५-६२-९_END
BEGIN_All those monkeys together took vessels of honey in their arms and drank them. Some others 
banged those who obstructed them._END

B_5_C_63_0
BEGIN_ततो मूर्ध्ना निपतितम् वानरम् वानर ऋषभः |
दृष्ट्वा एव उद्विग्न हृदयो वाक्यम् एतत् उवाच ह || ५-६३-१_END
BEGIN_Just on seeing Dadhimukha, who fell touching his feet with his head, Sugreeva the chief 
of monkeys, with an agitated mind, spoke the following words:_END

B_5_C_61_16
BEGIN_उवाच कांश्चित् परुषाणि धृष्टम् |
असक्तम् अन्यान् च तलैः जघान |
समेत्य कैश्चित् कलहम् चकार |
तथैव साम्ना उपजगाम कांश्चित् || ५-६१-२१_END
BEGIN_He spoke harsh words with some and courageously struck some others with his palms uninterruptedly, 
created a quarrel by coming into collusion with some, and approached some in a conciliatory manner._END

B_5_C_58_36
BEGIN_बाढम् इति एव ताम् वाणीम् प्रत्यगृह्णाम् अहम् ततः |
आस्य प्रमाणात् अधिकम् तस्याः कायम् अपूरयम् || ५-५८-४०_END
BEGIN_"Saying 'Amen', I actually accepted those words. Thereupon, I expanded my body to a size 
larger than the capacity of her mouth."_END

B_5_C_62_8
BEGIN_केचित् पीत्वा अपविध्यन्ति मधूनि मधु पिन्गलाः |
मधु उच्चिष्टेन केचिच् च जघ्नुः अन्योन्यम् उत्कटाः || ५-६२-१०_END
BEGIN_Some monkeys, with their skin-colour as yellow as honey, after drinking vessels of honey, 
also threw some honey away. Some others, with the remnant of honey in their arms, after drinking, whipped 
up one another with their excessive intoxication._END

B_5_C_63_1
BEGIN_उत्तिष्ठ उत्तिष्ठ कस्मात् त्वम् पादयोः पतितो मम |
अभयम् ते भवेत् वीर सत्यम् एव अभिधीयताम् || ५-६३-२_END
BEGIN_"O valiant monkey! Stand up, rise! Why have you fallen on my feet? I grant you immunity 
from fear. Let the entire truth be spoken!"_END

B_5_C_61_17
BEGIN_स तैः मदाच् च अप्रतिवार्य वेगैः |
बलाच् च तेन अप्रतिवार्यमाणैः |
प्रधर्षितः त्यक्त भयैः समेत्य |
प्रकृष्यते च अपि अनवेक्ष्य दोषम् || ५-६१-२२_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha was dragged, after coming into collusion with him by those monkeys, who 
were being forcibly hindered by him, eventhough those monkeys overpowered him with unrestrained emotion 
arising out of their intoxication, those who had abandoned their fear disregarding any bad consequence 
of their act._END

B_5_C_58_37
BEGIN_तस्याः च आस्यम् महत् भीमम् वर्धते मम भक्षणे |
न च माम् सा तु बुबुधे मम वा विकृतम् कृतम् || ५-५८-४१_END
BEGIN_"Her terrific large mouth too began to grow to devour me. She could not understand well 
about me or about the change subsequently gone through by me (in the shape of a minute form)"_END

B_5_C_62_9
BEGIN_अपरे वृक्ष मूलेषु शाखाम् गृह्य व्यवस्थितः |
अत्यर्थम् च मद ग्लानाः पर्णानि आस्तीर्य शेरते || ५-६२-११_END
BEGIN_Some others, seizing a branch of a tree, stood rooted at the foot of a tree. Some, who 
were highly intoxicated, laid down spreading leaves on the ground._END

B_5_C_63_2
BEGIN_स तु विश्वासितः तेन सुग्रीवेण महात्मना |
उत्थाय च महाप्राज्ञो वाक्यम् दधि मुखो अब्रवीत् || ५-६३-३_END
BEGIN_Thus inspired by the high-souled Sugreeva with confidence, that highly intelligent Dadhimukha, 
rising up, spoke the following words:_END

B_5_C_61_18
BEGIN_नखैः तुदन्तो दशनैः दशन्तः |
तलैः च पादैः च समाप्नुवन्तः |
मदात् कपिम् तम् कपयः समग्रा |
महावनम् निर्विषयम् च चक्रुः || ५-६१-२३_END
BEGIN_Bruising with their nails, biting with their teeth on account of their inebriety and 
making short work of that Dadhimukha with their palms and feet, all those moneys made that large grove, 
divested of its flowers, fruits and honey._END

B_5_C_58_38
BEGIN_ततो अहम् विपुलम् रूपम् सम्क्षिप्य निमिष अन्तरात् |
तस्या हृदयम् आदाय प्रपतामि नभः तलम् || ५-५८-४२_END
BEGIN_"Then, having contracted my large body within another moment, I extracted her heart and 
leapt back into the sky."_END

B_5_C_62_10
BEGIN_उन्मत्त भूताः प्लवगा मधु मत्ताः च हृष्टवत् |
क्षिपन्ति अपि तथा अन्योन्यम् स्खलन्ति अपि तथा अपरे || ५-६२-१२_END
BEGIN_Those monkeys, who were intoxicated by drinking the honey, became inebriated and started 
pushing one another cheerfully and some others began to stumble._END

B_5_C_63_3
BEGIN_न एव ऋक्ष रजसा राजन् न त्वया न अपि वालिना |
वनम् निसृष्ट पूर्वम् हि भक्षितम् तत् तु वानरैः || ५-६३-४_END
BEGIN_"O king! Madhuvana was indeed not set free previously at any time by Riksharajas, your 
father, or by you, or by even Vali. That Madhuvana has been consumed away by the monkeys."_END

B_5_C_58_39
BEGIN_सा विसृष्ट भुजा भीमा पपात लवण अम्भसि |
मया पर्वत सम्काशा निकृत्त हृदया सती || ५-५८-४३_END
BEGIN_"When her heart has been cut off by me, that terrific Simhika looking like a mountain, 
fell into the ocean with her arms emanating from it."_END

B_5_C_63_4
BEGIN_एभिः प्रधर्षिताः च एव वारिता वन रक्षिभिः |
मधूनि अचिन्तयित्वा इमान् भक्षयन्ति पिबन्ति च || ५-६३-५_END
BEGIN_"When these guards of the grove obstructed the monkeys, they disregarded the guards and 
continue to eat the fruits and drink the honey too."_END

B_5_C_62_11
BEGIN_केचित् क्ष्वेडान् प्रकुर्वन्ति केचित् कूजन्ति हृष्टवत् |
हरयो मधुना मत्ताः केचित् सुप्ता मही तले || ५-६२-१३_END
BEGIN_Some were roaring like lions. Some, with joy, whistled like birds. Some monkeys, inebriated 
as they were by drinking honey, simply slept on the floor._END

B_5_C_58_40
BEGIN_शृणोमि ख गतानाम् च सिद्धानाम् चारणैः सह |
राक्षसी सिम्हिका भीमा क्षिप्रम् हनुमता हृता || ५-५८-४४_END
BEGIN_"I heard great sages along with wandering celestial singers, moving in the sky, saying 
that Simhika the dreadful demon was instantly killed by Hanuma."_END

B_5_C_63_5
BEGIN_शिष्टम् अत्र अपविध्यन्ति भक्षयन्ति तथा अपरे |
निवार्यमाणाः ते सर्वे भ्रुवौ वै दर्शयन्ति हि || ५-६३-६_END
BEGIN_"Some are throwing away a remnant of honey, after drinking it there and some others are 
consuming that remnant. When prevented by us, all of them are indeed exhibiting their eye-brows to us 
(in anger)."_END

B_5_C_62_12
BEGIN_कृत्वा केचिर्धसन्त्यन्ये केचित्कुर्वन्ति चेतरत् |
कृत्वा केचिद्वदन्त्यन्ये केचिद्बुध्यन्ति चेतरत् || ५-६२-१४_END
BEGIN_Doing something or other, some were laughing. Some others were doing something else. 
Some were telling what they were doing, while some others were understanding some things else._END

B_5_C_58_41
BEGIN_ताम् हत्वा पुनः एव अहम् कृत्यम् आत्ययिकम् स्मरन् |
गत्वा च महत् अध्वानम् पश्यामि नग मण्डितम् || ५-५८-४५
दक्षिणम् तीरम् उदधेः लन्का यत्र च सा पुरी |_END
BEGIN_"After killing her and again recollecting the task to be performed quickly, I travelled 
for a long distance and saw the southern shore of the ocean, where that City of Lanka, adorned with 
its trees, was situated."_END

B_5_C_63_6
BEGIN_इमे हि सम्रब्धतराः तथा तैः सम्प्रधर्षिताः |
वारयन्तो वनात् तस्मात् क्रुद्धैः वानर पुम्गवैः || ५-६३-७_END
BEGIN_"When these guards of the grove became angry and tried to keep them off from the grove, 
those enraged monkeys threatened them."_END

B_5_C_62_13
BEGIN_ये अपि अत्र मधु पालाः स्युः प्रेष्या दधि मुखस्य तु |
ते अपि तैः वानरैः भीमैः प्रतिषिद्धा दिशो गताः || ५-६२-१५_END
BEGIN_The honey-keepers, who were there as messengers of Dadhimukha in that Madhuvana, were 
warded off by the terrific monkeys and they fled to different directions._END

B_5_C_64_0
BEGIN_सुग्रीवेण एवम् उक्तः तु हृष्टो दधि मुखः कपिः |
राघवम् लक्ष्मणम् चैव सुग्रीवम् च अभ्यवादयत् || ५-६४-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Sugreeva, Dadhimukha the monkey was pleased and offered his salutation 
with reverence to Rama, Lakshmana_END

B_5_C_58_42
BEGIN_अस्तम् दिन करे याते रक्षसाम् निलयम् पुरीम् || ५-५८-४६
प्रविष्टो अहम् अविज्ञातो रक्षोभिः भीम विक्रमैः |_END
BEGIN_"While the sun was setting, I, without being noticed by the demons of dreadful prowess, 
entered the city of Lanka, the abode of demons."_END

B_5_C_63_7
BEGIN_ततः तैः बहुभिः वीरैः वानरैः वानर ऋषभाः |
सम्रक्त नयनैः क्रोधाद्त् हरयः सम्प्रचालिताः || ५-६३-८_END
BEGIN_"O chief of monkeys! Then, those valiant monkeys in large numbers, having their red eyes 
in anger, drove away these monkeys."_END

B_5_C_62_14
BEGIN_जानुभिः च प्रकृष्टाः च देव मार्गम् च दर्शिताः |
अब्रुवन् परम उद्विग्ना गत्वा दधि मुखम् वचः || ५-६२-१६_END
BEGIN_Dragged by their knees and tossed up in the air by the monkeys, those honey-keepers were 
very much depressed, went to Dadhimukha and complained as follows:_END

B_5_C_64_1
BEGIN_स प्रणम्य च सुग्रीवम् राघवौ च महाबलौ |
वानरैः सहितैः शूरैः दिवम् एव उत्पपात ह || ५-६४-२_END
BEGIN_After offering salutation to Sugreeva and to the mighty Rama and Lakshmana, that Dadhimukha 
accompanied by his valiant monkeys, sprang into the air._END

B_5_C_63_8
BEGIN_पाणिभिः निहताः केचित् केचिज् जानुभिः आहताः |
प्रकृष्टाः च यथा कामम् देव मार्गम् च दर्शिताः || ५-६३-९_END
BEGIN_"Those monkeys struck some of the guards with their hands. They beat some of them with 
their knees. They dragged some of them and tossed them into air."_END

B_5_C_58_43
BEGIN_तत्र प्रविशतश्चापि कल्पान्तघनसन्निभा || ५-५८-४७
अट्टहासम् विमुञ्चन्ती नारी काप्युत्थिता पुरः |_END
BEGIN_"While I was entering the City, a woman, resembling a cloud at the time of dissolution 
of the world, stood up in front of me, emitting a loud laughter."_END

B_5_C_62_15
BEGIN_हनूमता दत्त वरैः हतम् मधु वनम् बलात् |
वयम् च जानुभिः कृष्टा देव मार्गम् च दर्शिताः || ५-६२-१७_END
BEGIN_"The monkeys, as permitted by Hanuma, violently destroyed Madhuvana. We were dragged 
by our knees and further tossed up in the air."_END

B_5_C_64_2
BEGIN_स प्रविष्टो मधु वनम् ददर्श हरि यूथपान् |
विमदान् उद्धतान् सर्वान् मेहमानान् मधु उदकम् || ५-६४-३_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha, after entering Madhuvana, saw all the chiefs of monkeys, who were free 
from their intoxication, having passed off the honey and who were inwardly excited._END

B_5_C_63_9
BEGIN_एवम् एते हताः शूराः त्वयि तिष्ठति भर्तरि |
कृत्स्नम् मधु वनम् चैव प्रकामम् तैः प्रभक्ष्यते || ५-६३-१०_END
BEGIN_"While you are in the position of a king, those monkeys have beaten these valiant guards 
and are eating away the entire Maduvana too."_END

B_5_C_58_44
BEGIN_जिघांसन्तीम् ततस्ताम् तु ज्वलदग्निशिरोरुहाम् || ५-५८-४८
सव्यमुष्टिप्रहारेण पराजित्य सुभैरवाम् |
प्रदोषकाले प्रविशम् भीतयाहम् तयोदितः || ५-५८-४९_END
BEGIN_"Then defeating that woman, having her hair looking terrific like a blazing fire and 
who was trying to kill me, by striking her with a blow of the fist of my left hand and entered the land 
of Lanka at the dusk of early night. she, being frightened, spoke to me as follows:_END

B_5_C_62_16
BEGIN_ततो दधि मुखः क्रुद्धो वनपः तत्र वानरः |
हतम् मधु वनम् श्रुत्वा सान्त्वयामास तान् हरीन् || ५-६२-१८_END
BEGIN_Hearing that Madhuvana was damaged, Dadhimukha, the grove-protector there was enraged 
and thereafter consoled those monkeys (as follows):_END

B_5_C_64_3
BEGIN_स तान् उपागमत् वीरो बद्ध्वा कर पुट अञ्जलिम् |
उवाच वचनम् श्लक्ष्णम् इदम् हृष्टवत् अन्गदम् || ५-६४-४_END
BEGIN_With his hands joined together for salutation, that valiant Dadhimukha approached them 
and cheerfully spoke the following gentle words to Angada._END

B_5_C_63_10
BEGIN_एवम् विज्ञाप्यमानम् तु सुग्रीवम् वानर ऋषभम् |
अपृच्छत् तम् महाप्राज्ञो लक्ष्मणः पर वीरहा || ५-६३-११_END
BEGIN_Lakshmana, the killer of hostile heroes and a very wise man, asked that Sugreeva, the 
excellent of monkeys (as follows) while Dadhimukha was thus reporting to him:_END

B_5_C_58_45
BEGIN_अहम् लङ्कापुरी वीर निर्जिता विक्रमेण ते |
यस्मात्तस्माद्विजेतासि सर्वरक्षांस्यशेषतः || ५-५८-५०_END
BEGIN_"O hero! I am (the personified) City of Lanka. Therefore, by the same prowess you conquered 
me, you can defeat all the demons here completely."_END

B_5_C_62_17
BEGIN_इह आगच्छत गच्छामो वानरान् अतिदर्पितान् |
बलेन आवारयिष्यामो मधु भक्षयतो वयम् || ५-६२-१९_END
BEGIN_"Come here let us go there and prevent by our force, the monkeys who are arrogant of 
their strength and are consuming the honey."_END

B_5_C_64_4
BEGIN_सौम्य रोषो न कर्तव्यो यत् एभिः अभिवारितः |
अज्ञानात् रक्षिभिः क्रोधात् भवन्तः प्रतिषेधिताः || ५-६४-५_END
BEGIN_"O gentle sir! Due to their ignorance, these guards in anger obstructed you to enter 
the grove. No resentment should be harboured by you about this obstruction."_END

B_5_C_63_11
BEGIN_किम् अयम् वानरो राजन् वनपः प्रत्युपस्थितः |
कम् च अर्थम् अभिनिर्दिश्य दुह्खितो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ५-६३-१२_END
BEGIN_"O king! Why has this monkey the garden-protector, come here?' Pointing out what matter 
has this monkey in grief, spoken these words to you?"_END

B_5_C_58_46
BEGIN_तत्र अहम् सर्व रात्रम् तु विचिन्वन् जनक आत्मजाम् |
रावण अन्तः पुर गतो न च अपश्यम् सुमध्यमाम् || ५-५८-५१_END
BEGIN_"Searching there for Seetha that whole night in Ravana's gynaecium, I could not find 
that Seetha, the slender-waisted lady."_END

B_5_C_62_18
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा दधि मुखस्य इदम् वचनम् वानर ऋषभाः |
पुनः वीरा मधु वनम् तेन एव सहिता ययुः || ५-६२-२०_END
BEGIN_Hearing these words of Dadhimukha, the foremost of those monkeys who displayed their 
heroism, quickly went again to madhuvana along with him._END

B_5_C_64_5
BEGIN_युव राजः त्वम् ईशः च वनस्य अस्य महाबल |
मौर्ख्यात् पूर्वम् कृतो दोषः तत् भवान् क्षन्तुम् अर्हति || ५-६४-६_END
BEGIN_"O exceedingly strong Angada! You are the prince and also the master of this grove. We 
have done a mistake_END

B_5_C_63_12
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवो लक्ष्मणेन महात्मना |
लक्ष्मणम् प्रत्युवाच इदम् वाक्यम् वाक्य विशारदः || ५-६३-१३_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of the high-souled Lakshmana, the eloquent Sugreeva replied to him 
as follows:_END

B_5_C_58_47
BEGIN_ततः सीताम् अपश्यन् तु रावणस्य निवेशने |
शोक सागरम् आसाद्य न पारम् उपलक्षये || ५-५८-५२_END
BEGIN_"Unable to find Seetha in Ravana's dwelling and facing a sea of sorrow, I could not then 
perceive its other shore."_END

B_5_C_62_19
BEGIN_मध्ये च एषाम् दधि मुखः प्रगृह्य सुमहातरुम् |
समभ्यधावत् वेगेना ते च सर्वे प्लवम्गमाः || ५-६२-२१_END
BEGIN_Grasping a tree, Dadhimukha speedily took up his position in the middle of those monkeys 
in Madhuvana. All his follower-monkeys also ran with him._END

B_5_C_64_6
BEGIN_आख्यातम् हि मया गत्वा पितृव्यस्य तव अनघ |
इह उपयानम् सर्वेषाम् एतेषाम् वन चारिणाम् || ५-६४-७_END
BEGIN_"O faultless Angada! After going there, I indeed informed your uncle about the arrival 
of all these monkeys here."_END

B_5_C_63_13
BEGIN_आर्य लक्ष्मण सम्प्राह वीरो दधि मुखः कपिः |
अन्गद प्रमुखैः वीरैः भक्षितम् मधु वानरैः || ५-६३-१४
विचित्य दक्षिणामाशामागतैर्हरिपुङ्गवैः |_END
BEGIN_"O esteemed Lakshmana! Dadhimukha, the valiant monkey is informing that the foremost 
of monkeys, who returned from the southern direction, after searching for Seetha as also Angada and 
other heroes consumed honey."_END

B_5_C_58_48
BEGIN_शोचता च मया दृष्टम् प्राकारेण समावृतम् |
कान्चनेन विकृष्टेन गृह उपवनम् उत्तमम् || ५-५८-५३_END
BEGIN_"While bemoaning, I saw an excellent grove near that gynaecium, concealed by a prolonged 
fence painted with golden colour."_END

B_5_C_62_20
BEGIN_ते शिलाः पादपान् च अपि पाषाणान् च अपि वानराः |
गृहीत्वा अभ्यागमन् क्रुद्धा यत्र ते कपि कुन्जराः || ५-६२-२२_END
BEGIN_Those enraged monkeys, taking rocks, trees and even mountains, went to the place wehre 
those foremost of monkeys were there._END

B_5_C_65_0
BEGIN_ततः प्रस्रवणम् शैलम् ते गत्वा चित्र काननम् |
प्रणम्य शिरसा रामम् लक्ष्मणम् च महाबलम् || ५-६५-१
युव राजम् पुरः कृत्य सुग्रीवम् अभिवाद्य च |
प्रवृत्तम् अथ सीतायाः प्रवक्तुम् उपचक्रमुः || ५-६५-२_END
BEGIN_Keeping Angada the prince in their forefront those monkeys, on reaching Mount Prasravana 
having forests of variegated appearance, offered their salutation by bowing their heads in reverence 
to Rama and the mighty Lakshmana, greeting Sugreeva respectfully. Then, they started narrating the news 
of Seetha._END

B_5_C_64_7
BEGIN_स त्वत् आगमनम् श्रुत्वा सह एभिः हरि यूथपैः |
प्रहृष्टो न तु रुष्टो असौ वनम् श्रुत्वा प्रधर्षितम् || ५-६४-८_END
BEGIN_"Hearing your arrival along with these leaders of monkeys, your uncle was exceedingly 
pleased. Even after hearing of Madhuvana having been attacked, he did not develop any anger."_END

B_5_C_63_14
BEGIN_न एषाम् अकृत कृत्यानाम् ईदृशः स्यात् उपक्रमः || ५-६३-१५
आगतैश्च प्रमथितम् यथा मधुवनम् हि तैः |
धर्षितं च वनम् कृत्स्नमुपयुक्तम् च वानरैः || ५-६३-१६_END
BEGIN_"By seeing the manner in which these returned monkeys overpowered, destroyed and behaved 
towards Madhuvana, we can deduce that the monkeys would not have indulged in such an exploit, had they 
not accomplished my purpose."_END

B_5_C_58_49
BEGIN_स प्राकारम् अवप्लुत्य पश्यामि बहु पादपम् |
अशोक वनिका मध्ये शिंशपा पादपो महान् || ५-५८-५४
तम् आरुह्य च पश्यामि कान्चनम् कदली वनम् |_END
BEGIN_Crossing the fence, I saw that grove having copious trees. Amidst that Ashoka garden, 
I saw a large Shimshupa* garden. After ascending it, I beheld an yellow-pigmented thicket of banana 
plants."_END

B_5_C_62_21
BEGIN_ते स्वामि वचनम् वीरा हृदयेष्व् अवसज्य तत् |
त्वरया हि अभ्यधावन्त साल ताल शिला आयुधाः || ५-६२-२३_END
BEGIN_Those heroic monkeys, keeping the words of their master in mind, briskly ran with Sala 
trees, palm trees and rocks as their weapons._END

B_5_C_65_1
BEGIN_रावण अन्तः पुरे रोधम् राक्षसीभिः च तर्जनम् |
रामे समनुरागम् च यः च अपि समयः कृतः || ५-६५-३
एतत् आख्यान्ति ते सर्वे हरयो राम सम्निधौ |_END
BEGIN_Those monkeys started to narrate, in the presence of Rama, about, the female-demons, 
and frightening Seetha in Ravana's gynaecium, her complete affection towards Rama and the time-limit 
of two months given by Ravana._END

B_5_C_64_8
BEGIN_प्रहृष्टो माम् पितृव्यः ते सुग्रीवो वानर ईश्वरः |
शीघ्रम् प्रेषय सर्वान् तान् इति ह उवाच पार्थिवः || ५-६४-९_END
BEGIN_"Sugreeva, your uncle, the lord of monkeys and the king was pleased and told me, 'send 
all the monkeys here'."_END

B_5_C_63_15
BEGIN_वनम् यथा अभिपन्नम् तैः साधितम् कर्म वानरैः |
दृष्टा देवी न संदेहो न च अन्येन हनूमता || ५-६३-१७_END
BEGIN_"When those monkeys have overpowered Madhuvana, then it means that our task has been 
accomplished by the monkeys. Seetha was found. There is no doubt. None other than Hanuma must have seen 
Seetha."_END

B_5_C_58_50
BEGIN_अदूरात् शिंशपा वृक्षात् पश्यामि वन वर्णिनीम् || ५-५८-५५
श्यामाम् कमल पत्र अक्षीम् उपवास कृश आननाम् |
तदेकवासःसंवीताम् रजोध्वस्तशिरोरुहाम् || ५-५८-५६
शोकसन्तापदीनाङ्गीम् सीताम् भर्तृहिते स्थिताम् |
राक्षसीभिः विरूपाभिः क्रूराभिः अभिसम्वृताम् || ५-५८-५७
मांस शोणित भक्ष्याभिः व्याघ्रीभिः हरिणीम् यथा |_END
BEGIN_"Not far from that Shimshupa tree. I saw Seetha, of youthful complexion, with eyes looking 
like lotus-petals, with her face emaciated by fasting, clad in a single piece of cloth, her hair soiled 
with dust, her limbs afflicted with grief and agony, devoted as she was to the good of her lord and 
surrounded on all sides by ugly and cruel female-demons living on flesh and blood, as a doe encircled 
by tigresses."_END

B_5_C_62_22
BEGIN_वृक्षस्थान् च तलस्थान् च वानरान् बल दर्पितान् |
अभ्यक्रामन्त ते वीराः पालाः तत्र सहस्रशः || ५-६२-२४_END
BEGIN_Then, the valiant guards of the grove running in thousands invaded the monkeys who were 
on trees, at the foot of the trees and who were arrogant of their strength._END

B_5_C_65_2
BEGIN_वैदेहीम् अक्षताम् श्रुत्वा रामः तु उत्तरम् अब्रवीत् || ५-६५-४
क्व सीता वर्तते देवी कथम् च मयि वर्तते |
एतन् मे सर्वम् आख्यात वैदेहीम् प्रति वानराः || ५-६५-५_END
BEGIN_Hearing of Seetha being alive, Rama on his part replied, "Where is Seetha, the princess? 
How is she disposed towards me? O monkeys! Tell me all that about Seetha."_END

B_5_C_64_9
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा दधि मुखस्य एतत् वचनम् श्लक्ष्णम् अन्गदः |
अब्रवीत् तान् हरि श्रेष्ठो वाक्यम् वाक्य विशारदः || ५-६४-१०_END
BEGIN_Hearing these smooth words of Dadhimukha, the eloquent Angada, the foremost among the 
monkeys, spoke to those monkeys as follows:_END

B_5_C_63_16
BEGIN_न हि अन्यः साधने हेतुः कर्मणो अस्य हनूमतः |
कार्य सिद्धिः हनुमति मतिः च हरि पुम्गव || ५-६३-१८
व्यवसायः च वीर्यम् च श्रुतम् च अपि प्रतिष्ठितम् |_END
BEGIN_"There is none other than, Hanuma who is the executor in accomplishing this work. In 
that Hanuma, the foremost among the monkeys, capacity to accomplish any object; intelligence; strenuous, 
vigour effort; and learning are well established in his life."_END

B_5_C_58_51
BEGIN_सा मया राक्षसीमध्ये तर्ज्यमाना मुहुर्महुः || ५-५८-५८
एकवेणीधरा दीना भर्तृचिन्तापरायणा |
भूमिशय्या विवर्णाङ्गी पद्मिनीव हिमागमे || ५-५८-५९
रावणाद्विनिवृत्तार्था मर्तव्यकृतनिश्चया |
कथंचिन्मृगशाबाक्षी तूर्णमासादिता मया || ५-५८-६०_END
BEGIN_"Seetha, who had eyes like those of a deer, was somehow quickly found by me looking depressed 
in the amidst of female-demons, frightened (as she was by them) again and again, putting on a single 
braid of hair (as a mark of desolation), wholly devoted to the thought of her lord, having floor as 
her bedstead, pale-limbed like a lotus-stalk in a cool season, turning away the request of Ravana, and 
determined to die."_END

B_5_C_62_23
BEGIN_अथ दृष्ट्वा दधि मुखम् क्रुद्धम् वानर पुम्गवाः |
अभ्यधावन्त वेगेन हनूमत् प्रमुखाः तदा || ५-६२-२५_END
BEGIN_Seeing Dadhimukha coming with anger, Hanuma along with eminent monkeys ran towards him 
with speed._END

B_5_C_65_3
BEGIN_रामस्य गदितम् श्रुत्व हरयो राम सम्निधौ |
चोदयन्ति हनूमन्तम् सीता वृत्त अन्त कोविदम् || ५-६५-६_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Rama, the monkeys urged Hanuma to tell, in the presence of Rama, 
all the incidents because he knew them better, about Seetha._END

B_5_C_64_10
BEGIN_शन्के श्रुतो अयम् वृत्त अन्तो रामेण हरि यूथपाः |
तत् क्षमम् न इह नः स्थातुम् कृते कार्ये परम् तपाः || ५-६४-११_END
BEGIN_"O the foremost of monkeys, the tormentators of enemies! I assume that Rama might have 
heard the news (of our arrival). Hence, it is not proper for us to remain here any longer, now that 
our work has been accomplished."_END

B_5_C_63_17
BEGIN_जाम्बवान् यत्र नेता स्यात् अन्गदस्य बल ईश्वरः |
हनूमान् च अपि अधिष्ठाता न तस्य गतिः अन्यथा || ५-६३-१९_END
BEGIN_"Where Jambavan as well as Angada are leaders and Hanuma is an administrator, the progress 
of that work cannot be as otherwise."_END

B_5_C_58_52
BEGIN_ताम् दृष्ट्वा तादृशीम् नारीम् राम पत्नीम् अनिन्दिताम् |
तत्र एव शिंशपा वृक्षे पश्यन्न् अहम् अवस्थितः || ५-५८-६१_END
BEGIN_"Seeing that illustrious woman, the consort of Rama in such a state, I stayed perched 
on the same Simsupa tree, looking at her."_END

B_5_C_62_24
BEGIN_तम् सवृक्षम् महाबाहुम् आपतन्तम् महाबलम् |
आर्यकम् प्राहरत् तत्र बाहुभ्याम् कुपितो अन्गदः || ५-६२-२६_END
BEGIN_The enraged Angada struck there with his arms, that long-armed Dadhimukha the maternal 
uncle his father, who was endowed with extraordinary might and who was rushing with speed with a tree 
in his hand._END

B_5_C_65_4
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा तु वचनम् तेषाम् हनूमान् मारुत आत्मजः |
प्रणम्य शिरसा देव्यै सीतायै ताम् दिशम् प्रति || ५-६५-७
उवाच वाक्यम् वाक्यज्ञः सीताया दर्शनम् यथा |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of those monkeys, the eloquent Hanuma, the son of wind-god saluting 
towards the direction of the Seetha the princess by bowing his head, spoke the following words, explaining 
how he saw Seetha._END

B_5_C_64_11
BEGIN_पीत्वा मधु यथा कामम् विश्रान्ता वन चारिणः |
किम् शेषम् गमनम् तत्र सुग्रीवो यत्र मे गुरुः || ५-६४-१२_END
BEGIN_"The monkeys are taking, rest, after drinking the honey to their heart's content. What 
is there remaining, except to go to the place where Sugreeva my uncle is there?"_END

B_5_C_63_18
BEGIN_अन्गद प्रमुखैः वीरैः हतम् मधु वनम् किल || ५-६३-२०
वारिताः सहिताः पालाः तथा जानुभिः आहताः |_END
BEGIN_"It is so reported that Madhuvana has been destroyed by the heroes with Angada as the 
chief and the garden-guards who were together preventing the damage, were beaten up with knees."_END

B_5_C_58_53
BEGIN_ततो हलहला शब्दम् कान्ची नूपुर मिश्रितम् |
शृणोमि अधिक गम्भीरम् रावणस्य निवेशने || ५-५८-६२_END
BEGIN_"Meanwhile, I heard an exceedingly roaring and hallooing sound, mixed with sounds of 
girdles and anklets in the abode of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_62_25
BEGIN_मद अन्धः अ न वेद एनम् आर्यको अयम् मम इति सः |
अथ एनम् निष्पिपेष आशु वेगवत् वसुधा तले || ५-६२-२७_END
BEGIN_Blinded with arrogance, that Angada did not show any mercy to him on the score of his 
being the maternal uncle of his father and caused him at once to fall down and began to crush him against 
the ground._END

B_5_C_65_5
BEGIN_समुद्रम् लन्घयित्वा अहम् शत योजनम् आयतम् || ५-६५-८
अगच्छम् जानकीम् सीताम् मार्गमाणो दिदृक्षया |_END
BEGIN_"Having gone across the ocean, a hundred Yojanas wide, I reached the southern shore looking 
in search of Seetha, Janaka's daughter, with a wish to see her."_END

B_5_C_64_12
BEGIN_सर्वे यथा माम् वक्ष्यन्ति समेत्य हरि यूथपाः |
तथा अस्मि कर्ता कर्तव्ये भवद्भिः परवान् अहम् || ५-६४-१३_END
BEGIN_"I shall do whatever all the leaders of monkeys together tell me. I am obedient to you, 
in the matter of what ought to be done."_END

B_5_C_63_19
BEGIN_एतत् अर्थम् अयम् प्राप्तो वक्तुम् मधुर वाग् इह || ५-६३-२१
नाम्ना दधि मुखो नाम हरिः प्रख्यात विक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_"To tell this matter in sweet words, the monkey renowned by Dadhimukha by name, with 
his celebrated prowess, has come here."_END

B_5_C_58_54
BEGIN_ततो अहम् परम उद्विग्नः स्वरूपम् प्रत्यसम्हरम् |
अहम् च शिंशपा वृक्षे पक्षी इव गहने स्थितः || ५-५८-६३_END
BEGIN_"Then, I was very much frightened and contracted my physique. I, on my part, remained 
hidden like a bird in that Simsupa tree dense with foliage.'"_END

B_5_C_62_26
BEGIN_स भग्न बाहुः विमुखो विह्वलः शोणित उक्षितः |
मुमोह सहसा वीरो मुहूर्तम् कपि कुन्जरः || ५-६२-२८_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha, the valiant elephant among the monkeys, who was afflicted with his broken 
arms, thighs and shoulders, drenched as he was in blood, lost his consciousness for a moment._END

B_5_C_65_6
BEGIN_तत्र लन्का इति नगरी रावणस्य दुरात्मनः || ५-६५-९
दक्षिणस्य समुद्रस्य तीरे वसति दक्षिणे |_END
BEGIN_"There at the southern shore of the southern ocean, there is city called Lanka of the 
evil-minded Ravana."_END

B_5_C_63_20
BEGIN_दृष्टा सीता महाबाहो सौमित्रे पश्य तत्त्वतः || ५-६३-२२
अभिगम्य यथा सर्वे पिबन्ति मधु वानराः |_END
BEGIN_"O the long-armed Lakshmana! Perceive the truth that Seetha has been seen and see that 
all monkeys, getting together, are drinking honey."_END

B_5_C_64_13
BEGIN_न आज्ञापयितुम् ईशो अहम् युव राजो अस्मि यदि अपि |
अयुक्तम् कृत कर्माणो यूयम् धर्षयितुम् मया || ५-६४-१४_END
BEGIN_"I am not the master to command you, eventhough I am the crown prince. It is not befitting 
for me to play the lord over you, who have accomplished the task."_END

B_5_C_58_55
BEGIN_ततो रावण दाराः च रावणः च महाबलः |
तम् देशम् समनुप्राप्ता यत्र सीता अभवत् स्थिता || ५-५८-६४_END
BEGIN_"Then, the mighty Ravana and his wives reached that place where Seetha was staying."_END

B_5_C_62_27
BEGIN_स समाश्वस्य सहसा सम्क्रुद्धो राजमातुलः |
वानरान्वारयामास दण्डेन मधुमोहितान् || ५-६२-२९_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha, Sugreeva's maternal uncle, quickly recovering his breath, was enraged 
and resisted those monkeys, who were highly intoxicated because of drinking of honey, by a proper reprimand._END

B_5_C_65_7
BEGIN_तत्र दृष्टा मया सीता रावण अन्तः पुरे सती || ५-६५-१०
सम्न्यस्य त्वयि जीवन्ती रामा राम मनो रथम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! There, living in Ravana's gynaecium in the city, I saw the lady Seetha, your 
virtuous wife, centering her heart's desire in you."_END

B_5_C_63_21
BEGIN_न च अपि अदृष्ट्वा वैदेहीम् विश्रुताः पुरुष ऋषभ || ५-६३-२३
वनम् दात्त वरम् दिव्यम् धर्षयेयुः वन ओकसः |_END
BEGIN_"O Lakshmana, the foremost among men! If the renowned monkeys have not seen Seetha, they 
would not have abused the charming grove; which was granted as a boon."_END

B_5_C_64_14
BEGIN_ब्रुवतः च अन्गदः च एवम् श्रुत्वा वचनम् अव्ययम् |
प्रहृष्ट मनसो वाक्यम् इदम् ऊचुः वन ओकसः || ५-६४-१५_END
BEGIN_Hearing the indeclinable words spoken thus by Angada, the monkeys with their pleased 
minds, spoke to him (as follows:_END

B_5_C_58_56
BEGIN_तम् दृष्ट्वा अथ वराअरोहा सीता रक्षो गण ईश्वरम् |
सम्कुच्य ऊरू स्तनौ पीनौ बाहुभ्याम् परिरभ्य च || ५-५८-६५_END
BEGIN_"Thereupon, seeing that Ravana the chief of a troop of demons, Seetha with her lovely 
waist, sat compressing her thighs enclosing her swollen breasts with her arms."_END

B_5_C_62_28
BEGIN_स कथंचित् विमुक्तः तैः वानरैः वानर ऋषभः |
उवाच एक अन्तम् आगम्य भृत्यान् तान् समुपागतान् || ५-६२-३०_END
BEGIN_Somehow released by those monkeys that Dadhimukha the foremost among the monkeys, went 
to a solitary place and spoke to his messengers who came there (as follows):_END

B_5_C_65_8
BEGIN_दृष्टा मे राक्षसी मध्ये तर्ज्यमाना मुहुः मुहुः || ५-६५-११
राक्षसीभिः विरूपाभी रक्षिता प्रमदा वने |_END
BEGIN_"In that pleasure garden, I saw Seetha sitting in the midst of female demons, guarded 
by those ugly-faced female-demons as also time and again being threatened by them."_END

B_5_C_64_15
BEGIN_एवम् वक्ष्यति को राजन् प्रभुः सन् वानर ऋषभ |
ऐश्वर्य मद मत्तो हि सर्वो अहम् इति मन्यते || ५-६४-१६_END
BEGIN_"O prince, the foremost of monkeys! Who would speak like this, while he is the lord? 
Every one indeed thinks one's supremacy with an excited arrogance and says 'I, I'."_END

B_5_C_63_22
BEGIN_ततः प्रहृष्टो धर्म आत्मा लक्ष्मणः सह राघवः || ५-६३-२४
श्रुत्वा कर्ण सुखाम् वाणीम् सुग्रीव वदनाच् च्युताम् |
प्राहृष्यत भृशम् रामो लक्ष्मणः च महायशाः || ५-६३-२५_END
BEGIN_Then, the righteous Lakshmana, together with Rama, felt delighted. Hearing the words 
coming from the mouth of Sugreeva, which were pleasant for the ears, Rama was rejoiced. The mighty Lakshmana 
too was very much rejoiced._END

B_5_C_58_57
BEGIN_वित्रस्ताम् परमोद्विग्नाम् वीक्षमाणामितस्ततः |
त्राणम् किंचिदपश्यन्तीम् वेपमानाम् तपस्विनीम् || ५-५८-६६
ताम् उवाच दशग्रीवः सीताम् परम दुह्खिताम् |
अवाक् शिराः प्रपतितो बहु मन्यस्व माम् इति || ५-५८-६७_END
BEGIN_"Ravana, bowing his head and coming down, spoke (as follows) to that Seetha who was frightened, 
very much grieving for her lord, glancing hither and thither, not finding any protection for her, trembling, 
distressed and extremely sorrowful saying, 'Treat me with respect.'"_END

B_5_C_65_9
BEGIN_दुह्खम् आपद्यते देवी तव अदुह्ख उचिता सती || ५-६५-१२
रावण अन्तः पुरे रुद्ध्वा राक्षसीभिः सुरक्षिता |
एक वेणी धरा दीना त्वयि चिन्ता परायणा || ५-६५-१३
अधः शय्या विवर्ण अन्गी पद्मिनी इव हिम आगमे |
रावणात् विनिवृत्त अर्था मर्तव्य कृत निश्चया || ५-६५-१४
देवी कथंचित् काकुत्स्थ त्वन् मना मार्गिता मया |_END
BEGIN_"O hero! Seetha, who deserves to live happily with you, is obtaining grief. O Rama! I 
somehow searched that princess, Seetha wearing a single plait (as a as a mark of desolation), looking 
miserable, remaining absorbed in your thought, reposing on the floor, having discoloured limbs like 
a lotus in winter, turning back the wish from Ravana, having determined to die, but thinking of you 
alone."_END

B_5_C_62_29
BEGIN_एते तिष्ठन्तु गच्छामो भर्ता नो यत्र वानरः |
सुग्रीवो विपुल ग्रीवः सह रामेण तिष्ठति || ५-६२-३१_END
