BEGIN_"Let these monkeys stay here. We will go to the place where the thick-necked Sugreeva, 
our lord of the monkeys stays together with Rama."_END

B_5_C_64_16
BEGIN_तव च इदम् सुसदृशम् वाक्यम् न अन्यस्य कस्यचित् |
सम्नतिः हि तव आख्याति भविष्यत् शुभ भाग्यताम् || ५-६४-१७_END
BEGIN_"It is so worthy of you alone that you have spoken such words. None else can utter like 
this. Your humility itself is telling of your future suitableness for prosperity."_END

B_5_C_63_23
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा दधि मुखस्य इदम् सुग्रीवः तु प्रहृष्य च |
वन पालम् पुनः वाक्यम् सुग्रीवः प्रत्यभाषत || ५-६३-२६_END
BEGIN_Hearing those words of Dadhimukha, Sugreeva with a charming neck, was very much pleased 
and further spoke to Dadhimukha, the guardian of the grove (as follows):_END

B_5_C_58_58
BEGIN_यदि चेत् त्वम् तु माम् दर्पान् न अभिनन्दसि गर्विते |
द्वौ मास अनन्तरम् सीते पास्यामि रुधिरम् तव || ५-५८-६८_END
BEGIN_" 'O arrogant lady! O Seetha! If you refuse me by your arrogance, I will be drinking 
your blood after a period of two months.'"_END

B_5_C_65_10
BEGIN_इक्ष्वाकु वंश विख्यातिम् शनैः कीर्तयत अनघ || ५-६५-१५
स मया नर शार्दूल विश्वासम् उपपादिता |_END
BEGIN_"O faultless tiger among men! Seetha established confidence in me, after I slowly described 
to her the fame of Ikshvaku dynasty."_END

B_5_C_62_30
BEGIN_सर्वम् चैव अन्गदे दोषम् श्रावयिष्यामि पार्थिव |
अमर्षी वचनम् श्रुत्वा घातयिष्यति वानरान् || ५-६२-३२_END
BEGIN_"I will make known to the king, all the misdeed of Angada. Hearing my words, the enraged 
king will get the monkeys killed."_END

B_5_C_64_17
BEGIN_सर्वे वयम् अपि प्राप्ताः तत्र गन्तुम् कृत क्षणाः |
स यत्र हरि वीराणाम् सुग्रीवः पतिः अव्ययः || ५-६४-१८_END
BEGIN_"All of us, who reached here, are waiting for the right moment to go to that place where 
Sugreeva, the imperishable king of the heroic monkeys, is."_END

B_5_C_63_24
BEGIN_प्रीतो अस्मि सौम्य यत् भुक्तम् वनम् तैः कृत कर्मभिः |
मर्षितम् मर्षणीयम् च चेष्टितम् कृत कर्मणाम् || ५-६३-२७_END
BEGIN_"I am happy that Madhuvana has been enjoyed by those monkeys, who have accomplished their 
act. Since the act (damage to the grove) done by those monkeys, who have accomplished their purpose 
is fit to be forgiven, I pardon them._END

B_5_C_58_59
BEGIN_एतत् श्रुत्वा वचः तस्य रावणस्य दुरात्मनः |
उवाच परम क्रुद्धा सीता वचनम् उत्तमम् || ५-५८-६९_END
BEGIN_"Hearing those words of the evil-minded Ravana, Seetha was very much irritated and spoke 
the following excellent words:_END

B_5_C_65_11
BEGIN_ततः सम्भाषिता देवी सर्वम् अर्थम् च दर्शिता || ५-६५-१६
राम सुग्रीव सख्यम् च श्रुत्वा प्रीतिम् उपागता |
नियतः समुदाचारो भक्तिः च अस्याः तथा त्वयि || ५-६५-१७_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, I spoke and explained to Seetha, about the entire significance of my arrival 
there. On hearing about the alliance between Rama and Sugreeva, she was quite pleased. Her morality 
as well as her devotion in you are steadfast."_END

B_5_C_62_31
BEGIN_इष्टम् मधु वनम् हि एतत् सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
पितृ पैतामहम् दिव्यम् देवैः अपि दुरासदम् || ५-६२-३३_END
BEGIN_"This Madhuvana is indeed cherished by our high-souled king, Sugreeva and it derived 
from his father and grand father. It is so charming, but is dangerous to be approached even by celestials."_END

B_5_C_63_25
BEGIN_इच्छामि शीघ्रम् हनुमत् प्रधानान् |
शाखा मृगान् तान् मृग राज दर्पान् |
द्रष्टुम् कृत अर्थान् सह राघवाभ्याम् |
श्रोतुम् च सीता अधिगमे प्रयत्नम् || ५-६३-२८_END
BEGIN_"I, together with Rama and Lakshmana, soon desire to see those monkeys, with Hanuma as 
their chief, who having acquired the pride of a lion and who attained his purpose; and also to hear 
about their effort in finding out Seetha."_END

B_5_C_64_18
BEGIN_त्वया हि अनुक्तैः हरिभिः न एव शक्यम् पदात् पदम् |
क्वचित् गन्तुम् हरि श्रेष्ठ ब्रूमः सत्यम् इदम् तु ते || ५-६४-१९_END
BEGIN_"O the excellent of monkeys! Without your command, it is not possible for the monkeys 
anywhere, even a step forward. We are speaking this truth to you."_END

B_5_C_58_60
BEGIN_राक्षस अधम रामस्य भार्याम् अमित तेजसः |
इक्ष्वाकु कुल नाथस्य स्नुषाम् दशरथस्य च || ५-५८-७०
अवाच्यम् वदतो जिह्वा कथम् न पतिता तव |_END
BEGIN_"How did your tongue not fall of, O the worst demon, by speaking such words not to be 
uttered, to the consort of Rama, of boundless glory, and the daughter-in-law of Dasaratha the lord of 
Ikshvaku dynasty?"_END

B_5_C_65_12
BEGIN_एवम् मया महाभागा दृष्टा जनक नन्दिनी |
उग्रेण तपसा युक्ता त्वत् भक्त्या पुरुष ऋषभ || ५-६५-१८_END
BEGIN_"O, the foremost of men! I thus saw that illustrious Seetha, endowed with severe penance 
and devotion towards you."_END

B_5_C_62_32
BEGIN_स वानरान् इमान् सर्वान् मधु लुब्धान् गत आयुषः |
घातयिष्यति दण्डेन सुग्रीवः ससुहृज् जनान् || ५-६२-३४_END
BEGIN_"The longevity of these monkeys got reduced, as they were very much lustful of honey. 
That Sugreeva can get these monkeys together with their companions, killed as a matter of punishment."_END

B_5_C_63_26
BEGIN_प्रीतिस्फीताक्षौ सम्प्रहृष्टौ कुमारौ |
दृष्ट्वा सिद्धार्थौ वानराणाम् च राजा |
अङ्गैः सम्हृष्टैः कर्मसिद्धिम् विदित्वा |
बाह्वोओरासन्नाम् सोऽतिमात्रम् ननन्द || ५-६३-२९_END
BEGIN_Seeing Rama and Lakshmana with their eyes filled with ecstatic delight, the princes, 
who were thrilled with joy and who accomplished their aim, Sugreeva that king of the monkeys was very 
much delighted, knowing that accomplishment of their work is coming close to their hands and his limbs 
were thrilled with joy._END

B_5_C_64_19
BEGIN_एवम् तु वदताम् तेषाम् अन्गदः प्रत्यभाषत |
बाढम् गच्छाम इति उक्त्वा उत्पपात मही तलात् || ५-६४-२०_END
BEGIN_While they were thus speaking; Angada replied, "Let us go." The mighty monkeys then sprang 
into the air._END

B_5_C_58_61
BEGIN_किंस्वित् वीर्यम् तव अनार्य यो माम् भर्तुः असम्निधौ || ५-५८-७१
अपहृत्य आगतः पाप तेन अदृष्टो महात्मना |_END
BEGIN_"O ignoble soul! Of what account is your prowess, when you came unnoticed during the 
absence of my lord, that great soul and abducted me, O sinful one?"_END

B_5_C_65_13
BEGIN_अभिज्ञानम् च मे दत्तम् यथा वृत्तम् तव अन्तिके |
चित्र कूटे महाप्राज्ञ वायसम् प्रति राघव || ५-६५-१९_END
BEGIN_"O Rama, of great intelligence! To me, she gave as a token of remembrance, a previous 
event of a crow occurred at your vicinity in Mount Chitrakuta."_END

B_5_C_62_33
BEGIN_वध्या हि एते दुरात्मानो नृप आज्ञा परिभाविनः |
अमर्ष प्रभवो रोषः सफलो नो भविष्यति | ५-६२-३५_END
BEGIN_"These evil-minded beings, who disregarded the royal command, are fit to be capitally 
punished. Our wrath, springing from our impatience, will indeed become fruitful."_END

B_5_C_64_20
BEGIN_उत्पतन्तम् अनूत्पेतुः सर्वे ते हरि यूथपाः |
कृत्वा आकाशम् निराकाशम् यज्ञ उत्क्षिप्ता इव अनलाः || ५-६४-२१_END
BEGIN_All those leaders of monkey-troops, like stones shot from a catapult, making the space 
space-less, followed Angada, who was springing forward._END

B_5_C_58_62
BEGIN_न त्वम् रामस्य सदृशो दास्ये अपि अस्या न युज्यसे || ५-५८-७२
यज्ञीयः सत्य वाक् चैव रण श्लाघी च राघवः |_END
BEGIN_" 'You have no similarity with Rama. You are unfit even to do service to Rama. Rama performs 
sacrifices. He speaks only truth. He is a lover of battle'."_END

B_5_C_65_14
BEGIN_विज्ञाप्यः च नर व्याघ्रो रामो वायु सुत त्वया |
अखिलेन इह यत् दृष्टम् इति माम् आह जानकी || ५-६५-२०_END
BEGIN_"Seetha spoke to me saying, 'O Hanuma! Inform Rama, the foremost among men, all that 
you have seen here."_END

B_5_C_62_34
BEGIN_एवम् उक्त्वा दधि मुखो वन पालान् महाबलः |
जगाम सहसा उत्पत्य वन पालैः समन्वितः || ५-६२-३६_END
BEGIN_Thus speaking to the garden-guards, the mighty Dadhimukha quickly springing up all at 
once, went (to Kishkindha) together with the garden-guards._END

B_5_C_64_21
BEGIN_ते अम्बरम् सहसा उत्पत्य वेगवन्तः प्लवम्गमाः |
विनदन्तो महानादम् घना वात ईरिता यथा || ५-६४-२२_END
BEGIN_Those monkeys with speed, sounding forth a loud noise, sprang into the sky, like clouds 
driven by the wind._END

B_5_C_58_63
BEGIN_जानक्या परुषम् वाक्यम् एवम् उक्तो दश आननः || ५-५८-७३
जज्वाल सहसा कोपाच् चितास्थ इव पावकः |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing these harsh words from Seetha, Ravana was at once ablaze with anger, as a fire 
blazes in a pile of wood."_END

B_5_C_65_15
BEGIN_अयम् च अस्मै प्रदातव्यम् यत्नात् सुपरिरक्षितम् |
ब्रुवता वचनानि एवम् सुग्रीवस्य उपशृण्वतः || ५-६५-२१_END
BEGIN_"While Sugreeva is hearing nearby and while you are telling the words in this way, let 
this jewel, which is deliberately well-guarded, be given to Rama."_END

B_5_C_62_35
BEGIN_निमेष अन्तर मात्रेण स हि प्राप्तो वन आलयः |
सहस्र अंशु सुतो धीमान् सुग्रीवो यत्र वानरः || ५-६२-३७_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha, the monkey, reached the place where that Sugreeva, the intelligent monkey 
was there, within an interval of only a moment._END

B_5_C_64_22
BEGIN_अन्गदे हि अननुप्राप्ते सुग्रीवो वानर अधिपः |
उवाच शोक उपहतम् रामम् कमल लोचनम् || ५-६४-२३_END
BEGIN_Even before Angada landed there, Sugreeva, the king of monkeys spoke to the louts-eyed 
Rama, who was afflicted with grief (as follows):_END

B_5_C_58_64
BEGIN_विवृत्य नयने क्रूरे मुष्टिम् उद्यम्य दक्षिणम् || ५-५८-७४
मैथिलीम् हन्तुम् आरब्धः स्त्रीभिः हाहा कृतम् तदा |_END
BEGIN_" 'Rolling his cruel eyes and lifting his right fist, Ravana was about to kill Seetha. 
Then, an alarm was raised by a women there'."_END

B_5_C_65_16
BEGIN_एष चूडा मणिः श्रीमान् मया ते यत्न रक्षितः |
मनः शिलायाः तिकलः तम् स्मरस्व इति च अब्रवीत् || ५-६५-२२
त्वया प्राष्टे तिम्के तम् किल स्मर्तुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_"This beautiful jewel for the head has been well-guarded by me. You also ought to recall 
a mark indeed painted by you (by slip) on the curve of my cheek with powder of an orange-red rock, when 
my former mark on my forehead got effaced."_END

B_5_C_62_36
BEGIN_रामम् च लक्ष्मणम् चैव दृष्ट्वा सुग्रीवम् एव च |
सम प्रतिष्ठाम् जगतीम् आकाशान् निपपात ह || ५-६२-३८_END
BEGIN_Seeing Rama, Lakshmana and Sugreeva, Dadhimukha descended to a level ground, from the 
sky._END

B_5_C_64_23
BEGIN_समाश्वसिहि भद्रम् ते दृष्टा देवी न संशयः |
न आगन्तुम् इह शक्यम् तैः अतीते समये हि नः || ५-६४-२४_END
BEGIN_"Be pacified! Happiness to you! The princess has been seen. There is not doubt. When 
the time earlier fixed by us exceeds beyond limit, it is not possible for them to come here."_END

B_5_C_58_65
BEGIN_स्त्रीणाम् मध्यात् समुत्पत्य तस्य भार्या दुरात्मनः || ५-५८-७५
वरा मन्द उदरी नाम तया स प्रतिषेधितः |_END
BEGIN_"Springing up from the midst of those women, a royal woman named Mandodari, the wife 
of that evil-minded Ravana, ran to him. He was restrained by her."_END

B_5_C_65_17
BEGIN_एष निर्यातितः श्रीमान् मया ते वारि सम्भवः || ५-६५-२३
एतम् दृष्ट्वा प्रमोदिष्ये व्यसने त्वाम् इव अनघ |_END
BEGIN_"This beautiful jewel, which has its origin in sea-water, has been sent to you. Seeing 
this in my grief, I am feeling always happy as though I am seeing you."_END

B_5_C_62_37
BEGIN_स निपत्य महावीर्यः सर्वैः तैः परिवारितः |
हरिः दधि मुखः पालैः पालानाम् परम ईश्वरः || ५-६२-३९
स दीन वदनो भूत्वा कृत्वा शिरसि च अञ्जलिम् |
सुग्रीवस्य शुभौ मूर्ध्ना चरणौ प्रत्यपीडयत् || ५-६२-४०_END
BEGIN_That Dadhimukha of a great prowess, the supreme lord of the guards, surrounded by all 
those garden-guards keeping a sad face, made a respectful salutation to Sugreeva with his head, by falling 
down and touching with his head, the auspicious feet of Sugreeva._END

B_5_C_64_24
BEGIN_न मत् सकाशम् आगच्छेत् कृत्ये हि विनिपातिते |
युव राजो महाबाहुः प्लवताम् प्रवरो अन्गदः || ५-६४-२५_END
BEGIN_"Angada, the long-armed prince and the most excellent of monkeys does not make his appearance 
before my vicinity, if the work is ruined."_END

B_5_C_58_66
BEGIN_उक्तः च मधुराम् वाणीम् तया स मदन अर्दितः || ५-५८-७६
सीतया तव किम् कार्यम् महाइन्द्र सम विक्रम |_END
BEGIN_"She spoke to Ravana, smitten with love, the following sweet words: 'O Ravana having 
a prowess similar to that of Indra! Of what need is with Seetha to you?"_END

B_5_C_65_18
BEGIN_जीवितम् धारयिष्यामि मासम् दशरथ आत्मज || ५-६५-२४
ऊर्ध्वम् मासान् न जीवेयम् रक्षसाम् वशम् आगता |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! I shall be sustaining my life for a month. Having come into the control of demons, 
I cannot survive beyond one month."_END

B_5_C_64_25
BEGIN_यदि अपि अकृत कृत्यानाम् ईदृशः स्यात् उपक्रमः |
भवेत् तु दीन वदनो भ्रान्त विप्लुत मानसः || ५-६४-२६_END
BEGIN_"Even if such an exploit may be possible by these monkeys who have not been able to accomplish 
their work, Angada would have worn a sad face and felt perplexed and scattered in mind."_END

B_5_C_58_67
BEGIN_देव गन्धर्व कन्याभिः यक्ष कन्याभिः एव च || ५-५८-७७
सार्धम् प्रभो रमस्व इह सीतया किम् करिष्यसि |_END
BEGIN_" 'O lord! Enjoy yourself with the daughters of gods, Gandharvas the celestial musicians 
and Yakshas the semi-divine beings. What will you do with Seetha?'"_END

B_5_C_65_19
BEGIN_इति माम् अब्रवीत् सीता कृश अन्गी धर्म चारिणी || ५-६५-२५
रावण अन्तः पुरे रुद्धा मृगी इव उत्फुल्ल लोचना |_END
BEGIN_"Seetha, with her emaciated body, practicing virtue, confined in Ravana's gynaecium and 
with her wide-open eyes like that of a doe, spoke to me the following words:_END

B_5_C_66_0
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तो हनुमता रामो दशरथ आत्मजः |
तम् मणिम् हृदये कृत्वा प्ररुरोद सलक्ष्मणः || ५-६६-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of Hanuma, Rama the son of Dasaratha, having Lakshmana by his side, 
pressing that jewel on his bosom, began to weep._END

B_5_C_64_26
BEGIN_पितृ पैतामहम् च एतत् पूर्वकैः अभिरक्षितम् |
न मे मधु वनम् हन्यात् अहृष्टः प्लवग ईश्वरः || ५-६४-२७
कौसल्या सुप्रजा राम समाश्वसिहि सुव्रत |_END
BEGIN_"If Angada the lord f the monkeys is not rejoiced, he would not have damaged my madhuvana, 
which belongs to my father and grandfather as well as protected by my forbears. Get consoled well, O 
virtuous Rama, the splendid son of Kausalya!"_END

B_5_C_58_68
BEGIN_ततः ताभिः समेताभिः नारीभिः स महाबलः || ५-५८-७८
उत्थाप्य सहसा नीतो भवनम् स्वम् निशा चरः |_END
BEGIN_"Thereupon, those women together propitiated that mighty Ravana and quickly took him 
to his palace."_END

B_5_C_65_20
BEGIN_एतत् एव मया आख्यातम् सर्वम् राघव यत् यथा || ५-६५-२६
सर्वथा सागर जले सम्तारः प्रविधीयताम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! I have narrated to you whatever has occurred, in its entirety. Let a bridge 
be constructed, by all means, across the waters of the ocean."_END

B_5_C_66_1
BEGIN_तम् तु दृष्ट्वा मणि श्रेष्ठम् राघवः शोक कर्शितः |
नेत्राभ्याम् अश्रु पूर्णाभ्याम् सुग्रीवम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ५-६६-२_END
BEGIN_Seeing that excellent jewel, Rama emaciated with grief, having his eyes filled with tears, 
spoke to Sugreeva as follows:_END

B_5_C_64_27
BEGIN_दृष्टा देवी न संदेहो न च अन्येन हनूमता || ५-६४-२८
न हि अन्यः कर्मणः हेतुः साधने तत् विधो भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_"Seetha was seen. There is no doubt. None other than Hanuma must have seen Seetha. There 
is indeed none other than Hanuma, who is the executor."_END

B_5_C_58_69
BEGIN_याते तस्मिन् दशग्रीवे राक्षस्यो विकृत आननाः || ५-५८-७९
सीताम् निर्भर्त्सयाम् आसुः वाक्यैः क्रूरैः सुदारुणैः |_END
BEGIN_"When that Ravana left, the ugly-faced female-demons frightened. Seetha with their cruel 
and very dreadful words."_END

B_5_C_65_21
BEGIN_तौ जात आश्वासौ राज पुत्रौ विदित्वा |
तच् च अभिज्ञानम् राघवाय प्रदाय |
देव्या च आख्यातम् सर्वम् एव आनुपूर्व्यात् |
वाचा सम्पूर्णम् वायु पुत्रः शशंस || ५-६५-२७_END
BEGIN_Coming to know that the two princes, Rama and Lakshmana have become confident and having 
given that token of remembrance to Rama, Hanuma apprised completely in so many words, in regular succession, 
all that was conveyed by Seetha, the princess._END

B_5_C_66_2
BEGIN_यथैव धेनुः स्रवति स्नेहात् वत्सस्य वत्सला |
तथा मम अपि हृदयम् मणि रत्नस्य दर्शनात् || ५-६६-३_END
BEGIN_"Even as a cow, who is affectionate towards her offspring, gushes forth the milk (from 
her teats) due to her love at the very sight of her calf, so does my heart too melt through the sight 
of this excellent jewel."_END

B_5_C_64_28
BEGIN_हनूमति हि सिद्धिः च मतिः च मति सत्तम || ५-६४-२९
व्यवसायः च वीर्यम् च सूर्ये तेज इव ध्रुवम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama, having a very good understanding! In Hanuma, qualities like capacity to accomplish 
any object, intelligence, strenuous effort and vigour are unchangeable, like a splendour in the sun."_END

B_5_C_58_70
BEGIN_तृणवत् भाषितम् तासाम् गणयामास जानकी || ५-५८-८०
तर्जितम् च तदा तासाम् सीताम् प्राप्य निरर्थकम् |_END
BEGIN_"Seetha reckoned the utterance of those women as a blade of grass. At that time, the 
roaring of those female-demons reached Seetha in vain."_END

B_5_C_66_3
BEGIN_मणि रत्नम् इदम् दत्तम् वैदेह्याः श्वशुरेण मे |
वधू काले यथा बद्धम् अधिकम् मूर्ध्नि शोभते || ५-६६-४_END
BEGIN_"This excellent jewel was presented by my father-in-law to Seetha when she had become 
a bride and was tied to her head in such a way that it looked additionally beautifying."_END

B_5_C_64_29
BEGIN_जाम्बवान् यत्र नेता स्यात् अन्गदः च बल ईश्वरः || ५-६४-३०
हनूमान् च अपि अधिष्ठाता न तस्य गतिः अन्यथा |_END
BEGIN_"Where Jambavan is a leader; Angada as the commander of troops and moreover Hanuma as 
the administer, the progress of that work cannot be as otherwise."_END

B_5_C_58_71
BEGIN_वृथा गर्जित निश्चेष्टा राक्षस्यः पिशित अशनाः || ५-५८-८१
रावणाय शशंसुः ताः सीता अव्यवसितम् महत् |_END
BEGIN_"As their roaring frittered away, those flesh-eating female-demons became helpless and 
reported that great resolve of Seetha to Ravana."_END

B_5_C_66_4
BEGIN_अयम् हि जल सम्भूतो मणिः प्रवर पूजितः |
यज्ञे परम तुष्टेन दत्तः शक्रेण धीमता || ५-६६-५_END
BEGIN_"The jewel, which was found in the waters and recommended by the good, had been presented 
to him earlier by the intelligent Indra the lord of celestials, who was highly pleased in Yajna, a sacrificial 
rite (intended to propitiate him)."_END

B_5_C_64_30
BEGIN_मा भूः चिन्ता समायुक्तः सम्प्रति अमित विक्रम || ५-६४-३१
ततः किल किला शब्दम् शुश्राव आसन्नम् अम्बरे |
हनूमत् कर्म दृप्तानाम् नर्दताम् कानन ओकसाम् || ५-६४-३२
किष्किन्धाम् उपयातानाम् सिद्धिम् कथयताम् इव |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama, of unlimited prowess! Do not encounter troubled thoughts now!" Meanwhile, when 
the monkeys, who are proud of Hanuma's performance and who are making noise as though they are proclaiming 
about the accomplishment of their act are approaching Kishkindha Sugreeva heard certain sounds expressing 
joy, in the vicinity of the sky."_END

B_5_C_58_72
BEGIN_ततः ताः सहिताः सर्वा विहत आशा निरुद्यमाः || ५-५८-८२
परिक्षिप्य समन्तात् ताम् निद्रा वशम् उपागताः |_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, all those women joined together, warded off their hopes and held back their 
effort. In the end, they encircled Seetha and were overpowered with sleep."_END

B_5_C_66_5
BEGIN_इमम् दृष्ट्वा मणि श्रेष्ठम् तथा तातस्य दर्शनम् |
अद्य अस्मि अवगतः सौम्य वैदेहस्य तथा विभोः || ५-६६-६_END
BEGIN_"O gentle Sugreeva! Seeing now this excellent jewel, I am considering it as surely as 
obtaining the sight of my father as well as Janaka, the king of Videha."_END

B_5_C_64_31
BEGIN_ततः श्रुत्वा निनादम् तम् कपीनाम् कपि सत्तमः || ५-६४-३३
आयत अन्चित लान्गूलः सो अभवद्त् हृष्ट मानसः |_END
BEGIN_Then, hearing that clamour of the monkeys, Sugreeva the chief of the monkeys became rejoiced 
at heart, duly stretching and curling up his tail (in joy)._END

B_5_C_58_73
BEGIN_तासु चैव प्रसुप्तासु सीता भर्तृ हिते रता || ५-५८-८३
विलप्य करुणम् दीना प्रशुशोच सुदुह्खिता |_END
BEGIN_"When those women went to sleep, Seetha, intent upon the welfare of her husband, was 
deeply aggrieved, miserable and sore depressed as she was, lamenting pitifully."_END

B_5_C_66_6
BEGIN_अयम् हि शोभते तस्याः प्रियाया मूर्ध्नि मे मणिः |
अस्य दर्शनेन अहम् प्राप्ताम् ताम् इव चिन्तये || ५-६६-७_END
BEGIN_"This jewel indeed looks splendid on the head of my beloved Seetha. By seeing this now, 
I am considering as though I obtained the sight of Seetha herself."_END

B_5_C_64_32
BEGIN_आजग्मुः ते अपि हरयो राम दर्शन कान्क्षिणः || ५-६४-३४
अन्गदम् पुरतः कृत्वा हनूमन्तम् च वानरम् |_END
BEGIN_Keeping Angada and Hanuma in front of them, those monkeys too arrived with their eagerness 
to see Rama._END

B_5_C_58_74
BEGIN_तासाम् मध्यात्समुत्थाय त्रिजटा वाक्यमब्रवीत् || ५-५८-८४
आत्मानम् खादत क्षिप्रम् न सीता विनशिष्यति |
जनकस्यात्मजा साध्वी स्नुष दशरथस्य च || ५-५८-८५_END
BEGIN_"Trijata, rising from the midst of those female-demons, spoke the following words; 'Feed 
on yourself quickly rather than on Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, a virtuous woman and the daughter-in-law 
of Dasartha who des not get destroyed'."_END

B_5_C_66_7
BEGIN_किम् आह सीता वैदेही ब्रूहि सौम्य पुनः पुनः |
पिपासुम् इव तोयेन सिन्चन्ती वाक्य वारिणा || ५-६६-८_END
BEGIN_"O gentle one! Repeat again and again, what Seetha the daughter of Videha's king said 
to you, sprinkling me with your stream of words, like offering water to a thirsty person."_END

B_5_C_64_33
BEGIN_ते अन्गद प्रमुखा वीराः प्रहृष्टाः च मुदा अन्विताः || ५-६४-३५
निपेतुः हरि राजस्य समीपे राघवस्य च |_END
BEGIN_Those heroes, having Angada as their chief, exceedingly pleased as they were and filled 
with joy, landed at the vicinity of Sugreeva and Rama._END

B_5_C_58_75
BEGIN_स्वप्नो ह्यद्य मया दृष्टो दारुणो रोमहर्षणः |
रक्षसाम् च विनाशाय भर्तुरस्या जयाय च || ५-५८-८६_END
BEGIN_"'Now, I have seen a dreadful dream, causing my hair to stand erect. It is pointing towards 
the ruin of our demons and the victory of her husband."_END

B_5_C_66_8
BEGIN_इतः तु किम् दुह्खतरम् यत् इमम् वारि सम्भवम् |
मणिम् पश्यामि सौमित्रे वैदेहीम् आगतम् विना || ५-६६-९_END
BEGIN_"O Lakshmana! What could be more painful than the fact that I am seeing this jewel found 
in waters, without the arrival of Seetha?"_END

B_5_C_64_34
BEGIN_हनूमान् च महाबहुः प्रणम्य शिरसा ततः || ५-६४-३६
नियताम् अक्षताम् देवीम् राघवाय न्यवेदयत् |_END
BEGIN_Thereafter, the mighty armed Hanuma, offering his salutation in bending his head low, 
informed Rama that Seetha the princess is constant in devotion to Rama and sound in body._END

B_5_C_58_76
BEGIN_अलमस्मात्परित्रातुम् राघवाद्रक्षसीगणम् |
अभियाचाम वैदेहीमेतद्धि मम रोचते || ५-५८-८७_END
BEGIN_" �We will pray Seetha, who is capable of protecting all our female-demons from Rama. 
I feel that it is batter for us'."_END

B_5_C_66_9
BEGIN_चिरम् जीवति वैदेही यदि मासम् धरिष्यति |
क्षणम् सौम्य न जीवेयम् विना ताम् असित ईक्षणाम् || ५-६६-१०_END
BEGIN_"O gentle one! If Seetha can survive for a month, it means that she is surviving for 
long. O gentle one! Without that black-eyed Seetha, I cannot survive for even a moment."_END

B_5_C_64_35
BEGIN_दृष्टा देवीति हनुमद्वदनादमृतोपमम् || ५-६४-३७
आकर्ण्य वचनम् रामो हर्षमाप सलक्ष्मणः |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the nectar-like words, saying "Seetha was found" from the mouth of Hanuma, Rama 
and Lakshmana felt happy._END

B_5_C_58_77
BEGIN_यस्या ह्येवम्विधः स्वप्नो दुःखितायाः प्रदृश्यते |
सा दुःखैर्विविधैर्मुक्ता सुखमाप्नोत्यनुत्तमम् || ५-५८-८८
प्रणिपातप्रसन्ना हि मैथिली जनकात्मजा |_END
BEGIN_" 'When such a dream is seen while a woman is weeping, that woman gets relieved of many 
kinds of sorrows and will obtain happiness. Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, indeed will be pleased on 
receiving a salutation'."_END

B_5_C_66_10
BEGIN_नय माम् अपि तम् देशम् यत्र दृष्टा मम प्रिया |
न तिष्ठेयम् क्षणम् अपि प्रवृत्तिम् उपलभ्य च || ५-६६-११_END
BEGIN_"Take me too to that place where my beloved Seetha has been seen. I cannot halt even 
for a moment, after receiving the news of her location."_END

B_5_C_64_36
BEGIN_निश्चित अर्थम् ततः तस्मिन् सुग्रीवम् पवन आत्मजे || ५-६४-३८
लक्ष्मणः प्रीतिमान् प्रीतम् बहु मानात् अवैक्षत |_END
BEGIN_Thereupon, Lakshmana with love looked with reverence on the joyful Sugreeva, who earlier 
decidedly apprised about the aforesaid Hanuma, having accomplished the task._END

B_5_C_58_78
BEGIN_ततह् सा ह्रीमती बाला भर्तुर्विजयहर्षिता || ५-५८-८९
अवोचद्यदि तत्तथ्यम् भवेयम् शरणम् हि वः |_END
BEGIN_"Delighted at hearing the victory of her lord, that girl Seetha then basfully spoke: 
'If it is true, I will be protecting you all'."_END

B_5_C_66_11
BEGIN_कथम् सा मम सुश्रोणि भीरु भीरुः सती तदा |
भय आवहानाम् घोराणाम् मध्ये तिष्ठति रक्षसाम् || ५-६६-१२_END
BEGIN_"How does Seetha, my virtuous wife with her charming limbs, who is very shy, stay all 
the time with demons who are terrific and cruel?"_END

B_5_C_67_0
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः तु हनुमान् राघवेण महात्मना |
सीताया भाषितम् सर्वम् न्यवेदयत राघवे || ५-६७-१_END
BEGIN_Hearing the words of the high-souled Rama, Hanuma reported to Rama, all the words spoken 
by Seetha._END

B_5_C_58_79
BEGIN_ताम् च अहम् तादृशीम् दृष्ट्वा सीताया दारुणाम् दशाम् |
चिन्तयामास विश्रान्तो न च मे निर्वृतम् मनः || ५-५८-९०_END
BEGIN_"Taking rest for some time and seeing such a dreadful state of Seetha, I reflected upon 
it. My mind could not satisfy itself."_END

B_5_C_64_37
BEGIN_प्रीत्या च रममाणो अथ राघवः पर वीरहा || ५-६४-३९
बहु मानेन महता हनूमन्तम् अवैक्षत |_END
BEGIN_Rama, the annihilator of hostile heroes, who obtained a great joy, looked on Hanuma with 
a high esteem._END

B_5_C_66_12
BEGIN_शारदः तिमिर उन्मुखो नूनम् चन्द्र इव अम्बुदैः |
आवृतम् वदनम् तस्या न विराजति राक्षसैः || ५-६६-१३_END
BEGIN_"Her countenance, surely like automnal moon, though liberated of darkness, but screened 
by clouds, does not shine at present."_END

B_5_C_67_1
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तवती देवी जानकी पुरुष ऋषभ |
पूर्व वृत्तम् अभिज्ञानम् चित्र कूटे यथा तथम् || ५-६७-२_END
BEGIN_"O Rama the foremost of men! Seetha, the princess, spoke a detailed account of an event 
which occurred long ago in Mount Chitrakuta, as a token of recollection."_END

B_5_C_58_80
BEGIN_सम्भाषण अर्थे च मया जानक्याः चिन्तितो विधिः || ५-५८-९१
इक्ष्वाकु कुल वंशः तु ततो मम पुरः कृतः |_END
BEGIN_"Thinking about a means for starting a conversation with Seetha, I started to describe 
the history of Ikshvaku's dynasty."_END

B_5_C_66_13
BEGIN_किम् आह सीता हनुमन् तत्त्वतः कथयस्व मे |
एतेन खलु जीविष्ये भेषजेन आतुरो यथा || ५-६६-१४_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Tell me now, correctly what Seetha told you. I shall surely survive, by hearing 
her words, even as a sick man would with the help of a medicine."_END

B_5_C_67_2
BEGIN_सुख सुप्ता त्वया सार्धम् जानकी पूर्वम् उत्थिता |
वायसः सहसा उत्पत्य विरराद स्तन अन्तरे || ५-६७-३_END
BEGIN_"Seetha, who slept happily by your side (at one instance) got up before you. A crow coming 
down quickly, tore her flesh at an area in the midst of her breasts (with its beak)."_END

B_5_C_58_81
BEGIN_श्रुत्वा तु गदिताम् वाचम् राज ऋषि गण पूजिताम् || ५-५८-९२
प्रत्यभाषत माम् देवी बाष्पैः पिहित लोचना |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the words spoken by me, which are adored by the assemblies of royal sages, Seetha 
the princess, with her eyes filled with tears, spoke to me, as follows:"_END

B_5_C_66_14
BEGIN_मधुरा मधुर आलापा किम् आह मम भामिनी |
मत् विहीना वराअरोहा हनुमन् कथयस्व मे || ५-६६-१५_END
BEGIN_"Tell me, what my beautiful consort, who is sweet-natured, and who utters sweet words, 
having fine hips and has been separated from me, said to you."_END

B_5_C_67_3
BEGIN_पर्यायेण च सुप्तः त्वम् देवि अन्के भरत अग्रज |
पुनः च किल पक्षी स देव्या जनयति व्यथाम् || ५-६७-४_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! You slept in your turn on the lap of the princess. That crow again began to 
torment the princess."_END

B_5_C_58_82
BEGIN_कः त्वम् केन कथम् च इह प्राप्तो वानर पुम्गव || ५-५८-९३
का च रामेण ते प्रीतिः तन् मे शंसितुम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_" 'O the foremost among the monkeys! Who are you? Why did you come here? How did you 
come? What type of friendship do you have with Rama? You ought to tell me all this?"_END

B_5_C_67_4
BEGIN_पुनः पुनरुपागम्य विरराद भृशम् किल |
ततः त्वम् बोधितः तस्याः शोणितेन समुक्षितः || ५-६७-५_END
BEGIN_"Coming near again and again, it tore her breast severely. Dampened by her blood, you 
then were awakened by her."_END

B_5_C_58_83
BEGIN_तस्याः तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा अहम् अपि अब्रुवम् वचः || ५-५८-९४
देवि रामस्य भर्तुः ते सहायो भीम विक्रमः |
सुग्रीवो नाम विक्रान्तो वानर इन्दो महाबलः || ५-५८-९५_END
BEGIN_"Hearing those words of Seetha, I spoke the following words: 'O princess! There is a 
courageous king of monkeys, by name Sugreeva, who is a mighty companion to your husband, possessing 
a terrific prowess."_END

B_5_C_67_5
BEGIN_वायसेन च तेन एव सततम् बाध्यमानया |
बोधितः किल देव्याः त्वम् सुख सुप्तः परम् तप || ५-६७-६_END
BEGIN_"O tormentator of enemies! Though lying happily asleep, you were awakened by Seetha the 
princess, who was being ceaselessly tormented by the crow."_END

B_5_C_58_84
BEGIN_तस्य माम् विद्धि भृत्यम् त्वम् हनूमन्तम् इह आगतम् |
भर्त्रा अहम् प्रहितः तुभ्यम् रामेण अक्लिष्ट कर्मणा || ५-५८-९६_END
BEGIN_"Know me, who came here, as Hanuma, a servant of that Sugreeva, Rama, you husband, who 
is unwearied in his actions, sent me here for your sake."_END

B_5_C_67_6
BEGIN_ताम् तु दृष्ट्वा महाबाहो रादिताम् च स्तन अन्तरे |
आशी विष इव क्रुद्धो निह्श्वसन्न् अभ्यभाषथाः || ५-६७-७_END
BEGIN_"O long-armed Rama! Seeing her, who was lacerated at the midst of her breasts, you were 
enraged like a hissing snake and spoke to her as follows."_END

B_5_C_58_85
BEGIN_इदम् च पुरुष व्याघ्रः श्रीमान् दाशरथिः स्वयम् |
अन्गुलीयम् अभिज्ञानम् अदात् तुभ्यम् यशस्विनि || ५-५८-९७_END
BEGIN_"O illustrious lady! Rama, the foremost among men and the glorious man, gave this finger-ring 
personally to you as a token of remembrance."_END

B_5_C_67_7
BEGIN_नख अग्रैः केन ते भीरु दारितम् तु स्तन अन्तरम् |
कः क्रीडति सरोषेण पन्च वक्त्रेण भोगिना || ५-६७-८_END
BEGIN_" 'O bashful Seetha! By whom was the middle of your breasts lacerated with nail-points? 
Who is playing with an angry five-hooded serpent?"_END

B_5_C_67_8
BEGIN_निरीक्षमाणः सहसा वायसम् समवैक्षताः |
नखैः सरुधिरैः तीक्ष्णैः माम् एव अभिमुखम् स्थितम् || ५-६७-९_END
BEGIN_"Looking around, you suddenly saw a crow, which perched in front of Seetha, with its 
sharp nails stained with blood."_END

B_5_C_58_86
BEGIN_तत् इच्छामि त्वया आज्ञप्तम् देवि किम् करवाणि अहम् |
राम लक्ष्मणयोः पार्श्वम् नयामि त्वाम् किम् उत्तरम् || ५-५८-९८_END
BEGIN_"O princess! For that reason, I wish to have a command from you. What am I to do? I shall 
take you to the proximity of Rama and Lakshmana. What do you say?"_END

B_5_C_67_9
BEGIN_सुतः किल स शक्रस्य वायसः पतताम् वरः |
धरा अन्तर चरः शीघ्रम् पवनस्य गतौ समः || ५-६७-१०_END
BEGIN_"That crow, foremost of the birds was indeed the son of Indra the lord of celestials; 
dwelling in the middle of the mountains and equal in speed to the wind."_END

B_5_C_58_87
BEGIN_एतत् श्रुत्वा विदित्वा च सीता जनक नन्दिनी |
आह रावणम् उत्साद्य राघवो माम् नयतु इति || ५-५८-९९_END
BEGIN_"Hearing my words and understanding them, Seetha the daughter of Janaka said as follows: 
'Let Rama take me back, after killing Ravana'."_END

B_5_C_68_0
BEGIN_अथ अहम् उत्तरम् देव्या पुनः उक्तः ससम्भ्रमम् |
तव स्नेहान् नर व्याघ्र सौहार्यात् अनुमान्य च || ५-६८-१_END
BEGIN_"O excellent among men! Having shown respect for me out of her affection and good-heartedness 
for you, I, who was in a haste to go, was spoken to again by Seetha the princess about the further course 
of action."_END

B_5_C_67_10
BEGIN_ततः तस्मिन् महाबाहो कोप सम्वर्तित ईक्षणः |
वायसे त्वम् कृत्वाः क्रूराम् मतिम् मतिमताम् वर || ५-६७-११_END
BEGIN_"O great armed Rama, the excellent among the wise! With your eyes rolling with anger, 
you then harboured a cruel intention against that crow."_END

B_5_C_58_88
BEGIN_प्रणम्य शिरसा देवीम् अहम् आर्याम् अनिन्दिताम् |
राघवस्य मनो ह्लादम् अभिज्ञानम् अयाचिषम् || ५-५८-१००_END
BEGIN_"Bowing my head in salutation to the noble and irreproachable Seetha, I asked for a token 
of remembrance which would gladden the heart of Rama."_END

B_5_C_68_1
BEGIN_एवम् बहु विधम् वाच्यो रामो दाशरथिः त्वया |
यथा माम् आप्नुयात् शीघ्रम् हत्वा रावणम् आहवे || ५-६८-२_END
BEGIN_"Rama, the son of Dasaratha, is to be informed by you thus in several ways, for quickly 
killing Ravana in battle and also as to how he can get me back."_END

B_5_C_58_89
BEGIN_अथ मामब्रवीत्सीता गृह्यतामयम्त्तमः |
मणिर्येन महाबाहू रामस्त्वाम् बहुमन्यते || ५-५८-१०१_END
BEGIN_"Then, Seetha spoke to me as follows: 'Let this foremost jewel, be taken, by which the 
long-armed Rama will be having a high opinion of you'."_END

B_5_C_67_11
BEGIN_स दर्भम् संस्तरात् गृह्य ब्रह्म अस्त्रेण न्ययोजयः |
प्रदीप्त इव काल अग्निः जज्वाल अभिमुखः खगम् || ५-६७-१२_END
BEGIN_"Taking a blade of grass from your bed of the sacred grass, you charged it with the potency 
of Brahma missile. That flaming blade blazed forth like the fire of universal dissolution, with its 
end facing the bird."_END

B_5_C_68_2
BEGIN_यदि वा मन्यसे वीर वस एका अहम् अरिम् दम |
कस्मिंश्चित् सम्वृते देशे विश्रान्तः श्वो गमिष्यसि || ५-६८-३_END
BEGIN_" 'O hero the annihilator of enemies! If you deem it fit, stay for a day in a secret 
place. You can go tomorrow after taking rest'."_END

B_5_C_58_90
BEGIN_एवम् उक्ता वराअरोहा मणि प्रवरम् उत्तमम् |
प्रायच्छत् परम उद्विग्ना वाचा माम् संदिदेश ह || ५-५८-१०२_END
BEGIN_"Speaking thus, Seetha having fine hips, gave that wonderful and the foremost jewel. 
Highly distressed, she gave a message also in words to me."_END

B_5_C_67_12
BEGIN_क्षिप्तवांस्त्वम् प्रदीप्तम् दर्भम् तम् वायसम् प्रति |
ततः तु वायसम् दीप्तः स दर्भो अनुजगाम ह || ५-६७-१३_END
BEGIN_"You hurled that flaming blade of grass towards the crow. Then that flaming blade of 
grass for its part followed the crow."_END

B_5_C_68_3
BEGIN_मम च अपि अल्प भाग्यायाः साम्निध्यात् तव वानर |
अस्य शोक विपाकस्य मुहूर्तम् स्यात् विमोक्षणम् || ५-६८-४_END
BEGIN_"'O the valiant one! Because of your presence, the termination of my full-blown grief 
may continue for a while'."_END

B_5_C_58_91
BEGIN_ततः तस्यै प्रणम्य अहम् राज पुत्र्यै समाहितः |
प्रदक्षिणम् परिक्रामम् इह अभ्युद्गत मानसः || ५-५८-१०३_END
BEGIN_"Then, offering salutation to Seetha the princess in utmost devotion, I circumambulated 
her from left to right, of course with my mind setting out to come here."_END

B_5_C_67_13
BEGIN_स पित्रा च परित्यक्तः सुरैः सर्वैः महर्षिभिः |
त्रीन् लोकान् सम्परिक्रम्य त्रातारम् न अधिगच्छति || ५-६७-१४_END
BEGIN_"Forsaken by all the celestials, Indra, its father and the sages too, that crow did not 
find a protector even after going round all the three worlds (heaven, earth and the lower regions)."_END

B_5_C_68_4
BEGIN_गते हि त्वयि विक्रान्ते पुनः आगमनाय वै |
प्राणानाम् अपि संदेहो मम स्यान् न अत्र संशयः || ५-६८-५_END
BEGIN_"'When you, the courageous one, have actually left to come back, there will be a danger 
even to my life. There is no doubt about this'."_END

B_5_C_58_92
BEGIN_उत्तरम् पुनः एव आह निश्चित्य मनसा तदा |
हनूमन् मम वृत्त अन्तम् वक्तुम् अर्हसि राघवे || ५-५८-१०४_END
BEGIN_"Determining something in mind, she spoke to me again as follows: 'O Hanuma! You ought 
to tell Rama about my tale of woes occurring here'."_END

B_5_C_67_14
BEGIN_पुनरेवागतस्त्रस्तस्त्वत्सकाशमरिंदम |
स तम् निपतितम् भूमौ शरण्यः शरणा गतम् || ५-६७-१५
वध अर्हम् अपि काकुत्स्थ कृपया परिपालयः |_END
BEGIN_"O destroyer of enemies! Being frightened the crow came to your presence once again and 
sough your protection. Though fit to be killed, you on your part, affording shelter, in mercy to the 
crow, protected that crow which had fallen flat on the ground."_END

B_5_C_68_5
BEGIN_तव अदर्शनजः शोको भूयो माम् परितापयेत् |
दुह्खात् दुह्ख पराभूताम् दुर्गताम् दुह्ख भागिनीम् || ५-६८-६_END
BEGIN_"'The sorrow born of your disappearance will further torment me, who is overtaken by 
one sorrow after another, miserable and doomed to grief as I am'."_END

B_5_C_58_93
BEGIN_यथा श्रुत्वा एव नचिरात् ताव् उभौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |
सुग्रीव सहितौ वीराव् उपेयाताम् तथा कुरु || ५-५८-१०५_END
BEGIN_" 'Act so that both those heroes Rama and Lakshmana together with Sugreeva quickly arrive 
here, soon after hearing my tale'."_END

B_5_C_67_15
BEGIN_मोघम् अस्त्रम् न शक्यम् तु कर्तुम् इति एव राघव || ५-६७-१६
भवांस्तस्यक्षि काकस्य हिनस्ति स्म स दक्षिणम् |_END
BEGIN_'O Rama! Since it is not possible to make the missile a waste, you destroyed the right 
eye of the crow."_END

B_5_C_68_6
BEGIN_अयम् तु वीर संदेहः तिष्ठति इव मम अग्रतः |
सुमहान् त्वत् सहायेषु हरि ऋक्षेषु असंशयः || ५-६८-७_END
BEGIN_"'O best among the monkeys! O valiant one! In the matter of monkeys and bears who are 
your helpmates, this very grave doubt stands before me'."_END

B_5_C_58_94
BEGIN_यदि अन्यथा भवेत् एतत् द्वौ मासौ जीवितम् मम |
न माम् द्रक्ष्यति काकुत्स्थो म्रिये सा अहम् अनाथवत् || ५-५८-१०६_END
BEGIN_"'If proves to be otherwise, my survival will be only for two months. Rama cannot see 
me thereafter. As such, I will be dying like a helpless woman'."_END

B_5_C_67_16
BEGIN_राम त्वाम् स नमः कृत्वा राज्ञो दशरथस्य च || ५-६७-१७
विसृष्टः तु तदा काकः प्रतिपेदे खम् आलयम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! Then, that crow, having been discharged by you, went back to its own habitation, 
after offering salutation to you and to king Dasaratha."_END

B_5_C_68_7
BEGIN_कथम् नु खलु दुष्पारम् तरिष्यन्ति महाउदधिम् |
तानि हरि ऋक्ष सैन्यानि तौ वा नर वर आत्मजौ || ५-६८-८_END
BEGIN_"'How indeed can those troops of monkeys and bears or Rama and Lakshmana can cross that 
great insurmountable ocean?'"_END

B_5_C_58_95
BEGIN_तत् श्रुत्वा करुणम् वाक्यम् क्रोधो माम् अभ्यवर्तत |
उत्तरम् च मया दृष्टम् कार्य शेषम् अनन्तरम् || ५-५८-१०७_END
BEGIN_"Hearing those miserable words, I became angry. Thereafter, I thought of my remaining 
successive action to be done."_END

B_5_C_67_17
BEGIN_एवम् अस्त्रविदाम् श्रेष्ठः सत्त्ववान् शीलवान् अपि || ५-६७-१८
किम् अर्थम् अस्त्रम् रक्षह्सु न योजयसि राघव |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! Why are you not employing the same type of a missile on the demons, though you 
are the foremost among the wielders of missiles, though courageous and possessed of good disposition?"_END

B_5_C_68_8
BEGIN_त्रयाणाम् एव भूतानाम् सागरस्य अस्य लन्घने |
शक्तिः स्यात् वैनतेयस्य वायोः वा तव वा अनघ || ५-६८-९_END
BEGIN_"'Three beings viz. Garuda the eagle, or yourself or the wind-god only have the capacity 
of crossing this ocean'."_END

B_5_C_58_96
BEGIN_ततो अवर्धत मे कायः तदा पर्वत सम्निभः |
युद्ध कान्क्षी वनम् तच् च विनाशयितुम् आरभे || ५-५८-१०८_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, my body grew up to a size equal to that of a mountain. Then, I started destroying 
that garden, thereby longing for a combat."_END

B_5_C_67_18
BEGIN_न नागा न अपि गन्धर्वा न असुरा न मरुत् गणाः || ५-६७-१९
न च सर्वे रणे शक्ता रामम् प्रतिसमासितुम् |_END
BEGIN_"Neither the Nagas the celestials serpents nor even Gandharvas the celestial musicians 
nor the demons nor the troop of Maruts the host of gods, nor all of them joined together are capable 
of fighting with Rama."_END

B_5_C_68_9
BEGIN_तत् अस्मिन् कार्य नियोगे वीर एवम् दुरतिक्रमे |
किम् पश्यसि समाधानम् ब्रूहि कार्यविदाम् वर || ५-६८-१०_END
BEGIN_"'O valiant monkey! That is why, what strategy are you visualizing to fulfill this act, 
which is so difficult to accomplish thus? You are indeed excellent of those who know how to accomplish 
any work'."_END

B_5_C_58_97
BEGIN_तत् भग्नम् वन षण्डम् तु भ्रान्त त्रस्त मृग द्विजम् |
प्रतिबुद्धा निरीक्षन्ते राक्षस्यो विकृत आननाः || ५-५८-१०९_END
BEGIN_"The female-demons; with their ugly faces woke up and saw that thicket of garden being 
broken and with its frightened animals and birds moving about unsteadily."_END

B_5_C_67_19
BEGIN_तस्य वीर्यवतः कच्चिन् मयि यदि अस्ति सम्भ्रमः || ५-६७-२०
क्षिप्रम् सुनिशितैः बाणैः हन्यताम् युधि रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"If that powerful Rama is eager to save me, let him kill Ravana in battle quickly with 
his exceptionally sharp arrows."_END

B_5_C_68_10
BEGIN_कामम् अस्य त्वम् एव एकः कार्यस्य परिसाधने ||
पर्याप्तः पर वीरघ्न यशस्यः ते बल उदयः || ५-६८-११_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma the annihilator of hostile enemies! You, as one alone, are capable of fulfilling 
this task. Your act of fulfilling this task your act of fulfilling the result is well-known."_END

B_5_C_58_98
BEGIN_माम् च दृष्ट्वा वने तस्मिन् समागम्य ततः ततः |
ताः समभ्यागताः क्षिप्रम् रावणाय आचचक्षिरे || ५-५८-११०_END
BEGIN_"Coming from their respective places and seeing me in that garden, those female-demons 
quickly went and reported the matter to Ravana (as follows):"_END

B_5_C_67_20
BEGIN_भ्रातुः आदेशम् आदाय लक्ष्मणो वा परम् तपः || ५-६७-२१
स किम् अर्थम् नर वरो न माम् रक्षति राघवः |_END
BEGIN_"Why even that Lakshmana, the annihilator of adversaries and the foremost of men born 
in Raghu dynasty is not saving me, by taking orders from Rama his brother?"_END

B_5_C_68_11
BEGIN_बलैः समग्रैः यदि माम् हत्वा रावणम् आहवे |
विजयी स्वाम् पुरीम् रामो नयेत् तत् स्यात् यशः करम् || ५-६८-१२_END
BEGIN_""It would result in his glory, if Rama, after killing Ravana along with his entire army, 
takes me to his city in his victory'."_END

B_5_C_58_99
BEGIN_राजन् वनम् इदम् दुर्गम् तव भग्नम् दुरात्मना |
वानरेण हि अविज्ञाय तव वीर्यम् महाबल || ५-५८-१११_END
BEGIN_"O mighty king! Indeed not knowing your prowess, an evil-minded monkey ahs demolished 
your inaccessible garden."_END

B_5_C_67_21
BEGIN_शक्तौ तौ पुरुष व्याघ्रौ वाय्व् अग्नि सम तेजसौ || ५-६७-२२
सुराणाम् अपि दुर्धर्षौ किम् अर्थम् माम् उपेक्षतः |_END
BEGIN_"Wherefore those two competent brothers Rama and Lakshmana, with their splendour equal 
to that of air and fire, and excellent among men, even though they can conquer the celestials, are ignoring 
me?"_END

B_5_C_68_12
BEGIN_यथा अहम् तस्य वीरस्य वनात् उपधिना हृता |
रक्षसा तत् भयात् एव तथा न अर्हति राघवः || ५-६८-१३_END
BEGIN_"'Rama ought not to take me back for fear that Ravana, in the same manner as Ravana the 
demon took me away from the forest in the absence of Rama by cheating that heroic Rama."_END

B_5_C_58_100
BEGIN_दुर्बुद्धेः तस्य राज इन्द्र तव विप्रिय कारिणः |
वधम् आज्ञापय क्षिप्रम् यथा असौ विलयम् व्रजेत् || ५-५८-११२_END
BEGIN_"O emperor! Give orders quickly for killing him, so that the evil-minded monkey, who 
caused offence to you, will get destroyed."_END

B_5_C_67_22
BEGIN_मम एव दुष्कृतम् किंचिन् महत् अस्ति न संशयः || ५-६७-२३
समर्थौ सहितौ यन् माम् न अपेक्षेते परम् तपौ |_END
BEGIN_"There is no doubt that I had done some big impure act, for which reason those two brothers 
Rama and Lakshmana, who torment the enemies, even though capable, are not paying attention to me."_END

B_5_C_68_13
BEGIN_बलैः तु सम्कुलाम् कृत्वा लन्काम् पर बल अर्दनः |
माम् नयेत् यदि काकुत्स्थः तत् तस्य सदृशम् भवेत् || ५-६८-१४_END
BEGIN_If Rama, the destroyer of rival army, fills the entire Lanka with arrows and takes me 
home, it will be quite worthy of him."_END

B_5_C_58_101
BEGIN_तत् श्रुत्वा राक्षस इन्द्रेण विसृष्टा भृश दुर्जयाः |
राक्षसाः किम्करा नाम रावणस्य मनो अनुगाः || ५-५८-११३_END
BEGIN_"Hearing those words, Ravana sent invincible demons called Kinkaras, who were adapted 
to the mind of Ravana."_END

B_5_C_68_14
BEGIN_तत् यथा तस्य विक्रान्तम् अनुरूपम् महात्मनः |
भवति आहव शूरस्य तथा त्वम् उपपादय || ५-६८-१५_END
BEGIN_"For that reason, you act in such a way, that the high-souled Rama, valiant in battle, 
exhibits the prowess befitting of him."_END

B_5_C_67_23
BEGIN_वैदेह्या वचनम् श्रुत्वा करुणम् साश्रु भाषितम् || ५-६७-२४
पुनः अपि अहम् आर्याम् ताम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रुवम् |_END
BEGIN_Hearing the miserable words of Seetha spoken with tears, I again spoke to that venerable 
Seetha the following words:_END

B_5_C_58_102
BEGIN_तेषाम् अशीति साहस्रम् शूल मुद्गर पाणिनाम् |
मया तस्मिन् वन उद्देशे परिघेण निषूदितम् || ५-५८-११४_END
BEGIN_"In that portion of the garden, I destroyed with an iron rod, eight thousand kinkaras, 
having darts and hammers in their hands."_END

B_5_C_68_15
BEGIN_तत् अर्थ उपहितम् वाक्यम् प्रश्रितम् हेतु सम्हितम् |
निशम्य अहम् ततः शेषम् वाक्यम् उत्तरम् अब्रुवम् || ५-६८-१६_END
BEGIN_"Hearing that appeal (of Seetha), that was somewhat good in its meaning, courteous and 
duly furnished with reasons, I gave then my remaining reply (as follows):_END

B_5_C_67_24
BEGIN_त्वत् शोक विमुखो रामो देवि सत्येन ते शपे || ५-६७-२५
रामे दुह्ख अभिभूते च लक्ष्मणः परितप्यते |_END
BEGIN_" 'O Seetha the princess! Rama has grown indifferent because of grief born of separation 
from you. I swear it to you truly. Rama, being overwhelmed with grief, Lakshmana too is feeling pain."_END

B_5_C_58_103
BEGIN_तेषाम् तु हत शेषा ये ते गता लघु विक्रमाः |
निहतम् च मया सैन्यम् रावणाय आचचक्षिरे || ५-५८-११५_END
BEGIN_"Taking quick steps, those few who have survived, went and reported the news to Ravana, 
of their large army having been killed by me."_END

B_5_C_68_16
BEGIN_देवि हरि ऋक्ष सैन्यानाम् ईश्वरः प्लवताम् वरः |
सुग्रीवः सत्त्व सम्पन्नः तव अर्थे कृत निश्चयः || ५-६८-१७_END
BEGIN_"'O Seetha the princess! Sugreeva, the lord of the troops of monkeys and bears, excellent 
among the monkeys and endowed with strength, is firmly determined to rescue you."_END

B_5_C_67_25
BEGIN_कथंचित् भवती दृष्टा न कालः परिशोचितुम् || ५-६७-२६
अस्मिन्मुहूर्तम् दुह्खानाम् अन्तम् द्रक्ष्यसि भामिनि |_END
BEGIN_" 'O faultless one! You can give now, a token of recollection, which Rama can recognize 
and which can beget happiness to him."_END

B_5_C_58_104
BEGIN_ततो मे बुद्धिः उत्पन्ना चैत्य प्रासादम् आक्रमम् |
तत्रस्थान् राक्षसान् हत्वा शतम् स्तम्भेन वै पुनः || ५-५८-११६
ललाम भूतो लन्काया मया विध्वंसितो रुषा |_END
BEGIN_"Then, an idea came to me. Occupying a lofty palatial mansion of a sanctuary which was 
an eminent ornament of Lanka. I killed again a hundred demons stationed there with a pillar."_END

B_5_C_67_26
BEGIN_ताव् उभौ नर शार्दूलौ राज पुत्राव् अरिम् दमौ || ५-६७-२७
त्वत् दर्शन कृत उत्साहौ लन्काम् भस्मी करिष्यतः |_END
BEGIN_" 'Those two princes, the foremost among men and the faultless ones are eager to see 
you. They can reduce Lanka to ashes'."_END

B_5_C_68_17
BEGIN_तस्य विक्रम सम्पन्नाः सत्त्ववन्तो महाबलाः |
मनः सम्कल्प सम्पाता निदेशे हरयः स्थिताः || ५-६८-१८
येषाम् न उपरि न अधस्तान् न तिर्यक् सज्जते गतिः |
न च कर्मसु सीदन्ति महत्स्व् अमित तेजसः || ५-६८-१९_END
BEGIN_"So many monkeys, endowed with prowess, perseverance great strength and who can rush 
to any place as they wish, are intensely committed to Sugreeva's command. There is no hindrance to their 
movement either in the sky or the ground or in a horizontal region between the sky and the ground. Those 
monkeys with unlimited splendour are not indolent in performing any great task."_END

B_5_C_58_105
BEGIN_ततः प्रहस्तस्य सुतम् जम्बु मालिनम् आदिशत् || ५-५८-११७
राक्षसैर्बहुभिः सार्थम् घोररूपैर्भयानकैः |_END
BEGIN_"Then, Ravana dispatched Jambumali, the son of Prahasta together with numerous dreadful 
demons having terrific forms."_END

B_5_C_67_27
BEGIN_हत्वा च समरे रौद्रम् रावणम् सह बान्धवम् || ५-६७-२८
राघवः त्वाम् महाबाहुः स्वाम् पुरीम् नयते ध्रुवम् |_END
BEGIN_" 'O lady with charming hips! Killing the terrific Ravana together with his relatives 
in battle, Rama will certainly take you to his City of Ayodhya'."_END

B_5_C_68_18
BEGIN_असकृत् तैः महाभागैः वानरैः बल सम्युतैः |
प्रदक्षिणी कृता भूमिः वायु मार्ग अनुसारिभिः || ५-६८-२०_END
BEGIN_"Those illustrious monkeys, proud of their strength and following the path of wind, circumambulated 
the entire earth several times."_END

B_5_C_58_106
BEGIN_तम् अहम् बल सम्पन्नम् राक्षसम् रण कोविदम् || ५-५८-११८
परिघेण अतिघोरेण सूदयामि सह अनुगम् |_END
BEGIN_"I destroyed that demon, though endowed with a great strength and skilled in warfare, 
along with his followers, with my terrific iron bar itself."_END

B_5_C_67_28
BEGIN_यत् तु रामो विजानीयात् अभिज्ञानम् अनिन्दिते || ५-६७-२९
प्रीति सम्जननम् तस्य प्रदातुम् तत्त्वम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_" 'O faultless one! You can give now, a token of recollection, which Rama can recognize 
and which can beget happiness to him."_END

B_5_C_68_19
BEGIN_मत् विशिष्टाः च तुल्याः च सन्ति तत्र वन ओकसः |
मत्तः प्रत्यवरः कश्चिन् न अस्ति सुग्रीव सम्निधौ || ५-६८-२१
अहम् तावत् इह प्राप्तः किम् पुनः ते महाबलाः |
न हि प्रकृष्टाः प्रेष्यन्ते प्रेष्यन्ते हि इतरे जनाः || ५-६८-२२_END
BEGIN_"'In them, some of the monkeys are superior to me and some are even equal to me. No one 
in the vicinity of Sugreeva is inferior to me. When I have arrived here, why to talk about those mighty 
ones? Generally, superior ones are not sent for errands. Only others are indeed sent'."_END

B_5_C_58_107
BEGIN_तत् श्रुत्वा राक्षस इन्द्रः तु मन्त्रि पुत्रान् महाबलान् || ५-५८-११९
पदाति बल सम्पन्नान् प्रेषयामास रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing of it, Ravana, the king of demons, dispatched the son of his minister, endowed 
with great strength and strengthened with a regiment of infantry."_END

B_5_C_67_29
BEGIN_सा अभिवीक्ष्य दिशः सर्वा वेणि उद्ग्रथनम् उत्तमम् || ५-६७-३०
मुक्त्वा वस्त्रात् ददौ मह्यम् मणिम् एतम् महाबल |_END
BEGIN_"O mighty Rama! Having surveyed all the directions and having untied from the end of 
her garment, this excellent jewel which was being strung together in her hair that Seetha gave it to 
me."_END

B_5_C_68_20
BEGIN_तत् अलम् परितापेन देवि मन्युः व्यपैतु ते |
एक उत्पातेन ते लन्काम् एष्यन्ति हरि यूथपाः || ५-६८-२३_END
BEGIN_"'O Seetha the princess! Enough of your lamentation. Take away your sorrow. Those leaders 
of monkeys will reach Lanka by one single leap'."_END

B_5_C_58_108
BEGIN_परिघेण एव तान् सर्वान् नयामि यम सादनम् || ५-५८-१२०
मन्त्रि पुत्रान् हतान् श्रुत्वा समरे लघु विक्रमान् |
पन्च सेना अग्रगान् शूरान् प्रेषयामास रावणः || ५-५८-१२१_END
BEGIN_"I killed all of them also by that iron bar itself. Hearing of the minster's sons, who 
were quick in exhibiting their valour in battle, having been killed, Ravana dispatched five valiant 
generals."_END

B_5_C_67_30
BEGIN_प्रतिगृह्य मणिम् दिव्यम् तव हेतो रघु उत्तम || ५-६७-३१
शिरसा सम्प्रणम्य एनाम् अहम् आगमने त्वरे |_END
BEGIN_"O Rama! Taking that wonderful jewel for your sake from her, and offering my salutation 
by bowing my head to that venerable Seetha, I was seized with a haste to come back."_END

B_5_C_68_21
BEGIN_मम पृष्ठ गतौ तौ च चन्द्र सूर्याव् इव उदितौ |
त्वत् सकाशम् महाभागे नृ सिम्हाव् आगमिष्यतः || ५-६८-२४_END
BEGIN_"Rama and Lakshmana, those two lions among men, also of great strength, ascending on 
my shoulders, can come to you, like the rising sun and the moon."_END

B_5_C_58_109
BEGIN_तान् अहम् सह सैन्यान् वै सर्वान् एव अभ्यसूदयम् |
ततः पुनः दशग्रीवः पुत्रम् अक्षम् महाबलम् || ५-५८-१२२
बहुभी राकसैः सार्धम् प्रेषयामास रावणः |_END
BEGIN_"I got all the minster's sons together with their army destroyed. Then, Ravana, the ten-headed 
monster, sent his mighty son, Aksha together with a multitude of army for the combat."_END

B_5_C_67_31
BEGIN_गमने च कृत उत्साहम् अवेक्ष्य वर वर्णिनी || ५-६७-३२
विवर्धमानम् च हि माम् उवाच जनक आत्मजा |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing me who was in a hurry to come back and augmenting my body abundantly, Seetha 
having a beautiful complexion spoke to me."_END

B_5_C_68_22
BEGIN_अरिघ्नम् सिम्ह सम्काशम् क्षिप्रम् द्रक्ष्यसि राघवम् |
लक्ष्मणम् च धनुष् पाणिम् लन्का द्वारम् उपस्थितम् || ५-६८-२५_END
BEGIN_"Rama, the annihilator of enemies, similar to a lion, and Lakshmana wielding a bow in 
his hand, will surely approach the entrance-gate of Lanka and you will see them soon."_END

B_5_C_58_110
BEGIN_तम् तु मन्द उदरी पुत्रम् कुमारम् रण पण्डितम् || ५-५८-१२३
सहसा खम् समुत्क्रान्तम् पादयोः च गृहीतवान् |
चर्म असिनम् शत गुणम् भ्रामयित्वा व्यपेषयम् || ५-५८-१२४_END
BEGIN_"I suddenly caught by the feet, that prince, son of Mandodari, who was skilled in warfare 
and who was jumping into the sky with his sword and shield. I whirled him round a hundred times and 
crushed him."_END

B_5_C_67_32
BEGIN_अश्रु पूर्ण मुखी दीना बाष्प संदिग्ध भाषिणी || ५-६७-३३
ममोत्पतनसम्ब्रान्ता शोकवेगसमाहता |_END
BEGIN_"With her eyes filled with tears, looking miserable, with her words ambiguously coming 
out of her coked throat, bewildered as she was, at the though of my flying away and afflicted with a 
gush of grief; (she spoke to me as follows):_END

B_5_C_68_23
BEGIN_नख दम्ष्ट्र आयुधान् वीरान् सिम्ह शार्दूल विक्रमान् |
वानरान् वानर इन्द्र आभान् क्षिप्रम् द्रक्ष्यसि सम्गतान् || ५-६८-२६_END
BEGIN_"'You can see soon those valiant monkeys, with their claws and tusks as weapons, having 
the prowess of lions and tigers and looking like lordly elephants, coming here together'."_END

B_5_C_58_111
BEGIN_तम् अक्षम् आगतम् भग्नम् निशम्य स दश आननः |
तत इन्द्रजितम् नाम द्वितीयम् रावणः सुतम् || ५-५८-१२५
व्यादिदेश सुसम्क्रुद्धो बलिनम् युद्ध दुर्मदम् |_END
BEGIN_"Hearing of the death of Aksha in combat, that ten-headed Ravana was very much enraged 
and thereupon dispatched his second son, by name Indrajit, who was strong but foolishly arrogant in 
battle."_END

B_5_C_67_33
BEGIN_हनुमन् सिम्ह सम्काशौ ताव् उभौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ५-६७-३४
सुग्रीवम् च सह अमात्यम् सर्वान् ब्रूया अनामयम् |_END
BEGIN_"O Hanuma! Inquire those two brothers Rama and Lakshmana looking like lions, Sugreeva 
together with his ministers and all others about their welfare."_END

B_5_C_68_24
BEGIN_शैल अम्बुदन् निकाशानाम् लन्का मलय सानुषु |
नर्दताम् कपि मुख्यानाम् अचिरात् शोष्यसे स्वनम् || ५-६८-२७_END
BEGIN_"'You will hear within a short time, the clamour of the excellent of monkeys resonating 
like a mountains and clouds, on the peaks of Mount Malaya in Lanka'."_END

B_5_C_58_112
BEGIN_तस्य अपि अहम् बलम् सर्वम् तम् च राक्षस पुम्गवम् || ५-५८-१२६
नष्ट ओजसम् रणे कृत्वा परम् हर्षम् उपागमम् |_END
BEGIN_"By conquering all that army in battle and making that Indrajit the foremost among demons; 
lusterless, I experienced a great joy."_END

B_5_C_67_34
BEGIN_यथा च स महाबाहुः माम् तारयति राघवः |
अस्मात् दुह्ख अम्बु सम्रोधात् तत् समाधातुम् अर्हसि || ५-६७-३५
इमम् च तीव्रम् मम शोक वेगम् |
रक्षोभिः एभिः परिभर्त्सनम् च |
ब्रूयाः तु रामस्य गतः समीपम् |
शिवः च ते अध्वा अस्तु हरि प्रवीर || ५-६७-३६
एतत् तव आर्या नृप राज सिम्ह |
सीता वचः प्राह विषाद पूर्वम् |
एतच् च बुद्ध्वा गदितम् मया त्वम् |
श्रद्धत्स्व सीताम् कुशलाम् समग्राम् || ५-६७-३७_END
BEGIN_" 'You ought to clear up difficulties for that mighty armed Rama, so that he can help 
me to cross this ocean of sorrow. O best of heroes among monkeys! Approaching Rama, tell this horrible 
gush of my grief and the threats of these female-demons. Have a happy journey!' "O illustrious princes, 
the protector of men! The venerable Seetha filled with sorrow spoke these words to be conveyed to you. 
Comprehending this matter spoken by me, believe that Seetha is completely safe."_END

B_5_C_58_113
BEGIN_महता हि महाबाहुः प्रत्ययेन महाबलः || ५-५८-१२७
प्रेषितो रावणेन एष सह वीरैः मद उत्कटैः |_END
BEGIN_"Ravana himself dispatched, with a great confidence, that long-armed and mighty Indrajit 
along with valiant demons excited with their arrogance."_END

B_5_C_68_25
BEGIN_निवृत्त वन वासम् च त्वया सार्धम् अरिम् दमम् |
अभिषिक्तम् अयोध्यायाम् क्षिप्रम् द्रक्ष्यसि राघवम् || ५-६८-२८_END
BEGIN_"'You will see Rama, the annihilator of enemies, returning from exile, and getting anointed 
to the crown in Ayodhya, along with you soon'."_END

B_5_C_58_114
BEGIN_सोऽविषह्यम् हि माम् बुद्ध्वा स्वम् बलम् चावमर्दितम् |
ब्राह्मेण अस्त्रेण स तु माम् प्रबध्नाच् च अतिवेगतः || ५-५८-१२८_END
BEGIN_"Knowing me to be irresistible and his own army being perishable, that Indrajit with 
a great haste, captured me with a Brahma-missile."_END

B_5_C_68_26
BEGIN_ततो मया वाग्भिः अदीन भाषिणी |
शिवाभिः इष्टाभिः अभिप्रसादिता |
जगाम शान्तिम् मम मैथिल आत्मजा |
तव अपि शोकेन तथा अभिपीडिता || ५-६८-२९_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, soothened by me with comforting, well-disposed and agreeable words, Seetha, 
though tormented with thought of your grief, obtained peace of mind."_END

B_5_C_58_115
BEGIN_रज्जूभिः अभिबध्नन्ति ततो माम् तत्र राक्षसाः || ५-५८-१२९
रावणस्य समीपम् च गृहीत्वा माम् उपानयन् |_END
BEGIN_"Then, the demons, after capturing me, tied me there with ropes and carried me away to 
Ravana's presence."_END

B_5_C_58_116
BEGIN_दृष्ट्वा सम्भाषितः च अहम् रावणेन दुरात्मना || ५-५८-१३०
पृष्टः च लन्का गमनम् राक्षसानाम् च तत् वधम् |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing me, the evil-minded Ravana spoke to me. He asked, why did you come to Lanka? 
'Why did you kill the demons?'"_END

B_5_C_58_117
BEGIN_तत् सर्वम् च मया तत्र सीता अर्थम् इति जल्पितम् || ५-५८-१३१
अस्य अहम् दर्शन आकान्क्षी प्राप्तः त्वत् भवनम् विभो |
मारुतस्य औरसः पुत्रो वानरो हनुमान् अहम् || ५-५८-१३२_END
BEGIN_"I answered 'I have done all these acts for the sake of Seetha. O king of demons! I came 
to your abode with a desire to see Seetha. I am the offspring of wind-god and a monkey by name Hanuma'."_END

B_5_C_58_118
BEGIN_राम दूतम् च माम् विद्धि सुग्रीव सचिवम् कपिम् |
सो अहम् दौत्येन रामस्य त्वत् समीपम् इह आगतः || ५-५८-१३३_END
BEGIN_" 'Know me to be a monkey, an envoy of Rama and a minister of Sugreeva. As Rama's messenger, 
I sought your presence here!"_END

B_5_C_58_119
BEGIN_सुग्रीवश्च महातेजाः स त्वाम् कुशलमब्रवीत् |
धर्मार्थकामसहितम् हितम् पथ्यमुवाच च || ५-५८-१३४_END
BEGIN_" �That Sugreeva of great splendour enquired about your welfare. He told you (the following) 
beneficiary words, endowed with righteousness wealth and pleasure, appropriate for you'."_END

B_5_C_58_120
BEGIN_वसतो ऋष्यमूके मे पर्वते विपुल द्रुमे |
राघवो रण विक्रान्तो मित्रत्वम् समुपागतः || ५-५८-१३५_END
BEGIN_" 'While I was dwelling in Mount R^ishyamuka, abounding with numerous trees, Rama having 
a great prowess in battle became a friend to me'."_END

B_5_C_58_121
BEGIN_तेन मे कथितम् राजन् भार्या मे रक्षसा हृता |
तत्र साहाय्य हेतोः मे समयम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ५-५८-१३६_END
BEGIN_" 'The king Rama told me that his wife had been taken away by a demon and that I had 
to help him in that matter by all means'."_END

B_5_C_58_122
BEGIN_मया च कथितम् तस्मै वालिनश्च वधम् प्रति |
तत्र साहय्यहेतोर्मे समयम् कर्तुमर्हसि || ५-५८-१३७_END
BEGIN_" 'I also told him about the killing of Vali and requested him to come to a mutual agreement 
for helping me in that matters'."_END

B_5_C_58_123
BEGIN_वालिना हृत राज्येन सुग्रीवेण सह प्रभुः |
चक्रे अग्नि साक्षिकम् सक्यम् राघवः सह लक्ष्मणः || ५-५८-१३८_END
BEGIN_" 'Rama, the great lord along with Lakshmana made friendship with Sugreeva, (whose kingdom 
was taken away by Vali) taking Agni the fire-god for a witness.'_END

B_5_C_58_124
BEGIN_तेन वालिनम् उत्साद्य शरेण एकेन सम्युगे |
वानराणाम् महाराजः कृतः सम्प्लवताम् प्रभुः || ५-५८-१३९_END
BEGIN_" 'Killing Vali by a single arrow in combat, Rama made Sugreeva (lord of monkeys) an 
emperor of monkeys'."_END

B_5_C_58_125
BEGIN_तस्य साहाय्यम् अस्माभिः कार्यम् सर्व आत्मना तु इह |
तेन प्रस्थापितः तुभ्यम् समीपम् इह धर्मतः || ५-५८-१४०_END
BEGIN_" 'Now we have to extend help to that Rama in all ways. Therefore, I am sending Hanuma 
rightly to your presence'."_END

B_5_C_58_126
BEGIN_क्षिप्रम् आनीयताम् सीता दीयताम् राघवस्य च |
यावन् न हरयो वीरा विधमन्ति बलम् तव || ५-५८-१४१_END
BEGIN_" 'Even before the heroic monkeys destroy your army, bring Seetha quickly and give her 
back to Rama'."_END

B_5_C_58_127
BEGIN_वानराणाम् प्रभवो हि न केन विदितः पुरा |
देवतानाम् सकाशम् च ये गच्छन्ति निमन्त्रिताः || ५-५८-१४२_END
BEGIN_" 'To whom is this strength of the monkeys not already known, who go even to the presence 
of gods, when invited by them for help?'"_END

B_5_C_58_128
BEGIN_इति वनर राजः त्वाम् आह इति अभिहितो मया |
माम् ऐक्षत ततो रुष्टः चक्षुषा प्रदहन्न् इव || ५-५८-१४३_END
BEGIN_" 'Sugreeva the king of monkeys has sent the foregoing message to you. 'When spoken by 
me in these words, Ravana was enraged and looked on me, as though he was going to reduce me to ashes 
with his very looks."_END

B_5_C_58_129
BEGIN_तेन वध्यो अहम् आज्ञप्तो रक्षसा रौद्र कर्मणा |
मत्र्पभावमविज्ञाय रावणेन दुरात्मना || ५-५८-१४४_END
BEGIN_"Without knowing my glory ( in the form of my immunity to death), the evil-minded Ravana, 
the demon doing terrific acts, ordered for my killing."_END

B_5_C_58_130
BEGIN_ततो विभीषणो नाम तस्य भ्राता महामतिः |
तेन राक्षस राजो असौ याचितो मम कारणात् || ५-५८-१४५_END
BEGIN_"Then, there is the brother of that Ravana, called Vibhishana having a great intelligence. 
He entreated Ravana, the king of demons, on my behalf (as follows)"_END

B_5_C_58_131
BEGIN_नैवम् राक्षसशार्दूल त्यज्यतामेष निश्चयः |
राजशास्त्रव्यपेतो हि मार्गः संसेव्यते त्वया || ५-५८-१४६_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana the foremost among the demons! No such attempt should be made in this way. 
Let this design be abandoned forthwith. Your are indeed following a path which is contrary to the statesmanship."_END

B_5_C_58_132
BEGIN_दूत वध्या न दृष्टा हि राज शास्त्रेषु राक्षस |
दूतेन वेदितव्यम् च यथा अर्थम् हित वादिना || ५-५८-१४७_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana! It is not indeed found in states' policies of killing an envoy. The real truth 
is to be known from an envoy speaking a good counsel."_END

B_5_C_58_133
BEGIN_सुमहति अपराधे अपि दूतस्य अतुल विक्रमः |
विरूप करणम् दृष्टम् न वधो अस्ति इह शास्त्रतः || ५-५८-१४८_END
BEGIN_"O Ravana of great prowess! Even if a very high offence is committed by an envoy, an 
act of disfiguring the person is mentioned in a treatise of state-policy and not of killing."_END

B_5_C_58_134
BEGIN_विभीषणेन एवम् उक्तो रावणः संदिदेश तान् |
राक्षसान् एतत् एव अद्य लान्गूलम् दह्यताम् इति || ५-५८-१४९_END
BEGIN_"Hearing the words of Vibhishana, Ravana ordered those demons to burn my tail by fire."_END

B_5_C_58_135
BEGIN_ततः स्तस्य वचः श्रुत्वा मम पुच्छम् समन्ततः |
वेष्टितम् शण वक्लैः च पटैः कार्पासकैः तथा || ५-५८-१५०_END
BEGIN_"Thereupon, hearing Ravana's words; the demons wrapped up my entire tail with bark of 
hemp and torn cotton-clothes."_END

B_5_C_58_136
BEGIN_राक्षसाः सिद्ध सम्नाहाः ततः ते चण्ड विक्रमाः |
तत् आदीप्यन्त मे पुच्छम् हनन्तः काष्ठ मुष्टिभिः || ५-५८-१५१
बद्धस्य बहुभिः पाशैः यन्त्रितस्य च राक्षसैः |_END
BEGIN_"Thereafter, the demons of terrible prowess, who completed their arrangements, striking 
me with their wooden staffs and fists, burnt my tail. Eventhough I was bound with many ropes, I maintained 
restraint."_END

B_5_C_58_137
BEGIN_ततः ते राक्षसाः शूरा बद्धम् माम् अग्नि सम्वृतम् || ५-५८-१५२
अघोषयन् राज मार्गे नगर द्वारम् आगताः |_END
BEGIN_"Then, having reached the city-gate, those strong demons made a loud proclamation of 
my presence in the principal streets, bound and enveloped in flames as I was."_END

B_5_C_58_138
BEGIN_ततो अहम् सुमहत् रूपम् सम्क्षिप्य पुनः आत्मनः || ५-५८-१५३
विमोचयित्वा तम् बन्धम् प्रकृतिस्थः स्थितः पुनः |
आयसम् परिघम् गृह्य तानि रक्षांसि असूदयम् || ५-५८-१५४_END
BEGIN_"Then, after contracting my gigantic form once more and releasing my bondage, I stood 
in my native form again. Seizing an iron bar, I killed those demons."_END

B_5_C_58_139
BEGIN_ततः तन् नगर द्वारम् वेगेन आप्लुतवान् अहम् |
पुच्छेन च प्रदीप्तेन ताम् पुरीम् साट्ट गोपुराम् || ५-५८-१५५
दहामि अहम् असम्भ्रान्तो युग अन्त अग्निः इव प्रजाः |_END
BEGIN_"Then, I quickly jumped on to that city-gate and without any bewilderment, I set fire 
that city with its attics, ramparts and gates with my tail inflamed, even as a fire at the end of the 
world, burns all living creatures."_END

B_5_C_58_140
BEGIN_विनष्टा जानकी व्यक्तम् न ह्यदग्धः प्रदृश्यते || ५-५८-१५६
लङ्कायाम् कश्चिदुद्देशः सर्वा भस्मीकृता पुरी |
दहता च मया लन्काम् दघ्दा सीता न संशयः || ५-५८-१५७
रामस्य हि महत्कार्यम् मयेदम् वितथीकृतम् |_END
BEGIN_"The entire Lanka has been reduced to ashes. No place is seen unburnt in this City. Therefore 
Seetha also must have been surely burnt."_END

B_5_C_58_141
BEGIN_इति शोकसमाविष्टश्चन्तामहमुपागतः || ५-५८-१५८
अथ अहम् वाचम् अश्रौषम् चारणानाम् शुभ अक्षराम् |
जानकी न च दग्धा इति विस्मय उदन्त भाषिणाम् || ५-५८-१५९_END
BEGIN_"Thus filled with grief, I came about to reflect as above. Meanwhile, I heard the auspiciously 
worded utterance of charanas the celestial signers who were narrating a tale of astonishment saying 
that Seetha has not been burnt."_END

B_5_C_58_142
BEGIN_ततो मे बुद्धिः उत्पन्ना श्रुत्वा ताम् अद्भुताम् गिरम् |
अदग्धा जानकीत्येवम् निमित्तैश्चोपलक्षिता || ५-५८-१६०_END
BEGIN_"After hearing those surprising words, a thought arose in me that Seetha escaped being 
burnt. This indicated by the following good omens:_END

B_5_C_58_143
BEGIN_दीप्यमाने तु लाङ्गूले न माम् दहति पावकः |
हृदयम् च प्रहृष्टम् मे वाताः सुरभिगन्धिनः ५-५८-१६१_END
BEGIN_"In the first place, even though me tail is burning, the fire is not burning my body. 
My heart too is delighted. The winds are sweet-smelling."_END

B_5_C_58_144
BEGIN_तैर्निमित्तैश्च दृष्टार्थैः कारणैश्च महागुणैः |
ऋषिवाक्यैश्च सिद्धार्थैरभवम् हृष्टमानसः || ५-५८-१६२_END
BEGIN_"My heart was delighted by seeing those good omens having their fruits apparent, by looking 
into the their fruits apparent, by looking into the reasons of high characteristics and by hearing the 
words of accomplished sages."_END

B_5_C_58_145
BEGIN_पुनः दृष्टा च वैदेही विसृष्टः च तया पुनः |
ततः पर्वतमासाद्य तत्ररिष्तमहम् पुनः || ५-५८-१६३
प्रतिप्लवनमारेभे युष्मद्दर्शनकांक्षया |_END
BEGIN_"Seeing Seetha once more, relieved by her again and then reaching the Mount Arishta there 
again, I started leaping back (over the sea) with a longing to see you (all)."_END

B_5_C_58_146
BEGIN_ततः पवनचन्द्रर्क सिद्धगन्धर्व सेवितम् || ५-५८-१६४
पन्थानमहमाक्रम्य भवतो दृष्टवानिह |_END
BEGIN_"Then, treading upon the path of the sky, frequented by the wind, the moon, the sun, 
Siddhas the semi-divine beings and Gandharvas the celestial musicians, I saw you all here."_END

B_5_C_58_147
BEGIN_राघवस्य प्रभावेन भवताम् चैव तेजसा || ५-५८-१६५
सुग्रीवस्य च कार्य अर्थम् मया सर्वम् अनुष्ठितम् |_END
BEGIN_"I performed all tasks for accomplishing the purpose of Sugreeva, by the grace of Rama 
and also through your energy."_END

B_5_C_58_148
BEGIN_एतत् सर्वम् मया तत्र यथावत् उपपादितम् || ५-५८-१६६
अत्र यन् न कृतम् शेषम् तत् सर्वम् क्रियताम् इति |_END
BEGIN_"I have done all this properly there. Do accomplish that which remains undone in this 
task by me and complete it."_END
